Ukunguut nengllugutet , sivunghi Jesus Christ-am . Tagikaaguq David-em nengllugutanganeng . David Abraham-enkuneng pinguuq .
Abraham atakaa Isaac-em , Isaac atakaa Jacob-em , Jacob atakaat Judah-nkut anglegutkullghiit ,
Judah atakaak Perez-enkuk , Zerah-nkuk ( Naangak Tamar ) , Perez atakaa Hezron-em , Hezron atakaa Ram-em ,
Ram atakaa Amminadab-em , Amminadab atakaa Nahshon-em , Nahshon atakaa Salmon-em ,
Salmon atakaa Boaz-em , ( Boaz-em naakaa Rahab ) . Boaz atakaa Obed-em , ( Obed-em naakaa Ruth ) , Obed atakaa Jesse-m ,
Jesse atakaa Umiilgem David-em . David atakaa Solomon-em . ( Solomon-em naakaa Uriah-m nulighqesaqanga . )
Solomon atakaa Rehoboam-em , Rehoboam atakaa Abijah-m , Abijah atakaa Asa-m ,
Asa atakaa Jehoshaphat-em , Jehoshaphat atakaa Joram-em , Joram atakaa Uzziah-m .
Uzziah atakaa Jotham-em , Jotham atakaa Ahaz-em , Ahaz atakaa Hezekiah-m ,
Hezekiah atakaa Manasseh-m , Manasseh atakaa Amos-em , Amos atakaa Josiah-m .
Josiah atakaat , Jechoniah-nkut anglegutkullghhiit allgeqaagut tamaani Jews-et tuguluki aglaataqngatki Babylon-mun .
Kingunganeng aglaatellghita Babylon-mun , Jechoniah atakaa Shealtiel-em , Shealtiel atakaa Zerubbabel-em ,
Zerubbabel atakaa Abiud-em , Abiud atakaa Eliakim-em , Eliakim atakaa Azor-em ,
Azor atakaa Zadok-em , Zadok atakaa Achim-em , Achim atakaa Eliud-em ,
Eliud atakaa Eleazar-em , Eleazar atakaa Matthan-em , Matthan atakaa Jacob-em ,
Jacob atakaa Joseph-em . Joseph ugiikaa Mary-m . Mary naakaa Jesus-em . Jesus Messiah-nguuq .
Sivunghi Jesus Christ-am whatetut : 14-ngukaagut kingunqullghiit Abraham-emeng David-mun . 14-ngukaagutlu kingunqullghiit David-meng kenlanga Jews-et tuguluki aglaatellghitnun Babylon-mun . Taagken Babylon-mun aglaatellghitneng 14-ngukaagutlu kingunqullghiit kenlanga Christ-am allgellghanun .
Jesus Christ-a allgeqaaguq whaten : naanga Mary aang始ghutngwaaqaq Joseph-mun , iwernga nengughutellghillukek Agleghnalghiim Taghnegham qumingestekaa .
Ugikaghqaan Joseph-em kenqigneghutmineng kayngusaakneghmeng Mary piluku , aksaqluku peggnaqegkaa .
Sumeghtaghaatkumaluku tawaten pilleghqani , Atanghem yaqulgan aliighvikluku qavangukun pikaa , " Joseph , David-em kingungha , alingegpenang nulighqigu Mary qayughllak Agleghnalghiim Taghnegham aqsangestekaqaa .
Ighnengnaqnguuq ; atighnaken Jesus-meng qayughllak ellmi yuni yuguliyaghqaqii seghleghqellghitneng . "
Qamaglluni tawaten aneghtekaaguq apeghiighnaluku Atanghem akuzitkegkaa uuknaliqistekun whaten ,
" Aghnaghaq yugem atuqellghilkanga qumingluni , ighnengellequq . Aatqesaghqaqaa Emmanuel " whaten pisiq , " Kiyaghneq whangkunnilnguq . "
Enkaam Joseph taghtughluni Atanghem yaqulgan pisqellghatun pikaq . Mary nulighqegkaa ,
iwernga atuqumangilkanga kenlanga ighnengellghanun . Taagken Joseph-em Jesus-meng atiqaa .
Jesus allgeghaqngan Bethlehem-emi Judea-melngughmi , Herod umiilgulghii . Allgellghan kingunganeng ighaleqetaaghneng liitkaghllaget asivaghmeng kaatkat Jerusalem-emun .
Aapqughwaaqat , " Naagu taghnughhaq allgelghii umiilgat Jews-et ? Ighaleqetaagha esghaamaaghput asivaghmelluku enkaam manigughyaghtughaqaghput . "
Umiilgem Herod-em nagaqughluku teggellghiighllakaq , qamagtengngwaaghlutengllu Jerusalem-eghmiit maligulluteng .
Tagsiqlighteghluki qamaglluki chief priest-etlu , apeghtughikayugetlu Liilightuusaneng aaptekii , " Nani Christ-a allgeghyaghqaawa ? "
Kiimsiqaat , " Bethlehem-emi Judea-melngughmi . Uuknaliqistem whaten igaqegkaqaa :
' Elpek Bethlehem , Judah-melnguq , igleghutisteyaggiitneng Judah-m ukavantelleghpigaanghituten , qayughllak elpeneng taginaqnguuq igleghutista , igleghutiyaghqaq yumneng Israel-eghmiineng . ' "
Taagken Herod-em aksaqluku tagsiqliqii ighaleqetaaghneng liitkaghllaget , liigiknaluku qavngaq aliighyuwhaaqaatanga ighaleqetaaq .
Taagken pikii , " Bethlehem-emun aghulaqlusi elngaatall ivaghteggu taghnughhaq . Naalkegkufsigu ungipaasaghtughnakefsinga , whangallu manigughyaghtughlleqaqa . "
Tawaten umiilgem piyisteng igleghtekat . Esghaghlaataqaat ataasiq taana ighaleqetaaq asivaghmelluku , enkaam elngaatall quyateghllakat . Maligtekaat kenlanga aghuliillghanun taghnughhaam nengan quulngani .
Iteghluteng mangteghamun esghaqaat taghnughhaq , naangallu Mary . Segesqughquulluteng maniguqaat . Taagken aqeftaghaateng qelpeghlluki tunquqaat tunusameng : gold-meng , frankincense-meng , myrrh-meng .
Taagken Kiyaghneghem qavangukun yitkii Herod-mun uteghnifqiita pisqelluki enkaam aglaqat nunameggnun allatgun tumetgun .
Ighaleqetaaghneng liitkaghllaget aghulaqsata , qavangukun Atanghem yaqulgan aliighvikluku Joseph pikaa , " Makelluten taghnughhaqlu naangallu anagutikek Egypt-mun . Tamaanlleghhaten uteghniisqellemnun kenlanga qayughllak Herod-em ivaghtesnaqa taghnughhaq tuqutesnaluku . "
Enkaam unugmi tawani Joseph-em makelluni aghulaqutkakek taghnughhaqlu naangallu Egypt-mun .
Tamaantekat kenlanga Herod-em tuqullghanun . Enkaam apeghiiqaaguq Atanghem akuzitkegkaa uuknaliqistekun whaten , " Tuqluqaqaqa ighneqa tagisqelluku Egypt-meng . "
Herod-em liigiksamigu ighaleqetaaghneng liitkaghllagnun puughsimaniluni sakriteghllakaq . Taagken pilluwaghtet kayagtekii Bethlehem-emun , uvitanganunllu tuquqiisqelluki qamaglluki mekelghiighhaat allgenghhaghhaghneng , maalghugegnun ayumiqulleghtutkalghiinun kenlanga . Tamaakut taghnughhaat nakmikegkaqii qayughllak ighaleqetaaghem allgellghaneng maalghugughlleghhiik ayumiqullghek , ighaleqetaaghneng liitkaghllaget apellghitni .
Tawaten pilleghqun uuknaliqistem Jeremiah-am uuknaliqellgha apeghiiqaq :
" Ramah-mi nagaquqaat leghaghllagaataq . Rachel-nguftuq qiyalghii avaqutaminun , repall ilutughsaghyaghqaaghhaagpenani , qayughllak qamaglluteng tuqulaghaatkat . "
Joseph-enkut Egypt-melluki Herod tuqukaq , qavangukun Atanghem yaqulgan aliighvikegkaa Joseph
pikaa , " Makelluten taghnughhaqlu naangallu uteghniitikek Israel-mun , qayughllak tuqutinaqsalghiit taghnughhaghmeng tuqulaghaasimaat . "
Enkaam Joseph-em makelluni taghnughhaqlu naangallu aglaatkakek Israel-mun .
Iwernga Joseph-em nagaqughluku nutaghaq umiilga Judea-m , Archelaus-nguniluku Herod-em ighnegha , alingegkaq tawavek aglaneghmeng . Qavangukun Kiyaghneghem ungipaatkaa Joseph Judea-tefqaan pisqelluku , enkaam Nazareth-mun aglaqat Galilee-melngughmun . Tamaantekat uuknaliqistet whaten pillghat , apeghiighesqelluku , " Messiah Nazareth-eghmiinguyaghqaaguq . "
Taakwaningani John Paaptaayesta aglaghluni kilgaanganun Judea-m , piinliqaq ungipaqimeng .
Whaten pikaq , " Avuteghqellusi taaqitek seghleghqenneghmeng , qayughllak Ataneghpagullgha Qilagem kaasaghtuumaaq . "
John-nguuq uuknaliqistem Isaiah-am akuzitkegkaa whaten piiqngami , " Kilgaani kina akilghuugaquq whaten : ' Yataaghqiteggu Atanghem tuumkaghqaa , taklaghrukegsaghteggu igleghavigkaa ! ' "
John-em aatkii camel-em melqwaaneng ulimaaghet , meqameng tafsiluni , neqekluni locust-mengllu honey-mengllu .
Yuget aglaghtuutkat ellnganun Jerusalem-emengllu Judea-mengllu uvitanganengllu Kiiwem Jordan-em .
Seghleghqelleteng qayvighqenghatki , John-em paaptaayaaqegkangi Jordan-egni .
John-em esghaghluki Pharisees-elghutetlu Sadducees-elghutetlu tagilghiit ellminun paaptaayesqelluteng pikii , " Elpesi nemeghyani ! Kitum anagesqisi Kiyaghneghem nanqigtelleghqaaneng kaannaqelghiimeng ?
Sivuklusi pinitun pilleghpesigun ipapighqiteggu seghleghqelleghpesineng avuteghqelleghsi .
Whaten始ngam sumeghtaghaghpenasi , ' Kiyaghneghem nanqiggnaanghitiinkut qayughllak kingunqiinkut Abraham-em . ' Ungipaatamsi Kiyaghneghem Abraham kingunengllaannayaghaa maaken uyghagneng !
Whaa maaten qalqalimayaqleggiinaghlluteng ayuqut uqfiget akwiitgun . Qamaglluteng uqfiget pinilghiimeng piitestinghilnguut kepluki , kenghegnun miluusaghqaagut .
Meghqun paaptaayeghiiqunga avuteghkegkanun seghleghqelleghmeggneng . Iwernga tagiyaghqam kingumneng paaptaayelleqiisi Agleghnalghiignengllu Taghneghagneng , keneghmengllu . Aghtughyaghqaanghiteghllagtuq whangamneng , repall talwa kamegkek tugumiiqepagningitagka .
Taana tagiyaghqaq nanqigtiyaqleggiinaaguq . Aafsaghqaqii pinilghiit yuget seghleghneng , katam piitesiighaghtem pekutamineng malliillghatun grain-et . Kagpagluki grain-et mallaq tamaana miluusaghqaqaa qaamyaghqaanghilnguugnun kenghegnun . "
Taagken Jesus Galilee-meng tagikaq Jordan-egnun , John-mun paaptaayesqelluni .
Iwernga John-em akuzinnaqutkegkaqsaqanga whaten , " Whanga elpek paaptaayeyaghqaqsaghaghpenga . Sangavek whangamnun tagizin ? "
Iwernga Jesus-em pikaa , " Legan saaqsin paaptaayenga qayughllak tawaten pikumtung apeghiighlleqaghpung Kiyaghneghem piyukellgha . " Enkaam John-em paaptaayekaa .
Jesus paaptaayeyatni meghmeng aanegkaq . Taagken qilak qelpeghluni esghaqakek Kiyaghneghem Taghneghakek ukilghiik dove-etun ayuqlutek , enkaam ellngakun nalukak .
Taagken ma qilagmeng pikaq , " Unanguuq piniqegkaghllaka Ighneqa , efquqepigtaqa . "
Taagken Agleghnalghiim Taghnegham aghulaqutkaa Jesus kilgaanun , Tughneghaghmun seghleghqesnaqutkesqelluku .
40 aghneq , 40 unuk Jesus neghumangilnguq ; taagken taakut aghneghet kingungitneng iyataqaq .
Taagken Tughneghaam takuluku pikaa , " Kiyaghneghem Ighneqngukangaten , neqngughtesqiki tamaakut uyghaget . "
Iwernga Jesus-em pikaa , " Akuzitet Igaqegkat pikaagut , ' Yuuk kiyaghhnaanghituq neqnginaghhaghqun , iwernga kiyaghsaghqaaguq tamaghhaakun Kiyaghneghem akuzitangakun . ' "
Taagken Tughneghaam Jesus aglaatkaa Jerusalem-emun , Agleghnalghiimun Neghllagmun . Tawani Temple-m uusqallghakun nekevesluku
pikaa , " Kiyaghneghem Ighneqngukangaten , qetgeghi tesamavek ; qayughllak Akuzitet Igaqegkat pikaagut , ' Kiyaghneghemnguq yaqulegminun paqnasightesaghtughlleqaaten ; iiggmeggneng nuqneqelleqaaten luuraq itegaghten uyghaghquunnayukata . ' "
Jesus-em pikaa , " Iwernga Akuzitet Igaqegkat whatenllu pikaagut , ' Ataneq Kiyaghneghen nanghiiqugpenaan sasqelluku ellngan piyukelqenghilkanganeng . ' "
Taagken Tughneghaam Jesus mayuulluku uusqapiglleghiimun naayghamun kelgutkii qamagtengngwaaghluki ataneghpagullghi nunam , pinighnalleghllagillu .
Enkaam pikaa , " Qamagtengngwaaghluki maakut tuunelleqanka elpenun , segesqughlluten manigughyaquvnga . "
Taagken Jesus-em pikaa , " Tughneghaq , iqiten ! Akuzitet Igaqegkat whaten pikaagut , ' Manigughyaghqaqan Ataneq Kiyaghneghen , ellnginaaguqlu qepghaasaghqan ! ' "
Taagken Tughneghaam unisagu Jesus , yaqulget aflengaksaghtuqaat .
Jesus-em nagaqughluku John anusimingllaghvigmenniluku , Galilee-mun uteghniqaq .
Nazareth-meng aglaqaq Capernaum-emun tamaannaluni . Capernaum esnenganituq Naayvam Galilee-m , nunami Zebulun-enkuk Naphtali-nkuk kingunghita kiyaghfigitni .
Jesus-em tawaten pilleghmikun apeghiiqaa uuknaliqistem Isaiah-m uuknaliqellgha . Qavngarugllak Isaiah-m uuknaliqutkegkaqii yuget kiyaghlleghhiit nunagkeni Zebulun-enkuk Naphtali-nkuk . Taakuk nunak naayvam tunganganilnguuk , nallangani Kiiwem Jordan-em , Galilee-melngughmi Gentile-et kiyaghfigitni !
Isaiah-m pikaqegkangi whaten , " Tamaakut kiyaghlleghhiit seghleghqellghem mamleghqestellghani esghaasaghqaagut nighugllagmeng . Alingellghita tuqumeng llangaqa nunangat saapngalghii taghneghangutellghaneng tuqullghem . Iwernga maaten aghtaghaataqii . "
Galilee-mun uteghnilleghmineng kenlekluku Jesus-em piinliqaa ungipaqilleni , " Avuteghqellusi seghleghqennanightek , qayughllak Ataneghpagullgha Qilagem kaasaghtuumaaq . "
Jesus-em igleghutkelluku esnengani Naayvam Galilee-m , esghaqakek anglegutkullghiik , Simon-enkunguftuk ( aatghan allgha Peter ) , Andrew-nkuk . Iqalliniilghiik negaghpagtek miluutaqluku naayvamun .
Taagken Jesus-em pikakek , " Maligtegnenga , apeghtughlleqamtek iqalliniightengughtesqellutek yugneng . "
Tawaninginaq negaghpatek unilluki maligtekaak .
Taaganiqaaghaq esghaqakek anglegutkullghiik , James-enkuk John-enkuk ighneghqek Zebedee-m . Angyameggni atakullghiit negaghpateng ilaaghtughaqeftiit . Jesus-em tuqluqakek .
Tawaninginaq angyaghtek unitkaak atayeklu enkaam Jesus maligtekaak .
Jesus igleghakaq tamanganun Galilee-mi , synagogue-ngitni apeghtughiiqluni . Nani alngunak ungipaqaq Pinilghiineng Ungipaaneng Ataneghpagullghem , naallghuquqaq tamaghhaaneng aqnighneghnengllu , qinuyugnengllu .
Ungipaq mingitkaalghii naallghuqullgha tamaghhaani Syria-mi . Enkaam yuget tagitkiit ellnganun qamaglluki qinuyulghiit , allaaghhiinaaghneng aqnighnelget , ikfiqngalghiit , tughneghalget , sayugpagtaqayuget , uniiqatlu . Qamaglluki Jesus-em naallghutkii .
Uglaapiglleghhiim maligtekaat Galilee-meng , Decapolis-meng , Jerusalem-emeng , Judea-meng , Jordan-emllu inglunganeng taagegken .
Jesus-em esghaghluki yulghuteghllaget maligullghiit , qemimun mayughluni aqumegkaq . Maligsaaghtemi takulaghaasatni ,
apeghtughikaq :
" Tamaakut liisimakilghiit aklukingalleghmeggneng Kiyaghneghem kayusillghaneng quyastellelguut , qayughllak yukii Ataneghpagullghan Qilagem .
Tamaakut qivghulghiit quyastellelguut , qayughllak Kiyaghneghem ilutughsaghyaghqaqii .
Tamaakut qusevegngalghiit quyastellelguut , qayughllak Kiyaghneghem tuunyaghqaqaa nuna ellngitnun .
Tamaakut atuqiyupiglleghhiit Kiyaghneghem piyukellghaneng quyastellelguut , qayughllak Kiyaghneghem tuunyaghqaqii piyukellghitneng .
Tamaakut nangllegtalghiit quyastellelguut , qayughllak Kiyaghneghem nangllegyagusaghqaqii .
Tamaakut umyugaqegtat quyastellelguut , qayughllak esghaghyaghqaqaat Kiyaghneq .
Tamaakut nekeggmellengestikayuget yugneng quyastellelguut , qayughllak Kiyaghneghem avaqutaqniyaghqaqii .
Tamaakut amyuutkellengelghiit atuqutmeggneng Kiyaghneghem piyukellgha , qaatkutngatmeggneng quyastellelguut , qayughllak yukii Ataneghpagullghan Qilagem .
" Quyastellelguusi yuget seghlequuqangisi , amyuutkegkangisi , iqlengiqutkegkangisi maligsaaghtengutegpesineng whangamnun .
Elngaatall quyaghllagtek qayughllak qilagmi pama akileghtuusaghqalegllaguusi . Amenqun , neghighluku uuknaliqistet amyuutkegkiit katam maaten amyuutkellghistun elpesi .
" Taghyustun ayuqusi nunam yuganun . Iwernga taghyuq taghyughningiiskuni , alla naten taghyughnighsaghqaanghituq . Atuunanighllequq samun alngunak enkaam egllequq taagken yuget tutmaasghaqelleqaat . "
" Nighugestun ayuqusi nunam yuganun . Neghllak qemim qaaynganilnguq talughngayaghqaanghituq .
Talwa kitum alngunak kenelghutak kumaghllukek sagneghmun asingiinnaanghitaak . Itupill quulvaqun llilleqaak nighugutesqellukek tamaghhaanun ilunganilngughnun .
Tawateghpigaq nighugsi kuukgutesteggu yugnun esghiisqelluku aneghneghqilleghsi , enkaam usuqnakangat Atazi qilagmelnguq .
" Sumeghtaghaatkegpenanga taaqesaghtuuniluki atuqneghmeng Moses-em Liilightuusiillu uuknaliqistetlu apeghtuusiit . Tagingunga apeghtuutkennaluki ipa sameng pisighpigaatangi .
Ipa piimsi , qilagenkuk nunankuk kenletghuutellghegkenun kenlanga , talwa sasquvegaghhaq allangughhnaanghituq Liilightuusanilnguq kenlanga qamaglluteng Liilightuusanilnguut apeghiillghitnun .
Enkaangam kitum alngunak qaatkenghilkumigu ataasiq Liilightuusaq , apeghtuusaqegkumigullu yugnun qaatkefqaan pisqelluku , Kiyaghneghem pilleqaa ukalighpigaaniluku Ataneghpagullghani Qilagem . Naqamenraq kitum alngunak qaatkegkumiki Liilightuusat , apeghtuqumikillu ilangi yuget qaatkesqelluki , Kiyaghneghem pilleqaa aangyaghqaaniluku Ataneghpagullghani Qilagem .
Enkaam ungipaatamsi , iteghnaanghitusi Ataneghpagullghanun Qilagem , wetkuqun qaatkutngaaghataghaqufsi Kiyaghneghmun , apeghtughikayugneng Liilightuusaneng , Pharisees-enengllu .
" Nagaquqaqaghsi sivunesinguq ungipaatkaqiit , ' Yugtaghpenasi . Kina alngunak yugtalghii nanqigsaqleguuq aghyuughyaghqaaluni . '
Iwernga whanga piimsi , kitum alngunak ugumiyaguskumigu yulgutni , nanqigtivigmun aglaghsaqleguuq . Kitum alngunak pikumigu yulgutni , ' Uyuq nallughllak ' , agghistenun aglaghsaqleguuq . Kitum alngunak sasiinghinnikumigu yulgutni , aglaghsaqleguuq kumaghulghiimun hell-mun .
Enkaangam aghqefigegni Kiyaghneghmun tuuninaqumaluten tunusaghpeneng , neqaaskuvgu sugagsimaniluku yulguten ,
tunusan unilluku ilaliighyaghtughnaken . Taagken tagiluten tunusan tuunaken Kiyaghneghmun .
" Kitum avutkumakangaten seghletun pimaniluni , ilaliighaghhnaken aglaasimaluten nanqigtivigmun , luuraq avutkistegpek tuunayukangaten nanqigtistemun . Taagken nanqigtistem kelengakistemun anusimingllaghtesnayukangaten .
Ipa piimken , anusimingllaghtesimakangaten aanaanghituten kenlanga nanqigtistem llivikesqellgha qamaglluku llivikegkuvgu .
" Nagaquqaqaghsi whaten pilleq , ' Gelgaghniighpenasi ' .
Iwernga whanga piimsi , kitum alngunak esghaghluku aghnaq qiliiqegkumigu taawa gelgaghniighuuq qamagun ilumikun .
Enkaam aghenqigneghem iyegpek seghleghqestekangaten , iikluku eggnaken ! Itagnaghyaghqaaguq yugusin nalighneghiteghngaaghmi , iingunaghmi hell-mun miluutelleghqaaneng .
Aghenqigneghem iiggegpek seghleghqestekangaten , kepluki eggnaketen ! Pinighataghaghyaghqaaguq yugusin nalighneghiteghngaaghmi , iingunaghmi hell-mun pilleghqaaneng .
" Nagaquqaqaghsi whaten pilleq , ' Kitum alngunak nuliini pegtekumigu , igangllaannakanga kelgutusighqameng pegsimaniluku . '
Iwernga whanga piimsi , yugem nuliini pegsaghqaqenghita wetkuqun gelgaghniiqan . Gelgaghniinghiteghngaan pegtekumigu , gelghaghniightesleqaa allaneng yugmeng ugiiqan . Kitum nulighkegkumigu , taana yuuk ellngallu gelgaghniighullequq .
" Nagaquqaqaghsillu sivunesinguq ungipaatkaqiit , ' Akequsan avelghaghpenaan , iwernga Ataneghmun akequsan atuqaqigu ' .
Iwernga whanga piimsi , akeqigpenang atuqluku Kiyaghneghem aatgha , nalighmeng sakun alngunak . Akeqigpenang qilagkun qayughllak aqumutaqaa Kiyaghneghem igleghutilleghminun ,
nalighmeng nunakun qayughllak itegaghiitaqaa Kiyaghneghem , nalighmeng Jerusalem-kun qayughllak neghllakaa Umiilegpagllagem .
Akeqigpenangllu naasqughpegun qayughllak talwa ataasighhaq nuyaq qateghtesnaanghitan nalighmeng tagneghtesnaanghitan .
Yeghlegi legan ' aang始ghhaasi ' , nalighmeng ' nakaaghhaasi ' . Sangwaat ilaskufsiki taakugnun Tughneghaghmeng pinguut .
" Nagaquqaqaghsi whaten pilleq , ' Kina iiyngiquvgu elpeklu iiyngighyaghqaaguten . Kitum gguutnga mughugaghtekuvgu elpeklu gguten mughugaghsaghqaaguq ' .
" Iwernga whanga piimsi , seghletun pistesi akitegpenaki . Kitum qasaghtekangaten ullungagpegun inglungallu tuunaken .
Enkaam kitum aglaaskangaten nanqigtistemun , ggategken ellmi pinalukek qaasligkenllu tuunakegken ellnganun .
Kitum alngunak qelghuskagu akmagtani igleghutesqelluku ataasimun mile-mun , alla ataasiq mile-a ilannaken .
Kitum sameng tungsighvikegkangaten , tuunaken . Kitum sameng navghaghvikegkangaten , navghinnaken .
" Nagaquqaqaghsi whaten pilleq , ' Piniqluki ilakumtaasi , ugumikluki ugumikilghiit elpesineng ' .
Iwernga whanga piimsi , ' Piniqluki ugumikilghiit elpesineng , yughaatkaqitekillu amyuutkistesi Kiyaghneghmun quyastesqelluki ' .
Tawaten pikufsi yuget liisimakelleqiisi avaqutaqutsi Atagpesinun qilagmelngughmun . Yuuk tamaghhaan tawateghlluwaaq piiqaa . Siqineni piitestaqaa seghleghnunllu pinilghiinunllu . Tawateghpigaq eslallugughtestaqaa qaatkutkayugnunllu qaatkusigalngughnunllu .
Kiyaghneghem akileghtughlleqisii-i piniqistenginaghhasi piniqegkufsiki ? Talwa tax-meng qerngughtistet piniqaqiit piniqisteteng .
Enkaam ilakumtaghhiinasi quyakaataqufsiki , naten allangulleqetsi ilangitneng yuget ? Talwa maniguusigalnguut Kiyaghneghmun quyakaqiit ilakumtaateng !
Elpesi avaqutaqngutanganeng Atagpesi qilagmelnguum pinightek tawateghpigaq Atagpesi pinillghatun . "
Jesus-em apeghtuusani nagneghutkii , " Wataghllak pinitun pillesi esghaghsaqegpenaki . Esghaghsaqegkufsiki Atagpesi qilagmelnguum akileghtughnaanghitiisi .
" Enkaam tuunikuvek aklumalghiinun , piniiyugneghestun pigpenang . Qalghightaghtestikayuguut tuunivagilgameng esghiisqelluteng . Tawaten piiqut , synagogue-nillu tumenillu usuqesqelluteng . Ipa ungipaatamsi akileghtuusangwaaghluteng ayuqut .
Iwernga tuunikuvek aklumalghiinun , kina alngunak ungipaategpenaan ,
kitumun alngunak nallukesqelluku tuuniillghen . Atagpek esghapagaqaaten enkaam akileghtughlleqaaten . "
" Yughaneghpesini piniiyugneghestun pigpenasi . Yughaghyuneghtuut nekevghaghmeng synagogue-nillu tumenillu esghiisqelluteng yugnun . Ipa ungipaatamsi akileghtuusangwaaghluteng ayuqut .
Iwernga yughaghnaqneghpeni , iteghluten negpenun uumgulluten yughaghaqi Atagpenun aliinneghilgughmun . Atagpek liisimakaa aksaqluku sallghen enkaam akileghtughlleqaaten .
" Yughaneghpesini Kiyaghnepigmun maniguusigalngughestun pigpenasi . Yughaneghmeggni uteghpagtaghaqiit akuzitet sameng pisiinghilnguut . Sumeghmeggni akuzilleghllagmegteggun kiimsighlleqniluki yughalleteng piiqiit .
Ellngistun ayuqegpenasi qayughllak Atagpesi liisimakaa aklukegkaghsi , talwa aaptestegpenasi .
" Enkaam whaten yughaghaqitek , ' Whangkuta Atavut qilagmelnguq pamani , agleghnalghii aatghen quulvallengli .
Yughaghtukut Ataneghpagullghen tagisqelluku , piyukellghenllu apeghiighesqelluku nunami whani , katam qilagmelngughestun .
Neghyaghqaliteqeghtikut aghneghmi whani .
Seghevutaghtiki seghleghqelleput seghevusimaluki seghletun pisteput .
Nanghiiqullengestegpenaamta , iwernga yugulikut taagken Seghleghmeng . Ataneghpagulleq , aghtughyaghqaanghilleq , nighughqelleq , elpek pikaten quunperugllak . Amen . '
" Seghevuskufsiki seghletun pistesi , Atagpesi qilagmelnguum seghevulleqiisi .
Iwernga seghevunneghilkufsiki seghletun pistesi , Atagpesi seghevunnaanghitii seghleghqellesi .
" Fast-eneghpesini iilqesugnighqegpenasi piniiyugneghestun . Aghmigigatut , mesuunangigatut liigikesqelluteng fast-enguniluteng . Ipa ungipaatamsi , akileghtuusangwaaghluteng ayuqut .
Fast-eneghpeni aghmigaqillu mesuunaaqillu ,
ilagpenun nallukesqelluku fast-ellghen . Iwernga Atagpek aliinneghilnguum liisimakaa saaquten enkaam akileghtughlleqaaten .
" Nunami whani kagpagpenasi aklungimeng qayughllak kingugemllu anaghtaallghemllu naafqelleqii , teglegniightetlu naafqiiluteng teglegllequt .
Iwernga elpesineng katam qilagmi kagpagitek aklungimeng qayughllak moth-ngituq , anaghtaangituq naafqiiyaghqameng , tegleghniightengituqlu naafqiiluteng teglegughyaghqameng .
Sumeghtaghaatkumanginaghlleqaghsi aklungigpesinun kagpagvigsi .
" Iyek kenelghutastun ayuquk yugusimun . Iiskegtekuvek iingunaghmi yugusin nighugllagullequq ,
iwernga iyellugmeskuvek iingunaghmi yugusin mamlegllagullequq . Enkaam nighuk ilugpenilnguq mamlegukumi , elngaatall mamlepigtuq !
" Kitum alngunak qepghaannaanghitaak maalghuk umiilgek . Maalghugegneng umiilelgukumi ugumikelleqaa ataasiq , piniqelleqaa ilanga . Qaatkutngallequq ataasimun , pitkennaanghitaa ilanga . Enkaam piniqnaanghitaghsi Kiyaghneq piniqumaluku mani .
" Tamaaken apalluqluku ungipaatamsi , nulqaviighutkegpenaan ungvalleghsi , sameng neghelleghqaghsi , meghelleghqaghsi , nalighmeng sameng aatelleghqaghsi . Sumeghtaghaqaghtekqun , unguvalleq megnunaghataghaghtuq neqmeng , yugusiqlu megnunaghataghaghtuq aatkaneng .
Esghaqaghtekiqun qawaaget , piitesighiigatut , unatiigatut , kagpagingigatut . Naqamllu Atagpesi qilagmelnguum neghqaqii ! Elpesi megnunaghataghanghitsii qawaagneng ?
Nalighpesi nulqaviighutkelluku unguvalleni taakughlleqaguu ?
" Sangan nulqaviightaqetsi aasaghqameng ? Esghaqaghtekiqun piitesighaat piitellghit , qepghiigatut talwa aatkanglliigatut ellmeggneng .
Ungipaatamsi talwa Solomon aklungighllagmini aasigatuq piitesighaghestun pinightutkalghiimeng .
Kiyaghneghem aasightughaqii vegaaghet , iwernga aga unaami quukaqiit . Kiyaghneghem aasightuqayugukaki veghaaget , aasightughataghaghnaanghitisii elpesi ? Ugpeqilleghqestaapigutsi !
Tamaaken apalluqluku nulqaviightegpenasi whaten , ' Sameng neghnaqesta ? ' nalighmeng ' Sameng meghnaqesta ? ' nalighmeng ' Sameng aannaqesta ? '
Gentile-et tamaana nulqaviighutkaqaat . Atagpesi qilagmelnguum liisimakii qamaglluki aklukegkasi .
Tamaaken apalluqluku kiyaghtelleghpesini megnunalleghpigaaghtestekek Kiyaghneghem Ataneghpagullghallu , piyukellghallu . Tawaten pikufsi Kiyaghneghem tuunelleqii qamaglluki aklukegkasi .
Nulqaviighutkegpenaan unaamilleghqaq , qayughllak unaamim seghleliighi itagnaghyaghqaagut tawavek aghneghmun . Seghleliiq pikayuguuq aghhutanga tamaghhaan , ilaaghataghaghpenaan unaamim seghleliilleghqaaneng . "
Jesus-em apeghtuusani nagneghutkii , " Nanqigtigpenasi ilagpesineng enkaam Kiyaghneghem nanqiggneghillisi ,
qayughllak Kiyaghneghem nanqiglleqiisi tawatengngwaaq nanqigtilleghpesistun ilagpesineng . Atuqelleqiillu elpesinun ataasit tamaakut pikasi ilagpesinun .
Sangan esghaghsigu yulgutegpek iisqughutnga , elpek katam iisqughuten unaghsighllak avelghaghluku ?
Salghiimeng yulguten pizigu , ' Entaa-a iisqughutngiqaghlaken ' , elpek paninang iisqughutelguluten unaghsighllagmeng ?
Uyuq piniiyugneq ! Sivukluku unaghsighllak iyegpeneng nusugluku elngaatall whateghlluwaaq esghaghluku yulguten iisqughutngighnaken . "
Taagken Jesus-em pikii , " Legasiighwaghtenun apeghtuusaqegpenaki Kiyaghneghem Akuzitangi , qayughllak qikmistunllu kurugaghestunllu ayuqut . Sangwaat agleghnalghiit tuunegpenaki qikminun luuraq sughugnayukangisi . Akituqat sungaat miluutegpenaki kurugaghnun , luuraq tutmaasghaqnayukatki .
" Aaptek , allgeghullequsi ; ivaghitek , naalkullequsi ; tenglugtughtek amigkun , qelpeghulleqiisi .
Qayughllak kina alngunak aapleghhii , allgeghusaghqaaguq ; kina alngunak ivaghilghii , naalkusaghqaaguq , kina alngunak tenglugtulghii amigkun , qelpeghulleqaa .
Kitum yugem ighneni tungsiqan neqekrangllameng , tuunelleqaguu uyghagmeng ?
Nalighmeng tungsiqan iqallugmeng , tuunelleqaguu nemeghyameng ?
Seghleghughngaaghpesi , avaqutasi tuunyaghqaqasi pinilghiimeng tunusameng . Atazi qilagmelnguq tuuniyugataghaghluni ayuquq pinilghiimeng tunusameng tamaakunun aapleghhinun ellminun .
" Enkaam yulgutegpesinun pinitun pistesukufsi , elpesillu pinitun piiqiteki . Tawaten apeghtughinguut Moses-em Liilightuusiillu , uuknaliqistetlu igaqegkiit . "
Taagken Jesus-em pikii , " Iteghtek kagpestaaghhaghqun amigkun . Amik hell-mun ayuqelghii nuqutuuq , tuumkegtuqlu enkaam uglaq taakwagun igleghtaquq .
Iwernga amik unguvalleghmun ayuqelghii kagpestaaghhaaguq , tuumllugmetuqlu enkaam qafsinkuuraghhaam naalkaqii tumet unguvalleghmun ayuqelghiit .
" Kelengalusi uuknaliqistesighwaaghneng . Takulleqiisi penniighsugnighqelluteng , taawanginaq ugighsalghiistun amaastun ayuqut .
Liigikelleqasi nangaghneghitgun liigikelleghpesistun uqfiget sameng piitestillghitgun . Sikughlluget piitestingigatut grapes-meng nalighmeng figs-meng , tawateghpigaq seghleghet yuget pinitun pingigatut .
Uqfik pinilghii piitestiyaghqaaguq pinilghiimeng , taawanginaq uqfik seghleq piitestiyaghqaaguq seghleghmeng .
Uqfik pinilghii piitestinaanghituq seghleghmeng , uqfik seghleq piitestinaanghituq pinilghiimeng .
Enkaam alngunak uqfik piitestinghilnguq pinilghiimeng kepluni kumaghsaghqaaguq .
Enkaangam tawatetellghitgun liigikelleqasi uuknaliqistesighwaaghutangi . "
Jesus-em apeghtuusani nagneghutkii , " Ilangi yugem whangamnun maligsaaghtekniiqut enkaam piiqaatnga , ' Atanqamken ' iwernga iteghnaanghitut Ataneghpagullghanun Qilagem . Tamaakunginaat atuqilghiit piyukellghaneng Atama qilagmelnguum iteghyaghqaagut Ataneghpagullghanun Qilagem .
Nanqigtillghem Aghneghani , uglam piyaghqaqaanga whaten , ' Ataneq , Ataneq ! Ateghpegun Kiyaghneghem ungipaa aapqaqaghput . Ateghpegun aanesquqaqaput tughneghaat uglalghiineng yugneng . Ateghpegun allaaghlluwhaghtiighaataqaagukut uglaghngaan ! '
Iwernga whaten pilleqanka , ' Nallukngwaaghamsi , iqitek whangamneng , seghletun pisteni ' .
" Kina alngunak nagallghii apeghtughillemnun , qaatkegkumiki peghqinelghiitun yugtun ayuquq mangteghangllaqaq uyghagem qaayngakun .
Eslallugughteghllagyalghiimi , kiiwet ulevumaghmeng , anuqlighllagyalghiimillu , tawallima mangteghaq uullghumangilnguq qayughllak uyghagkun nekeftekaalghii .
" Iwernga kina alngunak nagateghngaaghmi apeghtughillemnun , qaatkenghilkumiki , nalluqatun yugtun ayuquq mangteghangllaqaq qenaaghllugkun .
Eslallugughteghllagyalghiimi , kiiwet ulevumaghmeng , anuqlighllagyalghiimillu , aga mangteghaq uulqaq naavngwaaghluni . "
Jesus tamaaken apeghtughineghmeng taaqsan , yulghuteghllaget saghiighayukat ,
qayughllak apeghtughikaq aghtughyaghqaanghillelighluni , apeghtughikayugestun Liilightuusameng pigpenani .
Jesus qemimeng ukigyan , yulghuteghllagem maligtekaa .
Taagken yuuk , leprosy-lek , tagiluni ellnganun , segesqughfikluku , pikaa , " Ataneq , piyukelqegkuvgu , ukmangiqaghnga . "
Enkaam Jesus-em tawavek saafluku pikaa , " Piyukelqaqa , ukmangiighten ! " Tawaninginaq leprosy-ngiitkaq .
Taagken Jesus-em pikaa , " Wataghllak kina alngunak ungipaategpenaan naallghutelleghpeneng , yeghlegi aglaa priest-mun esghaghligu naallghutellghen . Taagken aghqerraaghhaaten Moses-em Liilightuusaan pisqellghatun ipapighqesqelluku naallghutellghen . "
Taagken Jesus Capernaum-emun pikaq . Kaataquqlu , Rome-em umiilwaaghan takuluku kayusiitaghtesqelluni pikaa ,
" Ataneq , whangkunni qepghaghteka , uniighumaaq , ikfiqeghllaguuq . "
Jesus-em pikaa , " Naallghusaghtughnaqaqa . "
Iwernga umiilwaaghem pikaa , " Ataneq , itagnanghitunga elpenun iteghviksaghqaalunga mangteghamnun . Legan tawanlluten naallghutesqigu qepghaghteka enkaam naallghulli .
Qelghikayugmeng umiilelguunga enkaam whangallu qelghaqanka pilluwaghtenka . Ataasiq qelqumkun , ' Aghulaqi ' aga aghulaqellequq . Ilanga whaten pikumkun , ' Tagi ' tagillequq . Qepghaghteka qelqumkun , ' Una piightigu ' , aga pilleqaa . "
Jesus-em nagalluku saghiighayukaq , enkaam yuget maligullghiit ellminun pikii , " Ipa ungipaatamsi , nallaasigatunga kitumeng alngunak Israel-eghmiimeng , uutun yugtun ugpeqineghtutkalghiimeng .
Ungipaatamsi , asivaghmengllu pakfallamengllu yulghutet tagilaghaasaghqaagut Ataneghpagullghanun Qilagem . Tawani aqumuulluteng neghelgusighlleqiit sivuneput Abraham-enkut , Isaac-enkut , Jacob-enkut .
Iwernga tamaakut Ataneghpagulleghmesaghqaayalghiit aanesaghqaagut mamlegllagmun , tawani elngaatall qiyaaghwaghllagllequt gguteteng terqitaagtaamiita avuteghqem angtalanganeng . "
Taagken Jesus-em pikaa umiilwaaq , " Aglaghhaaten , ugpeqilleghpetun apeghiighllequq . " Enkaam tawaninginaq umiilwaaghem qepghaghtenga naallghutkaq .
Jesus Peter-enkunun piluni , esghaqaa aghnaq Peter-em sakinga qavaghvigmeteftuq puqleghaluni .
Saafsaqminigu iiggakun puqleghangiitkaq , aga makelluni kepsiiqukaa .
Ighivgaghyagu Jesus-mun tagiquutkiit tughneghalget ilumegteggun enkaam aanesquqii tughneghiit akuzilleghmikun , qamagllukillu qinuyuget naallghutkii .
Tawaten pikaq apeghiighnaluku uuknaliqistem Isaiah-m whaten pillgha , " Tugukaqii qinuyulleput , iqitkaqii aqnighneput . "
Jesus-em esghaghluki uvitminilnguut yulghuteghllaget , yataaghqesqegkii naayvam inglunganun aghvighnaluteng .
Taagken apeghtughikayugem Liilightuusameng takuluku pikaa , " Apeghtughista , maliglleqamken natmun alngunak pikuvek . "
Jesus-em pikaa , " Kaviighet riigtelguut , qawaaget unglutelguut , iwernga Ighnegha Yugem ingaghfigitaquq . "
Ilangan maligsaaghtengan pikaa , " Ataneq , maliglleqamken iwernga sivukluku ataka lliveghyaghtuqaghlakun . "
Iwernga Jesus-em pikaa , " Maligtinga . Tamaakut maligusunghilnguut whangamnun tuqukaagut taghneghamegteggun ; lliveghlitki tuqumasliiteng . "
Taagken Jesus angyamun uugsan maligsaaghtengillu uuglleghaatkat .
Puglellghita kiingungiighhaaneng esla nuuskagllagan naafteghllakaq , naayvaqlu imaghllugughteghllagumaghmi , repall angyaq imighaataqegkaa . Iwernga Jesus qavaalghii .
Maligsaaghtet takuluku taghtughtekaat whaten pimaan , " Ataneq , yugulikut ! Tuqulaghaannaqukut ! "
Jesus-em pikii , " Sangafsi alingetsi ? Ugpeqilleghqestaapiguusi ! " Taagken nekevluni ineghtekakek anuqallu imaghllugetlu enkaam amsanaghllugughtekaq .
Qamaglluteng saghiighayukat . Whaten pikat , " Natelnguuwa yuuk una ? Talwa anuqemllu imaghllugetlu qaatkegkangat ! "
Jesus-enkut kaasameng inglunganun naayvam , aglaqat Gadara-ghmiit nunangitnun . Taagken maalghuk yugek tughneghalgek ilumegnegun tagilutek lliveghneng nallaqaak Jesus . Suugllugllagek repall kina alngunak taakwagun tuumkun igleghsigalnguq .
Legan esghaghluku Jesus akilghuukak , " Sanaqsikut , Ighneghani Kiyaghneghem ? Ikfiqesnaqsikut pilleghqaq kaatestegpenaan ? "
Taawanguq qantaghani kurugalghutet , neghaqeftut .
Tughneghaat maniguutepiglluteng Jesus pikaat , " Aanestekufkut , kurugaghnun iteghaatesnakefkut . "
Enkaam Jesus-em pikii , " Aanleghaatek ! " Aanleghaalluteng kurugaghnun iteghaatkat . Aga kurugaat pangalgutkat asitmun naayvamun nagneghluteng meghmi tuqulaghaatkat .
Kurugaghneng aflengakilghiit qimaaguutkat nemun . Tawani aapqagket samatkek tughneghalguyalghiik ilumegnegun , samatangillu kurugalghutet .
Enkaam qamagtengngwaaghluteng tamaakumiit esghaghyaghtuutkaat Jesus . Esghaghyamegteggu maniguutepiglluteng aghulaqesqegkaat nunameggneng .
Taagken Jesus angyamun uuglluni inglunganun naayvam aghviqaq . Enkaam Capernaum-emun aglaqaq neminun .
Ilangita yuget ellnganun tagitkaat uniiqaq yuuk allighaakun . Jesus-em liigikluki ugpeqilleghtulngit , pikaa uniiqaq , " Ighnemni , quya ! Seghleghqelleghten seghevutut . "
Taagken ilangi apeghtughikayuget Liilightuusaneng sumeghtaghaqat , " Una yuuk seghleghqeghllagtuq . Kiyaghneghuyugtuq seghevutilleghmikun seghleghqelleghneng ! "
Jesus-em liisimakluki sumeghtaghallghit , pikii , " Sangan seghleghmeng sumeghtaghaghetsi ?
Naliq akuzilleq piyaqniita , ' Seghleghqelleghten seghevutut ' nalighmeng ' Makelluten piyugi ' ?
Liigikesnaqamsi Ighnegha Yugem seghevutilleghqalgutanga seghleghqelleghmeng nunami whani . " Enkaam uniiqaq yuuk pikaa , " Makelluten , allighan tuguluku , aglaa ! "
Yuuk makelluni aglaqaq .
Yulghutet esghapagluku tallughyukat , usuqegkaat Kiyaghneq tawatelngughmeng aghtughyaghqaanghilleliskangi yuget .
Taam kingunganeng Jesus-em igleghutkelluku esghaqaa tax-em qerngughtistenga , aqumluni qepghaghvigmini ; Matthew-nguftuq . Pikaa , " Maligtinga . " Enkaam Matthew-m nekevluni maligtekaa .
Mulugpenateng Jesus-enkut maligsaaghtekullghiit neghyaghtuqat Matthew-nkunun . Neghuusimaluki tax-meng qerngughtistelghutetlu , seghleghqestelghutetlu aqumluteng Jesus-enkut neghelgusiqiit .
Ilangita Pharisees-et esghaghluku neghelgusiighilghii , maligsaaghtengi aaptekiit , " Sangan apeghtughistegpesi neghelgusightaki tax-meng qerngughtistetlu , seghleghqestetlu ? "
Jesus-em nagalluki kiimsiqii , " Yugunqegtat aghallegtaghsughniitut , tamaakunginaat qinuyulghiit .
Liisaghtughteggu sameng pisiitanga una Akuzitnilnguq Igaqegkaq whaten pilghii , ' Piyukenghitanka aghqutesi , itupill nangllegtaghtesugamsi . ' Tagingunghitunga tagsighnaluki elqughutngalghiit , iwernga taginguunga tagsighnaluki seghleghqestet . "
Taagken John-em Paaptaayestem maligsaaghtengita takuluku Jesus aaptekaat , " Sangan whangkutallu Pharisees-etlu awen fast-aaqesta , naqam maligsaaghteten fast-egpenateng ? "
Jesus-em kiimsiqii , " Nulightughyaghqam tagsiqliqii qivghungayaghqaawaat tawanlluku nulightughnaqelghii ? Yeghlegillu ! Iwernga pilleghqaq kaasaghqaaguq nulightughnaqelghii ellngitneng iqitestekumegteggu , elngaatall tamaani aghneghni fast-ellequt . "
Taagken Jesus-em pikii , " Kitum alngunak ilaaghnaanghitaak aatkalugek nutaghameng liiqneghmeng . Ilaalleq qellughtekumi piigullequq , enkaam piilleq sullevellequq .
Talwa kitum alngunak wine-eghraghaghmeng imighnaanghitaa awataghpaluk qayughllak awataghpaluk imiqumi aafkaghluni imiighullequq . Enkaam awataghpaluk atuuyaghqaananighllequq . Iwernga awataghpagraghaq imiqumi wine-eghraghaghmeng qerngaagmek naavnaanghituk . "
Paninang Jesus akuzimaluku Jews-et igleghutistengat iteghluni segesqughlluni manungakun pikaa , " Panika whaa tuqun始ghhaaguq , iwernga takuluku saaftekuvgu unguvaghllequq . "
Enkaam Jesus-em nekevluni maligtekaa , maligsaaghtengillu maligutkat .
Aglaamaluki , qinuyulghiim aghnam takukaa Jesus tunutanganeng . Qula maalghuk siipneqluku ayumiqulleq kiitelqungigalnguq . Whaten sumeghtaghaqaq , " Saafteqeghsaqumkun aatkaakun , naallghunnayaghtunga . " Enkaam saaftekaa atkuyaaghan keniikun .
Jesus-em qiivutkelluku esghaghluku aghnaq pikaa , " Panimni alingegpenang ! Ugpeqilleghpegun naallghututen . " Aga aghnaq naallghutkaq .
Taagken Jesus-em kaalluni igleghutistenkunun , esghaqii tuqiilghiini qalghightaghtetlu , yulghutetlu qiyaaghuuteghllalghiit .
Tawavek pikii , " Aanleghaatek ! Aghnaghaghhaq tuqullghituq qavaaguq ! " Iwernga nenglaqegkaat .
Aanleghaatesatki , iteghluni Jesus-em tugukaa iiggakun , enkaam aghnaghaghhaq unguvaqaq .
Enkaam taana allaaghlluwhaghtilleq ungipaqegkaat tamangani .
Taagken Jesus aghulaqegkaq nemeng . Ayaakak yugek maligsaaqaak , akilghuumaagmek whaten , " Ighneghani David-em , nangllegyagutikung ! "
Aga mangteghamun iteghyan maligtekaak , enkaam Jesus-em aaptekakek , " Ugpeqestegneguu naallghutilleghqaqa ? " Kiimsiqaak , " Aa-a Ataneq ! "
Taagken Jesus-em iyegkenkun saaflukek pikakek , " Ugpeqilleghpetegetun apeghiighli . "
Enkaam esghaghyagutkak . Jesus-em ineghtengngwaaqakek , " Ungipaghpenatek kitumun alngunak . "
Iwernga navek pineghmegni aapghaqegkangak Jesus-em apeghiiqaa ellmegnun .
Taakuk yugek aghulaqumalukek , Jesus-mun tagitkaat yuuk akuzingigalnguq qayughllak ilumikun tughneghalek .
Legan Jesus-em tughneghaq aanestaa , yuuk aga akuzikaq . Enkaam yulghutet saghiighayugulluteng whaten pikat , " Whatelngughmeng allaaghlluwaghtilleghmeng esghaasigatukut Israel-mi ! "
Iwernga Pharisees-et pikat , " Umiilgita tughneghaat aghtughyaghqaanghillelisimaat aanesqiisqelluku tughneghaghneng . "
Taagken Jesus igleghtekaq tamaghhaani Galilee-mi , apeghtughimaghmi synagogue-ngitni , ungipaqimaghmillu Pinilghiineng Ungipaaneng Ataneghpagullghem . Naallghuquqii qamaglluki aqnighnelgetlu qinuyulghiitlu .
Esghaghluki yulghuteghllaget nangllegyagutkii , qayughllak seghleliighngaghllaget , kayutngunateng ; penniighestun penniighnightengilngughestun .
Taagken maligsaaghteni pikii , " Uglalghiim yugem ugpeqsugaqiit Pinilghiit Ungipat . Tamaakunguut usputngalghiit nunivagseghanun unataghyaqleggiinaaghtekat . Taawanginaq palapiguut qepghaghtet .
Enkaangam yughaghtek Atanghanun unataghyaghqat , kayagtisqelluku qepghaghtekaghqameng unataghyaghqaanun . "
Jesus-em qerngughlluki qula maalghuk siipneqluku maligsaaghteni , aghtughyaghqaanghillelitkii aanestiyaghqaaluki tughneghaghneng , naallghutiyaghqaaluki tamaghhaaneng aqnighneghnengllu , qinuyugnengllu .
Ukunguut qula maalghuk siipneqluku apostle-et : sivuliq , Simon ( alla atelek Peter-meng ) , Andrew ( anglegutanga ) , James-enkuk John-enkuk ( Zebedee-m ighneghqek ) ,
Philip-enkut , Bartholomew-nkut , Thomas-enkut , Matthew-nkut ( tax-meng qerngughtistenguyalghii ) , James-enkut ( ighnegha Alphaeus-em ) , Thaddaeus-enkut ,
Simon-enkut Zealot-a , Judas Iscariot-lu ( uveghpagutiyaghqaq Jesus-meng ) .
Jesus-em , taakut qula maalghuk siipneqluku apostle-et kayagtekii qelghuumiita , " Gentile-etlu , Samaria-ghmiitlu nunangitnun pifqaafsi .
Yeghlegi Israel-eghmiinun pitek qayughllak iflakastun penniighestun ayuqut .
Navek alngunak pineghpesini whaten ungipaghaqitek , ' Ataneghpagullgha Qilagem kaasaghtuumaaq ! '
Qinuyuget naallghuteki , tuqukat unguvaghteki , leprosy-lget naallghuteki , tughneghaatlu aanesqughteki yugneng . Akingunaan allgeghutkaagusi , enkaam akingunaan tuunitek .
Kelqegpenasi manimeng : gold-meng , silver-meng , talwa copper-meng .
Kelqegpenasi akmagtameng , simiitkaghqameng , kamegmeng talwa ayaviighmeng , qayughllak qepghaghta aklukegkaaneng tuunyaghqaaguq .
" Town-enun nalighmeng village-enun kaanneghpesini ivaghiiqitek kitumeng pinilghiimeng enkaam ellnganitaqitek kenlanga aghulaqsaghqaaghtelleghpesinun .
Iitqufsi mangteghaanun quyastaqiteki tawanlenguut whaten , ' Kiyaghneghem nekeggmellgha elpesinilli . '
Upughaskangisi , quyastilleghsi tawantesnakesi . Iwernga upughanneghilkangisi , quyastilleghsi veghhnakesi .
Kitum alngunak upughanneghilkangisi nalighmeng naganneghilkangisi , aanutkelluku mangteghameng nalighmeng aghulaqutkelluku town-meng , itegaghpesi pagulangi ufsugunnakesi .
Ipa ungipaatamsi , Nanqigtillghem Aghneghani , Sodom-eghmiitlu Gomorah-ghmiitlu aghyuulleghqestaaghhaayaghqaagut taam nem yuganeng ! "
" Ukughsi ! Kayagtekumsi penniighestun qungangitnilngughestun amaat lliighlequsi enkaam peghqinghulusi nemeghyastun , nekeggmellusi doves-tun .
Kelengalusi , qayughllak yuget tugulusi aglaalleqiisi agghistenun , kagsagmiglleqiisillu synagogue-meggni .
Whanga apalluqlunga , nekevesleqiisi sivungitgun igleghutistetlu umiilgetlu . Enkaam liigikesaghqaaghlleqaghpesinga ellngitnunllu Gentile-enunllu .
Nanqigtestemun aglaaskangisi , teggellghiighpenasi naten akuzilleghqaghpesineng , nalighmeng sameng pilleghqaghpesineng . Akuziyaghqaaghtekufsi akuzitkaghqalgullequsi .
Akuzitet elpesi pikenghitasi qayughllak Atagpesi Taghneghakek akuzillequk elpesigun .
" Yuget ellmeng katam angleguteteng tuqutesleqiit , atatlu avaqutateng tawaten piyaghqaqiit . Avaqutat anguyiilluki angayuqateng tuqutesleqiit .
Whangamneng apalluqlusi yugem qamaglluni ugumikelleqiisi . Iwernga nuqenneghtuqat kenlanga kenlemun yugulillengyaghqaagut .
Takukaghpesini amyuutkegkangisi , ilanganun town-em qimaggaasi . Ipa ungipaatamsi , qamaggnaanghitasi Israel-em town-ngi , sivungani Ighneghan Yugem tagilleghqaan .
" Maligsaaghta qaasghutinganghituq apeghtughistemineng , talwa qepghaghta qaasghutinganghituq umiilegmineng .
Itagnaghiyaghqaaguq maligsaaghta apeghtughistemitun lliiqumi , qepghaghtallu umiilegmitun lliiqumi . Naasquutilghii nengllugutmineng , Beelzebul-meng atiimakatgu , nengllugutangi seghleghataghaaluki atighyaghqaqiit .
" Enkaam alikegpenaki tamaakut amyuqetaghtet . Sangwaa alngunak nallukegkaq liitesaghqaaguq , qamagllunillu aksaqegkaq qayvighqesaghqaaguq .
Elpesinun sangwaat aapqanka apeghyaghqaqasi tamanganun . Sigutquutkegkanka elpesinun , ungipaqsaghqaqasi mangteghat qaayngitneng .
" Enkaam alikegpenaki yuget tuqutikayuget yugusighhiinaghmeng iwernga tuqutinaanghitut unguvasimeng . Itupill alikiteggu Kiyaghneq , qayughllak hell-mi naafqiiyaghqaaguq tamaghhaagkeneng yugusimengllu unguvasimengllu .
Penny-meng tukfighyaghqaqagsi qawaaggaak , naqamllu aallgha ifkaqan Atagpesi liisimakaa .
Iwernga elpesi aflengakataghaghlusi ayuqiisi , qayughllak talwa nuyaghpesi uglaghtalngi liisimakii .
Enkaam alingegpenasi , Atagpesi megnukataghaghiisi qawaaggaghneng !
" Kitum alngunak ungipaaskaki yuget , whangamnun pikniluni , whangallu Ataka qilagmelnguq ungipaalleqaqa whangamnun pikniluku .
Iwernga kitum alngunak ungipaaskaki yuget whangamnun pikenghinniluni whangallu Ataka qilagmelnguq ungipaalleqaqa whangamnun pikenghinniluku . "
Jesus-em paninang aleghquqii , " Sumeghtaghaghpenasi nekeggmellengestiyaghtuunilunga nunam yuganun . Yeghlegillu ! Nekeggmellengestiyaghtuunghitunga , taawanginaq pillugutestiyaghtuugunga .
Taginguunga yugmun anguyaliitesqelluku atanga , aghnamun anguyaliitesqelluku naanga , ukaaghanun anguyaliitesqelluku sakinga aghnaq .
Enkaam yuuk nengllugutangita anguyaliilleqaat .
" Kitum alngunak piniqegkumigu atani nalighmeng naani pakiggulluku whangamneng , whanga pikepagningitaqa . Kitum alngunak piniqegkumigu ighneni nalighmeng panini pakiggulluku whangamneng , whanga pikepagningitaqa .
Kitum alngunak qaquurani tuguyunghilkumigu maliggnaanghitaanga , enkaam whangamni itagnanghituq .
Kitum alngunak unguvalleni ellminun piknikumigu iflayaghqaqaa . Iwernga kitum alngunak unguvalleni pegtekumigu whanga apalluqlunga allgeghsaghqaqaa unguvallepik .
" Kitum alngunak upughaskangisi , whangallu upughalleqaanga , enkaam kitum alngunak upughaskuminga , upughalleqaa kayagtisteka .
Kitum alngunak upughaskumigu uuknaliqista uuknaliqistengutanganeng , akileghtuusangellequq uuknaliqistetun . Kitum alngunak upughaskumigu elqughutngalghii yuuk elqughutngatanganeng , akileghtuusangellequq elqughutngalghiitun yugtun .
Kitum alngunak nenglekeglleghhiimeng meghsikumigu ukalighpigaq maligsaaghteka apalluqluku maligsaaghtekutemneng , ipa piimsi akileghtuusangepestaaghyaghqaaguq . "
Jesus-em qula maalghuk siipneqluku maligsaaghteni apeghiighyamiki apeghtughaneghmeng , tamaaken aghulaqegkaq ilangitnun town-et apeghtughinalunillu ungipaqinalunillu .
Anusimingllaghvigmelluni John-em Paaptaayestem nagaqughluku Christ-a saaqutanga , ilangi maligsaaghteni kayagtekii Jesus-mun .
Aaptekaat Jesus , " Elpengwaa taginaqnikaat , nalighmeng kina tagiyaghqaawaa ? "
Jesus-em kiimsiqii , " Ungipaasaghtughteggu John nagatkaghpesinengllu esghaqaghpesinengllu :
ayakaayalghiit esghaghyagutut , piyugigasalghiit piyugyagutut , leprosy-lguyalghiit naallghutut , tuuslaghyalghiit nagaquusagutut , tuqukaayalghiit unguvaghtut , aklumalghiinunllu Pinilghiit Ungipat ungipaqut .
Kina alngunak ugpeqinaninghilkumi whangamneng quyastekaaguq ! "
Aga John-em maligsaaghtengi aghulaqsata , Jesus-em akuzitkegkaa John yulghutnun , " Kilgaanun piiqngafsi , sangwaa esghaghyaghtughesteggu ? Vegaaq anuqem ufsuguskangaa ?
Saqutsimi ? Esghaghnalukuu aatkaqegtaq yuuk ? Tamaaken aatkaqelghiit kiyaghtaqut umiilget mangteghiitni !
Sangwaami esghaghyaghtughesteggu ? Uuknaliqistaa ? Aa-a , ungipaatamsi , esghaqaghsi John uuknaliqistenginaanghituq . Megnunaghataghaghtuq
qayughllak ellnganguuq Akuzitet Igaqegkat aapqaat whaten , ' Kiyaghneq piiq , Sivugpeni kayaglleqaqa ungipaghteka , yataaghqesaghtiisqelluku tuumkaghqan ' .
Ipa ungipaatamsi , John Paaptaayesta megnunalleghpigaaguq yugneng allgeqaghyaggaghneng . Iwernga kina alngunak ukalighpigaq Ataneghpagullghani Qilagem John-meng megnunaghataghaghtuq .
John Paaptaayesta ungipaqiyuggaallghaneng whavemun kenlanga , suuglluget wayaghnaqutkaqaat Ataneghpagullgha Qilagem .
Qamaglluteng uuknaliqistetlu Moses-emllu Liilightuusiita uuknaliqutkengngwaat Ataneghpagullgha Qilagem kenlanga John-em tagillghanun .
John-nguuq uuknaliqistet uuknaliqutkegkaat taginaqnilleghmeggteggun Elijah . Ugpeqsukufsigu uuknaliqelleq , John Elijah-nguuq .
Sigutelguusi , nagatek !
" Maaten kiyaghlleghhit yuget samun uspunnaqsingi ? Taghnughhaaghestun ayuqut aqumuulluteng akilpegaghvigni , naghaalgutmeggnun akilghuullghiit whaten ,
' Qalghightaatamsi , tukaleganghitusi ! Qiyiqutukut , qiyiqenghitusi ! '
" John tagiiqngami fast-aaquq , meghigatuqlu wine-meng , enkaam yuget whaten pikaagut , ' Tughneghalguuq ' .
Ighnegha Yugem tagiiqngami , neghelgusighaqii , meghelgusighaqiillu yuget , enkaam yuget whaten pikaagut , ' Yuukqun taana esghaqaghteggu ! Neghetupigtuq , meghetupigtuq , ilakumtaaqaatlu tax-em qerngughtistengita , seghleghqestetlu ! ' Naqamllu Kiyaghneghem peghqinellgha ipapighqengngaaq sallghakun . "
Jesus-em allulluki allaaghlluwhaghtilleni atuqegkaqii Chorazin-mi , Bethsaida-mi , Capernaum-emillu . Iwernga yugit avuteghqelluteng taaqellghilnguut seghleghqenneghmeng enkaam Jesus-em aghyuughmikii .
Pikii , " Seghleghwaaghunaqnguusi , Chorazin-eghmiini ! Seghleghwaaghunaqnguusi , Bethsaida-ghmiini ! Elpesini allaaghlluwaghtilleghllaget apeghiiqat pikaayaqata Tyre-millu Sidon-millu , neghipiglluteng yugit avuteghqelluteng seghleghqennanighnayaghtut . Tamaaken apalluqluku suvinalghiimeng qiipaghaghqameng aalluteng aqumnayaghtut panetelleghteggun .
Ipa ungipaatamsi , Nanqigtillghem Aghneghani Tyre-eghmiitlu Sidon-eghmiitlu aghyulleghqestaaghhaayaghqaagut elpesineng !
Enkaam elpesi , Capernaum-eghmiini ! Qaywa anglisteghllagyaghngaaghpesi elpesineng katam repall sumeghpesini usuqellengelleqnillusi qilagmi , yeghlegi ukiglleqiisi hell-mun . Allaaghlluwhaghtilleghllaget pikaayaqata Sodom-emi , paninang aghneghmi whani nekevghanayaghtuq !
Iwernga ungipaatamsi Nanqigtillghem Aghneghani Kiyaghneghem nangllekataghaghyaghqaqii Sodom-eghmiit pakiggulluki elpesineng ! "
Taagken Jesus pikaq , " Kaay Ata , Atanqaaten qilagemllu nunamllu ! Iyamsiqayugvikamken qayughllak liitkaanghilngughnun liitestekaqan ipapighqelleq iiqan liitkanengllu peghqineghnengllu .
Aa-a , Ataay , efquqelleghpetun pikaaguten .
" Atama tagivaqaqaa sangwaa qamagtengngwaaghluku . Kitum alngunak nallukaa Ighneq , iwerngaqun Atam . Kitum alngunak nallukaa Ata , iwerngaqun Ighneghem , enkaam Ighneghem nakmikegkaminun liitesleqaa Ata .
" Tagitek whangamnun qamagllusi ughleghilghiini , uqigtuqamengllu akmalegllagni , meghnaalisleqamsi .
Iisqaghmiitagka aallukek liitivikitengnga , qayughllak yakumanginneghitunga , iluka qusevegngaaq . Enkaam meghnaalillequsi unguvasighpesinun .
Iisqaghmiitagka piyaqniituk , akmakallu uqengestaaghhaaguq . "
Taagken Sabbath-em aghneghani Jesus igleghtekaq wheat-em piitfigakun . Maligsaaghtengi iyataqat enkaam wheat-meng qesugutaqluteng neghegkat .
Pharisees-et esghaghluki maligsaaghtet wheat-meng qesugutaatalghiit , Jesus pikaat , " Ii-i , Sabbath-mi maligsaaghteten qepghaghtut , Liilightuusaq naafqaat ! "
Jesus-em pikii , " Atightuumangistegguu David-enkut yukullghiit sakaatangi iyataghaqngameng ?
Iitqaaguq tabernacle-mun enkaam yukullghiit neghegkaqaat neqekrangllaq Kiyaghneghmun tuunegkaq . Tawaten pilleghmegteggun Liilightuusaq naafqegkaqaat qayughllak priest-nginaat neghyaghqaqsaqangat .
Atightiigasteggullu Liilightuusanilnguq priest-et Temple-mi qepghaneghmeggni Sabbath-mi naafqaqegkangat Sabbath-em Liilightuusaa ? Naqamllu priest-et anaggusigatut .
Ungipaatamsi , whaantuq Temple-mi kina aangataghalghii .
Akuzitni Igaqegkani Kiyaghneq pikaaguq , ' Nangllegtiisqesugamsi yulgutegpesinun pakiggulluku aghqutegpesineng . ' Taakut akuzitet liigikngwaaghyaqufsiki sameng pitangi , nanqiggnayanghitasi aghyuughyaghqaaluki anaggutellghilnguut ,
qayughllak Ighnegha Yugem , Atanqaa Sabbath-em . "
Taaken Jesus aglaghluni synagogue-ngitnun iitqaq .
Taawanguq yuuk iiggan inglungi uniiqat . Ilangita yuget tawanlenguut aaptekaat Jesus naalkefiknaluku anaggutelleghmeng , " Liilightuusamnni itagnaghtaa-a naallghutilleghqaq Sabbath-mi ? "
Jesus-em kiimsiqii , " Nalighpesi penniigha kalefkagsaqan laawaaghmun Sabbath-mi , nusugnayaghestegguu ?
Yuuk megnunaghataghaghtuq penniighmeng ! Enkaam Liilightuusani itagnalghiinguuq pinitun pilleghqaq Sabbath-mi . "
Taagken yuuk uniighngalghiimeng iiggelek pikaa , " Nengugutiki iiggeten . " Iiggeni nengugutkii , aga naallghutkat , inglumegestun lliiqat .
Taagken Pharisees-et aanluteng agghisaghtuqat naten tuqunnaluku Jesus .
Jesus-em liisimakluku agghillghat , aghulaqegkaq . Yulghuteghllaget maliglleghaatkaat , enkaam naallghuquqii qinuyulghiit qamaglluki ,
ineghtekiillu ungipaqefqaami pisqelluni .
Tawaten pilleghmikun apeghiiqaa Kiyaghneghem pillgha uuknaliqistekun Isaiah-kun whaten :
" Una esgha nakmikegkaqa qepghaghtenguluku . Piniqegkaqa unguvasigma efquqepigtaa . Taghneghagka ellngakun nekeglleqagka . Ungipaalleqii Gentile-et tawateghlluwaaq nanqigtilleghqamneng tamaghhaanun yugnun .
Aaghtiiraaghnaanghituq nalighmeng akilghuunaanghituq , tumeni iglagtupiglluni akuzinaanghituq .
Iiknaanghitaa vegaaq ulleghngalghii , qaamyaghtuungestaqak kenelghutak qaamnnaanghitaak . Tawaten piyaghqaaguq kenlanga qamaglluni yuuk whaten piyugluni lliiqan , Kiyaghneghem nanqigtellgha yugneng avutangituq .
Enkaam Kiyaghneghem nakmikegkaakun Gentile-et sighimallequt . "
Taagken Jesus-mun tagitkaat yuuk ayaakaq , akuzingigalnguq qayughllak ilumikun tughneghalek . Jesus-em naallghutkaa enkaam akuziyagutkaqlu esghaasagutkaqlu .
Yulghuteghllaget saghiighayugllakat repall ellmeggneng aapqughaaghutkat whaten , " Una David-em Ighneqenghitaguu ? "
Pharisees-et nagalluteng pikat , " Yugneng aanestaqii tughneghaat qayughllak atuqngukanga aghtughyaghqaanghillgha Beelzebul-em , igleghutistengat Tughneghaat . "
Jesus-em liisimakegkangi sumeghtaghallghit enkaam pikii , " Alngunak ataneghpagulleq aafquulluni pilluguskumi , naavellequq . Tanemlleqa neghllaget nalighmeng nengllugutet aafquulluteng pilluguskumeng , qerngaghmennaanghitut .
Tawateghpigaq Tughneghaam aanestekumigu Tughneghaq , taawa ellmineng pilluwaaguq enkaam ataneghpagullgha kenletghuullequq .
Aanesquungukuma tughneghaghneng Beelzebul-kun , natenmi yugpesi aanesqughaqatki tughneghaat ? Enkaam yusi nanqigtistekelleqasi .
Iwernga Kiyaghneghem Taghneghagkenka aghtughyaghqaanghillghakun aanesquungukuma tughneghaghneng , taawa taam ipapighqaa Ataneghpagullgha Kiyaghneghem kaasimaaq elpesinun .
" Kina alngunak iteghyukumi iknaqelghiim yugem mangteghaanun teglegughnaluni saghyanganeng , sivukluku yuuk asighqesaghqaqaa . Taagken wayaghteghlleqii saghyangi .
" Kina alngunak whangamninneghilnguq kipullginaaghtekaqa ; kitum alngunak qerngughtilgusinghilkuminga mingitistenguuq .
Tamaaken apalluqluku ungipaatamsi yuget seghevutellengyaghqaagut alngunak seghleghqelleghmeggneng , alngunaklu seghlequulleghmeggneng . Iwernga kitum alngunak seghlequuqumikek Agleghnalghiik Taghneghak , seghevutellengnaanghituq .
Kitum alngunak kipullegmun sameng pikumigu Ighnegha Yugem , seghevutellengyaghqaaguq . Iwernga kitum alngunak kipullegmun sameng pikumikek Agleghnalghiik Taghneghak , seghevutellengnaanghituq maaten kiyaghtaalleghmi , nalighmeng tuunglighhaani .
" Uqfik aflengakegkaq pinilghiinguuq , piitestekii pinightut . Uqfik aflengakellghilnguq seghleghuuq , piitestekii seghleghuut . Piitestillghakun liisimakelleqaghsi uqfigem natetulanga .
Ukughsi nemeghyani ! Naten akuziiqetsi pinilghiimeng seghleghughngaaghpesi ? Sangwaa alngunak yugem ilunganilnguq aanegkaayuguuq akuzillghakun .
Pinilghii yuuk pinilghiimeng ilumikilghii pinilghiimeng aanestikayuguuq . Seghleq yuuk seghleghmeng ilumikilghii seghleghmeng aanestikayuguuq .
" Ungipaatamsi , Nanqigtillghem Aghneghani yuget apeghyaghqapestaaqiit Kiyaghneghmun qamaglluki seghleghet akuzitet atuqegkateng sangita atuqumatangi .
Qayughllak Kiyaghneghem nanqiglleqaaten akuzitegpegun . Akuzitegpek ipapighqelleqaaten avutnginniluten nalighmeng nanqiglleqaaten aghyuughyaghqaaluten . "
Taagken ilangita apeghtughistengita Liilightuusam , ilangitallu Pharisees-et pikaat Jesus , " Apeghtughista , allaaghlluwhaghtilghiiten esghapagyuwamken liigiknaluku aghtughyaghqaanghillghen Kiyaghneghmeng pingutanga . "
Iwernga Jesus-em pikii , " Aghneghem uum yugi seghleghqumanguut , ataasiighneghilnguut Kiyaghneghmun . Naqam allaaghlluwhaghtitesqut whangamnun . Yeghlegillu ! Taananginaghhaq allaaghlluwhaghtilleq esghaghlleqaghsi Kiyaghneghem allaaghlluwhaaghtillgha Jonah-mun .
Jonah iqallugrugllagem aqsaqghwanitkaaguq pingayut aghneghet , pingayut unuget . Tawateghpigaq Ighnegha Yugem samansaghqaaguq nunami pingayut aghneghet , pingayut unuget .
Nanqigtillghem Aghneghani Kiyaghneghem nanqigtekangisi elpesi kiyaghlleghhiini aghneghmi whani , Nineveh-ghmiit nekevluteng anaggunnilleqiisi aghyuughyaghqapestaaghunilusi . Uuknaliqista Jonah ungipaghyan Nineveh-ghmiit avuteghqelluteng seghleghqennaniqaagut . Iwernga elpesi avuteghqellusi seghleghqennanillghitusi qaywa nagatkaqeghngaaghpesigu kina aangataghalghii Jonah-meng .
Nanqigtillghem Aghneghani Kiyaghneghem nanqigtekangisi elpesi kiyaghlleghhiini aghneghmi whani , Queen-ngan Sheba-m nekevluni nanqigsaghqaanilleqiisi . Tagikaaguq uyavaghpanilngughmeng nemineng nagannaluku Solomon-em peghqineghllak apeghtughillgha . Iwernga kina aangataghalghii Solomon-meng whaantuq , tawalliima ighsakaqaghsi . "
" Tughneghaq yugmeng aanegkumi igleghllequq meqraggiilngughmi nunami , ivaghillequq meghnaalivigkameng . Iwernga naalkunneghisami ,
pikaq , ' Kiyaghfiksaqemnun uteghhnaqunga . ' Kaasalghiimi paaghqiteftuq , aallwaaghluni , mingllegtengngwaaghluni ayuqeftuq .
Taagken aanluni tagitkii maaghraghvinlek tughneghaat ellmineng seghleghataghalghiit . Iteghaalluteng yugmun tawantekat . Enkaam taana yuuk sivunghaneng wataqaaghaq seghleghwaaghughtekaq . Tawateghpigaq ayuqsaghqaagut seghleghet yuget kiyaghlleghhiit maaten , wataqaaghaq seghleghughtaghaghyaghqaagut sivunghani pilleghmeggneng . "
Paninang Jesus-em aleghquumaluki yuget , Jesus-em naangallu anglegutangillu kaalluteng manughami aleghqughyukaat .
Enkaam kitum ungipaatkaa , " Ii-i , qakma naanllu anglegutetenllu , aleghqughyugaqaaten . "
Jesus-em aaptekaa , " Kinangaawa naaka ? Kinkungaawat anglegutenka ? "
Taagken kenighluki maligsaaghteni , pikaq , " Taakusta naakallu anglegutenkallu !
Kina alngunak Atama qilagmelnguum piyukellghatun pikumi , anglegutkaqa , nayakaqa , naakaqallu ! "
Tawani ataasimi aghneghmi Jesus aanluni mangteghameng , naayvam esnengakun aqumluni apeghtughikaq .
Yulghuteghllaget kanglluqaghsatni , angyamun uuglluni aqumegkaq , enkaam yulghuteghllaget esnemetkat .
Ungipaghaatetgun allaaghhiinaghmeng apeghtuqii . Pikii , " Piitesighaghta piitesighaghvigminun aglaghluni , ifkaghquqaq piitutneng .
Piitesighaghvigmini ifkaghqiyalghiimi piitutneng , ilangi tumetgun tekitkat , enkaam qawaaget tagiluteng neghuqiit .
Ilangi piitutet tekitkat uyghagaghtuqakun sunapagilngughqun . Tawaninginaq piitkat qayughllak sunanga ugmestaaghhaq .
Iwernga siqineq piisalghiimi maatneghan paneghtekii qayughllak akupagilnguut .
Ilangi piitutem tekitkat sikughllugtuqakun , sikughlluget piisalghiimeng piitfigiqiit piitutet .
Iwernga ilangi piitutet tekitkat sunakegtakun piitestikat grain-meng , ilangi 100 , ilangi 60 , ilangi 30 .
Sigutelguusi , nagatek ! "
Taagken maligsaaghtengita takuluku Jesus aaptekaat , " Sangan ungipaghaatmeng atuqaqsin apeghtuneghpeki yuget ? "
Jesus-em kiimsiqii , " Elpesinun Kiyaghneghem liitestekaqaa talughngalghii ipapighqellgha Ataneghpagullghan Qilagem , iwernga ellngitnun liitesimangitaa .
Enkaam yuuk liigikellengegkaq , wataqaaghaq liigikellengataghaghyaghqaaguq , iwernga yuuk liigikellepagilnguq liigikellgha iqillequq .
Tamaaken apalluqluku apeghtughaqanka ungipaghaatetgun , qayughllak esghaateghngaaghmeng esghaasigalnguut , nagateghngaaghmeng nagaqiigalnguut , talwa liigikigalnguut .
Enkaam ellngitgun Isaiah-m uuknaliqutkillgha apeghiightuq . Taaggun uuknaliqellghakun Kiyaghneq pikaaguq , ' Ellngit nagatepestaaghllequt taawanginaq liigiknaanghitiit ; esghaatepestaaghllequt , taawanginaq liigiknaanghitiit esghaqateng ,
qayughllak ellngita umyugiit pineghllugtekaagut . Sigutngit tusaqneghlluugtekaagut , iyetengllu quneghtekaqiit . Tawatelnguunghisaqumeng iiymeggneng esghaannayaghtut , sigutmeggneng nagaquunnayaghtut , umyugamegteggun liigiknayaghtut , enkaam qiivnayaghtut whangamnun naallghutesqelluteng . '
" Iwernga quyanaghhalek elpesi ! Iyesi esghaataqut , sigutesillu nagaquutaqut .
Ipa ungipaatamsi , uuknaliqistelghutetlu , yulghutanganllu Kiyaghneghem , esghaghyukaqsaghiit esghaqasi , iwernga esghaamangitiit . Nagaqughyukaqsaghiitlu nagaquqasi , iwernga nagaquumangitiit .
" Nagateggu sameng piiqutanga ungipaghaatkegkaqa piitesighaghta .
Piitutet tumet saaghwitgun tekitkat usputngaat kitumun alngunak nagaquullghiimun ungipameng Ataneghpagulleghmeng ayuqelghiimeng . Liigikenghilkagu ungipaq Tughneghaam tagiluni wayaghlleqaa tekitkaayalghii ilungakun .
Tamaakut piitutet uyghagtuqakun sunakun tekitkat usputngaat kitumun alngunak nagaquullghiimun ungipameng , tawaninginaq ungipaq tugukliqaa quyakusiqluku .
Iwernga ungipaq ilungani mulumangilnguq qayughllak akungellghilnguq . Enkaam seghleliighyalghiimi nalighmeng amyuqetaatkellengyalghiimi , apalluqluku ungipaq tawaninginaq ugpeqinanightuq .
Tamaakut piitutet sikughllugtuqakun sunakun tekitkat usputngaat kitumun alngunak nagaquullghiimun ungipameng , taawanginaq teggellghiillghan kiyaghtaaghusighqameng , aklungighiyulleghllaganllu piitfigighaqaa ungipaq . Tamaaken apalluqluku piitestingigatuq .
Tamaakut piitutet tekitkat sunakegtakun usputngaat yugnun nagaquullghiinunllu liigikilghiinunllu ungipameng . Enkaam piitesqughaqut ilangi 100 , ilangi 60 , ilangi 30 . "
Taagken Jesus-em aapqaa ilanga ungipaghaan ellngitnun , pikii , " Ataneghpagullgha Qilagem yugtun piitesighaqatun pinilghiimeng piitutmeng piitesighaghvigmini ayuquq .
Unugmi ataasimi qavasimaluki , anguyaga tagiluni piitesighaqaq weeds-meng akulngitgun wheat-et , taagken aghulaqegkaq .
Nunivagseghat piisalghiimeng , wheat-et akumluteng weeds-meng ayuqeftut .
Piitesighaghta qepghaghtelghutngan takuluku aaptekaat , ' Ataneq , pinilghiimengmi piitutmeng piitesiighaghsin piitesighaghvigpeni ; naken weeds-et piit ? '
Yugem kiimsiiqii , ' Anguyagem tawaten pikaqii ' . Aaptekaat , ' Weeds-et ikuultekii ? '
Kiimsiqii , ' Nakaa , qayughllak weeds-et ikuqufsiki qemall wheat-etlu ilalkiilleqasi .
Qerngiita wheat-etlu weeds-etlu nagusteki kenlanga unatalleghqamun . Enan unataghyaghqaaghtekata unataghtet ungipaannaaghanka weeds-et sivukesqelluki , qepughluki paneghsaghqaaluki . Enkaam wheat-et unataghtesluki kagpagtesnaaghanka kagpagvimnun . ' "
Allameng Jesus-em aapqaa ungipaghaan , " Ataneghpagullgha Qilagem piitutngatun mustard-em ayuquq . Piitutem mekestaalleghpigaqaa , iwernga yugem piitesighaneghminigu piitesighaghvigmikun nunivagseghaghyaggaghneng aangelleghpigaakayuguuq . Uqfigughhneghani qawaaget tagiluteng avayaakun unglusiiqut . "
Allameng Jesus-em aapqaa ungipaghaan , " Ataneghpagullgha Qilagem yeast-atun ayuquq . Aghnam tuguluku akuutuskanga avlawaghllagmun , enkaam akuutaghllaga ghhuughtesteghllakaa . "
Jesus-em apeghtuneghminiki yulghuteghllaget quunpeng atuqaqii ungipaghaatet . Ipapestaaq sangwaa qamaglluku apeghtuusaqegkaa ungipaghaatetgun ayuquq .
Tawaten pikaalghii apeghiighnaluku uuknaliqistem pillgha , " Ungipaghaatet atuqelleqanka aleghququmki . Ungipaalleqanka Kiyaghneghem liitesimangilkanganeng ima ulimayuggaallghaneng nuna . "
Taagken Jesus-em unilluki yulghutet iitqaq mangteghamun . Maligsaaghtengita takuluku aaptekaat , " Sameng pisiigwat ungipaghaatkegkaghten weeds-et piitesighaghvigmelnguut ? "
Jesus-em kiimsiqii , " Yuuk piitesighaqaq pinilghiimeng piitutmeng , Ighneqaa Yugem ;
piitesighaghvik nunanguuq ; pinilghiit piitutet yuguut Ataneghpagullghem pikii ; weeds-et yuguut Tughneghaam pikii .
Anguyak piitestikaq weeds-meng Tughneghaaguq . Unatalleq nunam kenletghuutelqaa , unataghtet yaqulguut .
Unatalleghmi weeds-et qerngughlluki paneghtaqiit . Tawateghpigaq kenletghuutellghani nunam , yuget Tughneghaam pingi qerngughlluki paneghsaghqaagut .
Ighnegha Yugem yaqulegmineng kayagtiyaghqaaguq iqitesqelluki Ataneghpagulleghmineng qamaglluki seghleghqusitlu , seghletunllu pistet .
Enkaam kenghegnun miluulleqiit , tawani qiyaaghwaghllagllequt , gguteteng terqitaagtaamiita .
Taagken Kiyaghneghem yugi kuukgullequt siqineghtun Ataneghpagullghani Atameng . Sigutelguusi , nagatek ! "
" Ataneghpagullgha Qilagem aklungistun ayuquq iighngalghii piitesighaghvigmi . Yugem naalkelluki iinqigtekii . Quyam angtalanganeng , aghulaqluni qamaglluki saghyani akikluki , taagken taana piitesighaghvik tukfiqaa . "
" Whatetuqlu Ataneghpagullgha Qilagem : tukfightughta ivaghilghii piniipiglleghhiimeng pearl-meng tukfighyaghqameng .
Naalkunneghmini piniipiglleghhiimeng akituqameng , akikughaqaa qamaglluku saghyani , tukfighnaluku taana pearl-a . "
" Ataneghpagullgha Qilagem , negaghpagtunllu ayuquq . Iqalliniightet negaghpagteng naayvamun ateghlluku aghqellaaqut enkaam allaaghhiinaghmeng iqallugteghllagaqut .
Negaghpak sayugluku quutmun , aqumluteng iqalluget avughaqiit , pinilghit kanaghsimiita qaltanun , enkaam seghlellghi egtaqiit .
Tawatesaghqaaguq kenletghuutellghani nunam . Yaqulget tagiluteng avughlleqiit seghleghet yuget pinilghiineng .
Enkaam seghleghet kenghegnun miluulleqiit , tawani qiyaaghwaghllagllequt , gguteteng terqitaagtaamiita . "
Taagken Jesus-em aaptekii maligsaaghteni , " Qamaglluki tamaakut liigikestekii ? " Kiimsiqaat , " Aa-a . "
Taagken pikii , " Tamaghhaghmi apeghtughikayuk Liilightuusaneng apeghtuqaq Ataneghpagullghaneng Qilagem whatelnguuguq : mangteghalek yuuk nusugralghii kagpagvigmineng nutaghamengllu neghightamengllu . "
Jesus taaqsami apeghtughineghmeng ungipaghaatneng aghulaqegkaq .
Aglaghluni neminun apeghtughiyan synagogue-ngitni , yuget saghiighayagutkaat . Ellmeggneng aapqughaaghutkat , " Naken peghqinellenga ? Nakenllu aghtughyaghqaanghillenga allaaghlluwhaghtimun ?
Ighneqenghitaguu kaapentam ? Mary naakenghitaguu , uuk anglegutkenghitakii James-enkut , Joseph-enkut , Simon-enkut , Judas-enkut ?
Nayagillu maanneghitaat ? Naken liitellengeghllagtallu aghtughyaghqaanghillengallu ? "
Enkaam tuguklighyunghitkaat . Jesus-em pikii , " Nani alngunak yuget siivakaqaat uuknaliqista iwerngaqun ellngan katam nunanganillu nengllugutanganillu . "
Tamaani allaaghlluwhaghtipagumangilnguq qayughllak ugpeqenghilkangat .
Tamaani pilleghmi Herod-em , igleghutistengan Galilee-m , nagaquqaa Jesus-em apeghseghuumallgha .
Herod-em qepghaghteni pikii , " Ipa una John-nguuq Paaptaayesta , unguvaamaaq . Esghaghhuqun aghtughyaghqaanghillelek allaaghlluwhaghtilleghmun . "
Qavnganghhaq Herod-em tuqutestekaqegkanga John Paaptaayesta , qayughllak John-em ungipaatkaqegkanga , " Qaatkunneghituten Liilightuusamnnun tugulleghpegun Herodias , anglegutegpek nulighha . " ( Herodias-em ugiksaqanga Philip , Herod-em uyughaa . ) John-em ungipaatellgha apalluqluku Herod-em tugusqegkaa John , asighqelluku anusimingllaghvigmun kanaghtesqelluku . Herod-em tuqutesuguyaqanga John , naqam alikegkii Jews-et seghleliighqiinayukata qayughllak ugpeqeqkangat John uuknaliqestenguniluku .
Taagken Herod-em allgeghvigan aghneghani , Herodias-em paniga tukalegaqaq Herod-emllu aqelqatlu sivungitni . Elngaatall Herod efqughyugllakaq ,
repall akeqegkaa , " Ipapestaaq sameng alngunak tungsiquvek tuunelleqamken . "
Naami kayagtellghatun pikaa , " Whaa maaten tagivaghhu qayuutaghraagkun lliluku naasqwa John-em Paaptaayestem . "
Umiilek qivghukaq iwernga akeqikaatmineng aqelqami sivungitni piyukellgha kayagutkaa .
Enkaam Herod-em anusimingllaghvigmi John-em naasqwa kepestekaa .
Naasquq qayuutaghraagkun lliluku tuunegkaat aghnaghaghmun , enkaam naaminun aglaatkaa .
John-em maligsaaghtengi tagiluteng yugusii lliveghyaghtuqaat . Taagken Jesus ungipaasaghtuqaat .
Jesus-em nagaqughyamigu ungipaq , angyamun uuglluni aghulaqegkaq paaghqillghanun ellnginaghhaanaluni . Iwernga yulghutet nagaqughyamegteggu nemeggneng maligtekaat piyugmeng .
Jesus quutmun uuglluni esghaghluki yulghuteghllaget nangllegyaguteghllakii , enkaam naallghuquqii qinuyugtengit .
Whanikuyagu maligsaaghtengita takuluku pikaat , " Whanikwaa , maana paaghqituq ; aglaghtuutesqiki nenun ellngitneng neqengesqelluki . "
Jesus-em pikii , " Maanllit . Elpesi neghyaghqaliteki . "
Pikaat , " Whaa legan tallimaggaagut neqekrangllat , iqalluggaaklu . "
Jesus-em pikii , " Tagiteki whavek . "
Taagken yulghutet aqumuutesqegkii vegaaghqun . Tuguluki tallimat neqekrangllat , iqalluggaaklu , sivuglluni qilagmun Kiyaghneq iyamsiqayugvikegkaa . Iiggmineng aavgughluki neqekrangllat , maligsaaghteminun tuunegkii uyegtesqelluki yulghutnun .
Qamaglluni neghuutkaq kepsuulluni . Taagken maligsaaghtet tugukiit qula maalghuk siipneqluku pasketet esleqngalghiit kagimleghitneng neqekrangllat siipneghet .
Entaqun 5,000-nguut yuget neghuutkat , aghnatlu taghnughhaatlu kesutkegpenaki .
Taagken Jesus-em maligsaaghteni kayagtekii angyakun aghviqestiisqelluki naayvam inglunganun , ellngan aglaghtuutesimaluki yulghuteghllaget .
Yulghuteghllaget aglaghtuutesamiki ellnginaghmi naayghamun mayuqaq yughaghnaluni . Tawani ighivgaghmi Jesus ellnginaamaluku ,
angyat un始ga naayvami awavaghluteng , elngaatall imaghlliiqat qayughllak aygughnaghuskangi .
Akulegkeni three-kellaagenkuk , six-eklaagenkuk unaanguluku Jesus-em takukii maligsaaghteni meghem qaayngakun piyugmeng .
Maligsaaghtet esghaghluku meghqun piyulghii kakavniiqat . Enkaam akilghuukat , " Taghneghaaguq . "
Tawaninginaq Jesus-em pikii , " Alingegpenasi , Whanganguunga ! "
Taagken Peter-em pikaa , " Ataneq , ipa elpengukuvek tagsighnga elpenun aglaghlanga meghem qaayngakun . "
Jesus-em pikaa , " Tagi . " Enkaam Peter ateghluni angyameng , meghem qaayngakun piyugmeng aglaqaq Jesus-mun .
Iwernga anuqa elpeksamigu alingegkaq , kalevutkelluku akilghuukaq , " Ataneq , yugulinga ! "
Tawaninginaq Jesus-em akuqaghluku pikaa , " Ugpeqilleghqestaapiguuten ! Sangavek malghuklizin ? "
Angyamun uugtaquklu ellmaaragtekaq .
Enkaam angyamelnguut maniguqaat Jesus . Pikaat , " Ipapestaaq Kiyaghneghem Ighneqaaten ! "
Taagken naayvaq aghvighluku tamlakat Gennesaret-kun .
Tamaakumiit liisuqsamegteggu Jesus , ungipaasaghtiisqegkiit village-enilnguut qinuyugtiighit tagitesqelluki Jesus-mun .
Maniguututkiit qinuyulghiit waran saaftesqelluku keniikun enkaam qamaglluteng tamaakut saaftilghiit naallghutellengegkat .
Taagken ilangi Pharisees-etlu , apeghtughikayugetlu Liilightuusaneng Jerusalem-emeng tagiluteng aaptekaat Jesus ,
" Sangameng maligsaaghteten qaatkusigatat sivunemta apeghtuusiitnun ? Neghnaqneghmeggni uughtiigatut elqughulluteng apeghtuusiitnun . "
Jesus-em aaptekii , " Sangan elpesi qaatkigataqestiki Kiyaghneghem qelghusii maliggnaluki elpesi katam apeghtuusasi ?
Kiyaghneghem qelghusaqaa , ' Quulvaghlukek atanllu naanllu ' . Whatenllu pikaaguq , ' Kitum alngunak atani , nalighmeng naani seghlepestaatun akuzitkegkumigu , tuqusaghqaaguq ' .
Iwernga elpesi apeghtughiiqusi , ' Yugem quulvanghisaghngaagu atani nalighmeng naani whaten pikagu , ' Kayusiisaghqalguunga elpenun , iwernga tuunaanghitaqa qayughllak akequsaqegkaqaqa tuunelleqniluku Kiyaghneghmun . Tawaten pilleghpesigun pakigaqasi Kiyaghneghem Liilightuusii apalluqluki elpesi katam apeghtuusasi .
Ukughsi piniiyugneghni ! Elqughllusi whaten Isaiah-m uuknaliqutkegkaqiisi !
Kiyaghneq piiq , ' Ukut yuget akuzitmegteggun quulvaghaqaatnga , nakaan ilumeggneng .
Temngi manigughaqaatnga qayughllak apeghtuusaqaqiit liilightuusangllaqateng , katam whanga Liilightuusaqepiglleghhiistun . ' "
Taagken Jesus-em yulghutet tagsighluki pikii , " Nagallunga liigikitek !
Yugem sangwaa qaneghminun kanaghtekaa nukeggnaghqingigatuq , iwernga yugem qaanghaneng aanegkaq nukeggnaghqikayuguuq . "
Taagken maligsaaghtengita takuluku aaptekaat , " Liisimakenghisiguu Pharisees-et anagteketen tawaten pilleghpegun ? "
Jesus-em kiimsiqii , " Nunivagseghaq qamaglluku Atama qilagmelnguum piitesighaamangilkanga nusugyaghqaaguq .
Avelghaqiinaghluki Pharisees-et ! Ayaakastun maghyaghqughiiqut . Yugem ayaakam ilanga ayaakaq tasluqumigu , laagwaaghmun kalefkagtaallequk . "
Peter-em aaptekaa , " Ungipaataghtikut , sameng pisiigwa ungipaghaaten yuget nukeggnaghqiganniketen neghegkamegteggun ? "
Jesus-em pikii , " Elpesillu salin liigikigatsii ?
Liisimakenghisteggu sangwaa alngunak yugem qaneghminun kanaghtekaa aqsaqghwanun piiquq , taagken aanaquq yugusiineng ?
Iwernga sangwaa qamaken aanegkaq qaneghqun nukeggnaghqikayuguuq yugmeng .
Qayughllak yugem ilunganeng seghleq sumeghtaghalleq pikaayuguuq , yugtaq , gelgaghniiq , allaniiq , teglegniiq , iqlengiqutki , seghlequuq yugneng .
Tamaakusta nukeggnaghqikayuget yugneng , iwernga uughtughpenani neghellghem nukeggnaghqennaanghitaa yuuk . "
Taagken Jesus aghulaqegkaq tamaaken nunameng tungegkenun Tyre-enkuk Sidon-enkuk .
Taawanguq Canaan-eghmii aghnaq . Jesus takukaa akilghuumaghmi , " Kaay Ataneq , Ighnegha David-em , nangllegyaguteqeghtinga ! Panika tughneghaam iitghumaa , seghleghwaaghuuq . "
Iwernga Jesus-em avelghaqiinaqaa . Maligsaaghtengita takuluku kayagtaghwaaqaat , " Iqitesqigu ! Maligsaaghumaamta akilghuuguq ! "
Taagken Jesus-em pikii , " Kiyaghneghem kayagtekaqaanga Israel-eghmiinginaghhaghnun , penniighestun iflakastun ayuqelghiinun . "
Iwernga aghnaq tagiluni Jesus-em sivungakun qungughtutkelluku pikaq , " Ataneq , kayusiitaghtinga ! "
Jesus-em pikaa , " Anaggutngaaq taghnughhaat neqngit tuguluki qikminun miluuskumeng . "
Aghnam pikaa , " Aa-a , Ataneq , talwa yugem qikmii ifkaghqellghaneng neghaqut . "
Taagken Jesus-em pikaa , " Aghnaq elpek , ugpeqilleghtupigtuten ! Apeghiighli piyukelleghpetun . " Tawaninginaq paniga naallghutkaq .
Taagken Jesus aghulaqegkaq tamaaken nunameng , esnengakun Naayvam Galilee-m . Qemimun mayughluni aqumegkaq .
Yulghuteghllaget takulaghaatkaat , tagisimiita Jesus-em sivunganun piyugpagningilnguut , aqnightekat , ayaakat , akuzingigalnguut , ilangillu qinuyulghiit . Enkaam naallghuquqii .
Yulghuteghllaget saghiighayukat esghapagluki akuzingigalnguut akuziyagullghiit , aqnightekat naallghullghiit , piyugpagningilnguut piyugyagullghiit , ayaakatlu esghaasagullghiit . Enkaam usuqegkaat Kiyaghnegha Israel-em .
Taagken Jesus-em maligsaaghteni tagsighluki pikii , " Maakut nangllegyagutepigtanka qayughllak whangamnitut pingayut aghneghet , talwa neghyaghqiitut . Neghestegpenaki aghulaqesunghitanka , luuraq tumangani kayaalinayukata . "
Maligsaaghtengita aaptekaat , " Maani kilgaani naken neqengnaqesta naamayaghqameng yulghuteghllagnun ? "
Jesus-em aaptekii , " Naten uglaghqakaan neqekrangllalgutsi ? " Kiimsiqaat , " Maaghraghvinleguut , qafsinatlu iqalluggaat . "
Enkaam Jesus-em yulghuteghllaget qelqii aqumuutesqelluki nunakun .
Taagken tuguluki maaghraghvinlek neqekrangllat iqallugetlu , Kiyaghneq iyamsiqayugvikegkaa . Aavgughluki tuunegkii maligsaaghteminun enkaam uyegtekiit yulghuteghllagnun .
Qamaglluteng neghuutkat kepsuulluteng . Taagken maligsaaghtet siipneq qerngughlluku maaghraghvinlek pasketet imiiqiit esleqaghaghluki .
Uglaghtalangit neghuutkat yuget 4,000-nguftut , kesutkegpenaki aghnatlu taghnughhaatlu .
Taagken Jesus-em yulghuteghllaget aglaghtuutesluki ellngitnun ellnga angyamun uuglluni uvitanganun Magadan-em aglaqaq .
Taagken ilangi Pharisees-etlu Sadducees-etlu tagikat Jesus-mun anagniilqavigighnaluku . Enkaam allaaghlluwhaghtisqegkaat esghaasighqaaluku aghtughyaghqaanghillgha Kiyaghneghmeng pingutanga .
Iwernga Jesus-em kiimsiqii , " Siqineq tevighyaghtungestanghani esla kavighrugunghani piiqusi , ' Unaami pinighnaquq . '
Siqineq piitekestanghani qilaga kavighrugunghanillu qilagiinghanillu piiqusi , ' Aghneghmi esla seghleghunaquq . ' Esghapagluku qilaga liisimakaqaghsi esla natennaqutanga . Iwernga esghapaneghpesiki sallghet aghneghni maani liigikepagningitasi sameng pisiitangi .
Aghneghem uum yugi seghleghqumanguut , ataasiighneghilnguut Kiyaghneghmun , naqam allaaghlluwhaghtitesqut whangamnun . Yeghlegillu ! Taananginaghhaq allaaghlluwhaghtilleq esghaghlleqaghsi Kiyaghneghem allaaghlluwhaghtillgha Jonah-mun . " Taagken Jesus-em unilluki aghulaqegkat .
Maligsaaghtekullghiit inglunganun naayvam kaalluteng , maligsaaghtet piyalghiimeng puygumalghiit neqekrangllameng kelqegpenateng .
Jesus-em pikii , " Kelengalusi Pharisees-etlu Sadducees-etlu yeast-angitneng . "
Ellmeggneng akuzimghhutkegkaat , " Tawaten piiq qayughllak kelqenghilnguukut neqekrangllameng . "
Jesus-em liisimakegkangi sameng pitangi enkaam pikii , " Elpesi yugni , ugpeqilleghqestaapiguusi ! Sangafsi neqekranglliinnitsi ?
Taawa liigikigatsii ? Neqamikenghistekii tallimat neqekrangllat aavguqanka 5,000 yugnun , qafsin始gutangillu pasketet siipneghmeng imiqasi esleqaghaghlluki ?
Taakutlu neqamikenghistekii maaghraghvinlek neqekrangllat 4,000 yugnun neghestekanka , qafsin始gutangitlu pasketet siipneghmeng imiqasi esleqaghaghlluki ?
Naten sangan liigikenghitesteggu neqekrangllaanghilnguq akuzitkegkegka ? Kelengalusi Pharisees-etlu Sadducees-etlu yeast-angitneng ! "
Taagken maligsaaghtet liigikegkaat sameng piiqutanga . Yeast-angunghiteftuq neqekrangllamelnguq kelengasaaghutkegkaa , iwernga kelengasqaqeftii apeghtuusiitneng Pharisees-etlu Sadducees-etlu .
Taagken Jesus kaasami tunganganun Caesarea Philippi-em , aaptekii maligsaaghteni , " Yuget kinanguniiqatgu Ighnegha Yugem ? "
Kiimsiqaat , " Ilangi piiqut John-nguniluku Paaptaayesta , ilangita Elijah , paninang ilangita Jeremiah-nguniiqaat nalighmeng naliit uuknaliqistet . "
Aaptekii , " Elpesimi kinanguniiqestengnga ? "
Simon Peter-em kiimsiqaa , " Christ-anguuten , Ighnegha unguvalghiim Kiyaghneghem . "
Jesus-em pikaa , " Quyastellelguuten , Simon , ighnegha Jonah-m ! Qayughllak yugmeng liisimangitan , Atama qilagmelnguum elpenun liitestekaqaa .
Enkaam piimken , Peter-nguuten , Uyghak . Whagun uyghagkun nekefleqaqa yughaghvika , tuqullghem aghtughyaghqaanghillghan kayaalqesaghqaqenghitngwhaaghaa .
Elpenun tuunelleqanka key-ngi Ataneghpagullghan Qilagem . Sangwaa alngunak asightekuvgu nunami whani , asighsaghqaaguq qilagmillu . Sangwaa alngunak itemuskuvgu nunami whani , itemusaghqaaguq qilagmillu . "
Taagken Jesus maligsaaghteminun apeghtesnanighwaaqaq kitumun alngunak Christ-anguniluni .
Taagken kenlanga Jesus-em liigikesnaqegkii maligsaaghteni , Jerusalem-etepestaaghyaghqaaniluni , tawani allaaghhiinakun ikfiqesleqniluni Elder-enun , chief priest-enun , apeghtughikayugnunllu Liilightuusameng . Ungipaatkii tuqusaghqaaniluni taagken pingayaani aghneghem Kiyaghneghmun unguvaghsaghqaaniluni .
Peter-em iqitulluku aghyuuniiqaa , " Ataneq , Kiyaghneghem pisnaanghitaaten ! Tawaten pinaanghituten ! "
Jesus-em qiivluku Peter pikaa , " Tughneghaq , iqiten whangamneng ! Amigighaghpenga , qayughllak sumeghtaghallghen yugem sumeghtaghalqaa , Kiyaghneghem sumeghtaghalqenghitaa ! "
Taagken Jesus-em maligsaaghteni pikii , " Kitum alngunak maligsukuminga , ellmi katam piyukelleni peglluku , qaquurani uyamigluku maligllinga .
Qayughllak kitum alngunak unguvalleni ellminun katam piknikumigu iflayaghqaqaa . Kitum alngunak pegtekumigu unguvalleni whanga apalluqlunga allgeghlleqaa .
Sangwaangam yugem pinighqusiqelleqagu piliilluku nunaghllak , iflakumigu unguvasigni ? Taawa avangituq veghtusighqameng unguvasigminun .
Aapghanka tamaakut elpesinun qayughllak Ighnegha Yugem tagiyaghqaaguq Atamineng aghtughyaghqaanghillelighluni yaqulegtuumaghmi . Taagken tamaghhaa yuuk nallangightughlleqaa apeghiighutellghatun .
Ipa ungipaatamsi , whaanlenguut ilagpesi unguvalleghmeggni esghaghyaghqaqaat Ighnegha Yugem tagilghii Umiilguluni . "
Aghvinlek aghneq atughluku , Jesus-em kelqegkii Peter , James-enkuklu , John-enkuk , anglegutkullghiik , mayuutkii uusqalghiimun naayghamun ellnginiita .
Iiyngitneng taagken Jesus allangughtekaq : gginaa kuukgutkaq siqineghtun , aatkiillu qateghrakguughtekat nighugestun .
Taagken maligsaaghtet esghaqagket Moses-enkuk Elijah-nkuk aliighlutek aleghquqangak Jesus .
Enkaam Peter-em pikaa Jesus , " Ataneq , itagnapigtuq whaantelleghput ! Piyukelqegkuvgu nekeflangi pingayut azigutat , elpenunllu , Moses-munllu , Elijah-munllu . "
Salin akuzimaluku , qilagwaaghem nighugrakegtam saapegkii , enkaam qilawaaghmeng mem pikii , " Una Ighneqaqa , piniqepigtaqa , efquqepigtaqa , nagataqiteggu ! "
Maligsaaghtet nagalluku ma , alingruughem angtalanganeng niinghutkat nunamun .
Taagken Jesus-em takuluki saafluki , pikii , " Nekevitek , alingegpenasi ! "
Sivugsalghiimeng Jesus-nginaghhaq esghaqaat .
Ukigutkelluku naayghameng Jesus-em ineghtengngwaaqii , " Kitumun alngunak apeghyaqunaan esghaghwaalleq pinakesi kenlanga Ighnegha Yugem unguvaghtekan tuqulleghmeng . "
Taagken maligsaaghtet aaptekaat Jesus , " Sangan apeghtughistengita Liilightuusat piiqatgu Elijah sivukluni tagipestaaghyaghqaaniluku ? "
Jesus-em kiimsiqii , " Ipa Elijah tagipestaaghyaghqaaguq , enkaam sangwaa qamagtengngwaaghluku nallghusanqiglleqaa .
Iwernga ungipaatamsi Elijah tagingwaaqaaguq , iwernga yuget kinangutanga nallukegkaqaat , piyukelleghmegestunllu pikaqaat . Tawateghpigaq Ighnegha Yugem ikfiqesleqaat . "
Taagken maligsaaghtet liigikegkaat John Paaptaayesta akuzitkaqeftaa .
Yulghuteghllagnun uteghnighyata , yugem takuluku Jesus , aga segesqughtengnginaamaghmi manungakun pikaq .
Pikaa , " Ataneq , ighneqa nangllegyagutaghtigu ! Sayugpagtalguuq , elngaatall ikfiqnguuq . Awen kenghegnun uullghaghtaquq nalighmeng meghquutaquq .
Maligsaagtegpenun tagisaghaqa , iwernga naallghutepagningitkaat . "
Jesus-em pikii , " Elpesi yugni , ugpeqillghitusillu , seghleghwaaghuusillu ! Naten tagkaan elpesininnaqsinga ugpeqesqellunga ? Mekelghiiq whavek tagiteggu ! "
Jesus-em aghyuuqaa tughneghaq , taagken aanegkaq mekelghiighmeng enkaam tawaninginaq naallghutkaq mekelghiiq .
Taagken Jesus ellnginaaghsan maligsaagtengita takuluku aaptekaat , " Sangan whangkuta aanesneghmeng aghtughesteggu tughneghaq ? "
Jesus-em kiimsiqii , " Qayughllak ugpeqilleghqestaaghhaalghiisi . Ipa ungipaatamsi , ugpeqillelguyaqufsi mustard-em piitutesqughhan angtalngatun , una naayghaq pikufsigu , ' Ingavek nuugten ! ' nuuggnayaghtuq . Enkaam sangwaa alngunak aghtughnayanghitaghsi ! "
Iwernga tawatelnguq tughneghaq yughaghhiinaghqunllu , fast-elleghqunllu aanesaghqaqaghsi .
Maligsaaghtet qerngughusata Galilee-mi Jesus-em pikii , " Ighnegha Yugem tuguluku tuunelleqaat yugnun ,
enkaam tuqulleqaat . Iwernga pingayiitangani aghneghem unguvaghtesaghqaaguq . " Taagken maligsaaghtet qivghughllakat .
Taagken Jesus-enkut maligsaaghtekullghiit Capernaum-emun tagiyata , Temple-em tax-meng qerngughtistengita takuluku Peter aaptekaat , " Apeghtughistezi Temple-em tax-nganeng llivikiiqaa ? "
Peter-em kiimsiqii , " Aa-a , piiquq . " Peter iteghyan mangteghamun Jesus-em aleghqughyuwhaaqaa , " Simon , nateta elpek sumeghpeni ? Kinkungwaaqat nunat umiilgita llivikistaqegkangit allaaghhiinaghmeng tax-emeng ? Nunalgutmeggneng piiqaat nalighmeng nakumiineng ? "
