Peter-em kiimsiqaa , " Nakumiineng . " Jesus-em pikaa , " Enkaam umiilget yugit llivikinaanghitut .
Iwernga seghleghyugsunghitapung tax-meng qerngughtistet . Enkaam nulughyaa naayvamun iqallugtaqsuggaaghpek qaanghani naalkelleqan mani . Tuguluku llivikusaghtughnakefkung . "
Taam kingunginaaneng maligsaaghtet Jesus-mun tagiluteng aaptekaat , " Ataneghpagullghani Qilagem kina angelleghpigaawa ? "
Jesus-em tagsighluku taghnughhaq nekevestekaa qukiitgun .
Pikii , " Ipa ungipaatamsi , iteghnaanghitngwaaghtusi Ataneghpagullghanun Qilagem wetqukun taghnughhaghestun lliiqufsi .
Kina alngunak ukaliighlleghhii uutun taghnughhaghtun , angelleghpigaaguq Ataneghpagullghani Qilagem .
Kitum alngunak atemkun tuguklineghminigu whatelnguq taghnughhaq , whanga tuguklighaqaanga .
Iwernga kitum alngunak seghleghqestekagu naliit mekestaaghhaat ugpeqingalghiit whangamneng , itagnaghnayaghtuq yuget qaamqaghfikluku uyaqwaghkun uyghagllagmeng kalefsaqumegteggu uusqallghanun kelliim .
" Seghleghwaaghunaqnguut yuget qayughllak nunami whani nanghiiqulleghtupigtut seghleghqelleghmun . Nanghiiqullghet seghleghqistimun piyaghqaagut , iwernga seghleghwaaghunaqnguuq kina seghleghqestilghii yugneng !
" Iiggegpek nalighmeng itegaghpek seghleghqestekangaten , kepluki eggnaketen ! Itagnaghataghaghnayaghtuten kenlengilngughmun unguvalleghmun iitquvek , iiggiteghngaaghpek nalighmeng itegiiteghngaaghpek miluutelleghqaghpeneng kenlengilnguugnun kenghegnun , inglugtun iiggelighluten nalighmeng itegalighluten .
Iyegpeklu seghleghqestekangaten ipugluku eggnaken ! Itagnaghataghaghnayaghtuten kenlengilngughmun unguvalleghmun iitquvek inglupigaq iiskelluku , miluutelleghqaghpeneng kenghanun hell-em inglugtun iyelguluten .
" Wataghllak , ukaliqegpenaki nalighhiiniit ukut mekestaghhaat . Ungipaatamsi , qilagmi yaqulgita quunpeng Atama qilagmelnguum gginaa esghaghaqaat .
Ighnegha Yugem tagikaaguq yugulinaluki iflakat .
" Sumeghpesini sanayaghta yuuk 100 penniilek , ataasiq aghulaqsaqan ? Ivaghyaghtughnayaghtaguu aghulaqegkaq unilluki 99 penniini qeminilluki ?
Ipa piimsi , naalkegkumigu quyakeghllagyaghqaqaa pakiggulluku 99-eneng aghulaqumangilngughneng .
Tawateghpigaq Atagpesi qilagmelnguum piyukelqenghitaa nalighhiiniit maakut mekestaghhaat iflasqelluki .
" Ugpeqaalgutegpek seghletun pikangaten , ellnginaaghulluku ungipaannaken anaggutellghaneng . Nagaskumiten taawa ilaliighunneqigllequtek .
Iwernga nagasunghilkangaten , takunqiggnaken kelqelluku ataasiq nalighmeng maalghuk ugpeqaalgutek liisimakestengulukek sameng pilleghpetegneng . Tawaten pilghaaten qayughllak Akuzitet Igaqegkat apeghtuusaqaat maalghuk nalighmeng pingayut liisimakistet ipapighqesaghqaqaat anaggutelleq .
Iwernga nagasunghilkaki apeghnakesi yughaghvigem yugitnun . Nagasunghilkaki talwa yughaghvigem yugi , kiyaghunnakesi Gentile-ngulghiistun , tax-mengllu qerngughtistengulghiistun .
" Ipa ungipaatamsi , sangwaa alngunak asightekufsigu nunami whani , asighsaghqaaguq qilagmillu . Sangwaa alngunak itemuskufsigu nunami whani , itemusaghqaaguq qilagmillu .
" Ilanganengllu ungipaannaqamsi , nunami whani maalghugulutek itagnaqutngukuftek aapnalutek sameng alngunak , Atama qilagmelnguum apeghiighlleqaa elpetegnun .
Qayughllak maalghuggaat nalighmeng pingayuggaat qerngughuskata whanga atemkun , akulngitnisaghqaagunga . "
Taagken Peter-em takuluku Jesus aaptekaa , " Ataneq , ugpeqaalgutma seghletun pimanginaqanganga naten uglaghqakaan seghevusaghqaqsikun ? Ketwell maaghraghvinlaak ? "
Jesus-em kiimsiqaa , " Maaghraghvinleggiinaq seghevusaghqaqenghitan , iwernga 70 x 7 .
Tawaten piimken qayughllak Kiyaghneghem igleghutillgha Ataneghpagullghani Qilagem whatetuq : Umiilgem qepghaghtemi igiit yuvghiighyaghtuqii esghaghnaluki asengetulangit .
Iiwenllu igiit yuvghiighaqii , umiilegmun itghutkaat qepghaghta asengelek 10,000 manimeng .
Tawaten angkaan maningilnguq llivikuusaghqameng asengeminun . Enkaam umiilgem akikesqegkii ellnga , nulighha , avaqutii , saghyangillu llivikuusaaluki asengenganun .
Iwernga qepghaghta sikmuulluni umiilegmi manungakun maniguutepiglluni pikaa , ' Utaqiigaghten ! Lliviknaaghaqa qamagtengngwaaghluku ! '
Umiilgem nangllegyagulluku puygusqegkaa asengenga enkaam aanestekaa .
" Taagken taana qepghaghta aanluni nallaqaa qepghaghtelgutni 100 manimeng asengekaq . Akuqaghluku uyaqwhakun pikaa , ' Llivikinga asengegpeneng ! '
Qepghalgutangan sikmuulluni nangllegsipiglluni pikaa , ' Utaqiigaghten , llivikelleqamken ' .
Iwernga yugem nagasimangilkanga , yeghlegi anusimingllaghtestekaa kenlanga asengenga llivikellghanun .
Ilangita qepghaghtet esghapagluku tawaten pillgha , seghleghyaguteghllagluku umiilegmeggnun apeghyaghtuqaat .
Enkaam umiilgem qepghaghta taana tagsiqlighluku pikaa , ' Uyuq seghlepestaaq qepghaghta ! Legan始ngam seghevutamken asengeghllagpeneng , qayughllak nangllegsilghiiten .
Qepghalguten nangllegyagusaqlegestun katam whanga nangllegyagutellemtun elpek ! '
Umiilgem sakritepiglluni taana qepghaghta aglaatestekaa amyuutkistenun anusimingllaghvigmelngughnun kenlanga qamagtengngwaaghluku asengenga llivikellghanun .
" Esgha tawateghpigaq Atama qilagmelnguum qamagllusi piyaghqiisi , qamaken ilugpesineng seghevunneghilkufsiki yulgutesi . "
Jesus-em tamaakut apeghtuusaqneghmeng taaqsamiki aghulaqegkaq Galilee-meng , nunanganun Judea-m , inglunganilngughmun Kiiwem Jordan-em .
Yulghuteghllaget maliglleghaatkaat enkaam tawani naallghuquqii qinuyuget .
Ilangita Pharisees-et takuluku anagniilqavigighnaluku aaptekaat , " Liilightuusamnni itagnaghtaa yugem pegtekumigu nuliini sangwaa alngunak apalluqluku ? "
Jesus-em kiimsiqii , " Atightiigastekii Akuzitet Igaqegkat whaten pillghit , ' Piinlighyuwhaalleghmi Kiyaghneq yungllaghaqngami ulimakaqegkek yugenkuk aghnaankuk ' ? "
Enkaam pikii , " Taana apalluqluku yugem atanillu naanillu unillukek , nulighqullghiik qerngughullequk , enkaam ataasiighllequk yugusiik .
Enkaangam maalghugunanightuk , ataasiightuk yugusiik . Tamaaken apalluqluku Kiyaghneghem qerngughutestekakek yeqay yugem pellghututesneghillikek . "
Pharisees-et aaptekaat , " Sanganmi Moses-em Liilightuusalitinkut yugmun igalitesqelluku nulighha pegtugsighqameng , aanesimaanllu ? "
Jesus-em kiimsiqii , " Moses-em pegtesaghqaaghtestekaqii nuliisi qayughllak pineghllugulghiisi . Iwernga piinlighyuggaalleghmeng Kiyaghneghem tawatetesaghqaanghinniluku pikaqsaghaa .
Enkaam whanga piimsi , yugem pegsaghqaqenghitaa nuliini wetkuqun gelghaghniiqan . Pegtekumigu sameng allaneng apallulighluni , nulightunqigtekumi gelgaghniighullequq nulighqenghhamikun . "
Maligsaaghtengita pikaat , " Taananginaghhaakan apalluq yugem pegtusighqaa nuliighminun , yuuk nulightunghiteghngaaghmi itagnaghnayaghtuq . "
Iwernga Jesus-em pikii , " Taana apalluq tamaghhaghmi tuguklighnaanghitaat , iwernga Kiyaghneghem ilangitnun tuguklighyaghqaaghtestekaqaa .
Ilangi yuget nulightiigatut allgeqaatmeggneng eunuch-ngnguluteng . Ilangi nulightiigatut qayughllak yuget eunuch-engllaqaqiit . Paninang ilangi eunuch-ngwaaqut pinighataghatun qepghaannaluku Kiyaghneq Ataneghpagullghani Qilagem . Kitum alngunak taana tuguklighyaghqaqegkumigu , tuguklighligu . "
Taagken taghnughhaat tagitkiit Jesus-mun saafluki yughaatkesqelluki . Taawanginaq maligsaaghtet ineghtekiit tagitistengit taghnughhaat .
Iwernga Jesus-em pikii , " Yeqay taghnughhaat tagilit whangamnun . Ineghtegpenaki , qayughllak Ataneghpagullgha Qilagem taghnughhaghestun ayuqelghiit pikaat . "
Enkaam saaftaqluki quyastekii , taagken aghulaqegkaq .
Taagken yugem takuluku Jesus aaptekaa , " Apeghtughista , sangwaa pinilghii piyaghqaqsikun allgeghutusighqaaluku kenlengilngughmeng unguvalleghmeng ? "
Jesus-em pikaa , " Sangan aapsinga sangwaa piniitanga ? Ataasighhaaguq pinilghii . Kenlengilngughmeng unguvallengyukuvek qaatkiki Kiyaghneghem qelghusii . "
Nukalpigam aaptekaa , " Nakut ? " Jesus-em kiimsiqaa , " Yugtaghpenang , Gelgaghniighpenang , Teglegpenang , Iqlengiqutkigpenang ,
Quulvaghlukek atanllu naanllu , Piniqluki yulguteten piniqelleghpetun elpeneng . "
Nukalpigam pikaa , " Qamaglluki taakut qaatkaqanka . Sangwaallu piyaghqaqsikun ? "
Jesus-em kiimsiqaa , " Naamigtengngwaaghyukuvgu Kiyaghneghem pisqellgha elpenun , aglaghluten qamaglluku saghyan akikluku , akinga tamaana aklumalghiinun tunqughnaken . Enkaam qilagmi aklungilgullequten , taagken tagiluten maliggnakevnga . "
Nukalpigam nagalluku , aghulaqegkaq iilqepiglluni qayughllak aklungitepiglleghhii .
Taagken Jesus-em maligsaaghteni pikii , " Ipa piimsi , piyaqnaghyaghqaaguq aklungilngughmun yugmun itelleghqaa Ataneghpagullghanun Qilagem .
Ungipaannaqlaataghamsi ilanganeng , piyaqniisaghqaaguq camel-em suflughutelleghqaa sikuum iiyngakun , aklungilnguum yugem itelleghqaaneng Ataneghpagullghanun Kiyaghneghem . "
Maligsaaghtet nagasamegteggu tawaten pilleq saghiighayugllagumaghmeng pikat , " Kinangam yugulillengelleqa ? "
Iwernga Jesus-em tawaveghlluwaaq esghaghluki pikii , " Yuget piyaghqaqenghilkangit , Kiyaghneghem piyaghqaqii . "
Taagken Peter-em pikaa , " Esghaqaghqutqun , sangwaa qamaglluku unilluku maligtekaqamken . Sangwaangam allgeghlleqesteggu ? "
Jesus-em pikii , " Ipa piimsi , nutaghami nunami Ighnegha Yugem aqumellequq umiilgusignekun aqumutagmikun nighughqelleghmini . Taagken elpesillu maligutkani whangamnun aqumlusi qula maalghuk siipneqluku umiilgem aqumutiitgun , igleghutillequsi qula maalghuk siipneqluku ramkenganeng Israel-em .
Enkaam whanga apalluqlunga kinkut alngunak uniskumegteki mangteghateng , angleguteteng , nayateng , atateng , naateng , avaqutateng , nalighmeng piitesighaghviteng , nulallequt 100-alpagluku . Kenlengilngughmengllu unguvalleghmeng allgeghullequt .
Iwernga aangelghiilghutet ukaliighllequt enkaam ukavanlenguut angellghughllequt . "
Paninang Jesus-em pikii , " Ataneghpagullgha Qilagem yugtun ayuquq grapes-meng piitesighaghvilek . Unaanguluku aanluni tugulaasaghtuqaq qepghaghtekaghqameng piitesighaghvigminun .
Aghneghmun tawavek itagnaqegkii akileghtughnaluki ataasikaghtaan denarius-meng , taagken qepghaghyaghtestekii .
Nine-eklaagmi aaneqiglluni esghaqii yuget nekevghataaghullghiit sagpenateng akilpegaghvigmi .
Enkaam pikii , ' Elpesillu piitesighaghvimnun qepghaghyaghtek , akileghtughnaaghamsi qepghalleghpesistun ' .
Enkaangam qepghaghyaatkat . Taagken aghneghem qukaanillu , three-klaagmillu tawaten pilaataqaq .
Iiwenllu five-eklaagnaqaqaa , akilpegaghvigmun pikaq , taawanguq paninang yugem ilangi nekevghataaghaqeftut . Aaptekii , ' Sangafsi whaantaqetsi aghnelqusiq sagpenasi ? '
Kiimsiqaat , ' Qayughllak kitum alngunak tugunghilkanginkut qepghaghtenguluta . ' Enkaam pikii , ' Naqam elpesillu qepghaghyaghtek piitesighaghvimnun ' .
" Ighivgaghyagu piitesighaghvilgem pikaa qepghaghtet naasquutistengat , ' Qepghaghtet tuqlughteghluki akileghtughteghqi kingulighneng sivulighnun . '
Five-eklaagmi qepghaghyaatkat tagilaghaasameng akileghtuusangegkat denarius-kaghtaan .
Enkaam sivuliit qepghaghtet akileghtuusangataghaghnaqniluteng pikaayalghiit , iwernga tagilaghaasalghiimeng ellngitlu akileghtuusangegkat denarius-kaghtaan .
Akileghtuusangyameng qivraaghutkaat piitesighaghvigem yuga .
Pikaat , ' Kinguliiluki tugukaghten qepghaghtut ataasighhaghmun aflumun . Whangkuta ughleghiightukut puqlaghllagmi aghnelqusiq , iwernga akileghtughaten whangkutestun angkaan . '
Iwernga yugem pikaa ataasiq , ' Nagataghten , ilakumtaamni , puughhneghitamken . Itagnaqegkaqan qepghaghnaluten ataasimun denarius-mun .
Enkaam tuguluku akileghtuusan aglaa . Akileghtughyuganka kinguliit yuget tugukanka akileghtuusaghpetun angkaan .
Piyukellemtun manika atughyaghqaqaqa . Aqinaziin ighlegitutemneng ? ' "
Taagken Jesus-em pikii , " Enkaam tamaakut kinguliit sivuliighsaghqaagut , sivuliit kinguliighsaghqaagut . "
Jesus-em Jerusalem-emun mayuutkelluku yulghutneng aafutkii qula maalghuk siipneqluku maligsaaghteni aleghqughnaaluki .
Pikii , " Nagatek , Jerusalem-emun mayughnaqukut . Tawani Ighnegha Yugem tuunelleqaat chief priest-enunllu , apeghtughikayugnunllu Liilightuusaneng enkaam nanqiglluku tuqusaghqaanilleqaat .
Taagken Gentile-enun tuunelleqaat . Tawani legasiighwaatkelleqaat , kagsagmiglleqaat , qaquuraghlleqaatlu . Iwernga pingayiitangani aghneghem unguvaghtesaghqaaguq . "
Taagken Zebedee-m ighneghegkenka naangak tagikaq Jesus-mun ighneghegni kelqellukek . Manungakun segesqughtekaq aapfiknaluku .
Jesus-em aaptekaa , " Sameng piighsin ? " Aghnam kiimsiqaa , " Akeqinga Ataneghpagulleghpeni ighneghegka aqumesnakegken aallgha aghenqigneghpegun , ilanga saghumigneghpegun . "
Iwernga Jesus-em pikii , " Liigikenghitaghsi sangutanga tungsiqaghsi . Meghviknayaghestegneguu qayuusiq meghyaghqaqa ? " Kiimsiqaak , " Piyaqleguukung . "
Jesus-em pikakek , " Qaywa qayuusimneng meghellequtek , iwernga whangangunghituq nakmiighyaghqaq kinkuk aqumyaghqaatkek aghenqignemkunllu saghumignemkunllu . Atama yataaghqegkaqaak taakuk aqumvigkak nakmikegkaminun . "
Taakut ilangita qula maligsaaghtet nagaqughyamegtekek samatkek anglegutkullghiik ugumiyagutkagket .
Taagken Jesus-em tuqlughluki maligsaaghteni , pikii , " Liisimakasi Gentile-et igleghutistengita atanghutaqiit yuteng , aangwaaghughtekatlu yugita yukeghqutkaqiit .
Iwernga elpesi tawatesaghqaanghitusi . Nalighsi igleghutistenguyukumi qepghaghtengughlli elpesinun .
Nalighsi aangelleghpigaayukumi qepghaghtelaaghughsaghqaaguq elpesinun ,
katam tawaten Ighneghan Yugem pillghatun . Tagimangituq qepghaatesqelluni iwernga tagikaaguq qepghaatinaluni , tuunalukullu unguvalleni naveghqellisiqnaluku uglapiglleghhiinun yugnun . "
Jesus-enkut maligsaaghtekullghiit Jericho-meng aghulaqumaluki yulghuteghllagem maligtekaat Jesus .
Taawanguq tumet saningitni ayaakak yugek aqumlutek . Nagaqughyamegnegu Jesus naghughhniluku akilghuukak , " Ataneq , Ighneghani David-em , nangllegyagutaghtikung ! "
Yulghutem ineghtekakek , nepiighesqellukek . Iwernga qevuutaghalluku wata akilghuukak , " Ataneq , Ighneghani David-em , nangllegyagutaghtikung ! "
Enkaam Jesus-em aghuliighluni tuqlughlukek aaptekakek , " Sasqellutek piiqestek whangamnun ? "
Kiimsiqaak , " Ataneq , iyepung esghaghtestaghtiki ! "
Jesus-em nangllegyagullukek iiyngik saaftekii . Tawaninginaq esghaasagutkak enkaam maligtekaak .
Jesus-enkut maligsaaghtekullghiit tughaaghyalghiimeng Jerusalem-emun , kaatkaat Bethphage-mun Mount Olives-melngughmun . Tawani kayagtekakek maalghuk maligsaaghtegni igleghtekestiisqellukek .
Whaten pikakek , " Ingavek nenun aglaghlutek tawaninginaq esghaghlleqaghtek petugngalghii donkey nughalek . Itemllukek taginnakegtek whangamnun .
Kitum alngunak sameng pikangistek , whaten pinaketek , ' Atanghem aklukaak . ' Tawaninginaq tagitesleqaak whangamnun . "
Whaten pikaaftuq apeghiighnaluku uuknaliqistem pillgha ,
" Ungipaasaghtughqi , Zion-eghmiit , ' Esghaqaghtegguqun , umiilegpesi takwaaqiisi . Qusevegngaaq donkey-kun igleghtaquq , donkey-m nughaakun . ' "
Enkaam maligsaaghtek igleghtekestaghlutek sivungitni , Jesus-em pisqellghatun pikak .
Donkey nughaghtuumaan tagitkaak Jesus-mun . Qaasliit aatkateng mataghlluki teghikusak qaayngitgun llikiit . Taagken Jesus aqumegkaq .
Yulghuteghllagem tumetgun aatkateng saagtekiit , enkaam ilangi uqfigem avayaaneng ikutaqluteng tumet llilaghtughvikegkiit .
Yulghuteghlaget Jesus-em sivunganilnguutlu kingunganilnguutlu akilghuutkat , " Usuqnaghhalek Ighnegha David-em ! Kiyaghneghem quyasligu tagilghii aatghakun Atanghem ! Usuqilleq qilagmelngughmun ! "
Jesus iteghyan Jerusalem-emun , qamaglluteng Jerusalem-eghmiit kagaygunneqegsaatkat whaten pimaghmeng , " Kinangaawa una yuuk ? "
Jesus-em maligtestengita yulghuteghllaget kiimsiqiit , " Jesus-nguuq , uuknaliqista , Nazareth-meng Galilee-melngughmeng pinguuq . "
Jesus Temple-mun iteghluni aanesquqii qamaglluki tukfightulghiitlu , akikulghiitlu . Taagken manimeng naveghqughtetlu tipelngit ulleghquqii , aqumutiitlu qawaagmeng akilpegaghtet .
Enkaam pikii , " Igaqngaaq Akuzitni Igaqegkani , ' Mangteghama atilqesaghqaqaa , Yughaghvik . ' Iwernga elpesi iighaghvigughtaghsi teglegniightenun ! "
Taagken ayaakatlu , ighullugmelnguutlu takukaat Jesus Temple-mun , enkaam naallghuquqii .
Chief priest-etlu apeghtughikayugetlu Liilightuusaneng esghapagluki allaaghlluwhaghtillghi Jesus-em , nagallukillu taghnughhaat Temple-mi akilghuulghiit whaten , " Usuqilleq Ighneghanun David-em ! " elngaatall ugumiyukat .
Enkaam Jesus aaptekaat , " Naganneghisikii taghnughhaat sameng pitangi ? " Jesus-em kiimsiqii , " Aa-a , nagatanka . Atightiigastegguu Akuzitet Igaqegkat pillghit , ' Qaanghitgun taghnughhaatlu allgenghhaghhaatlu yataaghqegkaqan usuqilleq elpenun katam ? ' "
Taagken Jesus-em unilluki , Jerusalem-emeng Bethany-tkaq qavaghnaluni tamaani .
Jesus unaanguluku uteghniitkelluku Jerusalem-emun iyataqaq .
Tumet saaghwitni esghaqaa figs-em uqfiga . Takuluku piyaqminigu ququngaraaghinaaftuq figs-ngunani . Enkaam uqfik tawavek pikaa , " Allamengllu piitestinaanghituten . " Tawaninginaq uqfik paliqaq .
Maligsaaghtet tawaten pilghii esghapagluku , saghiighayugutkelluku aaptekaat , " Naten uqfik sukatepiglluni palighta ? "
Jesus-em kiimsiqii , " Ipa piimsi , malghuklillngunaan ugpeqillelgukufsi , whangamtun pillequsi , esghapalleghpesistun figs-em uqfiga . Tawatenginaq pinaanghitusi talwa una naayghaq kayagtekufsigu , ' Iikluten elpeneng meghmun miluuten ' , legan pillequq .
Sameng alngunak aaptekufsi yughakun ugpeqillelgukufsi allgeghusaghqaagusi . "
Jesus kaalluni Jerusalem-emun Temple-mun iitqaq . Apeghtughimaluku , chief priest-etlu , siivanlleghetlu takuluku aaptekaat , " Ungipaatikut kitum qeleghtaten tawaten pisqelluten , nalighmeng kitum qelellghakun tawaten pinguzin ? "
Jesus-em kiimsiqii , " Whangallu aapnaqamsi . Kiimsiqufsinga whangallu ungipaalleqamsi kitumun qelghumatka .
Kitum qeleghtagu John paaptaayeghisqelluku ? Kiyaghneghtaawaa nalighmeng yugmeng pingwaa ? " Taagken ellmeggneng akuzimghhutkat , " Sameng pinaqesteggu ? Kiimsiqumteggu Kiyaghneghmeng pinguniluku , whaten pilleqiinkut , ' Sangan始ngam ugpeqenghisteggu John ? '
Iwernga , ' Yugmeng pingunikumteggu ' , qemall yulghutet salleqiinkut , qayughllak qamaglluteng ugpeqegkaat John uuknaliqistenguniluku . "
Enkaam kiimsiqaat Jesus , " Nallukaghput . " Jesus-em pikii , " Whangallu ungipaannaanghitamsi kitumun qelellengegkaatka tawaten pillemnun . "
Taagken Jesus-em aaptekii , " Naten una sumeghtaghaatkelleqesteggu ? Yugnguq taawa maalghugegneng ighnelek . Sivulighmun piluni pikaa , ' Ighnemni , aghneghmi whani grapes-meng piitesighaghvimnun qepghaghyaghhaaten ! '
Ighneghan pikaa , ' Wiin piyunghitunga . ' Iwernga aghneghmi taakwani avuteghqelluni qepghaghyaqaq .
Taagken tuunglighhaanun ighneghmi piluni , tawateghpigaq pikaa . Ighneghan pikaa , ' Aa-a , pillequnga ' , iwernga pimangilnguq . "
Jesus-em aaptekii , " Naliim ighneghan qaatkegkaqagu atani ? " Kiimsiqaat , " Sivuliim . " Enkaam Jesus-em pikii , " Ungipaatamsi tax-meng qerngughtestetlu , aghnatlu akikikayuget yugusimeggneng sivugpesini iteghaatnguut Ataneghpagullghanun Kiyaghneghem .
John-em Paaptaayestem ungipaasaghtuqaqiisi naten kiyaghtelleghqameng Kiyaghneghem piyukellghatun , iwernga ugpequmangitaghsi . Naqam tax-meng qerngughtistetlu , aghnatlu akikikayuget yugusimeggneng ugpeqegkaqaat . Talwa kingunganeng esghapakaqeghngaaghpesiki ugpeqegkangat John , paninang elpesi avuteghqellusillu seghleghqennanillghitusi , ugpequmangitaghsillu . "
Jesus-em pikii , " Ilanga ungipaghaan nagateggu . Taawanguq yuuk piitesighaqaq grapes-meng nunamikun . Minglluluku , laagutkakek grapes-mun qageghquusik , nekeftekaallu uusqalghii kelengakivigkaq . Taagken navghitkaa grapes-meng piitesighaghvini piitesighaghtenun aflengakesqelluku . Taagken ellnga ilanganun nunam aglaqaq .
Saghnayaghqaaghsata grapes-et , piitesighaghvilgem qepghaghteni kayagtekii nengini aqfasqelluki .
Iwernga piitesighaghtet akuqaghluki qepghaghtet , ataasiq anaguleghtaakaat , ilanga tuqutkaat , pingayaat milughpagaataghhiinaq tuqutkaat .
Qepghaghtemi ilangi kayagllaataqii , sivulighneng uglaghataghaghluki , ellngitlu tawatengwaaq pilaataqiit .
Qenwat ighneni kayagtekaa ellngitnun , whaten pimaghmi , ' Ipapestaaq siivakelleqaat ighneqa . '
Iwernga piitesighaghtet esghaghluku piitesighaghvilgem ighnegha whaten pikat , ' Uum ighneghan piliilleqaa una nuna atani tuqukan . Tuquskumteggu whangkuta piliilleqaghput una grapes-meng piitesighaghvik . '
Enkaangam akuqaghluku , piitesighaghvigmeng miluulluku tuqutkaat . "
Jesus-em aaptekii , " Piitesighaghvilgem tagikumi salleqaki piitesighaghtet ? "
Chief priest-etlu siivanlleghetlu kiimsiqaat , " Seghlepestaatun tuqulleqii taakut seghleghet yuget . Taagken navghilleqaa piitesighaghvini allanun piitesighaghtenun . Saghnalleghqaq kaaskan nengiilleqaat . "
Jesus-em pikii , " Atightiigastekii Akuzitet Igaqegkat whaten pillghit ? ' Uyghak taana mangteghangllaghtet ighsakegkaat megnunalleghpigaaghtekaaguq uyghak . Taana Atanghem pilqaa , urang pinilleghpigaaguq whangkunnun ! '
" Enkaangam ungipaatamsi , Ataneghpagullgha Kiyaghneghem elpesineng awisaghqaaguq , enkaam tuunyaghqaaguq yugnun piitestiyaghqanun fruit-nganeng Ataneghpagullghem . "
" Kina alngunak taaggun uyghagkun iqukumi , pelimyaghqaaguq . Kina alngunak taam uyghagem ifkaghvikegkumigu siftaaghqelleqaa . "
Chief priest-etlu Pharisees-etlu nagalluki Jesus-em ungipaghaatangi liigikegkat Jesus-emnguq ellngit akuzitkaqeftii .
Enkaam tuguyukaqsaqangat , iwernga alingegkat yulghuteghllagneng qayughllak ugpeqegkangat Jesus uuknaliqistenguniluku .
Taagken Jesus-em apeghtughlaataqii taakut yuget ungipaghaatetgun . Pikaq ,
" Ataneghpagullgha Qilagem whatetuq , umiilgem ighneni nengughhnaqelghii yataaghqutkaa neqenghaghqunnaluku .
Qepghaghteni kayagtekii ungipaasaghtiisqelluki tagsiqliqat nengughutem neqenghaghqellghanun tagilaghaatesqelluki , iwernga tagiyunghitkat .
Taagken umiilgem pikii ilangi qepghaghteni , ' Ungipaasaghtughteki tagsiqliqanka neqenghaghqellemnun , neghyaghqan始nguq apeghiightut . Tuqutiightesimaanka yugtaaneghneng teghikusaneng , quwintalghiinengllu nughaghneng . Enkaam sangwaa qamaglluni apeghiightuq . Tagilin始nguq nengughutem neqenghaghqellghanun ! '
Iwernga aqelqaghqat tagsiqliqiit waakumangilnguut . Yeghlegi navek sayaghtuutkat , ataasiq piitesighaghvigminun pikaq , ilanga estugaghminun ,
umiilgem qepghaghtengi ilangita akuqaghluki sakusiiqluki tuququqiit .
Umiilek sakriteghllakaq enkaam pilluwaghteni kayagtekii . Tuququqiit yugtaqat , kumaghtekaatlu nengat .
Taagken qepghaghteni pikii , ' Nengughhnaqem neqenghaghqusighqii apeghiightut . Aqelqangllaqaqsaqenka seghletun pikaatmeggneng tagipagningitut .
Enkaangam aanlusi tumenun nallaqasi qamaglluki yuget neqenghaghqesaghtiisqiteki . '
Qepghaghtet aanluteng tumeni qamaglluki nallaqateng seghleghuyaghngaata , pinighyaghngaata neghyaghtiisqegkiit , enkaam nengughutfik esleqaghaghtekaq .
" Umiilgem esghaghyaghtughyaqminiki aqelqat , esghaqaa yuuk aasimangilnguq nengughhnaqelghiim aatkaaneng .
Enkaam aaptekaa , ' Ilakumtaamni , naten iteghsin nengughhnaqelghiim aatkaaneng aategpenang ? ' Yugem kiimsighpagningitkaa .
Taagken umiilgem qepghaghtet pikii , ' Iiggillu , itegiillu asighlluki qagavek mamlegmun miluuteggu , tawani yuget qiyallequt ggutetengllu terqitaagtaghlleqiit . ' "
Jesus-em taaqniqii akuzilleni whaten , " Uglapestaaq tagsiqliqaaghngaan , iwernga palaghhaagut nakmikegkat . "
Taagken Pharisees-et unilluku Jesus agghitkat naten anagniilqavigighnaluku Jesus akuzillghakun .
Enkaam kayagtekiit ilangi maligsaaghteteng , ilangillu Herodian-et Jesus-mun . Whaten pikaat , " Apeghtughista , liisimakamken akuziiquten ipanguluku . Apeghtuusanllu naten Kiyaghneghem kiyaghtesqesullgha ipanguuq . Aangwaaghuyaghngaata , ukavansaghngaata paninang apeghtughaqaten tawateghpigaq .
Enkaam ungipaataghtikut naten sumeghtaghalleghpeneng . Kiyaghneghem Liilightuusaani elqughutngaa llivikilleghqaghput tax-emeng Caesar-mun ? Llivikiltaa-a nalighmeng pinghitelta ? "
Jesus-em liisimakegkii seghletun piyugukangat , enkaam pikii , " Piniiyugneghni elpesi ! Sangama anagniilqavigighnaqutkestengnga ?
Kelguvikitengnga manimeng tax-mun llivikisighqameng . " Enkaam tagitkaat manimeng .
Taagken aaptekii , " Kitum gginaqagu una ? Kitum aatqagu una ? "
Kiimsiqaat , " Caesar-em . " Enkaangam Jesus-em pikii , " Tuuniteki Caesar-mun tamaakut Caesar-em pingi , tuuniteki Kiyaghneghmun tamaakut Kiyaghneghem pingi . "
Nagasamegteggu saghiighayukat taagken unilluku aghulaqegkat .
Tawani aghneghmi Sadducees-et aapsaghtuqaat Jesus . Tamaakunguut ugpeqingigalnguut tuqukat unguvaghtekayugutangi .
Pikaat , " Apeghtughista , Moses-em Liilightuusii pikaagut , ' Yuuk nulightughluni tuqukan avaqutigpenani , anglegutangan tuguyaghqaqaa ugingighaq avaqutinnaluku anglegutni tuqukaq . '
Maansaghtut maaghraghvinlek yuget anglegutkullghiit . Nuyekliq nulightughluni avaqutigpenani tuqukaaguq . Enkaam nulighha anglegutangan tugukaa .
Tuunglighhaallu anglegutanga tuquuq avaqutigpenani . Enkaam pingayaan anglegutangan tugaa taana aghnaq . Qamaglluteng tugaaqluku tuqulaghaatut avaqutigpenateng .
Kinguliiluni aghnaq tuqukaaguq .
Ungipaataghtikut , unguvaghtuutellghem aghneghani kitum aghnaq nulighqelleqagu , qamagllutengqun tugukaqegkangat ? "
Jesus-em kiimsiqii , " Anaggutngaasi qayughllak liigikigatasi Akuzitet Igaqegkat , talwa aghtughyaghqaanghillgha Kiyaghneghem .
Tuqukat unguvaghtuuskumeng nengughusaghqaanghitut , yaqulgestun qilagmelngughestun .
Atightiigastegguu Kiyaghneghem apellgha elpesinun tuqukat unguvaghtuutelleghqiitneng ? Whaten pikaaguq ,
' Kiyaghneqaanga Abraham-em , Kiyaghneqaanga Isaac-em , Kiyaghneqaangallu Jacob-em . ' Kiyaghneq Kiyaghneqaat unguvalghiit , nakaan tuqukat . "
Jesus-em apeghtughillgha yulghuteghllaget nagalluku , saghiighayaguteghllakaat .
Pharisees-et nagaqughyamegteki Sadducees-et Jesus-mun nepiighqwaaniluki qerngughutkat .
Ataasim Pharisees-em apeghtughistengan Liilightuusat aapqughaaqaa Jesus anagniilqavigighnaluku .
Whaten aaptekaa , " Apeghtughista , natungaawa angelleghpigaq Liilightuusani ? "
Jesus-em kiimsiqaa , " ' Ataneq Kiyaghneghen piniqsaghqaqan qamaglluku ilugpegun , qamaglluku unguvasighpegun , qamaglluku umyugaghpegun . '
Taana angelleghpigaaguqlu , megnunalleghpigaaguqlu Liilightuusaq .
Tuunglighhaa angelleghpigaq Liilightuusaq sivulightun ayuquq : ' Piniqsaghqaqaten yulguteten piniqelleghpetun elpeneng katam . '
Taakuk Liilightuusak tunemaaguk tamaghhitnun Liilightuusanunllu , apeghtuusiitnunllu uuknaliqistet . "
Taagken Jesus-em aaptekii Pharisees-et qerngughutngamaluki ,
" Naten sumeghtaghaatkaqesteggu Christ-a ? Kitum ighneqagu ? " Kiimsiqaat , " Ighneqaa David-em . "
Jesus-em aaptekii , " Sangan始ngam David-em akuziiqngami Agleghnalghiignekun Taghneghagnekun atightagu , ' Ataneghmeng ' ? Whaten pikaalghii ,
' Atanghem pii Atanqa , Aqumi aghenqignemkun , kenlanga anguyagten itegaghpek asinganun lliightellemnun . '
David-em atiimakagu , ' Ataneghmeng ' naten ighneqagu ? "
Nalighhiiniita Pharisees-et kiimsighpagningitkaat Jesus . Taagken kenlekluku kitum alngunak tetugyagutkaat aapneghmeng .
Taagken Jesus-em pikii yulghutetlu , maligsaaghtenillu ,
" Apeghtughikayugetlu Liilightuusaneng , Pharisees-etlu aqumgaat Moses-em aqumutaakun .
Tamaaken apalluqluku qaatkaqiteki qamaglluki apeghtuusiit elpesinun , iwernga ellngita sallghit maligtegpenaki . Sasqaqiisi naqam ellngita pingigatiit .
Apeghtughillghit Liilightuusaneng piyaqnapigtut yugnun qaatkesaghqaaluteng . Apeghtuusiit uqigtuqastun akmagestun ayuqut akmagtestaqegkangit yugnun , naqamllu talwa ataasighhaq ighneghwaaghteng atuqigataat kayusiinnaluki akmagitneng .
" Qamaglluki pinitun pilleteng piiqiit esghaghsaqnaluki yugnun . Tallimegteggunllu qagumegteggunllu qillghutaqiit pateghtaaghalluki salngawaaghhaat Akuzitneng Igaqegkaneng imalget , qaaslimengllu qughalkutiit taakluki ulimaaqiit .
Neqenghaghqemmi , aqumyuneghtuut aangwaaghughtekat aqumutiitgun , synagogue-nillu tawatelngughteggun aqumyuneghtuut .
Quulvaghtesugaqut akilpegaghvigni , atiisqesugaqutlu , ' Apeghtughistemeng ' .
Iwernga elpesi atightestegpenasi , ' Apeghtughistemeng ' qayughllak ataasiiguq Apeghtughistezi , anglegutkullghiistun ayuqusi .
Kina alngunak atighpenaan , ' Atameng ' nunami whani , qayughllak ataasiiguq Atazi qilagmelnguq .
Talwa kitumun alngunak atightestegpenasi , ' Igleghutistemeng ' qayughllak ataasiiguq igleghutistezi , Christ-anguuq .
Taana angelleghpigaq qepghaghtekaghqaqaghsi .
Kina alngunak ellmineng anglistekumi qusevegtesaghqaaguq , enkaam kina alngunak ellmineng qusevegtekumi anglistellengyaghqaaguq .
" Iwernga seghleghwaaghunaqnguusi elpesi apeghtughikayugni Liilightuusaneng , Pharisees-enillu ! Piniiyugneghuusi ! Uumgutaqasi iteghnaqelghiit Ataneghpagullghanun Qilagem . Elpesi katam iitghigatusi , aghuliightaqasillu iteghyulghiit !
" Seghleghwaaghunaqnguusi elpesi apeghtughikayugni Liilightuusaneng , Pharisees-enillu ! Piniiyugneghuusi ! Esghaghlaataquluki ugingighat mangteghiighaqasi . Taagken pinighnilusi pisqellusi taakluku yughaghaqusi . Tamaaken apalluqluku aghyuullengeghllagyaghqaagusi !
" Seghleghwaaghunaqnguusi elpesi apeghtughikayugni Liilightuusaneng , Pharisees-enillu ! Piniiyugneghuusi ! Igleghaaqusi kelliikunllu , quutkunllu ivaghnaluku ataasiq yuuk ugpeghhnnaluku elpesistun . Taagken apeghtuusasi ugpeqegkaki apeghtuusaghpesi aglaghtesaghqaaghlleqaa hell-mun , enkaam elpesi aghyuulleghpesineng malghughqengngaan aghyuullengyaghqaaguq !
" Seghleghwaaghunaqnguusi elpesi , ayaakani igleghutisteni ! Apeghtughiiqusi whaten , ' Kina whaten pikumi , " Akeqiinga Temple-kun " taana pitngunghituq . Iwernga kina whaten pikumi , " Akeqiinga gold-ngakun Temple-em " piyaghqapestaaqaa akequsani ' .
Elpesi ayaakani temngitwhasteni ! Nalikek megnunaghataghaghtak , gold-a , nalighmeng Temple-a agleghnaghtestilghii gold-meng ?
Apeghtughiiqusillu whaten , ' Kina whaten pikumi , " Akeqiinga aghqefigegnekun " , taana pitngunghituq . Iwernga kina whaten pikumi , " Akeqiinga tunusakun aghqefigegnilngughqun , " piyaghqapestaaqaa akequsani . '
Ayaangaghhaalek elpesi ! Nalikek megnunaghataghaghtak , tunusaq nalighmeng aghqefigek agleghnaghtestilghiik tunusameng ?
Enkaangam kina akeqikumi aghqefigegnekun , akeqinguuq taaggunllu sakunllu tamaghhaakun aghqefigegnilngughqun .
Kinallu akeqikumi Temple-kun , akeqinguuq taaggunllu kiyaghlleghhiikunllu tawani .
Kinallu akeqikumi qilagkun , akeqinguuq Kiyaghneghem aqumutagkenkunllu aqumgalghiikunllu tawani .
" Seghleghwaaghunaqnguusi elpesi apeghtughikayugni Liilightuusaneng , Pharisees-enillu ! Piniiyugneghuusi ! Kiyaghneghmun tuunaqasi qulaghqellghi neqmun neqnighsaatet , mint-et , dill-et , cummin-et . Iwernga avelghaghaqasi apeghtuusat megnunaghataghalghiit Liilightuusanilnguut katam : taniillghitelleq , nangllegtalleq , ataasiighmetelleq . Taakut atughqaqsaghasi avelghafqiita ilangillu Liilightuusat .
Ayaakani igleghutisteni ! Yugtun ayuqusi nguuyngaaghaq meghyaghqamineng iqilluku taagken camel-a tuufleqaa !
" Seghleghwaaghunaqnguusi elpesi apeghtughikayugni Liilightuusaneng , Pharisees-enillu ! Piniiyugneghuusi ! Qayuusisillu sagnesillu qaayngi sangigtaqasi , naqam imighngaat wayaghniiqaghpesinengllu , pakigniilleghpesinengllu .
Ayaangalghii Pharisee ! Sivuklukek sangigtikek ilungik qayuusimllu sagneghemllu enkaam qaaskulluteklu ukmangiillik !
" Seghleghwaaghunaqnguusi apeghtughikayugni Liilightuusaneng , Pharisees-enillu ! Piniiyugneghuusi ! Tuqukat salngagistun ayuqusi piineqegkat qatelghiimeng . Esghaqaaluteng qaayngi pinighhalek , iwernga qama imaqut neghqughrugmengllu aghulleghmengllu .
Elpesillu tawatetusi . Qayegpesineng pinighsugnighllaget , iwernga ilugpesini piniiyugneghuusi , apeghtuutkasi Liilightuusat atuqigatasi . "
" Seghleghwaaghunaqnguusi elpesi apeghtughikayugni Liilightuusaneng , Pharisees-enillu ! Piniiyugneghuusi ! Mangteghasqwaangllaghaqasi lliivghitgun uuknaliqistet , pinighnaghsaghaqasillu lliivghit tamaakut kiyaghtekat elqughulluteng Kiyaghneghmun .
Taagken whatenllu piiqusi , ' Neghighluku kiyaghtekaayaqumta sivunemnni , tuququlgusighnayanghitngwaaghaput uuknaliqisteneng ' .
Tawaten akuzilleghpesigun liigikestusi , kingunqennilusi tuququghtengitnun uuknaliqistet .
Enkaam saaqetsi sivuneghpesi piinliqaat apeghiighteggu .
Nemeghyani elpesi , avaqutiitni nemeghyat ! Kiyaghneghem nanqigtekangisi aghyuughyaghqaanilusi , naten anagnaqesteggu aghyuulleghqaghsi hell-mi ?
Enkaam ungipaatamsi kayagfikamsi uuknaliqistenengllu , liisimalghiinengllu , apeghtughistenengllu . Ilangit tuququghlleqasi , ilangit qaquuraghlleqasi , enkaam ilangit synagogue-egpesini kagsagmiglleqasi , ilangit town-eneng ilangitnun malighqughlleqasi .
Tamaaken apalluqluku elpesi Kiyaghneghem aghyuughyaghqaqiisi tuququllghitnun qamaglluki kiyaghtekat elqughulluteng Kiyaghneghmun nunami whani , Abel-meng Zechariah-mun , ighnegha Barachiah-m . Tuqutkaghsi akulegkeni Temple-emllu aghqefigemllu .
Ipa ungipaatamsi , elpesi unguvalghiini maaten Kiyaghneghem aghyuughyaghqaqiisi tamaakunun seghletun pilleghnun !
" Kaay , Jerusalem , Jerusalem ! Tuququqaqaten uuknaliqistet , milughpagaataghlukillu tuququqaten kayagtekanka elpenun . Uglaapiglluku qerngughsugaqsaghanka yugten whangamnun , katam qawaagem qerngughtellghatun amaaghaghhani yaqugmi asinganun , iwernga tawaten pistesugumangitaghpenga .
Enkaangam mangteghan paaghqiilleqaa .
Ungipaatamsi , whaken kenlekluku esghaghnaanghitaghpesinga alla kenlanga whaten pilleghpesinun , ' Kiyaghneghem quyasligu tagilghii aatghakun Atanghem . ' "
Jesus aanluni Temple-meng aghulaqumaluku maligsaaghtengita takuluku kelgutkiit mangteghat Temple-em pingi .
Pikii , " Esghaghasi tamaakut mangteghat . Ipa piimsi , talwa ataasiq uyghak nemininnaanghituq . Qamaglluteng ulleghqughyaghqaagut . "
Jesus aqumyan Mount Olives-kun , maligsaaghtengita takuluku ellnginaghhaamaaghluteng aaptekaat , " Ungipaatikut , qakun tamaakut piyaghqaawat ? Sangulleqa liisimakusighqaghput tagilleghqaghpenun , nunamllu iqugtelleghqaanun ? "
Jesus-em kiimsiqii , " Kelengalusi , kitumun alngunak puughtestegpenasi .
Qayughllak uglaapiglleghhii tagiyaghqaaguq atuqluku aatqa , whaten piiqluteng , ' Whanga Christ-anguunga ' , puughqughtaayaghqaqaatlu yulghun .
Nagaquullequsi pilluwaneng , akusqaghtaatkellghitnengllu pilluwat ; alingegpenasi qayughllak tamaana piyaghqaaguq . Iwernga salin iquggnaqngunghituq .
Nunat yugit pillugutullequt , ataneghpagullghetlu pillugutullequt , nani alngunak neqangisagllagllequq , nunat uvelegtaghllagllequt .
Qamaglluni tamaana aghnam ighniyukestallghatun ayuqellequq .
" Taagken tamaana pimaluku yuget tugulleqiisi , amyuqetaatkelleqiisi , tuqulleqiisillu . Nunataghhaan tamaghhaan ramkengan ugumiilleqiisi whanga apalluqlunga .
Enkaam uglaapiglleghhiim ugpeqnanighlleqaatnga , uveghpagutusagullequt , ugumiisagullequtlu .
Taagken uuknaliqistesighwaalghutet tagiluteng puughqughlleqiit yulghutet .
Seghleq nulam angtalanganeng apalluqluku allulluteng yuget piniqinanighllequt .
Iwernga kina alngunak nuqenneghtuqaq kenlemun yugulillengyaghqaaguq .
Ukutlu Pinilghiit Ungipat Kiyaghneghem Ataneghpagullghaneng ayuqelghiit ungipaqsaghqaagut nunataghhaani tamaghhaani ramkengitnun nagaqiisqelluki . Taagken nuna iqugllequq . "
" Yeqay atightughtem liigikligu sameng pisiitanga uuknaliqistem Daniel-em uuknaliqutkegkaa . Uuknaliqutkegkaa taana agleghniilnguuguq paaghqiitestilghii agleghnalghiimi nemi . Esghaqufsigu tesqamani nekevelghii ,
Judea-melnguut anagniighhaat naayghanun .
Yuuk mangtegham qaaynganilnguq ukigluni saghyaqufqaami pilghaaq .
Yuuk piitesiighaghvigmelnguq qaaslighqufqaami pilghaaq .
Tamaani aghneghni seghleghwaaghunaqnguut qumilget aghnat , mamaghtalgetlu !
Yughaghtek anagniifqaafsi uksumi pisqellusi nalighmeng Sabbath-mi ,
qayughllak tamaani seghleliiq elngaatall seghleghllagughsaghqaaguq . Seghleghataghaayaghqaaguq seghleliighaqelleghneng ima piinlighyuggaallghaneng nunam whavemun kenlanga . Allamengllu tawatelnguq pinaanghitngwaaghtuq .
Tamaakut aghneghet Kiyaghneghem palallimangisaqaki , kina alngunak unguvanayanghituq . Iwernga apalluqluki nakmikegkani aghneghet palalliyaghqaqii .
" Tamaani kitum alngunak pikangisi , ' Ii-i , Christ-a whaa ' , nalighmeng , ' Tazingantuq ! ' ugpeqegpenaan ,
qayughllak Christ-asighwaaghetlu , uuknaliqistesighwaaghetlu tagillequt . Allaaghlluwhaghtighllagllequt , saghiighanaghqeghllagllequtlu puughhnaluki yuget , talwa Kiyaghneghem nakmikegkii puughsaqlegukumegteki .
Taawa ungipaatamsi sivutghulluku pilleghqaq .
" Enkaangam whaten pikangisi , ' Ii-i , Christ-a paaghqillghanituq ! ' takugpenaan ; nalighmeng whaten pikata , ' Ii-i , mangtegham ilunganituq ' , ugpeqegpenaki .
Qayughllak Ighnegha Yugem tagikumi tawatesaghqaaguq nighugpaguutelleghtun kuukgullequq asivaghmeng pakfallamun .
" Qawaagpaget qerngughtaqut nani alngunak kemegqwaalgunghani .
" ' Kingungiighhiitneng tamaakut seghleliilleghllaget Kiyaghneghem siqineq mamlegtesleqaa , tanqiq nighugunnanightesleqaa , ighaleqetaaghet ifkaquutesleqii qilagameng , aghtughyaghqaanghillghet qilagamelnguut igleghallghit allangughquutesleqii . '
" Taagken qilagakun sangwaa allgeghllequq liisimakusighqaq Ighneghaneng Yugem . Taagken qamagtengngwaaghluteng nunam ramkengi qivghum qiyaaghuuteghllagllequt . Esghaghlleqaat Ighnegha Yugem tagilghii qilagwaaghteggun , aghtughyaghqaanghilleghtuumaghmillu nighughqellelighllaglunillu .
Enkaam Ighneghan Yugem qalghightaan qalghightesteghllakumigu kayaglleqii yaquleni navek alngunak qerngughtesqelluki nakmikegkani nunataghhaaneng tamaghhaaneng .
" Liitfikiteggu uqfiga figs-em . Esghaqufsiki avayii uniilliighalghiit , ququngii piitekestalghiit , liisimakaghsi kiigyaghtungestaghaa .
Tawateghpigaq qamagtengngwaaghluki aapqanka tamaakut esghaqufsiki , liisimakelleqaghsi ellnga kaasaghtungestaamaaq , aaqun amigmun lliighumaaq .
Ipa ungipaatamsi , maaten unguvalghiit tuqulaghaatestegpenaki qamaglluteng tamaakut piyaghqaagut .
Qilagallu , nunallu aviighusaghqaaguk , iwernga whanga akuzitenka aviighunnaanghitut .
" Kitum alngunak nallukaa taam aghneghem aflunga qakun kaasaghqaatanga . Talwa qilagmelnguut yaqulget nallukaat , Ighneghemllu nallukaa , Atanginaghhaam liisimakaa .
Katam tamaani Noah-m kiyaghtellghani , yuget tawatesaghqaagut Ighneghan Yugem tagilleghqaani .
Tamaani aghneghni , sivungani ulevem yuget neghaqluteng , meghaqluteng , nengughutaqluteng ayuqegkat kenlanga tawavek aghneghmun Noah-nkut itellghitnun ark-mun .
Nallukegkaat natesaghqaatanga kenlanga ulevelleghmun , enkaam qamagtengngwaaghluteng tuqulaghaatkat . Tawateghpigaq Ighnegha Yugem tagikan , nallukelleqaat natesaghqaatanga .
Tawani pilleghmi maalghuk yugek piitesiighaghvigmegni qepghaatek , aallgha tugulleqaa , ilanga uneglleqaa .
Aghnak kagimtilghiik grain-meng , aallgha tugulleqaa , ilanga uneglleqaa .
" Enkaangam kelengalusi , qayughllak nallukngwaaghaghsi nani aghneghmi Ataneghpesi tagilleghqaa .
Nalluneqniituq , mangtegham yugan liisimaksaqumigu teglegniightem tagilleghqaa , qavaghpenani kelenganayaghtuq naafqulluni iteghnayukan mangteghaminun .
Enkaam tamaaken apalluqluku elpesillu apeghiighsaghlusi quunpeng , qayughllak Ighnegha Yugem tagiyaghqaaguq waakenghillghaghllusi .
" Kinangaawa ataasiighmelnguq peghqinelghii qepghaghta ? Taananguuq umiilgan igleghutistengllaqaa qepghaghtelgutanganun , neqelitaatiisqellukillu aghhutanga tamaghhaan .
Taana qepghaghta quyastellengyaghqaaguq umiilgan kaalluni esghaqumigu qelelleghmitun pilghii .
Ipa ungipaatamsi , taana qepghaghta umiilgan aflengakistengllaghyaghqaqaa saminun tamaghhaanun .
Iwernga taana qepghaghta seghleghukumi sumeghtaghaghllequq whaten , ' Umiilka tagilghaghtughnaanghituq ' ,
enkaam amyuutkesagulleqii qepghaghtelgutni . Ilallequqlu suumelghiinun , neghelgusighaqluki , meghelgusighaqluki lliighllequq .
Taagken ataasimi aghneghmi umiilga kaallequq qepghaghta yataaghqellghillukullu , sighimakellghillukullu .
Enkaam umiilgan qevuulluku aghyuughlleqaa , aglaghtesleqaa piniiyugneghnun aghyuughyaghqaaluku maligulluku . Tawani qiyiqellequt , gguteteng terqitaagtaamiita .
" Tawani pilleghmi Ataneghpagullgha Qilagem uspusaghqaaguq qulaghyagnun aghnaghaghnun kelqelluki kenelghutateng paayghilghiit nulightughnaqelghiimeng .
Tallimat nalluuqat tallimat peghqinelghiit .
Nalluuqat kelqegkiit kenelghutateng uqughqangunaki ,
iwernga peghqinelghiit kelqegkiit kenelghutateng uqughqalighluki .
Nulightughnaqelghii muluuqaq , qenwat aghnaghaat qavaghnikat enkaam qavatghutkat .
" Unugem qukaani kina akilghuukaq whaten , ' Uka tagiiquq nulightughyaghqaq ! Aanlusi payeghteggu ! '
Aghnaghaat taghtughaghtaalluteng kenelghutateng kenghit nallghusaqiit .
Taagken nalluuqat pikat peghqinelghiinun , ' Uqughqalitaghtikut , kenelghutaput qaamnaqut . '
Peghqinellghita pikiit , ' Seghleghhalek tamaghhamnnun uqughqapagitukut , akilpegaghtenun tukfighiyaghtughtek . '
Enkaam nalluuqat uqughqangyaghtuutkat . Aviisimaluki nulightughnaqelghii kaatkaq . Taakut yataaghqengngalghiit itelgusiqaat nengughutem neqenghaghqellghanun , enkaam amik uumkaat .
" Kingunganeng nalluuqat aghnaghaat kaalluteng , akilghuukat , ' Ataneq , Ataneq ! Qelpeghutaghtikut ! '
Iwernga nulightughnaqelghiim kiimsiqii , ' Ipa ungipaatamsi , nallukamsi kinkungutsi . ' "
Jesus-em ungipaghaatni taaqniqaa whaten , " Enkaangam kelengatek , qayughllak nallukaghsi natungutanga aghneq nalighmeng natungutanga aflu Ighneghan Yugem tagilleghqaa .
" Ataneghpagullgha Qilagem uspusaghqaaguq whavek ungipaghaatmun : Taawanguq yuuk igleghanaqelghii navek uyavanun . Tuqluqii qepghaghteni aviilleghmini aflengakistenguluki saghyaminun .
Ataasimun 5,000 manit tuunegkii , ilanganun 2,000 , kingulighmun 1,000 . Tamaghhiita tunquqii pillegtulngistun . Taagken aghulaqegkaq .
Yuuk taana 5,000-nengegkaq , tawaninginaq aghulaqluni akiksaghqameng tukfightuqaq . Enkaam alla 5,000 allgeghtekaa .
Taanallu 2,000-nengegkaq , allgeghutkaq alla 2,000-meng .
Iwernga taana 1,000-nengegkaq aanluni laagulluki iiqii umiilegmi maningi .
" Muluughllagluni qepghaghtet umiilgat uteghnighyami ungipaghsuqii samatangi manini .
5,000-nengegkam esnevaghluni pikaa , ' Umiilemni , tagivaqaqaten 5,000 manit . Taawa alla 5,000 allgeghsimaaqaa . '
Umiilgan pikaa , ' Seghleghhalek itagnapigtuten , pinightuten ataasiighmelnguq qepghaghta ! Ataasiighmetkaategpeneng palaghhaghnun aflengakistengughtesnaqamken uglalghiinun . Iitghi quyalgusighyaghtughnga ! '
Taagken 2,000-nengegkam esnevaghluni pikaa , ' Umiilemni , tagivaqaqaten 2,000 manit . Taawa alla 2,000 allgeghsimaaqa . '
Umiilgan pikaa , ' Seghleghhalek itagnapigtuten , pinightuten ataasiighmelnguq qepghaghta ! Ataasiighmetkaategpeneng palaghhaghnun aflengakistengughtesnaqamken uglalghiinun . Iitghi quyalgusighyaghtughnga ! '
Taagken 1,000-nengegkam esnevaghluni pikaa , ' Umiilemni , liisimakamken elpek aaghsaghqaanghituten . Unataghaquten piitesighaqaqenghilkegpeneng . Qerngughtaqaten piitkat piitutngit ifkaghquqaqenghilketeng .
Enkaam alinglunga laagulluki maniten iiqaqanka . Ang , taawa elpek pin . '
Iwernga umiilgan pikaa , ' Uyuq seghleq , ighsanitalghii qepghaghta ! Elpek piighpenga unataghaqnilunga piitesighaqaqenghilkemneng , qerngughtiiqnilungallu piitkaneng piitutngit ifkaghquqaqenghilkemneng .
Sangan始ngam manika kanaghhnanighsigu bank-amun ? Tawaten pikaqsaquvgu , uteghnillemni veghhnayaghaqa allgeghnelighluku . '
Taagken umiilgem qepghaghteni pikii , ' Tuguluku 1,000 maninga , tuuniteggu taamun 10,000-nelegmun .
Tamaakut pilget tuunataghaghyaghqaagut enkaam siiptiillequt . Iwernga taana avangilnguq pillgaayaghngaan iqisaghqaqiit ellnganeng . '
Taagken umiilgem pikii , ' Aanesteggu taana satngunghilnguq qepghaghta qagavek mamlegllagmun . Tawaani yuget qiyaaghwaghllagllequt , ggutetengllu terqitaagtaamiita . '
" Ighnegha Yugem tagikumi nighughqelleghmikun , yaqulegtuumaghllagmi , taagken aqumellequq nighughqengngalghiignekun aqumutagmikun .
Sivungakun qerngughutesleqiit qamagtengngwaaghluki nunam yugi . Taagken avughlleqii , katam penniighniightem avullghatun penniighet goat-neng .
Penniighet aghenqigneghminitesleqii , goat-et saghumigneghmini .
Taagken Umiilgem aghenqigneghminilnguut pilleqii , ' Tagitek , Atama quyastekiitni , piliiteggu Ataneghpagulleq yataaghqegkaq elpesinun ima nuna ulimaaqngan .
Iyatiqngulunga neghqegkaqaghpesinga ; meqsugulunga meghsikaqaghpesinga ; allaneghtaalunga upughatkaqaghpesinga .
Amsikaghmellunga aasightuqaqaghpesinga , qinuyugulunga laalighfikegkaqaghpesinga , anusimingllaghaalunga esghaghyaghtuqaqaghpesinga . '
Taagken elqughutngalghiit pilleqaat , ' Ataneq , qavngaq iyatiqnguluten neghesiken , nalighmeng meqsuguluten meghsiziken ?
Qavngaq allaneghtaaluten upughasiken , nalighmeng amsikaghmelluten aasightughsiken ?
Qavngaq qinuyuguluten , nalighmeng anusimingllaghvigmelluten laalighfiksiken ? '
Umiilgem kiimsighlleqii , ' Ipapestaaq ungipaatamsi , sangwaa alngunak pikaghsi ukalighpigaghnun anglegutemnun , whangamnun piiqasi ! '
" Taagken Umiilgem saghumigneghminilnguut pilleqii , ' Elpesinguut Kiyaghneghem aghyuughyaghqii . Awiitek whangamneng , aglaghtek kenlengilnguugnun kenghegnun Kiyaghneghem yataaghqegkaanun Tughneghaghmunllu , yaqulganunllu !
Iyatiqngulunga neghestellghitaghpesinga , meqsugulunga meghsillghitaghpesinga ,
allaneghtaalunga upughatellghitaghpesinga , amsikaghmellunga aasightuumangitaghpesinga . Qinuyugulungallu , anusimingllaghvigmellungallu laalighfikumangitaghpesinga . '
Taagken pilleqaat , ' Ataneq , qavngaq iyatiqnguluten , meqsuguluten , allaneghtaaluten , amsikaghmelluten , qinuyuguluten , nalighmeng anusimingllaghvigmelluten , kayusiisimangisiken ? '
Taagken Umiilgem kiimsighlleqii , ' Ipapestaaq ungipaatamsi , tawaten pinghitelleghpesistun nalighhiiniitnun ukut ukalighpigaat , whanga pinghitaqaghpesinga . '
Enkaam taakut aglaghllequt kenlengilngughmun aghyuulleghmun , iwernga elqughutngalghiit aglaghllequt kenlengilngughmun unguvalleghmun . "
Jesus-em taaqsamiki apeghtuusaqneghmeng tamaakut , maligsaaghteni pikii ,
" Liisimakaghsi maalghuk aghneghek atughlukek Neqenghaghqelleghqaa Passover-em pinaqnguuq . Enkaam Ighnegha Yugem tuunelleqaat qaquuriisqelluku . "
Tawani aghneghmi , chief priest-etlu , siivanlleghetlu qerngughutkat palace-ngani High Priest-em , Caiaphas-em .
Agghitkegkaat Jesus aksaqluklu tuguluku , tuqunnaluku .
Iwernga pikat , " Neqenghaghqemmi pinaanghitaghput , luuraq yuget seghleliighqiighllagnayukata . "
Jesus Bethany-metaqngami Simon-enkunitkaq leprosy-lguyalghiimi .
Aghnam takukaa Jesus , tugumiiqlukek alabaster-ek aqimleghutak imalgek akitupiglleghhiimeng tepengllaasimeng . Neghumaluku naasqwakun kuuvegkakek tepengllaasik .
Iwernga maligsaaghtet esghaghluku tawaten pilghii , ugumiyagutkaat whaten pimaghmeng , " Sangan sakusiiqakek ?
Akikegkaqsaqumikek tepengllaasik maningutkeghllaglukek aklumalghiinun tunqughnayaghaa ! "
Jesus-em liisimakluki sameng pitangi pikii , " Sangan seghlequughesteggu aghnaq ? Piniipigtuq whangamnun tawaten pillgha .
Aklumalghiit quunpeng tamaansaghqaagut , iwernga whanga quunpeng elpesininnaanghitunga .
Tepengllaghqelleghmikun yugusiqa yataaghqengngwaa llivelleghqamnun .
Ipa ungipaatamsi , nunataghhaani tamaghhaani nani alngunak una Pinilghii Ungipaq ungipaqneghmegteggu , aghnam tawaten pillgha aapghaqelleqaat yugnun neqamikesqelluku . "
Taagken Judas Iscariot ilangat qula maalghuk siipneqluku maligsaaghtet , chief priest-enun piluni ,
aaptekii , " Sameng tuunelleqestengnga Jesus elpesinun tuunegkumkun ? " Enkaam kestulluku 30 silver manimeng llivikegkaat .
Taagken kenlekluku Judas pilleghqangnaqegkaq uveghpagunnaluku Jesus .
Sivulighmi aghneghani Neqenghaghqellghan Yeast-alillghillnguum Neqekrangllam , maligsaaghtet Jesus takuluku aaptekaat , " Nani yataaghqutesugsin whangkunnun Passover-em Neqenghaghqellghaneng neghesqelluten ? "
Jesus-em kiimsiqii , " Jerusalem-emun pitek . Yuuk tamaantuq ; ungipaannakesi , ' Apeghtughista piiq , Pilleghqaqa kaannaquq . Maligsaaghtekullghiini neghnaqaghput Passover-em Neqenghaghqellgha elpesini . ' "
Maligsaaghtet Jesus-em pisqellghatun pikat , Passover-em Neqenghaghqellgha yataaghqegkaat .
Ighivgaghyagu Jesus-enkut qula maalghuk siipneqluku maligsaaghtekullghiit tipelngi aqumuutkat neghnaluteng .
Neghuusimaluki , Jesus-em pikii , " Ipa piimsi , nalighpesi uveghpagunnaqngwaanga . "
Maligsaaghtet qivghughllagumaghmeng tuungliqutaghluteng aaptaataqaat , " Ataneq , whangangwaa ? "
Jesus-em kiimsiqii , " Uveghpagutiyaghqaq taananguuq neqni neptekanga sagneghmun whangamnun maligulluni .
Ipapestaaq Ighnegha Yugem tuquyaghqaaguq Akuzitet Igaqegkat pinaqnillghistun . Iwernga seghleghwaaghunaqnguuq taana yuuk uveghpagutilghii Ighneghaneng Yugem ! Itagnaghnayaghtuq allgeghumangisaqumi ! "
Uveghpagutistem Judas-em aaptekaa , " Apeghtughista , whangangwaa ? " Jesus-em pikaa , " Taawa elpeneng apeghtuten . "
Neghuutnguluteng Jesus-em tuguluku neqekrangllaq iyamsiqayugvikluku Kiyaghneq , aavgughluku tunquqii maligsaaghteni . Pikii , " Tuguluku neghiteggu , una yugusiqaqa . "
Taagken tuguluku qayuusiq wine-meng imalek iyamsiqayugvikluku Kiyaghneq tuunegkaa ellngitnun . Pikii , " Meghvikaataghteggu qamagllusi .
Taana aakwaqa , taaggun Kiyaghneghem akequsaa apeghiighyaghqaaguq . Tuqukuma aakwa kuuvellequq uglapiglleghhiinun yugnun seghevutusiiluni seghleghqellghitnun .
Ungipaatamsi , wine-meng alla meghnaanghitunga kenlanga aghneghmi tawani , wine-eghraghaghmeng meghelgusighlleqamsi Atama Ataneghpagullghani . "
Taagken ilagaghluteng aanluteng Mount Olives-mun pikat .
Taagken Jesus-em pikii , " Unugmi whani , whanga apalluqlunga uniqaghaalleqaghpesinga , qayughllak Akuzitni Igaqegkani Kiyaghneq pikaaguq , ' Tuqulleqaqa penniighniighta enkaam penniighet mingiqellequt . '
Iwernga unguvaghtestekanganga tuqulleghmeng sivugpesini aglaghllequnga Galilee-mun . "
Peter-em pikaa Jesus , " Apalluqluten elpek qaywa ilama uniqaghaateghngaaten , whanga uninnaanghitngwaaghamken ! "
Jesus-em pikaa , " Ipa ungipaatamken , unukun rooster-a qalghightestegpenaan , pingayuneng ketwell nallunqelleqaghpenga . "
Peter-em pikaa , " Qaywa tuqumalgusighyaghngaamken , nallunqennaanghitamken . " Maligsaaghtetlu qamaglluteng ungipaatkaat tawaten .
Taagken Jesus-enkut maligsaaghtekullghiit kaatkat tawavek atilqelghiimeng Gethsemane-meng . Pikii , " Aqumuutek taaggun , ingavek yughaghyaghtuumalunga . "
Tazingavek kelqegkii , Peter , Zebedee-mllu ighneghqek . Taagken qivghughllagemllu seghleliighemllu kaatekestaqaa ,
enkaam pikii , " Qaamnaka qivghughllaguuq , repall tuquyaghqaaghllunga . Tawanllusi kelengalgusightengnga . "
Tazingapighqaaghluni nunamun sikmuulluni yughaqaq , " Atamni , piyaghqaakan , meghenghillanga whaken qayuusimeng ; iwernga nakaan piyukellemtun , elpek piyukelleghpetun pigu . "
Taagken Jesus-em takuyaqminiki pingayut maligsaaghteni qavaaftut . Enkaam Peter pikaa , " Kelengalgusighpagningitestengngaa ataasiq aflu ?
Kelengatek , yughaghtek nanghiiqullengenghitesqellusi . Ipaapestaaq taghneghak piyaghqaaghngaaghmek , iwerngaqun yugusiq kayaatuq . "
Allameng Jesus tazingavek aglaghluni yughaqaq , " Atamni , meghyaghqaqngukumkun una qayuusiq elpek piyukelleghpetun apeghiighli . "
Takunqigsaqminiki maligsaaghteni , taawa qavaatnguftut , qayughllak qavam sakniqestekangi .
Jesus-em unillaataghluki , tazingani pingayiqii yughalleni taakut ataasit yughat atuqluki .
Taagken maligsaaghteni takuluki pikii , " Taawa qavaawaqetsii , meghnaaliiqetsii ? Taawa aflu kaatuq , Ighnegha Yugem uveghpagusaghqaaghtuq seghleghqestenun .
Nekevitek , igleghtelta . Ii-i , uka uveghpagutisteka . "
Jesus paninang akuzimaluku , Judas kaatkaq , qula maalghuk siipneqluku maligsaaghtet ilangat . Yulghutet maligtekaat , ilangi savigpalighluteng , ilangi anagutalighluteng . Chief priest-etlu , siivanlleghetlu kayagtekiit maligtesqelluku Judas .
Uveghpagutistem Judas-em kaatfagilgameng ilani salleghqamineng ungipaatkaqegkangi , " Yuuk naaghyaghqaqa ellnganguuq piyukegkaghsi . Tugunakesi . "
Judas-em takwaaghaghlluku Jesus pikaa , " Seghleghhalek , Apeghtughista ! " Taagken naaqaa .
Jesus-em pikaa , " Ilakumtaamni , aga saaqsin pilleghqan pigu ! " Taagken takuluku Jesus akuqaghluku nuqneghteqaat .
Tawani naliita yuget Jesus-melnguut savigpani nusugluku kepqaghtekaa sigutnga High Priest-em qepghaghtelaaghan .
Taagken Jesus-em pikaa , " Savigpagen kanaghtigu qantanun , qayughllak qamaglluteng savigpagmeng atuqilghiit savigpagkun tuqusaghqaagut .
Sumeghpenii-i Ataka kayutengllaghnaanghinniluku piziguu ? Aaptekumkun tawaninginaq 72,000-eneng uglalghiit yaqulelghuteghllaget pilluwaghtet kayaggnayaghii .
Iwernga tawaten pinaanghitunga qayughllak Akuzitet Igaqegkat apeghiighyaghqaalghiit igaqelleghmegestun . "
Taagken Jesus-em yulghutet pikii , " Tuguyaghtughestengngaa savigpagtuumaghpesi , anagutaghtuumaghpesi , nikimqun wayaghniightestun ayuqlunga ? Aghhutanga tamaghhaan aqumlunga apeghtughiiqunga Temple-mi tugungigataghpesinga .
Iwernga qamaglluteng tamaakut tawaten pinguut , apeghiighnaluki uuknaliqistet igaqegkiit Akuzitni Igaqegkani . " Taagken qamaglluteng maligsaaghtet unilluku qimaguutkat .
Taagken Jesus-em tugustengita aglaatkaat High Priest-em , Caiaphas-em , mangteghaanun . Tawani apeghtughikayuget Liilightuusaneng , siivanlleghetlu qerngughutkat .
Uyavaqaanlluni Peter-em maligtekaa courtyard-nganun High Priest-em mangteghaan . Iteghluni aqumelgusiqii kelengakistet esghapagnaluku Jesus sayaghqaatangat .
Chief priest-etlu , qamagllutengllu agghistet iqlengiqutkestengnaqutkegkat Jesus tuqutestepigesnaghnaluku .
Iwernga naalkunneghmeng aghtuqat . Qaywa uglalghiim esnevaghaqluteng aapghaataghyaghngaaghmegteggu aapqiit allakutkat . Qenwatlu yugek esnevaghlutek
pikak , " Una yuuk whaten pikaaguq , ' Temple-a naafqesaqlegwaaqa enkaam nekefleqaqa pingayani aghneghem . ' "
Taagken High Priest-em nekevluni aaptekaa Jesus , " Sameng piyaghqiisiin yugek apellghegkenun ? "
Iwernga Jesus qaalkaamangilnguq . Enkaam High Priest-em aaplaataqaa , " Aatghakun Unguvalghiim Kiyaghneghem qelghamken ungipaatikut Christ-anguziin ? Ighneqaten Kiyaghneghem ? "
Jesus-em kiimsiqaa , " Elpek pilleghpetun ayuquq . Iwernga ungipaatamsi , uum kingunganeng esghaghlleqaghsi Ighnegha Yugem aqumluni aghenqigneghakun Aghtughyaghqaanghilnguum , esghaghlleqaghsillu tagilghii qilawaaghitgun qilagam . "
Taagken tawaten piyatni High Priest-em aatkani piiguumiita pikaq , " Una yuuk Kiyaghneghuniluni pilghii ! Alla liisimakistengisaghngaamta pilta . Legan whaa nagataghsi Kiyaghneghunilghii !
Naten elpesi nanqigtesteggu ? " Kiimsiqaat , " Tuqusaghqaaghsimaaq . "
Taagken gginaakun qesiqukaat , tenglugpagaataqaatlu , enkaam qasaghtestengita
pikaat , " Elpek Christ-a uuknaliqutikut ! Kitum tenglugtaten ? "
Tawaten taakut pimaluki courtyard-mi Peter aqumgakaq . Qepghaghtem aghnaghaam takuluku pikaa , " Elpeklu Jesus-metkaaguten , Galilee-ghmiimi . "
Iwernga Peter mesighaqaq sivungitni tamaakut pikaa , " Nallukaqa sameng piiquten . "
Aanyan courtyard-em iteghviganun ilangan qepghaghtem aghnaghaam esghaghluku Peter , tawanlenguut pikii , " Una yuuk Jesus-metkaaguq Nazareth-eghmiimi . "
Peter mesighaghlaataqaq , " Ipapestaaq piimsi , Kiyaghneghem aatghakun nallukngwaaghaqa yuuk . "
Mulunghituq , yuget nekevghataaghullghiit tagiluteng , Peter pikaat , " Ipa ilakaaten Jesus-em malighsaghtengita qayughllak akuzillghen Galilee-ghmiistun ayuquq ! "
Taagken Peter-em pikii , " Ipapestaaq Kiyaghneghem aatghakun ungipaatamsi nallukngwaaghaqa yuuk ! Iqlengiqngukuma Kiyaghneghem aghyuughlinga ! " Tawaninginaq rooster-a qalghiqaq .
Taagken Peter-em neqaatkaa Jesus-em pillgha , " Rooster-a qalghightestegpenaan pingayuneng nallunqelleqaghpenga . " Enkaam aanluni qiyaaghwaghllakaq .
Unaanguluku qamaglluteng chief priest-etlu , siivanlleghetlu agghitkegkaat tuqutesnaluku Jesus .
Enkaam asighqelluku aglaalluku tuunegkaat Pilate-mun , Rome-em governor-nganun .
Uveghpagutistem Judas-em , liigiksaqminiki agghistet nanqigsimakangat Jesus tuqutesaghqaaluku , qemall avuteghqeghllakaq . Enkaam chief priest-enunllu , siivanlleghnunllu veghusaghtuqii 30 silver-et manit .
Pikii , " Seghleghqumaanga uveghpagutellemkun seghleghqumangilnguq yuuk tuqutesqelluku ! " Pikaat , " Whangkunnun sasiilleqa ? Elpek tawaten pilqan ! "
Enkaam Judas-em miluutkii manit Temple-em ilunganun . Taagken aghulaqluni qemitkaq .
Chief priest-et saghnatkelluki manit pikat , " Liilightuusamnni ukut manit kanaghsaghqaanghitut manilghutaanun Temple-em qayughllak llivikuusaqegkaagut tuqutusighqaaluteng yugmun . "
Enkaam agghitkegkaat mani tukfighisiqnaluku nunamun atelqelghii , " Potter始s Field " lliveghvigkaaluku nakuumiinun .
Enkaam whavemun kenlanga taam nunam ateliitkaa , " Nunanga Aawem " .
Neghighluku uuknaliqistem Jeremiah-m uuknaliqutkegkaqii whaten , " Ilangita Israel-eghmiit itagnaqegkaqiit angtalangit 30 silver manit , qayughllak sumeghmeggni tawaten akitutkaniluku pikaat . Taagken taakut manit tukfighisiqegkiit Potter始s Field-mun . Tawaten Atanghem qelqaqaanga . " Jeremiah-m uuknaliqellgha apeghiightestekaqaat chief priest-et tukfighaqngamegteggu Potter始s Field .
Tawani Jesus nekevghalghii sivungakun Rome-em governor-ngan . Governor-em aaptekaa , " Jews-et Umiilkataan ? " Jesus-em kiimsiqaa , " Elpek tawatenniluku piin . "
Iwernga chief priest-etlu , siivanlleghetlu anaggunnighngaatni , sameng pimangitkaq .
Taagken Pilate-em aaptekaa , " Nagasikii qamaglluki anaggunnillghit ? "
Iwernga Jesus-em kiimsiimangilkanga talwa ataasimun anaggunnilleghmun , enkaam governor-a saghiighayugllakaq .
Ayumiitanga tamaghhaan Passover-em Neqenghaghqellghani Rome-em governor-ngan itemutaqaa ataasiq anusimingllaghaq yulghutet nakmikegkaat .
Tamaani pilleghni tamaanteftuq apeghseghuq anusimingllaghaq , aatgha Barabbas .
Enkaam yulghun qerngughsan , Pilate-em aaptekii , " Naliq itemutesugesteggu Barabbas nalighmeng Jesus , atilqelghii Christ-ameng ? "
Pilate-em liisimakngukangi Jews-et igleghutistengita aqinakluku Jesus tagitngukangat ellminun .
Pilate aqumgamaluku nanqigtivigmi , nulighhan ungipaatesaghtuqaa , " Sanaqefqaan taana seghleghqellghilnguq yuuk qayughllak qavanguqegkaqaqa enkaam aghnelqusiq seghleliighusiqaqa . "
Tawaten pimaluku chief priest-etlu , siivanlleghetlu aaghqutaqegkiit yulghutet itemutesqelluku Barabbas , Jesus tuqutesqelluku .
Governor-em aaplaataqii yulghutet , " Naliq itemutesugesteggu elpesinun ? " Kiimsiqaat , " Barabbas ! "
Pilate-em aaptekii , " Sanaqsikun始ngam Jesus atilqelghii Christ-ameng ? " Kiimsiqaat , " Qaquuraghtestigu ! "
Pilate-em aaptekii , " Sangan ? Sangwaa seghleq pikaqagu ? " Iwernga iglagtaaghalluteng akilghuukat , " Qaquuraghtestigu ! "
Pilate liigikluni alla sapagningisami esghaghluki yulghutet seghleliiqestalghiit , tugulukek aghmigusik uughtuqaq sivungitni yulghutet . Taagken pikii , " Whanga avutngitunga tuqutelleghqaanun , elpesi tawaten pistengngwaaghsi ! "
Yulghutem iingunaghhaghmeng akitkaat , " Whangkuta kingunqullghiini avutngullequkut tuqutellghanun . "
Taagken Pilate-em Barabbas itemulluku , enkaam Jesus kagsagmigtesluku tuunegkaa pilluwaghtenun qaquuriisqelluku .
Taagken governor-em pilluwaghtengita aglaatkaat Jesus qerngughtaaghvigmeggnun governor-em mangteghaani . Tawani ilateng qerngughlluki kangllukaat .
Aatkii mataghqughluki , kavirrakegtagneng atkuyaaghegneng aatesfikegkaat .
Taagken sikughllugtuqameng avayameng qaghpangllaghluku naasqwakun aatestekaat . Aghenqigneghanllu iiggakun tugusluku unaghsiighwaq , segesqughquulluteng sivungakun legasiighwaatkegkaat . Pikaat , " Quulvaghamken Umiilgat Jews-et ! "
Taagken qesiquluku , tuguluku unaghsiighwaq naasqwakun anagulqaat .
Legasiighwaatkenneghmeng apeghiighyamegteggu , atkuyaaghqek mataghllukek ellngan katam aatkii aatesquqiit . Taagken qaquuraghyaghtuqaat .
Aanumaluteng neghllagmeng esghaghluku yuuk , Cyrene-eghmii , aatgha Simon , qelqaat uyamigesqelluku Jesus-em qaquuraa .
Kaasameng Golgotha-mun ( Golgotha whaten pisiiguq , " Yugem Naasqwan Nenga " ) ,
pilluwaghtet Jesus-mun tuunegkaat meghesqelluku wine-a sungaghnilngughmeng akumegkaq . Iwernga naasiighluku meghyunghitkaa .
Pilluwaghtet qaquuraghyamegteggu , nengiitkiit aatkii ateghtiiraaghutkaqluki .
Taagken tawani aqumuulluteng kelengakegkaat .
Naasqwan quulngakun nekegtekaat qaquurallghanun apalluq igaqngalghii whaten , UNA JESUS-NGUUQ , UMIILGAT JEWS-ET .
Maalghuklu wayaghniightek qaquuraqagket , aallgha aghenqigneghakun , ilanga saghumigneghakun .
Yuget naghughlleghhiit , legasiighwaatkegkaat Jesus , naasquteng ufsugusimiita
akilghuukaat , " Elpek pikaaguten Temple-a naafqennaqniluku enkaam pingayuni aghneghni nekefneqiggnaqniluku . Kiyaghneghem Ighneqngukangaten elpeneng katam yuguli , qaquurameng ukigi ! "
Tawateghpigaq Chief priest-et , maligulluteng apeghtughikayugnun Liilightuusaneng , siivanlleghnunllu , legasiighwaatkegkaat ,
" Yuguliiqii ilangi , naqam ellmineng katam yugulipagningituq ! Umiilgukuni Israel-eghmiinun ukigli qaquuramineng enkaam ugpeqnayaghaghput .
Neghyukngwaa Kiyaghneq , piiquqlu Kiyaghneghmun Ighneqniluni . Kiyaghneghem piyukngukumigu yuguliligu maaten . "
Qaquuralgutegkenkallu wayaghniightek legasiighwaatkegkaak .
Taagken qamaglluni nuna mamleghqwaakaq aghneghem qukaaneng kenlanga three-klaagmun .
Tamani nani three-klaagmi Jesus akilghuughllakaq whaten , " Eli , Eli , lama sabachthani ? " Whaten pisiq , " Kiyaghnemni , Kiyaghnemni , sangama unisinga ? "
Ilangita yuget tawanlenguut nekevghallghiit nagalluku pikat , " Uum yugem Elijah tuqlughaghaa . "
Tawaninginaq yuuk ataasiq aqfaquqaq nepsagusimeng . Taagken nepluku quwaalghiimun wine-mun , unaghsiighwaghqun nekeglluku nengugutkaa Jesus-mun melugriisqelluku .
Iwernga ilangita pikaat , " Wiintaku , esghapakaalteggu Elijah-m yuguliyaghtughnayukagu ! "
Allameng Jesus araghllagluni pegtekakek taghneghagni .
Tawani pilleghmi Temple-melnguq safkaaghun , pikegken kanavek piikaq malghughqelluni . Nuna ufsugusan , uyghaget quupaghtaatkat ,
lliivghet qelpeghaghtaatkat , uglalghiitlu Kiyaghneghem yugi tuqulaghaatkaayalghiit unguvaghtuutkat ,
enkaam lliveghmeggneng aanleghaatkat . Kingunganeng Jesus-em unguvaghtellghan aglaghtuutkat Agleghnalghiimun Neghllagmun , tawani yulghutem esghaqiit .
Tawani qaquuraghvigmi , umiilwaaghenkut pilluwaghtekullghhiit kelengakegkangat Jesus , esghaghyamegteggu nuna qapragllalghii , tamaanallu sangwaa piyan , alingruughuteghllakat . Pikat , " Ipapestaaq una Ighnequmayaghtagu Kiyaghneghem ! "
Tamaanteftut aghnalghutet esghapalghiit uyavaneng . Galilee-meng maligtekaat Jesus kayusiinnaluki .
Akulngitniteftut Mary Magdala-ghmii , Mary-llu naangak James-enkuk Joseph-enkuk , Zebedee-mllu ighneghegkenka naangak .
Whanikuyagu aklungilnguq yuuk aatgha Joseph , Arimathea-ghmii , maligsaaghtenga Jesus-em kaatkaq .
Pilate-mun piluni Jesus-em yugusii tungsiqaa . Enkaam Pilate-em qelghutkaa yugusiq Joseph-mun tuunesqelluku .
Enkaangam tuguluku yugusii , nutaghaghllugkun qiipaghakun iimgutkaa .
Taagken llikaa ellmi lliveghraghaghmikun , uyghagrugllagkun laagtestekamikun siklaqumeng . Taagken paaynganun ullghitaghlluku uyghagllak , apeghiighyami aghulaqegkaq .
Tawanteftuk Mary Magdala-ghmiinkuk , aallghallu Mary lliveghmun ayuqlutek aqumgalghiik .
Unaamingani kingunganeng Yataghqefigem Aghneghan , chief priest-etlu , Pharisees-etlu aleghqughyaghtuqaat Pilate .
Pikaat , " Yuguniiq , neqamikaghput taana puughtista salin unguvaluni pikaaguq , ' Pingayut aghneghet atughluki unguvaghteslequnga . '
Enkaangam kayagutigu lliivgha kelengakngwaaghesqelluku pingayunun aghneghnun , luuraq maligsaaghtengita yugusii teglegluku ungipaannayukatki yuget unguvaamaniluku . Una iqlengaq seghleghataghaayaghqaaguq sivulighmeng . "
Pilate-em pikii , " Kelengakistelguusi , elngaatall kelengakestengngwaaghteggu lliveq . "
Enkaam lliveghmun aglaghluteng maghqalluku nalluniiqaat uyghak qelpeghhnayukatgu . Taagken qelghutkaat pilluwaghtenun kelengakesqelluku .
Sabbath-em kingunganeng , aghtaghaghaqaallu sivulighmi aghneghani santillghem , Mary Magdala-ghmii , ilangallu Mary-m , lliveq esghaghyaghtuqaak .
Tawani pilleghmi nuna qapragllakaq qayughllak Atanghem yaqulga qilagmeng ukikaq . Lliivghem paayngan uyghaga ullghitaghtaghluku aqumegkaa .
Esghaqaaluni nighugpaguullghiistun nighugtutkaghmi , aatkiillu qatelghiit anigustun .
Kelengakistet yaqulegmeng alingruuqat repall ungeleglluteng , tuqukastunllu lliiqat .
Iwernga aghnak yaqulgem pikakek , " Alingegpenatek . Liisimakamtek Jesus ivaghaqaghtek , qaquuraqaayalghii .
Whaanneghituq ; unguvaamaaq pinaqnilleghmitun . Tagitek , esghaghyaghtughtegnegu lliviksaqanga .
Enkaam ungipaatqaghsaghtughtegneki maligsaaghtengi unguvaamaniluku tuqulleghmeng , agallu sivullgaaghumaaq Galilee-mun . Taagani esghaghlleqaghsi ! Taawa ungipaatamtek . "
Enkaangam tawaninginaq lliveghmeng aghulaqegkak , alingumaagmeklu quyaghllagumaagmeklu , ketanqusnaq ungipaasaghtuqiik maligsaaghtengi .
Jesus-em aliighaghfiklukek pikakek , " Nekeggmelleq elpetegnilli . " Enkaam taakuk aghnak takuluku , itegii nuqneqluki maniguqaak .
Taagken Jesus-em pikakek , " Alingegpenatek . Ungipaasaghtughtegneki malighsaaghtenka anglegusiitkanka , Galilee-mun始nguq aglaghlit taaganinguq esghaghlleqaatnga . "
Aghnak igleghsimalukek , lliveghmelnguut ilangi kelengakistet Jerusalem-emun iteghluteng , chief priest-enun aapqaat qamaglluku tamaana apeghiiqaq .
Enkaam chief priest-etlu , siivanlleghetlu qerngughlluteng agghitkat . Taagken maniliteghllagluki pilluwaghtet ,
pikiit , " Ungipaannakesi yuget , ' Unugmi qavaasimaluta maligsaaghtengita tagiluteng teglegumaat yugusii . '
Governor-em nagaquumakagu whangkuta aleghqughlleqaghput enkaam seghleliillengnaanghitusi . "
Kelengakistet mani tuguluku pisqelleghmegestun pikat . Enkaam whavemun kenlanga Jews-et paninang aapghaqaat Jesus-em yugusii teglekaqniluku maligsaaghtenganun .
Tawaten pimaluki , taakut qula ataasiq siipneqluku maligsaaghtet aglaqat Galilee-mun , naayghamun Jesus-em pisqellghatun tawaten .
Esghaghyamegteggu Jesus maniguqaat , iwernga ilangita aygughikegkaat ellngangutanga .
Jesus-em takuluki pikii , " Qamaglluni aghtughyaghqaanghilleq qilagmillu , nunamillu whangamnun tagivaqaaguq .
Tamaaken apalluqluku aghulaqlusi qamaglluki yuget maligsaaghtengllaghteki whangamnun , paaptaayelaghteki Aatghakun Atam , Ighneghem , Agleghnalghiimllu Taghnegham .
Apeghtuusaqiteki qaatkesqelluki qamaglluki qelghutkanka elpesinun . Elpesinitepestaaghllequnga quunpeng kenlanga kenletghuutellghanun nunam . "
Pinilghiit Ungipat Jesus Christ-ameng ayuqelghiit , Ighneghaneng Kiyaghneghem piinliqaagut whaten :
Uuknaliqistem Isaiah-m igaqegkaqaa Kiyaghneghem whaten pillgha , " Ungipaghteka kayagtekestaghnaqaqa sivugpeni yataaghqesqelluku tuumkaghqan .
Kilgaani ma akilghuugaquq whaten , ' Atanghem tuumnga yataaghqiteggu , taklaghteggullu ! ' "
Taana ungipaghta John-nguuq Paaptaayesta . Kilgaani paaptaayelaghaquqlu ungipaghaquqlu whaten , " Avuteghqellusi , seghleghqennanighlusi paaptaayetek , enkaam Kiyaghneghem seghevulleqiisi . "
Judea-ghmiitlu Jerusalem-eghmiitlu nagasaghtuutkaat John . Enkaam seghleghqelleteng apeghranghatki paaptaayaaqegkangi kiiwegni Jordan-meng aatqelghiigni .
John-em aatkii camel-em melqwaneng ulimaaghet , meqameng tafsiluni , neghaqelghii locust-mengllu honey-mengllu .
Ungipaqikaq whaten , " Kingumneng yuuk tagiyaghqaaguq aghtughyaghqaanghitaghalghii whangamneng . Whanga sasiinghitunga repall itemtepagningitanka singii .
Meghmeng paaptaayaaqamsi , iwernga ellngan paaptaayelleqiisi Agleghnalghiigneng Taghneghagneng . "
John tawaten aneghsimaluku Jesus kaatkaq Nazareth-meng , Galilee-melngughmeng , enkaam John-em paaptaayekaa Jordan-egni .
Paaptaayeneghmeng taaqsatni Jesus-em tawaninginaq esghaqii qilaget qelpelghiit , Agleghnalghiiklu Taghneghak ukilghiik ellminun dove-etun ayuqlutek .
Memllu qilagmeng pikaa , " Ighneqamken , piniqegkamni . Efquqepigtamken . "
Tawaninginaq Agleghnalghiim Taghnegham Jesus aghulaqestekaa kilgaanun .
Ellnginaghhaakaq iwerngaqun nuyaalghiit teghikusat tamaantekat . Tamaansimaluku Tughneghaam nanghiiqukaa ketwhell 40 aghneq , iwernga yaqulget aflengakegkaat .
Tagtalmi taakwani kingunganeng John-em anusimingllallghan , Jesus Galilee-lluni ungipaqikaq Pinilghiineng Ungipaneng Kiyaghneghtaneng .
Pikaq , " Pilleghqaq whaa kaasimaaq enkaam Ataneghpagullgha Kiyaghneghem whaa whaantuq ! Avuteghqellusi , seghleghqennanighlusi ugpeqiteki Pinilghiit Ungipat ! "
Jesus igleghutkelluku Naayvam Galilee-m esnengakun esghaqakek maalghuk iqalliniightek siiftilghiik negaghpagmeng . Simon-enkunguftuk Andrew-nkuk anglegutkullghiik .
Jesus-em pikakek , " Maligtegnenga , apeghtughnaqamtek yugmeng naapsagutesqellutek . "
Tawaninginaq negaghpatek unilluki maligtekaak .
Tazingapighqaaghluni esghaghlaataqakek James-enkuk John-enkuk anglegutkullghiik , ighneghqek Zebedee-m . Negaghpagmegneng ilaaghtulghiik angyamegni .
Jesus-em esghaqiinaghlukek pikakek , " Maligtegnenga ! " Enkaam angyakun unilluku atayek Zebedee , taakutlu qepghaghtenguluki tugukateng , maligtekaak Jesus .
Jesus-enkut maligsaaghtekullghiit Capernaum-emun kaatkat . Sabbath-ngughsagu , Jesus synagogue-elluni apeghtughikaq .
Nagallghiit saghiighayagutkaat apeghtughillgha , qayughllak apeghtughikaq Kiyaghneghem pilleghqalitellghakun , apeghtughistengistun Liilightuusat pigpenani .
Taagken yuuk ilumikun tughneghalek iteghluni synagogue-mun akilghuukaq ,
" Jesus , Nazareth-eghmii , sangamta qinuyugsikut ? Naafqesaghtuuzikuut ? Kinanguten liisimakaqa , Yugulighistenguuten Kiyaghneghem akequsaqegkaa kayaglleqniluku . "
Jesus-em aghyuuqaa tughneghaq , " Nepngunang , aani yugmeng . "
Tughneghaam yuuk sayugpagtaghtesluku , araghllagumaghmi aanegkaq .
Yuget saghiighayugluteng ellmeggneng aapqughaaghutkat , " Una sangaawa ? Una apeghtuusaghraghaaguq ! Kiyaghneghem aghtughyaghqaanghillghakun uum yugem qelghii tughneghaat aanesqelluki , legan qaatkaat . "
Enkaam Galilee-lqaaghaghmi yuget ungipaqnginaamaan Jesus pikaat .
Taagken Jesus aanaghesnaghluni synagogue-meng , Simon-enkuk Andrew-nkuk mangteghiitnun pikaq , James-enkuklu John-enkuk maligtekaak .
Simon-em sakinga ingaghmeteftuq , puqleghaluni . Legan Jesus kaatuq ungipaatkaat aghnaq qinuyuguniluku .
Iteghluni aghnaq iiggakun tuguluku nekevestekaa enkaam puqleghangiilluni , kepsiiqunginaamiita pikii .
Sabbath-em ighivgaani siqineq tevighyan Jesus-mun tagiquutkiit qinuyulghiit , tamaakutlu tughneghalget ilumegteggun .
Qamagtengngwaaghluteng Capernaum-eghmiit mangtegham manughaani qerngughutkat .
Enkaam Jesus-em uglalghiit naallghuquqii allaaghhiinaghneng aqnighneghitneng , aanesquqiillu tughneghaat yulghutet ilungitneng . Tughneghaat sameng pisimangilkangi , qayughllak kinangutanga liisimakegkangat .
Salin aghsugniiteghllagluku , Jesus makelluni aanegkaq yughaghnaluni kilgaani .
Simon-enkut ilakulghiit ivaghyaghtuqaat ,
naalkesamegteggu pikaat , " Yuget ivanghiighutaqaaten . "
Yeghlegi Jesus-em pikii , " Ilangitnun nunat pinaqukut . Ellngitnillu ungipaqiyaghqaagunga , qayughllak tamaaken apalluqluku taginguunga . "
Enkaam Galilee-lqaaghaghmi igleghutkelluku ungipaqikaq synagogue-nni , aanesquqiillu tughneghaat yuget ilungitneng .
Yuuk leprosy-lek tagiluni Jesus-mun manungakun segesqughlluni nangllegsipiglluni pikaa , " Piyukelqegkuvgu naallghutaghtinga ukmangiightesqellunga . "
Jesus-em nangllegyagulluku nengugluku saaftutkelluku pikaa , " Piyukelqaqa , naallghuten ! "
Tawaninginaq yuuk naallghulluni ukmangiightekaq .
Taagken Jesus-em ineghtengngwaaqaa , " Nagataghten , wataghllak kinkut alngunak ungipaategpenaki naallghunniluten whangamnun . Itupill priest-mun yuvghiighsighyaghtaa . Enkaam aghqerraaghhaaten Moses-em Liilightuusiita pisqellghistun ipapighqesqelluku yugnun naallghutellghen . " Taagken tawaninginaq aghulaqestekaa .
Iwernga yugem igleghutkelluku nani alngunak aapghumanginaqaa Jesus-mun naalghusimaniluni . Taagken kenlanga Jesus alngunak nenun pinaniqaq , qayughllak yulghuteghllaget takwaaqegkangat , enkaam paaghqillghani kiyaghtekaq . Iwernga naken alngunak yulghutet paninang takwaaqegkangat .
Mulugpenani Jesus uteghniqaq Capernaum-emun , enkaam ungipaqegkaat nayuqaqegkemininniluku mangteghami .
Yuuk tagilaghaasalghiimi ellnganun kangsuutkat repall manughamun qakmavek . Jesus ungipaqimaluku Kiyaghneghem akuzitanganeng ,
estamat yuget kevegtughluku uniiqaq yuuk tagitkaat ellnganun .
Kaatulluku itghunneghmeng aghtuqaat , qayughllak yuuk kangsuuteghllagulghii . Enkaam mangtegham qaayngan tile-ngi ikughluki reghighulluku , yuuk allighaakun ukigtekaat Jesus-em nallangakun .
Jesus-em liisimakegkangi ugpeqilleghtulngit , enkaam uniiqaq yuuk pikaa , " Ighnemni , seghleghqelleghten seghevutellengut . "
Tawani apeghtughikayuget Liilightuusaneng aqumgallghiit sumeghtaghaqat ,
" Sangami yuuk una tawaten akuzii ? Akuzillgha seghleghuuq , qayughllak Kiyaghneghunilghii ! Kiyaghneghhiinaaguq seghleghqelleghneng seghevutiyaghqaq ! "
Tawaninginaq Jesus-em sumeghtaghallghit liisimakegkii enkaam pikii , " Sangan tawaten sumeghtaghaghetsi ?
Nalikek piyaqniitaghaghlleqak uniiqaq yuuk piyaqumkun , ' Seghleghqelleghten seghevutellengut ' nalighmeng , ' Makelluten , allighan tuguluku piyugi ? '
Iwernga liisimakesugaqa Ighnegha Yugem seghevutiyaqleguuq seghleghqelleghneng nunami whani . " Enkaam uniiqaq yuuk pikaa ,
" Ungipaatamken , maketen , allighan tuguluku , elpesinun aglaa ! "
Yuget esghapakaat yuuk tawaninginaq nekevluni , allighani tuguluku aanelghii . Enkaam qamagtengngwaaghluteng tawanlenguut saghiighayukat , usuqegkaatlu Kiyaghneq , " Whatelngughmeng esghaasigasaghtukut ! "
Taagken Jesus , esnenganun Naayvam Galilee-m pinqigtekaq . Yulghuteghllaget takulaghaasatni apeghtuqii .
Igleghutkelluku esghaqaa tax-neng qerngughtista , aatgha Levi , ighnegha Alphaeus-em . Aqumgaftuq qepghaghvigmini . Jesus-em pikaa , " Maligtinga . " Levi-em nekevluni maligtekaa .
Tawani ighivgaghmi , Jesus-enkut maligsaaghtekullghiit Levi-enkunun neghyaghtuqat . Neghelgusiqiit tax-neng qerngughtistelghutetlu tamaakutlu qaatkusigalnguut Jews-et Liilightuusiitnun . ( Tawatelnguutlu yuget maligsaaghukangat Jesus . )
Ilangi apeghtughistengit Liilightuusat Pharisees-ngulghiit , esghaghyamegteggu Jesus neghelgusighilghii , aaptekiit maligsaaghtengi , " Sangami Jesus neghaqa tax-em qerngughtistengitnillu seghleghqestenillu ? "
Jesus-em nagalluki pikii , " Aghallegtaq qinuyulghiinun pinguuq , yugunqegtanun pingunghituq . Tawateghpigaq ungipaasaghtuuganka seghleghqestet avuteghqesqelluki , nakaan tamaakut seghleghqiganniluteng pilghiit . "
Ataasimi aghneghmi , John-em Paaptaayestem maligsaaghtengillu Pharisees-etlu fast-engulghiit . Ilangita yuget takuluku Jesus aaptekaat , " Sangameng John-em Paaptaayestem maligsaaghtengillu Pharisees-etlu maligsaaghtengit fast-aaqat , naqam elpek maligsaaghteten pigpenateng ? "
Jesus-em kiimsiqii , " Nulightughnaqelghiim aqelqii fast-elleqaat neqenghaghqellghani ? Yeghlegillu ! Nulightughnaqelghii paninang tawanlluku tawaten pinaanghitut .
Nulightughnaqelghiistun ayuqunga , maligsaaghtenka nulightughnaqelghiim aqelqiistun ayuqut . Aghulaqestekanganga elngaatall tawani aghneghmi maligsaaghtenka fast-ellequt .
" Kitum alngunak nutaghaq qiipaghaq qellughsimangilnguq ilaaghusiqnaanghitaa qaaslilugegnun . Ilaaghusiqegkumigu piigutaaghaghllequq , enkaam piilleq sullevataghllequq .
Enkaamllu kitum alngunak awataghpaluk imighnaanghitaa wine-eghraghaghmeng . Imiqumigu awataghpaluk quupaghllequq enkaam wine-a sakusiiqellequq , awataghpaluklu naavellequq . Tamaaken apalluqluku wine-eghraghaq awataghpagraghaghmun kuuvyaghqaaguq ! "
Ataasimi Sabbath-mi , Jesus igleghtekaq wheat-et piitfigitgun . Maligsaaghtengita igleghalgusiitkelluku wheat-et piitutangitneng ikutaghtaqukat neghnaluteng .
Taagken Pharisees-et aaptekaat Jesus , " Esghaqaghqiqun ! Sangameng maligsaaghteten saghnaat wheat-et piitutangitneng ? Tawaten pilleghmegteggun qepghaghtut Sabbath-mi , enkaam qaatkunneghitnguut Liilightuusamnnun . "
Jesus-em pikii , " Atightiigasteggu David-em pillgha qavngarugllak ? Yukullghiit iyatiqaqngameng ,
David iteghluni Kiyaghneghem Mangteghaanun neghegkaaguq neqekrangllameng Kiyaghneghmun tuunegkameng . Tawaten pikaaguq Abiathar , High Priest-nguluku . Liilightuusamta pillghani priest-nginaghhaat neghyaghqaayaghtut tamaaken neqekrangllameng , iwernga David neghluni yunillu tuunegkaqii . "
Taagken Jesus-em pikii , " Sabbath-a nakmikegkaaguq meghnaliviguluni yugem pinighqelleghqaanun . Sabbath-a nakmikegkaanghituq yugmun ikfiqliighutkesqelluku .
Enkaangam whanga , Ighneghani Yugem , Atanghuunga talwa Sabbath-mun . "
Taagken Jesus aglanqigtekaq synagogue-mun , tawanteftuq yuuk inglungi iiggan uniiqat .
Ilangita yuget tawanlenguut riirngingwaaqaat Jesus-em naallghunnayukagu Sabbath-mi . Naallghuskagu whaten pinaluku , " Anaggututen ! "
Uniiqameng iiggelek yuuk Jesus-em pikaa , " Tagi whavek . "
Taagken yuget aaptekii , " Liilightuusamta sasqinkut Sabbath-mi ? Pinitun pisqinkuut , nalighmeng seghletun ? Yugulighisqinkuut , nalighmeng tuqutisqinkuut ? " Iwernga yuget qallegnanighwaaghutkat .
Jesus-em esghapagngaaghmiki ugumiyagutkii , naqam iilqutkumiita pineghllugullghitnengllu waakigatngitnengllu . Taagken Jesus-em qiivluku yuuk pikaa , " Iiggeten nengugutiki . " Legan nengugutii aga naallghutkat .
Enkaam Pharisees-et aanaghesnaghluteng synagogue-meng , Herod-em ilapgastengitnun aglaghluteng agghitkegkaat naten tuqutelleghqameng Jesus .
Jesus-enkut maligsaaghtekullghiit Naayvamun Galilee-mun aglaqat . Yulghuteghllaget maligtekiit , qayughllak nagaquqaqegkangit Jesus-em allaaghllugwhaghtillghi . Tamaana yulghun Galilee-meng , Judea-meng , Jerusalem-emeng , Idumea-meng , Jordan-em Kiiwem inglunganilngughneng nunaneng , Tyre-meng , Sidon-meng pingulghiit .
Yuuk uglaghighllagyan Jesus maligsaaghteminun angyameng yataaghqutesqegkaq luuraq ighlleghnayukangatni meghmun .
Yulghun naallghuquqaqutanganeng qamaglluteng qinuyuget ellnganun kaannaqeghllakat saaftepigesnaghnaluku .
Tamaakutlu tughneghaat yuget ilungitnilnguut esghaneghmegteggu Jesus , sivungakun ullghaghlluteng akilghuugaqelghiit , " Kiyaghneghem Ighneqaaten ! "
Iwernga Jesus-em ineghtengngwaaqii tughneghaat kinangutni apefqaan pisqelluku .
Taagken Jesus qemimun mayughluni yuget piyukegkani tagsighteqii . Tagilaghaasata
nakmikegkii qula maalghuk siipneqluku yuget apostle-nguluki . Taagken pikii , " Whangamnitesqellusi nakmikamsi , kayaglleqamsillu ungipaghyaghtiisqellusi .
Aghtughyaghqaanghillelgullequsillu tughneghaat aanestesqelluki yugneng . "
Ukut nakmikegkaqii , Simon , ( Jesus-em ateghiqaa Peter-meng ) ;
James-enkuk John-enkuk , ighneghqek Zebedee-m , ( Jesus-em atiqakek Boanerges-meng , whaten pisimeng , " Ighneghqek Kallugem " ) ;
Andrew-nkut , Philip-enkut , Bartholomew-nkut , Matthew-nkut , Thomas-enkut , James-llu ighnegha Alphaeus-em , Thaddaeus-enkut , Simon-llu Zealot-a ,
Judas Iscariot-lu uveghpagutiyaghqaq Jesus-meng .
Taagken Jesus tukughminun aglaqaq . Yulghuteghllaget aglaghtuullaataqat ellngitnun , repall Jesus-enkut maligsaaghtekullghiit neghepagningiitkat .
Nengllugutangan nagaqughluku tawaten aneghtellgha aqfakaat , qayughllak yuget pikangat nallungughhniluku .
Ilangi apeghtughikayuget Liilightuusaneng Jerusalem-emeng tagikat whaten pimaaqelghiit , " Beelzebul Jesus-em ilunganituq ! Enkaam aanesqughaqii tughneghaat yugneng aghtughyaghqaanghillghakun Beelzebul-em , umiilwaaghitgun tughneghaat . "
Enkaam Jesus-em tagsighluki yuget ungipaghaatkii , pikii , " Tughneghaq ellmineng aanesleqaa ?
Ataneghpagulleq aafquuskumi , taana ataneghpagulleq qerngaghmennaanghituq .
Nengllugutet aafquuskumeng , taakut nengllugutet qerngaghmennaanghitut .
Tawateghpigaq Tughneghaankut aafquulluteng pilluguskumeng , Tughneghaq nekevghapagningiilluni kenlekaghqaminun kaallequq .
" Kina alngunak iteghnaanghituq iknaqelghiim yugem mangteghaanun wayaghteghnaluki saghyangi . Sivukluku iknaqelghii yuuk asighqaghlluku , taagken wayaghteghlleqii saghyangi .
" Ipa ungipaatamsi , yuget seghevutellengyaghqaagut seghleghqellghitneng , seghletunllu akuzitkellghitneng Kiyaghneq .
Iwernga kitum alngunak seghletun akuzitkegkumikek Agleghnalghiik Taghneghak seghevutellengnaanghituq , qayughllak seghleghqengnguuq Kiyaghneghem seghevusaghqaqenghilkanganeng . Taana seghleghqelleq kenglengilnguuguq . "
Jesus tawaten akuzikaq qayughllak ilangita pikaqegkangat , " Tughneghalguuq ilumikun . "
Taagken Jesus-em naangallu anglegutangillu kaatkat . Manughamelluteng aanesqegkaat esghaghyugniluku .
Yulghutet aqumuutngalghiit Jesus-em uvitangani ungipaatkaat , " Qakma naagpeklu anglegutegpeklu esghaghyugaqaaten . "
Jesus-em aaptekii , " Kinangaawa naaka ? Kinkungaawat anglegutenka ? "
Yugsughaluni aqumgalghiit pikii , " Elpesi naakamsillu , anglegutkamsillu !
