Kitum alngunak atuqegkumigu Kiyaghneghem piyukellgha , anglegutkaqallu naakaqallu . "
Taakwaningani Jesus apeghtughilaataqaq Naayvam Galilee-m esnengani . Elngaatall uglapiglleghhii yuuk tagilaghaateghllakaq ellnganun , repall angyamun uuglluni aqumegkaq , llaaghanwha yulghutet naayvam esnenganitkat .
Ungipaghaatetgun allaaghiinaghmeng apeghtuqii . Apeghtughitkelluku pikii ,
" Nagatek ! Piitesighaghta aglaghluni piitesiighaghvigminun
ifkaghquqaq piitutneng . Ilangi piitutet tekitkat tumetgun , enkaam qawaaget tagiluteng neghuqiit .
Ilangi piitutet tekitkat uyghagtuqakun sunapagilngughqun . Tawaninginaq piitkat , qayughllak sunanga ugmestaaghhaq .
Enkaam siqineq piisalghiimi maatneghan paneghtekii piinneghhat , akungellghitutmeggneng palirakegtekat .
Ilangi piitutet tekitkat sikughllugtuqakun , sikughlluget piisalghiimeng piitfigiqiit grain-et .
Naqamalla tamaakut tekitkat sunakegtakun piitestighllakat grain-meng , ilangi 30 , ilangi 60 , enkaam ilangi 100 . "
Jesus-em taaqniqii whaten , " Sigutelgukufsi nagatusighqameng , nagatek ! "
Taam kingunganeng Jesus ellnginaaghsan , qula maalghuk siipneqluku maligsaaghtengitallu ilangitallu tamaakut nagatkat aaptekaat ungipaghaatkegkaaneng .
Jesus-em pikii , " Elpesinun Kiyaghneghem liigikestaa talughngalghii ipapighqellgha Ataneghpagullghem . Sivunghani liitesimangisaghaa . Iwernga tamaakut iqitngalghiit Kiyaghneghem Ataneghpagullghaneng nagaqughaqut sameng tamaghhaaneng ungipaghaatetgun .
Enkaam ' Esghaannaqaqut , esghaannaqaqut esghaategpenateng . Nagataqut , nagataqut liigikegpenateng . Pikaayaquyeng qiivnayaghtut Kiyaghneghmun , enkaam seghevunnayaghii . ' "
Taagken Jesus-em aaptekii , " Taana ungipaghaan piitesighaghta liigikenghitestegguu ? Natenmi liigiknaqesteki alngunak ungipaghaatet ?
Piitesighaghta ifkaghqilghii piitutneng , Kiyaghneghem akuzitanganeng ungipaghtengatun ayuquq .
Ilangi yuget qellighllakastun tumestun ayuqut . Piitutet tekinneghata tumetgun qawaaget neghaqiit . Tawateghpigaq tamaakut yuget nagaquunneghata Kiyaghneghem akuzitanganeng tawaninginaq Tughneghaam puygustaqii .
Ilangi yuget uyghagtuqastun sunastun ayuqut . Akut uyghagtuqamelnguut asivapagigatut . Tamaakut yuget nagaquunneghmeggni Kiyaghneghem akuzitanganeng tawaninginaq tuguklighaqiit quyakusiqluki .
Iwernga ugpeqngwaaghigalkangit akuzitangi enkaam ugpellghit mulungigatut . Seghleliineghmeggni , nalighmeng amyuutkellengneghmeggni apalluqluku ugpeqilleghteng Kiyaghneghem akuzitanganeng tawaninginaq ugpeqinanighaqut .
Ilangi yuget sikughllugtuqastun sunastun ayuqut . Piitutet sikughllugtuqakun tekitkat nagungigatut , qayughllak sikughlluget piitfigighaqegkangit . Tamaakut yuget nagaquneghmegteki Kiyaghneghem akuzitangi qaatkigatiit ,
qayughllak una unguvalleq nulqaaviighutkaqaat , teghhwaaghiitkaqaatlu aklungi , samengllu wata allgeghutaghaghyugaqut . Tawateghpigaq sikughlluget piitfigillghistun piitutet , tamaakut yuget piyukellghita puygustaqiit Kiyaghneghem akuzitangi .
Iwernga ilangi yuget pinilghiistun sunastun ayuqut . Piitutet tekitkat pinilghiikun sunakun elngaatall nawaaqut . Ilangi piitestiiqut 30 , ilangi 60 , ilangi 100 . Tawateghpigaq tamaakut yuget nagaquneghmegteki Kiyaghneghem akuzitangi qaatkaqiit , enkaam elngaatall qepghaghaqut Kiyaghneghmun . Ilangi wataqaaghaq qepghaghataaghaghaqut ilameggneng . "
Jesus-em nagneghutkii , " Kitum alngunak kenelghutak itghullukek sagneghem asinganun llinaanghitaak , nalighmeng qavaghvigem asinganun . Itupill quulvaqun llilleqaak .
Sangwaa alngunak iiqaq qaaynganun lliighyaghqaaguq , sangwaallu alngunak saapegkaq saaputiighyaghqaaguq .
Sigutelgukufsi nagatusighqameng , nagatek ! "
Whatenllu pikii , " Nagatngwaaghtengnga ! Tuunilleghpesistungwaaq Kiyaghneghem tuunelleqiisi , paninang tuunataghaghlleqiisi .
Yuuk salek tuunataghaghyaghqaaguq . Yuuk sapagllagilnguq sangiighhii tuguyaghqaagut . "
Whatenllu Jesus-em pikii , " Ataneghpagullgha Kiyaghneghem whatetuq : yuuk ifkaghqughaquq piitutneng piitesiighaghvigmini .
Piitutet piilluteng nawaaqut unugtuumaan , aghneghtuumaan yuuk qavaayaghngaan , teghhumayaghngaan , paninang piitutet nagwaaqut . Yugem nallukaqii naten nawaaqutangi .
Sunanginaghhaam kayutngunani piitutet nagustaqii enkaam piitestekangaqut : sivukluteng sungaghyukegtaghhaat piitaqut , taagken napaaziingaqut qenwatlu grain-engaqut .
Grain-et qigunghata unataghyaghqaaghtaqut , enkaam yugem kepughaqii kepuusimikun . "
Jesus-em aaptekii , " Samun uspunnaqesteggu Ataneghpagullgha Kiyaghneghem ? Sangwaa ungipaghaatkennaqesteggu liigikestisiiluku ?
Ataneghpagullgha Kiyaghneghem mustard-em piitutngatun ayuquq . Mekestaalleghpigaaguq piitutneng nunami whani iwernga yugem piitesiighaneghminigu ,
anglighllagaquq angelleghpigaaghlluni nunivagseghaghyaggaghneng . Uglaapiglleghhiit avayaghrugllagi enkaam qawaaget unglusiiqut ququngaan akulngakun siqinghillghakun . "
Jesus-em atuqluki ungipaghaatelghutet yugnun akuzitkegkaqii Kiyaghneghem Akuzitangi . Aapqaqii yugnun liigikelleghtulangistun .
Quunpeng yuget apeghtughaqegkangi ungipaghaatetgun , iwernga maligsaaghtekullghiit ellnginaaghhneghmeggni whateghlluwaaq liigikestaqegkangi sameng pisiitangi ungipaghaatet .
Taam ighivgaani Jesus-em angyamelluni maligsaaghteni pikii , " Aghviilta naayvam inglunganun . " Enkaam maligsaaghtet uuglluteng angyamun unitkiit yulghutet . Ilangitallu angyat maligtekiit .
Taagken anuqlighllakaq , repall imaghllugem imighaataqegkaa angyaq qenwat esleqsaghtuqaq .
Jesus angyallimi qavaq akisighluni . Maligsaaghtengita taghtughlluku pikaat , " Apeghtughista , tuquyaghngaamtaa pizikuut ? "
Jesus-em taghtughluni anuqallu imaghllugetlu ineghtekii , " Anuqa taaqingam , imaghlluget aghuliightek ! " Enkaam ellmaaragutkelluku amsanaghllugughtekaq .
Taagken maligsaaghteni aaptekii , " Sangafsi alingetsi ? Taawa ugpeqigastengngaa ? "
Saghiighayugllakat repall tallughyugllakat alingruughumaghmeng , enkaam aapqughaaghutkat ellmeggneng , " Kinangaawa una yuuk , talwa anuqemllu imaghllugetlu qaatkegkangat ? "
Naayvam inglunganun kaatkat Jesus-enkut maligsaaghtekullghiit , nunangitnun Gerasa-ghmiit .
Legan Jesus angyameng quutmun uugtuq yuuk aanluni sufliitneng llivghet , paasqaa .
Taana yuuk ilumikun tughneghaghtuqaq lliveghnitaqelghii . Awen qiipraghutneng asightaqsaqangat iiggitgunllu itegiitgunllu iwernga sakeqaqegkangi qiipraghutet , kagimtaqegkangillu savikenghaaghet itegaminilnguut . Kitum alngunak asighqepagningitkaallu aghuliightepagningitkaallu , qayughllak iknaqepiglleghhii .
Unugtuumaan , aghneghtuumaan igleghtaqelghii lliivghet qungangitnillu qeminillu , quunpeng araghaataamaghmi , uyghagteggun kiitiqumaghmi ellmineng .
Jesus esghaghyamigu uyavaqaanlluku ketanqusnaq takuluku segesqughfikluku maniguqaa .
Taagken Jesus-em yugem ilunganilnguq tughneghaq pikaa , " Uyuq seghleq tughneghaq , aani yugmeng ! " Tughneghaam araghaataqaa , " Jesus , Ighnegha Kiyaghneghem , sanaqsinga ? Akeqi Kiyaghneghmun ikfiqestesaghqaafqaama pisqellunga ! "
Jesus-em aaptekaa , " Kinanguzin ? " Yugem kiimsiqaa , " Aatqaqa ' Uglaghllak ' qayughllak uglaghllagtukut ! "
Elngaatall Jesus-mun aapuquutkii tughneghaat aghulaqestefqiita pisqelluki taagken nunameng .
Taawanguq qemim minglengani kurugalghuteghllaget , neghuullghiit .
Tughneghaat aapuquutkat Jesus-mun , " Kurugaghnun kayagtikut , ellngitnun iteghtestikut . "
Enkaam angeghqumakegkii . Tughneghaat yugmeng aanaghesnaghluteng kurugaghnun iteghaatkat . Entaqun 2,000-nguut kurugaat , pennaneng asitmun pangalgulluteng naayvamun ateghaatkat enkaam tuqulaghaatkat .
Kurugaat aflengakistengit qimaguutkat neghllagmunllu uvitanganilngughnunllu nunanun . Tamaani ungipaqegkiit ilumikun tughneghaghtuqaqlu , kurugaatlu . Enkaam yuget esghaghyaghtuutkiit samatangi .
Jesus-mun kaalluteng esghaqaat yuuk tughneghaghtughllagyalghii ilumikun . Taawanguq aqumgaftuq piluguwaaghluni , umyugakeklu naallghullutek enkaam alingruuqat .
Tamaakut esghapakat aapqaat naallghusimaniluku yuuk tughneghaghtughllagyalghii , aapqiitlu kurugaat samatangi .
Taagken yulghutet maniguutepiglluteng Jesus aghulaqesqegkaat nunameggneng .
Jesus uugtaquqlu angyamun , yugem tughneghaghtuyalghiim maniguutepiglluni aaptekaa , " Maligllaken ? "
Iwernga Jesus-em ighsakluku pikaa , " Nengllugutegpenunllu , ilakumtaaghpenunllu aglaghluten apeghnaken Atanghem nangllekepiglluten apeghiillgha elpenun . "
Enkaam yuuk aghulaqegkaq . Tamaani nunami aatqelghiimi , Qula Neghllaget , ungipaqegkaa Jesus-em apeghiillgha ellminun , tamaakut nagaquutkat allaaghlluwhaghyukat .
Jesus angyakun uteghnighyan inglunganun naayvam , esnemi yulghuteghllaget qerngughutkat uvitanganun .
Taagken ataasiq synagogue-em umiilwaagha , Jairus-nguftuq aatgha , tagiluni Jesus-mun segesqughtekaq manungakun .
Maniguutepiglluni pikaa , " Paniggaqa qinuyugllaguuq , tuquyaghtungestaamaaq . Takwaaghtigu saafsaghtuqaghhu , enkaam naallghulluni kiyaghlli ! "
Enkaam Jesus-em maligtekaa . Yulghuteghllagetlu maliglleghaatkaat Jesus , repall kanglluqaghlluku .
Aghnaqlu tawanteftuq aagtuqaataq qula maalghuk siipngaan ayumiqulleghni . Talwa aghallegtalghutet kayusiitaqsaghngaatni naallghusigalnguq , yeghlegi naavnginalghii . Qenwat maniqraggiighutkaq .
Nagaqughaqegkanga Jesus , enkaam yulghuteghllaget akulangitgun tunutanganeng takukaa .
Sumeghtaghaqaq , " Aatkii saafteqeghsaqumki naallghunayaghtunga . "
Legan atkuyaaghqek saaftaak kiitnginaamaghmi pikaq , enkaam elpekegkaa naallghutellgha qaamnami .
Tawaninginaq Jesus-em liigikegkaa aghtughyaghqaanghilleq aanelghii ellmineng , enkaam yulghuteghllaget qiivluki aaptekii , " Kitum aatkanka saaftaki ? "
Maligsaaghtengita pikaat , " Yulghuteghllaget qungangitnilnguuten sangan kitumun saafniluten pizin ? "
Iwernga Jesus-em esghaghnaqegkaa kitumun saaftutni .
Aghnam liigikluku naallghutelleni alingem ungelegsimaghmi takukaa Jesus . Taagken manungakun segesqughlluni ungipaatkaa salleghmineng .
Jesus-em pikaa , " Panimni , ugpeqilleghpek naallghutestaaten . Nekeggmellelighluten aglaa , naallghutngwaaghumaaten . "
Jesus-em aleghquumaluku aghnaq , kevgat tagiluteng ungipaatkaat Jairus , " Panigen tuqumaaq , takusqegpenaan始ngam Apeghtughistemun . "
Jesus-em nagateghngaaghmiki avelghaqiinaghluki Jairus pikaa , " Alingegpenang , taawanginaq ugpeghi . "
Taagken kitumun alngunak maligtesnaniqaq , iwerngaqun kelqegkii Peter-enkut James-enkut John-enkut , anglegutanga James-em .
Jesus-enkut kaasalghiimeng Jairus-enkunun , yulghuteghllaget elngaatall qiyaaghuuteghllaguftut metuumaghmeng .
Jesus-em iteghluni yulghutet pikii , " Sangafsi qiyaaghuuteghllagutsi ? Sangafsi nepugtiighllagutsi ? Taghnughhaq tuqullghituq , qavaaguq ! "
Iwernga nenglaqegkaat tawaten piyisteng . Qamaglluki aanesamiki angayuqakeklu taakutlu maligsaaghteni itghutkii taghnughhaam nenganun .
Jesus-em iiggakun tuguluku aghnaghaghhaq pikaa , " Talitha kum ! " ( whaten pisiq , " Aghnaghaghhaq , maketesqamken ! " )
Tawaninginaq makelluni piyukaq . ( Aghnaghaghhaq qula maalghuk siipngaan uksughtutkaftuq . ) Angayuqakeklu maligsaaghtetlu elngaatall saghiighayukat !
Taagken Jesus-em ineghtengngwaaqii kitumun alngunak ungipaqefqaan pisqelluku , pikiillu , " Neghyaghqaghhaghmeng tuuniteggu . "
Taagken Jesus aghulaqegkaq Capernaum-emeng , aglaqaq neminun Nazareth-mun , maligsaaghtengitallu maligtekaat .
Sabbath-ngughsagu synagogue-mi apeghtughikaq . Yulghutet nagalluku saghiighayagutkaat . Aapqughaaghutkat ellmeggneng , " Naken liitaki ? Kitum peghqinghughtestagu ? Saghiighayugnaghllaguut allaaghlluwhaghtillghi !
Naten tawaten pii ? Kaapentangunghitaa , Mary-m ighnegha ? James-enkut , Joses-enkut , Judas-enkut , Simon-enkut anglegutkenghitakii ? Nayagillulli maantaat ? " Enkaam tugukliimangilkangat .
Jesus-em pikii , " Kitum alngunak uuknaliqista siivakaqaa , iwerngaqun nunalgutangitallu nalleqliitallu nengllugutangitallu pingigataat . "
Enkaam tamaani allaaghlluwhaghtipagningitkaq , iwerngaqun qafsinkuuraghhaat saafluki naallghutkii .
Enkaam Jesus saghiighayugllakaq , qayughllak ugpeqenghilkangat . Taagken Jesus Nazareth-em uvitanganilngughnun nenun piiqluni apeghtuqii yuget .
Tagsighluki qula maalghuk siipneqluku maligsaaghteni , kayaggnaqnikii malghukaghtiita ungipaqisqellukillu naallghuqiisqellukillu . Aghulaqfagilgata aghtughyaghqaanghilleliquqii yugneng aanesqiisqelluki tughneghaat .
Liilightuqiillu , " Igleghalleghpesini sameng alngunak kelqegpenasi iwerngaqun ayaviighmeng . Neqekrangllangunasi , aqeftaghaangunasi , maningunasi pilghaasi .
Iwernga kameglusi , simiitkaghqameng ggaatmeng kelqegpenasi . "
Whatenllu pikii , " Nani alngunak tukughpesi upughaskangisi tawanlleghhaasi kenlanga aghulaqelleghpesinun .
Nenun kaaskufsi upughatingigalngughnun , nalighmeng nagasugigalngughnun , uninnakesi taana nuna itegasi pagulangiimiita . Tawaten pikufsi kelengasaaghlleqasi Kiyaghneghem aghyuulleghqaaneng ! "
Enkaam maligsaaghtet aghulaqluteng ungipaqikat yugnun avuteghqelluki seghleghqennaniisqelluki .
Tughneghalghutet aanesquqiit yugneng , mesiighqaqlukillu qinuyulghutet naallghuquqiit .
Umiilgem Herod-em nagaquqaa qamaglluku Jesus-em tawaten pillgha , qayughllak tamaghhaani aapqangit Jesus-em allaaghlluwhaghtillghi . Ilangi yuget pikat , " John-nguuq Paaptaayesta , unguvaamaaq enkaam esgha aghtughyaghqaanghillelek allaaghlluwhaghtilleghmun . "
Iwernga ilangit yuget pikat , " Elijah-nguuq . " Ilangit pikat , " Uuknaliqistenguuq , neghighluku uuknaliqistestun ayuquq . "
Herod-em nagaqughluku pikaq , " John-nguuq Paaptaayesta , naasqwightestekaqa iwernga unguvaamaaq ! "
Qavnganghhaq Herod-em kayagutkaqegkanga John tuguluku , asighqesluku anusimingllaghtestekaa . Tawaten pistekaa , qayughllak John-em piighaataqaa Herod whaten , " Liilightuusamnni anaggusimaaten tugulleghpegun anglegutegpek Philip-em nulighha Herodias . "
Enkaam Herodias-em ugumiyaguteghllakaqegkanga John repall tuqutesupigtekaqsaqanga . Iwernga pipagningitkaa qayughllak Herod-em tawaten pistepagningitkaa .
Herod-em alikegkaqegkanga John liisimakutmineng yuuk pinilghii , Kiyaghneghmun qaatkutngaghllalghii . Enkaam kelengakestengngwaaqaa sanayukatgu . Herod-em nagasugaqegkanga John qaywa seghleghyugaqeghngaaghmi naganneghminigu .
Taagken Herodias qenwatlu pilleghqangegkaq . Herod-em allgeghvini aghneq kaasan neqenghaghqestimalghii kavemem umiilwaaghitnun , pilluwaghtet umiilwaaghitnun , igleghutistengitnunllu Galilee-ghmiit .
Taagken paniga Herodias-em iteghluni neghuullghiinun tukalegaqaq . Herod-enkut aqelqaqullghiit elngaatall efquqegkaat . Enkaam umiilgem pikaa aghnaghaq , " Sameng alngunak tungsighvikegkuvnga tuunelleqamken . "
Akeqegkaallu whaten , " Ipapestaaq tuunelleqamken sameng alngunak tungsiquvek , talwa umiilgutimalleghma aklungingan avellgha ! "
Taagken aghnaghaq aanluni naani aapsaghtuqaa , " Sameng tungsighnaqsinga ? " Naangan pikaa , " John-em Paaptaayestem naasqwa tungsighhu . "
Aghnaghaq agliighwaghlluni umiilegmun tungsighvikegkaa , " Whaa maaten , John-em Paaptaayestem naasqwa piyugaqa qayuutaghraagkun lliluku ! "
Umiilek elngaatall qivghughllakaq iwernga saluku ighlekligu , qayughllak akeqngwaaqaqegkanga aqelqalghutni nagatestekluki .
Enkaam tawaninginaq umiilgem kayagtekaa kelengakista tagitesqesluku John-em naasqwa . Kelengakista aanluni anusimingllaghvigmun aglaqaq John-em naasqwa kepnaluku .
Naasquq qayuutaghraagkun lliluku aglaalluku aghnaghaghmun tuunegkaa . Enkaam aghnaghaam naaminun tuunegkaa .
John-em maligsaaghtengita nagaqughluku , yugusii aqfaluku lliifqaat .
Apostle-et uteghnightuulluteng Jesus-mun aapqiit apeghtughilleteng , naallghuqulleghteng , tughneghaghnengllu aanesqulleghteng yugneng .
Yugllagulghii tagimaghmengllu aghulaqumaghmengllu pilghiit repall Jesus-enkut maligsaaghtekullghiit neghepagningiitkat . Enkaam maligsaaghteni pikii , " Natmun aghulaqelta paaghqillghanun , elpesiqun meghnaaliightesqellusi . "
Enkaam angyakun paaghqillghanun aghulaqegkat ellnginaghhaaghhnaluteng ,
iwernga yulghutem esghaqiit aghulaqelghiit . Liisimakluki navek pinaqutangit , ketanqusnaq naayvam esnengakun maligtekiit . Nenun nallangiinneghata legan yuget maligtaqegkangit . Kaatkat takukameggnun ingyaghaghlluki Jesus-enkut .
Jesus-em angyameng uuglluni quutmun yulghutet esghaghluki nangllegyagutkii , qayughllak penniighestun penniighniightengilngughestun ayuqelghiit . Enkaam allaaghhiinaghmeng apeghtughtaakii .
Whanikupigsagu maligsaaghtengita takuluku Jesus pikaat , " Maana paaghqituq , whanikughllagaallu . Yuget aglaghtuutesqiki piitesighaghtenunllu , nengiighhaghnunllu . Ellmeggneng neqengyaghtughlit neqhyaghqameng . "
Iwernga Jesus-em pikii , " Elpesi neghyaghqaliteki . " Aaptekaat , " Tukfighiyaghtughtesugsikuut 200 denarii-m akinganeng neqekrangllameng neghesqelluki ? "
Jesus-em aaptekii , " Naten uglaghqakaan neqekrangllalgutsi ? Enta ivaghiightek . " Naalkusameng ungipaatkaat , " Taawa tallimat neqekrangllat , maalghuklu iqallugek . "
Taagken Jesus-em maligsaaghteminun qafsinkaghtiita aqumestesqegkii vegaaghqun .
Enkaam aqumuutkat 100-ngwaaqluteng 50-ngwaaqluteng .
Jesus-em tuguluki tallimat neqekrangllat , maalghuklu iqallugek , quulmun sivuglluni iyamsiqayugvikegkaa Kiyaghneq . Taagken neqekrangllat iiggmineng aavgughluki maligsaaghteminun tunquqii uyegtesqelluki . Iqallugeklu iigmineng aavgughlukek tunqughtestekii .
Qamagtengngwaaghluni neghuutkaq kepsuulluni .
Taagken maligsaaghtet tugulaqiit qula maalghuk siipneqluku pasketet esleqngalghiit kagimleghughtekaneng neqekrangllaneng , iqallugnengllu .
Yuget neghuutkat 5,000-nguftut , kesutkegpenaki aghnatlu taghnughhaatlu .
Legan taaqut Jesus-em maligsaaghteni qelqii angyakun igleghtekestiisqelluki Bethsaida-mun , naayvam inglunganilngughmun . Taagken ellngan yulghutet aglaghtuutestekii nengitnun .
Aglaghtuutesamiki yughaghyaghtuqaq qemimun .
Unugmi taakwani angyat naayvamelluki Jesus ellnginaghhaakaq quutmi .
Esghaqii malighsaaghteni aygughnaqutkelghiit yaavuqumeng , qayughllak anuqliiskangi . Akulegkeni three-kellaagenkuk six-ekellaagenkuk unaanguluku , takukii meghem qaayngakun piyugmeng . Naghughhnaqaqiillu
esghaqaat meghqun piyulghii . Sumeghmeggni taghneghaaniluku araghllakat .
Qamaglluteng alingruughutkat . Tawaninginaq Jesus-em pikii , " Ilutughtek ! Whanganguunga , alingegpenasi . "
Legan angyamun uugtuq ellmaaragllugughtekaq . Maligsaaghtet saghiighayugllakat ,
qayughllak paninang liigikigalkangat Jesus kinangutanga , qaywa esghapagngaaghmegteggu neqekrangllat nulastekangi . Tawatetkaalghiit qayughllak salin umyugiit reghiigalnguut .
Taagken nagneqat naayvam inglunganun enkaam Gennesaret-kun tamlagluteng angyaghteng petukaat .
Legan angyaghteng unitaat yuget liisuqnginaamaan Jesus pikaat .
Enkaam kelkaghtaarragkiiqat Jesus kaasimaniluku . Jesus navek piyaghngaan qinuyuget aglaataqegkangit allighiitgun ellnganun .
Jesus kaanneghmini neghllagnunllu , nenunllu , eslamelngughnun akilpegaghvignun aglaghaqelghii . Enkaam yuget tagitaqegkangit qinuyuget akilpegaghvignun Jesus-mun naallghutesqelluki . Jesus-mun maniguututkiit qinuyugnun waran saaftesqelluku kenii , enkaam qamaglluteng saaftilghiit naallghutkat .
Pharisees-etlu ilangillu apeghtughikayuget Liilightuusaneng Jerusalem-emeng pit , Jesus-em uvitanganun qerngughutkat .
Esghaqiit maligsaaghtengan ilangi uughtughpenateng neghelghiit . Uughtullghilnguut Pharisees-et pisqellghistun .
( Pharisees-etlu Jews-etlu qamaglluteng neghyaghqaanghilnguut wetkuqun sivukluteng uughtughwaaghluteng , qayughllak sivuneghmeng apeghtuusiit atuqngukangit .
Talwa akilpegaghvigmeng tagineghmeggni neghigalnguut wetku sivukluten ukmangighsaghwaaghaqelghiit . Ilangillu sivuneghmeng apeghtuusalghutangit atuqngukangit . Atuqfagilgamegtiki qayuusiteng , sagneteng , siilut gaaghusiteng sangighqughwaaghaqegkangit . )
Enkaam Pharisees-etlu apeghtughikayugetlu Liilightuusaneng aaptekaat Jesus , " Sangameng maligsaaghteten uughtughpenateng neghaqat ? Sivunemta apeghtuusiit atuqigatiit . "
Jesus-em kiimsiqii , " Elqughllusi Isaiah-m uuknaliqutkumakangisi piniiyugneghni elpesi . Whaten igaqaaguq , ' Kiyaghneq piiq , " Ukut yuget akuzitmegteggun quulvaghaqaatnga , nakaan ilumegteggun .
Temngi manigughaqaatnga , qayughllak apeghtuusaqaqiit liilightuusangllaqateng katam whanga Liilightuusaqepiglleghhiistun . " '
Enkaam elpesi Kiyaghneghem Liilightuusii pakigluki qaatkaqasi yuget apeghtuusiit . "
Jesus-em nagneghutkii , " Pakigillepiguusi Kiyaghneghem Liilightuusiitnun qaatkepigesnaghnaluki elpesi katam apeghtuusasi .
Una esgha usputaq tawaten pilleghpesinun : Moses-em aapqaqii Kiyaghneghem Liilightuusii whaten pilghiit , ' Quulvaghluku atanllu naanllu . ' Whatenllu pikaaguq , ' Kitum alngunak atanillu naanillu seghlequuqumikek tuqutellengyaghqaaguq . '
Iwernga elpesi allanguut apeghtughillesi . Whaten piiqusi , ' Yugemnguq atani nalighmeng naani whaten piyaghngaaghmigu , " Kayusiitusighqalguunga elpenun iwernga tuunaanghitaqa qayughllak Corban-nguuq . " ' ( Corban whaten pisiiguq , siingenllu Kiyaghneghmun akequsaqumaaqa . )
Tawaten pilleghpesigun apeghtughaqasi yuget kayusiinneghisaghngaatki atangitlu naangitlu pisqelluki .
Enkaam pakigaqasi Kiyaghneghem akuzitangi , apeghtuusaqepigesnaghnaluki yugnun elpesi katam akuzitesi . Tamaakut temngi usputaagut , uglaapigtut sangwaat piiqegkesi . "
Taagken Jesus-em yulghutet ellminun tagsinqiglluki pikii , " Qamagtengngwaaghlusi nagallusi liigikiteggu sameng pitka .
Yuuk neghegkaan nukeggnaghqigataa , seghletun sumeghtaghallghan , sallghanllu nukeggnaghqaqaa .
Sigutelgukufsi nagatusighqameng , nagatek ! "
Jesus-em unilluki yulghutet iteghyan maligsaaghtengita aaptekaat ungipaghaan sameng pisiitanga .
Jesus-em pikii , " Elpesillu liigikigatsii ? Sangwaa alngunak yugem neghaqegkanga nukeggnaghqusighqaanghituq ellnganun ,
qayughllak neghegkii ighsaqghwanun pinaanghitut . Aqsaqghwanun piiqut enkaam yugusiineng aanaqut . " ( Tawaten pilleghmikun Jesus-em aapghwaa neqet qamaglluteng neghyaghqaaniluki . )
Pikiillu , " Yugem qamaken ilumineng aanestekaan nukeggnaghqestaqaa .
Qaamken yugem ilunganeng aanaqut : sumeghtaghalleluget , nengughtegpenani kitumeng alngunak atuqilleq , teglegniiq , yugtaq ,
gelgaghniiq , pakigniiq , alngunak seghletun pilleq , puughti , kayngusaghaatelleq , aqina , yulgutmeng iqlengiqutki , qukaayugta , temngitwha .
Tamaakut qamaglluteng seghleghet yugem ilunganeng aanegkat nukeggnaghqikayuguut . "
Taagken Jesus aghulaqegkaq Tyre-m tunganganun , kaalluni mangteghamun iitqaq . Kitumun alngunak nallukesuguyaqanga kaatelleni , iwernga ilangita liisimakegkaat .
Aghnam Gentile-em , allgeqam Phoenicia-mi , Syria-melngughmi nagaquqaa Jesus kaasimaniluku . Paniggaa ilumikun tughneghalek . Enkaam aglaragkiighluni Jesus-mun segesqughlluni manungakun , maniguutkaq aanestaghtesqelluku tughneghaq panigmineng .
Iwernga Jesus-em pikaa , " Taghnughhaat sivukluteng neghesaghqaagut , qayughllak anaggutngaaq taghnughhaat neqngit tuguluki qikminun miluuskumeng . "
Aghnam kiimsiqaa , " Aa-a , Ataneq , talwa qikmit tipelem asinganilnguut neghaqut taghnughhaat ifkaghqellghitneng ! "
Enkaam Jesus-em pikaa , " Naqamqun tawaten kiimsighaghpenga aglaghhaaten , tughneghaq aanumaaq panigpeneng ! "
Aghnaq neminun aglaghyalghiimi paniga ingaghmeteftuq qavaghvigmi , taawa llaaghan tughneghaq aanumalghii paniganeng .
Taagken Jesus aghulaqegkaq Tyre-meng . Sidon-kunllu , Qula Neghllagteggunllu aagluni Naayvamun Galilee-mun pikaq .
Yuget ilangita , yuuk nagaquusigalnguq talwa akuziyiilnguq tagilluku Jesus-mun nangllegsiitkaat saaftesqelluku .
Enkaam Jesus-em awiitutkaa yulghutneng . Sivukluku tekghegni sigutegkenun kanaghllukek , taagken iqillukek qesighluki iiggeni , ulunga saaftekaa .
Taagken sivuglluni qilagmun aneghpakaghluni yuuk pikaa , " Ephphatha ! " ( Taana whaten pisiilghii , " Reghightek ! " )
Tawaninginaq yugem sigutkek reghiqak , ulungallu piniightekaq , aga akuzinginaamaghmi pikaq akuziyiilliqegpenani .
Taagken Jesus-em ineghtengngwaaqii kitumun alngunak ungipaqefqaan pisqelluku , iwernga ineghtaataghyisteng wata ungipaqegkaat .
Nagaquullghiit tamaakut elngaatall saghiighayugllakat , pikat , " Uum yugem sallgha qamaglluni piniperewaaghuuq ! Talwa nagaquusigalnguut nagaquusagutestii , akuziyiilnguutlu akuziyagutestii ! "
Taam kingungiighhaaneng yulghuteghllak qerngughullaataqaq . Neghyaghqaqraggiighusata Jesus-em maligsaaghteni tagsighluki pikii ,
" Ukut nangllegyagutepigtanka . Whangamninnaqneghmeng pingayuni aghneghni neghyaghqiighutut .
Nengitnun aglaghtestekumki neghestegpenaki tumemi taakwani ulleghaallequt , qayughllak ilangi uyavaneng tagilaghaatkaagut . "
Maligsaaghtengita aaptekaat , " Maani paaghqituq naken neqengnaqesta whaten uglaghqakalghiinun naamayaghqameng ? "
Jesus-em aaptekii , " Naten uglaghqakaan neqekrangllalgutsi ? " Kiimsiqaat , " Maaghraghvinleguut neqekrangllat . "
Enkaam Jesus-em yulghuteghllaget qelqii aqumuutesqelluki nunakun . Taagken tuguluki taakut maaghraghvinlek neqekrangllat Kiyaghneq iyamsiqayugvikluku , kagimlluki tuunegkii maligsaaghteminun uyegtesqelluki . Enkaam maligsaaghtengi uyegtekat .
Qafsinkuuraghhaghnengllu amsakalghiineng iqallulget . Jesus-em iyamsiqayugvikluku Kiyaghneq , taakutlu maligsaaghteminun uyegtesqegkii .
Entaqun 4,000-nguut yuget kepsuulluteng neghuutkat . Taagken maligsaaghtet qerngughsaqmegteggu siipneq , maaghraghvinlek pasketet imiqiit esleqaghaghlluki .
Jesus-em yulghuteghllaget aghulaquutesluki , enkaam maligsaaghtekullghiit angyamun uuglluteng aghulaqnginaamaghmeng pikat Dalmanutha-mun .
Tamaanlenguut Pharisees-et takuluku Jesus aaghtiiraaqaat . Pikaat , " Allaaghlluwhaghtighllagi , enkaam ugpeqelleqaghput aghtughyaghqaanghillghen Kiyaghneghmeng pingutanga . " Tawaten pikaat anagniilqavigighnaluku .
Jesus-em aneghpagluni pikii , " Sangameng maaten aghneghem yugi allaaghlluwhaghtilleghmeng tungsighaqat ? Ipa ungipaatamsi , allaaghlluwhaghtinnaanghitamsi . "
Taagken unilluki , angyamun uuglluni inglunganun naayvam aghviqat .
Maligsaaghtet puygumalghiit neqekrangllameng kelqegpenateng , ataasighhaaftuq kelqegkaat angyamelnguq .
Jesus-em kelengasaaqii , " Kelengangwaaghlusi yeast-atangitneng Pharisees-et , yeast-atanganengllu Herod-em . "
Taagken ellmeggneng aleghquutkat , " Tawaten piinkut qayughllak neqekranglliilnguukut . "
Jesus-em akuzitkengngukangi apeghtuusiit Pharisees-et , apeghtuusiillu Herod-em . Liisimakegkangi maligsaaghtengan liigikenghilkangat akuzitkegkaa enkaam aaptekii , " Sangan neqekranglliinnilusi pitsi ? Paninang nallukaqetsilluu , liigikigatetsilluu ? Umughtakii umyugasi ?
Iyelgulghiisi , esghiigatsii ? Sigutelguusi , nagaquusigatsii ? Neqamikenghistekii
tallimat neqekrangllat kagimtekanka 5,000-enun ? Qafsinat pasketet siipneghmeng imighesteki ? " Kiimsiqaat , " Qula maalghuk . "
Jesus-em aaptekii , " Maaghraghvinlek neqekrangllat kagimtaqngamki 4,000-enun , qafsinat pasketet siipneghmeng imighesteki ? " Kiimsiqaat , " Maaghraghvinlek . "
Aaplaataqii , " Sangafsi paninang liigikigatsi ? "
Bethsaida-mun kaasata ilangita yuget Jesus-mun tagitkaat ayaakaq yuuk , saaftaghtesqelluku .
Jesus-em ayaakaq tasluqluku aghulaqutkaa nemeng . Taagken qesighlukek iiskek saaflukek aaptekaa , " Sameng esghaanneghisiin ? "
Yugem sivuglluni yugsughaluni pikaa , " Aa-a , esghaghanka yuget , iwernga esghaqaaluteng llangaqa uqfiget piyugullghiit . "
Jesus-em allameng saaftekakek yugem iiskek . Maatenllaam yuuk esghaannaqeghllagyalghiimi , qemall esghaasagunneqigtuq whateghlluwaaq .
Jesus-em agliisqegkaa nenganun , pikaallu , " Aghuliifqaavek taakwani nemi . "
Taagken Jesus-enkut maligsaaghtekullghiit aghulaqegkat nenun tunganganilngughnun Caesarea Philippi-em . Tumemi taakwani maligsaaghteni aaptekii , " Kinangunilunga yuget piiqatnga ? "
Kiimsiqaat , " Ilangita piiqaaten John-nguniluten Paaptaayesta , ilangita Elijah-nguniiqaaten , enkaam ilangita naliqniluten uuknaliqistet . "
Aaptekii , " Elpesi kinganguniiqestengnga ? " Peter-em pikaa , " Christ-anguuten . "
Taagken Jesus-em ineghtengngwaaqii , " Kitumun alngunak apeghpenanga . "
Taagken Jesus-em apeghtuqestaqii maligsaaghteni , " Ighnegha Yugem elngaatall ikfiqepestaaghyaghqaaguq , ighsaksaghqaqaatlu siivanlleghet , chief priest-et , apeghtughikayugetlu Liilightuusaneng . Taagken tuqulleqaat iwernga pingayiitangani aghneghem unguvaghllequq . "
Whateghlluwaaq ungipaatkii . Peter-em iqitulluku aghyuuqaa .
Iwernga Jesus-em qiivluni esghaqii maligsaaghteni taagken Peter aghyuuqaa . Pikaa , " Awiiten whangamneng , Tughneghaq . Sumeghtaghalleghten yugem sumeghtaghalqii , Kiyaghneghem sumeghtaghalqenghitii ! "
Taagken Jesus-em yulghuteghllagetlu maligsaaghtenillu tagsighteghluki pikii , " Kitum alngunak maligsukuminga , ellmineng katam piyukelleni peglluki , qaquurani uyamigluku maligllinga .
Kitum alngunak yuguliyukumigu unguvalleni iflayaghqaqaa . Iwernga kitum alngunak iflakumigu unguvalleni whanga apalluqlunga , Pinilghiitlu Ungipat apalluqluki yuguliyaghqaqaa .
Sangwaangam yugem pinighqusiqelleqagu piliilluku nunaghllak , iflakumikek unguvasigni ?
Sameng始ngam yuuk veghtusiqelleqa unguvasigminun ?
Maaten aghneghem yugi ataasiighmenneghitut Kiyaghneghmun , seghleghqumanguutlu . Maani aghneghni kitum alngunak kaynguyaguskanganga , apeghtuusankallu , whangallu Ighneghani Yugem kaynguyagulleqaqa tagikuma aghtughyaghqaanghillelighlunga Atamneng kelqelluki agleghnalghiit yaqulget . "
Nagneghutkiillu whaten , " Ipa ungipaatamsi , ilasi nekevghallghiit whani tuqunaanghitut kenlanga esghalleghmeggnun Ataneghpagullgha Kiyaghneghem tagikan aghtughyaghqaanghilleghtuumaghmi . "
Aghvinlek aghneq atughluku , Jesus-em kelqelluki Peter-enkut , James-enkut , John-enkut , mayuqat uusqalghiimun naayghamun . Ellnginaghhaalghiit tawani Jesus-em yugusii allangughtekaq esghaamallghitni .
Aatkii qelmeghtekat qatetun , qaatghataghaghluteng kitum alngunak nunami qateghsaghaqegkanganeng .
Taagken maligsaaghtet esghapakagket Elijah-nkuk Moses-enkuk aliighlutek aleghquqangak Jesus .
Enkaam maligsaaghtet alingruughuteghllakat repall sameng pipagningitkat . Taagken Peter-em pikaa Jesus , " Apeghtughista , itagnapigtuq whaanlenguukut ! Pingayut azigutat nekefnaqaput , elpenunllu Moses-munllu Elijah-munllu . "
Taagken qilawaaq aliighluni saapegkii . Qilawaaghmeng mem pikii , " Unanguuq piniqepigtekegka Ighneqa ; nagataqiteggu ! "
Taagken yugsughaaghaghsalghiimeng Moses-enkuk Elijah-nkuk aviituk , Jesus-nginaghhaq tawanteftuq .
Ukigutkelluku naayghameng Jesus-em ungipaqesnanighwaaqaa esghaatellghat kenlanga Ighnegha Yugem tuqulleghmeng unguvaghtekan .
Enkaam ineghsisteng qaatkegkaat , iwernga ellnginaaghhneghmeggni piiqelghiit , " Samengtuq pisiiwa ' Tuqulleghmeng unguvaghtelleq ? ' "
Taagken aaptekaat Jesus , " Sangan apeghtughikayuget Liilightuusaneng piiqatgu Elijah sivukluni tagipestaaghyaghqaaniluku ? "
Kiimsiqii , " Ipanguuq Elijah sivukluni tagipestaaghyaghqaaguq yataaghqennaluku sangwaa tamaghhaan . Aaptaghllamsi , naqam sangan Akuzitet Igaqegkat pikaqatgu , Ighnegha Yugem ikfiqeghllagyaghqaaniluku , sasiinghilngughestunllu kiyaghusaghqaaniluku ?
Iwernga ungipaannaqamsi Elijah tagikaaguq , yuget piyukelleghmegestun pikaqaat katam tawaten Akuzitet Igaqegkat pinaqnillghistun . "
Takuyaqmegteki ilangi maligsaaghtet , yulghuteghllak tawantuteftuq . Ilangita apeghtughikayuget Liilightuusaneng aaghtiiraaghaqeftiit maligsaaghtet .
Legan yuget esghaghluku Jesus saghiighayugllagluteng paayghaghlluku quyakegkaat .
Jesus-em maligsaaghteni aaptekii , " Sameng aaghtiiraaghaqesteki apeghtughikayuget Liilightuusaneng ? "
Yulghuteghllaget akulngitneng yugem kiimsiqaa , " Apeghtughista , ighneqa tagisaghaqa elpenun , qayughllak ilumikun tughneghalguuq . Taam tughneghaam akuzisigataa .
Kaatepiggneghminigu iqustaqaa , qaanghallu nuvaglliighqestaqaa , gguutngi terqitaagtaghtestaqii , teveghqwaastaqaallu . Maligsaaghtegpenun kayagutaghsaghaqa tughneghaq aanestesqelluku iwernga pipagningitaat . "
Jesus-em maligsaaghteni pikii , " Elpesi yugni ugpeqillghitusi ! Naten tagkaan elpesininnaqsinga ugpeqesqellunga ? Mekelghiiq whavek tagiteggu ! "
Enkaam tagitkaat . Legan tughneghaam esghaghluku Jesus , mekelghiiq iqusluku sayugpagtaghtestekaa . Tamaani temngi ullghitaperewaaghtestekaa , qaanghallu nuvaglliightestekaa .
Jesus-em aaptekaa atanga , " Qavngaghhaaneng tawateta ? " Kiimsiqaa , " Mekestaghhaatmineng ima .
Uglaghngaan kenghegnunllu meghmunllu iqustaqsaghaa tuqusqelluku . Piyaghqaakuvek nangllegyagullutung kayusiitaghtikung ! "
Jesus-em pikaa , " Sangavek tawaten pizin , ' Piyaghqaakuvek ' ? Kiyaghneghem sangwaa alngunak piyaghqaqaa yugmun ugpelghiimun . "
Tawaninginaq mekelghiighem atanga iglagtuluni pikaq , " Ugpeghtunga , iwernga ugpelleghtughtaghaqaghnga ! "
Jesus-em esghaghluki wata yuget tagilaghaallghiit qevuulluku aghyuuqaa tughneghaq , " Uyuq tughneghaq tuuslaghtestilghiillu akuzistingigalnguqlu qelghamken aani mekelghiighmeng , allamengllu itefqaavek ellnganun pilghaaten . "
Tughneghaam mekelghiiq araghaataghtesteghllagluku , sayugpagtaghtesteghllagluku , aanegkaq . Legan mekelghiiq esghaqaaluni tuqukaq repall esghapalghiit pikat , " Tuqumaaq ! "
Iwernga Jesus-em iiggakun tuguluku kayusiitkaa nekevesqelluku enkaam nekevegkaq .
Jesus mangteghamun iteghyan ellnginaghhaaghsameng maligsaaghtengita aaptekaat , " Sangan whangkuta aanesneghmeng aghtughesteggu tughneghaq ? "
Jesus-em kiimsiqii , " Tawatelnguq tughneghaq yughaghhiinaam aanesaghqaqaa , saam alla pinaanghitaa . "
Taagken nemeng aghulaqluteng nagneqat Galilee-kun . Jesus-em kitumun alngunak liisimakesugumangitkaa naantuleni ,
qayughllak apeghtuungukangi maligsaaghteni tuqulleghqamineng . Pikii , " Ighnegha Yugem tuguluku tuunelleqaat yugnun tuqutesqelluku , naqamenraq pingayut aghneghet atughluki unguvaghllequq . "
Iwernga liigikumangilkangat apeghtuusaa sameng pisiitanga , enkaam aapsugumangilkangat tetugluteng .
Capernaum-emun kaalluteng , iteghaasameng Jesus-em aaptekii , " Igleghutkelluku sangwaa aaghtiiraaghutkaqesteggu ? "
Kiimsighyugumangilkangat , qayughllak igleghutkelluku aaghtiiraaghutkat nalighteng angelleghpigaayaghqaatanga .
Jesus-em aqumluni , qula maalghuk siipneqluku maligsaaghteni tuqlughluki pikii , " Kina alngunak sivuliighsukumi nekeglli kinguliiluni , qepghaghtengulillu tamaghhaanun . "
Taagken taghnughhaq tuguluku nekevestekaa qukiitgun . Qelluku pikii ,
" Kitum alngunak tugukliqumigu taghnughhaghhaq uutun ayuqelghii whanga apalluqlunga , tuguklighaqaanga whanga . Kitum alngunak tugukliquminga , tuguklighlleqaa Ataka kayagtikaq whangamneng . "
Mulugpenateng John-em pikaa , " Apeghtughista , yuuk esghaamaaghput ateghpegun aanesqulghii tughneghaghneng . Ineghsimaaghput qayughllak whangkunnun ilatnganghilnguq . "
Jesus-em pikii , " Ineghtegpenaan ! Qayughllak kina alngunak atemkun allaaghlluwhaghtingukumi seghletun akuzitkelghaghtughnaanghitaanga .
Kitum alngunak kipullegmun pinghilkanginkut , qepghalgutkaghput .
Ipa ungipaatamsi , kitum alngunak meghsikangisi whanga pikutemneng , ipapestaaq akileghtuusangyaghqaaguq . "
" Ataasiq taghnughhaq ugpeqingalghii whangamneng , yugem seghleghqestekagu , pinighataghaghnayaghtuq taana yuuk meghmun ateghsaqumi uyaqghwakun qaamqaghfikluku uyghagllagmeng .
Iiggegpek seghleghqestekangaten kepnaketen . Pinighataghaghnayaghtuten yugusighpek nalighnegha iflakuvgu unguvalleghpek iflalleghqaaneng quunperugllak . Taana pinighataghaghtuq inglugtun iiggelighluten hell-mun aglalleghqaghpeneng . Tawani kumaghughngalghii keneq qaamyaghqaanghituq .
Tawani ' kinguget neghegkayuget yugmeng tuquyaghqaanghitut , kumaghughngalghiillu keneq qaamyaghqaanghituq ' .
Itegaghpek seghleghqestekangaten , iiknaketen ! Pinighataghaghnayaghtuten yugusighpek nalighnegha iflakuvgu unguvalleghpek iflalleghqaaneng quunperugllak . Taana pinighataghaghtuq inglugtun itegalighluten hell-mun miluutelleghqaghpeneng .
Tawani ' kinguget neghegkayuget yugmeng tuquyaghqaanghitut , kumaghughngalghiillu keneq qaamyaghqaanghituq ' .
Iyegpek seghleghqestekangaten , ipugnaken ! Pinighataghaghnayaghtuten Ataneghpagullghanun Kiyaghneghem iitquvek inglupigaghmeng iiskelluten , inglugtun iyelguluten hell-mun miluutelleghqaghpeneng .
Tawani ' kinguget neghegkayuget yugmeng tuquyaghqaanghitut , kumaghughngalghiillu keneq qaamyaghqaanghituq ' .
Tamaghhaghmi taghyulighllequq keneghmeng .
" Taghyuq pinightuq iwernga taghyughningiiskan , naten elpesi taghyughnighllaataghnayaghesteggu ? Taghyughningiitegpenasi , nekeggmetullusillu . "
Taagken Jesus aghulaqegkaq tamaaken nunameng . Aglaghluni nunamun aatqelghiimun Judea-mun , aghviqakek Kiiwek Jordan-ek . Yulghutem qerngughfiklaataqaa enkaam apeghtuqii piiqelleghmitun .
Ilangita Pharisees-et takuluku anagniilqavigighnaqutkelluku aaptekaat , " Liilightuusamnni itagnaghtaa yugem nuliini pegtekumigu ? "
Jesus-em kiimsiqii aaptemmeng , " Sangaawami Moses-em qelghusaa ? "
Kiimsiqaat , " Moses-em pilleghqalitkaqaa yuuk pegtusim igii imighluki pegtesqelluku nulighha . "
Jesus-em pikii , " Tawaten Moses-em Liilightuusalitkaqiisi pineghllugllagutegpesineng .
Iwernga nunangllaghyuwhaalleghmeng ' Kiyaghneghem ulimakaqaak yuuklu aghnaqlu . '
Taana apalluqluku yugem unillukek atanillu naanillu nuliighminun lliighwaaghyaghqaaguq .
Enkaam maalghugunanighllequk , ataasiighllequk .
Tamaaken apalluqluku Kiyaghneghem qerngughutestekakek yeqay yugem pellghututesneghillikek . "
Mangteghamun iteghaasameng maligsaaghtet aaptekaat Jesus tamaaken pillghaneng .
Jesus-em pikii , " Yugem nuliini peglluku allaneng nulightuqumi , taawa gelgaghniighllequq .
Tawateghpigaq aghnam ugini peglluku allaneng ugiiqumi , taawa gelgaghniighllequq . "
Ilangita yuget tagitkiit taghnughhaat Jesus-mun saafluki quyastesqelluki , iwernga maligsaaghtet ineghtekiit tagitilghiit .
Jesus-em esghaghluki seghleghyagulluki maligsaaghteni pikii , " Taghnughhaat tagilit whangamnun . Ineghtegpenaki , qayughllak Ataneghpagullgha Kiyaghneghem taghnughhaghestun ayuqelghiit pikaat .
Ipa ungipaatamsi , kitum alngunak tuguklinghilkumigu Ataneghpagullgha Kiyaghneghem taghnughhaghtun , iteghnaanghituq . "
Taagken taghnughhaat tugaaqluki , saaftaqluki quyastekii .
Jesus igleghhneqigtaquqlu , yugem ketanqusnaq takuluku manungakun segesqughlluni aaptekaa , " Pinilghii Apeghtughista , naten salunga kenlengilnguq unguvalleq allgeghhnayaghsikun ? "
Jesus-em aaptekaa , " Sangan pinighnizinga ? Kina alngunak pininghituq , Kiyaghneghhiinaaguq pinilghii .
Liilightuusat liisimakaten : ' Yugtaghpenang ; gelgaghniighpenang ; teglegpenang ; iqlengiqutkegpenaki yuget ; puughtigpenang ; quulvaghlukek atanllu naanllu . ' "
Yugem pikaa , " Apeghtughista , ima nukalpigaatemneng qaatkengngwaanka taakut Liilightuusat . "
Jesus-em piniqepiglluku qiivluku pikaa , " Ataasiiguq piyaghqan . Akikughyaghtughhu qamaglluku saghyan , enkaam akinga tunqughnaken aklumalghiinun . Tawaten pikuvek aklungillequten qilagmi . Taagken maligsaghtughnakevnga . "
Tawaten piyatni yuuk nulgiiqaq , iqitkaq iilqepiglluni qayughllak aklungitepiglleghhii .
Jesus yugsughaluni maligsaaghteni pikii , " Piyaqnapigtuq aklungilngughni itelleghqaa Ataneghpagullgha Kiyaghneghem ! "
Tawaten piyisteng maligsaaghtet saghiighayukat . Jesus-em pilaataqii , " Taghnughhaghni , piyaqnapigtuq itelleghqaq Ataneghpagullghanun Kiyaghneghem !
Piyaqniisaghqaaguq camel-em suflughutelleghqaa sikuum iiyngakun , aklungilnguum yugem itelleghqaaneng Ataneghpagullghanun Kiyaghneghem . "
Maligsaaghtet wataqaaghaq saghiighayukat , enkaam ellmeggneng aapqughaaghutkat , " Kinangam yugulillengelleqa ? "
Jesus-em qiivluki pikii , " Yuget piyaghqaqenghilkangit , Kiyaghneghem piyaghqaqii . "
Taagken Peter-em pikaa , " Esghaqaghqutqun , sangwaa qamaglluku unilluku maliglleghaatamken . "
Jesus-em pikii , " Ipa ungipaatamsi , kitum alngunak uniskumiki mangteghani , anglegutni , naani , atani , avaqutani , nunani apalluqlunga whanga , Pinilghiitlu Ungipat ,
allgeghutaaghaghyaghqaaguq whani kiyaghtaalleghmi . Mangteghaa , anglegutangi , naanga , avaqutii , nunanga , nulaghllagyaghqaagut ; tamaakunun maligulluku amyuutkellengyaghqaaguq . Taagken taakwaningani kenlengilngughmeng unguvallengyaghqaaguq .
Iwernga uglalghiit angelleghpigaat ukaliighsaghqaagut taagani , enkaam uglalghiit ukalighpigaat angelleghpigaaghsaghqaagut . "
Jesus aga sivungitnilnguq igleghanguluki tumetgun Jerusalem-emun ayuqelghiitgun . Maligsaaghtengi saghiighayukat , yugetlu alingumaghmeng maligtekaat . Jesus-em qula maalghuk siipneqluku maligsaaghteni aafulluki ungipaallaataqii salleghqamineng .
Pikii , " Nagatek , Jerusalem-ennaqukut . Tawani Ighnegha Yugem tuunelleqaat chief priest-enunllu apeghtughikayugnunllu Liilightuusaneng . Nanqiglluku tuqusaghqaanilleqaat , enkaam tuunelleqaat Gentile-enun .
Taakut legasiighwaatkelleqaat , qesiqulleqaat , kagsagmiglleqaat , tuqulleqaatlu . Pingayut aghneghet atughluki unguvaghllequq . "
Taagken James-enkuk John-enkuk , Zebedee-m ighneghegkenka takuluku Jesus pikaak , " Apeghtughista , elpenun sameng pisqesugtukung . "
Jesus-em aaptekakek , " Sasqesugestek whangamnun ? "
Kiimsiqaak , " Nighughqengngalghiimi Ataneghpagulleghpeni aqumegkuvek aqumelgusighyugamken , nalighpung aghenqigneghpenilluku , nalighpung saghumigneghpenilluku . "
Jesus-em pikakek , " Nallukaghtek sameng tungsilleghtek . Meghyaghqamneng qayuusimelngughmeng meghelleqestaak ? Paaptaayelleghqamtun paaptaayelleqestaak ? "
Kiimsiqaak , " Piyaghqaagukung . " Jesus-em pikakek , " Meghyaghqaqa qayuusimelnguq qaywa meghelleqaghtek , paaptaayellequteklu paaptaayelleghqamtun .
Iwernga whanga nakmiksaghqaqenghitanka kinkut aqumyaghqaatangi aghenqignemkunllu saghumignemkunllu , yataaghqutkat tamaakut aqumyaghqaagut . "
Taakut qula malighsaaghtet nagaqughlukek James-enkuk John-enkuk pillghak , ugumiyagutkagket .
Enkaam Jesus-em qerngughlluki pikii , " Liisimakasi Gentile-et igleghutistengita atanghutaqiit yuteng , aangwaaghughtekatlu yukeghqutaqiit .
Iwernga tawatesaghqaanghitusi elpesi . Nalighsi aangwaaghuyukumi qepghaghtenguli ilaminun ,
nalighsillu aangelleghpigaayukumi qepghaghtelaaghughlli tamanganun .
Talwa Ighnegha Yugem tagikaanghituq qepghaatesqelluni , tagikaaguq qepghaatinalunillu tuunalukullu unguvalleni yugulinaluki yulghutet . "
Taagken Jesus-enkut maligsaaghtekullghiit , yulghuteghllagetlu Jericho-mun kaalluteng , aghulaqegkat . Taawaanguq ayaakaq yuuk , aatgha Bartimaeus , ighnegha Timaeus-em aqumluni tumet saningitgun tungsighraghaqelghii .
Nagaqughyamigu Jesus Nazareth-eghmii , tughwaaghniluku akilghuukaq , " Jesus ! Ighneghani David-em ! Nangllegyagutaghtinga ! "
Uglalghiim yugem aghyuuqaat nepiighesqelluku iwernga qevuutaghalluni akilghuukaq , " Ighneghani David-em , nangllegyagutaghtinga ! "
Jesus-em aghuliighluni pikii , " Tagisqiteggu . " Enkaam tuqlughluku ayaakaq pikaat , " Seghleghhalek , tuqlughaaten nekevi ! "
Qaasliik atkuyaaghegni mataghaghllukek nekefqaghlluni takukaa Jesus .
Jesus-em aaptekaa , " Sasqelluten piiqsin ? " Ayaakam kiimsiqaa , " Apeghtughista , esghaasagunneqigsugtunga . "
Jesus-em pikaa , " Igleghlleghhaaten , ugpeqilleghpek naallghutestaaten . " Tawaninginaq esghaasagutkaq taagken maligtekaa Jesus .
Tughaaghyalghiimeng Jerusalem-emun , kaatkat Bethphage-munllu Bethany-munllu , Mount Olives-mi . Taagken Jesus-em kayagtekakek maalghuk maligsaaghtegni nemun pisqellukek . Pikakek , " Kaataghesnaquftek esghaghlleqaghtek donkey-ghaq petugngalghii kitum alngunak igleghutkumangilkanga . Itemulluku taginnakesek .
Kitum alngunak aaptekangistek whaten , ' Sanaqestegnegu ? ' ungipaannakesek , ' Atanghem atuqsugaa . Taaqaghesnaqumigu veghutesnaaghaa . ' "
Enkaam nemun kaallutek tumenilluku esghaqaak donkey-ghaq petugngalghii mangtegham amigan tungangakun . Itemsimaluku
yuget nekevghataaghullghiit tawani aaptekagket , " Sangan itemutestegnegu donkey-ghaq ? "
Kiimsiqiik Jesus-em apeghtullghatun enkaam yuget nepiighutkagket .
Jesus-mun kaatulluku donkey-ghaq , qaasliit atkuyaatek teghikusam qaayngakun lliyagneki , Jesus uuglluni igleghtekaq .
Tamaakut yulghutet igleghullghiit tumetgun saaghquqiit qaasliit atkuyaateng , ilangit avayameng ququngalegmeng ikutaqluteng tumet saaghqughvikegkiit .
Jesus-em sivunganilnguutlu kingunganilnguutlu akilghuutkat , " Usuqnaghhalek Kiyaghneq ! Kiyaghneghem quyasligu tagilghii aatghakun Atanghem !
Kiyaghneghem quyasligu tagilghii ataneghpagullgha sivunemta David-em ! Usuqnaghhalek Kiyaghneq qulighpigaghmelnguq qilagmi ! "
Jesus kaalluni Jerusalem-emun , aglaqaq Temple-mun . Tawani sangwaa qamaglluku yuvghiiqaa . Whanikungulghii , kelqelluki qula maalghuk siipneqluku maligsaaghteni aglaqaq Bethany-mun .
Unaamingani , Bethany-meng uteghniitkelluku Jesus iyataqaq .
Uyavaneng esghaqaa figs-em uqfiga ququngaghtuqaq , enkaam esghaghyaghtuqaa figs-elgunayukan . Kaasaqminigu ququngaraaghinaaftuq , qayughllak salin figs-et piisugniilnguut .
Jesus-em uqfik pikaa , " Allamengllu kitum alngunak figs-etughviknaanghitaaten ! " Maligsaaghtengita nagatkaat .
Kaasameng Jerusalem-emun , Jesus , Temple-mun pikaq . Tawani aanesquqii tukfightulghiitlu akilpegalghiitlu . Manimeng naveghqughtet tipelngit ulleghquqii , aqumutiitlu qawaagmeng akilpegaghtet .
Nangaqaghsaghqaananightestekiillu kinkut alngunak sameng tugumiilget Temple-em manughaakun .
Taagken apeghtuqii yuget , " Kiyaghneq pikaaguq Akuzitni Igaqegkani , ' Mangteghaqa , yughaghviguyaghqaaguq tamaghhaanun yuganun nunam . ' Iwernga elpesi iighaghvigughtaghsi wayaghniightenun ! "
Chief priest-etlu , apeghtughikayugetlu Liilightuusaneng nagaqughluku tawaten pillgha , akuzimghhutkegkaat naten tuqutelleghqameng , naqam alikumaan . Alikegkaat , qayughllak qamaglluteng yulghuteghllaget saghiighayagutngukangit apeghiillghi .
Ighivgaghyagu Jesus-enkut maligsaaghtekullghiit aghulaqegkat Jerusalem-emeng .
Unaanguluku igleghutkelluku esghaqaat figs-em uqfiga palighwaaghumalghii akughhaghminun kenlanga .
Peter-em esghaghluku neqaatkaa Jesus-em pillgha . Enkaam pikaa , " Apeghtughista , ii-i , figs-em uqfiga ineghtengngwaaqan palighwaaghumaaq . "
Jesus-em pikii , " Ugpeqiteggu Kiyaghneq .
Ipa ungipaatamsi , kitum alngunak malghuklillngunani ilumikun , ugpeqegkumikillu akuzitni piyaghqaatangi , una naayghaq whaten pikumigu , ' Kelliinun aatghi , ' taawa apeghiighyaghqaaguq ellnganun .
Enkaam ungipaatamsi : sangwaa alngunak aklukegkaghsi yughaatkegkufsigu ugpeqluku allgeghsaghqaqutsi , taawa allgeghlleqaghsi .
Nekevneghpesini yughaghnalusi , seghevutaqiteki seghletun pistesi , enkaam Atagpesi qilagmelnguum seghevulleqii seghleghqellesi . "
Iwernga seghevutinghilkufsi , talwa Atagpesi qilagmelnguum seghevunnaanghitii seghleghqellesi .
Jesus-enkut maligsaaghtekullghiit kaanneqigtekat Jerusalem-emun . Jesus igleghsimaluku Temple-em manughaani , chief priest-etlu , apeghtughikayugetlu Liilightuusaneng , Elder-etlu takuluku
aaptekaat , " Saam pilleghqaakun aanesqughsiki akilpegaghtet ? Kitum qelellghakun tawaten pinguzin ? "
Jesus-em kiimsiqii , " Ungipaalleqamsi kitum qelelghakun tawaten pikaatka kiimsiqufsinga .
John-em paaptaayeghillgha Kiyaghneghmeng pingwaa , nalighmeng yugneng ? Ungipaatengnga . "
Ellmeggneng akuzimghhutkat , " Kiyaghneghmeng piknikumteggu , pilleqiinkut , ' Sangan始ngam ugpeqenghisteggu John ? '
Yugneng piknikumteggu yuget anguyiilleqiinkut . " ( Alingegkat yugneng , qayughllak yuget qamaglluteng ugpeqngukangat John uuknaliqistengutanga . )
Enkaam Jesus kiimsiqaat , " Nallukaghput . " Jesus-em pikii , " Whangallu ungipaannaanghitamsi kitum qelellghakun tawaten pikaatka . "
Taagken Jesus-em ungipaghaatetgun aleghquqii . Pikii , " Taawanguq yuuk piitesiighaqaq grapes-meng , mingllusiqaallu uvitanga piitesighaghvini . Laagutkakek grapes-mun qageghquusik , nekeftekaallu kelengakivigkaq . Taagken piitesighaghvini navghitkaa grapes-meng piitesighaghtenun nengitesqelluni , enkaam ellnga natmun aghulaqegkaq .
Saghnayaghqaaghsata ataasiq qepghaghteni kevgaqegkaa nengini grapes-et aqfasqelluki .
Kaasan taakut aflengakistet akuqaghluku qevutiighluku avangunaan aglaghtestekaat .
Kevgaqlaataqaa ilanga qepghaghteni . Taana naasqwakun kiitiquluku , kayngusaghaatestekaat .
Kevgaqiilaataqaq ilanganeng qepghaghtemi enkaam taana tuqutkaat . Ilangillu qepghaghtelghuteni kevgaqenghaki legan tawaten piiqegkangit , ilangit qevutiiqiit , ilangit tuququqiit .
" Qenwat ataasighhaaghtuq kevgaqsaghqaa , ighnegha piniqumtaagha . Kevgaqegkaa sumeghtaghaamaghmi whaten , ' Ighneqa siivakelleqaat . '
Iwernga taakut aflengakistet ilateng pikiit , ' Uum piliisaghqaqaa una piitesiighaghvik . Tuqutelteggu enkaam piitesiighaghvik whangkuta piliilleqaghput ! '
Enkaam akuqaghluku , tuqulluku yugusii egtekaat piitesiighaghvigmeng . "
Jesus-em aaptekii , " Salleqang始ngam piitesiighaghvilek ? Tagiluni navghitivikegkaqsaqenni taakut tuququghluki , enkaam piitesiighaghvini allanun navghilleqaa .
Atightiigasteggu una Akuzitni Igaqegkani ? ' Uyghak mangteghangllaghtet ighsakegkaat piyalghiimi megnunalleghpigaaftuq uyghak .
Taana Atanghem apeghiiqaqaa , Allaaghlluwhaghyugnapigtuq ! ' "
Jews-et igleghutistengita tuguyupigtekaqsaqangat , qayughllak liigikelghiit ungipaghaatetgun Jesus-em ellngit akuzitkaqeftii . Iwernga alingegkat yulghutneng enkaam unilluku aghulaqegkat .
Taam kingunganeng Jews-et igleghutistengita kayagtekiit ilangi Pharisees-etlu maligsaaghtengillu Herod-em anagniilqavigiisqelluku Jesus . Kayagtekiit anagniilqavigiisqelluku akuzillghakun .
Kaalluku pikaat , " Apeghtughista , liisimakamken ataasiighmetuten . Waakigataten yuget sumeghtaghallghit , talwa waakigataten yuget sanguyaghngaata , iwernga ipapighqelluten apeghtuusaqaqan Kiyaghneghem piyukellgha yugnun . Ungipaataghtikut , Kiyaghneghem Liilightuusaani elqughutngaa llivikilleghqaghput tax-eneng Caesar-mun ? Llivikiltaa-a nalighmeng pinghitelta ? "
Iwernga Jesus-em liisimakegkangi seghletun pingukangat enkaam pikii , " Sangama anagvigighnaqutkestengnga ? Manilitaghtengnga , esghaqaghlakun . "
Tuunyatni aaptekii , " Kitum gginaqagullu aatqagullu una ? " Kiimsiqaat , " Caesar-em . "
Jesus-em pikii , " Tuuniteki Caesar-mun tamaakut Caesar-em pingi . Tuuniteki Kiyaghneghmun tamaakut Kiyaghneghem pingi . " Enkaam saghiighayagutkaat Jesus .
Taagken ilangi Sadducees-et , Jesus-mun pikat . ( Tamaakut piiqelghiit tuqukat unguvaghyaghqaanghinniluki . )
Pikaat , " Apeghtughista , Moses-em Liilightuusangllaqaqiinkut whaten , ' Yuuk nuliilek avaqutigpenani tuqukan anglegutangan tuguyaghqaqaa aghnaq avaqutinnaluku anglegutni tuqukaq . '
Taawanguq maaghragvinlek yuget anglegutkullghiit . Nuyeklighpigaq nulightughluni avaqutigpenani tuqukaq .
Enkaam tuunglighhaan tugukaa aghnaq , iwernga ellngallu tuqukaq avaqutigpenani . Pingayiitangan tuguluku aghnaq , tuqukaq avaqutigpenani .
Qamaglluteng tugaaqluku aghnaq tuqulaghaatkat avaqutigpenateng . Kingulighpigaaluni aghnaq tuqukaq .
Qamaglluteng maaghraghvinlek anglegutkullghiit nulighqegkaqsaqangat . Aghneghmi tawani tuqukat unguvaghtuutellghitni , naliita aghnaq nulighqelleqagu ? "
Jesus-em kiimsiqii , " Sumeghtaghallesi anaggutngaat qayughllak liigikigalkesi Akuzitet Igaqegkat , nallukegkesillu Kiyaghneghem aghtughyaghqaanghillgha .
Tuqukat unguvaghtuuskumeng tuqulleghmeng , qilagmelngughestun yaqulgestun ayuqsaghqaagut , nengughutusaghqaanghitut .
Atightiigastegguu Kiyaghneghem apellgha tuqukat unguvalleghqiitneng tuqulleghmeng ? Moses-em igaani apeghngaaq kumaghughngalghiimi uqfillegaghmi . Tawani Kiyaghneghem pikaqaa Moses , ' Whanga Kiyaghneqaanga Abraham-em , Kiyaghneqaanga Isaac-em , Kiyaghneqaanga Jacob-em . '
Taana whaten pisiiguq , Kiyaghneq , Kiyaghneqenghitaat tuqukat , Kiyaghneqaat unguvalghiit . Enkaam anaggutepigsimaasi ! "
Apeghtughikayuk Liilightuusaneng tagiluni nagatkii aaghtiiraaghullghiit . Nagalluku Jesus-em kiimsighilaataqullgha Sadducees-enun , aaptekaa , " Natungaawa Liilightuusaq megnunalleghpigaq ? "
Jesus-em kiimsiqaa , " Megnunallegpigaq unanguuq : ' Nagatek , Israel-eghmiini ! Ataneq Kiyaghneghput taananginaghhaaguq Ataneq .
Ataneq Kiyaghneghen piniqsaghqaqan tamaghhaakun ilugpegun , tamaghhaakun unguvasighpegun , tamaghhaakun umyugaghpegun , qamagllukullu iknaqelleghpegun . '
Tuunglighha whatetuq : ' Piniqsaghqaqaten yulguteten , piniqelleghpetun elpeneng katam . ' Alla Liilightuusiituq taakugetun megnunaghtutkalghiimeng . "
Apeghtughikayugem Liilightuusaneng Jesus pikaa , " Apeghtughista , elqughaghtan ! Ipanguuq taana pillghen , Ataneq taananginaghhaaguq Kiyaghneq , alla avangituq kiyaghneghmeng iwerngaqun ellnga .
Enkaam yugem piniqsaghqaqaa Kiyaghneq tamaghhaakun ilumi , tamaghhaakun umyugagmi , tamaghhaakunllu iknaqelleghmi . Piniqsaghqaqiillu yulgutni katam ellmineng piniqelleghmitun . Taakuk Liilightuusak megnunaghataghaghtuk paneghlluku tunusaqegkaneng , nalighmeng aghqutkegkaneng . "
Jesus-em liigiksamigu yugem kiimsiitnga elqughutngalghii , pikaa , " Qantaghantuten Ataneghpagullghaneng Kiyaghneghem . " Taam kingunganeng kitum alngunak tetugyagutkaa aapqughaaneghmeng Jesus .
Temple-mi , Jesus-em apeghtughitkelluku aaptekii , " Sangan apeghtughikayuget Liilightuusaneng piiqatgu Christ-a David-mun Ighneqniluku ?
Agleghnalghiim Taghnegham David whaten pistekaqaa , ' Atanghem pii Atanqa : Aqumi whagun aghenqignemkun kenlanga anguyagten itegaghpek asinganun lliightellemnun . '
" David-em ellngan katam atiqaqaa , ' Ataneghmeng ' enkaam naten Christ-a Ighneqagu David-em ? " Yulghutet quyakusiqinaghluku nagatkaat Jesus .
Apeghtuutkelluki pikii , " Kelengalusi apeghtughikayugneng Liilightuusaneng . Aasuneghtuut atkuyaaghmeng akughtuqameng , igleghsuneghtuutlu akilpegaghvigni yugnun qungughfikesqelluteng .
Aqumyuneghtuut aangwaaghughtekat aqumutiitgun , synagogue-nillu neqenghaghqelghiinillu .
Esghaghlaataqwaaqiit ugingighat mangteghiighaqluki . Taagken pinighniluteng pisqelluteng taakluku yughaghaqut . Tamaaken apalluqluku aghyuullengeghllagyaghqaagut ! "
Temple-mi , Jesus-em aqumgatkelluku tungangakun manilghutam , esghapakii yulghutet kanaghtiighaatalghiit manimeggneng . Aklungilnguut yulghutet manilghutmeng kanaghquqat .
Taagken aklumalghii ugingighaq iteghluni kanaghtekakek maalghuk maningiighhaak , qerngaagmek penny-nguftuk .
Jesus-em maligsaaghteni tuqlughluki pikii , " Ipa ungipaatamsi , uum aklumalghiim ugingigham tuunegkakek qaayghutinguuk aklungilnguut tuunegkiitneng .
Yuget kanaghtinguut aklungimeggneng , iwernga uum aghnam kanaghtaa qamaglluku maningiighhani , akluknguyaqanga ellminun kiyaghusighqaaluku . "
Jesus aanumaluku Temple-meng , ataasim maligsaaghtengan pikaa , " Apeghtughista , ii-i ! Esghaqaghqiqun maakut pinighnaghllaget mangteghat uyghagrukutaaghllagneng ulimaaghet . "
Jesus-em pikaa , " Esghaghsikii mangteghaghllaget maakut ? Talwa ataasiq uyghak nemininnaanghituq ; qamaglluteng ulleghqughyaghqaagut . "
Mount Olives-mi , Jesus ellnginaghhaghmi aqumgamaluku Temple-mun ayuqluni , Peter-enkut James-enkut John-enkut Andrew-nkut takukaat .
Aaptekaat , " Ungipaatikut , qakun tamaakut piyaghqaawat ? Sangulleqa liisimakusighqaghput tamaakut apeghiilleghqiitnun ? "
Jesus-em pikii , " Kelengatek , kitumun alngunak puughtestegpenasi .
Uglaapiglleghhii tagiyaghqaaguq atuqluku aatqa , whaten piiqluteng , ' Ellnganguunga ! ' Enkaam uglaapiglleghhii puughqughyaghqaqaat .
Nagaququfsiki pilluwat , akusqaghtaatkellghetlu pilluwat , alingegpenasi . Tamaana piyaghqaaguq , salin iquggnaqngunghituq .
Nunam ramkengi pilluwutullequt , nunamllu ataneghpagullghi sughugaallequt , nunatlu nani alngunak tuyepeghtaghaqluteng piyaghqaagut , neqangisagllagaqlunillu piyaghqaaguq . Qamaglluteng tamaakut aghnam ighniyukestallghatun ayuqut .
" Iwernga elpesi kelengalusi . Tugulusi agghistenun aglaalleqiisi . Synagogue-ni kagsagmiglleqiisi . Whanga apalluqlunga nekevellequsi sivungitni igleghutistetlu umiilgetlu ungipaghtengulusi Pinilghiineng Ungipaneng .
Pinilghiit Ungipat ungipaqsaghqaagut tamanganun ramkenun sivungani iqugtellghem .
Tugulusi aglaaskangisi nanqigtivigmun sumeghtaghaqestaghpenasi akuzitkaghqameng . Pilleghqaq kaataqegkan akuziiqnaaghtusi pisqelleghpesistun , qayughllak elpesingunaanghitut akuzilghiit , Agleghnalghiik Taghneghak elpesigun akuziiqnaaghtuk .
Yuget angleguteteng tuqutesleqiit , yuget avaqutateng tawateghpigaq pisleqiit . Taghnughhaatlu angayuqateng kipullginaaghluki tuqutesleqiit .
Whanga apalluqlunga qamaglluni yugem ugumiilleqiisi . Iwernga kina alngunak nuqenneghtuqaq kenlemun yugulillengyaghqaaguq . "
( Yeqay atightulghiim liigikligu una uuknaliqelleq ! ) " Esghaqufsigu agleghniighutista paaghqiitestilghii , nekaghqaqenghilkemini nekevelghii , tamaakut Judea-melnguut anagniighhaat naayghanun .
Yuuk mangtegham qaaynganilnguq qamavek kelqesaghqameng aqfatefqaami pilghaaq .
Yugem piitesighaghvigmelnguum qaasligni aqfafqaamikek pilghaaq .
Seghleghwaaghunaqnguut tamaakut qumilgetlu mamaghtilghiitlu tamaani aghneghni !
Yughaghtek Kiyaghneghmun uksumi tawaten pifqaan pisqelluku !
Qayughllak tamaani aghneghni seghleliiq seghleghataghaayaghqaaguq seghleliighaqelleghneng ima Kiyaghneghem ulimayuwhaallghaneng nuna whavemun kenlanga . Allamengllu tawatelnguq seghleliiq pinaanghituq .
Atanghem takellimangisaqaki tamaakut aghneghet , kina alngunak unguvanayanghituq . Iwernga apalluqluki nakmikegkani aghneghet takellikaqii .
" Taagken kitum alngunak pikangisi , ' Esghaghteggu , Christ-a whaa ! ' nalighmeng ' Esghaghteggu , tazigna esgha ! ' ugpeqegpenaan .
Christ-asighwaaghetlu uuknaliqistesighwaaghetlu allgeghtuusaghqaagut . Allaaghlluwhaghtighllagaataghyaghqaagutlu , saghiighanaghqeghllagaataghyaghqaagutlu puughqughnaluki yuget , talwa Kiyaghneghem nakmikegkii puughsaqlegukumegteki pilleqiit .
Enkaam kelengalusi ! Sameng tamaghhaaneng ungipaatekestaghamsi tamaakut pistegpenaki .
" ' Kingunganeng taam seghleliilleghllagem siqineq mamlegllequq , tanqiq nighugunnanighllequq ,
ighaleqetaaghet ifkaquullequt qilagameng , aghtughyaghqaanghillghet qilagamelnguut igleghallghit alngunaghqeslequt . '
" Taagken yuget esghaghlleqaat Ighnegha Yugem tagilghii qilawaaghteggun aghtughyaghqaanghillelighllaglunillu nighughqellelighllaglunillu .
" Taagken yaqulget kayaglleqii qerngughtesqelluki nakmikegkani yuget nunataghhaaneng tamaghhaaneng .
" Liitfikiteggu figs-em uqfiga . Avayii uniilliighaghluteng ququngii piitekestaqata sungaghyuketun liisimakelleqaghsi kiigyaghtulleq .
Figs-em uqfiganeng liitelleghpesistun esghaqufsiki tamaakut qilagamelnguut apellemtun pilghiit , liisimakelleqaghsi Ighneghan Yugem kaasaghtungestallgha , aaqun amigmun lliighumaaq .
Ipa ungipaatamsi , maaten unguvalghiit tuqunaanghitut sivungani qamaglluteng tamaakut pilleghqiita .
Qilagallu nunallu aviighusaghqaaguk , iwernga whanga akuzitenka aviighusagqaanghitut .
" Iwernga kitum alngunak nallukaa nani aghneghmillu aflumillu tagiyaghqaatanga . Talwa yaqulget qilagmelnguut nallukaat , Ighneghemllu nallukaa , Atanginaghhaam liisimakaa .
Kelengatek , waaknanighpenasi qayughllak nallukaghsi qakun tagilleghqaa .
Yugtun ayuqsaghqaaguq natmun pilghiitun . Aghulaqellghilluni qepghaghteni aflengakistengllaghlleqii mangteghaminun , ungipaalleqiillu sayaghqiitneng . Amigniighteminunllu kelengakesqegkaa uteghnilleghqani .
Enkaam elpesi kelengatek , qayughllak nallukaghsi qakun mangteghalek uteghnighyaghqaatanga . Walluumllu tagiiqli ighivgaghmi , unugem qukaani , aghtaghaqestami , nalighmeng unaanguluku .
Enkaangam kelengatek luuraq kaatqaghtekumi qavaalusi angunayukangisi .
Aapqegka una elpesinun , tamaghhaghllaganun pingwaaqa : Kelengalusi ! "
Neqenghaghqelleghqaa Passover-em , Neqenghaghqelleghqaallu Yeast-alillgilnguum Neqekrangllam kaasaghqak maalghuk aghneghek atughlukek . Chief priest-etlu , apeghtughikayugetlu Liilightuusaneng paninang agghitngulghiit aksaqluku tuguluku Jesus tuqunnaluku .
Iwernga neqenghaghqemmi piyugumangilkangat luuraq yuget seghleliighqiighllagnayukata .
Bethany-minguq taawa yuuk atighaqegkangat , Simon , Leper-a . Simon-enkuni Jesus neghumaluku , aghnaq iitqaq tugumiiqlukek alabaster-ek aqimleghutak akitupiglleghhiik tepengllaasik , nard-epigmeng ulimaaghek . Sigiqlukek aqimleghutam paaskek kuuvegkakek Jesus-em naasqwakun .
Tawanlenguut ilangi ugumiyugluteng ilateng pikiit , " Sangan tepengllaasik sakusiiqakek ?
Akiklukek allgeghutkennayaghtuk 300 siipngalghiimun denarii-mun enkaam akinga tunqughnayaghtuq aklumalghiinun ! " Taagken aghyuuqaat aghnaq .
Iwernga Jesus-em pikii , " Avelghaghteggu ! Sangan seghlequughesteggu ? Piniipigtuq whangamnun tawaten pillgha .
Aklumalghiit quunpeng tamaansaghqaagut , enkaam qakun alngunak kayusiitaqnaaghasi . Iwernga whanga quunpeng elpesininnaanghitunga .
Uum aghnam apeghiighaa piyaghqani ; tepengllaghqekestaghaa yugusiqa llivelleghqamnun .
Ipa ungipaatamsi , nani alngunak nunataghhaani tamaghhaani Pinilghiit Ungipat ungipaqneghmegteki , aapghaqnaaghaat aghnam tawaten pillgha yugnun neqamikesqelluku . "
Taagken Judas Iscariot , ilangat qula maalghuk siipneqluku maligsaaghtet , chief priest-enun pikaq uveghpagusugniluku Jesus ellngitnun , tugusqelluku .
Tawaten piyisteng elngaatall efquqegkaat , akeqegkaatlu manililleqniluku . Enkaam Judas pilleghqangnaqutkegkaq uveghpagunnaluku .
Sivuliq aghnegha Yeast-alillghilnguum Neqekrangllam Neqenghaghqellgha kaatkaq . Tawani aghneghmi , Jews-et iiwleng tuqutaqegkangit penniighaghaat Passover-em Neqenghaghqellghanun . Maligsaaghtet aaptekaat Jesus , " Nani yataaghqullaken Passover-em Neqenghaghqelleghqaaneng ? "
Taagken Jesus-em pikakek maalghuk maligsaaghtegni , " Jerusalem-emun aglaghtek , yugem meghtalghiim nallaghlleqiistek , maliggnakesek .
Mangteghamun iitqan taam mangtegham yuga pinakesek , ' Apeghtughistem whaten pisqaaten , Nani maligsaaghtekullghiini neghnaqesteggu Passover-em Neqenghaghqellgha ? '
Kelguvikelleqiistek qemtamelngughmeng neghllagmeng , sangwaa qamaglluni apeghiighwaaghluni ayuquq . Tawani yataaghqunnakefkut . "
Maligsaaghtek aghulaqlutek Jerusalem-emun , kaasalghiimek sangwaa qamaglluni Jesus-em apellghatun ayuqeftuq . Enkaam Passover-em neqekaghqaa yataaghqegkaak .
Ighivgaghyagu , Jesus-em kelqelluki qula maalghuk siipneqluku maligsaaghteni aglaqat tawavek mangteghamun .
Neghuutnguluteng tipelegni Jesus-em pikii , " Ipa ungipaatamsi , nalighpesi neghelgusighilghiim whangamneng uveghpagunnaqngwaanga . "
Maligsaaghtet seghleghyugluteng kipullgusnaq aapqughaaqaat , " Whangangwaa ? "
Jesus-em kiimsiqii , " Naliqaghsi elpesi qula maalghuk siipngalghiini , whangamnun maligulluni sagneghmun neptekanga neqekrangllaq .
Ighnegha Yugem tuquyaghqaaguq Akuzitet Igaqegkat pinaqnillghistun . Iwernga seghleghwaaghunaqnguuq taana yuuk uveghpagutilghii Ighneghaneng Yugem ! Itagnaghnayaghtuq allgeghumangisaqumi ! "
Neghuutnguluteng Jesus-em tugukaa neqekrangllaq . Iyamsiqayugvikluku Kiyaghneq , aavgughluku tunquqii maligsaaghteni . Pikii , " Tuguluku neghiteggu , una yugusiqaqa . "
Taagken tuguluku qayuusiq wine-meng imalek , iyamsiqayugvikluku Kiyaghneq , tuunegkaa ellngitnun , qamaglluteng meghvikaataqaat .
Jesus-em pikii , " Una aakwaqa , taaggun Kiyaghneghem akequsaa apeghiighyaghqaaguq . Tuqukuma aakwa kuuvellequq uglaapiglleghiinun yugnun .
Ipa ungipaatamsi , wine-meng alla meghnaanghitunga kenlanga aghneghmi tawani wine-eghraghaq meghegkumkun Ataneghpagullghani Kiyaghneghem . "
Taagken ilagaan atughluku , aanluteng Mount Olives-mun pikat .
Jesus-em pikii , " Uniqaghaalleqaghpesinga qayughllak Akuzitni Igaqegkani Kiyaghneq pikaaguq , ' Tuqulleqaqa penniighniighta enkaam penniighet mingiqellequt . '
Iwernga kingunganeng unguvaghtestekanganga Galilee-mun aglaqestaghllequnga sivugpesini . "
Peter-em pikaa , " Uniteqeghhnaanghitamken qaywa ilanka qamaglluteng qimaguuteghngaata ! "
Jesus-em pikaa Peter , " Ipa ungipaatamken , unukun rooster-em qalghilleni alghightestegpenaan nallunqelleqaghpenga ketwhell pingayuneng . "
Iwernga Peter-em sagiqepiglluni pikaa , " Qaywa tuqulgusighyaghngaamken , nallunqennaanghitamken ! " Ilangitallu qamaglluteng tawaten pikaat .
Kaalluteng tawavek atilqelghiimun Gethsemane-meng , Jesus-em pikii maligsaaghteni , " Aqumitek taaggun , yughaamalunga . "
Peter-enkut James-enkut John-enkut kelqegkii . Taagken Jesus alingruughllakestaqaqlu seghleliighllakestaqaqlu .
Enkaam pikii , " Unguvasigka qivghughllaguuq repall tuquyaghqaaghllunga . Tawanllusi kelengalgusightengnga . "
Tazingapighqaaghluni , nunamun sikmuulluni yughaqaq pilleghqalgukumi ikfiqusighqani atuqefqaan pinaluku .
Pikaq , " Abba , Ataay , sangwaa qamaglluku piyaghqaqan . Awiitigu una qayuusiq whangamneng , iwernga whanga piyukelqa avelghaghluku elpek piyukellghen pigu . "
Taagken takuyaqminiki pingayut maligsaaghteni , qavaaftut . Peter pikaa , " Simon , qavaaziin ? Ataasighhaq aflu teghhumatkenneghmeng aghtughsiguu ? "
Taagken pikii , " Kelengatek , yughaghtek , nanghiiqullengenghitesqellusi . Ipapestaaq taghneghak piyaghqaaghngaaghmek iwerngaqun yugusiq kayaatuq . "
Tazingavek aglanqiglluni yughaqaq taakut ataasit akuzitkelluki .
Takunqigsaqminiki maligsaaghteni , taawa qavaatnguftut , qayughllak qavam sakniqestekangi . Kukriqegkatlu sameng pilleghqameng .
Pingayiitkun takuluki pikii , " Taawa qavaawaqetsii , meghnaaliiqetsii ? Tawaten始ngam ! Taawa aflu kaatuq , Ighnegha Yugem uveghpagusaghqaaghtuq seghleghqestenun .
Nekevitek , igleghtelta . Esghaqaghtegguqun , uka uveghpaqutisteka ! "
Jesus paninang akuzimaluku , Judas kaatkaq , qula maalghuk siipneqluku maligsaaghtet ilangat . Yulghutet maligtekaat , ilangi savigpalighluteng , ilangi anagutalighluteng . Chief priest-etlu , apeghtughikayugetlu Liilightuusaneng , siivanlleghetlu kayagtekiit maligtesqelluku Judas . ( Taana Judas qula maalghuk siipneqluku maligsaaghtet ilakegkangat . )
Uveghpagutistem pikaqegkangi , " Yuuk naaghyaghqaqa tugunakesi , enkaam aghulaqunnakesi kelengakistelighluku . "
Judas-em kaatutkelluku nagneghvikluku Jesus pikaa , " Apeghtughista ! " Taagken naaqaa .
Enkaam Jesus tuguluku nuqneqaat .
Iwernga ataasim tawanlenguum savigpani nusugluku high priest-em qepghaghtelaagha sigutngighaghtekaa .
Taagken Jesus-em pikii , " Tuguyaghtughestengngaa savigpagtuumaghpesi , anagutaghtuumaghpesi nikimqun wayaghniightestun ayuqlunga ?
Aghhutanga tamaghhaan apeghtughiiqunga Temple-mi tugungigataghpesinga . Iwernga tawaten pilleghpesigun Akuzitet Igaqegkat pillghit apeghiightestasi . "
Taagken qamaglluteng maligsaaghtet unilluku , qimaguutkat .
Nukalpigam maligtekaa Jesus qiipaghaghmeng saputaqiinaghluni . Tugukaqsaqangat
iwernga saputani unitqaghlluku qimakaq amsikaghmi .
Taagken Jesus aglaatkaat High Priest-em mangteghaanun . Chief priest-etlu , siivanlleghetlu , apeghtughikayugetlu Liilightuusaneng qamaglluteng tawantullghiit .
Uyavaqaanlluni Peter-em maligsaaqaa Jesus courtyard-nganun High priest-em mangteghaan . Tawani kelengakistet akulngitgun aqumluni ughugsiqaq kenghem manungani .
Chief priest-etlu qamagllutengllu agghistet tuqutesupigtekangat Jesus . Enkaam tagsiqlighaqluki yuget aapghesqegkaat Jesus sameng anaggusimatanga . Iwernga naalkusimangilnguut tuqutusighqameng ,
qayughllak uglapiglleghhiit temngi iqlengiqutkegkaat Jesus , aapqiitlu allakullghiit .
Taagken ilangi yuget nekevluteng iqlengiqutkegkaat Jesus , pikat ,
" Nagatkaqaghput whaten pilghii , ' Una Temple-a yuget ulimaaghat naafqelleqaqa . Enkaam pingayut aghneghet atughluki allaneng nekeftillequnga yugem ulimaaqenghilkanganeng ! ' "
Talwa taakutlu apellghit allakutkat .
High Priest-a sivungitgun nekevluni aaptekaa Jesus , " Avutkillghitnun sameng piyaghqiisiin ? "
Iwernga Jesus qaalkaamangilnguq , kiimsiimangilkanga . High priest-em aaplaataqaa , " Christ-anguziin , Ighnegha Manigughaqegkemta ? "
Jesus-em kiimsiqaa , " Taananguunga . Esghaghlleqaghsi Ighnegha Yugem aqumgalghii aghenqigneghakun Aghtughyaghqaanghillelgem . Esghaghlleqaghsillu tagilghii qilagem qilawaaghitgun ! "
High Priest-em aatkani piigluki pikaq , " Liisimakestengisaghngaamta lliightukut !
Nagataghsi seghletun akuzilghii , Kiyaghneghunilghii . Naten elpesi agghitkesteggu ? " Agghillghat ataasiightekaq , qamaglluteng tuqusaghqaanikaat .
Taagken ilangita qesiqukaat Jesus , gginaa saapluku tenglugpagaataqaat . Aaptekaat , " Uuknaliqistengukuvek , ungipaatikut kitum tenglugtaten ? " Taagken kelengakistet tuguluku qasaghtaataqaat .
Peter paninang qakma manughamelluku , ataasiq aghnaghaq high priest-em qepghaghtenga tagikaq .
Esghaqaa Peter ughugsilghii . Liisuqsamigu pikaa , " Elpeklu Jesus-metkayuguuten Nazareth-eghmiimi . "
Iwernga mesighaqaq , " Nallukaqa sameng piiquten talwa liigikenghitaqa sameng piten . " Taagken Peter aglaghaquqlu amigmun aanaluni , rooster-a qalghiqaq .
Aghnaghaam qepghaghtem esghaghyamigu allameng tawanlenguut pikii , " Una yuuk taakut ilakaat ! "
Iwernga Peter mesighaghlaataqaq . Mulunghituq nekevghallghiit pikaat Peter , " Mesighaghpagningituten , taakut ilakaaten qayughllak elpeklu Galilee-ghmiinguuten . "
Taagken Peter-em siingvallaghmeng pikii , " Iqlengiqngukuma Kiyaghneghem aghyuughlinga ! Nallukaqa yuuk akuzitkegkesi ! "
Legan nepiightuq rooster-em qalghilleni alghiqaa . Tawani Peter-em neqaatkaa Jesus-em whaten pillgha , " Rooster-em qalghilleni alghightestegpenaan nallunqelleqaghpenga ketwhell pingayuneng . " Taagken qiyaaghwaghllakaq .
Aghtaghaqiinaghyagu chief priest-etlu , siivanlleghetlu , apeghtughikayugetlu Liilightuusaneng , qamagllutengllu agghistet qerngughutkat agghinnaluteng . Taagken Jesus asighqesluku aglaalluku Pilate-mun , tuunegkaat ellnganun .
Pilate-em aaptekaa , " Jews-et umiilkataan ? " Jesus-em kiimsiqaa , " Elpek esgha umiilgunikevnga . "
Chief priest-et uglaapiglleghhiineng allaaghhiinaghneng anaggunikaat .
Pilate-em aaplaataqaa , " Kiimsiitkaghqiisiin ? Naganneghisikii uglaapiglleghhiineng allaaghhiinaghneng anaggunnikangaten ? "
Iwernga Jesus sameng pimangitkaq enkaam Pilate saghiighayukaq .
Tamaghhaani Passover-em Neqenghaghqellghani , Pilate-em aanestaqegkanga ataasiq anusimingllaghaq yuget nakmikegkaat .
Taawanguq Barabbas anusimingllaghvigmelnguq , maligulluni ilangitnun yugnun yugtaghaataqaq seghleliighqiighllagmi .
Yulghutet tagiluteng Pilate-mun aanestesqegkaat ataasiq anusimingllaghaq tawaten piiqellghatun .
Aaptekii , " Aanestesugestegguu Jews-et Umiilgat ? "
Pilate-em liisimakngwaaqangi chief priest-et aqinakluku Jesus tagitngukangat ellnganun .
Chief priest-et aaghqutaqegkiit yulghutet Barabbas aanestesqelluku avelghaghluku Jesus .
Pilate-em yulghutet aaplaataqii , " Sanaqsikunmi umiilkenniiqegkesi Jews-enun ? "
Akilghuukat , " Qaquuraghtestigu ! "
Pilate-em aaptekii , " Sangan , sameng seghleghmeng pimaa ? " Iwernga iglagtaaghalluteng akilghuukat , " Qaquuraghtestigu ! "
Enkaam Pilate-em efqughsugluki yulghutet , aanestekaa Barabbas . Taagken Jesus kagsagmigtesluku tuunegkaa pilluwaghtenun qaquuriisqelluku .
Pilluwaghtet itghutkaat Jesus umiilgem mangteghaanun ( atilqelghii Praetorium ) . Taagken pilluwaghtelghuteteng qerngughtekiit .
Jesus-mun aatestekagket esnegrukegtak atkuyaaghek . Sikughllugmeng qaghpangllaghluku aatestekaat naasqwakun .
Taagken legasiighwaatkegkaat , " Quulvaghamken elpek Umiilgat Jews-et ! "
Unaghsiighwaghmeng naasqwakun anaguleghluku , qesiquluku , manungakun segesqughlluteng qungughfikegkaat .
Legasiighwaatkenneghmeng taaqsamegteggu esnegrukegtak atkuyaaghqek mataghllukek ellngan katam aatkii aatestekiit . Taagken aanutkaat qaquuraghnaluku .
Tumeni taakwani nallaqaat yuuk , aatqelghii Simon-meng , Cyrene-eghmii , atangak Alexander-enkuk Rufus-enkuk . Naken qantaghaneng taginguftuq Jerusalem-emun . Pilluwaghtet qelghutkaat Simon-mun uyamigesqelluku Jesus-em qaquuraa .
Jesus aglaatkaat Golgotha-mun . ( Golgotha whaten pisiiguq , " Yugem Naasqwan Nenga . " )
Tawani tuunegkaat wine-meng myrrh-meng akumegkameng , iwernga Jesus-em ighsakegkaa .
Taagken pilluwaghtet qaquuraghyamegteggu ateghtiiraaghulluki aatkii tugulaqiit .
Qaquuraqaqegkangat unaanguluku 9-eklaagmi .
Qaquuraakun nekegtekaat avutkilleghteng igaqngalghii whaten , Umiilgat Jews-et .
Maalghuklu wayaghniightek qaquuraqagket , ataasiq Jesus-em aghenqigneghakun , aallgha saghumigneghakun .
Akuzitet Igaqegkat whaten pillghat apeghiightuq , " Ilalkiitkaqegkangat seghletun pistenun . "
Yuget naghughlleghhiit naasquteng ufsugusimiita legasiighwaatkegkaat Jesus , " Seghleghhalek , elpek ! Temple-a naafqelluku nekefsaghqaqngukuvgu pingayut aghneghet atughluki ,
sangan yuguliluten elpeneng qaquurameng ukignanighsin ? "
Chief priest-etlu apeghtughikayugetlu Liilightuusaneng legasiighwaatkegkaat Jesus , ilateng pikiit , " Yuguliiqi ilangit naqam ellmineng katam yugulipagningituq !
Christ-a , Umiilga Israel-em , ukigli maaten qaquurameng , enkaam esghapagluku ugpeqelteggu . " Qaquuralgutegkenkallu seghlequuqaak .
Taagken qamaglluni nuna mamleghqwaakaq aghneghem qukaaneng kenlanga 3-klaagmun .
Tawani 3-klaagmi Jesus akilghuughllakaq , " Eloi , Eloi , lama Sabachthani ? " whaten pisiq , " Kiyaghnemni , Kiyaghnemni , sangama unisinga ? "
Ilangita yuget nekevghallghiit nagalluku pikat , " Nagataghtekqun , Elijah tuqlughaghaa ! "
Yuuk ataasiq aqfaquqaq mesiqayugmeng . Taagken nepluku quwaalghiimun wine-mun unaghsiighwaghqun nekeglluku nengugutkaa Jesus-mun melugriisqelluku . Pikaq , " Wiintaku , esghapakaalteggu Elijah-m iiksaghtughaqsaaghaa qaquurameng ! "
Taagken Jesus araghllagluni tuqukaq .
Temple-melnguq safkaaghun malghughqegkaq , piikaq pikegken kanavek .
Pilluwaghtet umiilwaaghita qaquuram manunganilnguum , esghapagyamigu Jesus tawaten tuqulghii , pikaq , " Ipapestaaq una yuuk Ighnequmaagu Kiyaghneghem ! "
Aghnam ilangi uyavaneng esghapakat . Tawanteftut Mary , Magdala-ghmii , Salome-llu , Mary-llu naangak uyuqliim James-em , Joses-emllu .
Jesus , Galilee-melluku taakut aghnat maligsaaqaqegkangatlu kayusiitkaqegkangatlu . Ilangillu aghnalghutet tawanlenguut , maligulluteng ellnganun Jerusalem-etkat .
Taawanguq yuuk , aatqelghii Joseph-meng , Arimathea-ghmii , siivakumtaaq ilangat agghistet . Ellnganllu utaqangukanga piinlilleghqaa Ataneghpagullgha Kiyaghneghem . Whanikuyagu , Yataaghqellghem Aghneghani , sivungiighhaani Sabbath-em , tetugnanighluni Pilate-mun piluni tungsiqaa Jesus-em yugusii .
Pilate-em saghiighayagutkaa nagaqughluku Jesus tuqulghaghtuumaniluku . Enkaam pilluwaghtet umiilwaaghat tagsighluku aaptekaa , " Llaaghaan Jesus tuqulghaghtuumaa ? "
Umiilwaaghmeng liigiksamigu Jesus-em tuqullgha , Joseph-mun tugusqegkaa yugusii .
Enkaam Joseph tukfighiyaghtuqaq qatelghiimeng qiipaghaghmeng lliiveghyaghqanun atuqaqegkemeggneng . Taagken iikluku yugusii qaquurameng , iimgutkaa qiipaghaghqun . Taawanguq uyghagrukutaaghllak sanimineng ilutmun laakaq lliivghuluni . Tawavek yugusiq kanaghtekaa . Taagken uyghagrugllak ullghitaghtaqaa lliivghem paaynganun .
Mary-m Magdala-ghmiim , Mary-mllu Joses-em naangan esghapakaak nagun Jesus llimatanga .
Sabbath-a alpagyan Mary , Magdala-ghmii , Mary-llu naanga James-em , Salome-llu , tepengllaasingegkat Jesus-em yugusii angighhnaluku .
Sivuliim aghneghani santillghem , unaangupiglluku siqineq piitekestaaluku lliveghtekat .
Tumemi taakwani aapqughwaaghutkat , " Kitumngam ullghitaghtaannaqinkut uyghagllagmeng lliivghem paaynganilngughmeng ? "
Taagken sivugsalghiimeng uyghagllak awitngwaaghluni ayuqeftuq .
Lliveghmun iteghluteng esghaqaat nukalpigaq qatelghiimeng atkuyaalek aqumgalghii aghenqigneghani . Aghnat elngaatall saghiighayukat .
Nukalpigam pikii , " Saghiighayugpenasi , liisimakamsi ivaangwaaghsi Jesus , Nazareth-eghmii , qaquuraqaayalghii . Whaanneghituq , unguvaghtestekaaguq ! Esghaqaghtegguqun , whagun llikaqsaghaat .
Ungipaasaghtughteki maligsaaghtengi , Peter-llu , aga Galilee-mun sivullgaaghumaaq pinaqnilleghmitun . Taagani esghaghlleqaghsi . "
Aanluteng anagniiqat lliveghmeng , qayughllak kukragyugumaghmeng alingruughulghiit , repall ungeleglluteng . Talwa kina alngunak sameng pimangilkangat , qayughllak alingruughulghiit .
Sivuliim aghneghani santillghem , unaangupiglluku Jesus unguvaqaalghii tuqulleghmeng . Aliighviksuwhaaqaa Mary , Magdala-ghmii . ( Aghnameng taagken aanestekaqegkangi maaghraghvinlek tughneghaat . )
Ungipaasaghtuqii ellnganisalghiit qivghumaluki , qiyamaluki .
Iwernga ungipaasisteng Jesus unguvaamaniluku tuqulleghmeng , ellminunllu esghaamaniluku ugpequmangilkangat .
Taam kingunganeng Jesus-em allanguluni aliighvikegkakek maalghuk maligsaaghtegni , navek pimalukek .
Uteghnighlutek ungipitkaqsaqangik ilatek iwernga ugpequmangilkegket .
Taam kingunganeng Jesus-em aliighvikegkii qula ataasiq siipneqluku maligsaaghteni neghuusimaluki . Aghyuuqii ugpeqinghitellghitnengllu aygughikellghitnengllu esghaatkat ellmineng unguvaghtestelleghmi kingunganeng .
Pikii , " Aghulaqlusi nunataghhaanun tamaghhaanun ungipaqiteki Pinilghiit Ungipat tamaghhaanun yugnun .
Kina alngunak ugpeqilghiillu paaptaayelghiillu yugulillengyaghqaaguq . Iwernga kina alngunak ugpeqinghilnguq aghyuullengyaghqaaguq seghleghqelleghminun .
Ugpeqat allaaghlluwhaghtillequt liigikesqelluku aghtughyaghqaanghilleghteng Kiyaghneghmeng pingutanga . Enkaam atemkun aanesqughlleqiit tughneghaat yugneng ; akuzillequt allastun ulustun ;
tugusaghngaaghmeng nemeghyameng , nalighmeng meghyaghngaaghmeng tuqunalghiimeng sanaanghitut ; qinuyulghiit saafneghmegteki naallghutaqellequt . "
Atanghem Jesus-em maligsaaghteni aleghquneghmeng taaqsaki , Kiyaghneghem mayughtestekaa qilagmun , enkaam aqumegkaq Kiyaghneghem aghenqigneghakun .
Taagken maligsaaghtet aghulaqluteng tamanganun ungipaqikat Pinilghiineng Ungipaneng . Atanghem qepghalgusiqii , ipapighqestekaallu ungipaq allaaghlluwhaghtistelleghmikun . Amen .
Theophilus , igangllaqaqsuwhaamkun igaqegkaqaqa qamagtengngwaaghluku Jesus-em qepghallghallu apeghtughillghallu , piinlighyuwhaallghaneng kenlanga Kiyaghneghem qilagmun mayughtesleghanun . Sivukluni nakmiiqaaguq apostle-kaghqameng enkaam apeghtughllakaqii uglapiglleghhiimeng aghtughyaghqaanghillghakun Agleghnalghiim Taghnegham . Taakwaningani anguyagita qaquuraghluku tuqutkaqaat iwernga pingayut aghneghet atughluki unguvaqaaguq . Unguvalleghmi kingunganeng 40 aghneq nunametkaaguq , enkaam uglaapiglluku apostle-enun esghaghtestaataqaaguq ipapestaaq unguvaamaniluni , aleghqughnalukillu Ataneghpagullghaneng Kiyaghneghem . Allameng qerngughusata Jesus-em liilightuqii apostle-et , " Wataghllak aghulaqegpenasi Jerusalem-emeng kenlanga allgeghtelleghpesinun Agleghnalghiik Taghneghak . Atama akequsaqegkaqaak tuunelleqnilukek elpesinun katam tawaten apellemtun . John paaptaayeghikaaguq meghqun , iwernga Atama paaptaayeyaghtungestaghiisi Agleghnalghiigneng Taghneghagneng . " Taakusta igaqegkanka igangllaqaqsuwhaamkun .
Sivungiighhaani Jesus-em mayulleghqaan qilagmun , apostle-et qerngughusameng aaptekaat Jesus , " Ataneq , Israel-em atanghutillgha pisneqiggnaqsiguu ? "
Jesus-em pikii , " Atanginaghhaghma liisimakii qayughllak ellngan aghtughyaghqaanghilleghmikun uspeqegkaqii . Elpesi liisimaksaghqaqenghitasi sangwaat qakun pilleghqii .
Iwernga aghtughyaghqaanghillengellequsi Agleghnalghiik Taghneghak iitqayek ilugpesinun . Taagken ungipaqelleqaghpesinga Jerusalem-emi , Judea-mi , Samaria-mi , uyavaghpanillu nunani . "
Akuzineghmeng taaqngan Kiyaghneghem mayughtestekaa qilagmun . Esghapagusimaluku qilawaaghem talughtekaa esghaamallghitneng .
Apostle-et quulmun esghapagtuusimaluki , maalghuk yugek qatelghiimeng aatkaqelghiik aliighaghtekak saaghwitgun .
Pikiik , " Yugitni Galilee-m , sangafsi quulmun esghapagtuutaqetsi ? Taagna Jesus Kiyaghneghem mayughtestekanga ukigyaghqaaguq esghapalleghpesistungwaaq mayullghatun qilagmun . "
Taagken apostle-et uteghniqat Jerusalem-emun Mount Olives-meng . Mount Olives qantaghaghhanlenguq Jerusalem-emeng .
Peter-enkut , John-enkut , James-enkut , Andrew-nkut , Philip-enkut , Thomas-enkut , Bartholomew-nkut , Matthew-nkut , James , ighnegha Alphaeus-em , Judas , ighnegha James-em , Simon Zealot-a , kaalluteng Jerusalem-emun mayuqat qemtamun nayumeggnun .
Taakut apostle-et , aghnatlu ugpeqat , Mary-llu Jesus-em naanga , Jesus-em anglegutangillu qerngughulluteng elngaatall ipapighqelluteng yughaghaqelghiit ataasistun .
Taagken qafsinat aghneghet atughluki ugpeqat qerngughutkat , entaqun 120-nguut . Tawani Peter-em nekevluni pikii ,
" Ugpeqaalgutemni , neqamikaghsi qepghalgutfut Judas , Jesus-em nakmikegkaa . Ayumirugllak Agleghnalghiim Taghnegham uuknaliqutkegkaqaa David-kun . Taana uuknaliqelleq apeghiiqaaguq Judas-em uveghpagutaqngagu Jesus . Jesus-em tugiistengi Judas-em maghyaghquqaqii , enkaam akileghtuusangegkaaguq manimeng . Taagken akileghtuusamineng nunangluni qemitkaaguq ellmineng tawani . Yugusii ifkaghyalghiimi quupaghtekaq repall ighneghii aanqaghlluteng . Jerusalem-eghmiit nagaqughyamegteggu tuqumatanga tawani nunami , atiqaat taana nuna Akeldama-meng , whaten pisiq , ' Nuna aaghwqegkaq . ' "
