Peter-em nagneghutkii , " David whaten igaqaaguq Psalms-mi : ' Mangteghaa paaghqiilli , allamengllu kina alngunak tawantefqaami pili . ' Igaqegkaalghiillu whaten , ' Qepghaqaa kitumun tugusaqumi . '
" Enkaam nakmiighelta apostle-kaghqameng tugusqelluku Judas-em qepghaqaqsaqanga . Kina nakmikelteggu maligsaaghikaq whangkunneng igleghalgusighaqngamteggu Jesus . Tawantekaalghii ima John-em ungipaqellghaneng paaptaayelleq kenlanga Kiyaghneghem mayughtestellghanun Jesus qilagmun . Enkaam whangkunnun maligulluni ungipaghli ellminunllu esghaamaniluku Jesus unguvallghan kingunganeng . "
Enkaam ugpeqat nakmikegkagket maalghuk yugek : Matthias-enkuk , Joseph Justus-enkuk , allameng atelek Barsabbas-meng .
Taagken yughaqat , " Ataneq , simighistekaghqangyugaqukut Judas-mun , qayughllak uniskanga qepghaqani nekaghqaminun aglalghii . Qamaglluku umyugaq liisimakan . Enkaam naliq nakmiksigu apostle-nguluku qepghaghtekaghqaq elpenun ? "
Taagken maalghuk uyghagek samun kanaghllukek aghulasaqmegteggu aallgha aanqaghsalghiimi Matthias-nguftuq nakmikegkaq . Enkaam ilatkaq qula ataasiq siipneqluku apostle-enun .
Pentecost-em aghneghanun Jerusalem-eghmiit ugpeqat qerngughutkat ataasimi mangteghami .
Taagken nuuskagllagan anuqeghllagestun sulugllagem qilagmeng pamaken ukigluni imiqaa mangteghaq .
Taagken llangaqa ulusugnilnguut kenghhaat allgeqat , esghapakiit ilameggnun nekeghqaallghiit .
Enkaam Kiyaghneghem imiqii Agleghnalghiigneng Taghneghagneng qamaglluki tawanlenguut . Taghnegham aghtughyaghqaanghilleghmikun akuzistekii nakumiistun .
Tamaanguq Jerusalem-emi , Jews-et Kiyaghneghmun qaatkutngalghiit . Naken nunaneng tagiiqluteng Jerusalem-eghmiingughquutkat .
Nagaquusameng sulugllagmeng uplegutkiit ugpeqat qerngughfigitnun . Kaasalghiimeng nakumiistun ugpeqat akuziteghllaguftut repall kukriqutkegkiit .
Saghiighayagusimiita pikat , " Ukut akuzillghiit Galilee-ghmiinguut .
Naten ukut qamaglluta akuzillemtestun akuziit nallukngwaaqameggneng ?
Whaa whaantutut Parthia-ghmiit , Media-ghmiit , Elam-eghmiit , Mesopotamia-ghmiit , Judea-ghmiit , Cappadocia-ghmiit , Pontus-eghmiit , Asia-ghmiit ,
Phrygia-ghmiit , Pamphyllia-ghmiit , Egypt-eghmiit , Libya-ghmiit Cyrene-em tunganganeng pit , Crete-eghmiit , Arabia-ghmiit , whaa whaantutlu Rome-emeng laalightat Jews-et , Gentile-etlu maniguutkayuget Jews-estun . Nagataput akuzillemtestun ungipaghtut Kiyaghneghem apeghiilleghllaganeng . "
Qamagtengngwaaghluteng saghiighayagutkiitlu kukriqutkegkiitlu ugpeqat , enkaam ellmeggneng aapqughwaaghutkat , " Saaqat ukut ? "
Iwernga ilangita nenglaghyugsaatkumiita pikiit , " Ukut yuget megheghllaguut ! "
Peter-llu tawanlenguq apostle-elgutmini . Nekevluni iglagtuluni yuget pikii , " Jew-lgutemni , nagatngwaaqaghtengnga .
Megheghllagunighngaaghpesikut megheghllagunghitukut nutaanqun 9-eklaakanga unaanguluku .
Una whaten aneghtelleq Joel-em uuknaliqutkegkaqaa whaten :
' Kiyaghneq pikaaguq , Kingulighni aghneghni Taghneghagka kayagsaghqaqagka tamaghhaanun yugnun . Enkaam ighnesi , panisi uuknaliqsaghqaagut , nukalpigasi esghaghwaaghyaghqaagut , nanevgasi qavangughyaghqaagut .
Talwa qepghaghtemnun yugnunllu aghnanunllu Taghneghagka kayagsaghqaqagka uuknaliqesqelluki .
Yugnun esghaghtesaghqaqanka sangwaat saghiighanalghiit qilagmillu nunamillu : aakwh , keneq , agepsughllak ,
siqiineq mamlegsaghqaq , tanqiq kavighsaghqaq aawestun . Tamaakut kingungitneng megnunapiglleghhii Atanghem nanqigtivigkaa aghneq piyaghqaaguq .
Iwernga aghneq taana kaatestegpenaan , kina alngunak seghevutesqelghii Ataneghmun yugulillengyaghqaaguq . ' Tawaten Joel uuknaliqegkaaguq .
" Israel-eghmiini , nagataghtengnga , liisimakegkaghsi Nazareth-eghmii Jesus , uglapiglluku allaaghlluwhaghtighllagaataqaalghii . Kiyaghneghem tawaten pistekaqaa aghtughyaghqaanghilleghmikun elpesinun liitesqelluku ellminun nakmikegkaqutni .
Kiyaghneghem liisimalleghmikun tuunegkaqaa Jesus elpesinun piyukelleghpesistun pisqelluku . Taagken elpesi qaquuraghtestaghsi tamaakunun waakigalngughnun Kiyaghneghem Liilightuusaanun .
Iwernga Kiyaghneghem tuqulleghmeng unguvaghtestekaqaa , itemutkaqaa tuqullghem asighqutellghaneng , talwa tuqullghem nuqneghpagningitkaqaa .
David-em akuzitkegkaqaa Jesus whaten : ' Esghaghaqaqa Ataneq sivumnilluku quunpeng : unisigataanga , enkaangam seghleghmun qapragtesnaanghitunga .
Tamaaken apalluqluku qaamnaka quyaghllaguuq , akuzillghenka quyalleperewaaghmeng ayuqut . Tuquyaghqaaghngaaghma sighimaknaqamken Ataneq ,
qayughllak uninnaanghitagken unguvasigka tuqumalghiini , talwa Seghleghqumangilnguum yugusii aghusnaanghitan .
Apeghtuqaqaghpenga kenlengilngughmeng unguvallengelleghqameng , whangamnisimanginalleghpek quyasteghllawaanga . ' "
Peter-em nagneghutkii , " Jew-lgutemni , whateghlluwaaq apeghyugaqa sivuneghput David . Liisimakaghput tuqukaaguq , lliivghallu naantulanga liisimakaghput .
Unguvanguluku Kiyaghneghem akeqegkaqaa , ' Ipapestaaq kingunghen ataasiq igleghutiyaghqaaguq yugpeneng . ' David-em uuknaliqistengutmineng liisimakegkaqaa Kiyaghneghem akequsaa . Uuknaliqutkegkaqaa Christ-a tuqumalghiininnaanghinniluku talwa yugusii aghunaanghinniluku , unguvaqaaniluku tuqulleghmeng .
Taananguuq Jesus Kiyaghneghem unguvaghtekaa tuqulleghmeng enkaam whangkuta liisimakistenguukut .
Kiyaghneghem nekegtekaqaa Jesus aghenqigneghmikun , tawaten quulvaqaqaa . Akeqelleghmitun Jesus , tuunegkaqaak Agleghnalghiik Taghneghak ellnganun , enkaam Jesus-em whangkunnun tuunaak . Tamaakut saghiighanalghiit esghaqesi , nagaskesi Taghnegham aghtughyaghqaanghillghakun pillghuut .
" David pikaaguq whaten : ' Atanghem pii Atanqa , Aqumi aghenqignemkun kenlanga kayaalqestellemnun anguyagten . ' David mayuumangitutmineng qilagmun Jesus-etun , ellmineng akuzitkengngunghituq , akuzitkengngwaa Jesus .
" Ungipaataghllamsi qamagllusi Israel-eghmiini , Kiyaghneghem ipapestaaq nakmikegkaqaa Jesus Atanghulukullu Christ-angulukullu . Taananguuq Jesus qaquuraqaghsi ! "
Yuget nagalluku Peter , seghleghyugllakat enkaam Peter-llu apostle-elgutangillu aaptekiit , " Ugpeqaalgutemnni , sanaqesta ? "
Peter-em kiimsiqii , " Avuteghqellusi , seghleghqennanighlusi qiivitek Kiyaghneghmun , paaptaayeteklu Aatghakun Jesus Christ-am , seghleghqellesi seghevutellengesqelluki , enkaam Kiyaghneghem tunusakek Agleghnalghiik Taghneghak allgeghtekek .
Ataneq Kiyaghneghput tawaten piyaghqaaguq , qayughllak akequsaqegkaqaak Taghneghagni elpesinun , kinguneghpesinun , kitumunllu alngunak uyavaghpansaghngaan tuqluqaminun . "
Peter-em tawatenginaq pigpenaki wata sameng allaaghhiinaghmeng pikii . Kelengasaaqiillu , " Kiyaghneghem aghyuughyaghqaqii seghletun pistet , enkaam ellngistun seghletun pigpenasi luuraq elpesillu aghyuughyaaghiisi . "
Taagken ugpeqilghiit ungipaaneng paaptaayekat . Enkaam tawani aghneghmi 3,000 yuuk ilatkaq ugpeqanun .
Ugpeqat iiwleng qerngughutngulghiit liinnaluteng apostle-eneng . Christ-akun anglegutkullghiistun kiyaghtaaghet , neghaqelghiit , yughaghaqelghiit qerngaghmeng .
Apostle-et uglaghngaan allaaghlluwhaghtikaalghiit Kiyaghneghem aghtughyaghqaanghillghakun . Enkaam qamaglluni saghiighayukaalghii , tallughyagutkaqegkangatlu Kiyaghneq .
Ugpeqat qamaglluteng nagneqaalghiit ataasistun , saghyateng atunem atuqluki .
Akikluki nunatengllu saghyatengllu , allgeghtateng manit tuunaqegkangit sameng aklulghiinun .
Aghhutanga tamaghhaan qerngughutaqelghiit Temple-mi . Neghelgutengllaghaqluki ilateng , quyakusiqinaghluki neqeteng upughatusiqaqegkangit .
Kitumun alngunak piniqnighllaget , usuqumanginaghaqegkangatlu Kiyaghneq . Aghhutanga tamaghhaan Atanghem yugulingukangi yuget , enkaam ugpeqat nulamanginaqat .
Taagken Peter-enkuk John-enkuk aglaqak Temple-mun 3-klaagem yughaatellghani .
Taawanguq yuuk piyugigalnguq ima allgenghhaghhaatmineng , aqumluni tungangakun Temple-em iteghvigani atilqelghii , Pinighnalghii Amigllak . Aghhutanga tamaghhaan kinkut kevegtughaqegkangat tawavek naghughtaneng tungsighniighesqelluku manimeng .
Esghaghyamikek Peter-enkuk John-enkuk itelghiik Temple-mun tungsighvikegkakek manimeng .
Qerngaagmek esghaghluku yuuk tawavek , Peter-em pikaa , " Ukavek qiivi whangkutegnun . "
Sighimapiglluni tuunaqniluni qiivegkakek .
Peter-em pikaa , " Maniqraggiitngwaaghtunga iwernga sameng tuunaqamken . Aatghakun Jesus Christ-am Nazareth-eghmiim , piyugi ! "
Tuguluki aghenqigneghi iiggi nekevesimaluku yugem itegiillu tukughiillu iknaqughtekat ,
repall qetgeqaamaghmi nekevegkaq aga piyuginaamaghmi pikaq . Taagken maligllukek iitqaq Temple-mun piyugumaghmi , qetgeqaghaqluni , usuqumaan Kiyaghneq .
Temple-metullghiim esghaqaat piyulghii , usuqilghii Kiyaghneghmeng .
Liisuqegkaat tungsighraghtenguyalghii aqumluni tungangani iteghvigan Temple-em . Saghiighayagutkaat esghaghyamegteggu yuuk piyulghii .
Paninang naallghutkam yugem Peter-enkuk John-enkuk qetngamalukek , yulghutem saghiighayugumaghmeng kanglluqaghtekiit Solomon-em Porch-ngani .
Peter-em esghaghyamiki pikii , " Israel-eghmiini , sangafsi saghiighayugetsi ? Sangamta esghapagtuutestekut ? Piyugtesneghitaghpung una yuuk aghtughyaghqaanghillemtegnegun , nalighmeng piniitemtegneng . Piyugigalnguum yugem Jesus ugpeqsaqminigu naallghutuq .
Abraham-enkut , Isaac-enkut , Jacob-enkut , sivunemtallu qamaglluteng maniguqiita Kiyaghneghem quulvaghaa Qepghaghteni Jesus . Iwernga elpesi aglaatkaqaghsi Pilate-mun nanqigtesqelluku , ighsakegkaqaghsillu Pilate-em itemusugaqngagu .
Yeghlegi Pilate-mun yugtaghalqaq itemutesqegkaqaghsi ighsakluku Jesus , Seghleghqumangilnguq , Qaatkutngaghllalghii .
Tawaten pilleghpesigun tuqutestekaqaghsi Unguvallghem Allgeghvigpigaa , iwernga Kiyaghneghem unguvaghtestekaqaa tuqulleghmeng . Liisimakngwaaghaghpung , qayughllak esghaqaqaghpung unguvallghan kingunganeng enkaam apeghyaghqaqaghpung .
Esghaqesi una yuuk nekevghalghii sivugpesini , qamagllusi liisimakaghsi piyugigasalghiinguuq ima allgenghhaghhaatmineng . Iknaqughtekaaguq ugpeqluku aatgha taam ataasim Jesus-em Kiyaghneghem unguvaghtekaan tuqulleghmeng . Aa-a , ugpeqillghan Jesus-kun naallghutngwaaghaa , esghaqesi maaten .
" Jew-lgutemni , neghighluku Kiyaghneghem aapqaa uuknaliqistetgun nakmikegkani Christ-a ikfiqluni tuqulleqniluku . Taana uuknaliqellghat apeghiiqaaguq igleghutistekullghiini tuqutestaqngafsigu Jesus , nallukluku Christ-angutanga .
Tamaaken apalluqluku avuteghqellusi , seghleghqennanighlusi qiivitek Kiyaghneghmun . Ugpeqiteggu Ataneq enkaam sangiglleqii seghleghqellesi .
Tawaten pikufsi Atanghem nutaghtaqnaaghii taghneghasi , kayaggneqiglleqaallu Jesus nakmikegkani Christ-anguluku elpesinun .
Iwernga Jesus tagivagilgami qilagmesaghqaaguq kenlanga Kiyaghneghem nutaghtellghanun sangwaa qamaglluku . Tawaten Kiyaghneq akeqikaaguq neghighluku uuknaliqistetgun aaftekamikun ellminun qepghaghtenguluki .
Moses pikaaguq , ' Atanghem Kiyaghneghem uuknaliqista nakmikelleqaa yugpesineng , whanga nakmikelleghmitun uuknaliqistengulunga . Nagatngwaaghnakesi akuzillgha qamaglluku .
Tamaakut naganneghilnguut uuknaliqistemun Kiyaghneghem yuganeng aafluki tuqusaghqaagut . '
" Sangwaa maana atughput kiyaghtellemnni Samuel-em uuknaliqutkegkaqaa . Samuel-em kingunganeng ilangitallu uuknaliqistet uuknaliqutqegkaqiit .
Kingunqiisi uuknaliqistet enkaam Kiyaghneghem aapqii akequsat ellngitgun , elpesinunllu pinguut . Tawateghpigaq Abraham-emllu kingunqiisi . Tamaaken apalluqluku Kiyaghneghem akeqaqngamiki sivunesi Abraham-kun whaten , ' Abraham , kinguneghpegun quyasleqanka qamagtengngwaaghluki nunam yugi , ' akequsaq taana elpesinunllu pinguuq .
Enkaangam Kiyaghneghem nakmikegkani Qepghaghteni kayagsuwhaaqaqaa elpesinun . Kayagtekaqaa quyasnalusi qamagllusi tunutestelleghmikun seghleghqumalleghpesineng . "
Peter-enkuk John-enkuk paninang ungipaamalukek Solomon-em Porch-ngani , priest-etlu umiilgatlu Temple-em kelengakistengita , Sadducees-etlu tagilaghaatkat .
Piyukumangilkangat apostle-ek apeghtuusaak yugnun Jesus unguvaqaaniluku tuqulleghmeng , taam ipapighqegkanga tuqukat unguvaghyaghqaaniluki unguvalleghmun .
Tamaaken apalluqluku apostle-ek tugulukek anusimingllaqagket . Siingenllu unugnaqegkanga unaaqusitkagket nanqigtegpenakek .
Iwernga tamaana ilanga uglapiglleghhii nagatkaq Peter-enkugneng John-enkugneng ugpeghtuutkaq . Enkaangam yuggiinaat ugpeqat entaqun 5,000-ngughtekat , aghnatlu taghnughhaatlu ugpeqat ilategpenaki .
Unaamingani Jerusalem-emi qerngughutkat Jews-et igleghutistengit , siivanlleghet , apeghtughikayugetlu Liilightuusaneng ,
High Priest-a Annas , Caiaphas , John , Alexander , ilangillu high priest-em ilakwaaghi .
Taagken apostle-ek tagiteslukek aaptekagket , " Kitum aghtughyaghqaanghillghakun yuuk piyugtesagutestegnegu ? Kitum aatgha atuqluku tawaten pistek ? "
Peter-em kiimsiqii Agleghnalghiim Taghnegham aghtughyaghqaanghillghakun , " Igleghutistenillu siivanlleghnillu ,
aaptaghpesikung aneghneghtillemtegneng , naten naallghusimatanga piyugigalnguq yuuk .
Enkaangam liigikesugamsi qamagllusi , ilangillu Israel-eghmiit qamaglluki naten una yuuk naallghutkaatanga . Naallghutkaaguq Aatghakun Jesus Christ-am Nazareth-eghmiim . Ellngan aghtughyaghqaanghillghan naallghutkaqaa , elpesi qaquuraqaghpesi , Kiyaghneghem unguvaghtestekaan tuqulleghmeng . Enkaam una yuuk piyugigasalghii whaa maaten nekevghaaq sivugpesini .
Jesus-nguuq ukut Akuzitet Igaqegkat pikaat , ' Uyghak ighsakegkaghsi elpesi mangteghangllaghteni , piyalghiimi megnunalleghpigaaftuq uyghak . '
Enkaam Kiyaghneghem kayagtekaqaa nunamun , ellnginaghhaaguq yugulighiyaghqaq . Alla naten yuuk yugulillengnaanghituq iwerngaqun aataghakun Jesus-em . "
Jews-et agghistengita saghiighayagutkagket Peter-enkuk John-enkuk tetunghitellghegkeneng , qayughllak liisimakegkegket igaghyaamangilnguuk . Liigiksaqmegtekek Jesus-metkaatmegneng tawaten akuzinguftuk .
Enkaam aaghtiiraaghpagningitkagket , qayughllak esghaqaat yuuk naallghutngwaaghluni nekevghalghii Peter-enkugni John-enkugni .
Agghivigmeng agghistet aanestekiit Peter-enkut John-enkut naallghutkaqlu yuuk , enkaam ellngit agghitnginaamaghmeng pikat .
Aapqughaaghutkat ellmeggneng , " Naten pinaqestekek yugek ? Seghleghhalek ipanguninaqaghput allaaghlluwhaghtillghak , qayughllak Jerusalem-eghmiit qamaglluteng liisimakaat .
Taawanginaq ineghsaqumtekek allallu akuzitkefqaan Jesus pisqelluku kitumun alngunak wata kinkut alngunak nagaqughnayukatgu . "
Enkaam iteghteslukek ineghtengngwaaqagket , " Allamengllu akuzitkefqaan , apeghtuusaqefqaan Jesus pinakesek . "
Iwernga Peter-enkuk John-enkuk kiimsiqiit , " Qaatkellamsii Kiyaghneq avelghaghluku ? Naliq efqughnaghta Kiyaghneghmi ? Ataasiighteki umyugasi .
Whangkutung akuzitkenneghmeng taaqnaanghitaghpung esghaqaghpungllu nagaquqaghpungllu . "
Agghistet aghyuughpagningitkagket , qayughllak qamaglluteng yuget usuqegkangat Kiyaghneq allaaghlluwhaghtilleghmun . Enkaam temngi alingsequlukek aanestekagket .
Taana yuuk 40 ayumiqulleq siipngaan uksughtutkalghii , piyugpagningisalghii iwernga maaten naallghullghii .
Peter-enkuk John-enkuk aanesistek aglaqak ugpeqaalgutmegnun . Ungipaqak chief priest-etlu siivanlleghetlu pillghitneng .
Nagallukek ataasiighlluteng yughaqat Kiyaghneghmun , " Ataneq , ulimakaqaten qilak , nuna , meq , sangwaallu alngunak taakunilnguq , igleghutngwaatenllu qamaglluki .
Ayumirugllak Agleghnalghiignekun Taghneghagnekun akuzikaaguten sivunemteggun David-kun qepghaghtegpegun whaten , ' Sangan Gentile-et temngi sakrituteghllagtatkek Atanghenkuk Christ-akullghiik , sanganllu yuget seghletun piyupigtatkek pipagningiteghngaaghmegtekek ?
Nunam umiilgillu igleghutistetlu qerngughulluteng yataaghqutut pilluwaghnalukek Atanghenkuk Christ-akullghiik ! '
" Ipapestaaq maani Jerusalem-emi tawaten pikaagut . Herod-enkuk Pontius Pilate-enkuk ilatkaaguk Gentile-enunllu Israel-eghmiinunllu kipullginaaghnaluku , Jesus Seghleghqumangilnguq Qepghaghten , nakmikegkan Christ-anguluku .
Ataneq liisimakngwaaqenllu yataaghqegkaqegkenllu tawaten pilleghqaa enkaam tawaten pikaagut .
Nagataqaten maaten whaa alingsiqukanginkut ikfiqesleqniluta . Ataneq , iknaqughsaqaghtikut enkaam tetugpenaamta ungipaalta ungipaghpeneng ,
whangkutgun naallghutiki qinuyuget , allaaghlluwhaghtistikutlu aatghakun Jesus-em , Seghleghqumangilngughqun Qepghaghtegpegun . "
Yughaneghmeng taaqaqutlu qerngughutfigat mangteghaq ufsugutkaq . Agleghnalghiim Taghnegham imiqii qamaglluki , enkaam tetugpenateng ungipaghyagutkat Kiyaghneghem ungipaaneng .
Apostle-et aghtughyaghqaanghillelighllagluteng ungipaqegkaat Ataneq Jesus unguvaqaaniluku tuqulleghmeng . Kiyaghneghem quyasteghllagukangillu qamaglluki ugpeqat . Ugpeqat ataasistun lliiqat ilumegteggunllu unguvasimegteggunllu . Enkaam kina alngunak pingigalnguq saghyateng ellnginaghmeggnun pikniluki , atunem atuqaqegkangit .
Nunalget , mangteghalget akikneghmegteki nunatengllu mangteghatengllu , allgeghtateng manit apostle-enun tuunaqegkangit . Enkaam ugpeqat sameng aklunghata manilitaqegkangit , tawaten kina alngunak aklumangilnguq .
Joseph tawanlenguq , Cyprus-eghmii , Levi-em kingungha , ellnganllu akikluku nunani tuunegkaa allgeghtani apostle-enun . Apostle-et atiqaat Barnabas-meng whaten pisimeng , " Kayemesta . "
Taawanguq yuuk aatgha Ananias , nulighha Sapphira . Akikegkaa nalighnegha nunami .
Nuliighmi liisimanghani aksaqegkaa ilanga manim ellminun pinguluku . Taana siipneni tuunegkaa apostle-enun sumeghmini qamaglluku tuuniluku pisqelluku .
Yeghlegi Peter-em aaptekaa , " Sangan qaatkesigu Tughneghaam nanghiiqullgha iqlengiqesqelluten Agleghnalghiignun Taghneghagnun aksaqelleghpegun ilanga manim ?
Sangan tawaten sumeghtaghaamazin ? Yugnun iqlengiqenghituten , Kiyaghneghmun iqlengiquten . Akikellghilluku nunan elpek piksaghan , enkaam akikaqngavgu maningallu taana piyukelleghpetun piyaghqaqsaghan . "
Legan Ananias-em Peter nagalluku uullghaghlluni tuqukaq . Nukalpigat iteghluteng qiipaghakun iimgulluku yugusii aanulluku lliifqaat . Ungipaq Ananias-em iqlengiqellghallu tuqullghallu mingitkaq , enkaam nagaquutkat alingruughuteghllakat .
Pingayut aflut atughluki Ananias-em tuqullghaneng , nulighha iitqaq nallukluku ugini samatanga .
Peter-em aaptekaa , " Tawaten akitutkaan akikestegneguu nunayek ? " Sapphira-m kiimsiqaa , " Aa-a . "
Peter-em aaplaataqaa , " Sangaftek ugikullghiigni sumeghtaghaamastek nanghiiqunalukek Atanghem Taghneghakek ? Yuget lliivghikat ugigpeneng qakma manughametut . Elpeklu tawaten pilleqaaten . "
Tawanighlluggiinaq ellngallu uullghaghlluni tuqukaq . Nukalpigat iteghyalghiimeng Sapphira-llu taawa tuqumalghii , enkaam aanulluku ugingan saaghwakun lliifqaat .
Qamagtengngwaaghluteng ugpeqat , qamagllutengllu nagaquullghiit Ananias-enkuk Sapphira-nkuk tuqullghegkeneng alingruughuteghllakat .
Yulghutet qungangitni apostle-et allaaghlluwhaghtighllagumanginaqat . Qamaglluteng ugpeqatlu apostle-etlu qerngughutaqelghiit Temple-em manughaani aatqelghiimi , Solomon-em Porch-ngani .
Iwernga yuget ugpeqillghilnguut Jesus-meng ilasigalnguut ugpeqanun qayughllak alingekanighaqelghiit , naqam pinighniiqegkangit .
Iwernga uglapiglleghiit yugetlu aghnatlu ugpeqngukangat Ataneq Jesus , enkaam ugpeqat nulamanginaqat .
Apostle-et allaaghlluwhaghtillghit apalluqluki kinkut alngunak qinuyugtiiteng allighiitgun tagilluki tumetgun lliiqegkangit . Tawaten pikiit qayughllak Peter-em naghughtekaki luuraq taghneghangutellghan naallghunnayukaki qinuyulghiit .
Enkaam Jerusalem-emun qantaghanlengughneng nunaneng tagilaghaatkaq yulghun Jerusalem-emun . Qinuyugtiitengllu tamaakutlu tughneghalget ilumegteggun tagitkiit apostle-enun , enkaam qamaglluteng tagitkiit naallghuquutkat .
High priest-enkut ilakullghiit Sadducees-et aqinatkat apostle-neng
enkaam tugusluki kanaghtestekiit anusimingllaghvigmun .
Iwernga unugyan yaqulgan Atanghem qelpeghtekii anusimingllaghvigem amigi . Enkaam aanulluki apostle-et pikii ,
" Aglaghlusi Temple-mun , qamaglluku apeghteggu una nutaghaq kiyaghtaalleq Jesus Christ-akun ayuqelghii . "
Apostle-et qaatkegkaat yaqulek . Aghtaghaghaqaallu iteghluteng Temple-mun apeghtughikat . High priest-enkut ilakullghiit qerngughtekiit Jews-et siivanlleghitlu qamagllukillu agghistet , agghitkennaluki apostle-et . Taagken anusimingllaghvigem umiilwaaghitnun aqfastekiit apostle-et .
Iwernga umiilwaaghet anusimingllaghvigmun kaasalghiimeng apostle-et aviiteftut . Enkaam agghistenun aglaghluteng ungipaatkiit ,
" Anusimingllaghvigmun kaasalghiikut amiget maghqaqughwaaghngaftut , kelengakistetlu amignituteftut naqam iteghyalghiikut paaghqiteftuq ! "
Temple-em kelengakistengita umiilgatlu , chief priest-etlu ungipaasisteng kukriqutkegkiit samatangi apostle-et .
Taagken kitum iteghluni pikii , " Taakut yuget anusimingllaqaqsaqesi inga Temple-mi apeghtughiiqut . "
Kelengakistet umiilkullghiit aqfakiit apostle-et . Seghletun pimangilkangit , qayughllak alingelghiit yugneng Temple-melngughneng tuqunnayukangisteng milughpagaataghhiinaq .
Tagilluki itghutkiit agghistenun enkaam high priest-em pikii apostle-et ,
" Ineghtengngwaaqaqsaghamsi allamengllu apeghtughifqaafsi Aatghakun Jesus-em pisqellusi , iwernga qaatkumangitaghpesikut ! Yeghlegi allulluteng Jerusalem-eghmiit liitaat apeghtuusaghsi , whangkutallu avutngusnaqutkaghpekut Jesus-em tuqullghanun . "
Peter-em kiimsiitkii apostle-et , " Qaatkesaghqaqaghput Kiyaghneq avelghaghluki yuget .
Qaquuraghluku tuqutestekaqaghsi Jesus , iwernga Kiyaghneghem , sivunemta maniguqiita unguvaghtestekaqaa tuqulleghmeng .
Enkaangam quulvaghnaluku Jesus aghenqigneghmikun nekegtekaqaa Igleghutistengulukullu Yugulighistengulukullu . Tawaten pikaqaa Israel-eghmiit avuteghqesaghqaaghtesqelluki seghleghqennaniisqelluki , qiivesqelluki Kiyaghneghmun , seghevunnalukillu seghleghqellghitneng .
Whangkuta ungipaghtenguukut tamaakunun pilleghnun , maligulluta Agleghnalghiignun Taghneghagnun Kiyaghneghem tuunegkagkenun tamaakunun qaatkullghiinun ellminun . "
Agghistet sakritutkaalghiit Peter-em kiimsighyisteng tawaten , repall tuqusukaqegkangit apostle-et .
Iwernga ataasiq agghista nekevegkaq akuzinaluni . Gamaliel-nguftuq , Pharisee , apeghtughistengat Jews-et Liilightuusiita , elngaatall kitum alngunak qaatkumtaagha . Kelengakistenun aanutaghtesqegkii apostle-et .
Taagken agghistelgutni pikii , " Israel-eghmiilgutemni , piraamsilluki taakut yuget piteki .
Neqamikenghistegguu qavnganghhaq Theudas pikaalghii igleghutesteghllaguniluni . Enkaam 400 yuuk maligsaaghikaq ellnganeng . Iwernga Theudas tuqusatgu maligsaaghtengi qimaguutkat , talwa kitum alngunak allamengllu akuzitkesugumangilkangat .
Taakwaningani Judas-llu Galilee-ghmii , qerngughtikaq yugkameng kavema kestistiiqngan yugem uglaghtalanganeng . Iwernga ellngallu tuqutaqngatgu yugi mingitkaagut .
Enkaam whaa sumemni itagnaghnayaghtukut safqiita qakemkut yuget piyaqumteki . Ellmeggneng pingukumeng tawaten pillghat satngunanighllequq .
Iwernga Kiyaghneghem pilqegkagu aghuliighhnaanghitasi , kipullginaaghlleqaghsillu Kiyaghneq . " Enkaam agghistet qaatkegkaat Gamaliel .
Taagken kelengakistenun itghutesluki apostle-et kagsagmigtestekiit . Ineghtengngwaaqiitlu ungipaqnaniisqelluku Jesus . Apeghiighyamegteki aanestekiit .
Apostle-et aanesisteng quyaghllakat , qayughllak Kiyaghneghem kayngusaghaatestekaqegkangi Jesus apalluqluku .
Aghhutanga tamaghhaan Temple-millu kinkunillu ungipaqaqegkangat , apeghtuusaqaqegkangat Jesus , Christ-anguniluku Kiyaghneghem nakmikegkaa .
Tamaani aghneghni ugpeqat nulanguluki Greek-stun akuzikayuget Jews-et seghleghyukat , Hebrew-stun akuzikayugneng Jews-eneng , qayughllak ugingighaghtiiteng aklukegkiitneng tuunlaaghigalkangit . Enkaam yiillgikiit , " Aghhutanga tamaghhaan uyegtistet palasqughhaan tuunaqiit whangkuta ugingighaput . "
Tamaaken apalluqluku qula maalghuk siipneqluku apostle-et , qerngughlluki ugpeqat pikiit , " Anaggullequkut pegtekumteggu ungipaqilleghput Kiyaghneghem akuzitanganeng uyegtistengughhnaluta .
Ugpeqaalgutemnni , tamaaken apalluqluku nakmikiteki maaghraghvinlek yuuk pinilghii , Agleghnalghiigneng Taghneghagneng imighngalghiit , peghqinelghiit , uyegtistengllaghlleqaput .
Tawaten pikumta whangkuta apostle-eni yughaamanginaghllequkut , ungipaqimanginaghllequkut Kiyaghneghem ungipaaneng . "
Ugpeqat efquqegkiit apostle-et agghillghit . Enkaam nakmikegkaat Stephen , elngaatall ugpeqingaghllak Kiyaghneghmeng , imighngalghiillu Agleghnalghiigneng Taghneghagneng . Nakmikegkiitlu Philip-enkut , Prochorus-enkut , Nicanor-enkut , Timon-enkut , Parmenas-enkut , Nicolaus-llu Gentile-a Antioch-eghmii Jews-estun maniguusagutkaq .
Taakut yuget tagitkiit apostle-enun yughaatkesqelluki , naasqwitgun saafluki yughaatkegkiit .
Kiyaghneghem ungipii mingisimanginaqiit . Enkaam nulakaalghiit ugpeqat Jerusalem-emi , priest-elghutetlu ilalghutngit ugpeghtuutkat maligulluteng .
Stephen kayusillelegllagutminengllu aghtughyaghqaanghillelegllagutminengllu Agleghnalghiigneng Taghneghagneng allaaghlluwhaghtighllagaataqaq .
Taagken ilangita Jews-et , Cyrene-eghmiinguyalghiitlu , Alexandria-ghmiinguyalghiitlu aaghtiiraaghyaghtuqaat Stephen . Taakut yuget synagogue-ngita aatqeftaa , " Itemutkat Qepghaghtelaaghet . " Yuget Cilicia-ghmiinguyalghiitlu , Asia-ghmiinguyalghiitlu ilatkat taakunun .
Iwernga Stephen , Agleghnalghiim Taghnegham peghqinepiglluku akuzistekaa repall kiimsighpagningitkaat .
Tamaaken apalluqluku ilangi yuget aksaqluku akileghtuqiit iqlengiqutkesqelluku Stephen whaten , " Nagatkaqaghput seghlequuqek Moses-enkuk Kiyaghneghenkuk . "
Siivanlleghetlu , apeghtughikayugetlu Liilightuusaneng , ilangillu yuget nagalluteng iqlengiqellghitneng sakritutkat . Taagken aaghtiiraaghulluteng aglaatkaat Stephen agghistenun .
Taam kingunganeng yuget tagitkiit agghistenun iqlengiqutkesqelluku Stephen . Pikat , " Stephen-em quunpeng seghletun akuzitkaqaa Temple-a , Liilightuusatlu Moses-em tuunegkii whangkunnun .
Nagatkaqaghputlu pilghii Jesus-emnguq Nazareth-eghmiim naafqelleqaa Temple-a , allangughlleqaallunguq kiyaghtaalleghput Moses-em apeghtuutkaa whangkunnun . "
Qamaglluteng tawanlenguut esghaqaat Stephen-em gginaa kuukgullghii yaqulgem gginaatun .
Taagken high priest-em aaptekaa Stephen , " Ipa tawaten akuzikaaziin ukut avutkistegpek apellghistun ? "
Stephen-em kiimsiqaa , " Anglegutemnillu , siivanlleghnillu , nagataghtengnga ungipamsugunnaqamsi ! Sivuneghput Abraham salin Mesopotamia-melluku , nuugtellghilluku Haran-mun , Nighughqengngalghiim Kiyaghneghem aliighvikluku
pikaa , ' Unitigu allgeghvigen nuna , ilakwaaghtenllu , aghulaqi maghyaghqughnaaghamken . '
Enkaam Abraham aghulaqegkaq Chaldea-meng , nuugtekaq Haran-mun . Atanga tuquyan , Kiyaghneghem maghyaghquqaa Abraham nunamun maaten kiyaghfigpesinun .
Tagisuwhaaghaqngamigu natengiighhaq nunalisimangitaa ellnganun pikaghqameng . Iwernga talwa salin avaqutiilluku Kiyaghneghem akequsaqegkaqaa una nuna ellnganunllu kingunghanunllu .
Kiyaghneghem whatenllu pikaqaa , ' Kinguneghten aghulaqsaghqaagut nunakenghilkemeggnun enkaam nunataallequt . Tamaani qepghaghtelaaghuyaghqaagutlu amyuqetaatkesighllagyaghqaagutlu 400 ayumiqullelghutni .
Iwernga aghyuughlleqanka qepghaghtelaaghughtestilghiit . Kingunganeng aghyuughilleghma kinguneghten tagillequt nunamun akequsaqegkamnun , tamaani manigughlleqaatnga . ' Tawaten Kiyaghneq pikaaguq .
Taagken Kiyaghneq akequsangllaqaq Abraham-emun nalluniighutkesqelluku circumcise-elleq . Enkaam Abraham circumcise-ekaq . Ighnengyami Isaac-meng pingayuneng inglulek aghneq atughyagu circumcise-ekaa ellngallu . Tawateghpigaq Isaac-em circumcise-ekaa ighneni Jacob . Jacob-em circumcise-elaqii qula maalghuk siipneqluku ighneni . Taakut piinliisiqii ramkengan Israel-em .
" Anglilaghaalluteng Jacob-em ighneghita aqinakepigtekaat anglegutseng Joseph , enkaam akikegkaat Egypt-eghmiinun qepghaghtelaaghuluku . Iwernga Kiyaghneghem nayuqegkaa ,
seghleliinghani kayusighaqegkanga . Kiyaghneghem peghqinellelitkaa enkaam Pharaoh-m umiilgan Egypt-em , efquqluku umiilgataghaaghtestekaa Egypt-mun , igleghutistengllaqaallu mangteghaminunllu , qepghaghteminunllu .
Taagken neqangisagllakaq Egypt-millu , Canaan-millu , elngaatall uglaq iyatiquteghllakaq . Sivuneputlu neqangisagllakat .
Jacob-em nagaqughyamiki Egypt-eghmiit grain-meng kagpagllagumaniluki , ighneni pikengyaghtiisqegkii .
Tuunglighhaani alla piyata , Joseph-em anengani ungipaatkii ellngitnun uyughaqniluni . Enkaam umiilgem Pharaoh-m anglegutkututangi liigikegkii .
Taagken Joseph-em lipeghsaqaa atani Jacob , nengllugutelghutangillu nuugtesqelluki Egypt-mun . Qamaglluteng 75-nguftut .
Enkaam Jacob-enkut nuugtekat . Tamaani Jacob tuqukaq , kingunganeng tagtalmi taakwani ilangillu sivuneput tuqulaghaatkat .
Taakwaningani neghqwaaghit aglaalluki Shechem-emun , llivenqigtekiit nunakun Abraham-em tukfiqaakun Hamor-em kingunghaneng .
" Kiyaghneghem Abraham-emun akequsaa piyaghtungestaghaquqlu , sivuneput nulaghllakat Egypt-mi .
Taagken Egypt nutaghameng umiilengegkaq , taam umiilgem nallukngwaaqanga Joseph .
Sivunemta nulaghllallghit apalluqluki umiilgem peghqiniqulluki ikfiqestekii sivuneput , talwa taghnughhaghhiit aanutestaqluki pikii tuqusqelluki .
Tawaten kiyaghsimaluki Moses allgeqaq , yuukegtepiglleghii taghnughhaq . Angayuqagkenka nemegni iighaghtumeng aflengakegkaak pingayut tanqit .
Iighaghtughpagningiisamegnegu aanutkaak . Umiilgem panigan naalkelluku allughqiluku , anglistekaa ighneqelghiistun .
Egypt-eghmiit apeghtuqaat liitkameggneng . Enkaam Moses peghqinghughighllagyalghiimi akuzillguughqaaghllakaq , aghtiigalnguqlu sameng tamaghhaaneng .
" Moses 40 uksughtutkalighyami Israel-eghmiilgutni esghaghyugluki esghaghyaghtuqii .
Tawani esghaqaa Egypt-eghmiim amyuutkegkanga Israel-eghmii . Enkaam Moses-em Israel-eghmii igughluku tuqutkaa Egypt-eghmii .
Tawani sumeghtaghaqaayalghii Israel-eghmiilgutminun liigikelleqniluku Kiyaghneghmun kayagtelleni ellngitnun aghulaqutistenguluku Egypt-meng . Iwernga liigikumangilkangat .
Unaamingani esghaqakek Israel-eghmiik pillugullghiik . Akuzinnaqutkegkaqsaqek , ' Pillugutegpenatek yulgutkututek . '
Yeghlegi amyuqetiqelghiim yugem ayagaghlluku Moses pikaa , ' Kitum igleghutistengllaghtaten , nanqigtistengllaghtatenllu whangkunnun ?
Whangallu tuqusugsingaa ighivgaq tuqutelleghpetun Egypt-eghmii ? '
Yugem tawaten piyatni Moses qimakaq Midian-mun , tamaani allaneghtaakaq . Qenwat nulightughluni ighnengegkaq maalghugegneng .
" Moses , 40 ayumiqulleq Midian-metutkelluku kilgaanun aghulaqegkaq Mount Sinai-em uvitanganun . Tawani esghaqaa yaqulek kumaghulghiimi uqfillegami .
Allaaghlluwhaghyagutkaqegkanga . Kenqigtengngwaaghnaluku takukaa , kaasaghtughaqaallu Atanghem pikaa ,
' Kiyaghneghuunga , sivuneghpek Abraham-enkut Isaac-enkut Jacob-enkut Kiyaghneqaatnga . ' Moses alingruuqaq repall ungelegtekaq talwa esghaghyugumangitkaa .
Atanghem pikaa , ' Kaamgegken mataghtikek qayughllak whanga apalluqlunga agleghnalghiinguuq nekevghavigen .
Esghapaganka yugenka amyuutkegkangit Egypt-mi , nagatanka ngilleglleghhiit . Ukigtunga yugulinaluki Egypt-eghmiineng . Enkaam whaa kayaggnaqamken Egypt-mun . '
" Taananguuq Moses Israel-eghmiit ighsakaqngamegteggu pikaat , ' Kitum igleghutistengllaghtatenllu nanqigtistengllaghtatenllu whangkunnun ? ' Iwernga ellnganguuq Kiyaghneghem uteghnightestekaa Egypt-mun igleghutistengulukullu yugulighistengulukullu ellngitnun . Tawaten Kiyaghneghem pikaqaa yaqulegkun kumaghulghiimi uqfillegami .
Moses allaaghluwhaghtighllagaataghluni Egypt-mi , aghulaqutkaqii sivuneput Egypt-meng . Wata allaaghlluwhaghtiighaataqaaguq Red Sea-millu , igleghalleghmeggnillu kilgaani maghyaghqughaqngamiki 40 ayumiqulleghni .
Taananguuq Moses Israel-eghmiinun whaten pikaq , ' Kiyaghneghem uuknaliqista nakmikelleqaa yugpesineng whanga nakmikelleghmitun uuknaliqistengulunga . '
Taananguuq Moses sivunemnnitkaq qerngughutaqngata kilgaani Mount Sinai-em tungangangi . Tawani naayghami yaqulgem aleghqughyatni tugukii Kiyaghneghem Liilightuusii apeghtuusat naten kiyaghtelleghqameng . Taagken aapqii taakut sivunemnnun enkaam ellngita nagneghtekaqiit whangkunnun .
" Iwernga sivunemta Moses qaatkesugumangitaatlu , igleghutisteksugumangitaatlu , yeghlegi uteghsukaagut Egypt-mun .
Enkaam Moses-em anengaa Aaron pikaat , ' Kiyaghnengllaghteghqut maghyaghqiisqelluta . Nallukaghput Moses samatanga , legan aghulaqulluta Egypt-meng unitiinkut . '
Enkaam kiyaghnengllaqat kaawaghaghsugnilngughmeng , aghqerraaqaatlu . Neqenghaghqegkatlu quulvaghnaluku ulimaaghteng .
" Tawaten piyata Kiyaghneghem tunutkiillu , pegtekiillu elngaatall maniguutesqelluki siqineghmun , tanqimun , ighaleqetaaghnunllu . Ataneq whaten pikaaguq uuknaliqistet igaqellghitni , ' Israel-eghmiini , 40 ayumiqulleghni igleghangulusi kilgaani aghqerraaghumangitaghpesinga tuqutiineghpesini teghikusameng .
Yeghlegi kelqutaaqegkaqasi tiintat manigughviguluki kiyaghnengllaqamun Moloch-mun , kelqutaaqegkaqaghsillu ighaleqetaangllaqaq maniguusiiluku Rephan-mun . Tamaaken apalluqluku anguyagpesinun aghulaqutesleqamsi naghughlluku Babylon . ' "
Stephen paninang akuzikaq , " Sivuneput kilgaanilluki Kiyaghneghem tiintanglliisqegkii amimeng manigughviguluki ellminun . Ulimakaqiit tawatengwaaq Kiyaghneghem apeghtuutellghatun Moses-mun . Kelqutaaqegkiit taakut tiintat neqanguusiiluki Kiyaghneghem nayuutngallghanun .
Taakwaningani Moses tuquyan Kiyaghneghem nakmikegkaa Joshua igleghutistekesqelluku sivunemnnun . Joshua-m maghyaghqughyisteng nunamun Kiyaghneghem akequsaqegkaanun taakut tiintat kelqegkiit . Takukameggnun nunamun kaasalghiimeng yulguftuq . Iwernga Kiyaghneghem sivunemnnun ighlleghtestekii yugi , enkaam sivuneput nelikat taaggun nunakun . Tamaani nagneghutkiit taakut tiintat maniguutfiguluki Kiyaghneghmun kenlanga umiileliitelleghmeggnun David .
David-em kiyaghtaallgha elngaatall efqughnapigtekaalghii Kiyaghneghmi . Enkaam David-em aaptekaqsaqanga whaten , ' Kiyaghnegha Jacob-em , mangteghangllaghlakaan ? ' Iwernga Kiyaghneghem pisimangilkanga ,
yeghlegi David-em ighneghan Solomon-em mangteghangllaqaa Kiyaghneq .
" Iwernga Kiyaghneghllak kiyaghsigatuq mangteghani yuget ulimaaghitni . Whaten Ataneq pikaaguq uuknaliqistem igaqellghani ,
' Qilak aqumutaqaqa , nunallu itegaghiitaqaqa . Sangan mangteghangllaghnaqestengnga ? Meghnalivigitaangunghitunga .
Ulimaaqenghiisikuun sangwaa qamatengngwaaghluku ? ' "
Stephen-em nagneghutkii , " Pineghllugllagni elpesi , qaatkesugigataghsi , ugpeqsugigataghsi Kiyaghneq . Kiyaghneghem ungipii nagasugigatasi , ighsakeraaghaqagsillu Agleghnalghiik Taghneghak sivuneghpesistungwaaq .
Qamaglluki Kiyaghneghem uuknaliqistengi sivuneghpesi amyuutkegkaqiit . Tuququqaqiit uuknaliqistet uuknaliqutkesatgu Seghleghqumangilnguq tagiyaghqaaningatgu . Enkaam kaasan , uveghpagulluku tuqutkaqaghsi .
Elpesinguusi Kiyaghneghem yaqulegteggun tuunegkii Liilightuusaneng , qaatkumangitasi . "
Agghistet nagalluku Stephen sakrituteghllakat repall ggiistaghaatkaat .
Iwernga Stephen , imighngalghii Agleghnalghiigneng Taghneghagneng , sivugsalghiimi qilagmun esghaqaa Kiyaghneghem nighughqellgha , Jesus-llu nekevghalghii Kiyaghneghem aghenqigneghani .
Pikii , " Esghaqaghtegguqun ! Esghaghaqa qilak qelpelghii , Ighneghallu Yugem nekevghalghii Kiyaghneghem aghenqigneghani ! "
Agghistet siguteteng saapluki iiggmeggneng , araghaataasimaghmeng qamaglluteng sughukaat Stephen .
Siingvagaatameng aghulaqutkaat Jerusalem-emeng , tuqunnaluku milughpagaataghhiinaq . Taagken Stephen-em avutkistengita qaasliteng mataghlluki nukalpigam Saul-em saaghwakun lliluki milughpagaataghyuggaaqaat . Tamaakutlu ilangita milughpagaataqaat .
Whaa uyghagem tekiqaghvikngatni Stephen yughaqaq , " Ataneq Jesus , taghneghagka tuguklighqek . "
Segesqughlluni iglagtupiglluni pikaq , " Ataneq , seghevutiki whaken seghleghqellghitneng . " Tawaten piluni tuqukaq .
Saul-em itagnaqegkaa Stephen-em tuqutellgha . Yuget piniqingalghiit Kiyaghneghmeng lliifqaat Stephen qiyakeghllagumaan . Taagken aghneghmeng kenlanga amyuutkeghllagyagutkiit ugpeqat Jerusalem-emelnguut . Saul-em elngaatall amyuutkegkii ugpeqat naangesqelluki . Iitghaqluni nengitnun qamughsiighmeng aanuquqii aghnatlu , yugetlu anusimingllaghtesqughnaluki . Qamagtengngwaaghluteng ugpeqat , pelleghmun qimaguutkat nunanun Judea-melngughnunllu , Samaria-melngughnunllu , apostle-nginaghhaat qimagumangilnguut .
Tamaakut ugpeqat qimaguutkat tamanganun ungipaqikat Pinilghiineng Ungipaneng naansaghngaaghmeng .
Philip Samaria-lluni ungipaqegkaa Christ-a , allaaghlluwhaghtighllagaataqaqlu .
Enkaam yuget nagatngwaaqaqegkangat esghapagluki allaaghlluwhaghtillghi .
Uglapiglleghhiineng yugneng aanesquqii tughneghaat akilghuungitgun . Tamaakutlu piyugigalnguut , uniiqatlu naallghuquqii .
Enkaangam Samaria-ghmiit elngaatall quyaghllakat .
Samaria-minguq taawa alignalghii yuuk , aatgha Simon . Salin Philip kaatellghilluku alignaghtaalleghmikun saghiighayugtaqegkangi yuget , qukaayugtaqelghiillu aghtiiganniluni .
Enkaam qamaglluteng tamaanlenguut , pingwaaghllagneng , ukavanlleghpigaghnun nagasukestaghluku ayuqegkangat . Pikaat , " Una yuuk aghtughyaghqaanghillengeghllakaaguq Kiyaghneghmeng . "
Yuget nagasupiglluku ayuqegkangat , qayughllak qavngarugllaggaaneng allaaghlluwhaghyugtekayugukangi alignaghtaalleghmikun .
Iwernga Philip-em ungipaqsaki Pinilghiit Ungipat Kiyaghneghem Ataneghpagullghaneng ayuqelghiit , Aatghanengllu Jesus Christ-am ugpeqegkiit ungipii . Tamaakut yugetlu , aghnatlu ugpeqilghiit paaptaayekat .
Talwa Simon-emllu ugpeqegkii . Enkaam paaptaayelleghmi kingunganeng maligsaaqaa Philip . Esghapagluku Philip allaaghhiinaghneng allaaghlluwhaghtiighaatalghii saghiighayukaq .
Apostle-et Jerusalem-emelnguut nagaqughluki Samaria-ghmiit ugpeghniluki Kiyaghneghem Ungipaaneng , kayagtekagket Peter-enkuk John-enkuk ellngitnun .
Samaria-ghmiit ugpeqiit paaptaayekat Aatghinaghhaakun Atanghem Jesus-em , naqam salin nalighhiiniita allgeghsigalkegket Agleghnalghiik Taghneghak . Peter-enkuk John-enkuk Samaria-mun kaallutek aglaqak ugpeqanun . Taagken saaftaqluki yughaatkaataqiik , enkaam Agleghnalghiik Taghneghak allgeghtekagket .
Simon-em esghapakakek apostle-ek , saafneghmegneki ugpeqat allgeghutaqelghiit Agleghnalghiigneng Taghneghagneng .
Enkaam apostle-ek pikakek , " Tukfighiighllanga aghtughyaghqaanghilleghmeng whangallu saaftekumki yuget allgeghutesqelluki Agleghnalghiigneng Taghneghagneng . "
Iwernga Peter-em pikaa , " Yeqay Kiyaghneghem naafqelliten manituumaghpek . Sumeghpenii-i Kiyaghneghem tunusaa tukfighlleqniluku pizigu ?
Qepghalgusighinaanghituten , qayughllak sumeghtaghallghen anaggutngaaq Kiyaghneghem esghaamallghani .
Avuteghqelluten seghleghqusiqnanighhungam taana seghlepestaaq piyukellghen . Enkaam yughaa Ataneghmun luuraq seghevunnayukagu taana seghlepestaaq seghleghqellghen .
Taawa liigikamken aqinallelegllaguutenllu asighqengngaatenllu seghleghqelleghpeneng . "
Simon-em pikakek , " Yughaatkaghtegnenga Ataneghmun tawaten pilleghpesistun pifqaama pisqellunga . "
Taagken Peter-enkuk John-enkuk tistemunilutek , ungipaqilutek Atanghem ungipaaneng aghulaqegkak Jerusalem-emun . Samaria-mi igleghangulutek , nenun kaanneghmegni Pinilghiineng Ungipaneng ungipaghaqelghiik .
Taagken yaqulgan Atanghem pikaa Philip , " Yataaghqelluten ikevaam tunganganilengughnun tumenun aglaa paaghqillghanilngughnun , Jerusalem-emeng Gaza-mun ayuqelghiinun . "
Enkaam yataaghqelluni aghulaqegkaq . Taakwani tumangani esghaqaa Ethiopia-ghmii eunuch , Ethiopia-m Queen-ngan Candace-em , manimeng aflengakistenga . Jerusalem-emeng uteghnighaqeftuq neminun maniguusaghtughluni Kiyaghneghmun . Chariot-mikun igleghutkelluku atightughaqeftii uuknaliqestem Isaiah-m igaqegkii .
Agleghnalghiim Taghnegham pikaa Philip , " Chariot-ngan saaghwanun aglaghluten maligsaaghhu . "
Enkaam malighqaghluku nagatkaa atightulghii uuknaliqestem Isaiah-am igaqegkaaneng . Philip-em aaptekaa , " Liigiksikii atightuqaghten ? "
Kiimsiqaa , " Naten liigikesqelluki piziki , wetkuqun kitum liigikestekaki whangamnun sameng piiqutangi . " Taagken uugtesluku saaghwmikun aqumesqegkaa .
Eunuch-em atightughaqeftii Kiyaghneghem akuzitangi whaten pilghiit : " Penniighet tuqusaghtunghisteng qalghiigatut , penniighaghaatlu qigunghisteng qalghiigatut , tawateghpigaq ellngallu sameng piighsimangilnguq .
Kayngusaakestaqngatgu igughistengitkaq . Unguvallgha kenletghuutestekaq nunami . Enkaam kitumngam aapghwaaghlleqaki seghleghtulangi yulgutangan tamaani pilleghmi ? "
Eunuch-em aaptekaa Philip , " Ungipaataghtinga uuknaliqista ellmineng akuzitkaqaa , nalighmeng kina alla piiqagu ? "
Philip-em piinliisiqluki Isaiah-am igaqegkii , ungipaatkaa Pinilghiineng Ungipaneng Jesus-meng .
Igleghutkelluku meghmun kaasamek eunuch-em pikaa , " Esgha taana meq ! Sangwaangam eltuusiqelleqsikun paaptaayelleghqamnun ? "
Philip-em pikaa , " Ipapighqelluten ugpequvek paaptaayelleqamken . " Eunuch-em kiimsiqaa , " Aa , ugpeqaqa Jesus Christ-a Ighneqaa Kiyaghneghem . "
Enkaam eunuch-em igleghutisteni aghuliighesqegkaa . Ateghlutek chariot-meng meghmun aatqak , enkaam Philip-em tawani paaptaayekaa .
Meghmeng uugsayek Atanghem Taghneghagkenka aghulaqutkaa Philip , enkaam eunuch-em alla esghamangitkaa , iwernga nagneqaq quyallelighllagluni .
Taana Philip piyalghiimi Azotus-meteftuq . Caesarea-mun aglaatkelluku nenun kaanneghmini Pinilghiineng Ungipaneng ungipaghaqelghii .
Saul Jerusalem-emelluni taawa paninang alingsiqukii tuququghnaqniluki maligsaaghtengi Atanghem . Qenwat Damascus-esukaq , luuraq Jesus-em maligsaaghtengi yugetlu aghnatlu tamaannayukata . Esghaqumiki taginnaluki Jerusalem-emun anusiminglliisqelluki . Enkaam high priest-mun piluni latangllaatesqegkaq pilleghqalitesqelluni igleghutistengitnun synagogue-et Damascus-melngughnun , tawaten pinaluni .
Enkaam Saul aghulaqegkaq Damascus-mun . Iiwenllu kaasaghtughaquq , qilagmeng nighugllagem kukegtekaa .
Uullghaghlluni nagaquqaa ma whaten pilghii , " Saul , Saul , sangama amyuutkumanginaghsinga ? "
Saul-em aaptekaa , " Kinanguzin Ataneq ? " Mem kiimsiqaa , " Jesus-nguunga amyuutkegkan .
Makelluten aglaa Damascus-mun , tawani kitum ungipaalleqaaten naten pilleghqaghpeneng . "
Yuget igleghalgutangi aghuliiqat tawani , akuzipagningunateng nagatkaat ma , naqam kina alngunak esghaamangilkangat .
Saul makesalghiimi esghaanneghituq qayughllak ayaamalghii . Enkaam tasluqluku aglaatkaat Damascus-mun .
Pingayut aghneghet ayaangakaq , talwa neghumangilnguqlu , meghumangilnguqlu .
Taawanguq Damascus-mi , yuuk ugpeqingalghii Jesus-meng , aatgha Ananias . Esghaaghwaalleghqun Atanghem tuqluqaa , " Ananias . " Kiimsiqaa , " Ay , Ataneq ? "
Atanghem pikaa , " Tumenun aglaa aatqelghiinun , ' Taklaghrukegtaq ' Taagken Judas-enkunun aapsaghtughhu yuuk , Saul-nguuq , Tarsus-meng pinguuq , yughaghaquq .
Esghaghwaaghqun esghamaa yuuk itelghii , aatgha Ananias , saafsaqminigu esghaghyagunneqigtuq . "
Iwernga Ananias-em pikaa , " Ataneq , nagaqughaqaqa taana yuuk uglapiglleghhiineng , apeghnaqepigtaqaat seghletun pilleghllaga yugpenun Jerusalem-emi .
Pilleghqangegkaaguq chief priest-eneng tagiluni Damascus-mun tugulaghnaluki qamaglluki yughaqayuget ateghpegun . "
Iwernga Atanghem pikaa , " Aglaa , takugu qayughllak nakmikumaaqa ungipaqesqellunga Gentile-enun , umiilegnun , Israel-eghmiinunllu .
Liigikesnaqngwaaqa aangluku ikfiqelleghmeng whanga apalluqlunga . "
Enkaam Ananias-em takukaa Saul . Iteghluni saafsimaan pikaa , " Anglegutemni Saul , Atanghem Jesus-em esghaqaghpek tumeni taginguluten , kayagtaanga elpenun . Kayagutaaten saaftesqelluten esghaasagunneqigtesqelluten , imiisqellutenllu Agleghnalghiigneng Taghneghagneng . "
Tawaninginaq iqallugem qaltesugningi iyegkeneng ifkaquutkat , enkaam esghasagutkaq . Taagken makelluni paaptaayekaq .
Taam kingunganeng neghyalghiimi iknaqsuugtekaq . Saul ugpeqanitkaq Damascus-mi qafsinat aghneghet .
Mulugpenani synagogue-ni ungipaqegkaa Jesus , Ighneqniluku Kiyaghneghmun .
Nagatullghiim saghiighayagutkaat repall ellmeggneng aapqughaghutkat , " Unangunghitaa-a yuuk Jerusalem-emi amyuqetiqeghllakaq yughaqayugneng Jesus-em aatghakun ? Maavek taginguyalghii tawaten pinaluni , ugpeqat tugulaghnaluki , aglannaluki chief priest-enun . "
Saul-em ungipaqilleghmikun wata liigikestaghaqaa Jesus , Christ-angutanga repall Jews-et Damascus-melnguut aaghtiiraaghpagningitkaat .
Saul ungipaqilqinaghyan tawaten qafsinegyagllak aghneq , Jews-et wataqaaghaq ugumiyagutkaat , repall qerngughulluteng agghitkegkaat tuqunnaluku .
Enkaam aghneghtuumaan , unugtuumaan Damascus-em amigllalghutngani kelengakegkaat tuqunnaluku . Iwernga Saul-em nagaquqaa tawaten agghillghat .
Enkaam unugmi ataasimi , Saul-em maligsaaghtengita pasket-eghrugllagegnekun mingllutmeng eslatmun ukigtekaat .
Taagken Saul kaasami Jerusalem-emun ilannaqegkaayaalghii Jesus-em maligsaaghtengitnun . Taawanginaq iingunaghhaghmeng alikegkaat , qayughllak aygughikegkaat ellngallu maligsaaghtengughsimatanga .
Iwernga Barnabas-em Saul aglaalluku apostle-enun aapqaa Saul-mun tumemi esghaamaniluku Ataneq , aleghquutkaaniluteklu . Aapqaallu Damascus-mi ungipaqaaniluku tetugpenani Aatghakun Jesus-em .
Enkaam tugukliqaat . Taagken kenlanga Saul ugpeqanitkaq . Igleghutkelluku Jerusalem-emi , ungipaqikaq tetugpenani aatghakun Atanghem . Iwernga ilangita Jews-et Greek-estun akuzikayuget aaghtiiraaqaan tuqusukaqegkangat .
Ugpeqat liigiksamegteggu Jews-enun tuqunnaqniluku Saul , aglaatkaat Caesarea-mun , taagken kayagtekaat Tarsus-mun .
Qamaglluteng ugpeqat Judea-mi , Galilee-mi , Samaria-millu amyuutkestengngunateng kiyaghtekat . Ugpellghit iknaqughtekat , alingaqelghiit qaatkunneghitelleghqameggneng Ataneghmun , Agleghnalghiimllu Taghnegham kayusiingukangi enkaam ugpeqat nulakat .
Peter-em igleghatkelluku laalighfikuqii Kiyaghneghem yugi naansaghngaata . Ataasimi aghneghmi laalightekaq Lydda-melngughnun .
Tamaani esghaqaa yuuk aatgha Aeneas , pingayuneng inglulek ayumiqulleq makesigalnguq uniighngatmiineng .
Peter-em pikaa , " Aeneas , Jesus Christ-am naallghutaaten , makelluten allighan iimggu . " Tawaninginaq Aeneas maketkaq .
Uglapiglleghhiit Lydda-ghmiitlu Sharon-eghmiitlu esghaghyamegteggu Aeneas naallghulluni , ugpeghtuutkat Ataneghqun .
Joppa-minguq taawa ugpeqaq aghnaq aatgha Tabitha , ( Greek-stun Dorcas , whaten pisiq , quyngiq ) , quunpeng kayusighimaghllak , kiyang tamaakunun aklumalghiinun .
Taagken qinuyugluni tuqukaq enkaam ughvughqelluku qemtamun mayuutkaat .
Joppa-ghmiit ugpeqat nagaquqaat Peter Lydda-menniluku . Lydda , Joppa-meng qantaghaghhanlenguq , enkaam ugpeqat kevgaqegkagket maalghuk yugek Peter-mun tagiragkiighesqelluku Joppa-mun .
Peter-em yataaghqelluni maligtekakek . Kaasan qemtamun mayuutkaat . Legan iteghtuq ugingighat qiyamaghmeng kanglluqaghlluku kelguvikegkaat aatkaneng Dorcas-em ulimaaghaneng .
Peter-em aanesqughluki segesqughlluni yughaqaq . Taaqluni yughaneghmeng qiivluku yugusiq pikaa , " Tabitha , maketen . " Tabitha esghaatkelluku esghaghyamigu Peter aqumegkaq .
Peter-em iiggakun tuguluku nekevestekaa . Taagken tuqluqii ugpeqatlu ugingighatlu esghiisqelluku unguvaamatanga .
Qamagtengngwaaghluteng Joppa-ghmiit nagaquqaat Tabitha-m unguvallgha enkaam uglapiglleghhiim ugpeqegkaat Ataneq .
Peter mulukaq Joppa-mi , Simon-enkunitkaq sanaghtistemi .
Caesarea-minguq taawa yuuk aatgha Cornelius . Umiilgat Rome-em pilluwaghtengita Italy-meng pit .
Yuuk pinilghii , kayusighimaghllak aklumalghiinun , yughatuqaqlu Kiyaghneghmun . Nengllugutkullghiit , qepghaghtekullghiit maniguutkayuget Kiyaghneghmun .
Ataasimi aghneghmi 3-klaagmi esghaghwaaqaq . Whateghlluwaaq esghaqaa Kiyaghneghem yaqulga itelghii , yaqulgem tuqluqaa , " Cornelius ! "
Alingruughumaghmi esghapagtughluku yaqulek aaptekaa , " Ataneq , sameng pizin ? " Yaqulgem pikaa , " Kiyaghneghem nagaquumii yughalleghten , efquqepigtaallu kayusighillghen aklumalghiinun enkaam neqamikaaten .
Joppa-mun aqfastigu yuuk aatqelghii Simon Peter-meng .
Simon-enkunituq sanaghtistemi , mangteghaa esnemetuq . "
Yaqulgem tawaten piluku unitkaa . Taagken Cornelius-em tuqluqakek maalghuk qepghaghtegni , pillugwaghtallu . Taana pilluwaghta Cornelius-em kayutanga maniguutkayuk Kiyaghneghmun .
Tagiyata ungipaatngwaaqii esghaghwaalleghmineng , taagken kevgaqegkii Joppa-mun .
Unaamingani aghneghem qukaani kevgat kaasaghtughaqutlu Joppa-mun , Peter mayuqaq mangtegham qaaynganun yughaghnaluni .
Taagken iyataqaq , sameng neghyukaq . Sama neqmeng yataaghqumaluki Peter esghaghwaaqaq .
Esghaqaa qilak qelpelghii , taagken esghaqaa qiipaghaghllagsugnilnguq ukigtekangat nunamun estamatgun tekerqaakun .
Taawanguq imaqeftuq allaaghhiinaghneng teghikusaneng , reptile-eneng , qawaagnengllu tengaakayugneng .
Taagken mem pikaa , " Peter , makelluten tuqutiluten neghi ! "
Iwernga Peter-em pikaa , " Yeghlegillu , Ataneq ! Neghigatunga iinghutkameng ukmanginneghilngughmeng teghikusameng . "
Mem pilaataqaa , " Kiyaghneghem ukmangiqaqii taakut , ukmanginneghinniluki pigpenaki . "
Tawaten pikaq pingayuneng ketwhell . Taagken tawaninginaq taana iingunaghmi qilagmun mayuutkaq .
Peter-em kukriqutkegkaa sameng pisiitanga esghaghwaalleni . Tawaten pimaluku Cornelius-em kevgiita liitkaat Simon-em mangteghaa naantulanga , enkaam manughaanun kaatkat .
Qamavek aaptekiit , " Whani aqelqaanghitaa yuuk aatgha Simon Peter ? "
Peter-em paninang sumeghtaghaatkumaluku esghaghwaalleni , Taghnegham pikaa , " Uyuq , yuget pingayut ivaghaqaaten .
Ukigluten qaqilqafqaavek maligtiki , qayughllak whanga kayagtanka elpenun . "
Enkaam Peter-em ukigluni pikii , " Whanganguuq ivaqaghsi . Sameng pistengnga ? "
Kiimsiqaat , " Cornelius-em kevgaqiinkut , umiilguuq Rome-em pilluwaghtengitnun . Yuuk pinighllagtuq maniguutkayuk Kiyaghneghmun , qamagllutengllu Jews-et siivakepigtaqaat . Kiyaghneghem yaqulgan pikaqaa Cornelius , ' Aqfastigu Peter elpesinun pisqelluku , nagatesqelluku sameng pilleghqaa elpenun . ' "
Taagken Peter-em iitghesqegkii , tawanillu qaviisqegkii . Unaamingani yataaghqelluni maligtekii Cornelius-em kevgii , ugpeqatlu ilangi Joppa-meng maligutkat .
Taagken unaamingani kaatkat Caesarea-mun . Cornelius-em ilakwaanillu ilakumtaanillu tagilaghaatesluki ellmeggnun utaqakaat Peter .
Peter iitghaquqlu Cornelius-em payeghluku segesqughfikegkaa manigughnaluku .
Iwernga Peter-em nekevestutkelluku pikaa , " Nekevi , whangallu yuguunga . "
Iitghutkelluku Peter-em aleghquqaa Cornelius . Iteghyalghiimi taawa yuuk qerngughuteghllagumalghii tawani .
Peter-em pikii , " Liisimakngwaaghaghsi whangkuta Jews-eni Liilightuusamta ineghtekaqiinkut ilatefqaamta pisqelluta Gentile-enun , talwa laalighfikesnaniqaqii . Iwernga Kiyaghneghem kelguvikaanga kina alngunak ukmanginneghinniluku sumeghtaghaatkefqaan pisqelluku .
Aqfasafsinga tagiinga qaqilqagpenanga . Sangama piiqestengnga ? "
Cornelius-em pikaa , " Whaten lliighumaan akuwaaq piiqellemtun yughaamalunga 3-kellaagmi , yuuk manumkun nekevuq aatkii nighugllaget .
Whaa piinga , ' Cornelius ! Kiyaghneghem yughalleghten nagaquumii , neqamikiillu aklumalghiinun kayusighilleghten .
Joppa-mun kina kevgaqigu aqfasqelluku Simon Peter . Simon-enkunituq sanaghtistemi , mangteghaa esnemetuq . '
Enkaam tawaninginaq aqfasqamken , quyakamken tagilghiiten . Liisimakluku Kiyaghneghem nayuqellgha qamaglluta whaanlengughni nagaqughyugaghput sangwaa qamaglluku Atanghem elpenun aapghesqegkaa whangkunnun . "
Taagken Peter-em pikii , " Taawa ipa liigikaqa Kiyaghneq taniillghiteftuq , tawatengwaaq pikayuguftaa tamaghhaghllagan yuuk ataasistun .
Tuguklighyaghqaqaa kina alngunak nakumiinguyaghngaan alikilghii ellmineng , pinitunllu pikayuk .
Liisimakaghsi Kiyaghneghem ungipaa ungipaqegkaq Israel-eghmiinun , taana Pinilghii Ungipaq yuget nekeggmellengusighqaqaat Kiyaghneghmun Jesus Christ-akun . Jesus Christ-a , Atanqaa tamaghhaghwaaghmi yugem .
Liisimakaghsi taana ungipaq mingitkaaguq Judea-lqaaghaghmi , piinliqaq Galilee-mi John-em ungipaqaqngagu paaptaayelleq .
Liisimakaghsi Jesus Nazareth-eghmii , Kiyaghneghem imiqaa Agleghnalghiigneng Taghneghagneng , aghtughyaghqaanghilleghmengllu . Navek alngunak pineghmini pinitun piiqegkangi yuget , naallghuquqiillu tamaakut Tughneghaam aaghqutaqegkii , qayughllak Kiyaghneq Jesus-melnguq .
Whangkuta apostle-eni liisimakistenguukut tamaghhaanun tawaten pillghanun Jews-et nunangitni , Jerusalem-emillu . Tuqutkaqaat tuquuqaalluku qaquurakun .
Iwernga pingayiitangani aghneghem Kiyaghneghem unguvaghtestekaqaa tuqulleghmeng , esghaghtestekaqaallu yugnun .
Iwernga qamaglluni yugem esghaamangitaa . Whangkuta esghaqaqaghput qayughllak Kiyaghneghem nakmikegkaqiinkut liisimakistenguluta . Talwa neghelgusiqaqaghputlu meghelgusiqaqaghputlu kingunganeng unguvaghtestellghan tuqulleghmeng .
Taagken kayagtekaqiinkut ungipaqesqelluku Pinilghii Ungipaq , aapghesqegkaaguqlu Kiyaghneghmun nakmikegkaqniluni nanqigtistenguluni unguvalghiinunllu tuqukanunllu .
Qamaglluteng uuknaliqistet pikaagut , kitumnguq alngunak ugpeqegkumigu aatghakun , seghevutellengyaghqaaguq seghleghqelleghmineng . "
Peter paninang akuzimaluku qamaglluki nagallghiit ungipameng Agleghnalghiim Taghnegham iitqii , enkaam allaaghlluwhatun akuzistekiillu usuqistekiillu Kiyaghneghmeng . Circumcise-ekat ugpeqat Joppa-meng maligutkat Peter-mun saghiighayukat nagasamegteki tawaten akuzillghiit . Liigikegkaat Kiyaghneghem Agleghnalghiik Taghneghak tunusaqegkek talwa Gentile-enun . Taagken Peter-em pikii ,
" Ukut yuget allgeghutut Agleghnalghiigneng Taghneghagneng whangkuteghpigaghestun . Kitumngam paaptaayesnanighnaqaki meghqun ? "
Taagken qelqii paaptaayesqelluki Aatghakun Jesus Christ-am . Taam kingunganeng ellmeggnitaghiisqegkaat Peter .
Apostle-etlu ugpeqatlu Judea-melnguut nagaquqiit Gentile-enunllu ugpequmaniluki Kiyaghneghem akuzitangi .
Peter kaasan Jerusalem-emun , Jews-et ugpeqat circumcise-eghiyukat Gentile-et ugpeqiitneng seghlequuqaat Peter , pikaat ,
" Sangan circumcize-emangilnguut iteghvikluki nengitnun neghelgusighsiki ? "
Liigikesqelluki Peter-em esghaghwaalleghmineng kenlanga aapqaa sangwaa qamaglluku apeghiiqaq .
" Joppa-mi yughaamalunga esghaghwaaqaagunga . Esghaghaqa qiipaghaghllagsugni estamatgun tekerqaakun ukigtekangat qilagmeng whangamnun .
Tawavek yuvghiighwaaghyaqegka imaqeftuq allaaghhiinaghneng teghikusaneng , reptile-eneng , qawaagneng tengaakayugneng .
Taagken ma nagaqughaqa whaten pilghii , ' Peter , makelluten tuqutiluten neghi ! '
Iwernga kiimsighaqa , ' Yeghlegillu Ataneq ! Neghigatanka tamaakut ukmanginneghilnguut neqet iinghutkat . '
" Mem pilaataghaanga qilagmeng , ' Kiyaghneghem ukmangiqaqii tamaakut , ukmanginneghinniluki sumeghtaghaatkesaghqaqenghitaten . '
Tawaten pikaaguq pingayuneng ketwhell . Taagken qamaglluteng taakut aga qilagmun mayuutaqutlu ,
whaa yuget pingayut kaatut tukumnun , kevgaaftut whangamnun Caesarea-meng .
Agleghnalghiim Taghnegham qaqilqafqaama maligtesqii . Ukutlu aghvinlek yuget ugpeqaalguteput maligutut Joppa-meng Caesarea-mun . Kaalluta Cornelius-enkunun iteghaatukut .
Cornelius-em aapghaa yaqulegmeng esghaatelleni nemini , yaqulgemnguq whaten pii , ' Joppa-mun aqfastigu yuuk aatqelghii Simon Peter-meng .
Ungipaalleqiisi nengllugutkullghiini naten yugulillengelleghqameng . '
Enkaam akuziiqungallu Agleghnalghiim Taghnegham iitghii tawatengwaaq whangkunnun itelleghmitun Pentecost-em Aghneghani .
Taagken neqangughaqa Atanghem pillgha whaten , ' John paaptaayelaqaaguq meghqun , iwernga elpesi paaptaayellequsi Agleghnalghiignekun Taghneghagnekun . '
Enkaam Kiyaghneghem tuunumakaki Gentile-et taagken ataasimeng tunusameng tuunegkamineng whangkunnun ugpeqaqngamteggu Ataneq Jesus Christ-a , whanga kinanguzinga aghuliighhnaqsaghqaaluku Kiyaghneq tawaten pillghaneng Gentile-enun ? "
Tawaten Peter-em piyisteng qallegnanighluteng , yeghlegi usuqegkaat Kiyaghneq . Pikat , " Taawa liigikaghput Kiyaghneghem talwa Gentile-et pilleghqalisimakangi avuteghqesqelluki seghleghqellghitneng , unguvallengesqellukillu kenlengilngughmeng unguvalleghmeng ! "
Stephen-em tuqutellgha kenlekluku Jews-et amyuutkegkiit ugpeqat , enkaam anakat Jerusalem-emeng . Aghulaquutkat kenlanga Phoenicia-mun , Cyprus-mun , Antioch-munllu . Igleghutkelluku ungipaqegkiit Pinilghiit Ungipat Jews-nginaghhaghnun .
Iwernga ilangi ugpeqat Cyprus-mengllu Cyrene-mengllu Antioch-etkat , kaalluteng ungipaqegkaat Ataneq Jesus talwa Jews-ngunghilngughnun .
Atanghem aghtughyaghqaanghillgha ellngitnitkaalghii , enkaam uglapestaaq yuuk ugpeghtuulluni qiivuutkaq Ataneghmun .
Ugpeqat Jerusalem-emelnguut nagalluku Peter , Barnabas kayagtekaat Antioch-mun .
Kaasalghiimi uglaapiglleghhii yuuk ugpeghtuulluni ayuqeftuq , enkaam quyaghllakaq qayughllak liigikegkaa Kiyaghneghem piniqingalleghllaga yugnun . Barnabas pinilghiingulghii yuuk , imighngaghllaklu Agleghnalghiigneng Taghneghagneng , ugpeqillelegllaklu . Taagken allangughtefqiita ataasiighmetekestiisqegkii Ataneghmun . Wataqaaghaq ilangitallu yuget ugpeqegkaat Ataneq .
Taagken Barnabas-em Saul ivaghyaghtuqaa Tarsus-mun .
Naalkesamigu kelqegkaa Antioch-mun . Ataasiq ayumiqulleq tamaantelleghmegni ilataqlutek ugpeqanun apeghtughikak yulghuteghllagnun . Tamaani Antioch-mi ugpeqat atighyuwhaaqiit , " Christian-et . "
Tamaani ilangi uuknaliqistem Jerusalem-emeng Antioch-mun tagikat .
Ataasiq Agabus-nguftuq , nekevluni uuknaliqegkaq Taghneghagnekun neqangisagllagnaqniluku tamangani . Taawa neqangisagllakaq Claudius Umiilegpigaaluku .
Ugpeqat ugpeqaalguteteng Judea-melnguut kayusighyukiit pitutalmegestun .
Enkaam qerngughtiluteng manimeng tuyughikat elder-enun Jerusalem-emelngughnun Barnabas-enkugnekun Saul-enkugnekun .
Nani tamaani pilleghmi Umiilgem Herod-em amyuutkesagutkii ilangi ugpeqat .
John-em anglegutanga James tuqutestekaa savigpagkun .
Umiilgem Herod-em liigiksamigu Jews-eneng efqughtilleni tawaten pilleghmikun , qelghutkaa Peter tugusqelluku . ( Tawaten pikaaftuq Neqenghaghqengnguluki Yeast-aliimangilngughmeng Neqekrangllameng . )
Peter tuguyatgu , Umiilgem Herod-em qelghutkaa 16-eghyagnun pilluwaghtenun kelengakesqelluku estamakaghtiita kipullgutaqluki . Yugtuqami nanqigsukaa kingunganeng Passover-em .
Enkaam Peter anusimingllaghvigmetestekaa . Iwernga ugpeqat yughaatkeghllakaat Kiyaghneghmun .
Peter qavaalghii maalghuk kelengakistek akulegkeni , petugngalghiillu malghugneghteggun qiipraghutetgun . Allameng anusimingllaghvigem amiga kelengakistelek . Whaa aghtekan Herod-em tagitesnaqngukanga yugnun nanqigtesqelluku .
Atanghem yaqulga aliighaghtekaq , enkaam nighuk kuukgutkaq anusimingllaghvigem ilunganun . Yaqulgem Peter tuuyngakun aghulalluku , teghtughlluku pikaa , " Egmiinaq maketen ! " Tawaninginaq qiipraghutet ifkaquutkat iigganeng .
Taagken yaqulgem pikaa , " Pilugugluten kaamgegken aatikek . " Peter pisqellghatun pikaq . Yaqulgem pilaataqaa , " Qaasligken aallukek maligtinga . "
Enkaam Peter-em maligtekaa . Ugpequmangitngwaaqaqsaqanga aanutelleni , yeghlegi sumeghtaghaqaq esghaghwaaghniluni .
Sivuliitlu tuunglighhiillu kelengakistet naghughlluki kaatkak savikenghaaghmun amigmun . Amik ellmineng qelpeghyan , aanlutek igleghteghngaagmek tumetgun yaqulek aviitqaghtekaq .
Taagken Peter-em liigikngwaaqaa samatni enkaam pikaq , " Taawa ipanguftuq Atanghem kayagsimaa yaquleni iqitutesqellunga Herod-meng , Jews-etlu salleghqiitneng . "
Liigikluku samatni Mary-nkunun aglaqaq , John Mark-em naanganun . Tawani yulghun qerngughulluni yughaateghllagulghii qerngaghmi .
Peter eslaklighqun amigkun tenglugtughyan aghnaghaam qepghaghtem , Rhoda-m qelpeghusaghtuqaa .
Liisuqsamigu Peter-em menga , quyaghllagem angtalanganeng qelpeghutegpenaan , yeghlegi ilutmun iitqaghlluni aapqaa qakma Peter manughamenniluku .
Iwernga pikaat , " Temngi piiten ! " Iwernga sagiqutkii ipanguniluku . Taagken pikaat , " Yaqulkenghitaguwha . "
Qakma Peter tenglugtuumanginaqaq . Qelpeghusaqmegteggu ellnganguftuq enkaam saghiighayukat .
Peter-em apaqukii qallegnaniisqelluki , enkaam ungipamsugutngwaaqii Atanghem aanutellghaneng anusimingllaghvigmeng . Pikiillu , " Aapqaghnakefsinga James-munllu ugpeqaalgutemnnunllu tawaten pimanilunga . " Taagken aanluni natmun pikaq .
Aghtaghaghaqaallu kelengakistet aviilngaqaat Peter , alingrughumaghmeng kukriqegkat samatanga .
Herod-em ivaghtesimayaqanga iwernga naalkumangitkaat . Enkaam kelengakistet aapqughaaghtesluki nalluksatgu tuququghtestekii . Taam kingunganeng Herod Judea-meng Caesarea-lluni tamaanteghraakaq .
Umiilgem Herod-em ugumiyaguteghllagukangi Tyre-eghmiitlu Sidon-eghmiitlu , iwernga tamaakumiit yuget kayagtekiit Blastus-mun akuzitunnaqaghtesqelluteng Herod-mun . Blastus igleghutistekegkanga Umiilgem Herod-em mangteghaghllagan . Kaalluteng aaptekaat Blastus akuzitutaghtesqelluteng umiilegmun . Tawaten pikaalghiit neqengnanighnayukameng Herod-em nunanganeng .
Tawani aghneghmi pivigkameggni Herod-em umiilgusit aatkani aatqughluki aqumluni aqumutaghllagegmikun akuzikaq .
Taaqsan akuzineghmeng yuget akilghuukat , " Yugunghituq akuzilghii , naliqaat kiyaghneghet ! "
Tawaninginaq Atanghem yaqulgan qinuyugtesteghllakaa Herod , qayughllak tugukliqanga quulvalleq Kiyaghneghem pinga . Unguvaghmi kingugtaaghllagluni tuqukaq .
Taawa Kiyaghneghem ungipii mingisimanginaqat enkaam wata yuuk ugpeghtuutkaq .
Taakuk Barnabas-enkuk Saul-enkuk apeghiighyamegnegu qepghaqaghtek Jerusalem-emi , Antioch-mun uteghniqak kelqelluku John Mark .
Antioch-mi ugpeqam ilangi uuknaliqistenguftutlu apeghtughistenguftutlu . Taakunguftut Barnabas , Simeon , atilqelghii Niger-meng , Lucius ( Cyrene-meng pi ) , Manaen ( anglilgutanga umiilgem Herod-em ) , Saul-llu .
Maniguusimaluki Ataneghmun , fast-emalukillu , Agleghnalghiim Taghnegham pikii , " Aaftekek Barnabas-enkuk Saul-enkuk , qayughllak nakmikagka allaneng qepghaqameng qepghiisqellukek whangamnun . "
Taaqsameng fast-elleghmengllu yughalleghmengllu saaflukek yughaatkellukek aghulaqestekagket .
Barnabas-enkuk Saul-enkuk , Agleghnalghiim Taghnegham kayagsistek , Seleucia-tkak kelqelluku John Mark kayutnguluku . Tamaaken angyaghpagkun qiighqamun Cyprus-mun pikat . Kaasameng Salamis-mun synagogue-ngitni ungipaqikat akuzitanganeng Kiyaghneghem .
Salamis-meng igleghakat inglunganun qiighqam Paphos-mun kaatelleghmeggnun kenlanga . Tamaani nallaqaat yuuk alignalghii aatgha Bar-Jesus , uuknaliqestesighwaaq , Jews-a .
Qiighqam Governor-ngan Sergius Paulus-em ilakumtaagha . Sergius Paulus pillegllak . Aqfastekakek Barnabas-enkuk Saul-enkuk nagannaluki Kiyaghneghem akuzitangi .
Iwernga Bar-Jesus-em alignalghiim , ateghalgem Elymas-meng , aaghtiiraaqakek governor-a ugpeghnayukan . ( Ateq Elymas , Greek-stun whaten pisiilghii , alignalghii . )
Taagken Saul-em , ateghaqelghiim Paul-meng , imighngalghiim Agleghnalghiigneng Taghneghagneng , esghapagtughluku alignalghii
pikaa , " Uyuq Tughneghaam ighnegha ! Ugumikan sangwaa qamaglluku pinilghii . Iqlengasagllaguutenllu seghletunllu pisteghllaguuten . Taaqnaqenghisikii iqlengiqusiqneghmeng Atanghem apeghtuusii ?
Whaa Atanghem aghyuughnaqaaten ayaastemmeng , enkaam esghaatelghaghtughnaanghituten aghneghem nighuganeng . " Tawaninginaq Elymas-em iiskek mamleghqwaakak , enkaam tamaani eflughwaaghmeng ivaghikaq kitumun tasluqiisqelluni .
Governor-a ugpeqaq esghapagluku tawaten pilghii , saghiighayagutkaallu apeghtuusaq Ataneghmeng ayuqelghii .
Paul-enkut igleghalgutkullghiit angyaghpagkun igleghtekat Paphos-meng , Perga-mun Pamphylia-melngughmun . Tamaanlluki John Mark-em unilluki Jerusalem-emun uteghniqaq .
Taagken Paul-enkut Perga-meng , Antioch-etkat Pisidia-melngughmun . Sabbath-ngughsagu synagogue-ngitnun iteghluteng aqumegkat .
Igleghutistengi synagogue-em , taaqsameng atightuneghmeng Liilightuusanengllu uuknaliqistetlu igaqegkiitneng , kevgaqutkiit Paul-enkut whaten pisqelluki , " Ugpeqaalgutemnni , ungipalgukufsi iknaqsuugusighqameng ugpellemnnun , saaqetsi akuzitek . "
Taagken Paul nekevluni apaqumaghmi pikii , " Israel-eghmiini , elpesillu Gentile-eni maniguutkayugni Kiyaghneghmun , nagatengnga !
Whangkuta Israel-eghmiini maniguqamta Kiyaghneghem nakmikegkaqii sivuneput , nulasteghllakaqiillu nunataawaqngata Egypt-mi . Taakwaningani qepghaghtelaaghughtekat iwernga Kiyaghneghem aghtughyaghqaanghilleghllagmikun aghulaqutkaqii Egypt-meng .
Kilgaanilluki qaatkutepagllanghiteghngaata ellminun paninang aflengakegkaqii ketwhell 40 ayumiqulleghni .
Taagken Kiyaghneghem naafqesamiki taakut maaghraghvinlek ramket Canaan-melnguut nunaksaqangat piliitestekaqaa sivunemnnun pagitaqesqelluku .
Entaqun 450-nguut ayumiqullghet Kiyaghneghem nakmikellghaneng sivuneput kenlanga nuna piliitellghitnun . " Taam kingunganeng nanqigtistengestaataqaqii igleghutesqelluki kenlanga Samuel uuknaliqista igleghutistekaaghtellghitnun .
Taagken umiilengyuwaqngata Kiyaghneghem nakmikegkaqaa Saul umiilkesqelluku Kish-em ighnegha , Benjamin-em ramkenganeng pi . Umiilgukaaguq 40 ayumiqulleghni .
Kiyaghneghem umiilgunanightesamigu Saul , David umiileliitestekaa ellngitnun . Kiyaghneghem akuzitkegkaqaa whaten , ' Jesse-m ighnegha David umiilgughtesugaqa . Tawatelnguq yuuk piyukaqaqa , qayughllak piyaghqaqaa sangwaa alngunak piyukegkaqa . '
" Taakwaningani David-em kingunghakun Kiyaghneghem akeqilleghmitun allgeghtestekaqaa Yugulighista Israel-eghmiinun . Taana yugulighista Jesus-nguuq .
Jesus-em salin qepghaqani piinlillghilluku John ungipaqikaaguq Israel-eghmiinun whaten , ' Avuteghqellusi , seghleghqennanighlusi , paaptaayetek . '
John-em qepghaqani taaqsaghtungestaghluku pikaaguq , ' Kinangunilunga piiqestengnga ? Whangangunghituq utaqakaghsi . Kingumneng tagiyaghqaaguq aangeghllalghii , repall whanga pininghitunga singiinun itemtistengulunga . '
" Ugpeqaalgutemni , Abraham-em kingunghitni , Gentile-enillu maniguutkayugni Kiyaghneghmun , taana ungipaa yugulillghem whangkunnun pinguuq !
Jerusalem-eghmiit igleghutistekullghiit nallukegkaqaat Jesus Yugulighistengutanga , qaywa Sabbath-a tamaghhaan nagateghngaaghmegteki uuknaliqistet igaqegkiit . Naqam uuknaliqistet igaqegkiit apeghiiqaqiit agghitkaqngamegteggu Jesus tuqunnaluku .
Taawa legan temngi apalliiteghngaan tuqutusighqameng Pilate-mun tuqutesqegkaqaat .
Legan Akuzitet Igaqegkat pinaqnillghistun pikaqaat . Taagken qaquurameng ateghlluku lliifqaqaat ,
iwernga Kiyaghneghem unguvaghtestekaqaa tuqulleghmeng .
Taam kingunganeng igleghalgutkegkiita Jesus-em Galilee-meng , Jerusalem-emun esghaghaataqaqaat qafsinegyagni aghneghni . Ellnginguut ungipalghiit yumnnun esghaamaniluku Jesus unguvaluku .
" Whaten pikaagut , ' Ungipaatamsi Pinilghiineng Ungipaneng Kiyaghneghem akequsaqegkaaneng sivunemnnun .
Apeghiighumaa akequsani whangkunnun kingunghitnun , unguvaghtestelleghmikun Jesus tuqulleghmeng . ' Kiyaghneq pikaaguq whaten Psalm 2-mi , ' Elpek Ighneqamken , aghneghmi whani Ataliitaghpenga . '
Kiyaghneghem unguvaghtestekaqaa Jesus tuqulleghmeng enkaangam allamengllu tuqunaanghituq aghyughyaghqaaluni . Enkaam Kiyaghneq pikaaguq , ' Agleghnalghiit akequsaqegkanka David-mun ipapestaaq quyastisiqelleqanka elpesinun . '
Ilangani Psalms-em Kiyaghneq pikaaguq , ' Agleghnalghiin aghusnaanghitaqa lliveghmi . '
" David-em unguvalleghmini atuqegkaqaa Kiyaghneghem piyukellgha . Taagken qavaghyan qunguqaqaat sivunghan saaghwitgun , yugusii aghukaaguq lliveghmi .
Iwernga taana Kiyaghneghem unguvaghtestekaa tuqulleghmeng aghumangituq .
Ugpeqaalgutemni , elpesinun liitesqesugaqa Jesus-kun yuget seghleghqellghit seghevutellengegkayuguut . Taanata ungipaqegkegka elpesinun .
Qaatkutellghem Moses-em Liilightuusiitgun kina alngunak itemunnaanghitaa seghleghqellghaneng , iwernga kitum alngunak ugpeqegkumigu Jesus , itemusaghqaaguq tamaghhaaneng seghleghqelleghmineng .
Kiyaghneq pikaaguq uuknaliqistetgun whaten , ' Nagatek elpesi aygughitalghiini . Saaqetsi saghiighayuglusi tuqutek , qayughllak unguvangulusi sallequnga iwernga ugpeqnaanghitaghsi talwa kitum ungipaateghngiisi . ' Kelengalusi , luuraq tawaten pinayukafsi . "
Paul-enkuk Barnabas-enkuk synagogue-meng aanumalukek alla tagisqegkagket tuunglighhaani Sabbath-em , wata ungipiqutesqelluteng .
Aanleghaasameng Jews-elghutetlu , Gentile-elghutetlu maniguutkayuget Kiyaghneghmun Jews-estun , maligutkat Paul-enkugnun Barnabas-enkugnun . Apostle-ek kayemegkiik kiyaghtekestiisqelluki sighimakluku Kiyaghneghem nangllegtallgha .
Tuunglighhaani Sabbath-em qamagtevzighluteng Antioch-eghmiit nagasaatkat Atanghem ungipaaneng .
Jews-et aqinakat esghaghyamegteki yulghuteghllaget enkaam Paul kipullginaqaat , seghleqegkaatlu .
Iwernga Paul-enkuk Barnabas-enkuk tetugpenaki Jews-et pikiik , " Kiyaghneghem ungipaa elpesinun sivukluni apeghyaghqaayaghtuq iwernga nagasugumangitusi . Kiyaghneghem ungipaa ighsakegkaqutegpesineng , palaqegkaategpesinengllu kenlengilngughmeng unguvallengelleghqaghpesineng , whaa Gentile-enun ungipaqinaqukut Kiyaghneghem ungipaaneng .
Tawaten piikut qayughllak Atanghem qelqaqiinkut whaten , ' Nakmikegkaqamsi nighugulusi Gentile-enun , aapghesqelluku yugulilleq nunataghhaanun tamaghhaanun . ' "
Gentile-et nagaqughluki taakut akuzitet quyaghllakat , pikaalghiitlu , " Kiyaghneghem ungipaa piniipigtuq . " Tamaakut Kiyaghneghem nakmikegkii kenlengilngughmeng unguvallengesqelluki ugpeqikat ungipameng .
Enkaam tamaani Antioch-mi , uvitanganilngughnillu nunani Atanghem ungipaa mingitkaq .
Iwernga Jews-et takukiit Gentile-et aghniit maniguutkayuget Kiyaghneghmun , igleghutistengillu Antioch-em naavguunnalukek Paul-enkuk Barnabas-enkuk . Tamaaken apalluqluku amyuutkegkagket taakuk yugek , aghulaqestekagketlu nunameggneng .
Enkaam apostle-ek itegatek pagulangiqiik kelgunnaluku peggniluki kipullginaalghiit Kiyaghneghem ungipaaneng . Taagken Iconium-emun aghulaqegkak .
Iwernga tamaakut ugpeqat Antioch-melnguut quyangaghllagetlu , imighngalghiitlu Agleghnalghiigneng Taghneghagneng .
Iconium-emi Paul-enkuk Barnabas-enkuk piiqelleghmegetun synagogue-mun aglaqak . Tawani whateghlluwaaq akuzikak repall Jews-elghutetlu , Gentile-elghutetlu ugpeghtuutkat .
Enkaam Iconium-emetelqinaqak , tamaani tetugpenatek ungipaqikak Ataneghmeng . Paul-enkuk Barnabas-enkuk Atanghem allaaghlluwhaghtisteghllagaataqakek yugnun ipangutanga liigikesqelluku ungipaqegkaak Atanghem nangllegtallgha . Iwernga ugpeghyugumangilnguut Jews-et Gentile-enun seghletun sumeghtaghaatkestekiit ugpeqat .
Enkaam Iconium-eghmiit malghughkegkat , ilangi ilatkat Jews-enun , ilangi apostle-enun .
Taagken ilangita Gentile-etlu , Jews-etlu maligulluteng igleghutistemeggnun amyuutkesukagket apostle-ek , milughpagaataghhiinaqlu tuqusukagket .
Nagaqughyamek yugnun tawaten pinaqnilutek , qimakak Lycaonia-m neghllagegkenun Lystra-munllu , Derbe-munllu , uvitegkenilngughnunllu nenun .
Enkaam tamaani ungipaqegkiik Pinilghiit Ungipat .
Lystra-minguq taawa yuuk itegii natelnguut allgenghhaghhaatmineng ima enkaam piyugigalnguq .
Aqumgaghmi tawani nagatkaa Paul akuzilghii . Paul-em liigikegkaa yuuk ugpelghii Kiyaghneghmun naallghulleqniluni .
Enkaam qiivluku tawavek iglagtupiglluni pikaa , " Nekevngwaaghi itegaghpegun ! " Aga yuuk nekefqaghlluni tamaani piyukaq .
Yulghutet esghapagluku Paul-em naallghutillgha araghaataatkat Lycaonia-ghmiistun , " Yuguluteng kiyaghneghet takwiinkut ! "
Barnabas Zeus-ngunikaat enkaam Paul Hermes-ngunikaat kiyang akuzistengutanganeng .
Priest-ngan Zeus-emllu , yugetlu aghqerraaghyukagket Paul-enkuk Barnabas-enkuk . Enkaam priest-a tagitkaq teghikusamengllu piitesiighaghmengllu Lystra-m mingllutangan amigllaganun . ( Temple-a kiyaghnengllaqamun Zeus-mun amigllagem tunganganilnguq ) .
Iwernga apostle-ek Barnabas-enkuk Paul-enkuk liigiksamegneki sanaqutangi aatkatek piiguqiik . Taagken aqfaasnaq yugnun qungangiitkak araamaagmek ,
" Ukughsi yugni , sangafsi tawaten pitsi ? Whangkutungllu yuguukung elpesistungwaaq ! Ungipaqiyaghtuugukung Pinilghiineng Ungipaneng elpesinun , tunullusi satngunghilngughneng maniguqaghpesineng qiivesqellusi unguvalghiimun Kiyaghneghmun . Ellngan ulimakaqii qilak , nuna , kellii , sangwaallu tamaghhaan taakunilnguq .
Sivunghani agani Kiyaghneghem qamaglluki ramket Jews-ngunghilnguut piyukellghistun pistekaqii .
Iwernga tawateteghngaata paninang liisimakestekaaguq unguvaniluni pinitun pilleghmikun tamaghhaanun . Eslallugughtestaqaa nunivagseghat nagusqelluki . Ayumiqulleq kaspuglluku piitestaqii piisaghqat piitfigit kaanneghata neqelgusqellusi , quyangasqellusillu . "
Paul-enkuk Barnabas-enkuk tawaten akuzighngaayek taawa paninang Lystra-ghmiit aghqerraaghnaqutkegkagket . Iwernga pegnem pisneghitkak .
Taagken ilangi Jews-et Antioch-mengllu Iconium-emengllu kaatkat Lystra-mun . Lystra-ghmiinun naavguullukek ugumiitestekagket . Enkaam Jews-etlu , Lystra-ghmiitlu Paul milughpagaataghluku qamuqaat nem kelutanganun sumeghmeggni tuqumaniluku .
Iwernga ugpeqat takulaghaasatni Paul nekevluni aglanqigtekaq nemun . Taagken unaamingani elkek Barnabas-enkuk Derbe-mun aglaqak .
Paul-enkuk Barnabas-enkuk ungipaqikak Pinilghiineng Ungipaneng Derbe-mi enkaam uglaq maligsaaghtengughtekaq . Taagken Lystra-mun pinqigtekak , taagken Iconium-emun , Antioch-munllu pikak Pisidia-melngughmun .
Takuughaqamegni tamaani apeghtuqiik ugpeqat ugpeqillghit wata iknaqughtesqelluki , kayemegkiiklu ugpellghit aghuliitesqelluki . Pikiik , " Uglapestaaq seghleliilleq atuqsaghqapestaaqaghput iteghyaghqaaghhnaluta Ataneghpagullghanun Kiyaghneghem . "
Takuughaqamegnillu nakmiightuqak Elder-kaghqameng igleghutesqelluki ugpeqat . Taagken yughaamaagmek fast-ekak . Taam kingunganeng Ataneghmun ugpeqegkamegnun yughaatkegkiik Elder-et aflengakesqelluki .
Taagken Pisidia-kun igleghakak Pamphylia-mun .
Tamaani Perga-mi , Pamphylia-melngughmi ungipaqikak Kiyaghneghem akuzitanganeng . Taaqsamek tesamavek Attalia-mun pikak .
Taagken Antioch-mun angyaghpagkun aghulaqegkak . ( Tamaani Antioch-mi ugpeqat Paul-enkuk Barnabas-enkuk aghulaqellghillukek yughaatkegkaqegkegket . Aaputkaqegkegket Kiyaghneghmun kayusiitesqellukek ungipaqillghegkeni . Taananguuq qepghaqaq apeghiiqaak . )
Kaasamek Antioch-mun ugpeqat qerngughtekiik . Ungipaatkiik Kiyaghneghem apeghiillghaneng ellmetegnegun , aapqaaklu Kiyaghneghmun ugpeqilleghqalitellghi Gentile-et .
Tamaani muluughllakak ugpeqani .
Taagken Judea-meng ilangi yuget tagiluteng Antioch-mun ugpeqanun apeghtughikat , " Yugulillengnaanghitusi wetkuqun circumcise-ekufsi Moses-em Liilightuusaan qelellghatun . "
Iwernga Paul-enkuk Barnabas-enkuk elngaatall aaghtiiraaqiik taakut yuget apeghtuusiitneng . Enkaam ugpeqat nakmikegkiit Paul-enkuk , Barnabas-enkuk , ilangillu yuget Antioch-meng pit , Jerusalem-etesqelluki aapsaghtiisqelluki apostle-etlu Elder-etlu qerngaghmelnguut naliq apeghtuusaq elqughutngatanga .
Kayagsisteng Paul-enkut igleghatkelluku Phoenicia-kunllu , Samaria-kunllu ugpeqat tamaanlenguut ungipaatkiit Gentile-et Kiyaghneghmun qiivuusimaniluki , enkaam qamaglluteng ugpeqat quyateghllakat .
Kaasata Jerusalem-emun apostle-etlu , Elder-etlu , ugpeqatlu upughatkiit . Taagken Paul-enkut apeghlaataqaat Kiyaghneghem apeghiillgha ellmegteggun .
Ilangi ugpeqat Pharisees-et nekevluteng pikat , " Tamaakut Gentile-et yugulillengyaghqaanghitut wetkuqun circumcise-elutengllu , qaatkullutengllu Moses-em Liilightuusaanun . "
Taagken apostle-etlu Elder-etlu qerngughutkat agghitkennalukek taakuk .
Akuzitkenneghpagllakaat . Taagken Peter-em nekevluni pikii , " Ugpeqaalgutemni , liisimakaghsi qavngaq Kiyaghneghem nakmikegkaqaanga Gentile-enun ungipaqisqellunga Pinilghiineng Ungipaneng ugpeghesqelluki .
Kiyaghneghem liisimakilghiim yugem tamaghhaan sumeghtaghallghaneng , tugukliqaqii Gentile-et . Kelgutkaqaa tuguklighilleni ellngitneng tuunelleghmikun Agleghnalghiik Taghneghak katam tawaten whangkunnun tuunelleghmitun .
Whangkutestungwaaq kiyaghutaqii ; whangkutestungwaaq ukmangighaqii ilungit ugpenghata .
Enkaam sangan始ngam Kiyaghneq sakraasnaqutkengngusteggu qelelleghpesigun Gentile-et ugpeqiit qaatkelluki Liilightuusaput kiyaghtesqelluki ? Talwa sivunemtallu whangkutallu qaatkepagningilkeput taakut Liilightuusat yugulillengnaluta .
Iwernga ugpeqaghput Kiyaghneghem yugulikaqiinkut kayusillghakun Atanghem Jesus-em tawateghpigaq Gentile-enun pilleghmitun . "
Taagken tawantullghiit qallegnanighwaaghulluteng nagatkagket Barnabas-enkuk , Paul-enkuk aapqangik ellmetegnegun Kiyaghneghem allaaghlluwhaghtillghi Gentile-enun .
Akuzineghmeng taaqsayek James-em pikii , " Ugpeqaalgutemni , nagataghtengnga !
Simon Peter-em ungipaatiinkut naten Kiyaghneghem nakmikuqestallghi Gentile-et ellminun katam yuguluki . Tawaten pilleghmikun liigikestekaqii ellngitlu piniqniluki .
Enkaam Kiyaghneghem sallgha Gentile-enun elqughutuq uuknaliqistet igaqegkiitnun . Akuzitni Igaqegkani Ataneq pikaaguq :
' David-em mangteghaa uulqaaguq iwernga uteghnighlunga nekefneqiglleqaqa . Naavumayaghngaan nallghusaghlleqaqa .
Taagken qamaglluteng ilangi yuget Gentile-eneng nakmikegkama whangamnun katam pinguluki , ellngita liisuglleqaat Ataneq .
Atanghuuq tawaten akuzikaq , ima qavngarugllak ellngan liitestekaqii tamaakut . ' "
James-em nagneghutkii , " Enkaam whanga sumemni Gentile-et qiivegkat Kiyaghneghmun qaatkutesqughaafqiita Liilightuusamnnun pilteki .
Itupill latatgun neghesnaniilteki neqmeng aghqutkegkameng kiyaghnengllaqanun , qemitkameng teghikusameng , aawmeng ; ineghteltekillu seghleghqusiqefqaan sex pisqelluku .
Tawaten piyaghqaanghitut qayughllak Moses-em Liilightuusaan iinghutkaqii tamaakut . Ima qavngarugllaggaaneng Jews-et nagataqiit Liilightuusat atightughluki ungipaqenghatki Sabbath-a tamaghhaan , nani alngunak synagogue-ni . "
Taagken apostle-et , Elder-et , qamagllutengllu ugpeqat nakmiiqat yugmeggneng maligutesaghqameng Paul-enkugnun Barnabas-enkugnun Antioch-mun pinaqelghiignun . Nakmikegkagket Silas-enkuk Judas-enkuk ateghaqelghii Barsabbas-meng . Taakuk yugek Jerusalem-eghmiit ugpeqiita siivakepigtekagket .
Elkegnekun tuyuqiit latat whaten igaqegkat : " Whangkuta apostle-enillu Elder-enillu lataaqukut Gentile-enun ugpeqaalgutemnnun Antioch-melngughnun , Syria-melngughnun , Cilicia-melngughnunllu , quyakamsi !
Nagaquumaakut yumtanguq ilangita takulusi sameng pilusi seghleghyugtekaqiisillu kukragyugtekaqiisillu . Naqamllu whangkuta tawaten pisqumangitaput .
Enkaam qerngaamta agghilluta nakmikagput Judas-enkuk Silas-enkuk maligutesqellukek piniqegkamnnun ugpeqaalgutemnnun Barnabas-enkugnun Paul-enkugnun , elpesinun pinaqelghiignun .
Taakuk Barnabas-enkuk Paul-enkuk tuqusaghngiistek pikaaguk apalluqluku Ataneghput Jesus Christ-a .
Judas-enkuk Silas-enkuk kayaggnaqagput aapghwaaghesqelluki taakut ataasit latatkegkaput elpesinun .
Agleghnalghiimllu Taghnegham , whangkutallu itagnaqamsi allulluki Jews-et Liilightuusiit atuqenghisaghngaaghpesiki pisqelluki . Iwernga ukut Liilightuusat elpesinun atuqesugaput :
Neghegpenasi neqmeng aghqutkegkameng kiyaghnengllaqanun , aawmeng , teghikusameng qemitkameng , nuqetutaqiteggullu sex-kun seghleghqelleq . Maligtekufsiki taakut Liilightuusat taawa pinitun pillequsi . Tawatenginaq lataamsi . "
Taagken taakut yuget aghulaqegkat Jerusalem-emeng Antioch-mun . Kaasameng qerngughlluki ugpeqat tuunegkiit latat .
Atightughluki latat elngaatall quyateghllakat qayughllak ilutughlleghiit .
Judas-enkuk Silas-enkuk elkeklu uuknaliqistengulghiik , enkaam ungipaqiighaataghllakak ugpeqanun ugpellghit iknaqughtesqelluki .
Tamaantelqinaghlutek aghulaqsukak . Enkaam ugpeqat aghulaqestekagket whaten pilukek , " Nekeggmellelgutek igleghalleghpetegni . " Taagken uteghniqak kayagtistemegnun Jerusalem-emelngughnun .
Iwernga Silas tamaansukaq .
Taakuk Paul-enkuk Barnabas-enkuk Antioch-metaaghaqak . Elkeklu maligullutek uglapiglleghhiinun ugpeqanun apeghtughikaklu ungipaqikaklu ungipaaneng Atanghem .
Tagtalmi Paul-em pikaa Barnabas , " Takuughaqaaltegneki ungipaqivikegkapung Atanghem ungipaaneng , esghaghyaghtuultegneki natetulangi ugpeqaalgutepung . "
Barnabas-em kelqesukaa John Mark ,
iwernga Paul-em kelqesugumangilkanga , qayughllak Pamphylia-melluteng John Mark-em unitkakek qepghaqaghteng taaqestegpenaan .
Paul-enkuk Barnabas-enkuk aaghtiiraaghutkeghllagluku pelleghmun aghulaquutkak . Barnabas-em kelqelluku Mark angyaghpagkun Cyprus-mun pikaq .
Enkaam Paul-em aghulaqfagilgami nakmikegkaa Silas kelqennaluku . Taagken ugpeqat yughaatkellukek neghyukutkagket Ataneghmun aflengakesqellukek .
Igleghtekak Syria-kunllu Cilicia-kunllu iknaqughsaamiita ugpeqat ugpellghit .
Paul Derbe-tkaq enkaam taagken nagneqaq Lystra-mun , tamaani nallaqaa ugpeqaq yuuk aatqelghii Timothy-meng . Naangallu ugpeqaalghii Jews-a , naqam atanga Greek-a .
Ugpeqat qamaglluteng Lystra-melnguutlu Iconium-emelnguutlu akuzitkaqegkangat Timothy piniipiggniluku .
Paul-em kelqesukaa Timothy kayutnguluku enkaam circumcise-estekaa . Tawaten pistekaa tugukliisqelluku Jews-enun , qayughllak tamaanlenguut Jews-et liisimakegkangat atanga Greek-ngulghii .
Taagken igleghanguluteng neghllagnun kaanneghmeggni ugpeqat qaatkutesqaqegkangit apostle-etlu , Elder-etlu liilightuusangllaqiitnun Jerusalem-emi .
Enkaam ugpeqat wata ugpeqiighataghaqat , nulamanginaqatlu aghhutanga tamaghhaan .
