Paul-enkut igleghtekat akulegkenkun Phrygia-mllu , Galatia-mllu , qayughllak Agleghnalghiim Taghnegham ungipaghtesimangilkangi ungipameng Asia-mi .
Tughwaaghluteng Mysia-mun nagneghnaqegkaayalghiit Bithynia-mun , iwernga Jesus-em Taghneghagkenka pisneghitkii .
Enkaam Mysia naghughlluku tesamavek Troas-mun pikat .
Unugmi tawani Paul-em esghaghwaalleghqun esghaqaa yuuk Macedonia-ghmii tagsighralghii . Yugem maniguutepiglluni pikaa , " Tagiluten Macedonia-mun kayusiitaghtikut ! "
Legan Paul-em esghaghwaallghan kingunganeng yataaghqukut Macedonia-mun pinaluta , qayughllak liigikegkefut Kiyaghneghem ungipaqisukanginkut Pinilghiineng Ungipaneng tamaani .
Enkaam telanangameng nangaqaghtukut Troas-meng Samothrace-mun . Unaamingani Neapolis-mun piikut .
Taagken quutkun kaatukut neghllagmun Philippi-mun Macedonia-melngughmun Rome-eghmiit nelikiitnun . Qafsinat aghneghet tamaantukut .
Tamaansimaluta Sabbath-ngughsagu mingllutem amigllagakun aanluta kiiwegnun piikut , Jews-et tawani yughaataqnayukata . Aghnam ilangi tawantuteftut enkaam aqumuulluta aleghqughaput .
Ataasiq nagallghii Lydia-nguftuq , Thyatira-ghmii , akilpegaqayuk esnegrukegtameng qiipaghaghmeng , maniguutkayuk Kiyaghneghmun . Atanghem liigikestengngwaaqii Paul-em akuzitangi Lydia-mun enkaam ugpeqegkii .
Qamaglluteng nengllugutkullghiit paaptaayeyameng Lydia-m aqelqangllaghiinkut , " Sumeghpesini ipapik ugpeghumakuma Ataneghqun , whangkunnitaghhnayanghitsii ? " Enkaam sagiqusinkut ellngitnitukut .
Ataasimi aghneghmi kiiwem esnenganilngughmun yughaatfigmun aglaamaluta , nallaghaghput qepghaghtelaaq aghnaghaq ilumikun tughneghalek . Taam tughneghaam uuknaliqutkestaqegkangi sangwaat sayaghqat sivutghulluki . Enkaam piliitestengita aklungighisiqngukangat .
Taam aghnaghaam maligsaaghiinkut Paul-llu whangkuta akilghuumaghmi , " Ukut yuget qepghaghtekii Aangelleghpigaam Kiyaghneghem ! Ungipaataqiisi naten yugulillengelleghqameng ! "
Qafsinegllak aghneq tawaten piiq . Qenwatlu Paul-em qinuyagulluku tughneghaq ilunganilnguq qiivluku pikaa , " Aatghakun Jesus Christ-am qelghamken aanesqelluten ellnganeng ! " Tawaninginaq tughneghaq ilunganeng aanegkaq .
Piliitestengita liigiksamegteggu allgeghututkesaghqaananiimatseng aghnaghaq , Paul-enkuk Silas-enkuk akuqaqagket . Qamughsiighmeng aglaatkagket igleghutistenun akilpegaghvigmelngughnun .
Taagken igleghutistet aglaallukek Rome-eghmiit nanqigtistengitnun pikiit , " Yugek ukuk Jew-nguuk , seghleliighqiinguuk maani .
Apeghtughiiquk kiyaghtaalleghmeng whangkuta Rome-eghmiini liilightuusamta iinghutkiitneng . Tamaaken apalluqluku apeghtuusiik atuqnaanghitaput . "
Enkaam yulghun ilatqaghtaalluni sughukagket Paul-enkuk Silas-enkuk . Nanqigtistet qelghutkagket aatkiik qesugumeng mataghqughluki anagulghesqellukek .
Anaguleghtaaneghmeng taaqlukek anusimingllaghvigmun kanaghtekagket . Taagken anusimingllaghvigem umiilganun maghqatutngwaaghesqegkagket .
Anusimingllaghvigem umiilgan tawaten kayagsatni iluklighpigaghmun qamavek kanaghtekakek . Taagken umughllagmeng unaghsimeng tukughusighlukek , maghqatkiit taakut tukughutet qapragyaghqaagpenakek .
Nani tamaani unugem qukaani Paul-enkuk Silas-enkuk yughaamaagmek ilagaqak usuqilleghmeng Kiyaghneghmun , anusimingllaghat tawanlenguut nagatkagket .
Nuuskagllagan nuna tuyepeghtaqaq , repall anusimingllaghvik tunemaghtuumaan aghulatkaa . Tawaninginaq amiget qelpeghaghtaatkat , anusimingllaghanengllu qiipraghutet ilefkaghaghtaatkat .
Anusimingllaghvigem umiilga taghtughyalghiimi , amiget qelpatuteftut . Sumeghmini anusimingllaghat qimaguusimaniluki savigpani nusugluku ellmineng tuqunnaqegkaq .
Iwernga Paul-em iglagtupiglluni pikaa , " Tuqunnaqegpenang elpeneng qayughllak qamaglluta whaantutukut ! "
Anusimingllaghvigem umiilga keneghmeng tungsighluni iitqaghtekaq . Alingruughem ungelegsimaghmi Paul-enkuk Silas-enkuk manugkenkun segesqughtekaq .
Taagken aanututkellukek aaptekakek , " Yugegni ukughtek , naten salunga yugulillengnayaghsinga ? "
Pikaak , " Ugpeqigu Ataneq Jesus enkaam yugulillengellequten , nengllugutetenllu yugulillengellequt . "
Taagken Paul-enkuk Silas-enkuk ungipaqegkaak Ataneq ellnganunllu nengllugutanganunllu .
Tawani unugmi anusimingllaghvigem umiilgan ughvughteqii taakuk yugek anagulellghegkenka kiingik . Taagken nengllugutkullghiit paaptaayenginaamaghmeng pikat .
Paul-enkuk Silas-enkuk ellmeggnun aglaallukek neghestekagket . Nengllugutkullghiit quyateghllakat qayughllak ugpeqegkangat Kiyaghneq .
Aghsagu Rome-eghmiit nanqigtistengita kevgaqegkiit umiilwaateng ungipaasaghtiisqelluku anusimingllaghvigem umiilga whaten , " Paul-enkuk Silas-enkuk aanestikek . "
Enkaam anusimingllaghvigem umiilgan Paul pikaa , " Nanqigtistet kayagutiistek aaneslamtegnguq enkaam aanelghaatek , aghulaqitek nekeggmellutek . "
Iwernga Paul-em umiilwaaghet pikii , " Rome-eghmiingughngaamtung yugtuqami anaguleghtaakaqiinkung , talwa ipapighqutkegpenaan sameng anaggusimatfung . Taagken anusimingllaghiinkung . Enraghngam whaa maaten aksaqluku aanesnaqinkuung ? Yeghlegillu ! Ellmeggneng nanqigtistet tagiluteng aaneslinkung . "
Paul-em tawaten piyisteng umiilwaaghet ungipaasaghtuqiit nanqigtistet . Enkaam nanqigtistet alingegkat Paul-enkuk Silas-enkuk nagaqughlukek Rome-eghmiingutkek .
Taagken takulukek qivghuklukek aanestekagket anusimingllaghvigmeng , aghulaqesqegkagketlu .
Enkaam Paul-enkuk Silas-enkuk anusimingllaghvigmeng aanyamek , Lydia-nkunun pikak . Tawani laalighfikluki ugpeqat kayemluki aghulaqegkak .
Paul-enkut igleghtekat Amphipolis-kunllu , Apollonia-kunllu Thessalonica-mun kaatelleghmeggnun kenlanga . Tamaani Jews-et synagogue-elget .
Paul piiqelleghmitun synagogue-mun pikaq . Pingayuni Sabbath-eni Paul-em liigikesnaqutkegkii yuget Christ-ameng Akuzitetgun Igaqegkatgun .
Uuknaliqelleghteggun liigikesnaqutkegkaa ipa Christ-a tuquyaghqapestaaghunilukullu unguvaghyaghqapestaaghunilukullu tuqulleghmeng . Pikii , " Una Jesus aapqegka elpesinun Christ-anguuq . "
Ilangi Jews-et ugpeghluteng ilatkat Paul-enkugnun Silas-enkugnun . Tamaakutlu Greek-elghutet maniguutkayuget Kiyaghneghmun , aghnalghutetlu pingwaaghet ugpeghtuutkat .
Taagken ugpeqaanghilnguut Jews-et aqinaklukek Paul-enkuk Silas-enkuk tesqagantaqelghiineng sangigalngughneng yugneng qerngughtiluteng seghleliighqiighllakat . Qenwat qamagtengngwaaghluki Thessalonica-ghmiit qapraghqegkiit . Taagken ketanqusnaq Jason-enkunun aglaghluteng iitqaghtaatkat Paul-enkuk Silas-enkuk aanunnalukek yulghutnun .
Iwernga naalkenghisamegtekek , Jason-llu ilangillu ugpeqat qamughsiiqiit Thessalonica-m igleghutistengitnun . Akilghuukat , " Paul-enkuk Silas-enkuk navek alngunak pineghmegni seghleliighqiigaquk , whaa maanillu tawaten piiquk .
Caesar-em liilightuusii kipullegmun piiqiik whaten pilleghmegnegun , ' Jesus umiilegpigaaguq , Caesar umiilgunghituq . ' Jason-em ellmeggnitestaqaak Paul-enkuk Silas-enkuk . "
Tawaten piyata yugetlu igleghutistengillu Thessalonica-m sakraaghllakat .
Taagken igleghutistet pikiit Jason-enkut , " Qelghutagput Paul-enkuk Silas-enkuk elpesinun aghulaqestesqellukek Thessalonica-meng , iwernga sivuklusi manilitikut . Aghulaqegkayek manizi veghulleqaghput . " Taagken aglaghtestekiit .
Mamlegtaghesnaghyagu ugpeqat Paul-enkuk Silas-enkuk aghulaqestekagket Berea-mun . Kaasamek synagogue-mun pikak .
Tamaakut Jews-ngit nagasukestaghlukek ayuqegkegket Paul-enkuk Silas-enkuk , Thessalonica-melngughneng . Aghhutanga tamaghhaan Jews-et ellmeggneng liinnaqegkiit Akuzitet Igaqegkat , liigiknaluki Paul-enkuk Silas-enkuk apeghtughillghik ipangutangi .
Enkaam uglapiglleghhiit ugpeghtuutkat , uglapiglleghhiitlu pingwaaghet Greek-et aghniitlu yugitlu ugpeghtuutkat .
Iwernga Jews-et Thessalonica-melnguut nagaqughyamegteggu Paul ungipaqiniluku akuzitanganeng Kiyaghneghem Berea-mi , Berea-tkat . Kaalluteng qapraghqiikat yugneng seghleliighqiikat tamaani .
Enkaam ugpeqat Paul esnemun atghaatqaghtestekaat iwernga Silas-enkuk Timothy-nkuk Berea-metkak .
Yuget igleghutilghiit Paul-meng maligutkat Athens-mun kenlanga . Uteghnighnaqngata Berea-mun Paul-em lipeghsaqakek Silas-enkuk Timothy-nkuk takusqelluni piyaghqaaghtaghesnaqayek .
Athens-mi Paul utaqiitkelluku Silas-enkugneng Timothy-nkugneng , yuvghiighyalghiimi tamaani seghleghyugllakaq , qayughllak kiyaghnengllaqaghtupigteftuq .
Enkaam Paul-em synagogue-mi Jews-etlu Gentile-etlu , maniguutkayuget Kiyaghneghmun liigikesnaqutkegkii Jesus , Christ-anguniluku . Akilpegaghvigmillu aghhutanga tamaghhaan kinkut alngunak tawanneghata aapghaqegkanga Christ-a .
Ilangita apeghtughistengita Epicurean-etlu , Stoic-etlu takuluku Paul aaghtiiraaqaat . Ilangita ilateng aaptekiit , " Una akuzivallughllak sameng piiqa ? " Tamaakut ilangita pikaat , " Llangaqa nakumiit kiyaghneghit akuzitkaqii . " Tawaten pikat qayughllak Paul-em ungipaqngukanga Jesus , unguvallghallu tuqulleghmeng .
Taagken Paul-mun maligtestekat agghistenun Areopagus-melngughnun . Enkaam kaasameng pikaat , " Taana nutaghaq apeghtuusaqaqegken liisuwaghput .
Sangwaa taana aapqan allaaghlluwhaaguq whangkunni , enkaam liigiksuwaghput sameng pisiitanga . "
( Sangwaat nutaghat apeghtuusat pinghata Athens-eghmiitlu , nakumiitlu tamaavek lliiqat apeghyuwaqiitlu nagasugaqiitlu . )
Enkaam Areopagus-mi Paul-em nekevluni pikii , " Athens-eghmiini , liigikamsi elngaatall maniguutkayuguftusi elpesi yugni .
Igleghsalghiinga qagani akulmi , esghaghanka manigughvilghutesi , aghqefiklu ataasiq igaqfikngalghii whaten , ' Nallukegkamun Kiyaghneghmun . ' Taananguuq Kiyaghneq nallukeghngaaghpesigu maniguqaghsi apeghyukegka elpesinun .
Taam Kiyaghneghem ulimakaqaa nuna , sangwaallu qamagtengngwaaghluku nunamelnguq . Atanqaa qilagemllu nunamllu enkaam maniguutfingllaqanisigatuq .
Taananguuq Kiyaghneq tuunikayuk unguvalleghmeng , aneghneghmeng , samengllu tamaghhaaneng yugnun . Akluksaghqaqenghitaa yuget kayusillghat qayughllak sangwaa tamaghhaan aklukigataa .
Kiyaghneghem ulimakaqaa ataasiq yuuk , enkaam taagken ataasimeng allgeqaaguq allaaghhiinaq yuuk nunamelnguq whani . Iingkerugllak yataaghqegkaqiillu qakun yuget allgeghyaghqaatangi , nanillu kiyaghsaghqaatangi .
Tawaten pikaqii yugnun iviisqelluni luuraq naalkennayukangatni . Naqamllu nalighhiinamnneng uyavanneghituq
qayughllak ' Ellngakun kiyaghtengnguukutlu , qapraguukutlu , allgeqaagukutlu . ' Talwa ilangi igangllaghtesi whaten pikaalghiit , ' Ipapestaaq avaqutaqiinkut . '
" Kiyaghneghem avaqutaqutanganeng sumeghtaghaatkesaghqaqenghitaghput yuget ulimaaghistun gold-meng , silver-meng , nalighmeng uyghagmeng ayuqluki . Yuget sumeghtaghallghistun ayuqenghituq .
Sivunghani agani yuget salin nallukluku Kiyaghneq , aghyuughyugumangitii aghyuusaqeghngaata . Iwernga maaten qelghwii qamaglluki yuget naansaghngaata avuteghqelluki , seghleghqennaniisqelluki .
Kiyaghneghem tawaten qelqaqii qayughllak nekegtekaqaa aghneq nanqigtiviguluku . Nakmikegkamikun yugkun yuuk tamaghhaan tawateghlluwaaq nanqigsaghqaqaa . Liitesnaluku nakmikegkani yuuk unguvaghtestekaqaa tuqulleghmeng . "
Nagalluku Paul-em aapqanga yuuk unguvaghtesimaniluku tuqulleghmeng , ilangita legasiighwaatkegkaat , iwernga ilangita pikaat Paul , " Wataqaaghaq nagasuwaghput alla apeghnaqegkuvgu . "
Taagken Paul-em unitkii ,
iwernga ilangita maligsaaghluku Paul ugpeghtuutkat . Ataasiq Dionysius-nguftuq , Areopagus-mi agghista , aghnaqlu aatqelghii Damaris-meng , kinkutlu ilangi ugpeghtuutkat .
Taam kingunganeng Paul Corinth-etkaq Athens-meng .
Tamaani nallaqaa Jew aatgha Aquila , Pontus-mi allgeqaq . Italy-meng kaanneghhaaftuk nulighqullghiik Priscilla-nkuk , qayughllak Umiilegpigaam Claudius-em eflequqii Jews-et Rome-emeng . Paul-em laalighfiklukek
elkegkenitkaq qayughllak qepghaqaak ellngan qepghaqaatun ayuqelghii . Tiintangllallghem akinga kiyaghusiqegkangat .
Sabbath-a tamaghhaan Paul synagogue-mun piluni ungipaghaqelghii Jews-enunllu , Greek-enunllu ugpeghesqelluki .
Silas-enkuk Timothy-nkuk kaatkak Macedonia-meng , taagken kenlekluku Paul ungipaqinginaghluni lliiqaq . Jews-enun aapqaa Jesus , Christ-anguniluku .
Jews-et kipullginaaghyatnillu seghletunllu akuzitkesatni , aatkami pagulangi ufsugulluki pikii , " Iflakufsi elpesi pilqaghsi , whanga pilqennaanghitaqa . Whaken kenlekluku Gentile-enun ungipaqinaqunga . "
Enkaam unilluki Jews-et Titius Justus-mun lliiqaq , Gentile-mun maniguutkayugmun Kiyaghneghmun . Mangteghaa synagogue-em saaghwanilnguq .
Synagogue-em igleghutistenga Crispus-nguftuq . Qamaglluteng nengllugutkullghiit ugpeqegkaat Ataneq . Corinth-eghmiilghutetlu nagalluku Paul ugpeghluteng paaptaayekat .
Taagken unugmi ataasimi Paul esghaghwaalleghqun Atanghem pikaa , " Alingegpenang , yeghlegi ungipaqikestaa iilqayufqaavek
qayughllak elpenitaqunga . Kitumun alngunak aqnightesnaanghitamken , qayughllak neghllagmi whani uglapiglleghhii yuuk whanga pikaqa . "
Enkaam Paul tamaani apeghtughikaq Kiyaghneghem akuzitanganeng ataasiq ayumiqulleq alla aghvinlek tanqit ilalluki .
Gallio , Rome-em umiilgughtestaqngagu Greece-mun , Jews-et qerngughulluteng sughugluku Paul aglaatkaat nanqigtivigmun .
Kaatulluku pikat , " Uum yugem apeghtughaqii yuget Kiyaghneq manigiisqelluku allanguluku Liilightuusamnneng ! "
Iiwenllu Paul akuzinaqaquq , Gallio-m Jews-et pikii , " Una yuuk tegleguqaayaqan , yugtaqaayaqan nalighmeng sangwaa alngunak seghlepestaaq pikaqsaqagu ilapgapestaaghnayaghamsi .
Iwernga una yuuk tawaten pimangituq . Aaghtiiraaghutkengngunghitasi Rome-em liilightuusii , aaghtiiraaghutkengngwaasi elpesi katam Liilightuusasi , akuzitetlu aatghetlu sameng pisiitangi . Tamaaken nanqigtiyaghqaanghitunga , elpesineng piteki . "
Enkaam eflequqii aanesqelluki .
Taagken yuget akuqaghluku synagogue-em igleghutistenga Sosthenes , qevutiiqaat nanqigtivigem manughaani iwernga Gallio-m avelghaqiinaqii .
Taam kingunganeng Paul paninang ugpeqanitkaq qafsinegllak aghneq Corinth-mi . Taagken angyaghpagkun aghulaqegkaq Syria-mun kelqellukek Priscilla-nkuk Aquila-nkuk . Kaasameng Cenchrea-mun Paul qiguqaq liigikesqelluku akequsani Kiyaghneghmun apeghiillgha .
Kaalluteng Ephesus-mun , tamaani Paul-em unitkakek Priscilla-nkuk Aquila-nkuk , synagogue-elluni liigikesnaqutkegkaa Jews-enun Jesus , Christ-anguniluku .
Ellmeggnitaghiisqegkaqsaqangat iwernga pipagningitkaq .
Enkaam aghulaqnaqngami pikii , " Kiyaghneghem piyukelqegkagu alla tagillequnga . " Taagken Ephesus-meng angyaghpagkun aghulaqegkaq .
Kaalluni Caesarea-mun nagneqaq Jerusalem-emun laalighfiknaluki ugpeqat , taagken Antioch-etkaq .
Tamaantaghlluni aghulaqegkaq . Igleghutkelluku Galatia-kunllu Phrygia-kunllu , qamaglluki ugpeqat kayemumiita pikii .
Paul tawaten aneghsimaluku Apollos , Ephesus-mun kaatkaq . Jew-ngulghii allgeqaq Alexandria-mi . Elngaatall akuzillegllaklu liiteghllakaqlu Akuzitneng Igaqegkaneng .
Salin Alexandria-melluku kitum apeghtuqaqegkanga Atanghem tumanganeng . Enkaam sagiqepiglluni akuzitkengngukangallu apeghtuusaqngukangallu elqughaghlluku Jesus , apeghtuusiillu . Naqam liisimakegkanga paaptaayelleq John-em apeghtuutellghiinaatun ayuqelghii .
Ephesus-mi Apollos synagogue-elluni tetugpenani ungipaqikaq . Priscilla-nkuk Aquila-nkuk nagalluku aqelqangllaqaak liigikestaghaghnaluku Kiyaghneghem tumanganeng , wataqaaghaq elqughaghlluku .
Apollos Greece-mun piyugyan , ugpeqat kayemegkaat enkaam latakat Greece-eghmiit ugpeqiitnun upughatesqelluku . Taakut Greece-eghmiit ugpeqegkaqegkangat Jesus Kiyaghneghem kayusillghakun . Apollos-em kaalluni elngaatall iknaqughsaqaqegkangi ugpellghit apeghtughilleghmikun .
Yugtuqami aaghtiiraaghllakii Jews-et , Akuzitet Igaqegkat ipapighqusiqluki Jesus , Christ-anguniluku .
Apollos Corinth-melluku , Paul quutkun igleghakaq Ephesus-mun kenlanga . Tamaani ilangi maligsaaghtet nallaghluki
aaptekii , " Agleghnalghiik Taghneghak allgeghsimastekek ugpeghaqngafsi ? " Pikaat , " Nakaa , nallukngwaaghagput Agleghnalghiik Taghneghak . "
Aaplaataqii , " Samunmi paaptaayematsi ? " Kiimsiqaat , " John-em paaptaayellghatun . "
Paul-em pikii , " John-em paaptaayeghillgha avuteghqelluteng seghleghqennanilghinun ayuquq . Pikaqiillu ugpeqesqelluku kingumineng tagiyaghqaq , taana Jesus-nguuq . "
Nagaqughyamegteggu taana , paaptaayekat aatghakun Atanghem Jesus-em .
Paul-em saafsaqminiki Agleghnalghiik Taghneghak iitqak ellngitnun . Taagken akuzikat allaaghhiinaastun ulustun , uuknaliqumaghmengllu pikat .
Entaqun qula maalghuk siipneqluku yuuk tawantuq .
Pingayuni tanqini Sabbath-a tamaghhaan Paul-em tetukaghpenani aleghquqii yuget synagogue-mi . Aaghhnaqutkegkii , liigikesnaqutkegkii Ataneghpagullghaneng Kiyaghneghem .
Iwernga ilangi pineghllulghiit ugpeghyunghitkat , enkaam sivungitni yuget seghletun akuzitkegkaat kiyaghtaalleq Atanghem apeghtuusaa . Enkaam Paul-em unitkii kelqelluki ugpeqat . Taagken aghhutanga tamaghhaan Tyrannus-em apeghtughivigani , Paul-em aleghqughaqegkangi yuget .
Tawaten pikaq maalghuk ayumiqullghek , enkaam tamaghhaghmeng Jews-etlu Greek-etlu Asia-melnguut nagaquqiit akuzitangi Atanghem .
Kiyaghneq allaaghlluwhaghtiighaataqaq saghiighanalghiimeng Paul-kun .
Talwa ilangita yuget Paul-em kakegllugiitiillu , aatkiillu llineghmegteki qinuyugnun naallghutaqelghiit , tughneghaatlu ilungitnilnguut aanaqelghiit .
Ilangi Jews-et igleghangulghiit nunanun , yugneng aanesquungukangit tughneghaat . Taagken Atanghem Jesus-em aatgha aanesquusiqnaqutkegkaqsaqangat . Pikat , " Qelghamken aanesqelluten taaggun ataasikun Jesus-kun Paul-em ungipaqegkaakun . "
Sceva-m maaghraghvilek ighneghi tawaten pikat . ( Taana Sceva Jew-ngulghii high priest-a . )
Iwernga tughneghaam pikii , " Liisimakaqa Jesus , liisimakaqa Paul , elpesi kinkungutsi ? "
Taagken yugem ilumikun tughneghalgem qetgeghvikluki taakut yuget qevutiiqii , iknaqepigtutmineng qamaglluki avangilkegkii . Enkaam mangteghaaneng aanqaghtalluteng qimaguutkat amsikaghmeng , kiitiqullelighluteng .
Qamaglluteng Ephesus-eghmiit , Jews-etlu Greek-etlu alingruughutkat taana nagaqughluku , enkaam aatgha Jesus-em wataqaaghaq quulvaqaat .
Uglapiglleghhiit ugpenghhaqaniit yugtuqami apeghraqiit alignaghtaalleteng .
Uglapiglleghhiit alignaghtaaqayuguyalghiit tagiquulluki alignaghtaaghusit igateng paneghquqiit yulghutet esghaamanghitni . Igalghutet akitulesughyaqmegteki 50,000 silver drachmas-et akikeftiit .
Tamaana apalluqluku wataqaaghaq akuzitangi Atanghem mingitkat , enkaam uglapiglleghhiit ugpeqegkiit .
Kingungitneng tamaakut Paul qakiqniqegkaq Jerusalem-emun pinaluni , Macedonia-kunllu Greece-kunllu aagluni . Pikaq , " Jerusalem-etaghllunga taagken Rome-esaghqapestaaghuunga . "
Taagken Paul-em kayutegni Timothy-nkuk Erastus-enkuk kayagtekakek aglaqestiisqellukek Macedonia-mun , ellnga Asia-metaghaqaq .
Nani tamaani pilleghmi uglaapiglleghhiit Ephesus-eghmiit elngaatall seghleliighutkegkaat kiyaghtaalleq Atanghem apeghtuusaqegkaa .
Tamaana seghleliilleq Demetrius-em silver-meng ulimastem piinliqaa . Tawaten pikaq qayughllak ulimalgutkullghiit elngaatall maningllaasiqngukangit silver-meng ulimaaghet temple-engwaaghhaat . Tamaakut temple-engwaaghhaat kiyaghnengllaqamun Artemis-mun maniguutfigestun ayuqelghiit .
Demetrius-em ulimalgutnillu ilangillu tawatelngughmeng ulimakayuget qerngughlluki pikii , " Ukughsi yugni , liisimakaghsi elngaatall maningllaghaqukut qepghaqamnneng .
Iwernga esghapagaghsillu nagataghsillu Paul-em pillgha . Piiquq kiyaghnengllaqat kiyaghnepigunghinniluki . Enkaam uglapiglleghhii yuuk allangughqughaa maani Ephesus-mi , maaninginaagpenaan tamaghhaanillu Asia-mi piiquq .
Seghleghhalek sanghilkumta qepghaqaghput ukavaghllequq . Liisimakaghsi qamaglluteng Asia-ghmiitlu nunataghhaanilnguutlu manigughaqaat aghnaq kiyaghneq Artemis . Sanghilkumta yuget sumeghtaghaatkesagulleqaat temple-a megnuniinniluku , Artemis-emllu aangelleghllaga satngunanighllequq . "
Taakut yuget nagalluku Demetrius elngaatall sakraakat , akilghuughllakatlu , " Aangeghllagtuq Artemis-nga Ephesus-em ! "
Mulugpenateng qamaglluteng Ephesus-eghmiit ketanqwaaghaatkat akilghuumaghmeng nallukeghngaaghmegteki saaqutangi . Paul-em igleghalgutkek Gaius-enkuk Aristarchus-enkuk Macedonia-ghmiik tamaanlenguuk uvitangitni . Ilangita yuget taakuk akuqaghlukek qamuqlukek ketarwakat qerngughutfigllagmun maliglluki yulghuteghllaget .
Paul iteghyukaayalghii yulghun aleghqughnaluku iwernga ugpeqat ighlekegkaat .
Talwa ilangita Asia-m igleghutistengita kevgaqutkaat ilakumtaaghteng Paul wataghllak itefqaan qerngughutfigllagmun pisqelluku .
Taakut qerngughutfigllagmelnguut wanlegi nepugllagughtekat . Ilangi yuget sameng akilghuughllaget , ilangi sameng allaneng akilghuughllaget . Kiyang allulluteng nallukegkangat sangameng qerngughusimatseng .
Taagken yuuk aatqelghii Alexander-meng , Jews-et apeghtughwaaghluku sameng pilleghqameng , akuziyaghtiisqegkaat sivungitnun yulghuteghllaget . Alexander-em iiggeni nengugutkii nagatesqelluni yugnun .
Iwernga yulghuteghllaget liigiksamegteggu Alexander Jew-ngutanga , qerngaghllagmeng akilghuughllakat , " Aangeghllagtuq Artemis-nga Ephesus-em ! " Tawaten akilghuukat ketwhell maalghuk afluk .
Ataasim Ephesus-em umiilwaaghan nepiightesteqaghsamiki yulghutet pikii , " Ephesus-eghmiini , tamaghhaghllagmi liisimakaa Ephesus aflengakistekaa aangelghiim Artemis-em temple-ngan , agleghnalghiimllu uyghagem ifkaqam qilagmeng .
Kitum alngunak aygughiknaanghitiinkut taakugneng aflengakestengutfut enkaam nepiightek . Sangwaa temngighllak apeghiighvagilgafsigu sumeghtaghaghtek .
Taakuk yugek whavek tagitkaqagsi talwa sameng teglenghiteghngaayek temple-eneng , akuzitkenghiteghngaagnegullu sameng seghleghmeng kiyaghneghput Artemis .
Una nanqigtivigunghituq . Demetrius-enkut qepghaghtekullghiit sameng apallulgukumeng nanqigtivigmun aglaghlit . Tawani nanqigtistenun apeghnakangit apalluteng enkaam elngaatall avutkiiraaghhaat .
Wata sameng piyaghqalgukufsi sameng tamaaken qerngughutfigpigaghmi agghitkennakesi .
Tawaten piimsi qayughllak Rome-em umiilgita nagaququmegteggu una seghleliilleq aghneghmi whani , taana apalluqluku qaatkunneghinniluta liilightuusameggnun pinaqiinkut . Sameng始ngam pilleqesteki qayughllak apalliitukut seghleliighqiillemnnun . "
Taam umiilwaaghem tawaten piluki aglaghtuutestekii .
Taana seghleliilleghllak alpagyan Paul-em aqfastekii ugpeqat . Kayemluki aghulaqegkaq Macedonia-mun .
Enkaam Macedonia-kun igleghutkelluku laalighqwaaghvikegkii ugpeqat , kayemumiita pikii . Taagken nagneqaq Greece-mun ,
tamaantekaq pingayut tanqit . Yataaghqaquqlu angyaghpagkun Syria-nnaluni , liigikegkii Jews-en始nguq yataaghqaqeftut tuqunnaluku . Tamaaken apalluqluku uteghsukaq Macedonia-kun Jerusalem-emun .
Maligtestekeftii Sopater , ighnegha Pyrrhus-em , Berea-ghmii , Aristarchus-enkuk Secundus-enkuk Thessalonica-ghmiik , Gaius Derbe-ghmii , Tychicus-enkuk Trophimus-enkuk Asia-ghmiik , Timothy-llu .
Taakut aghulaqekestaghluteng Troas-mun , tamaani utaqiigut whangkunneng .
Kingunganeng Neqenghaghqellghan Yeast-aliimangilnguum Neqekrangllam , Philippi-meng angyaghpagkun aghulaqukut . Tallimat aghneghet atughluki kaataput ilaput Troas-mi . Tamaantukut maaghraghvinlek aghneq .
Sivulighmi aghneghani santillghem Troas-eghmiit ugpeqiitlu whangkutallu qerngughutukut neghnaluta Atanghem Neqenghaghqellghaneng . Sivukluni Paul ungipaqikaq unugem qukaanun kenlanga , qayughllak unaami aghulaqsugulghii .
Qemtamelnguukut kenelghutaghtuqami .
Nukalpigaq Eutychus , aqumluni qergesem esnengakun nagatkaq . Paul ungipaqimaluku qenwat Eutychus qavaghnikaq . Qenwatlu umuqilluni qavaghyalghiimi eslatmun ifkaqaq pamaken pingayaaneng qemtam . Aanluteng tuguyaqmegteggu tuquluni .
Iwernga Paul-em ukiragkiighluni segesqughfikluku qetkaa . Pikii , " Alingegpenasi , whaa unguvaamaaq ! "
Taagken mayughtuulluteng Paul-em neqekrangllaq aavgughluku neghegkat . Aleghquutkat unulqusiq kenlanga aghtelleghmun , taagken Paul aghulaqegkaq .
Ugpeqat nukalpigaq aglaatkaat nenganun ilutullengeghllagluteng unguvallgha apalluqlluku .
Angyaghpagkun aghulaqukut Assos-mun sivungani Paul-em , qayughllak quutkun Assos-mun piluni wetku tamaani uuggnaqnilghii angyaghpagmun .
Kaasan Assos-mun qaakluku angyaghpagmun Mitylene-etukut .
Unaamingani Mitylene-meng aghulaqluta aghuliightukut Chios-em tungangakun . Taagken unaamingani kaatukut Samos-mun , enkaam awakaghaani kaatukut Miletus-mun .
Paul-em naghughsukaa Ephesus qayughllak Asia-mi kimaawiyunghilnguq . Pilleghqalgukumi Jerusalem-emun kaasupigtengngulghii angiinnaluni Pentecost-mun .
Miletus-melluni Paul-em tagsiqliqii ugpeqat Elder-ngit Ephesus-melnguut .
Kaasata pikii , " Liisimakaghsi naten kiyaghtaalqa elpesinillunga Asia-mun kaasuwhaallemneng ima .
Qepghaatkaqaqa Ataneq qusevegtepigllunga , qunituumaghmallu qaywa Jews-et seghleliighqeghllagngaatngallu , tuqunnaqutkeghngaatngallu .
Iwernga liisimakaghsi nuqetusigatanka sangwaat kayutkaghqasi ungipaqinemni , apeghtunemsi yugtuqamillu negpesinillu .
Qevuulluki qelghaqsaghanka Jews-etlu Greek-etlu avuteghqelluki seghleghqennaniqata qiivesqelluki Kiyaghneghmun , ugpeqisqellukillu Atanemnneng Jesus Christ-ameng .
Whaa maaten qaatkullunga Agleghnalghiignun Taghneghagnun Jerusalem-ennaqunga , nallukaqa sayaghqaqaatnga Jerusalem-eghmiit .
Iwerngaqun tamaghhiitni nunani takukamni Agleghnalghiim Taghnegham ungipaataqaanga Jerusalem-emi seghleliighlleqnilungallu anusimingllaghlleqnilungallu yugnun .
Iwernga whanga katam unguvalqa waakigataqa apeghiiqaghhnaluku qepghaqaq Atanghem Jesus-em qelghutkaa whangamnun . Aapghesqegkaqii Pinilghiit Ungipat Kiyaghneghem piniqellghaneng ayuqelghiit .
" Liisimakaqa allameng esghaghnaanghitaghpesinga , elpesi ungipiqutkamni Ataneghpagullghaneng Kiyaghneghem .
Tamaaken apalluqluku aghneghmi whani ungipaannaqamsi malghuklillngunaan , nalighsi iflakan whanga pilqenghitaqa ,
qayughllak nuqetusimangitaqa sangwaa tamaghhaan Kiyaghneghem liitesukaa elpesinun .
Kiyaghneghem yugi penniighestun ayuqut , enkaam Agleghnalghiim Taghnegham elpesinun aflengakesqii katam tawaten penniighniightem aflengakellghatun penniini . Enkaam kelengangwaaghlusi , Kiyaghneghemllu yugi kelengakngwaaghluki . Aflengakiteki qayughllak Kiyaghneghem tukfiqaqii ellmi katam aawmikun .
Liisimakaqa uniskumsi apeghtughistesighwaaghet takulleqiisi . Katam tawatetut ugighsalghiistun amaastun naafqiinaqelghiit penniighmeng , naafqennaqutkelleqiit ugpeqat apeghtughilleghmegteggun .
Talwa ilangi ugpeqaalgutesi iqlengiqsaghqaagut ugpeqesqelluki apeghtughilleteng , ugpeghteqeghtekumegteki maligsaaghteknaluki .
Enkaam kelengangwaaghlusi puughtellengnayukafsi . Neqamikluku pingayut ayumiqullghet kelengasaaqaqamsi qamagllusi tamaaken aghneghtuumaan , unugtuumaan seghleliighllaghngaaghma , qunituumaghma .
" Naangniitkennaqaqa , neghyukutamsi Kiyaghneghmun aflengakesqellusi , ungipamunllu piniqellghanun quyastesqellusi . Nagatelleghpesigun taana ungipaq ugpellesi iknaqughllequtlu allgeghlleqaghsillu elpesi piliisaghqaghsi Kiyaghneghmeng . Taana piliisaghqaq tamaakunun pinguuq aaftekaminun ellminun katam yuguluki .
Elpesinitaqngama manigpesinengllu aatkaghpesinengllu qiliighumangitunga .
Liisimakaghpesinga sangwaa aklukegkaqa , ilamallu whangamnilnguut aklukegkiit qepghaatkayuwaanka allgeghhnaluki .
Sangwaa qamaglluku pikaqaqa elpesinun usputaasqelluku , whangamtun ughleghiilleghpesigun kayusiitesqelluki pipagningilnguut . Neqamikluku Atanghem Jesus-em whaten pillgha , ' Quyanaghataghaghtuq tuuniilleq allgeghutelleghmeng . ' "
Paul tawaten akuzineghmeng taaqsami , segesqughlluni yughalgusiqii .
Qamaglluteng qiyamaghmeng Paul qetaqluku naaghaataqaat .
Qivghukelleghpigaqegkangat qayughllak pikaqegkangi allamengllu esghaghnaanghinniluteng . Taagken qanikaat angyaghpagmun .
Unisamteki ugpeqat angyaghpagmun uuglluta nangaqaghtukut Cos-mun . Unaamingani Rhodes-mun kaalluta taagken nagneghtukut Patara-mun .
Tawani angyaghpagmeng naalkutukut Phoenicia-nnaqelghiimeng enkaam uuglluta aghulaqukut .
Esghaghyamteggu qiighqaq Cyprus uughqangakun nagneghtukut Syria-m esnengakun Tyre-mun . Tawani usingighaat angyaghpak .
Tamaani ivaghluki ugpeqat naalkesamteki ellngitnitukut ataasiq santilleq . Agleghnalghiignekun Taghneghagnekun ugpeqat Paul Jerusalem-etesnaniqaat .
Aghulaqsaghqaaghtengngamta ugpeqaalgutemta nulighqullghiit , avaqutaqullghiit maligtiinkut esnamun . Tawani segesqughquulluta yughaatukut .
Taagken uugtukut angyaghpagmun , qaniighisteput nemeggnun aglaghtuutut .
Aghulaqluta Tyre-meng kaatukut Ptolemais-mun . Tamaani quyakluki ugpeqaalguteput ataasiq aghneq ellngitnitukut .
Unamingani Caesarea-mun kaalluta Philip-enkunitukut evangelist-emi . Maaghraghvinleqegkangat nakmikegkat kayutnguluki .
Estamaneng panilek ugiighumangilngughmeng , qamaglluteng uuknaliqistet .
Salin tamaansimaluta uuknaliqista Agabus , Judea-meng kaatuq .
Whangkunnun tagiluni Paul-em tafsinga iikluku asighqelluki iteganillu iiggenillu piinkut , " Agleghnalghiik Taghneghak piik , ' Jerusalem-emi tafsim uum yumanga Jews-et asighqesaghqaqaat , taagken tuunelleqaat Gentile-enun . ' "
Whangkutallu ilangitallu yuget nagalluku Agabus tawaten pilghii ighlegaatkesaghaghput Paul Jerusalem-etefqaan pisqelluku .
Iwernga Paul-em piinkut , " Sangafsi qiyamaghpesi tawaten pistengnga ? Seghleliighqaghpesinga ! Whaa apeghiighwaaghlunga ayuqunga asighqesaghqaalunga Jerusalem-emi , talwa tuquyaghqaalunga apalluqluku Ataneq Jesus . "
Paul sagiqsan iilqayagutaghput enkaangam piighput , " Yeqay Atanghem piyukellgha apeghiighli . "
Enkaam qafsina aghneq atughluku yataaghqelluta aghulaqukut Jerusalem-emun .
Ilangita ugpeqat Caesarea-ghmiit maligtiinkut , kaasamta Jerusalem-emun aglaatiinkut tukughqamnnun Mnason-enkunun , Cyprus-eghmiimun . Ugpeqaqsuwhaaghteggun maligulluni ugpeqegkaa Jesus .
Jerusalem-emi ugpeqaalgutemta quyakluta upughatiinkut .
Unaamingani Paul maliglluku esghaghyaghtughyaqefut James , Elder-etlu qamaglluteng tawanteftut .
Paul-em quyakegkii . Taagken ungipaatkii tamaghhaaneng Kiyaghneghem apeghiillghaneng qepghalleghmikun Gentile-enilluni .
Nagalluku usuqegkaat Kiyaghneq . Taagken pikaat Paul , " Ugpeqaalgutemni , liisimakan uglapestaaghllaget Jews-et ugpeqaat Christ-a . Elngaatall qaatkusimanginaghyugaqutlu Moses-em Liilightuusaanun .
Ungipaataqiinnguq apeghtughaqatennguq qamaglluki Jews-et , Gentile-et nunangitnilnguut qaatkutefqiita Moses-em Liilightuusaanun pisqelluki . Piiqatenllunguq ighneghit circumcise-enghisaghngaata , talwanguq atuqesnanighaqan Jews-et kiyaghtaallghat .
Kaasimaniluten nagaqupestaaghnaqngwaaten . Sanaqestangam ?
Itagnapiggnayaghtuq pisqellemtestun piyaquvek . Estamat yumta apeghiighyaghtungestaamiit akeqilleghteng Kiyaghneghmun .
Elpeklu maliglluki Temple-mun ukmangighyaghtaa Moses-em Liilightuusaan qelellghatun . Tukfighnaketenllu teghikusat aghqutkaghqasi enkaam aghqerraghhaasi Kiyaghneghmun . Taam kingunganeng yuget taakut taawa meqestengngwaaghluteng qigughyaghqaaghllequt Liilightuusat pisqellghistun . Elpeklu ukmangiquvek qamaglluteng Jews-et liigikelleqaat qaatkutngallghen Moses-em Liilightuusaanun . Liigikelleqaatlu nagaquqaghteng tamaana temngingutanga .
Taakut Gentile-et ugpeqiit ungipaatkaqaput latatgun qaatkesqelluki ukut , ' Neghegpenasi neqmeng aghqutkegkameng kiyaghnengllaqanun . Neghegpenasi aawmeng . Neghegpenasi qemitkameng teghikusameng . Nuqetaqiteklu sex-kun seghleghqelleghmeng . ' "
Enkaam unaamingani Paul ukmangighyaghtuqaq Liilightuusat pisqellghistun maliglluki estamat yuget ukmangighyaghtulghiit . Taagken Paul Temple-mun iteghluni priest-et pikii , " Santilleq atughluku estamat yuget ukmangighsalleghteng apeghiighnaqaat Liilightuusat pisqellghistun . Tukfighlleqanka teghikusat aghqutkaghqiit enkaam aghqerraaghutaataqaghnakesi taakut yuget . "
Iiwenllu santilleq naangnaqaquq taakut yuget ukmangighsallghat , Asia-meng pit Jews-et esghaqaat Paul Temple-melluku . Aga akuqaghluku akilghuukat ,
" Israel-eghmiini , tagiightekqun ! Una yuuk navek alngunak pineghmini seghlequughaqiinkut Jews-eni whangkuta , Liilightuusaputlu . Wataqaaghaq seghleghataghaaguq tagitaqngamiki Gentile-et Temple-mun Liilightuusat iinghutkiit . Sakusiiqaqaallu una agleghnalghii Temple-a . "
( Tawaten pikiit sumeghmeggni Paul-mun Gentile-a itghusimaniluku Temple-mun , qayughllak Jerusalem-emi esghaqaqegkegket Trophimus-enkuk qerngaghmellukek . Trophimus Gentile-ngulghii Ephesus-eghmii . )
Jerusalem-eghmiit ugumiyugllakat , ketanqusnaq aglaghtuutkat Temple-mun akilghuusimaghmeng , seghleliighqiighllakat . Temple-mi Paul akuqaghluku qamuqaat eslatmun . Tawaninginaq kitum amigllaget uumkii .
Tuqunnaqutkumaluku Paul Rome-eghmiit pilluwaghtengita umiilgat ungipangegkaq qaga iingunaghmi seghleliighqiighllaguniluku .
Tawaninginaq Rome-eghmiit pilluwaghtengita umiilgat kelqegkaq umiilwaaghnengllu pilluwaghtenengllu enkaam aqfaasnaq aglaqat . Yulghuteghllaget esghaghluki pilluwaghtet qevuutiighnaniqaat Paul .
Taagken pilluwaghtet umiilgita tuguluku Paul asighqestekaa malghugneghneng qiipraghutneng . Pilluwaghtet umiilgita aaptekii , " Kinangaawa una yuuk ? Samaa ? "
Ataasikun akilghuumeng kiimsiisaqmegteggu repall umiilgem liigikenghitkii sameng pitangi . Enkaam pilluwaghtet umiilgita yugminun aglaatesqegkaa Paul pilluwaghtet mangteghiitnun .
Tutemqiiraaghnun kaatulluku pilluwaghtet kefkaat Paul , qayughllak yulghuteghllaget suugllugughteghllalghiit .
Yulghuteghllaget maliglleghaatkaat akilghuusimaghmeng , " Tuquteggu ! "
Pilluwaghtet itghunnaqngatni Paul-em aaptekaa pilluwaghtet umiilgat Greek-estun , " Aleghquqaghnayanghisikaan ? " Kiimsiiqaa , " Awii Greek-estun akuzikayuguziin ?
Taanangunghisiin Egypt-eghmii qavnganghhaq qerngughtikaq yugmeng awiinnaluku Rome-em kavemenga , kilgaanun aghulaqutkii 4,000 yuget atelget , Yugtaghtet ? "
Paul-em kiimsiiqaa , " Jew-nguunga , Cilicia-ghmii , allgeqaagunga neghllagmi Tarsus-mi . Aleghquqaghnayanghisingii yuget ? "
Pilluwaghtet umiilgita angeghqumaksatni , Paul nekevluni tutemqiiraaghteggun iiggeni nengugutkii nepighesqelluki . Enkaam qallegnanighyata aleghquqii Hebrew-stun .
Paul-em pikii , " Anglegutemnillu siivanlleghnillu nagataghtengnga , liigikesnaqutkaghhnaqamsi saaqutemneng . "
Jews-et nagasamegteggu akuzilghii ellmegestun elngaatall qallegnanighwaaghutkat .
Taagken pikii , " Jew-nguunga allgeqaq Tarsus-mi Cilicia-melngughmi iwernga maani Jerusalem-emi anglikaagunga . Gamaliel apeghtughistekluku liitngwaaqaqanka Liilightuusat sivunemta apeghtuusaqegkiit , enkaam tuunegkaagunga Kiyaghneghmun qaatkengngwaaghnaluku katam tawaten elpesistun .
Elngaatall amyuqetaatkegkaqanka tamaakut qaatkutngalghiit Jesus-em apeghtuusaanun repall tuqunnaqutkegkaqanka . Yugetlu aghnatlu tugustaqluki anusimingllaghtesquqaqanka .
High priest-emllu agghistetlu ipanguninaaghaat apelqa elpesinun . Whangamkun latat tuyughiit Jews-elgutemnnun Damascus-melngughnun , latatkumakangatnga ivaghiyaghtuunilunga ugpeqaneng . Naalkegkumki asighqelluki taginnaqnguyaghanka Jerusalem-emun aghyuughnaluki .
" Taagken Jerusalem-emeng Damascus-mun kaasaghtughaqungallu aghneghem qukaani qilagmeng nighugllak kuukgutqaghtuq whangamnun .
Uullghaghllunga nunamun nagaqughaqa ma pilghii , ' Saul , Saul , sangama amyuutkaqsinga ? '
Aaptaqa , ' Kinanguzin , Ataneq ? ' Kiimsighaanga , ' Jesus-nguunga Nazareth-eghmii amyuqetaatkegken . '
Tamaakut igleghalgutma esghaqaqaat nighuk iwernga aleghqughtema menga nagaquumangitaat .
Enkaam aaptaqa , ' Ataneq , salanga ? ' Atanghem piinga , ' Nekevluten aglaa Damascus-mun . Tawani kitum ungipaalleqaaten Kiyaghneghem yataaghqegkaaneng elpenun . '
Ayaamalghiinga nighugllagem angtalanganeng enkaam igleghalgutma taslughaatnga Damascus-mun .
" Kaasamta yugem Ananias-nguuniiqegkangita esghaghyaghtughaanga . Elngaatall qaatkutngalghii Liilightuusamnnun , Damascus-eghmiit Jews-et pinistaghhiinatun akuzitkaqegkangat .
Takulunga piinga , ' Anglegutemni Saul , esghasagunneqigten ! ' Enkaam tawaninginaq esghaasagullunga esghaghaqa .
Piinga , ' Kiyaghneghem , sivunemta maniguqiita , nakmikaaten elpenun liigikesqelluku piyukelleni , esghiisqelluku Seghleghqumangilnguq Qepghaghteni , nagatesqelluku aleghquqangaten .
Enkaam ungipaghtekelleqaaten tamanganun esghaatelleghpenengllu nagatelleghpenengllu .
Sameng utaqiigaqsin ? Saaqsin paaptaayesten , seghleghqelleghten ughvughtestiki tuqlughilleghpegun Aatghakun Atanghem . '
" Taagken Jerusalem-emun taginqigllunga , Temple-mi yughaamalunga esghaghwaalleghqun
esghaghaqa Ataneq . Piinga , ' Aghulaqragkiighi Jerusalem-emeng qayughllak maani tuguklighnaanghitaat ungipan whangamneng ayuqelghii . '
Kiimsighaqa , ' Ataneq , Jerusalem-eghmiit liisimakngwaaghaat synagogue-nnun piiqlunga tugulaqaqanka ugpelghiit elpeneng , anaguleghtestaqankallu anusimingllaghtestaqankallu .
Ungipaghten Stephen tuqutaqngatgu legan itagnaqegkaqaqa , taakut tuqutistengita qaasliit aatkiit aflengakegkaqanka . '
Atanghem piinga , ' Aghulaqi , kayaggnaqngwaamken agavek uyavanun Gentile-enun . ' "
Tamaakut yulghutet nagatkaat Paul kenlanga Gentile-enun pinaqnillghanun . Taagken akilghuughllakat , " Tuquteggu ! Unguvanguyaghqaanghituq ! "
Sakrituteghllagem angtalanganeng akilghuutkelluku qaasliit aatkateng nengugulluki aghulatkiit , sunamengllu quulmun milughmikat .
Pilluwaghtet umiilgita esghapagluki pilluwaghteminun itghutesqegkaa Paul pilluwaghtet mangteghiitnun . Kayagutkaallu kagsagmigesqelluku aapghesqelluku sangan yulghuteghllagnun akilghuutkutanga .
Iwernga asighqesatni Paul-em aaptekaa umiilwaaq , " Rome-em liilightuusiitni itagnaghyaghqaawaa kagsagmikufsigu Rome-eghmii , talwa nanqigtegpenaan sameng anaggusimatanga ? "
Paul-em tawaten piyatni umiilwaaghem umiilegteng takuluku pikaa , " Sanaqsin ? Una yuuk Rome-eghmiinguuq ! "
Taagken umiilgem takuluku Paul aaptekaa , " Ipa Rome-eghmiinguziin ? " Kiimsiqaa , " Aa-a . "
Pilluwaghtet umiilgita pikaa , " Whanga llivikuteghllaglunga Rome-eghmiingughtekaagunga . " Paul-em pikaa , " Whanga Rome-eghmiingulunga allgeqaagunga . "
Taakut aapqughaaghtekaghqaqsaqangi tawaninginaq iqillaghaatkat ellnganeng . Pilluwaghtet umiilgita liigiksamigu Paul Rome-eghmiingutanga alingegkaq qayughllak asighqestekaqegkanga .
Pilluwaghtet umiilgita liigikesukaa Jews-enun sameng apalluqutanga Paul . Enkaam unaamingani qiipraghutngightestekaa . Taagken chief priest-etlu agghistetlu qerngughutesluki aglaatkaa Paul ellngitnun .
Paul-em qiivluki agghistet pikii , " Jew-lgutemni , aghneghmun whavek kenlanga seghleghyugutangitunga kiyaghtellemni Kiyaghneghmun . "
Aga High Priest-em Ananias-em nekevghalghiinun Paul-em tungangani qelghutkaa Paul qasaghtesqelluku qaanghakun .
Taagken Paul-em pikaa , " Ipapestaaq Kiyaghneghem aghyuughlleqaaten , uyuq piniiyugneq ! Liilightuusatgun nanqigsaghqaqaghpenga iwernga elpek naafqaten Liilightuusat qasaghtestelleghpegun . "
Paul-em saaghwanilnguut nekevghalghiit pikaat , " Seghletun aleghqughan Kiyaghneghem high priest-nga . "
Paul-em pikii , " Jew-lgutemni , liisimaksaqumkun high priest-ngutanga tawaten pinayanghitaqa , qayughllak liisimaksaghaqa Akuzitngi Igaqegkani whaten pilleq , ' Igleghutilghiit yugpesineng seghletun akuzitkesaghqaqenghitasi . ' "
Paul-em liigikluki ilangi Sadducees-ngutangi , ilangi Pharisees-ngutangi iglagtuluni pikii , " Jew-lgutemni , Pharisee-nguunga , sivunghenkallu Pharisees-nguut . Whaa nanqiggnaqaghpesinga qayughllak ugpeqegkenka tuqukat unguvaghsaghqaatangi . "
Paul tawaten piyan Pharisees-etlu Sadducees-etlu aaghtiiraaghutkat aga malghughqengnginaamaghmeng pikat .
( Tawaten pikat qayughllak Pharisees-et ugpeqngukangit tuqukat unguvaghyaghqaaniluki , yaqulegtuniluku , taghneghaghtunilukullu , naqam Sadducees-et ugpeqigalkangit tamaakut ) .
Qenwat aaghtiiraaghullghiit iglagtughtekat . Ilangita Pharisees-et apeghtughikayuget Liilightuusaneng mesiighaatkaat Paul whaten , " Sameng seghleghmeng naalkefikneghmeng aghtughaghput , ipa entaqun taghnegham nalighmeng yaqulgem aleghquumaa . "
Wanlegi aaghtiiraaghuteghllagyata repall Paul wayaalluku lliighyatgu , pilluwaghtet umiilgita yakughyagulluku aqnighhnayukatgu pilluwaghteminun aqfasluku awitutesqegkaa agghisteneng . Enkaam aglaatesqegkaa pilluwaghtet mangteghiitnun .
Tawani unugmi Atanghem aliighvikluku Paul pikaa , " Ilutuluten , katam tawaten Jerusalem-emi ungipaqelleghpetun , Rome-emillu ungipaqelleqaghpenga . "
Unaamingani 40-neng uglalghiit Jews-et agghilluteng tuqunnaqegkaat Paul . Ellmeggneng akequtkat neghnaanghinnilutengllu , meghnaanghinnilutengllu kenlanga tuqutelleghmeggnun .
Enkaam chief priest-enunllu siivanlleghnunllu aglaghluteng pikiit , " Ipapestaaq akeqiikut neghnaanghinniluta kenlanga tuqutellemnnun Paul .
Elpesillu agghistetlu aapteggu pilluwaghtet umiilgat taginneqigtesqelluku Paul aapqughaaghwaaghnaqniluku . Enkaam tumemi taakwani whangkuta tuqulleqaghput . "
Iwernga Paul-em uyghungan nagaqughluki agghillghit ungipaasaghtuqaa Paul pilluwaghtet mangteghiitnun .
Ungipaasatni Paul-em tuqlughluku umiilwaaq pikaa , " Uum nukalpigaam ungipaasuwaqaa pilluwaghtet umiilgat sameng , aglaataghtigu . "
Umiilwaaghem tuguluku , aglaalluku pilluwaghtet umiilgat pikaa , " Anusimingllagham Paul-em tagitesqaa elpenun una nukalpigaq , samenguq ungipaasuwaaten . "
Umiilgem tasluqluku iqitulluku ellnginaaghsamek aaptekaa , " Sameng ungipaasugsinga ? "
Kiimsiqaa , " Jews-et agghisimaat aapnaluteng Paul aglaataghtesqelluku agghivigmun unaami , aapqughwaghataghaghnaqniluku .
Ugpeqegpenaki , qayughllak 40-neng uglaghtut yuget iighluteng tumemi utaqiinaqnilghiit tuqunnaluku . Akeqimaat neghnaanghinnilutengllu , meghnaanghinnilutengllu kenlanga tuqutelleghmeggnun Paul . Apeghiighluteng utaqiigaqut naten pilleghqaghpeneng . "
Umiilgem ineghtengngwaaqaa nukalpigaq , " Kina alngunak ungipaategpenaan ungipaasaghtuumanilunga . " Taagken aanestekaa .
Taagken pilluwaghtet umiilgita tagsiqlighlukek umiilwaaghek pikakek , " Ungipaasaghtughteki 200 pilluwaghtet , 70 kuunitistet , 200 panastet igleghsaqleggiinaaghllinnguq Caesarea-mun , ighivgaqun 9-eklaagmi .
Paul-llu kuunimeng yataaghqunnakesi igleghusighqameng , wataghllak pinitun kaatunnakesi Governor-mun Felix-mun . "
Taagken governor-mun latatkegkaa Paul :
Ukut latat Claudius Lysias-meng pinguut Angellemnun Governor-mun Felix-mun , quyakamken .
Jews-et tugukaqaat Paul , tuqunnaqaqsaghpetaatlu iwernga liigikluku Rome-eghmiingutanga pilluwaghtekullghiini aqfaaghput aqnighhnayukatgu .
Liigiksugluku Jews-enun sameng apalluqutanga agghistengitnun aglaataqa .
Iwernga liigiksaqegka sameng apalliiteftuq tuqusaghqaaluni , talwa anusimingllaghyaghqaaluni . Taawanginaq Jews-et qaatkuuneghinniluku Liilightuusameggnun piiqeftaat .
Ungipaasatnga Jews-ennguq tuqunnaqaqaat Paul , tawaninginaq elpenun aglaatestaqa . Taakutlu avutkistengi kayagtanka elpenun apeghyaghtiisqelluku apallaat .
Enkaam unugmi tawani pilluwaghtet kayagtelleghmegestun aghulaqutkaat Paul kenlanga Antipatris-mun .
Unaamingani ilangi uteghniqat pilluwaghtet mangteghiitnun , taakut kuunitistet nagneghutkaat Paul Caesarea-mun .
Kaalluteng Paul aglaatkaat governor-mun , latatlu tuunegkiit .
Governor-em latat atightughluki aaptekaa Paul , " Nalighneghaneng Rome-em pinguzin ? " Paul-em kiimsiqaa , " Cilicia-meng " .
Governor-em pilaataqaa , " Avutkisteten kaaskata nanqiglleqamken . " Taagken kelengakistenun kayagutkaa kelengakesqelluku Praetorium-emi mangteghami Herod-em ulimastekaani .
Tallimat aghneghet atughluki High Priest-a Ananias , ilangillu siivanlleghet , akuzistekaghqaatlu Tertullus , kaatkat Caesarea-mun . Nanqigtivigmi Governor-mun Felix-mun aapqiit Paul-em seghletun pillghi .
Tuqlughyatni Tertullus pikaq , " Angellemni Governor Felix-mi , elpek apalluqluten nekeggmellelguukut nunamnni qavngarugllaggaaneng . Tamaakutlu kiyaghtellemnni allangughquqaghten pinightut .
Salleghpenun tamaghhaanun iyamsiqayugllaguukut .
Kimaawisnayukamken takestaaghhaaluku akuzinaqunga , iyamsiqayugvikamken nagannaqegkefkut .
Una yuuk Paul seghleliighqistenguuq . Seghleliighqaqii qamaglluki Jews-et naansaghngaata . Maghyaghqughtekaat Jesus-em Nazareth-eghmiim maligsaaghtengita .
Talwa sakusiiqnaqegkaqsaghaa Temple-a , iwernga tugukaqaghput .
Nanqiggnaqegkaqsaghaghput liillightuusamta pillghatun , taawanginaq pilluwaghtet umiilgita Lysias-em tagiluni pilluwaghteminun wayaghtestekaqaa whangkunneng . Taagken qelghii avutkistengi elpenun tagisqelluki .
Governor Felix-mi , aapqughaaquvgu liigikelleqaten anaggunnilleput ipangutangi . "
Jews-et ilatqaghtekat Tertullus-mun , akuzillghi qamaglluki ipangunikiit .
Taagken governor-em Paul akuzisqegkaa . Enkaam Paul pikaq , " Governor Felix-mi , quyaanga mesighaghnaqelghiinga elpenun , qayughllak liisimakamken qavngarugllaggaaneng nanqigtistenguuten whangkunnun Jews-enun .
Elpeni liigiksugnaghtuq ipangutanga akugaarugllak Jerusalem-etelqa maniguunnalunga Kiyaghneghmun .
Anaggunnistema liisimakaatnga aaghtiiraaghumangitaqa kina alngunak , qapraghqiimangitungallu yugneng Temple-mi , synagogue-nnillu , talwa nani alngunak Jerusalem-emi .
Enkaangam tawaten pimanighngaaghmegtengnga ipapighqennaanghitaat .
Iwernga apeghnaqaqa una elpesinun , manigughaqaqa Kiyaghneghat sivunemta maliglluku Tumanga Jesus-em . Ukut yuget pikangat temnginguniluku . Iwernga whangallu ellngistun ugpeqanka Moses-em Liilightuusii , uuknaliqistetlu igaqegkiit .
Anaggunnistemtunllu ugpeqaqa Kiyaghneghem unguvaghtesaghqaqii qamagtengngwaaghluki tuqukat pinighyaghngaata , seghleghuyaghngaata .
Enkaangam quunpeng kiyaghhnaqutkaqunga seghleghyugutkaghqiillunga Kiyaghneghmunllu yugnunllu .
" Qafsinegyak ayumiqulleq atughluku qantaghaqunghhaq uteghnightunga Jerusalem-emun manilinnaluki aklumalghiit Jews-elgutenka , aghqerraaghnalungallu Kiyaghneghmun .
Pelungighsaneghmeng apeghiighlunga Temple-mi aghqerraaghumalunga , ilangita Jews-et Asia-meng pit esghaghaatnga . Uvitka paaghqituqlu seghleliighituqlu .
Taakut Jews-et sangameng taginghitat ? Sameng anaggusimakuma ellnginguyaghtut aapghistekaghqanka seghletun pillemneng iwernga aviitut .
Yeqay ukut whaanlenguut nagatkaqaatnga mesighaghaqngama Jews-et agghivigitni , apeghlitgu anaggutelleghmeng naalkefikumakumegtengnga .
Entaqun ellngitni seghleghuuq whaten piiqngamki , ' Nanqigtaghpesinga qayughllak ugpeqegkenka tuqukat unguvaghyaghqaaniluki . ' "
Iwernga Felix-em , liisimakngwaaghluku kiyaghtaalleq Jesus-em apeghtuusaa , wintakusitkaa nanqigtegpenaan Paul . Pikaq , " Pilluwaghtet umiilgat Lysias kaaskan agghitkelleqaqa Paul . "
Taagken umiilwaaghmun kayagutkaa Paul kelengakesqelluku , naqam anusimingllaghtesnaniqaa . Ighsakesnaniqiillu ilakumtaaghita sameng taginneghatgu aklukegkaaneng .
Qafsinat aghneghet atughluki Felix-em Jews-a nuliini , Drusilla , kelqelluku tagikaq . Tagsiqlighluku Paul , nagatkaak ungipalghii ugpeqilleghmeng Jesus Christ-akun .
Paul-em akuzitkesaki ukut : pinitun kiyaghtaalleq , nuqenneghtulleq , Kiyaghneghemllu nanqigtilleghqaa tamaghhaanun . Governor Felix-em alingluni pikaa , " Aanelghaaten始ngam , alla aqfasleqamken pilleghqangegkuma . "
Tawani pilleghmi Felix neghyunguyalghii Paul-mun manililleqniluni pegtekumigu . Tamaaken apalluqluku tagsiqlighaqegkanga mulutegpenaan aleghquunnalutek .
Taagken maalghuk ayumiqullghek atughlukek , Porcius Festus governor-ngughtekaq . Iwernga Felix-em efqughsugluki Jews-et Paul unitkaa paninang qiipraghusighngaluku .
Festus kaasami Caesarea-mun igleghutinaluni , pingayut aghneghet atughluki aghulaqegkaq Jerusalem-emun .
Tawani chief priest-etlu , igleghutistengitallu Jews-et ungipitkaat , Paul seghleliighqiighllakaaniluku Jews-eneng .
Sagiqutkaat Festus-mun , Paul tagitesqelluku Jerusalem-emun qayughllak aksaqluku tuqusukaat tumangani .
Iwernga Festus-em pikii , " Paul kelengakaqaghput Caesarea-mi . Qantaghaqun uteghnighyaghqaagunga ,
igleghutistegpesi maliggnakangatnga . Elngaatall tawani sameng anaggusimakan apeghnakangat . "
Festus Jerusalem-emetaghaqaq pingayuneng inglulek nalighmeng qula aghneq , taagken Caesarea-tkaq . Unaamingani nanqigtivigem aqumutagkenkun aqumluni aqfastekaa Paul .
Tagisatgu , Jerusalem-eghmiit Jews-et kanglluqaghlluku anaggutaataghllagumanikaat iwernga ipapighqepagningitkiit anaggutellghi .
Paul mesighaqaq , " Qaatkiganneghitanka Jews-et Liilightuusiit , seghletun pingigatunga Temple-mi , seghletun pimangitaqa Rome-em Umiilegpigaa . "
Festus-em efqughsugluki Jews-et aaptekaa Paul , " Jerusalem-emi whangamnun nanqigtesugsiin ? "
Paul-em kiimsiqaa , " Nakaa ! Whaa Umiilegpigaam nanqigtivigani nekevghaanga enkaam tamaaken apalluqluku whani nanqigsaghqaagunga . Liisimakngwaaghan Jews-enun anaggutellghitunga .
Anaggusimakuma Rome-em liilightuusaan pillghani repall tuqusaghqaalunga , anagnaqnaanghitaqa tuqulleq . Iwernga Jews-et anaggunnillghat temngingukan , kitum alngunak Jews-enun sastekanganga , taana yuuk qaatkunnaanghituq Rome-em liilightuusaanun . Rome-em Umiilegpigaanun nanqigtesugtunga . "
Festus-enkut agghilgutkullghiit agghinneghmeng taaqsameng Paul-em piyukellghaneng , Paul pikaa , " Nanqigtesugulghiiten Umiilegpigaghmun , Umiilegpigaghmun aglaghllequten . "
Taam kingungiighhaaneng Umiilek Agrippa kaatkaq Caesarea-mun kelqelluku nayani Bernice , quyaknaluku Governor Festus .
Tamaansimalukek Festus-em ungipamsugutkaa Agrippa Paul-meng . Pikaa , " Governor-ngughsalghiinga Felix-em yuuk anusimingllaghvigmetestaqeftaa maani .
Jerusalem-emellunga chief priest-etlu , igleghutistengitallu Jews-et ungipaataatnga Paul-em anaggutellghaneng . Taagken aaptaatnga whangamnun tuqutestesqelluku ,
iwernga kiimsiqaqanka , ' Whangkuta Rome-eghmiini kinkut alngunak nanqigtegpenaki tuqusigataput . Liilightuusaput whaten pikaagut , Seghletun pinikaat , sivukluni apeghtesaghqaaguq ipa pimatanga anaggunnistet nagatestekluki . Taagken liigikelleqaghput salleghqaghput . '
Enkaam Paul-em anaggunnistengi tagilaghaasata aga unaamingani aqumegkaagunga nanqigtivigkun , tagitestekaqaqallu Paul .
Anaggunistengi nekevuulluteng seghletun pillghi apeghyaqmegteki sumeghtaghaatkellemtun seghleghtutkanghiteftut .
Taawanginaghhaq aaghtiiraaghumakangat ugpeqilleghmeggneng , taanallu yuuk aatqelghii Jesus-meng tuqumaniluku , iwernga Paul-em sagiqutkaqaa unguvaamaniluku .
Liisimakepagunghitutemneng tamaakut , Paul aaptaqa nanqigtesugutanga Jerusalem-emi .
Iwernga Paul-em kiimsighaanga , ' Nanqigtesugtunga Umiilegpigaghmun . Kelengakestinga kenlanga aglaghtestelleghpenun ellnganun . ' Enkaam anusimingllaghvigmun kanaghtesneqigtaqa kenlanga aglaghtestelleghqamnun Umiilegpigaghmun . "
Agrippa-m pikaa Festus , " Whangallu nagasugaqa Paul . " Pikaa , " Unaami nagalleqan . "
Unaamingani Agrippa-nkuk Bernice-enkuk iitqak qerngughutfigllagmun elngaatall aarraghwaaghlutek umiilgem aatkaaneng , maligtestekluki umiilgitlu pilluwaghtet , igleghutistengillu Caesarea-m . Taagken Festus-em itghutesqegkaa Paul .
Festus-em pikii , " Umiilegmi Agrippa-mi , elpesillu qamagllusi whaanlengughni , una yuuk esghaqesi , Paul-nguuq . Qamaglluteng Jews-et maanlenguut , Jerusalem-emelnguutlu qikeghqukegkaqaat whangamkun repall akilghuutkegkaqaat tuqusaghqaaniluku .
Iwernga nanqigsaqegka sameng apalliiteftuq tuqusaghqaaluni . Ellmineng nanqigtesukaatanganeng Umiilegpigaghmun aglaghtesnaluku piiqaqa .
Iwernga latatgun sameng ipapighqengngalghiimeng apeghyaghqiitunga Umiilegpigaghmun uumeng yugmeng ayuqelghiimeng . Enkaam tagitaqa sivugpesinun , kiyang elpenun Umiilegmi Agrippa-mi ! Neghyukaqa aapqughaaqumteggu sameng latasighqameng naalkefiknayukamkun .
Whangamni temnginguuq aglaghtestekumkun anusimingllaghaq Umiilegpigaghmun sameng anaggutelleghmeng apallungunaan . "
Agrippa-m pikaa Paul , " Taawa mesighaghyaghqaaghtuten , saaqsin akuzi . " Paul-em iiggeni nengugulluki , pikaa ,
" Umiilegmi Agrippa-mi , aghneghmi whani elngaatall aneghneghtunga sivugpeni mesighaghnaqelghiinga Jews-et anaggutelqennikangitneng ,
qayughllak nallukenghitngwaaghaten Jews-et nangaghneghitlu apalluqutkaqegkangitlu . Enkaam nangllegsipigllunga aaptamken nagataghtesqellunga .
" Nunamnilnguutlu Jerusalem-emelnguutlu qamaglluteng Jews-et liisimakaat kiyaghtaalqa anglinghhaatemneng ima .
Apeghyugyaqumegteggu liisimakegkaghteng apeghnayaghaatnga iiwleng qaatkutngalghiinga Jews-et Liilightuusiitnun .
Whaa Jews-et tagistaatnga whavek nanqigtesqellunga qayughllak neghyukngukegka Kiyaghneghem unguvaghtilleghqaa tuqukaneng akequsaqegkaa sivunemnnun .
Taanata akequsaq qula maalghuk siipneqelghiit ramkemta neghyukegkangat allgeghhnaluku , elngaatall maniguutnguluteng Kiyaghneghmun unugtuumaan , aghneghtuumaan . Umiilegmi , iwernga taana ataasiq neghyukilleq apalluqluku Jews-et nanqigtesugaatnga .
Sangafsi sumeghtaghaghaqetsi Kiyaghneq unguvaghtipagninginniluku tuqukaneng ?
" Sivunghani agani ugpeqepigtekaqaqa kipullginaalleghllaka elqughutnganiluku aatghaneng Jesus-em Nazareth-eghmiim .
Tawaten pikaagunga Jerusalem-emi . Chief priest-eneng pilleghqangegkaagunga anusimingllaghtesnaluki ugpeqalghutet . Tuququghnaqngatki itagnaqepigtekaqanka tuqutesqelluki .
Uglaghngaan aghyuughtestekaqanka tamaghhiitni synagogue-nni , whatenllu pisnaqutkegkaqanka , ' Ugpeqnaniimaaqa Jesus . ' Ugumiyagutepigtekaqanka repall malighqaqaqanka talwa Gentile-et nunangitnun amyuutkennaluki .
" Tamaaken apalluqluku Damascus-etunga pilleghqalighlunga , qelellelighlunga chief priest-eneng .
Umiilegmi , igleghtaaluta aghneq qukaghitaquqlu esghaghaqa nighuk nighugataghalghii siqineghmeng , kuukgullghii qilagmeng pamaken . Elngaatall nighupiglluni kuukgutkaaguq uvitemnun , igleghalgutemnunllu .
Qamaglluta ulleghaatukut nunamun . Taagken ma nagaqughaqa whaten pilghii Hebrew-ghmiistun , ' Saul , Saul ! Sangama amyuutkesinga ? Aqnighquuguten elpeneng amyuutkilleghpegun , tawateghpigaq ox-em aqnighqullghatun ketngighqulleghmikun yugmi maghyaghquusii . '
Aaptaqa , ' Kinanguzin Ataneq ? ' Atanghem kiimsighaanga , ' Jesus-nguunga , amyuutkegken .
Nekevi . Aliighvikamken qayughllak nakmikamken qepghaghtengulutenllu liisimakistengulutenllu . Apeghnaketen tamaakut esghaaqaghten aghneghmi whani , tamaakutlu kelgusaghqanka kinguvaqun aliighvikegkumken .
Yuguliiqnaaghamkenllu elpek katam yugpeneng , Gentile-enengllu . Ellngitnun kayaggnaqngwaamken
esghaghtestesqelluki , tunulluki mamlegmeng qiivesqelluki nighughmun , tunulluki Tughneghaam aghtughyaghqaanghillghaneng qiivesqelluki Kiyaghneghem aghtughyaghqaanghillghanun . Taagken Kiyaghneghem seghevulleqii seghleghqellghitneng , ilalleqiillu tamaavek aaftekaminun ugpeqillghitgun whangamneng . '
" Umiilegmi Agrippa-mi , qaatkegkaqaqa taana esghaghwaalqa qilagmeng .
Sivuklunga ungipaqiinga Damascus-mi taagken Jerusalem-emi , tamanganillu Judea-mi . Ungipaqiinga Jews-enunllu Gentile-enunllu avuteghqelluki seghleghqennanighluki qiivesqelluki Kiyaghneghmun , pinitunllu pisqanka ipapighqutkesqelluku avuteghqelluteng seghleghqennaniimatangi .
Tawaten ungipaqilqa apalluqluku Temple-mi Jews-et tugulunga tuqunnaqutkegkaqaatnga .
Iwernga Kiyaghneghem kayusiitaqaanga whavemun kenlanga , enkaam sivugpesigun nekevlunga aapghaqa Christ-a pingwaaghllagnunllu ukavantalghiinunllu . Aapqaqa taananguuq ataasiq uuknaliqistetlu Moses-emllu uuknaliqutkegkaat .
Pikaagut Christ-a ikfiqepestaaghlleqniluku enkaam sivuliiluni unguvaghyaghqaaniluku tuqulleghmeng . Apeghyaghqaanilukullu nighuga yugulillghem yugnunllu Gentile-enunllu . "
Paul mesighaamaluku Festus-em akilghuughllakaa , " Paul , nallungughtuten ! Liitelleghllagpek nallungughtestaaten ! "
Iwernga Paul-em pikaa , " Governor Festus-mi , nallungughtellghitunga , liisimalunga ipameng akuzinguunga .
Umiilgem Agrippa-m liisimakngwaaghaa tamaana enkaam tetugpenaan aleghqughaqa . Liisimakaqa nagaquqaqii qamaglluki tamaakut qayughllak aksaqluku pikaanghitut .
Umiilegmi Agrippa-mi , ugpeqaqsikii uuknaliqistet igaqegkiit ? Liisimakamken ugpeqaqaten ! "
Umiilgem Agrippa-m aaptekaa Paul , " Sumeghpenii-i whaa takesqughhaan aleghqughlunga ugpeghtesnaqsingaa Christ-ameng ? "
Paul-em kiimsiqaa , " Takesqughhaaghngaan , nalighmeng taakluku aleghqughyaghngaamken yughaatkengngwaamken Kiyaghneghmun ugpeghesqelluten . Ellnginaghpek yughaatkengngunghitamken , yughaatkengngwaamsi qamagllusi nagallghiini whangamneng aghneghmi whani , whangamtun lliighesqellusi iwerngaqun qiipraghutngunasi ! "
Taagken Umiilek Agrippa , Governor Festus , Bernice , tamaakutlu ilangi nekevuutkat .
Aanluteng ellmeggneng aleghquutkat , " Uumun yugmun sameng apalliitukut tuqutusighqameng nalighmeng anusimingllaasighqameng . "
Agrippa-m pikaa Festus , " Aanesnayaghaghput Umiilegpigaghmun nanqigtesqelluni pikaanghisaqan . "
Festus-em Italy-tesqesugyinkut angyaghpagkun , aglaatestekii Paul-llu ilangillu anusimingllaghat umiilwaaghmun Julius-mun . Julius-enkut pilluwaghtekullghiit aatqelghiit , " Umiilegpigaam Pilluwaghtengi . "
Taawa angyaghpak Adramyttium-emeng pi , aghulaqsaqleggiinaaghtekaq nenun Asia-m esnenganilngughnun . Tawavek uuglluta aghulaqukut . Aristarchus-em maligtiinkut Thessalonica-ghmiim . ( Thessalonica Macedonia-melnguq ) .
Unaamingani kaatukut Sidon-mun . Julius-em pinitungwaaq pikaa Paul , laalightestaqluku ilakumtaaghanun Sidon-mi , sameng aklukegkaaneng tuunaqluku pisqelluku .
Sidon-meng aghulaqukut anuqa aygumun enkaam igleghtukut uqiinellghakun qiighqam Cyprus-em .
Igleghaakut esnengakun Cilicia-mllu Pamphylia-mllu , taagken nagneghtukut Myra-mun Lycia-melngughmun .
Tamaanteftuq angyaghpak Alexandria-meng pi , enkaam Umiilwaaghem Julius-em liigikluku Italy-nnaqutanga uugtestiinkut .
Nunmaasqughhaq igleghtukut qafsinegyagllak aghneq , iwernga piyaqliighngaamta kaatukut Cnidus-mun . Anuqliitem igleghapagningiitesinkut taagavek , igleghtukut uqiinellghakun qiighqam Crete-em , naghughlluku Salmone .
Esnengiighhaakun igleghtukut piyaqliighngaamta , kaatukut kangighamun aatqelghiimun , Uqitaghvik Kangighaq , taana qantaghanlenguq Lasea-meng .
Tamaanteghllagtukut qenwat yakughnaghtaa taakluku igleghamun , siingenllu Aghneq naghughlleghhii priest-et aghqerraaghvigat seghleghqellghitnun Jews-et . Enkaam Paul-em kelengasaaghii angyaghpagem umiilwaaghi .
Pikii , " Ukughsi yugni , sumemni whaa elngaatall yakughniighnaqukut igleghallemnni . Iflaaqelteggullu angyaghpagput usituumaan , entaqun talwa tuqulaghaallequkut . "
Iwernga Umiilwaaghem Julius-em nagatkaqegkek angyaghpagemllu umiilga , angyaghpaleklu yuuk avelghaghluku Paul .
Allullutengllu angyaghpagem yugi igleghsukat qayughllak taana kangighaq yakughnalghii angyaghpagmun uksughfiguluni . Kaannaqnaluteng Phoenix-mun pikat uksughsaghqaaluteng tamaani . Phoenix-em kangighaa qiighqamelnguq Crete-mi , northwest-munllu southwest-munllu ayuqelghii .
Ikegkemeng anuqataghaaghsan angyaghpagem yugi pikat , " Taanata anuqa utaqakaghput . " Enkaam uyghiita sayugluku telanangaakut Crete-em esnengiighhaakun .
Iwernga anuqlighllagtuq nakaghyameng enkaam qiighqameng atghaghteghllagaa .
Angyaghpak awatmun tengsagu quutmun taglaghnaqutkesaghluta iilqayugtukut enkaam upuupeng tengtestukut .
Qiighqasqughhaam Cauda-m uughqanganun lliighusinkut uqiteghraagtukut . Tawani qamuqsaqefut angyaghhaghput piyaqliighutkeghngaamteggu qaakaghput .
Taagken angyaghpak ayugighsaghaat asighlluku tapghaghmeng . Alingluteng qenaaghllughquunnayukameng Syrtis-mi telanangat ifkaghqughluki tengtestukut .
Unaamingani paninang esla almesiqeghllagyagu , angyaghpagem usingan ilangi meghmun ateghqughiit .
Awakaghaani esla almesiqsagu angyaghpagem sanqutngi ateghqughiit .
Qafsinegllak aghneq siqinngunani , ighaleqetaangunani piiq eslam seghleghllagem angtalanganeng . Enkaam talwa iilqayugtukut , isigimaqun tuqulaghaannaqelghiikut .
Yuget neghegpenateng muluughllagyata Paul-em nekevluni pikii , " Ukughsi yugni , nagatkaqsaqufsinga kennayanghilnguukut Crete-meng enkaam aghsaan seghleliighnayanghitusi , saghyangiinnayanghitusi .
Iwernga iilqayugpenasi , nalighhiinaghsi tuqunaanghituq iwerngaqun angyaghpagiillequkut .
Unuk Kiyaghneghem yaqulgan takukaqaanga . Taanata Kiyaghneq manigughaqegkegka , ellngan pikaanga .
Yaqulgem piinga , ' Paul , alingegpenang , kaallequten Rome-emun , nekevellequten sivungakun Umiilegpigaam . Yughaatkegkaqutegpeneng angyaghpagmetelguteten qamaglluki Kiyaghneghem yugulilleqii . '
Enkaam quyatek , ugpeqiinga Kiyaghneghqun tawatetngwaaghesqelluku ungipaatellemtun .
Iwerngaqun angyaghpagiillequkut qiighqami . "
Qula estamat siipneqluku unuk Kelliimi Adriatic-mi tengtiinkut . Taakwani unugem qukaani yulaaghet piiqut quutmun tughwaaghsugninniluta .
Tapghaq uqigkutighluku meghmun ateghsaqmegteggu yuginaq yaagneq uusqaghtutkaftuq . Tazingapighqaaghyamta tapghaq ateghllaataghyaqmegteggu akimigaq yaagneq uusqaghtutkaliimalghii .
Yulaaghet alingegkat angyaghpak qalmesinnayukan enkaam estamaneng uyghighaat kingungakun . Taagken yughaghtut aghhragkiighesqelluku .
Angyaghpagem yulaaghi anagnaqegkat sivuyaga angyaghpagem uyghiitelighnaqesighwaaghutkelluku , angyaghhaq meghmun ateghtekaat .
Iwernga Paul-em pikii umiilwaaqlu pilluwaghtetlu , " Ukut yuget aghulaqegkata kayutepagiillequkut enkaam elpesi tuqulaghaallequsi . "
Enkaam pilluwaghtet angyaghhaq keputkaat .
Aghtaghaghnaqaqaallu Paul-em qamaglluki neghesqughwaaqii , pikii , " Qula estamat siipneqluku aghneq neghelqunghitusi qayughllak elngaatall kelengaruulghiisi .
Tamaaken apalluqluku neghesqughwaaghnaqamsi iknaqughtesqellusi . Nalighhiinaghsi tuqunaanghituq talwa aqnighhnaanghituq . "
Nepiighyami neqekrangllameng tugulluni igamsiqayugvikluku Kiyaghneq manungitni ikulluni neghegkaq .
Yuget ilutughsaghyisteng ellngitlu qamaglluteng neghuutkat .
Qerngaghllagemta angyaghpagmelngughni 276-nguukut .
Qamaglluteng neghuunneghmeng apeghiighyameng angyaghpak uqengellinaluku wheat-a meghmun ateghqughaat .
Aghsagu quutmeng esghaatut , taawanginaq liisuqenghitaat natungutanga . Iwernga kangighalguftuq esnalegmeng enkaam taaggun tamlagnaqsugtut .
Kepuulluki uyghiitet unitkiit meghmelluki , petugutiiklu aquutak naghighquqiit . Taagken sayugluki telaanangat sivuyagmelnguut tengtestut tespikavek esnamun .
Iwernga angyaghpagem sivuyaga aghqitaghisan kingunga qagighllaget kagimtaat .
Pilluwaghtet piyaghiit anusimingllaghat tuququghnaluki luuraq quutmun pugimluteng navek anagnayukata .
Iwernga umiilwaaghem tuqutesugumangitkaa Paul enkaam iinghutkii . Yeghlegi qelqii pugimaqayuggaat quutmun tagliisqelluki .
Tamaakut pugimellgilnguut angyaghpagem ikellghaakun tuguluki taglaghnaqesqegkii quutmun . Tawaten qamaglluta yaywaaseng uuglleghaatukut quutmun .
Yaywaaseng quutmun uugsamta liigikaghput qiighqaq Malta-ngutanga .
Tamaakumiit elngaatall upughatiinkut kumaqisimaamta qayughllak aqlaghaghtekanga eslallugughsimaghmi .
Paul saqumigluni quugkameng qiighimaluku , tuqunalghii nemeghyaq maatneghem aanesluku quugneng , iiggakun amqeghtekaa .
Tamaakumiit esghaghluku nemeghyaq Paul-em iigganeng qughaghngalghii ilateng pikiit , " Ipapestaaq una yuuk yugtaghtenguuq . Qaywa un始gani meghmi tuqunghiteghngaaghmi esghaghhu tuquyaghqaamalghii . "
Paul-em iiggeni ufsugusaqminiki nemeghyaq ifkaghtuq kenghegnun iwernga talwa nemeghyam aqnighsimangilkanga .
Yuget pikaqsaqangat Paul puuveghllagnaqniluku nalighmeng tuqunaqniluku . Iwernga sagpenani muluughllagyan , sumeghtaghaatkegkaat , " Una naliqaat kiyaghneghet . "
Taam qiighqam umiilga Publius , nunalguftuq ughugsighvimta tungangani . Publius-em elngaatall upughatiinkut , ellnganitukut pingayut aghneghet .
Atanga puqleghanguftuq aqsalliqumaghmi . Paul-em esghaghyaghtughluku yughaatkelluku , saafsaqminigu naallghutuq .
Paul tawaten piyan qamaglluteng ilangi qinuyuget tagilaghaatkat enkaam naallghutkat .
Tamaaken apalluqluku tunqughtaagiinkut tunusameng . Tamaani pingayut tanqit atughluki aghulaqsaghqaaghsamta tunqughtaalaataghiinkut tumangani atughqamnneng . Angyaghpak Alexandria-meng pi uksughsimalghii tamaani qiighqami . Aatqeftaa " Malghik kiyaghneghek " sivuyaganiteftuklu ulimaaghulutek taakuk . Aghulaqsaghqaaghsan taaggun uugtukut .
Syracuse-mun kaalluta tamaantukut pingayut aghneghet .
Taagken qapiighwtaghtukut Rhegium-emun kaatellemnnun kenlanga . Aghneq ataasiq atughluku tamaani , unaamingani anuqataghaaghutiinkut ikevaghmeng enkaam awakaghaani Puteoli-mun kaatukut .
Tamaanteftut ugpeqat , ellmeggnitesqiinkut maaghraghvinlek aghneq . Taagken Rome-emun nagneghtukut .
Ugpeqat Rome-emelnguut nagaqughluta , paayghumakanginkut tungangitnun Akilpegaghviget Appius-melnguut , ilangita paayghumakanginkut tungangitnun Pingayut Aqelqalghutat . Paul-em esghaghluki ugpeqat ilutughtekaq enkaam iyamsiqayugvikegkaa Kiyaghneq .
Rome-emun kaasamta Paul ellnginaghmetestaat nani piyukelghani iwerngaqun ataasim pilluwaghtem kelengakaa .
Pingayut aghneghet atughluki Paul-em tagsiqlighii Jews-et igleghutistengit . Tagiyata pii , " Jew-lgutemni , sanghiteghngaamki yuput , nalighmeng kipullginaanghiteghngaamki nangaghneghit sivunemta , paninang igleghutistemta Jerusalem-emelnguut tugulunga tuunaatnga Rome-eghmiinun .
Aapqughaaghlunga sameng apalliisama tuqutusighqameng itemunnalunga piyaghaatnga .
Iwernga Jews-et ighlekaatnga enkaam tamaaken apalluqluku piiqa nanqigtista Umiilegpigaghmun nanqigtesugnilunga . Umiilegpigaghmun seghlequughyaghtuunghitanka yulgutenka .
Enkaam tagsiqlighamsi apeghnaluki tamaakut elpesinun . Liitesugaqallu elpesinun taana ataasiq Israel-eghmiit neghyukegkaat apalluqluku qiipraghusighngaanga . "
Kiimsiqaat , " Judea-ghmiit latatkigataaten whangkunnun . Talwa nalighhiiniita ugpeqaalgutemta taagegken tagiluteng ungipaqigataaten , nalighmeng seghletun akuzitkigataaten .
Whangkuta liisugaghput elpenun sameng sumeghtaghaatkaqutangi tamaakut ugpeqilghiit Jesus-meng , qayughllak liisimakaghput nani alngunak seghlequughaqiit . "
Taagken nakmikegkaat aghneq ataasiq qerngughutfiguluku . Taana aghneq kaasan uglapiglluteng tagilaghaatkat Paul-em kiyaghfiganun . Unaaghhaaneng unullghanun kenlanga apeghtuqii Ataneghpagullghaneng Kiyaghneghem , liigikestengngwaaghnaqutkegkiillu Jesus-meng atuqluki Liilightuusii Moses-em , uuknaliqistetlu igaqegkiit .
Ilangita ugpeqegkaat iwernga ilangita ugpequmangilkangat .
Enkaam aaghtiiraaghutkat . Nekevuutaqutlu aanleghaannaluteng Paul-em pikii , " Agleghnalghiik Taghneghak ipa pimalghiik sivuneghpesigun uuknaliqistekun Isaiah-kun .
Whaten pikaaguq , ' Takuluki ukut yuget whaten piki , Nagasaghngaaghpesi , esghapagngaaghpesi liigiknaanghitusi .
Taakut yuget tawatetut qayughllak umyugiit pineghlluugtekaagut enkaam sigutetengllu iyetengllu saapegkaqiit . Tawatenneghisaqumeng esghaannayaghtut , nagaquunnayaghtut , liigiknayaghtut , qiivnayaghtutlu whangamnun naallghutesqelluteng . ' "
Paul-em taaqniitkun pikii , " Elpesinun liigikesugaqa , Kiyaghneghem kayagtengngwaaqaqii ungipaghteni ungipiisqelluki yugulilleghmeng Gentile-enun . Ellngit nagatepestaaghyaghqaagut . "
Tawaten Paul piyan Jews-et aaghtiiraaghuteghllagumaghmeng aanleghaatkat .
Maalghuk ayumiqullghek Paul-em kiyaghfikegkaa mangteghaq llivikaqluku . Upughataqegkangi qamaglluki iteghteni ,
tetugpenanillu ungipaqaq Ataneghpagullghaneng Kiyaghneghem . Apeghtuutkegkaallu Ataneq Jesus Christ-a . Tawaten pillgha kitum alngunak aghuliighsimangilkanga .
Ukut latat Paul-meng pinguut ; qepghaghtekaanga Jesus Christ-am . Kiyaghneghem tuqluqaqaanga apostle-ngulunga , nakmikegkaqaangallu ungipaqesqelluki Pinilghiit Ungipani .
Ayumiq Kiyaghneghem akequsaqegkaqii taakut Pinilghiit Ungipat uuknaliqistemikun . Uuknaliqutkegkaqiit agleghnalghiitgun Akuzitetgun Igaqegkatgun .
Taakut Pinilghiit Ungipat Kiyaghneghem Ighneghaneng ayuqut . Yuguluni allgeqaaguq Umiilgem David-em kingunghitgun .
Agleghnalghiim Taghnegham liigikestiinkut Ataneghput Jesus Christ-a , Kiyaghneghem aghtughyaghqaanghilnguuguq Ighnegha . Taghnegham ipapighqegkaqaa unguvaghtesluku Jesus tuqulleghmeng .
Ellngakun nangllekellengumaanga apostle-ngulunga . Tawaten Kiyaghneghem pikaqaanga tuqliisqelluki nunataghhaan yugi ugpeqesqellukullu , qaatkesqellukullu Christ-a . Enkaam Christ-am aatgha quulvallengellequq .
Elpesillu Rome-emelngughni , Kiyaghneghem tuqluqaqiisi Jesus Christ-amun pikesqellusi .
Qamagllusi elpesi Rome-emelngughni Kiyaghneghem piniqegkiitni , tuqluqiitnillu yuknalusi : Kiyaghneghem Atamta , Atanghemllu Jesus Christ-am kayusiillisi , nekeggmellelisillillu .
Sivukluku tamaghhaghpesinun iyamsiqayugvikaqa Kiyaghneqa Jesus Christ-akun , qayughllak ungipaa ugpeqilleghpesi mingitnguuq yulghutnun tamaghhaani .
Pinaqelqa qamaglluku qepghaataqaqa Kiyaghneq , ungipaqnaluki Pinilghiit Ungipat Ighneghaneng ayuqelghiit . Kiyaghneq liisimakistekaqa quunpeng yughaatkengngukemsi .
Yughaghaqungallu Kiyaghneghmun piyukelqegkagu qenwatlu elpesinun piyaghqaalunga .
Esghaghyupigtaqamsi quyastellelinnalusi Kiyaghneghem Taghneghagkeneng iknaqsuugtesqellusi .
Whaten pingwaamsi : qerngaamta kayemutunnaluta , elpesi ugpeqillemkun , whanga ugpeqilleghpesigun .
Ugpeqaalgutemni , liisimakesugamsi awen laalighfiksugaqamsi iwernga saam quunpeng pinghitestaqaanga . Enkaam maaten kayusiisuganka Rome-eghmiit ugpeghesqelluki Christ-akun , ilangitnun Gentile-enun pillemtun .
Kiyaghneghem nakmikegkaqaanga ungipaqesqelluki Pinilghiit Ungipat . Enkaam ungipaqsaghqaqanka tamaghhaanun , Greek-enunllu Greek-ngunghilngughnunllu , peghqineghnunllu nalluuqanunllu .
Enkaam whaa ungipaqiyugllaguunga Pinilghiineng Ungipaneng elpesinunllu kiyaghlleghhiini Rome-emi .
Kayngukigatanka Pinilghiit Ungipat : Kiyaghneghem aghtughyaghqaanghilqii yugulilleghmun tamaghhaanun ugpeqilghiinun . Sivukluteng ungipaqegkaagut Jews-enun taagken Gentile-enun .
Taakut Pinilghiit Ungipat liigikestiinkut naten Kiyaghneghem nallghusaghaqutangi yuget elqughutngalleghminun . Ugpeqillghiniitgun Kiyaghneq tawaten piiquq . Katam Akuzitni Igaqegkani igaqngaaq , " Nallghughqegkaq Kiyaghneghem elqughutngallghanun kiyaghllequq neghyukluku ellnga . "
Qilagmeng Kiyaghneghem yuget liigikestii sakritutnguniluki , aghyuughlleqnilukillu seghleghqellghitnun , seghletunllu pillghitnun . Seghletun pillghita liigiknanightestiit Kiyaghneghem ipapillghaneng .
Sangwaa yuget liisimakegkaat Kiyaghneghmeng ayuqelghii whateghlluwaaghuuq ellngitnun qayughllak Kiyaghneghem whateghlluwaaghughtaa ellngitnun .
Kiyaghneghem ulimatanganeng nuna , yuget liigikngwaaghaqaat aghtughyaghqaanghillgha aghuliighigalnguq , ipallu Kiyaghneghutanga . Qaywa yuget esghaghpagningiteghngaaghmegtekek taakuk , paninang liisimakagket Kiyaghneghem ulimaaghakun . Enkaam yuget apalliitut whaten pilleghqameng , Nallukaghput Kiyaghnelgutanga .
Liisimakeghngaaghmegteggu Kiyaghneq , quulviigataat Kiyaghneghuluku , iyamsiqayugvikigataatlu . Yeghlegi sumeghtaghallghit Kiyaghneghmeng satngunaniqaagut , umyugiitlu liigiknaniqaagut .
Peghqinghuniiqut iwernga nalluughtaqut .
Enkaam manigughpenaan Kiyaghneq tuquyaghqaghhaanghilnguq , yeghlegi manigughaqiit kiyaghnengllaqateng yugsugnilnguut , qawaagsugnilnguut , teghikusaghsugnilnguut , nalighmeng nemeghyaghsugnilnguut .
Tamaaken apalluqluku Kiyaghneghem pegtii atuqesqelluki nukeggnalghiit sex-kun seghleghqellghet piyukeghllakiit . Enkaam atuqaqiit yugusiteng anagngaluki , seghleghqaqluteng sex-kun ilameggnun ,
qayughllak ipapilleq Kiyaghneghmeng ayuqelghii naavghusimaat iqlengamun . Enkaangam manigughaqiitlu , qepghaataqiitlu Kiyaghneghem ulimaaghi , avelghaghluku Ulimaghista ellnga katam . Ellnganguuq usuqsaghqaq quunperugllak kenlengunaan ! Amen .
Tamaaken apalluqluku Kiyaghneghem pegtii atuqesqelluki seghleghqellghet piyukeghllakiit . Aghnat sex-eyugnanighiit yuget , yeghlegi sex-eyagutut aghnaalgutmeggneng .
Tawateghpigaq yugetlu sex-eyugnanighiit aghnat , yeghlegi sex-eyaguteghllagtut yulgutmeggneng . Tawaten pikaatangitneng Kiyaghneghem aghyuughii yugusiitgun apalluqluki anaggutelleghllagit .
Tamaakut yuget sumeghmeggni satngunghinniiqaat liisimakipiilleq Kiyaghneghmeng ayuqelghii . Enkaam Kiyaghneghem pegtii satngunghilngughnun sumeghtaghallghitnun , atughqaqenghisaqangitnunllu .
Allaaghhinaghmeng seghleghmeng pimanginaghaqut , seghleghqaqut , pakigneghuut , ugumiketaghtutlu . Aqinaketaghtut , yugtaghyuneghtuut , pilluwaghyuneghtuut , puughtiyuneghtuut , sumeghtaghaatkaqiitlu ilateng seghlepiguluki . Yiillgiiqut ,
seghletun akuzitkaqiit ilateng . Ugumikaat Kiyaghneq , yukeghqenghuut , qukaayugneghuutlu . Sumeghtaghaghaqut wata seghletun pinaluteng ; qaatkusigatut angayuqameggnun ,
nalluut , akequsateng atuqigatiit , nangllegyugigatut , nafughtiitaqutlu ilameggnun .
Liisimakiit Kiyaghneghem Liilightuusii pilghiit tawatelnguut yuget allgeghsaghqaqaan始nguq tuqulleq . Nagneghutnginaghpenaki tamaakut atuqegkateng , talwa itagnaqaqiit tawaten pilghiit .
Tamaaken apalluqluku nanqigtikuvek yugneng anagniilqavigituten . Nanqiggneghpeki , elpeneng nanqigtaquten aghyuughyaghqaaluten qayughllak elpeklu ellngistun piiqelghiiten .
Kiyaghneq nanqigtiiquq yugneng seghlepestaatun pilghiineng , liisimakaghputlu nanqigtillghi elqughutngaat .
Iwernga nanqigtaqaten anaggullghiit , naqamllu elpek katam piiqaten tamaakut ataasit anaggutellghet . Enkaam sumeghpenii anagyaghqaaniluku piziguu Kiyaghneghem nanqigtillgha ?
Liigikenghisiguu nangllegtaghtulanga Kiyaghneghem ? Aghyuughaghsigalkangaten tawaninginaq qayughllak nuqetutaqegkangaten . Sumeghpenii-i taakut satngunghitaat ? Liisimakenghisiguu Kiyaghneghem nangllekaqegkangaten qayughllak avuteghqesqesukangaten ?
Iwernga elpek aleghquneghlluguuten , pineghlluguuten ; tamaaken apalluqluku avuteghqesugigatuten . Enkaangaam elpek katam ulimangwaan aghyuullengelleghqan seghleghataghaaluku Nanqigtillghem Aghneghani . Tawani Aghneghmi Kiyaghneghem aliighlleqaak sakraallenillu , elqughutngalghiillu nanqigtilleni .
Nanqiglleqii tamaghhiita yuget apeghiighutellghistun .
Ilangi yuget pinitun pimanginaghaqut qayughllak Kiyaghneghmeng allgeghsukangit usuqelleq , quulvalleq , yugusiqlu tuquyaghqaanghilnguq . Enkaam Kiyaghneghem kenlengilngughmeng unguvallelilleqii .
Iwernga ilangi yuget ellnginaayugneghuut . Ugpeqsugigataat ipapilleq seghlepestaatun pinaluteng . Enkaam Kiyaghneghem sakrituteghllagluki , aghyuughllaglleqii .
Qamagtengngwaaghluni nunamelnguq yuuk , Jews-a nalighmeng Gentile-a , seghlepestaatun pikaq , Kiyaghneghem aghyuughlleqaa seghleliighmengllu ikfiqelleghmengllu .
Iwernga qamagtengngwaaghluni yuuk , Jews-a nalighmeng Gentile-a , pinitun pikaq , Kiyaghneghem usuqelleqaa , quulvaghlleqaa , nekeggmellelilleqaallu .
Taniillngunaki Kiyaghneghem nanqiglleqii qamagtengngwaaghluki yuget .
Gentile-et allgeghtellghitiit Liilightuusat Kiyaghneghem tuunegkii Moses-mun . Enkaam seghleghqelghiit nallukluki Liilightuusat , tuqukata Kiyaghneghem nanqiggnaanghitii Liilightuusatgun . Jews-et Liilightuusalguut , enkaam seghleghqegkata Kiyaghneghem nanqiglleqii Liilightuusatgun .
Tamaakut nagataghesnalghiit Liilightuusaminun , Kiyaghneghem nallghusiigatii elqughutngalleghminun . Iwernga qaatkullghiit Liilightuusaminun nallghughqaqii elqughutngalleghminun .
Gentile-et allgeghtellghitiit Kiyaghneghem Liilightuusii . Iwernga qaatkenneghmegteki taakut Liilightuusat , qaatkutellghita Liilightuusalgestun ayuqestiit ilumegteggun , allgeghtekaqenghiteghngaaghmegteki .
Qaatkutellghita yugnun liigikestiit ilumegteggun liisimakiit Liilightuusat qelghusiit . Sumeghtaghallghitallu liisimakestiit Liilightuusat ilungitnitulangi , qayughllak sumeghtaghallghita ilangakun anaggunniiqiit nalighmeng ilangakun itagnaghniiqiit .
Nanqigtillghem Aghneghani , Kiyaghneghem nanqiglleqii yuget aksaqegkiit Christ Jesus-kun . Aapghaqaqa taana ungipaqnemki Pinilghiit Ungipat .
Maaten始ngam latayuganka Jews-et . Jew-ngukuvek , neghyukaten Liilightuusat Kiyaghneghem tuunegkaqii yugpenun . Qukaayugtutenllu Kiyaghneghmun pikniluten .
Liilightuusatgun liisimakan sangwaa Kiyaghneghem sasqesullgha elpenun , natenllu nakmiksaghqaatanga sangwaa elqughutngalghii .
Enkaam sumeghpeni maghyaghqughtenguniiquten ayaakanun , nighuguniiqutenllu mamlegmelngughnun .
Sumeghpeni nallghusaghtenguniiquten nalluuqanun , apeghtughistenguniiqutengllu taghnughhaghnun . Liilightuusalgutegpeneng , sumeghpeni liisimakniluku sangwaa tamaghhaan piiqan , qamagllukullu ipapilleq .
Apeghtughaqaten ilaten , sangan elpeneng apeghtiigasin ? Ungipaqiiquten , " Teglegpenang , " elpaa-ak , teglekiigasiin ?
Piiquten , " Gelgaghniighpenang , " elpaak , gelgaghniiqiigasiin ? Ugumikepigtaten kiyaghnengllaqat , elpaak , tugunniiqiigasiin temple-ngitneng ?
Qukaayugtaquten qayughllak Kiyaghneghem Liilightuusani tuunegkaqii yugpenun . Iwernga qaatkenghinneghpeki Liilightuusat quulviigatan Kiyaghneq .
Akuzitni Igaqegkani igaqngaaq , " Apalluqlusi elpesi Jews-eni , Gentile-et sanguughtaqaat Kiyaghneghem aatgha . "
Qaatkengngukufki Kiyaghneghem Liilightuusii circumcise-ellghen pinightuq . Iwernga qaatkenghilkufki Liilightuusat circumcise-ellghilngughestun ayuquten . Enkaam quyastellengnaanghituten Kiyaghneghem akequsaaneng .
Gentile-a circumcise-ellghilnguq qaatkullghii qelghusiitnun Liilightuusat , Kiyaghneghem tuguklighlleqaa nikimqun circumcise-ekaaluku .
Elpesi Jews-eni Liilightuusalguusi igaqngalghiineng , circumcise-ekaagusillu , taawanginaq qaatkigatasi Liilightuusat . Iwernga Gentile-et circumcise-ellghilnguut , qaatkaqiit Liilightuusat . Enkaam qaatkutellghitgun Kiyaghneghem nanqiglleqiisi aghyuughyaghqaalusi .
Circumcise-enginaghluku yugem yugusii Jew-pigughtesnaanghitaa . Circumcise-ellepiik pingigatuq yugusim qaaynginaakun .
Itupill , yuuk Jew-piiguuq Jew-ngukumi ilumikun . Ighsaqghwa circumcise-ekaaguq Agleghnalghiignekun Taghneghagnekun , nakaan igaqegkatgun Liilightuusatgun . Enkaam Kiyaghneghmeng usuqellengellequq , nakaan yugneng .
Sangwaa aneghneghqusiigwa yuuk allgequmi Jew-nguluni ? Sangwaa aneghneghqusiigwa circumcise-elleghmun ?
Uglaapigtut aneghneghqusit ! Sivulighpigaq Kiyaghneghem neghyukutkaqii Jews-enun Akuzitet Igaqegkat .
Ilangi ataasiighmenneghilkata Kiyaghneghmun , Kiyaghneq ataasiighmenneghitesleqatguu ?
Yeghlegillu ! Tamaghhaghmi yuuk iqlengiqestengughngaan , Kiyaghneq ipanguuq . Akuzitni Igaqegkani Kiyaghneghmeng ayuqelghii igaqngaaq whaten , " Akuzineghpeni , tamaghhaghmi liisimakelleqaaten elqughutnganiluten . Yuget nanqigtekangaten , ipapighqelleqaten anaggutnganiluki . "
Anaggunnemta , anaggutellemta yuget liigikestengngwaaghaqiit Kiyaghneq elqughutnganiluku . Enkaam pilleqestaa Kiyaghneq anaggunniluku aghyuuqanginkut anaggutellemnnun ? ( Akuzinguunga yugestun . )
Tawatenneghituq ! Kiyaghneq elqughutnganghilkan , natenmi Kiyaghneghem nanqiglleqaki nunam yugi ?
Iwernga yuuk pinayalghii , " Iqlengiqelleghma yuget usuqistaqiit Kiyaghneghmun qayughllak iqlengiqelleghma aliightaqaa Kiyaghneghem ipangullgha . Enkaam sangan始ngam Kiyaghneghem nanqigtanga aghyuughyaghqaalunga seghleghqestetun ? "
Yuuk pinayalghiillu , " Seghletun pilta sangwaa pinilghii apeghiighesqelluku seghletun pillemnneng . " Ilangi yuget temngimeng piiqut whangkuta apeghtughiiqniluta tawaten . Nanqigtellengyaghqaagut aghyuughyaghqaaluteng , aghyuulleghqamegestun .
Enkaam whangkuta Jews-enii , pinighataghaghestaa Gentile-eneng ? Nakaa , yeghlegillu ! Aapghwaaqaqanka Jews-etlu , Gentile-etlu tawateghpigaq seghleghqellghem aaghqutaqluki ayuqii .
Akuzitni Igaqegkani igaqngaaq , " Taawa kina alngunak elqughutnganghituq , talwa ataasighhaq .
Kina alngunak liigikigatuq , kitum alngunak iviigataa Kiyaghneq .
Qamaglluni yuuk tunutkaaguq Kiyaghneghmeng ; qamaglluteng anaggutkaagut ; kina alngunak pinitun pingigatuq , talwa ataasighhaq .
Ighsalqiit qelpalngughestun lliivghestun ayuqut ; uluteng atuqngwiit puughtimun , qezimegteggun poison-elguut nemeghyastun ;
qaanghit imighngaat curse-elleghnengllu , ugumiketiqelleghmengllu .
Yugtaghirakegtut ;
navek alngunak pineghmeggni naafqiistengwaaqut , seghleliighqistengwaaqutlu .
Nallukaat nekeggmelluni kiyaghtelleghqaq ,
talwa alikigataat Kiyaghneq . "
Liisimakaput Jews-et Liilightuusalget qaatkesaghqaqiit qelghusiit . Enkaam taakut Liilightuusat nepiighqelleqiit yuget whaten pilleghqiitneng , " Nallukaput sangutangi seghleghqellghet . " Liilightuusatlu liigikesleqiit Kiyaghneghmun nanqiglleqniluki qamaglluki nunam yugi .
Nanqigtekumiki yuget nallghusaghnaanghitii elqughutngalleghminun qaatkutellghitgun Liilightuusanun . Itupill Liilightuusat liitestii yuget seghleghqestenguniluki .
Iwernga Kiyaghneghem yuget liigikestii nallghusaghlleqniluki elqughutngalleghminun , nakaan qaatkutellghitgun Liilightuusanun . Kiyaghneghem aapqaqaa taana Liilightuusatgunllu , uuknaliqistetgunllu .
Kiyaghneghem yuget nallghusaqaqii elqughutngalleghminun ugpeqillghitgun Jesus Christ-akun . Taana ipanguuq tamaghhaanun ugpelghiinun Christ-akun qayughllak allakunneghitut
qamaglluteng seghleghqegkaatmeggneng . Enkaam nuughhutkaagut Kiyaghneghem aangelleghllaganun .
Iwernga Kiyaghneghem akingilngughqun tunusamikun nallghusaqaqii elqughutngalleghminun itemutistengitgun , Christ Jesus-kun .
Kiyaghneghem tuunegkaqaa Jesus aghqutnguluku seghleghqelleghnun . Enkaam Jesus-em aawakun seghevutaqii yuget seghleghqellghit ugpeqingalghiit ellngakun . Tawaten liigikestekaqaa elqughutnganiluni . Sivunghani agani Kiyaghneghem nuqetutkaqii yuget enkaam nepiighutkaqii seghleghqellghit .
