Iwernga uumi pilleghmi ipapighqaa elqughutnganiluni nallghusalleghmikun alngunak yuuk elqughutngalleghminun apalluqluki ugpeqillghit Jesus-kun .
Enkaam sangaawa qukaayugutkesaghqaghput ? Qukaayugutkaghqiitukut ! Qukaayuggnaanghitestaa qayughllak qaatkennaqutkegkeput Liilightuusat ? Nakaa , qayughllak Kiyaghneghem nallghusaqangi yuget elqughutngalleghminun ugpeqillghitgun Jesus-kun , nakaan qaatkutellghitgun Liilightuusanun .
Enkaam liigikaghput yuuk nallghusaqaaguq Kiyaghneghem elqughutngallghanun ugpeqilleghqun , nakaan qaatkutelleghqun Liilightuusanun .
Kiyaghneq Jews-nginaghhaat Kiyaghneqatguu ? Gentile-etlu Kiyaghneqenghitatguu ? Aa-a , Gentile-etlu Kiyaghneqaat ,
ataasighhaatanganeng Kiyaghneq . Enkaam nallghusaghlleqii Jews-et elqughutngalleghminun ugpeqillghitgun , Gentile-etlu ugpeqillghitgun .
Liilightuusaat satngunanighqestekii ugpeqillemteggun ? Nakaa ! Yeghlegillu ! Ugpeqillemta qaatkesugtestaqii Liilightuusat qelghutkiit .
Sameng始ngam pilleqesta Abraham-emeng , sivunemnneng whangkuta Jews-eni ? Sameng liitkaawa ?
Kiyaghneghem nallghusaqaqngukagu elqughutngalleghminun sallghakun , sameng qukaayugusighqalgunayaghtuq . Iwernga Kiyaghneghmun qukaayugutkepagningitii salleni .
Akuzitni Igaqegkani igaqngaaq whaten , " Abraham-em ugpeqegkaqaa Kiyaghneq enkaam ugpeqillgha apalluqluku Kiyaghneghem tugukliqaqaa elqughutngalghiinguluku . "
Yuuk qepghalleghmineng akileghtuusangegkayuguuq . Akileghtuusaa tunusaanghituq qayughllak ellngan allgeghtekaqaa qepghaalluku .
Kiyaghneghem nallghusaghnaanghitaa yuuk elqughutngalleghminun qepghaatillghakun ellminun . Itupill yugem neghyuksaghqaqaa Kiyaghneq nallghusaghikayuk seghleghqesteneng elqughutngalleghminun ugpeqillghitgun .
Umiilgem David-em igaqegkaqaa taana ataasiq . Pikaaguq yuget quyastepikaaniluki Kiyaghneghem nallghusaghaqngaki elqughutngalleghminun avelghaghluki qepghaatillghit Kiyaghneghmun .
" Quyastekaagut tamaakut seghleghqellghit Kiyaghneghem seghevutkii , anaggutellghit saapegkii !
Quyastekaaguq yuuk seghleghqellghi Atanghem sumeghmiknaniqangi . "
Taana quyastelleq David-em akuzitkegkaa , circumcise-ekaghhiinaghnun pingwaa ? Nakaa ! Circumcise-ellghilngughnunllu pinguuq . Akuzitni Igaqegkani igaqngaaq , " Abraham-em ugpeqegkaqaa Kiyaghneq , enkaam ugpeqillgha apalluqluku Kiyaghneghem tugukliqaqaa elqughutngaluku . "
Qavngaq Kiyaghneghem tugukliqaqagu ? Sivungani circumcise-ellghaan nalighmeng kingunganeng ? Sivungani circumcise-ellghan , nakaan kingunganeng .
Tagtalmi taakwani Abraham circumcise-ekaaguq . Circumcise-ellgha nalluniilkutaaguq ipapighqusiiluni Kiyaghneghem nallghusaqaqegkanga elqughutngalleghminun ugpeqillghakun . Salin circumcise-ellghilluku Kiyaghneghem tugukliqaqaa elqughutngaluku . Tamaaken apalluqluku Abraham atanguuq tamaghhaanun ugpeqilghiinun circumcise-ellghiteghngaata , enkaam Kiyaghneghem tugukliimii elqughutngaluki .
Abraham-llu atakaat circumcise-ekat . Taana ipanguuq taawanginaghhaq ugpeqillelgukuyeng Abraham-etun , salin circumcise-ellghilluku .
Kiyaghneghem akeqegkaqii Abraham-enkut kingunqullghiit iingunaghhaan nuna ellngitnun pagilleqniluku . Akequsaqellghitaa taana Abraham-emun qayughllak qaatkegkangi Liilightuusat . Itupill Kiyaghneghem akeqegkaqaa qayughllak ugpeqegkanga enkaam Kiyaghneghem tugukliqaqaa elqughutngaluku .
Kiyaghneghem akequsaa tuunyaghqaayaqan qaatkullghiinun Liilightuusanun , taawa ugpeqilleq satngunghituq . Kiyaghneghemllu akequsaa satngunghituq .
Kiyaghneq sakritaquq yuget qaatkunneghinneghata Liilightuusanun tuunegkaanun Moses-mun . Iwernga Liilightuusiisaqan taawa yuget qaatkunneghitusiinnayaghtut .
Tamaaken apalluqluku ugpeqilleghmegteggun yuget allgeghtaat Kiyaghneghem akequsaa akingilnguuluku tunusaq . Enkaam qamaglluteng Abraham-em kingunghita allgeghtepestaaghlleqaat Kiyaghneghem akequsaa . Taana akequsaq Jews-nginaghhaghnun ayuqenghituq Liilightuusalegnun . Iwernga ugpeqilghiinunllu ayuquq Abraham-em ugpeqillghatun . Enkaam Abraham qamaglluta atakaghput ugpeqilghiini .
Akuzitni Igaqegkani igaqngaaq , " Atangughtestamken uglapiglleghhiinun nunat yugitnun . " Kiyaghneghem tawaten akeqegkaqaa Abraham qayughllak ugpeqegkanga Kiyaghneq . Kiyaghneghuuq tuqukaneng unguvaghtikayuk , qelghilleghmikunllu ulimatkayuk sameng sangilngughmeng .
Abraham-em avaqutilleghqaa sighimaniitkaaguq . Iwernga ugpeqegkaqaa Kiyaghneq , sighimakumanginaqaqaallu . Enkaam atangughtekaaguq uglaapiglleghhiinun nunat yugitnun . Whaten Kiyaghneghem pikaqaa , " Kinguneghten kestepagningisaghqaagut . "
Abraham-em nulighha , Sarah , qumingepagningitkaalghii . Ellnga Abraham 100 ayumiqulleghtutkalighyaghtughluni , tuqumun tughaaghulghii . Iwernga tamaakut suumqeghngaaghmiki , ugpeqillgha Kiyaghneghmun ukavaamangilnguq .
Ugpeqinaniimangituq talwa aygughikumangitaa Kiyaghneghem akequsaa . Iwernga ugpeqiighataghaqaq , usuqegkaallu Kiyaghneq .
Abraham-em ipapighqutkengngwaaqaqaa Kiyaghneghmun piyaghqaqniluku akequsaqegkani .
Akuzitni Igaqegkani igaqngaaq , " Kiyaghneghem tuguqliqaqaa elqughutngaluku , " apalluqluku ugpeqillgha .
Taakut akuzitet , " Kiyaghneghem tuguqliqaqaa elqughutngaluku , " igaqegkaagut nakaan Abraham-nginaghmun ,
iwernga igaqegkaagut whangkunnunllu . Kiyaghneghem tuguklighlleqiinkut elqughutngaluta qayughllak ugpeqegkefut ellnga . Ellnganguuq Jesus-meng Atanemnneng unguvaghtestikaq .
Kiyaghneghem tuunegkaqaa Jesus tuqumatkesqelluki seghleghqelleput , unguvaghtekaqaallu nallghusaghnaluta elqughutngalleghminun .
Tamaaken apalluqluku nallghusaqaatemnneng Kiyaghneghem elqughutngallghanun ugpeqillemteggun , nekeggmellelguukut Kiyaghneghmi Atanemteggun Jesus Christ-akun .
Apalluqluku ugpeqilleghput Jesus-em kiyaghtestiinkut Kiyaghneghem piniqellghani . Enkaam quyaghllaguukut qayughllak liisimakngwaaghaghput Kiyaghneghem nengightesleqiinkut nighughqelleghmineng .
Taam saaghwakun quyaaqukut seghleliillemnni qayughllak liisimakaghput seghleliillghem nuqenneghtullengestaqiinkut .
Nuqenneghtullemteggun Kiyaghneghem itagnaqaqiinkut . Itagnaqillghan sighimallengestaqiinkut .
Taam sighimallghem iilqamiqnaanghitiinkut qayughllak Kiyaghneghem kuuvegkaqaa piniqelleni qamavek ilumnnun Agleghnalghiignekun Taghneghagnekun , Kiyaghneghem tuunegkamikun whangkunnun .
Yugulipagningilluta Christ-am tuqumatkegkaqii seghleghqestet , tawani pilleghqaghlluwaaghmi Kiyaghneghem nakmikegkaani .
Entaqun qafsinkuuraghhiinaat tuqumatkiyugnayaghtut elqughutngalghiimun yugmun . Nalighmeng entaqun kina tuqumatkiyugnayaghtuq pinilghiimun yugmun .
Iwernga Kiyaghneghem kelgutkaqaa piniqelleni whangkunnun , paninang seghleghqestenguluta Christ-am tuqumatkegkaqiinkut !
Nalluneqniighaghput Kiyaghneghem nallghusaamiinkut elqughutngalleghminun Christ-am aawakun . Nalluneqniighataghaghaghput yugulillengellequkut Christ-akun Kiyaghneghem sakraallghaneng .
Whangkuta Kiyaghneghem anguyaksaghiinkut , iwernga ilaliiqaqiinkut tuqullghakun Ighneghmi . Maaten Kiyaghneghem ilakumtaaqiinkut , enkaam nalluneqniighataghaghaghput yugulillengellequkut Christ-am unguvallghakun !
Taam saaghwakun , quyaghllaguukut Kiyaghneghmi Atanemteggun Jesus Christ-akun . Ellnganguuq whangkunnun ilaliighutestilghii Kiyaghneghmun .
Yuksuwhaaq , Adam , seghleghqaqngan , seghleghqellghan tuqulleq iteghtestekaqaa nunamun . Enkaam qamaglluni yuuk tuquyaghqaaguq qayughllak qamaglluni seghleghqegkaaguq .
Seghleghqellelgukaaguq nunami salin Kiyaghneghem tuunellghilluki Liilightuusat Moses-mun . Iwernga Kiyaghneghem nanqigtellghitii yuget aghyuughyaghqaaluki seghleghqellghitnun qayughllak Liilightusiilnguq .
Paninang yuget kiyaghtekaagut ima Adam-emeng Moses-mun , qamaglluteng tuquyaghqaagut , maligulluteng tamaakut seghleghqellghit Adam-em seghleghqellghatun ayuqenghilnguut . Adam Christ-atun ayuquq , tagiyaghqatun .
Iwernga Kiyaghneghem tunusaa Adam-em seghleghqellghatun ayuqenghituq . Ipanguuq uglapiglleghhiit yuget tuqukaagut apalluqluku ataasim yugem seghleghqellgha . Iwernga Kiyaghneghem piniqellgha seghleghllaguuq . Enkaam uglaapiglleghhiit yuget allgeghtekaqaat Kiyaghneghem aqeghqengngalghii akingilnguq tunusaa , piniqellghakun ataasim yugem Jesus Christ-am .
Allakuteghllagtuk , Adam-em seghleghqellghallu , tunusaallu Kiyaghneghem . Kingunganeng Adam seghleghqaqngan Kiyaghneghem nanqigtekaqaa aghyuughyaghqaaluku . Iwernga kingungitneng yulghuteghllaget seghleghqaqngata , Kiyaghneghem akingilngughqun tunusamikun nallghusaghtestekaqii elqughutngalleghminun .
Ataasiq yuuk seghleghqegkaaguq enkaam ellnga apalluqluku , tuqullghem igleghutii qamaglluki yuget . Iwernga sangwaa Kiyaghneghem apeghiiqaa ataasikun yugkun , Jesus Christ-akun , aangataghaghtuq seghleghqellghaneng ataasim yugem . Enkaam allgeghullghiit Kiyaghneghem kemnapiglleghhiimeng piniqellghaneng , tunusaanengllu elqughutngallghaneng , qamaglluteng igleghutillequt kiyaghtelleghmi ataasikun yugkun Jesus Christ-akun .
Apalluqluku Adam-em ataasiq seghleghqellgha , Kiyaghneghem nanqigtekaqii qamaglluki yuget aghyuughyaghqaaluki . Tawateghpigaq apalluqluku Christ-am ataasiq elqughutngalghii pillgha Kiyaghneghem nallghusaghii qamaglluki yuget elqughutngalleghminun , tuuniillu unguvalleghmeng .
Qaatkunneghitellghakun ataasim yugem , uglaapiglleghhiit yuget seghleghqestengughtekaagut . Tawateghpigaq , qaatkutellghakun ataasim yugem , uglaapiglleghhiit yuget nallghusaghyaghqaagut Kiyaghneghem elqughutngallghanun .
Liilightuusat Kiyaghneghem tuunegkii Moses-mun yuget liisaaghaghtestiit seghleghqelleghmeng . Iwernga yuget seghleghqataghaghyata Kiyaghneghem nangllegtallgha nulanginaqaq .
Seghleghqellghem igleghutkaqii yuget tuqulleghqun . Iwernga Kiyaghneghem piniqellghan igleghutngwii yuget nallghusalleghmikun ellngit elqughutngalleghminun . Enkaam allgeghtaat kenlengilnguq unguvalleq Jesus Christ-akun Atanemteggun .
Sameng始ngam pilleqesta ? Seghleghqumanginaaltaa-a Kiyaghneghem nangllegtallgha nulasqelluku ?
Nakaa ! Qayughllak tuqukastun ayuqukut , enkaam tuqukaakumta naten seghleghqumanginaghnaqesta ?
Liisimakaghsi , qamaglluta paaptaayaaqngamta ilatkaagukut Christ Jesus-mun . Ilatkaagutkutlu tuqullghanun paaptaayaaqngamta .
Paaptaayellemteggun tuquqaagukutlu qungukaagukutlu Christ-ami . Aghtughyaghqaanghilleghllagmikun Atam unguvaghtekaqaa Christ-a tuqulleghmeng . Enkaam kiyaghsaghqaaghllequkut kiyaghtaallelighraghaghluta .
Kiyaghneghem ilasimakanginkut Christ-amun tuqullghakun , taagken ilatestepestaaghlleqiinkutlu ellnganun unguvaghtesluta ellngatun .
Liisimakaghput whangkuteluguyalghiit qaquuraatkaagut Christ-akun igleqataqnaniisqelluta seghleghqellghem aghtughyaghqaanghillghanun , qepghaghtelaaghunanighnalutallu seghleghqelleghmun .
Yuuk tuquneghmini itemaquq aghtughyaghqaanghillghaneng seghleghqellghem .
Tuqumakumta Christ-ami , ugpeqaghput kiyaghtelgusighyaghqaqaghputlu ellnga .
Liisimakaghput Christ-a unguvaghtestekaaguq tuqulleghmeng enkaam allamengllu tuquyaghqaanghituq qayughllak tuqulleq aghtughyaghqaanghillghiitkaaguq ellnganun .
Ataasighhaghmeng tuqukaaguq kayaalqennaluku seghleghqelleq . Iwernga unguvatmineng , kiyaghtengnguuq Kiyaghneghmun .
Tawateghpigaq sumeghtaghaghtek tuqukaalusi seghleghqellghem aghtughyaghqaanghillghanun , sumeghtaghaghteklu unguvangulusi Kiyaghneghmun Christ Jesus-kun .
Tamaaken apalluqluku seghleghqelleghmun igleqataqestegpenaki yugusisi tuqukayuget . Seghleghqellghem igleqataqegkaki yugusisi , qaatkesuglleqasi yugusighpesi seghleghqengngalghiit piyukellghi .
Alngunak nalighneghi yugusighpesi tuunegpenaki seghleghqusiiluki , qayughllak tawaten pikufsi tuunelleqasi seghleghmun . Itupill tuunitek Kiyaghneghmun . Tuqukastun ayuqsaghtusi , iwernga Kiyaghneghem unguvaghtekaqiisi . Enkaam tuuniteki iinguniita yugusisi Kiyaghneghmun ellnganun atuqesqelluki elqughutngalleghmun .
Seghleghqellghem igleqataqnaanghitiisi qayughllak igleqataqngwiisi Kiyaghneghem piniqellghan ; igleqataqngunghitiisi Liilightuusat .
Enkaam sanaqestangam ? Itagnaghtaa-a seghleghqelleghqaghput qayughllak Kiyaghneghem piniqellghan igleqataqngukanginkut nakaan Liilightuusat ? Nakaa , itagnanghituq !
Liisimakaqusi tuunegkufsi kitumun qaatkesaghqaaluku , taawa ellngan qepghaghtelaaqaaghlleqiisi . Qaatkegkufsigu seghleghqelleq , tuqusleqiisi . Iwernga qaatkegkufsigu Kiyaghneq , nallghusaghlleqiisi elqughutngalleghminun .
Qepghaghtelaaghuyaghtusi seghleghqelleghmun . Iwernga iyamsiqayugvikaqa Kiyaghneq qayughllak maaten qamakerugllak qaatkegkesi apeghtuusaghraghaat apeghtuusaqegkat elpesinun .
Itemutkaagusi seghleghqelleghmeng enkaam qepghaghtelaaghughtekaagusi elqughutngalleghmun .
Tamaakut liigikneghllugutangitneng elpesinun , usputaqngwaanka qepghaghtelaaghetlu piliitestengitlu . Sivunghani tuunegkayuguyaghasi yugusisi qepghaghtelaaghuluki nukeggnalghiinunllu nulamanginalghiinunllu seghletun pilleghnun . Maaten tuuniteki yugusisi qepghaghtelaaghuluki elqughutngalleghmun kiyaghtesqellusi pelungillusi .
Qepghaghtelaaghwaaqngafsi seghleghqelleghmun , elqughutngallghem igleqataqellghitiisi .
Sivunghani seghletun pikaagusi , iwernga maaten kayngukaaghtasi tamaakut seghletun pikasi . Sangaawa allgeghtekaghsi tamaakut piluki ? Allgeghtekaqaghsi tuqullghiinaghhaq .
Iwernga maaten itemullusi seghleghqelleghmeng qepghaghtelaaghughtekaagusi Kiyaghneghmun . Enkaam Kiyaghneghem pelungiightesimiisi , allgeghutesimiisillu kenlengilngughmeng unguvalleghmeng .
Akileghtuusaa seghleghqellghem tuqullghuuq ; iwernga Kiyaghneghem akingilnguq tunusaa kenlengilnguuguq unguvalleq Christ Jesus-kun Atanemteggun .
Ugpeqaalgutemni , lataamsi liisimakilghiini Liilightuusaneng . Enkaam liigikasi Liilightuusat qelghaqiit yuget kiyaghtengnguluki .
Ugiiqaq aghnaq usputaaguq . Liilightuusam qelellghani aghnaq ugiminisaghqaaguq tagtalngatun ugimi kiyaghtellghan . Iwernga tuqukan ugini , taawa itemellequq Liilightuusaaneng nengughtellghem .
Iwernga , ugini unguvaluku allami yugmi kiyaghtekumi gelgaghniightenguluni atighyaghqaaguq . Iwernga uginga tuqumakan , itemellequq taagken Liilightuusameng . Gelgaghniighunghituq ugiinqigtekumi .
Ugpeqaalgutemni , elpesillu itemumaasi Liilightuusaneng qayughllak tuqukaagusi Christ-ami . Tamaaken apalluqluku Christ-am pikiisi . Ellnganguuq Kiyaghneghem unguvaghtekaa tuqulleghmeng , whangkunnun qepghaatesqelluku Kiyaghneq .
Sivunghani qaatkaqaput seghleghqengngalghiit piyukellghi yugusimta . Liilightuusat atuqistesugaqiinkut tamaakuneng . Enkaam atuqegkumteki tuqusleqiinkut .
Sivunghani anusimingllaghastun ayuqsaghtukut Liilightuusanun . Tuqukaatemnneng Christ-ami , itemutkaagukut qaatkusaghqaallemnneng Liilightuusanun . Enkaam qepghaatngwaaghput Kiyaghneq unguvalleghraghamteggun Taghneghagnekun , nakaan unguvallelumteggun Liilightuusatgun .
Sameng始ngam pilleqesta ? Liilightuusaat seghleghqellghwaat ? Yeghlegillu ! Taakut Liilightuusat liitestekaqii whangamnun seghleghqellghet sangutangi . Liinnayanghitaqa qiliiqetiqelleq sangutanga Liilightuusaq whaten qelghimangisaqan , " Qiliiqetiqegpenang . "
Iwernga atuqluku taana qelghusaq , seghleghqellghem allaaghhiinaghneng qiliiqetangllaqaqaanga . Liilightuusangunateng seghleghqellghet tuqungaat .
Sivunghani kiyaghtengnguyaghtunga Liilightuusangunaan ; iwernga liisaqegka taana qelghusaq , seghleghqelleq unguvaghluni enkaam tuquunga .
Qelghusaq unguvastiyaghqaayalghii whangamnun , yeghlegi tuqustaanga .
Taaggun qelghusakun , seghleghqellghem puughsaqlegughtaanga . Enkaam atuqluku qelghusaq seghleghqellghem tuqutaanga .
Iwernga Liilightuusat agleghnalghiinguut , qelghusaqlu agleghnalghiinguuq , elqughutngaaqlu , pinightuqlu .
Taam qelghusam pinilghiim , tuqustangaa ? Yeghlegillu ! Seghleghqellghem tuqutaanga atuqluku sangwaa pinilghii . Enkaam liitaghput qelghusakun seghleghqelleq elngaatall seghlepiguuq .
Liisimakaput Liilightuusat Kiyaghneghem Taghneghaaneng pinguut , iwernga maghyaghquunghitaanga Taghnegham . Maghyaghquungwaanga yugusima piyukellghan , enkaam qepghaghtelaaghuunga seghleghqelleghmun .
Liigikigataqa saaqutka qayughllak atuqigataqa sangwaa atuqsukaqa . Itupill atuqaqaqa sangwaa ugumikegkaqa .
Iwernga atuqegkumki ugumikegkanka atuqsunghiteghngaamki , taawa itagnaqaqanka Liilightuusat piniitangi .
Enkaam whangangunghituq tawaten piiqelghii , itupill seghleghqelleq ilumnilnguq tawaten piiquq .
Liisimakaqa avangitunga pinilghiimeng ilumni , yugusimni . Pinitun piyugaqsaghngaaghma , pipagningitaqa .
Pingigataqa pinilghii piyukegkaqa , yeghlegi seghleq piiqaqa piyukenghitkaqa .
Enkaam piyukenghitkaqa pinemkun , taawa whangangunghituq tawaten pilghii . Itupill seghleghqellghwaaquq ilumnilnguq tawaten piiqelghii .
Enkaam liitaqa taana : pinitun pinaqeghngaghma , paninang seghleq tawantaquq .
Qaamkerugllak pinighyuugusiqanka Kiyaghneghem Liilightuusii .
Iwernga liitaqa taawa ilanga liilightuusaq yugusimnituq . Pilluwaqangi Kiyaghneghem Liilightuusii umyugama itagnaqegkii . Liilightuusam yugusimnilnguum seghleghqestaqaanga , enkaam anusimingllaghastun ayuqunga taamun liilightuusamun .
Seghleghwaaghuunga ! Kitumngam itemulleqanga whaken yugusimeng tuqustiyaghqameng whangamneng ?
Iyamsiqanaghhalek Kiyaghneghmun itemuskanganga Jesus Christ-akun Atanemteggun ! Enkaangam qaatkanka Kiyaghneghem Liilightuusii umyugamkun , iwernga yugusimkun qaatkaqa liilightuusaq seghleghqestilghii whangamneng .
Enkaangam kinkut alngunak Christ Jesus-mun ilatkaakata Kiyaghneghem nanqiggnaanghitii aghyuughyaghqaaluki .
Qayughllak Liilightuusaan Taghnegham unguvallelitilghiim Christ Jesus-kun itemutkaqaanga liilightuusaaneng seghleghqellghemllu tuqullghemllu .
Moses-em Liilightuusii tawaten pipagningitut qayughllak yugusimta piyukellghita kayaaleghqegkaqii Liilightuusat . Iwernga Kiyaghneghem pikaqaa Liilightuusat pipagningitkaat . Kayagtekaqaa ellmi katam Ighneni nunamun seghleghqumalghiitun yugtun ayuqluku . Tuunegkaqaa Ighneni aghqutnguluku seghleghqellemnnun . Tawaten nanqigtekaqaa seghleghqelleq yugusimelluku ,
whangkunnun qaatkesaqlegughtesqelluki Liilightuusat elqughutngalghiit qelghusii . Whangkunguut kiyaghlleghhiit malighqutaqluta Taghnegham piyukellghanun , nakaan yugusimta piyukellghitnun .
Tamaakut kiyaghlleghhiit malighqutaqluteng yugusimeng piyukellghitnun , sumeghtaghaatkengnginaghaqiit piyukelleteng . Iwernga tamaakut kiyaghlleghhiit malighqutaqluteng Taghneghagnun , sumeghtaghaatkengnginaghaqiit Taghnegham piyukellghi .
Umyugaput malighqutaqegkata yugusimta piyukellghanun , tuqullequkut . Iwernga umyugaput malighqutaqegkata Taghneghagnun , Kiyaghneghem unguvallelilleqiinkutlu nekeggmellelilleqiinkutlu .
Umyugaput malighqutaqenghata yugusimta piyukellghanun , anguyagwaaqukut Kiyaghneghmun qayughllak qaatkigalkeput Liilightuusii . Ipa qaatkepagningitaput Kiyaghneghem Liilightuusii .
Tamaakut malighqutaqngalghiit yugusimeng piyukellghanun efqughtepagningitaat Kiyaghneq .
Iwernga elpesi igleqataqngunghitiisi yugusighpesi piyukellghan . Igleqataqngwiisi Kiyaghneghem Taghneghagkenka , qayughllak ipa kiyaghtengngulghii ilugpesini . Christ-am Taghneghakek kiyaghtengngunghilkayek ilungani yugem , pikenghitaa Christ-am .
Yugusisi tuqunaqnguut apalluqluki seghleghqellesi . Iwernga Christ-a kiyaghtengngukan ilugpesini , taawa Taghnegham unguvallelilleqiisi , qayughllak Christ-am nallghusaghtestekaqiisi Kiyaghneghem elqughutngallghanun .
Kiyaghneghem Taghneghakek unguvaghtikak Jesus-meng , kiyaghtengnguuk ilugpesini . Katam Kiyaghneghem unguvaghtestellghatun Christ Jesus , unguvaghtesleqii yugusisi Taghneghagmikun kiyaghlleghhiignekun ilugpesini .
Enkaangam ugpeqaalgutemni , kiyaghsaghqaagukut Kiyaghneghem Taghneghagkenka kiyaghtesqesullghatun , nakaan yugusimta kiyaghtesqesullghatun .
Kiyaghtengngukufsi malighqutaqlusi yugusighpesi piyukellghanun , tuqullequsi . Iwernga Taghneghagnekun tuquskufsiki yugusighpesi seghleghqeng始ngalghiit piiqegkangit , taawa kiyaghllequsi .
Qayughllak tamaakut maghyaghquqii Kiyaghneghem Taghneghagkenka Kiyaghneghem avaqutaqii .
Taghnegham allgeghtekaghpesi Kiyaghneghmeng qepghaghtelaaghughtesneqiggnaanghitiisi alingelleghmun . Yeghlegi Taghnegham Kiyaghneghmun avaqutaqestiisi . Enkaam ellngakun tuqlughaghaghput Kiyaghneq , " Abba ! Ataay ! "
Kiyaghneghem Taghneghakek ellmegneng ilatkaaguk taghneghamnnun ungipaannaluta Kiyaghneghmun avaqutaqniluta .
Kiyaghneghem avaqutaqutanganeng , Kiyaghneghem pagitistekiinkut , Christ-amllu pagitistelgutkiinkut . Nighughqellengellequkut Christ-atun ikfiqegkumta Christ-am ikfiqellghatun .
Sumemni ikfiqelleput unguvallemnni inglutepagningitut nighughqelleghmun Kiyaghneghem aliighsaghqaanun whangkunnun .
Ulimaaq qamaglluni utaqiinguuq qelanellelighluni Kiyaghneghmun aliightesqelluki kinkungutangi avaqutii .
Kiyaghneghem nanqigtekaqaa ulimaaq aghyughyaghqaaluku enkaam atuunanightestaa . Ulimaaq nanqigtesunghitkaaguq , iwernga Kiyaghneghem tawaten piyukegkaqaa . Naqamllu paninang sighimallelguuq
qayughllak ataasimi aghneghmi Kiyaghneghem itemulleqaa ulimaaq aghulleghmeng . Taagken ulimaaq ilallequq itemngalleghllagitnun Kiyaghneghem avaqutiitnun .
Liisimakaghput whavemun kenlanga iingunaghmi ulimaaq ngillegtengnguuq aqnighqellghatun ighniyulghiim .
Iwernga ulimaaghhiinaanghituq ngilleglleghhii , whangkutallu ngillegtengnguukut . Whangkunguukut Agleghnalghiigneng Taghneghagneng pilegni Kiyaghneghem tunusaqsugwhaagha whangkunnun . Ngillegtengnguukutlu ilumteggun utaqiimaluta Kiyaghneghmun allughqisqelluta avaqutaaluta ellnganun , itemutesqellukillu yugusiput seghleghqelleghmeng .
Taaggun sighimalleghqun yugulikaagukut . Iwernga allgeghsimakumteggu sighimakegkaghput , taawa sighimallghunghituq . Yuget sighimangigatut sameng allgeghtengngwaaqameggneng .
Iwernga sighimamakumta sameng allgeghtekaqenghilkemnneng , utaqalleqaghput qelaneghpenaamta .
Tawateghpigaq Taghnegham kayusighaqiinkut kayaatellemnni , qayughllak nallukelghiikut naten yughalleghqaqsaqemtestun . Iwernga Taghnegham ellmineng katam yughaataqiinkut Kiyaghneghmun ngillegtelleghllagkun akuzitngunaan .
Kiyaghneghem liisimakii yuget sumeghtaghallghit . Liisimakiillu sumeghtaghallghi Taghnegham , qayughllak Taghnegham yughaatkaqii yugi Kiyaghneghem piyukellghatun ayuqluki .
Liisimakaghput Kiyaghneghem sangwaat qamaglluki qepghaghtestaqii qerngiita pinighqelleghqiitnun piniqistemi . Ellnginguut tuqluqii uspeqelleghmitun .
Tamaakunguut Kiyaghneghem nakmikekestaqii . Aaftekaqiillu Ighneghmitun lliighesqelluki . Tawaten pikaaguq Ighneni allgeghyuwhaaghumasqelluku anglegutelghutanganeng .
Enkaam Kiyaghneghem aaftekani tuqluqaqii . Tamaakutlu tuqluqani nallghusaqaqii elqughutngalleghminun . Tamaakutlu nallghusaqani elqughutngalleghminun quulvaqaqii .
Sameng始ngam pinaqesteggu una ? Kiyaghneq whangkunnun ayuqngukan , kitumngam tengvimun pilleqinkut ?
Ighlekumangitaa ellmi katam Ighneni ; itupill tuunegkaqaa aghqutnguluku tamaghhamnnun ! Kiyaghneghem tuunumakanginkut Ighneghmineng , taawa ellngakun ighlegpenani tuunelleqiinkut sameng tamaghhaaneng .
Kitumngam anaggunnilleqaki Kiyaghneghem nakmikegkii yuget ? Kiyaghneghem ellmineng katam anaggutellghinnikaqii !
Kinangam pilleqa Kiyaghneghem yugi nanqigsaghqaaniluki aghyuughyaghqaaluteng ? Christ Jesus-em pilleqaguu ? Nakaa , qayughllak ellnganguuq tuqumatkikaq whangkunnun , unguvaghtekaaguqlu tuqulleghmeng . Maaten yughaatkaqiinkut aqumluni aghenqigneghani Kiyaghneghem .
Saamngam iqitesleqinkut piniqellghaneng Christ-am ? Seghleliillghaam , piyaqliillghaam , amyuqetaatkellghaam , paneghniqellghaam , aklumallghaam , yakughnaam , nalighmeng tuqutellghaam ?
Igaqngaaq Akuzitni Igaqegkani whaten , " Elpek apalluqluten aghhutanga tamaghhaan yuget tuqusugaqiinkut . Sumeghtaghalleghmeggni penniighestun ayuqniiqiinkut tuqusaghqat . "
Iwernga tamaakut qamaglluki kayaalqengngwaaqaqaput Christ-akun piniqistemteggun .
Liisimakngwaaghaqa saam alngunak iqitesnaanghitiinkut Kiyaghneghem piniqellghaneng : talwa tuqullghem , unguvallghem , yaqulget , nalighmeng tughneghat . Talwa sangwaa saghngaan aghneghmi nalighmeng sivumi agani , nalighmeng aghtughyaghqaanghillghet .
Talwa sangwaat qulemnni nalighmeng asimnni . Ulimaaghmi iqitestiyaghqaqraggiituq whangkunneng Kiyaghneghem piniqellghaneng Christ Jesus-kun Atanemteggun .
Apeghyukaqa elpesinun ipanguuq . Iqlengiqngunghitunga qayughllak Christ-am pikaanga , Agleghnalghiim Taghneghamllu igleghutngwaak umyugagka .
Ungipaasugamsi whaten : qivghughllaguunga qayughllak qaamggurugllak ilumkun naangigalngughmeng aqnighqutkeghllagwaanka
yulgutenka , Jews-et . Piyaqleguyaqan , ellngit apalluqluki Kiyaghneghemtuq nanqigtekanganga aghyuughnalunga , iqitestekangangallu Christ-ameng .
Yulgutenka Israel-em kingunqii , Kiyaghneghem allughqikaqii ellminun avaqutaaluki . Aliightekaqaa nighughqelleni ellngitnun . Akequuqaqii salleghqamineng ellngitnun . Tuunegkaqii Liilightuusamineng . Apeghtuqaqii ellminun maniguutelleghqameng elqughulluki . Akequuqaqiillu quyasleqniluki qaatkegkangatni .
Kingunqiit sivuneqsuwhaamta , taakutgun kinguneghteggun Christ-a allgeqaaguq yuguluni . Ellnga Kiyaghneghuuq igleghutilghii sameng tamaghhaaneng . Usuqellengi quunperugllak kenlengunaan ! Amen .
Kiyaghneghaam akequsani pimangitaguu Israel-eghmiinun ? Nakaa ! Akequsani pikaqaa ellngitnun , iwernga ilanginaghhii kingunghi Israel-em Israel-eghmiipiguut .
Ilanginaghhiillu Abraham-em kingunghi ellngan avaqutapiikii . Kiyaghneghem pikaqaa Abraham whaten , " Kingunghet elpenun akequsanka Isaac-ekun ayuqsaghqaagut . "
Taana whaten pisiiguq , ilangi avaqutat allgeqat Abraham-emun avaqutaqenghitii Kiyaghneghem . Iwernga allgeqaghhiinaat Kiyaghneghem akequsaakun Abraham-emun kingunepiikii Abraham-em .
Kiyaghneghem akequsaa Abraham-emun whatetuq , " Ayumiqun uteghniquma whaten lliiqan Sarah ighnengellequq . "
Taana Sarah-m ighnegha Isaac-nguuq , sivuneghput . Nulightughluni Rebecca-meng , atakaak malghik ighneghegkenka Rebecca-m .
Talwa salin allgellghillukek , salinllu pingigallukek pinilghiimeng nalighmeng seghleghmeng , Kiyaghneghem pikaqaa Rebecca , " Nuyekliim qepghaalleqaa uyuqliq . " Ataneq tawaten pikaaguq liigikesqelluku ellnginaghmi nakmiightenguniluni salleghqamineng . Kiyaghneghem nakmikegkaqaa taana ighneq qayughllak ellnganguuq Kiyaghneghem tuqlughyukaa . Nakmikegkaqenghitaa qayughllak taam ighneghem sangwaa pikaqutanganeng .
Akuzitni Igaqegkani igaqegkaalghii , " Piniqegkaqaqa Jacob , naqam ugumikegkaqaqa Esau . "
Sameng始ngam pinaqesteggu taana ? Kiyaghneq anaggutaa ? Yeghlegillu !
Qayughllak Moses whaten pikaqaa , " Nangllegtaghllequnga kitumun alngunak nanglleqsaghqamnun ; nafughtaghllequnga kitumun alngunak nafuqsaghqamnun . "
Enkaangam yuget allgeghtepagningitaat Kiyaghneghem nangllegtallgha piyukluku nalighmeng salleghmegteggun . Kiyaghneghhiinaaguq nakmiighyaghqaq nanglleksaghqaminun .
Akuzitni Igakegkani igaqngaaq Kiyaghneghem pikaqaa Pharaoh whaten , " Umiilgughtestekaqamken kelgunnaluku aghtughyaghqaanghilqa elpegun . Enkaam yuget nunataghhaani tamaghhaani ungipaqelleqaat aatqa . "
Enkaam Kiyaghneghem nangllegyagutkayugaa kina alngunak piyukegkani , pineghlluugtestaqaallu kina alngunak piyukegkani .
Enkaam aapleqaghpenga whaten , " Kiyaghneq tawatetngukan , sangan始ngam nanqiglleqaki kinkut alngunak aghyuughyaghqaaluki ? Kitum alngunak aygiinaghyaghqaqenghitaa Kiyaghneghem piyukellgha . "
Iwernga kinanguzin , yugmi , veghusnaasken Kiyaghneq ? Qikumeng ulimaaghem sagneghem aapsigataa ulimasteni whaten , " Sangama whatellunga ulimazinga ? "
Yugem qikumeng sagnengllaghtem piyukelleghmitun atuqsaghqaqaa qiku . Ulimayukumikek maalghuk ataasimeng qikumeng piyaghqaqaak , aallgha megnunalghiimun atuuluku , ilanga samun alngunak atuuluku .
Kiyaghneghem kelgusukaqaa ugumiyulleghllani , liisimakesugaallu aghtughyaghqaanghilleni . Iwernga nuqetunneghpakaqii nanqigtekani naafqennaluki .
Tawaten pikaaguq liisimakesqelluku nighughqelleghllani nangllekegkaminun . Yataaghqekestaqaqii ellngitnun allgeghtesqelluku nighughqelleni .
Talwa whangkutallu tuqluqaqiinkut , nakaan Jew-nginaghneng iwernga Gentile-enengllu .
Hosea-m uuknaliqellghani Kiyaghneq pikaaguq whaten Gentile-eneng , " Tamaakut yukenghilkenka , atighlleqanka , ' Yugenka ' . Tamaakut yuget piniqenghilkenka , atighlleqanka , ' Piniqegkanka ' .
Tawani Kiyaghneghem ungipaatfigitni , ' Yukenghitamsi ' , tawanillu atighlleqiit , ' Avaqutii unguvalghiim Kiyaghneghem . ' "
Isaiah-m akilghuutkegkaqaa Israel whaten , " Qaywa Israel-eghmiit esnem qenaavzeghaatun uglaghtatkalighngaata , tawalliima qafsinkuuraghhaat yugulillengyaghqaagut ,
qayughllak Atanghem kimaawillngunani nanqigtengngwaaghlleqii nunam yugi . "
Sivunghani Isaiah-m pinaqnillghatun ayuquq , " Atanghem aghtughyaghqaghhaanghilnguum siipusimangisaqanginkut kinguneghmeng , qamagtengngwaaghluta naafqellengnayaghtukut Sodom-enkuk Gomorrah-nkuk neghllagegketun . "
Sameng始ngam pilleqesta ? Gentile-et , ellmeggneng nallghusaghnaqutkumangitut Kiyaghneghmun , iwernga Kiyaghneghem nallghusaqaqii elqughutngalleghminun apalluqluku ugpeqillghat .
Israel-eghmiit malighqutaqnaqutkegkaagut Liilightuusanun elqughutnganaluteng Kiyaghneghmun , iwernga pilaataqumangitut .
Sangameng pilaataqunghitat ? Qayughllak nallghusaghnaqutkelghiit ellmeggneng Kiyaghneghmun salleghmegteggun , neghyukegpenaan Kiyaghneghmun nallghusiisqelluteng elqughutngallghanun . Enkaam naagtaqut " naagtusikun uyghagkun . "
Igaqegkaalghii Akuzitni Igaqegkani whaten : " Ii-i , Zion-mi nekegtaqa uyghak yuget naagtesqelluki , taam uyghagem iqusleqii . Iwernga kina alngunak ugpequmi ellngakun kaynguyugnaanghituq . "
Ugpeqaalgutemni , qamagun ilumkun piyukepigtaqanka whanga katam yugenka Jews-et yugulillengesqelluki ! Elngaatall Kiyaghneghmun yughaatkaqanka !
Whaten piighhnaqanka yugenka : Qepghaasupigtaqaat Kiyaghneq iwernga liigikigataat naten Kiyaghneq qepghaatesugaqutni ellngitnun .
Liigikellghitaat naten Kiyaghneghem nallghusaghaqutangi yuget elqughutngalleghminun . Enkaam elqughutngangllaghnaqutkaqut qaatkelluki Liilightuusii . Tawaten pilleghmegteggun tugukliigataat Kiyaghneghem elqughutngallgha .
Christ-a kenlekaat Liilightuusat . Enkaam tamaghhaghmi ugpeqillelek Kiyaghneghem nallghusaghlleqaa elqughutngalleghminun .
Moses igaqaaguq Kiyaghneghmeng nallghusaghilghiimeng yugneng elqughutngalleghminun qaatkutellghitgun Liilightuusanun . Whaten igaqegkaqaa , " Yugem qaatkumakaki Liilightuusat , taakutgun kiyaghllequq . "
Iwernga nallghusaqaq Kiyaghneghem elqughutngallghanun ugpeqilleghqun , qelqaaguq , " Aaptegpenang , ' Kina mayughlleqa qilagmun ? ' " ( ukiggnaluku Christ-a nunamun ) .
Nalighmeng aaptegpenang , " Kina ukiglleqa Abyss-mun ? " ( mayuunnaluku Christ-a tuqumeng . )
Akuzitni Igaqegkani whaten igaqngaaq , " Kiyaghneghem ungipaa qantaghantuq elpenun . Akuzitkelleqan qaneghpegun , ugpeqelleqanllu ilugpegun . " ( Kiyaghneghem ungipaa ugpeqilleghmeng ayuqelghii , taananguuq ungipaqegkefut . )
Aapquvgu qaneghpeneng , " Jesus Atanghuniluku , " ilugpenengllu ugpeqegkuvgu Kiyaghneghmun unguvaghtesimaniluku tuqulleghmeng , yugulillengellequten .
Yuuk ugpeghtuq ilumikun , enkaam Kiyaghneghem nallghusaghaa elqughutngalleghminun . Aapghaallu qaneghmikun ugpeqegkani , enkaam yugulillenguq .
Akuzitni Igaqegkani igaqngaaq , " Kitum alngunak ugpeqegkumigu ellnga kaynguyugnaanghituq . "
Allangughutngitut Jews-etlu Greek-etlu qayughllak ataasiiguq Ataneq , Atanqaa tamaghhaan . Quyasteghllagaqaa tamaghhaan tuqlughilghii ellmineng .
Katam Akuzitni Igaqegkani igaqngalghii , " Tamaghaghmi tuqlughilghii aatghakun Atanghem yugulillengyaghqaaguq . "
Iwernga naten yuget tuqlughlleqatgu ugpenghilkumeng ? Naten ugpeghlleqat , nagaquunneghilkumeng ? Natenllu nagaqughlleqat ungipaqistengunateng ?
Naten yuget ungipaqilleqat ellnganeng wetku kayagtellengegkuyeng ? Katam Akuzitni Igaqegkani igaqngalghii , " Pinighnaghhaghmeng itegiit tamaakut ungipaqilghiit Pinilghiineng Ungipaneng ! "
Iwernga ilanginiita qaatkegkaqiit Pinilghiit Ungipat . Isaiah aaptekaaguq , " Ataneq , kitum ugpeqegkaqagu ungipaghput ? "
Kina alngunak ugpeqillelgunaanghituq nagategpenani ungipameng Christ-ameng ayuqelghiimeng .
Iwernga piiqsingaa Israel-eghmiit nagaquunneghinniluki ungipameng ? Aa-a , nagaqupestaaqaagut . Akuzitni Igaqegkani igaqngalghii , " Mengit aghulaqumaat tamaghhaanun nunam ; akuzitangitlu kenlengitnun nunam . "
Alla aapqughaallelguunga : Israel-eghmiit liigikenghitatkii-i Israel-eghmiingunghilnguut ellngitlu Kiyaghneghem yukatkii ? Aa-a , liigikumiit . Sivukluku Kiyaghneghem Moses whaten pistaa : " Elpesinun aqinakesnaqanka Israel-eghmiingunghilnguut . Israel-eghmiingunghilngughteggun liigikigalngughteggun ugumiyugtesnaqamsi . "
Taagken Isaiah tetugpenani aapghikaaguq whaten Kiyaghneghem pillghaneng , " Tamaakut ivaghimangilnguut whangamneng , naalkegkaqaatnga . Tamaakunun aaptinghilngughnun whangamneng , liitestekaagunga . "
Iwernga Israel-meng Kiyaghneq whatenllu pikaaguq , " Aghnelqusighllak nengugutanka iiggenka qaatkusigalngughnunllu , kipullginaalghiinunllu whangamneng . "
Enkaam aaptamsi , " Kiyaghneghaam Israel-eghmiit yuksugnanightakii ? " Yeghlegillu ! Whanga katam Israel-eghmiinguunga , Abraham-em kingungha , Benjamin-em ramkenganeng pinguunga .
Kiyaghneghem yuksugnanillghitii yuni qayughllak nakmikegkaqii salin nunangllallghilluni . Liisimakenghistegguu Akuzitni Igaqegkani Elijah-m qikeghqutkegkaqegkangi Kiyaghneghmun Israel-eghmiit ? Whaten pikaalghii ,
" Ataneq , tuququqaqiit uuknaliqisteten , ulleghquqaqiit aghqefigten ; whanganginaghhaagunga siipneq , tuqunnaqutkaqaatngallu . "
Iwernga Kiyaghneghem pikaqaa , " Paninang 7,000-meng yulguunga maniguusigalnguut kiyaghnengllaqamun Baal-mun . "
Maatenllu tawatetut . Siipnelguuq Kiyaghneghem nakmikegkaaneng nangllegtalleghmikun .
Kiyaghneq nakmiighumakumi nangllegyulleghmikun , taawa nakmikellghitii pinitun pillghitgun . Tawaten nakmikumakumiki , taawa nakmikellghitii nangllegyulleghmikun .
Whaten piiqunga : Israel-eghmiit naalkellghitaat ivaqaghteng , Kiyaghneghem nakmikegkaghhiiniita naalkegkaqaat . Ilangi tamaakut Kiyaghneghem pineghlluugtestekaqii .
Katam Akuzitni Igaqegkani igaqegkaalghii , " Kiyaghneghem umyugiit liigiksaghqaananighqegkaqii . Whavemun kenlanga aghneghmun iiyngit esghaghyaghqaananighqegkaqii , sigutngitlu nagaquusaghqaananighqegkaqii . "
David-llu pikaaguq , " Neqenghaghqellghit negaghaaghllit , naaptellghughllit , naagtusiighllit , aghyuughisiighllit ellngitnun .
Iiyngit ayaallenglit esghaghnaniisqelluki , qukiitlu pakegnenglit uqigitneng seghleliillghita quunperugllak . "
Enkaam aaptamsi , Israel-eghmiit naagtaqngameng , alla nekevepagningitaqaat ? Yeghlegillu ! Iwernga Israel-eghmiit seghleghqellghit apalluqluki , Gentile-et yugulillengut . Enkaam yugulillengellghita Israel-eghmiit aqinastiit .
Kiyaghneghem atuqegkaqii seghleghqellghit Israel-eghmiit taginnaluku quyastelleghllak nunam yuganun . Israel-eghmiit ifliillghita tagitaat quyastelleghllak Gentile-enun . Taagken qamaglluteng nakmikegkat Israel-eghmiit , ilaskumeng yugulikanun , quyastellghet natenmi uglaghtatkalleqat !
Maaten aleghqughyugamsi elpesi Gentile-eni . Kiyaghneghem nakmikegkaqaanga apostle-ngulunga Gentile-enun . Enkaam piraamsipigllunga piiqaqa una megnunalghii qepghaqaq Kiyaghneghem qelghutkaa whangamnun .
Apeghtughillemkun elpesinun aqinasnaluki piinka Jews-elgutenka , ilangi yugulillengesqelluki .
Kiyaghneghem ighsakaqngaki Jews-et , nunam yugi Jew-ngunghilnguut ilaliightestekaqii ellminun . Enkaam Jews-et tuguklinqigtekumiki , unguvaghlleghhiistun tuqukat ayuqsaghqaagut .
Neqekrangllam ikelleqsuwhaagha tuunegkaq Kiyaghneghmun , agleghnaangukan , taawa iingunaghmi neqekrangllak agleghnaghtuq . Akghwi uqfigem agleghnaqata , avayiillu agleghnaghtut .
Jews-et piitesighaqastun olive-em uqfigatun ayuqut ilangi avayaan ayemtekat . Elpesi Gentile-eni avayastun ayuqusi ayemtekat piitesighallghilngughmeng olive-em uqfiganeng . Taameng uqfigmeng , kitum tuguluku avayaq nekegtekumigu piitesighaqamun olive-em uqfiganun , allgeghusaghqaaguq akum mesaaneng piinnapiglleghhiimeng .
Sumeghtaghaghpenasi pinighataghaghnilusi avayaneng ayemtekaneng . Qukaayugtegpenasi , qayughllak avayaraaghinaagusi . Akut iknaqughtesigatasi , akuugut iknaqughsaghilghiit elpesineng .
Iwernga pillequsi , " Aa-a , avayat ayemtekaagut nekeggnaluta uqfigmun . "
Taana ipanguuq . Kiyaghneghem ayemtaqii avayat qayughllak ugpeqenghilkangat ellnga . Iwernga elpesi nekegtestekaqiisi uqfigmun qayughllak ugpeqegkesi ellnga . Enkaam qukaayugtegpenasi , yeghlegi alingitek .
Jews-et avayaghpigaagut . Kiyaghneghem ayemtekaqutanganeng avayaghpigaat , taawa elpesillu ayemlleqiisi uqfigmeng nagneghunneghilkufsigu ugpelleghsi .
Enkaam liigikaghsi Kiyaghneq nangllegtaghtuq , aghyuutapigtuqlu . Aghyuughaqii seghleghqegkat , iwernga nangllekaqiisi neghyukumanginaneghpesigu nangllegtallgha . Iwernga neghyuknaniimakufsigu elpesillu kepulleqiisi .
Jews-et ugpeqenqigtekumegteggu Kiyaghneq , nekeggneqiglleqii uqfigmun . Kiyaghneq aghtughyaghqaanghillelguuq nekeggneqigsaghqaaluki neksaqangitgun .
Elpesi Gentile-eni avayapikenghitiisi piitesighaqam olive-em uqfigan . Kiyaghneghem kepegkaqiisi piitesighallghilngughmeng olive-em uqfiganeng . Taagken nekegtekaqiisi piitesighaqamun olive-em uqfiganun , qaywa yuget nekegtingigasaghngaata uqfigmun tawatelngughmeng avayameng . Jews-et piitesighaqameng olive-em uqfiganeng pingutmeggneng , Kiyaghneghmi piyaqniitut nekeggneqigsaghqaaluki ellngita katam uqfigitnun .
Ugpeqaalgutemni , liigikesugamsi sameng qayvighsimangilngughmeng sivunghani . Apeluugusiqa elpesinun unanguuq : peghqinghuyugneghufqaafsi pisqellusi sumeghtaghalleghpesigun . Ilangita Israel-eghmiit ugpeqsugumangitaat Kiyaghneq . Tawatellequt kenlanga Kiyaghneghem nakmikegkii Gentile-et qamaglluteng tagilaghaatellghitnun ellminun .
Taagken qamaglluteng Israel-eghmiit yugulillengellequt . Akuzitni Igaqegkani igaqngalghii , " Yugulighista tagillequq Zion-meng ; iqilleqii qamaglluki seghleghet kingunghaneng Jacob-em .
Taana akequsaqaqa ellngitnun iqiskumki seghleghqellghit . "
Jews-et ighsakegkaqiit Pinilghiit Ungipat enkaam Kiyaghneghem anguyakii . Elpesi apalluqlusi Gentile-eni Kiyaghneghem atuqegkaqaa ighsakillghat quyasnalusi . Iwernga Jews-et paninang Kiyaghneghem nakmikegkaqii yuget . Piniqumanginaawii apalluqluku akequsani sivunghitnun .
Kiyaghneghem umyugagni allangughteqaghhnaanghitaak . Veghhnaanghitii tunusani , peggnaanghitiillu nakmikegkani ellminun yuguluki .
Sivunghani elpesi Gentile-eni qaatkellghitaghsi Kiyaghneq . Iwernga maaten allgeghtaghsi Kiyaghneghem nangllegtallgha qayughllak Jews-et qaatkunneghilnguut .
Maaten Jews-et qaatkusigatut Kiyaghneghmun , enkaam nangllekaqiisi Gentile-eni . Iwernga ilangani aghneghem ellngitallu allgeghlleqaat Kiyaghneghem nangllegtallgha .
Qamagtengngwaaghluteng yuget qaatkigataat Kiyaghneq . Qaatkunneghitellghat anusimingllaghvigtun ayuquq , Kiyaghneghem tawavek kanaghtaqegkangi . Tawaten piiquq nanglleknaluki qamaglluki .
Kaay , seghleghllaguut Kiyaghneghem aklungingi , peghqinellgha , liisimallghallu ! Kitumngam liigikngwaaghlleqaki nanqigtillghi ? Kitumngam liigikngwaaghlleqaki igleghneghi ?
Katam Akuzitni Igaqegkani igaqngalghii , " Kitum liisimakakek umyugakek Atanghem ? Kitumngam aleghqughlleqagu apaqunnaluku ?
Kitum alngunak salisigataguu-u Ataneq , Ataneghmun llivikesqelluku uteghmun ? "
Sangwaa qamaglluni ellnganeng pinguuq , ellngakun pinguuq , ellnganunllu pinguuq . Ellnga usuqellengli quunperugllak ! Amen .
Ugpeqaalgutemni , Kiyaghneq nangllegtapigtutanganeng , elngaatall kayemamsi tuunesqelluki yugusisi Kiyaghneghmun unguvalghiinguluki aghqutet . Pelungillit , tuguklighyugnaghlitlu Kiyaghneghmun . Taananguuq maniguutellepigsi .
Uum nunam yugatun kiyaghtegpenasi . Yeghlegi Kiyaghneghmun allangughtestek nutaghtesluki umyugasi . Taagken liigikelleqaghsi piyukellgha Kiyaghneghem pinilghii , tuguklighyugnalghii , qamagtiingwaaghngalghiillu .
Kiyaghneghem tuunegkaqutanganeng tunusameng apostle-ngulunga , tamaghhaghpesinun piinga : Sumeghtaghaatkegpenasi elpesineng pinighataghaghnilusi ayuqelleghpesineng . Yeghlegi ipapighqellusi sumeghtaghaatkaqitek ugpeqilleghtulegpesigun Kiyaghneghem tuunegkaakun elpesinun .
Yugusiput nalighneghtupigtut , tamaghaghmi nalighneq allatun sayaghqaaguq .
Uglaghyaghngaamta , ataasigukut Christ-am yugusiini . Enkaam whangkuta nalighneghni whangkunneng pikutukut .
Qamaglluta allakullghiineng tunusalguukut Kiyaghneghem tuunegkaaneng nangllegtalleghmikun . Tunusaghput ungipaqingukan Kiyaghneghem ungipaaneng , ungipaqilta ugpeqilleghtutalemtestun .
Tunusaghput qepghaatingukan , qepghaatilta , apeghtughingukan , apeghtughilta ;
kayemingukan ilameng , kayemilta ; tuuningukan , ighlegpenaamta tuunilta ; igleghutingukan , sagiqluta igleghutilta ; nangllekingukan , quyakusiqluku nangllekilta .
Piniqitek ipapighqellusi . Ugumikluku seghleq , piyukumanginaghteggu sangwaa pinilghii .
Piniqututek anglegutkullghiistun . Quulvaatutaqitek pakiggulluku quulviisqesulleghpesineng .
Taakunginaghhaagneng qepghaghtek , ighsanifqaafsi . Sagiqulluku qepghaataqiteggu Ataneq qamaken ilugpesineng .
Quyangatek qayughllak sighimallelguusi , nuqetaqitek nekeggmellusi seghleliineghpesini , yughaghaqiteklu iiwleng .
Ugpeqaalgutegpesinun aklulghiinun tuuniiqitek , upughatiiqitek kinkuneng alngunak .
Yughaatkaqiteki amyuqetaatkistesi Kiyaghneghmun quyastesqelluki , nakaan aqnightesqelluki .
Quyalgusighaqiteki tamaakut quyalghiit , qiyalgusighaqiteki tamaakut qiyalghiit .
Kiyaghtek nekeggmetullusi . Qukaayugtegpenasi yeghlegi ilakiteki ukavantalghiit . Sumeghtaghaatkegpenasi peghqinghunilusi ilagpesineng .
Kitum seghletun pikangisi , akitegpenaki seghletun . Piiqiteki pinilghiit tuguklighyugnalghiit tamaghhaanun .
Piyaghqaakan , piiqiteggu sangwaa piyaghqaghsi kiyaghtesqellusi nekeggmellusi tamaghhaanun .
Piniqegkamni , akiniighnaqegpenaki seghletun pistesi , itupill pegteki Kiyaghneghem sakraallghanun . Akuzitni Igaqegkani igaqngalghii whaten , " Whanganguuq aghyuughiyaghqaq , whanganguuq akiniighyaghqaq , piiq Ataneq . "
Igaqngaaqlu Akuzitni Igaqegkani , " Anguyagen iyataangukan neghesnaken , meqsugukan meghsinaken . Tawaten pikuvgu naasqwakun mayughfikelleqan kumangalghiimeng coal-meng . "
Kayaalqestegpenasi seghleghmun , itupill kayaalqiteggu seghleq pinitun pilleghqun .
Tamaghhaghmi qaatkusaghqaaguq aangwaaghughtekanun igleghutistenun . Kina alngunak igleghutistengunaanghituq wetkuqun Kiyaghneghem igleghutistengughtestekumigu . Igleghutistenguut qayughllak Kiyaghneghem nekegtekaqii igleghutisqelluki .
Kitum alngunak qaatkenghilkumiki igleghutistet , qaatkigatii Kiyaghneghem nakmikegkii . Enkaam aghyuughteslequq .
Pinitun pikayuget alikigatiit igleghutistet , iwernga seghletun pikayuget aliksaghqaqiit . Aliksunghilkufsiki igleghutistet , pinitun pitek , enkaam usuqelleqiisi .
Igleghutistet Kiyaghneghem qepghaghtekii aneghneghqelleghqaghpesinun . Iwernga seghletun pikufsi , aliknakesi , qayughllak Kiyaghneghem qelghumii aghyuughesqelluki seghletun pikat . Kiyaghneghem qepghaghtekii , aghyuughistekiillu seghletun pilghiinun .
Tamaaken apalluqluku qaatkiteki igleghutistet . Qaatkiteki qayughllak Kiyaghneghmun aghyuughtesunghilnguusi . Iwernga taananginaq apalluunghituq . Qaatkiteki qayughllak liisimakaghsi qaatkutelleq elqughutngaaq .
Taakuklu apalluqlukek llivikaqasi tax-esi , qayughllak igleghutistet qepghaagut Kiyaghneghmun qepghaqaten pineghmegteki .
Enkaangam tax-et asengesi qamaglluki llivikiteki igleghutestegpesinun . Siivakitekillu quulvaghtekillu qamaglluki .
Asengegpenaan kina alngunak , iwerngaqun piniqelleghsi asengeknginaghteggu ilagpesinun . Kitum alngunak piniqegkumiki yulgutni qaatkengngwii iinguniita Liilightuusat .
Igaqngaat Liilightuusani whaten , " Gelgaghniighpenang , Yugtaghpenang , Teglegpenang , Qiliiqetiqegpenang . " Qaatkelleqaten taakut qelghusat , alngunaklu qelghusat , qaatkegkuvgu una qelghusaq : " Piniqluku yulguten piniqelleghpetun elpeneng . "
Kina alngunak piniqikumi yulgutmineng , seghletun pinaanghitii . Piniqilleghmikun qaatkutnguuq iinguniitnun Liilightuusat .
Tamaakut piteki qayughllak liisimakaghsi pilleghqaq kaasimaaq . Qavalghiistun ayuqusi iwernga maaten taghtughyaghqaaghtusi . Yugulilleghput tughaaghtuq ugpeghyuggaallemnneng .
Unuk alpagyaghtughtuq , whaa aghsaghtungestaghaa . Taaqeltekingam atuqneghmeng seghleghet yuget piiqegkangit mamlegmi . Enkaam tugulteki pilluwaasighqat nighugmi .
Pinitun kiyaghtelta katam yugestun kiyaghlleghhiit nighugani aghneghem . Seghletun teghigniqefqaamta , suumefqaamta , alngunak sex-kun seghleghqefqaamta , pilluwutefqaamta , aqinatefqaamta .
Itupill akulghaaghestun aateggu Ataneq Jesus Christ-a , sumeghtaghaatkefqiitallu atuqnaluki yugusighpesi piyukellghit .
Upughateggu yuuk ugpeqilleghqestaaghhaq akulegpesinilnguq . Aaghtiiraaghusiqegpenaan sangwaa upeqegkaa elqughutngatanga nalighmeng anaggutngatanga .
Ataasim yugem ugpeqaa neghyaghqaaniluni alngunak neqmeng . Iwernga yuuk ugpelleghqestaaghhaq neghaquq nunivagseghaghhiinaghmeng .
Yugem neghegkayugem alngunak neqmeng , siivakligu yuuk neqayuk nunivagseghaghhiinaghmeng . Yugem neghegkayugem nunivagseghaghhiinaghmeng , nanqiggneghilligu yuuk neqayuk alngunak neqmeng , qayughllak Kiyaghneghem tugukliimaa .
Kinanguniluten piiqsin nanqigtilghii kitum qepghaghtenganeng ? Qepghaghtem piliitistenginaan nanqiglleqaa pinitun pimatanga nalighmeng seghletun pimatanga . Atanghem qepghaghtenga pinitun pillequq qayughllak Atanghem kayusighyaqlegukanga pinitun pisqelluku .
Yugem ugpeqaa ataasiq aghneq megnunaghataghaghniluku ilangitneng aghneghneng . Ilangan yugem ugpeqii qamaglluteng aghneghet tawatelkunniluki . Tamaghhaghmi yugem umyugagni ataasiightengngwaaghlikek .
Kitum alngunak ugpeqegkumigu megnunaghluku aghneq tawaten piiquq quulvaghnaluku Ataneq . Kitum alngunak neghegkumigu alngunak neqa tawaten piiquq quulvaghnaluku Ataneq , qayughllak iyamsiqayugvikaqegkanga Kiyaghneq neqmeng . Kitum alngunak neghyunghilkumiki ilangi neqet tawaten piiquq quulvaghnaluku Ataneq , iyamsiqayugvikaqegkangallu Kiyaghneq .
Unguvangigatukut whangkunnun , tuqungigatukutlu whangkunnun .
Unguvakumta , Ataneghmun unguvanguukut . Tuqumakumta , Ataneghmun tuqullequkut . Enkaam unguvayaghngaamta nalighmeng tuquyaghngaamta Atanghem pikiinkut .
Christ-a tuquluni , unguvaghtekaaguq Atanghunaluni unguvalghiinunllu tuqukanunllu .
Elpesi , sangan nanqigtaqesteki ugpeqaalgutesi ? Sanganllu siivakigasteki ugpeqaalgutesi ? Neqamikluku , qamaglluta nekevyaghqaagukut sivungakun Kiyaghneghem , ellnganun nanqigtesqelluta .
Akuzitni Igaqegkani igaqngaaq , " Ataneq piiq , qayughllak whanga unguvalghiinga Kiyaghneq , tamaghhaghmi yuuk segesqughquullequq whangamnun , tamaghhaghmillu yugem usuqelleqaa Kiyaghneq . "
Enkaam qamaglluta Kiyaghneghmun apeghyaghqaqaghput salleghput , sanganllu tawaten pimatfut .
Enkaangam taaqelta nanqigtunneghmeng . Yeghlegi , umyugaput ataasiightelteki ugpeqaalgutfut naagtestefqaan nalighmeng seghleghqestegpenaan pisteggu .
Ataneghqun Jesus-kun liisimakngwaaghaqa avangituq iinghutkameng neqmeng . Iwernga yugem ugpeqegkumigu sangwaa iinghutkaaluku , taawa ellngani iinghutkaaguq .
Ugpeqaalguten uniighmiqumakan sameng neghegkaghpeneng , taawa piniqnaniimaan . Neghegkaghpenun naafqestegpenaan ugpeqillgha Christ-am tuqumatkegkaa .
Ugpeqegkan pinightuq ; akuzitkestegpenaan seghleghuluku .
Qayughllak Kiyaghneghem Ataneghpagullghani sangwaat neghegkaputlu meghegkaputlu megnunanghitut . Ukut megnunaghtut : elqughutngalleq , nekeggmelleq , quyalleqlu ; taakut Agleghnalghiigneng Taghneghagneng pinguut .
Taakut atuqluki qepghaatilghiim Christ-amun , efqughlleqaa Kiyaghneq , itagnaqelleqaatlu yuget .
Enkaam atuulteggu nekeggmellengestiyaghqaq , kayemututeltallu ugpelleghtughtaghaghnaluta .
Naafqegpenaan Kiyaghneghem qepghallgha apalluqluku neqa . Qamaglluni neqa neghyaghqaaguq , iwernga anaggutngaaq neghelleghqaq alngunak neqmeng seghleghqestiyaghqaq kitumeng .
Itagnaghyaghqaaguq kemekragtunghitelleq , wine-etunghitelleq , sangwaallu alngunak naagtestiyaghqaq ugpeqaalgutegpesinun .
Kiyaghneghhiinaqlu liisimaksaghqaqatek tamaakut ugpeqegkaghten . Quyangaaquq yuuk atuqneghminiki ugpeqegkani elqughutnganiluki seghleghnitkegpenaki .
Iwernga yugem neghegkani , ugpeqegkumigu anaggutnganiluku , Kiyaghneghem nanqiglleqaa qayughllak pinghilkanga sangwaa ugpeqegkani . Sangwaa alngunak ugpeqegkani anaggutnganiluku atuqumakumigu seghleghqellequq .
Whangkuta ugpeqilleghtuqani kayusiisaghqaqaput ugpeqilleghqestaaghhaat seghleliinghata . Efqughsaghqaanghitukut whangkunneng .
Itupill , tamaghhaamta efqughhnaqelteggu ugpeqaalgutfut ellngan katam pinighqelleghqaanun , ugpeqilleghtughtesqelluku .
Talwa Christ-a efqughsimangituq ellmineng katam . Yeghlegi igaqegkaaguq Akuzitni Igaqegkani , " Yuget seghlequulghiit elpeneng , seghlequullghit tekitaqut whangamkun . "
Sivunghani Akuzitet Igaqegkat igaqegkaagut apeghtughnaluta . Nuqenneghtustiinkut , kayemiinkutlu sighimallengnayukamta .
Nuqenneghtullghenkuk , kayemellghenkuk Kiyaghneghtaaguk . Ellngan kiyaghteslisi itagnaqullusi katam Christ Jesus-em pillghatun .
Taagken qamagllusi qerngaghpesi ataasistun usuqelleqaghsi Kiyaghneq , Atanga Atanemta Jesus Christ-am .
Tamaaken apalluqluku tugukliitullusi katam Christ-am tugukliqayugukangisi elpesi . Tawaten pikufsi yuget usuqelleqaat Kiyaghneq .
Amenqun Christ-a qepghaghtengughtekaalghii Jews-enun liigikesqelluki Kiyaghneq iiwleng ipapiiquq . Tamaaken apalluqluku Jews-et liisimakngwaaghaat Kiyaghneghem piyaghqaqii akequsaqegkani sivunghitnun .
Christ-a tagikaalghiillu Gentile-enun usuqesqelluku Kiyaghneq nangllegtallghanun . Igaqngaaq Akuzitni Igaqegkani , " Enkaangam usuqelleqamken akulngitni Gentile-et , ilagaghllequngallu usuqilleghmeng ateghpenun . "
Akuzitni Igaqegkani igaqngaaqlu whaten , " Gentile-eni , quyatek maligullusi Kiyaghneghem yugitnun ! "
Alla Akuzitni Igaqegkani igaqngaaq , " Usuqiteggu Ataneq , qamagllusi Gentile-eni ; usuqiteggu , qamagllusi yugni ! "
Isaiah pikaaguq , " Kingungha Jesse-m tagillequq igleghunnaluki Gentile-et , enkaam ellngakun sighimallequt . "
Kiyaghneghuuq sighimastilghii . Imighlisi quyalleghllagmengllu nekeggmelleghmengllu ugpeqelleghpesigun ellnga . Taagken sighimallengataghaghllequsi aghtughyaghqaanghillghakun Agleghnalghiim Taghnegham .
Ugpeqaalgutemni , liisimakngwaaghamsi piniipigtusi yugni . Liisimakaqallu liigikngwaaghluki ayuqasi apeghtuusat Kiyaghneghmeng ayuqelghiit , enkaam apeghtuusaqlegwaasi ilangitnun .
Iwernga tetullngunanga latakaqamsi sameng ilangitneng neqangughhnalusi tamaaken . Tawaten lataanga qayughllak Kiyaghneghem tunusightughaanga
qepghaghtengulunga Christ Jesus-mun Gentile-enun . Priest-etun ayuqaqunga ungipaqinemni Pinilghiineng Ungipaaneng Kiyaghneghem Gentile-enun . Tawaten ungipaqiiqunga ellngit tunusatun ayuqesqelluki tuguklighyugnalghii Kiyaghneghmun . Agleghnalghiim Taghnegham agleghnaghtestaa tunusaq .
Enkaam qukaayugtaqunga qepghaqamneng Kiyaghneghmun Christ Jesus-kun .
Akuzitkesaghqaqanka Christ-am apeghiiqaghhiinii whangamkun . Ellnganguuq Gentile-eneng qaatkutestilghii Kiyaghneghmun ungipaqillemkunllu qepghaqamkunllu .
Tawaten pikaaguq aghtughyaghqaanghillghakun allaaghlluwhaghtillghet , aghtughyaghqaanghillghakunllu Agleghnalghiim Taghnegham . Ungipaqngwaaqaqanka Pinilghiit Ungipat Christ-ameng ayuqelghiit tamaghhaani Jerusalem-emeng taagaverugllak Illyricum-emun .
Iiwleng piyukelqesaghaqa ungipaqnaluki Pinilghiit Ungipat nunani nagaquusigalngughni Christ-ameng . Tawaten pikaagunga qayughllak nekeftiyugunghilnguunga tunemakun ilangan yugem piinliqaakun .
Katam Akuzitni Igaqegkani igaqngalghii whaten , " Tamaakut salin ungipaasigalnguut ellnganeng , esghaghlleqaat , salinllu nagaquusigalnguut ellnganeng , liigikelleqaat . "
Tamaaken apalluqluku uglaghngaan elpesinun pipagningitaqunga qayughllak ilangitni nunani ungipaqiiqelghiinga .
Iwernga maaten apeghiighaqa qepghaqaqa maani . Uglalghiini ayumiqulleghni elpesinun piyupigtaqsaghtunga ,
enkaam sunanguq maaten laalighfiklamsi Spain-mun pitkelluku . Laalighutaghtellemta kingunganeng sunanguq kayusightengnga aghulaqnaqegkuma Spain-mun .
Iwernga elpesinun pivagilgama , Jerusalem-mennaqaqunga kayusiinnaluki Kiyaghneghem yugi tamaanlenguut .
Ugpeqat Macedonia-melnguutlu , Achaia-melnguutlu quyakusiqluku tuunikaagut manimeng kayusiinnaluki aklumalghiit akulngitnilnguut Kiyaghneghem yugan Jerusalem-emi .
Quyakusiqluku tawaten pikaagut . Taakut Gentile-et asengemiit Jews-et qayughllak allgeghutkaalghiit Kiyaghneghem quyastillghaneng ellngitgun . Enkaam Gentile-et kayusighyaghqaqiit Jews-et ugpeqiit Jerusalem-emelnguut tuyughluki manimeng .
Whaa kelqennaqaqa Gentile-et maningat Jews-enun . Apeghiiqumkun una qepghaqaq tuunluku mani ellngitnun , laalighfiksaghtughlleqamsi , taagken Spain-ellequnga .
Liisimakaqa kaaskuma elpesinun , pilgullequnga Christ-am iingunaan quyastellghaneng .
Ugpeqaalgutemni , Atanemteggun Jesus Christ-akun , piniqellghakunllu Taghnegham , maligullusi whangamnun yughaatkeghllakaghtengnga Kiyaghneghmun kayusiitesqellunga .
Yughaghtek Kiyaghneghmun paqniighsiisqellunga ugpeqaanghilngughneng Judea-mi . Yughaatkiteggullu qepghaqaqa Jerusalem-emi tuguklighyugniisqelluku Kiyaghneghem yugitnun .
Taagken Kiyaghneghem piyukelqegkagu , elpesinun pillequnga quyallelighllaglunga , enkaam pinighyuuggneqigllequnga laalighfikumalusi .
Kiyaghneq nekeggmellelitilghii tamaghaghpesinilli . Amen .
Ungipaasugamsi ugpeqaalgutemnneng , Phoebe-meng . Pinilghiinguuq deaconess-a ugpeqanun qerngughutkayugnun yughaghvigani Cenchreae-m .
Upughannakesi Kiyaghneghem yugita piiqellghistun qayughllak Atanghem pikaa . Kayutkesunghisi kayusighaqluku qayughllak kayuteghllaguuq uglalghiinun yugnun , whangamnunllu talwa .
Ungipaataghhnakegsi Priscilla-nkuk Aquila-nkuk suumqaqagkanguq . Qepghalgutkagka Christ Jesus-mun .
Talwa tuqutelleghqaghtek pitkegpenaan paqniighsaghqaqaagnenga . Tamaaken apalluqluku iyamsiqayugllaguunga elkegkeneng . Qamagllutengllu ugpeqat Gentile-et yughaghvigitnilnguut iyamsiqayuguut .
Ungipaataghhnakesi ugpeqat qerngughutkayuget mangteghagkeni suumqaqankanguq . Ungipaataghhnakesi piniqegkaqa Epaenetus suumqaqaqanguq . Asia-mi ellnga ugpeghyuggaaqaaguq Christ-akun .
Ungipaataghhnakesi Mary suumqaqaqanguq ; qevuulluni qepghaatkaqiisi .
Ungipaataghhnakegsi Andronicus-enkuk Junias-enkuk Jew-lgutegka , anusimingllaghalgutkegkaqagkallu , suumqaqagkanguq . Apostle-nguuk yuget liisimakngwaaqegket ; sivumni ugpeqaaghtekaaguk .
Ungipaataghhnakesi Ampliatus , piniqegkaqa Ataneghqun , suumqaqaqanguq .
Unipaataghhnakesi Urbanus , qepghalgutfut Christ-amun , piniqegkaqallu Stachys , suumqaqagkanguq .
Ungipaataghhnakesi Apelles suumqaqaqanguq . Nanghiighsaghallengaqngami ipapighqegkaqaa ataasighmitelleni Christ-amun . Ungipaataghhnakesi nengllugutangi Aristobulus-em suumqaqankanguq .
Ungipaataghhnakesi Herodion , Jew-elgutka , suumqaqaqanguq . Ungipaataghhnakesillu ugpeqat nengllugutanganilnguut Narcissus-em suumqaqankanguq .
Ungipaataghhnakegsi Tryphaena-nkuk Tryphosa-nkuk suumqaqagkanguq . Taakuk aghnak qepghaghtenguuk Ataneghmun . Ungipaataghhnakesillu piniqegkaqa Persis , suumqaqaqanguq ; qevulluni qepghaqaaguq Ataneghmun .
Ungipaataghhnakegsi Rufus-enkuk naakullghiik , suumqaqagkanguq . Rufus Atanghem nakmikegkaqaa , naanganllu ighneqelghiistun piiqaanga .
Ungipaataghhnakesi Asyncritus-enkut , Phlegon-enkut , Hermes-enkut , Patrobas-enkut , Hermas-enkut , qamagllukillu ugpeqaalgutet ellngitnilnguut , suumqaqankanguq .
Ungipaataghhnakegsi Philologus-enkuk , Julia-nkuk , Nereus-enkuk nayakullghiik , Olympas-llu qamagllukillu Kiyaghneghem yugi ellngitnilnguut , suumqaqankanguq .
Quyakutaqitek naaghutmeng Kiyaghneghem piniqellghakun . Qamaglluteng ugpeqat Christ-am yughaghviganilnguut , liisimakesugiisi suumqaqiisinguq .
Ugpeqaalgutemni , qelghamsi kelengasqellusi tamaakuneng aafquutestikayugneng , tunutestilghiineng yuget ugpeqillghitneng , kipullginaalghiineng apeghtuusaneng liitkaghpesineng . Iqitngatek tamaakuneng .
Yuget tawaten pikayuget qepghaatngunghitaat Christ-a Ataneghput . Taawanginaghhaq ellmeng katam efquqegkaghhiinateng piiqiit . Apeghtughineghmeggni akuziteghlluwhaat atuqaqiit , usuquughtaqiitlu yuget puughhnaluki puughsugumalghiit .
Qamaglluteng yuget nagaquumaat qaatkutngalleghsi Ataneghmun , enkaam tamaaken apalluqluku quyakeghllawaamsi . Peghqinghusugamsi samun pinilghiimun , iwernga anaggutellngunasi seghleghmun .
Kiyaghneghem nekeggmellelitilghiim qantaghaqun kagimlleqaa Tughneghaq itegaghpesi asingani . Ataneghput Jesus Christ-a nangllegtaghli elpesinun .
Qepghalgutma Timothy-m , Jew-lgutmallu Lucius-enkut , Jason-enkut , Sosipater-enkut suumqaqiisinguq .
Tertius-nguunga , igaataqaqa Paul latanganeng . Whangallu suumqaqamsi Ataneghqun .
Whanga Paul , Gaius-metaqunga . Mangteghaani qamaglluteng ugpeqat qerngughutkayuguut . Ellnganllu ugpeqatlu suumqaqiisinguq . Neghllamta manimeng aflengakistengan , Erastus-em , ugpeqaalgutemtallu Quartus-em suumqaqiisinguq .
Usuqelteggu Kiyaghneq ! Ellngan ayepsugighsaghyaqlegwii ugpeqillesi Pinilghiitgun Ungipatgun Jesus Christ-ameng ayuqelghiimeng ungipaqumanginaghaqegkemkun yugnun . Taananguuq aksaqegkaq ungipaq Kiyaghneghem qayvighsimangitkaa ima piinlighyuggaallghaneng nunam .
Iwernga maaten , piinleghilnguum Kiyaghneghem qayvighsimii Pinilghiit Ungipat igaqullghitgun uuknaliqistet . Qelghusimii Pinilghiit Ungipat liitesqelluki yugnun nunataghhaani tamaghhaani . Tawaten pikaaguq ellngitnun ugpeqesqellunillu qaatkesqellunillu .
Ellnginaaguq Kiyaghneq , peghqinelghii samun tamaghhaanun . Yuget usuqlitgu quunperugllak Jesus Christ-akun ! Amen .
Ukut latat Paul-meng pinguut , Kiyaghneghem nakmikegkaaneng Jesus Christ-amun apostle-nguluku . Ugpeqaalgutfut Sosthenes whangamnituq .
Lataaqunga Kiyaghneghem ugpeghtengitnun Corinth-melngughnun , Kiyaghneghem aaftekaanun yuknalusi Christ Jesus-kun . Nakmikegkaqiisillu pelungitesqellusi maligullusi yulghuteghllagnun tamanganilngughnun , yughaqayugnun Atanemnnun Jesus Christ-amun , qamagtengngwaaghluta Atanqaghput .
Kiyaghneghem Atamta , Atanemtallu Jesus Christ-am nanglleklisillu nekeggmellelguslilsillu .
Iyamsiqayugvikaqaqa Kiyaghneq qayughllak nangllekegkaqiisi Christ Jesus-kun .
Enkaam ellngakun aklungighikaagusi liigikelleghmengllu akuzilleghmengllu . Enkaam maaten liigikataghaghlleqaghsi Christ-a , akuzitkataghaghlleqaghsillu Ataneq .
Allangughtekamllu kiyaghtaalleghpesi ipapighqaa ungipaqegkaghput Christ-a .
Agleghnalghiigneng Taghneghagneng tunusalguusi sameng tamaghhaaneng , utaqiingulusi Atanemta Jesus Christ-am taginqigtelleghqaaneng .
Kiyaghneghem ugpellesi iknaqughsaamanginaghnaaghii kenlanga kingulighpigaghmun aghneghmun . Inqun anaggutellghitesqellusi Ataneghput Jesus Christ-a nanqigtikan yugneng .
Ataasiighmelnguum Kiyaghneghem nakmikegkaqiisi ilatesqellusi Ighneghminun Jesus Christ-amun Atanemnnun .
Ugpeqaalgutemni , Atanemta Jesus Christ-am aatghakun piimsi taaqesqellusi aaghtiiraaghunneghmeng . Aafquutegpenasi . Sumeghtaghallesillu sanaqellesillu ataasiighhnaqluki .
Ugpeqaalgutemni , ilangita Chloe-em nengllugutangan ungipaatkaqaatnga aaghtiiraaghutaqnilusi .
Ilasinguq piiqut , " Whanga Paul-em maligsaaghtekaanga . " Ilasi , " Whanga Apollos-em . " Ilasi " Whanga Peter-em . " Paninang ilasinguq piiqut , " Whanga Christ-am maligsaaghtekaanga . "
Enkaangam qafsinaghqaghsi Jesus Christ-a . Paul-em qaquraatkegkaqisii ? Paaptaayekaatsii Paul-em aatghakun ?
Iyamsiqayugvikaqaqa Kiyaghneq paaptaayemangilkegka nalighhiinaghsi iwerngaqun Crispus-enkuk Gaius-enkuk .
Enkaangam kina alngunak pinaanghituq paaptaayemaniluni atemkun .
( Atwhay paaptaayekaqankallu Stephanas-enkut nengllugutkullghiit . Iwernga neqamikenghitaqa kina alla alngunak paaptaayematka ) .
Christ-am paaptaayeliisqumangitaanga , iwernga kayagtekaqaanga ungipaqisqellunga Pinilghiineng Ungipaneng . Ungipaqingigatunga atuqluki yugem peghqinellghi , luuraq aghtughyaghqaanghillghiitesnayukamkun qaquuraa Christ-am .
Ungipaq Christ-am tuqullgha qaquurakun temnginguuq iflanaqelghiinun . Iwernga yugulillengelghiini whangkuta liisimakaghput Kiyaghneghem aghtughyaghqaanghilqaa .
Akuzitni Igaqegkani igaqngaaq , " Peghqinghet peghqinellghat atuunanightesleqaqa . Liitkaghllagetlu liitellghat sasiinanightesleqaqa . "
Enkaam sanaqan始ngam nunam peghqinelghiingi ? Sanaqan始ngam apeghtughistengi Liilightuusat ? Sanaqan始ngam aaghtiiraaghtet ? Qamagtengngwaaghluni liitelleghllallghat sasiinghituq qayughllak Kiyaghneghem temngitwhangllaqaqaa peghqinellgha nunam .
Peghqinelleghmikun Kiyaghneq pikaaguq nunam yuganun nallukelleqniluni peghqinellghitgun . Enkaam Kiyaghneghem nakmikii yugulinaluki qamaglluki ugpelghiit Christ-ameng ungipaqegkamnneng . Ugpeqaanghilnguut sumeghtaghaatkaqaat taana ungipaqegkaghput temnginguniluku .
Jews-et esghaasugaqut allaaghlluwhaghtilleghneng ugpeqnaluku Kiyaghneghem ungipaa ; Gentile-et peghqinellengyugaqut ugpeqnaluku ungipaq ipangutanga .
Iwernga paninang ungipaqnaqngwaaghput Christ-amun tuqutkegkaqniluki qaquurakun . Una ungipaq Jews-eni piyaqnapigtuq ugpeqsaghqaaluni , Gentile-eni temngiinguuq .
Iwernga whangkunnun Kiyaghneghem nakmikegkaanun Jews-ngughngaamta , Gentile-ngughngaamta tawatenneghituq . Christ-am tuqullghan qaquurakun liitestekaqiinkut Kiyaghneghem aghtughyaghqaanghillghanengllu peghqinellghanengllu .
Kiyaghneghem temngitwhallgha peghqinghataghgaghtuq yugem peghqinellghaneng . Kiyaghneghem kayaatellgha iknaqataghaghtuq yugem iknaqellghaneng .
Ugpeqaalgutemni , neqamikluku natesaatsi Kiyaghneghem tuqlughaqngisi . Qafsinkuuraghhaghni peghqinghuyaghtusi nunam yugan sumeghtaghaatkellghitni . Qafsinkuuraghhaghni aghtiigasaghtusi igleghutistet , nalighmeng aklungilngughneng nengllugutneng pinguyaghtusi .
Iwernga Kiyaghneghem nakmikegkaqii tamaakut nalluuqat nunami kayngusaaknaluki peghqinelghiit , Kiyaghneghem nakmikegkaqii kayaalnguut nunami kayngusaaknaluki tamaakut iknaqelghiit .
Kiyaghneghem nakmikegkaqii ukavanlenguutlu asitnginaaqiitlu nunami . Tamaakunguut Kiyaghneghem nakmikegkii , yugnun liigikesqelluki sumeghtaghaatkegkiit aangwaaghuluki iwernga Kiyaghneghmi aangwaaghunghitut .
Enkaangam kina alngunak aangaayuggnaanghituq nekevegkuni sivungani Kiyaghneghem .
Kiyaghneghuuq tuunistesi unguvalleghmeng Christ Jesus-kun . Kiyaghneghem Christ Jesus-mun tuunestiinkut peghqinelleghmeng , elqughutestiinkutlu Kiyaghneghmi , agleghnaghtestiinkutu , itemutestiinkutlu seghleghqellemnneng .
Enkaangam atuqelteggu , Akuzitni Igaqegkani igaqngalghii , " Kina alngunak aangaayugsukuni , aangaayugutkelliki Atanghem apeghiiqii ellminun . "
Ugpeqaalgutemni , ungipaqiyaghtughaqngama elpesinun , atuqumangitanka akuzitet liigikepagningilkesi . Peghqilleghllamkun ungipaqiyunghitunga Kiyaghneghem ungipaaneng elpesinun .
Pakikaqanka tamaakut qayughllak ungipaqiyulghiinga Jesus Christ-anginaghhaghmeng tuqullghanengllu qaquurakun .
Elpesinitaqngama tetugaataqaagunga , alingruuqaagunga , ungelegtekaagungallu .
Kukragnalghiimeng akuzitkumangitunga peghqineghllagem akuzitanganeng . Iwernga Agleghnalghiim Taghnegham aghtughyaghqaanghillghan ipapighqegkaqii apeghtughillghenka ipangutangi .
Enkaangam ugpeghtusi apalluqluku Kiyaghneghem aghtughyaghqaanghillgha , nakaan apalluqluku yugem peghqinellgha .
Angtaniitkanun ugpeqanun apeghtuusaqaqa Kiyaghneghem peghqinellgha . Iwernga taana peghqinelleq nunameng pingunghituq , talwa igleghutistenganeng . Qantaghaqun aviighusaghqaagut .
Peghqinelleq apeghtuusaqa Kiyaghneghem peghqinelqaa , nallukaat yuget . Yuget nallukngwaaghyaqangat taana peghqinelleq kenlanga Kiyaghneghem liitestellghanun . Talwa nunangllaamangilluni Kiyaghneghem usuqsaghqaaluta pikaqiinkut peghqinelleghmikun .
Nalighhiiniita nunam igleghutistengita liigikumangitaat taana peghqinelleq . Liigikegkaqsaqumegteggu , qaquuraghnayanghitaat Atangha nighughqellghem .
Igaqegkani Akuzitni igaqegkaaguq , " Tamaakut iyem esghamangilkangi , tamaakut sigutem nagaquumangilkangi , tamaakut umyugam sumeghtaghaatkumangilkangi . Kiyaghneghem yataaghqegkaqii piniqisteminun . "
Iwernga Kiyaghneghem liigikestekaqii whangkunnun Agleghnalghiignekun Taghneghagmikun . Taghnegham yuvghiighaqaa sangwaa tamaghhaan , talwa Kiyaghneghem qaamnarugllaganilnguut .
Yugem sumeghtaghallgha kitum alngunak nallukaa iwerngaqun ellngan katam taghneghagkenka . Tawateghpigaq Kiyaghneghem sumeghtaghallgha kitum alngunak nallukaa iwerngaqun ellngan katam Taghneghagkenka .
Nunam taghneghaaneng allgeghusimangitukut . Yeghlegi , allgeghtekaqagput Taghneghak Kiyaghneghmeng pik , liigiknaluki qamaglluki Kiyaghneghem tuunegkii whangkunnun .
Enkaam akuzingigatukut yugem peghqinellghakun , iwernga atuqaqaput akuzitet Agleghnalghiim Taghnegham apeghtuutkii . Tawaten piiqukut apeghtuusaqnemteki Taghnegham ipapillghi tamaakunun allgeghutkanun Agleghnaliigneng Taghneghagneng .
Iwernga kina alngunak allgeghusimangilnguq Agleghnalghiigneng Taghneghagneng , tuguklighingigatuq tunusaneng Taghneghagneng pineng . Tamaakut tunusat temngitwhanguut ellngani . Liigikepagningitii qayughllak Agleghnalghiim Taghnegham kayusillghiinaakun liigiksaghqaaguq .
Yugem allgeghutkam Agleghnalghiigneng Taghneghagneng nanqigtaqaa sangwaa qamaglluku . Iwernga kitum alngunak nanqigsaghqaqenghitaa ellnga .
Akuzitet Igaqegkat pillghistun , " Kitum alngunak nallukaa Atanghem sumeghtaghallgha . Enkaam kitum alngunak liilightughnaanghitaa . " Iwernga whangkuta ugpeqani sumeghtaghaghaqukut Christ-am sumeghtaghallghatun .
Ugpeqaalgutemni , elpesinitaqngama aleghqughpagningitkaqamsi aleghqughwaqellemtun ugpeqaghllaget . Yeghlegi aleghquqaqamsi ugpellesi anglillghilngughestun ayuqluki . Ugpeqillesi Christ-akun taghnughhaghhaghestun ayuqut .
Kukragnangunaan apeghtuqaqamsi . Katam tawaten mamaghhaghmeng meghesleghhiistun pikaqamsi . Neqepigmeng neghestepagningitkaqamsi qayughllak neqepigtughpagningilnguusi salin . Paninang maaten neqepigtughpagningitaqusi , qayughllak ugpeqaanghilngughestun ayuqusi salin . Liigikestengngwaaghsi ugpelleghpesi anglinghitellgha aqinalleghpesigunllu aghivatelleghpesigunllu . Ugpeqaanghilngughestun kiyaghtengnguusi .
Nalighsi pineghmini , " Whanga Paul-em maligsaaghtekaanga , " ilasillu pineghmeggni , " Whanga Apollos-em maligsaaghtekaanga , " ugpeqaanghilngughestun piiqusi .
Kinangaawa Apollos ? Kinanguzinga whanga ? Qepghaghtekiinkung Kiyaghneghem , kayusiitkaqamsi ugpeqesqelluku Christ-a . Qepghaqalestaghhiinaagukung Ataneghem qelghutkaaneng .
Elpesi Kiyaghneghem piitesighaghvikiisi . Piitesighaghaqunga , Apollos-em meghqaqaa , iwernga Kiyaghneghem nagustaqaa .
Enkaangam kina alngunak piitesiighalghiillu meghqilghiillu ukavantuq . Kiyaghneghhiinaq aangeghllagtuq nagustikayuguuq .
Piitesiighaghtallu meghqistallu tawatelkutuk . Kiyaghneghem akileghtughyaghqaqaak qepghallghegkenkun .
Qepghalgutkutukung Kiyaghneghmun ; elpesi Kiyaghneghem piitesiighaghvikiisi . Kiyaghneghem mangteghaqiisi .
Kiyaghneghem nangllegtalleq tagivaqaa atuqluku piinliqaqaqa qepghaqaq elpesini . Peghqinelghiistun tunemiqaqaqa mangteghaq ulimayaghqaq . Jesus Christ-anginaaguq tunemaq , alla saaghwakun tunemaghqiituq . Ilangita ulimavikngwaat qaayngakun . Qamaglluni piraamsiluni ulimali .
Ilangita atughlleqaat gold-a , silver-a , jewel-a , ilangita unaghsiq , paliqaq vegaaq , ungagaqlu tunemakun taaggun .
Sangwaa atuqegkaghput esghaghyaghqaqaghput ataasikaghtaamta qamagtengngwaaghluta aghneghmi tawani Christ-am nanqigtilleghqaani . Kenghem esghaghtesaghqaqaa qepghaqaghput natetulanga .
Sangwaa yugem atuqegkaa kumanghilkuni , akileghtusangyaghqaaguq .
Iwernga ilangan yugem qepghaqaa iflayaghqaaguq kumaquni , akileghtusangnaanghituqlu . Naqamenraq ellnga yugulillengyaghqaaguq , katam tawaten keneghmeng aanelghiistun .
Liisimakngwaaghaghsi Kiyaghneghem Temple-kiisi . Agleghnalghiik Taghneghakek kiyaghtengnguuk ilugpesini !
Kitum alngunak naafqegkagu Kiyaghneghem Temple-nga , Kiyaghneghem naafqesaghqaqaa ellnga , qayughllak Kiyaghneghem Temple-nga agleghnalghiinguuq . Elpesi Temple-kiisi .
Kina alngunak puughtefqaami ellmineng pili . Nalighsi sumeghtaghaangukumi liitepagllakaaniluni nunam peghqinellghaneng , yeqay maliglligu Christ-a , ugpeqaanghilnguut temngingunighngaatgu . Tawaten pikuni elngaatall peghqinghughtepiiglleqaa .
Kiyaghneghmi nunam peghqinellgha temnginguuq . Akuzitni Igaqegkani igaqngaaq , " Peghqinghet yuget nunami whani Kiyaghneghem pipagningiitestaqii ellngita katam peghqinellghitgun . "
Igaqegkaaguqlu , " Atanghem liisimakaa peghqinghem yugem sumeghtaghallgha sasiinghituq . "
Enkaangam kitum alngunak qukaayugutkesaghqaqenghitii sangwaat yuget piiqegkangit . Sangwaa qamaglluku Kiyaghneghem pinighqusighqaaghtestekaqaa elpesinun ,
talwa Paul , Apollos , Peter-llu . Nunallu una , unguvalleqlu , tuqulleqlu , sangwaallu alngunak kiyaghtaalleghmelnguq maaten , sangwaallu alngunak kaasaghqaq , qamagtengngwaaghluki elpesi pikasi .
Enkaam elpesi Christ-am pikiisi , Christ-a Kiyaghneghem pikaa .
Sumeghtaghaatkitekut qepghaghtekniluta Christ-amun . Qepghaghtenguukut apeghtughilghiit ipapighqelleghmeng Kiyaghneghem apeghtuutkaaneng whangkunnun .
Christ-am qepghaghtengi ataasiighmesaghqaagut .
Whanga , ataasiighmennilunga qepghaghta pikufsinga , nalighmeng ataasiighmenneghinnilunga kitum alngunak pikanganga , sumeghtaghaatkennaanghitaqa . Talwa whangamneng nanqigsigatunga .
Nallukaqa sameng anaggusimatka , iwernga anaggutellghinnilunga pinghitunga . Atanghhiinaam nanqigsaghqaqaanga .
Enkaangam wiin nanqigtegpenaan kina alngunak sallghaneng . Atanghem taginqigtekumi kukegsaghqaqii yuget ilungit aliighqelluki sangwaat iighngayalghiit tesqamani . Aliighqesaghqaqii sangameng saaqutangi . Taagken usuqsaghqat tamaakut usuqellengyaghqaagut Kiyaghneghmeng .
Ugpeqaalgutemni , elpesi apalluqlusi Apollos-lu whangkutung usputaqnguukung . Usputaagukung elpesinun liitesqelluku una igaqnalghii sameng pisiitanga . " Qaatkaqiteki sangwaat igaqngalghiit Akuzitni Igaqekani . " Nalighhiinaghpesi aangaayugutkesaqunaan ataasiq yuuk , aallgha ugumikluku .
Kitum pinighataghaghtestisi ugpeqaalgutegpesineng ? Sangwaa qamaglluku Kiyaghneghmeng pikaghsi . Kiyaghneghem tuunumakangisi , aangaayugtegpenasi . Ungipaghpenasi whaten , " Sangwa qamaglluku whangamneng pikaqaqa . "
Allgeghtengngwaaghumaaghsi aklukegkaghsi qamaglluku ! Aklungighingwaaghlusi ayuqusi ! Whangkungunasi umiilgughsimaasi ! Umiilgulghiisituq , enkaam umiilgutilgusighnayaghamsi !
Sumeghtaghallemni Kiyaghneghem nekegtekaqiinkut apostle-eni ukalighpigaaluta yugneng . Anusimingllaghastun ayuqukut , tuqusaghqastun . Yuget qamagtengngwaaghluteng , yaqulgetlu esghapagaqiinkut .
Whangkuta nallungughtekaagukut Christ-a apalluqluku , iwernga elpesi sumeghpesini peghqinepiguusi ugpeqani . Yuget waakigatiinkut , iwernga sumeghpesini elpesi nagataqiisillu quulvaghaqiisillu , whangkuta pingigatiinkut .
Whavemun kenlanga neqangisagaqukut , meghyaghqiisagaqukut , aatkiisagaqukut . Yuget qevutkaqiinkut . Nengitukut , igleghtaagukut quunpeng .
Qepghaghaqukutlu qevuulluta maningnaluta kiyaghtaaghusighqameng . Seghlequulghiit whangkunneng pinitun aleghqughaqaput . Ugpeqaatemnneng amyuutkenghinkut akuzilgiigatukutlu akisigataputlu .
Iqlengiqutkenghinkut pinitun aleghqughaqaput tawaten pifqiita pisqelluki . Whavemun kenlanga sumeghtaghaatkaqiinkut sakwaaghestunllu sasiinghilngughestunllu .
Latangunghitunga kaynguyuggnalusi . Iwernga piniqepigllusi whanga katam taghnughhaqelghistun liilightughyugaqamsi kiyaghtaalleghqaghpesineng .
Qaywa apeghtughistetupigsaghngaaghpesi Christ-ameng , atatughllanghitusi . Ugpeqsuwhaghaqngafsigu Jesus Christ-a nagaqughluki Pinilghiit Ungipat , tawanita atastun lliiqanga elpesinun .
Enkaangam kiyaghtesupigtamsi whangamtun .
Tamaaken apalluqluku Timothy kayagtengngwaaqa elpesinun . Ighneqelghiistun ayuqaqa Ataneghqun . Ataasiighmelnguq ugpeqaq piniqepigtaqa . Neqangughhnaaghiisi naten whanga kiyaghtaqellemneng Christ-amun . Tawatelnguq kiyaghtaalleq apeghtuusaqaqaqa ugpeqanun tamanganilngughnun .
Ilasi aangaayugneghughtaqut , qayughllak sumeghmeggni laalighhnaanghinnilunga pikaqaatnga Corinth-mun .
Iwernga Atanghem piyukelqegkagu , elpesinun piyaghtungestaghtunga . Taagken liigikelleqanka aangaayugneghet aangaayugtelleghmegestun piyaghqaatangi .
Kiyaghneghem Ataneghpagullgha akuzitetgun ayuqenghituq iwernga aghtughyaghqaanghilleghqun ayuquq .
Kaaskuma sasqesugestengnga ? Anagutalighlungaa aghyuughlamsii , nalighmeng piniqlusi , pinitungwaaq pilamsii ?
Nagaqughaqaqa nalighpesinguq atami nulighha nulighqelghiistun ayuqaa . Seghlepiglleghhiimeng seghleghqengnguuq talwa ugpeqaanghilnguut atuqesnayanghitaat taana seghleghqelleq .
Paninang yuukutkaqetsii elpesineng katam ? Qivghughllagyaqlegestun ! Elpesi iqisaqlegestun yuuk taana akulegpesineng .
Uyavanteghllagyaghngaaghma sumeghtaghaatkeghllawaaqa . Tawanlengughestun elpesini agghitkegkaqaqa naten pilleghqameng taana yuuk aatghakun Atanemta Jesus-em . Ugpeqani , allameng qerngughuskufsi , tawanlengughestun umyugaghmiklunga , aghtughyaghqanghillghakun Jesus Christ-am yuuk taana elpesinitestegpenaan allamengllu pinakesi . Tuuniteggu Tughneghagh-mun , piyukelleghmitun yugusii naafqelligu , enkaam taghneghakek yugulillengesqellukek Ataneq taginqigtekan .
Piniiyugtelleghsi seghleghuuq . Liisimakaghsi whaten pilleq , " Yeast-am ghhuughtesteghllakayuwaa akuutaq . "
Tamaaken apallukluku seghleghqellghet akulegpesinilnguut iqiteki . Tawaten pikufsi pelungillequsi akuutastun yeast-angilngughestun . Ipa pelungitusi qayughllak Christ-a Passover-em penniighaghaqaa aghqutkegkaaguq seghleghqellemnnun .
Katam Jews-et iqitellghistun yeast-at mangteghameggneng yataaghqutfagilgamegteggu Passover-em neqenghaghqellgha , tawateghpigaq seghleghqelleput iqilleqaput . Enkaangam pelungillequkut , ipapighqengngallequkutlu .
Ilangitgun latama ilatngasnanighamsi ugpeqanun anagngalghiikun atuqullghiinun .
Akuzitkengngunghitanka uum nunam yugi anagngalghiikun atuqullghiit , nalighmeng pakigneghet , wayaghniightet , nalighmeng tamaakut maniguutkayuget kiyaghnengllaqanun . Iqisukufsi tawatelngughneng yugneng nuna unisaghqaqaghsi .
Iwernga latamkun ilatesnaniqaqamsi tamaakunun ugpeqaalgutnguniluteng pilghiinun sex-kun seghleghqengngukata , nalighmeng pakigneghukata , maniguutkayugukata kiyaghnengllaqanun , seghlequughutngukata yulgutmeng , meghestengukata , wayaghniightengukatallu . Talwa neghelgusighpenaki tawatelnguut .
Whanga nanqigsaghqaqenghitanka ugpeqaanghilnguut ; Kiyaghneghem nanqigsaghqaqii . Iwernga elpesi nanqigsaghqaqsaghasi ugpeqaalgutesi . Akuzitet Igaqegkat piit , " Seghleghqesta iqiteggu akulegpesineng . "
Nalighsi aaghtiiraaneghmini ugpeqaalgutmineng , sangan aglaataqagu nanqigtivigmun ? Kaynguyugigatsii ugpeqaanghilngughnun nanqigtesneghpesini elpesi ugpeqani ? Ugpeqat ugpeqaalgutmeggnun taklaghutesaghqaayaghtut aaghtiiraaghutelleghmeggneng .
Liisimakenghistegguu Kiyaghneghem yugan nanqigsaghqii ugpeqaanghilnguut ilangani aghneghem ? Nanqigsaghqaqngukufsiki , naten piyaqnaghtutkalleqeftat elpesinun nanqigtelleghqii piyaqniilnguut ?
Liisimakenghistekii nanqigsaghqaqekeput yaqulget ? Enkaam taklaghqullghet aaghtiraaghutelleghneng whani unguvalleghmi piyaqniisaghqaayaghtut .
Aaghtiiraaghunneghpesini sangafsingam ugpeqaanghilngughnun piiqetsi nanqigtesqellusi ?
Kayngunaghhaghmeng elpesi ! Liisimakaqa akulegpesini liisimalghiimeng taklaghutistekaghqalguut ugpeqaalgutet aaghtiiraaghullghiit .
Yeghlegi ugpeqam ugpeqaalgutni aglaataqaa ugpeqaanghilngughnun nanqigtistenun , agghitkesqelluki aaghtiiraaghutelletek .
Tawatetelleghpesigun ugpeqaanghilngughestun kiyaghtaaghuusi . Ugpeqaalgutesi aglaategpenaki nanqigtivigmun . Nepiighutaqiteki anagteghngiisi , puughteghngiisi .
Itupill elpesi katam ugpeqaalgutesi anagtaqasillu puughtaqasillu .
Ipapestaaq liisimaksaghqaqsaghaghsi seghletun pistet nekaghqiilnguut Ataneghpagullghani Kiyaghneghem . Puughtestegpenasi kitumun alngunak . Kiyaghneghem Ataneghpagullghani nekaghqiitut : sex-kun seghleghqegkayuget , maniguutkayuget kiyaghnengllaqanun , gelgaghniightet , aghnaasit , yuget yulgutmeggneng atuqikayuget , aghnat aghnaalgutmeggneng atuqikayuget .
Tamaakutlu teglengalghiit , pakigneghet , meghestet , seghlequughtet yugneng , wayaghniightet , nekaghqiitut Ataneghpagullghani Kiyaghneghem .
Ilasi tawatesalghiit salin ugpeqillghilluteng Christ-ameng . Iwernga maaten Kiyaghneghem Taghneghagkenka ughvughqegkaqiisi seghleghqelleghpesineng , aaftekaqiisi Kiyaghneghmun , seghleghqumangilngughestunllu lliightekaagusi qayughllak ugpeqilghiisi Ataneghqun Jesus Christ-akun .
Ilasi pikaagut , " Itagnaghtuq sangwaa piyukelqa piyaghngaamkun . " Iwernga whanga piimsi , ilangan salleghpesi kayuusiinnaanghitii ugpellesi . Aa , entaqun , " Itagnaghtuq sangwaa piyukelqa piyaghngaamkun . " Iwernga sumeghtaghaghyalghiinga seghleghmun ayghipagllagnayukama pinaanghitunga .
Kinallu pinayalghii , " Neqa ulimaaghuuq aqsaqumun , aqsaquq neqmun . " Aa , iwernga ilangani aghneghem Kiyaghneghem naafqesaghqaqaak qamagllukek aqsaquqlu neqallu . Yugusiq sex-kun seghleghqusighqaanghisaghtuq qayughllak yugusiq Ataneghmun pinguuq , Ataneq yugusimnnun pinguuq .
Ilangani aghneghem Kiyaghneghem makesaghqaqii yugusiput tuqulleghmeng aghtughyaghqaanghilleghmikun , tawateghpigaq maketelleghmitun Ataneq Jesus Christ-a tuqulleghmeng .
Liisimakenghistegguu yugusisi nalighneqegkangi Christ-am yugusiin ? Yugusiqa Christ-am piliitkaa atuqnaaghsikuun aghnamun akikikayugmeng yugusimineng ? Nakaa ! Pinaanghitaqa .
Neqamikluku , yugem atuqegkumigu aghnaq akikilghii yugusimineng ataasiightekayugek yugusiik . Qayughllak igaqngaaq Akuzitni Igaqegkani , " Maalghuk yugusik ataasighsaghqaaguk . "
Iwernga Ataneghmun lliiquvek , ataasiigutek taghneghakun .
Liisimakenghistegguu yugusisi Kiyaghneghem Temple-kegkangi , Agleghnalghiim Taghneghagkenka kiyaghfigi ? Kiyaghneghem tuunegkaqiisi Agleghnalghiigneng Taghneghaghmineng , enkaam maaten Kiyaghneghem piliitkaqiisi . Elpesineng pikenghitusi . Tamaaken apalluqluku sex-kun seghleghqegpenasi . Sex-kun seghleghqegkufsi , nukeggnaghqelghiistun Kiyaghneghem Temple-nga pilleqaghsi . Ilangi seghleghqellghet tawatenneghitut . Kiyaghneghem tukfiqaqiisi akitupiglluku . Tamaaken apalluqluku quulvaghteggu Kiyaghneq yugusighpesigun .
Aaptekaqaghpesinga nengughutelleghmeng latagpesigun . Ukusta kiimsiitenka . Pinightuq yuuk nuliingunani .
Iwernga yuuk tamaghhaghmi nuliilguyaghqaaguq , aghnaq tamaghhaghmi ugilguyaghqaaguq , qayughllak nanghiiqullengnayukafsi sex-kun seghleghqelleghmun .
Yugem efqughsaghqaqaa nuliini . Tawategghpigaq aghnam efqusaghqaqaa ugini atuqutelleghmegni .
Aghnam ellnginaghmi yugusini pikenghitaa , uginganllu pikaa . Tawateghpigaq yugem ellnginaghmi yugusini pikenghitaa , nulighhanllu pikaa .
Nengughsimakufsi ighsakutegpenasi . Wetkuqun itagnaqullusi atuqusaghqaafqaafsi qafsinat unuget yughaghataghaghnalusi . Taagken atuqunneqiglleghhaasi nanghiiqullengnayukafsi Tughneghagh-meng qayughllak nuqesaghqaananiqaalghiisi .
Qelghunghitamsi nulightiisqellusi nalighmeng ugiighesqellusi . Iwernga piyukufsi pilghaasi .
Whangamtuntuq nulightufqaafsi , aghnanillu ugiifqaafsi . Iwernga allakutukut . Kiyaghneghem nuliilgustekayugii ilangi yuget , ugilgustekayugii ilangi aghnat . Iwernga itagnaghtestekayugii ilangi yuget nuliingunaki , aghnatlu ugingunaki . Kiyaghneghem allakullghii tunusaq tuunegkayuwaa yugnunllu aghnanunllu .
Unata pikegka nulightuumangilngughnun , ugiighumangilngughnunllu , ugingighanunllu : Pinighnayaghtusi nulightunghisaqufsi whangamtun , aghnanillu ugiinghisaqufsi .
Iwernga yuuk pinighataghaghnayaghtuq nulightughluni nuqetepagningilnguq aghnaghyulleghmineng . Aghnaqlu pinighataghaghnayaghtuq ugiighluni nuqetepagnengilnguq yugyulleghmineng . Pinighataghaghnayaghtusi nengughllusi nanghiiqullengelleghqaghpesineng seghleghqelleghmun sex-kun .
Ukut akuzitet whangamneng pingunghitut , qelghusaagut Ataneghmeng nengughtekanun . Aghnaq iqisaghqaanghituq ugimineng .
Iwernga iqiskumi , allaneng ugiighyaghqaanghituq nalighmeng ugiminun lliinqiglli . Yugemllu iqitesaghqaqenghitaa nuliini .
Una qelghusaq whangamneng pinguuq ilangitnun . ( Atanghem sameng piighsimangitaa . ) Yuuk ugpeqaq ugpeqaanghilngughmeng nuliilgukumi ellminisulghiimeng , iqitesneghilligu .
Aghnaqlu ugpeqaq ugpeqaanghilngughmeng ugilgukumi ellminisulghiimeng , iqinneghilli .
Inqun yuuk ugpeqaanghilnguq aaftengngwaaqaaguq Kiyaghneghmun qayughllak nulighha ugpeqaalghii . Aghnaqlu ugpeqaanghilnguq aaftengngwaaqaaguq Kiyaghneghmun qayughllak uginga ugpeqaalghii . Tamaaken apalluqluku taghnughhiit pelungitutlu aaftengngwaaqaagutlu .
Iwernga naliq ugpeqaanghilnguq iqisukumi , iqilli . Taagken ugpeqaq yuuk nalighmeng aghnaq itemli tawatelngughmeng nengughtelleghmineng . Kiyaghneghem nekeggmellusi kiyaghtesqesugaqiisi .
Ugpeqami aghnami , ugigpeniskuvek kayusiitaqsaaghan yugulilleghmun . Nalighmeng ugpeqami yugmi , nuliighpeniskuvek kayusiitaqsaaghan yugulilleghmun .
