Kiyaghneghem ataasikaghtaghpesi ugpeqistaqngisi Christ-ameng , nengughtekaatsii nalighmeng nengughsimangitsii ? Circumcise-ekaatsii nalighmeng pimangitsii ? Qepghaghtelaaghuyaghetsii nalighmeng qepghaghtelaaghunghitetsii ? Almesiqlusi tawaten nagneghtek qayughllak Atanghem tawatetestekaqiisi . Qamaglluki ugpeqat taagken apeghtughaqanka .
Yuuk circumcise-ekaq ugpeghaqngami , allangughtefqaami pilghaaq . Circumcise-emangilnguqlu ugpeqaq , circumcise-enaqefqaami pilghaaq .
Circumcise-elleqlu circumcise-enghitelleqlu pitngunghituk . Pitnguyaghqaqta taana qaatkelluki Kiyaghneghem Liilightuusii .
Ataasikaghtaghpesi ugpeqiiqngafsi , natetelleghpesistun almesiqiteggu .
Qepghaghtelaaghuyaghsiin Kiyaghneghem tuqlughaqngaten ? Sumeghtaghaatkegpenaan . Iwernga qepghaghtelaaghunanighnaqngukuvek , saaqsin legan tawaten pilghaaten .
Qepghaghtelaaq nakmikegkaa Atanghem , ellngan itemngalghiikaa . Tawateghpigaq qepghaghtelaaghunghilnguq yuuk nakmikegkaa Christ-am , ellngan qepghaghtelaaqaa .
Kiyaghneghem tukfighpakaqiisi , enkaam qepghaghtelaaghughtegpenasi yugnun .
Ugpeqaalgutemni , tamaghhaghpesi aghuliisaghqaagusi ilatngalleghpesigun Kiyaghneghmun almesiqlusi tawaten tuqlullghatun .
Aaptaqaghpesinga naten sumeghtaghaatkaqutangi ugiighumangilnguutlu nulightuumangilnguutlu . Atanghem ungipaasimangitaanga Liilightuusameng tamaakunun yugnun , iwernga ungipaannaqamsi sumeghtaghallemneng . Kiyaghneghem nangllegtallghakun apostle-ngughtekaagunga . Tamaaken apalluqluku neghyuknakefsinga .
Seghleliighllagughtuq nuna maaten . Sumemni whanga itagnaghyaghqaaguq yuuk almesiqluni .
Nulightuumaziin ? Iqitestegpenaan nulighhen . Nulightuumangilkuvek , nulightughnaqegpenang .
Iwernga nulightuquvek seghleghqengngunghituten . Ugiighumangilnguq ugiiqumi , seghleghqengngunghituq . Iwernga nulightuqufsi , aghnatlu ugiiqumeng piyaqliighataghaghyaghqaagusi whani kiyaghtaalleghmi . Piyaqliightesunghitepigtamsi tawaten .
Ugpeqaalgutemni , unata pikegka : Ataneghput tagiyaghtungestaghtuq . Taana apalluqluku nengughtekat qepghaallitgu Ataneq nengughsimangilngughestun .
Qivghulghiitlu qepghaallitgu qivghunghilngughestun . Quyangalghiitlu qepghaallitgu quyanghilngughestun . Tamaakutlu tukfightughllakayuget qepghaallitgu avangilngughestun .
Kiyaghtengngulusi nunami whani , megnukataghaghpenaan nunam sanqutanga . Qayughllak nuna almesiqluni aviighusaghqaaguq .
Kiyaghtaalleghmengtuq whaken sumeghtaghaatkegkiilnguusi . Nulightuumangilnguq qepghalleghqaghtaaghatuq Atanghem qepghaqaaneng qayughllak efqughsugaqegkanga .
Nuliilek qepghaghataghaqayuquuq kiyaghtaallghem qepghaqaaneng qayughllak efqughsugaqegkanga nuliini . Enkaam sumeghtaghallgha malghughqengngaaquq .
Tawateghpigaq aghnatlu ayuqut . Aghnat ugingiitkat , ugiighumangilnguutlu qepghalleghqaghtaaghatut Atanghem qepghaqaaneng , qayughllak yugusitengllu taghneghatengllu tuunyugaqiit iinguniita Ataneghmun . Iwernga ugilek qepghaghataghaqayuguuq kiyaghtaallghem qepghaqaaneng qayughllak efqughsugaqegkanga ugini . Ellnganllu sumeghtaghallgha malghughqengngaaq .
Tawaten piimsi kayusiinnalusi . Nengughtesnaninghitamsi . Iwernga nakmikesugaqa pinilleghpigaq elpesinun qepghaatesqelluku Ataneq uglafqusingunasi .
Nuliighqalgem atuqsugyaguskumigu nuliighqani , nengughllik . Enkaam nengughtekumek seghleghqengngunaanghituk .
Iwernga yugem liisimakngwaaqumigu naten pilleghqani , nuqetutngukumigullu atuqsulleghmineng nuliighqani , pinitun pinguuq . Kitum alngunak nulightiisqughaanghilkumigu , nulightughyunghilkumi pinitun pinguuq .
Nuliighqalek nengughlluni pinitun pinguuq , iwernga nuliighqalek nengughhneghilkumi pinighataghatun pinguuq .
Aghnaq allaneng ugiighyaghqaanghituq ugini kiyaghlluku . Iwernga ugini tuqukan , piyukelleghmineng ugiighyaghngaaghmi itagnaghtuq , taawanginaq ugpeqaghhiinaghmeng .
Iwernga quyangaaghataghaghyaghqaaguq ugiinqiggneghilkuni . Taakusta sumeghtaghallghenka . Ugpeqaqa Kiyaghneghem Taghneghakek whangamnituk .
Kiimsighyuganka aapqughaallesi neqneng aghqutkegkaneng kiyaghnengllaqanun . Ipanguuq whaten pilleghsi , " Liisimallelguukut qamaglluta . " Tawatelnguq liisimalleq aangaayugtestikayuguuq , iwernga piniqellghem iknaqughtengngwaa ugpelleghput .
Yuuk pillguyugneq , esghaghhuta taana paninang liisaghqaghtuqaq .
Iwernga Kiyaghneghem piniqisteni whaten piyaghqaqii , " Whanga pikanka . "
Enkaam neghelleqestaa aghqutkegkameng kiyaghnengllaqanun ? Liisimakaput kiyaghnengllaqat kiyaghneghunghitut . Ataasighhaaguq Kiyaghneq , alla kiyaghneghituq .
Ilangita yuget ugpeqaqaat kiyaghneghtuniluku , ataneghtuniluku qilaklu nunallu .
Iwernga whangkuta liisimakaghput ataasighhaaguq Kiyaghneq , ellnga Atanghuuq . Sangwaa qamaglluni ellnganeng pinguuq , kiyaghtengnguukut ellnganun . Liisimakaghputlu ataasighhaaguq Ataneq , Jesus Christ-anguuq . Ellngakun sangwaa qamaglluni ulimakaaguq , unguvanguukutlu ellngakun .
Ilangita ugpeqat nallukiit kiyaghnengllaqat kiyaghnepigunghitulangi . Tamaaken apalluqluku ugpeqaqiit neqet aghqutkaqniluki kiyaghnepignun . Enkaam neneghmeggni aghqutkegkameng sumeghtaghaghaqut , " Seghleghqunga . "
Iwernga neqa pitngunghituq . Kiyaghneghem usuqataghaghnaanghitiisi neghelleghpesigun neqmeng . Aghqutkegkameng neghenghilkumta sangwaa alngunak iflanaanghitaghput Kiyaghneghmeng ayuqelghii . Talwa negheghngaamta allgeghunnanghitukut ellnganeng .
Ugpeqaghllagni elpesi , piyukelleghpesistun piyaghqaalghiisi , liigikngategpesineng taana ipapighqelleq apeghtuusaqegkaqa . Iwernga kelengalusi kayaalnguut ugpellghit ayuqniighqegpenaki ellngita sumeghtaghallghitni anaggutngalghiimeng .
Naliita esghaqumiten neghumaluten kiyaghnengllaqat temple-ngitni , ellngallu neghyugyaaghtuq sumeghtaghalleghmini anaggutngayaghngaan .
Enkaam liisimalleghpek seghleghqestesaaghaa kayaalnguq ugpellgha iflasluku , ugpeqaalgutkan Christ-am tuqutkegkaa .
Enkaangam ayuqniighqegkufsiki sumeghtaghallghitni anaggutngalghiimeng , seghleghqellequsi ellngitnunllu Christ-amunllu .
Enkaam neghellemkun aghqutqegkameng seghleghqesnayukamkun ugpeqaalgutka , allamengllu neghnaanghitunga sameng tamaaken .
Itemngaanga , piyukellemtun piyaghqaagunga . Apostle-nguunga esghaatkaq Jesus-meng Atanemnneng . Qepghaatellemkun ellnga ugpeqaagusi elpesi .
Talwa ilangita apostle-epigunghinnighngaatnga elpesi liisimakaghpesinga apostle-epiiguunga Ataneghqun , qayughllak kiyaghtaalleghpesi Christ-amun kelguskanga .
Taakusta aapghaqegkenka seghleqistemnun .
Barnabas-lu whangkutung tungsighnaanghistuung neghyaghqamengllu meghyaghqamengllu elpesineng apeghtuqamtegneng ?
Navek pinemtung kelqepagningitestegnekii ugpeqat nuliipung ilangistun apostle-et , Atanghem anglegutangistunllu , Peter-etunllu ?
Barnabas-lu whangkutuung ellnginaghhaamtung qepghaasimanginaghyaghqaqestegneguu neqekaghqaghpung ?
Pilluwaghtem tukfighyaghqaqenghitii saghyani pilluwaghtenilluni . Tawateghpigaq grapes-meng piitesiighaghtem neghegkayugii ilangi piitestekani . Penniighniightemllu penniighmi mamaan ilanga pikayugaa .
Taakut usputat yugem apeghtuusaqii , iwernga Kiyaghneghem Liilightusaanillu apeghtuusat tawatetut .
Igaqegkaaguq Liilightuusani , Kiyaghneghem tuunegkaakun Moses-mun : " Sugrugiitalighpenan ox-a wheat-et tutmaghtesneghpesiki qantiit sigiqesqelluki . " Kiyaghneghem sumeghmikenghitaguu ox-a ?
Sangami Kiyaghneq tawaten pii ? Ox-nginaghhaaq suumqaguu ? Nakaa , whangkutallu suumqaqiinkut . Ipapestaaq whangkunnunllu igaqegkaaguq , qayughllak piitesighaghvigmeng yataaghqistenunllu saghnastenunllu neghyukegkayugaaput nengighqaput .
Kiyaghneghem akuzitangi piisaghqastun ayuqut . Whangkutung piitesighaghvikegkaqamsi , enkaam taghneghasi quyastekaagut . Tungsipaglleqestuung tungsighvikegkumsi aklukegkamtegneng ?
Apeghtughistem ilangi elpesineng allgeghutngukata aklukegkameggneng , whangkutung wataqaaghaq piyaghqaghpigaayaghtukung . Yeghlegi qepghaghyukaagukung maningeregaghnalutung aklukegkamtegneng allgeghunnalutung . Ilangani manipagitaqukung . Talwa tamaani aapsugigatamsi akileghtiisqellutung . Unata apalluqa , kitumun alngunak whaten pisunghitukung , " Paul ungipaqiiquq Pinilghiineng Ungipaneng akileghtuusangepigesnaghnaluni . "
Liisimakasi Temple-em qepghaghtengi neghegkayuget neqmeng Temple-mun tuunegkameng . Aghqefigemllu qepghaghtengi nengiqayuguut aghqutkaghqameng .
Tawatetuq Atanghem qelghusaa : Ungipaghtetlu Pinilghiineng Ungipaneng aklukegkateng allgeghsaghqaqiit tamaakuneng ugpeqikaneng Pinilghiineng Ungipaneng .
Elpesineng sameng alngunak allgeghusigatunga pikaghqaqsaqemneng . Sumeghtaghaatkegpenanga sameng alngunak tungsighnilunga maaten . Quyaaqunga akileghtiisqigalnguunga elpesinun ungipaqinemni Pinilghiineng Ungipaneng . Ungipaqinaqnguunga akileghtuusiiteghngaaghma talwa paneghyaghngaaghma . Enkaam kitum alngunak pinaanghitaanga , " Paul ungipaqiiquq Pinilghiineng Ungipaneng akileghtuusangepigesnaghnaluni . "
Iwernga aangaayugusighqiitunga ungipaqinemni Pinilghiineng Ungipaneng , qayughllak Kiyaghneghem qelqaqaanga ungipaqisqellunga . Seghleghwaaghunayaghtunga qaatkenghisaqumkun Kiyaghneq .
Nakmikegkaqsaqumkun una qepghaqaq whangamneng akileghtuusaghqalgunilunga pinayaghtunga , iwernga Kiyaghneghem nakmikegkaqutanganeng piyaghqaqaqa akileghtuusiiteghngaaghma . Alla naten pilleghqiitunga .
Sangaawa akileghtuusaqa ? Akileghtuusaqaqa una , quyapigtaqunga akileghtuusangunanga ungipaqinemni Pinilghiineng Ungipaneng , qaywa akileghtughyaghqaqsaghngaaghpesinga .
Qepghaghtelaaghunghisaghngaaghma , whangamneng katam qepghaghtelaaghughtekaagunga kitumun alngunak , yugmun uglalghiimun ugpeqesqelluku Christ-a .
Jews-eninnemni kiyaghtaqunga ellngistun , ugpeqesqelluku Christ-a . Kiyaghhnemni Gentile-eni Liilightuusatgun kiyaghtaaghni , ellngistun kiyaghtaqunga liisimakeghngaamkun qaatkutellemkun Liilightuusatgun yugulillengyaghqaanghiteghngaaghma , ugpeqesqelluku Christ-a .
Gentile-eninnemni nallukilghiini Liilightuusaneng , ellngistun kiyaghtaqunga nallukelghiistun Liilightuusat , ugpeqesqelluku Christ-a . Qaatkengngunghinniluki pingunghitanka Kiyaghneghem Liilightuusii , iwernga qaatkengngwaanka Christ-am Liilightuusii .
Kayaalngughni kiyaghhnemni ellngistun lliighaqunga , ugpeqesqelluku Christ-a . Enkaangam kinkustun alngunak kiyaghtaqunga natesaghngaata , naten alngunak yugulillengesqelluki .
Tawaten piiqunga nagaqiisqeqeghlluki Pinilghiineng Ungipaneng , qayughllak quyastellengaqelghiingallu ugpeqenghatgu Christ-a .
Qamaglluteng ketanqustet sivuliiyukayuguut , iwernga ataasighhaq kayaalqiikayuguuq . Kiyaghtaalleghpesini Christ-amun , ketanqustestun kayaalqiinaqaqitek .
Ketanqustet ulapaqut yugusiteng iknaqughhnaluki qayughllak qaghpangyugaqelghiit avayameng ququngalegmeng . Tamaakut palighyaghqaagut . Iwernga qaghpa ugpeqat allgeghsaghqaat quunpekaghqaaguq .
Ketanqustestun taklaghruketun ketanqwaaqunga kaannalunga kenlemun . Nalighmeng tenglugtestun , tenglugpagaataghaqunga kayaalqiinalunga .
Ungipaqiiqunga naten kiyaghtelleghqameng Christ-amun . Whangallu kiyaghtengnguunga ellnganun enkaam yugusimnun qaatkestaqunga , luuraq pinghilkuma Kiyaghneghem iqinnayukanganga ellmineng .
Ugpeqaalgutemni , sumeghtaghaatkesqesuganka Jews-et , maligsaaghikat Moses-meng . Egypt-meng aghulaqaqngameng qamaglluteng maligtekaqaat qilawaaq , maghyaghqughilghii tuumkaghqiitgun . Kaasata Kavilngughmun Kelliimun , Kiyaghneghem pelleghtekaqegkanga meq aghviisqelluki yaywaaseng .
Qamaglluteng paaptaayekaalghiit qilawaaghqunllu Kavilngughqunllu Kelliikun maligsaaghtenguluteng Moses-mun .
Qamaglluteng neghegkaagut manna-meng ,
meghegkaagut ataasimeng taagken meghmeng Kiyaghneghem Taghneghagkenka tuunegkaaneng . Meghegkaqaat meq maaqegkaq uyghagmeng . Taam uyghagem maligsaaqaqegkangi Kiyaghneghem Taghneghagkenkun . Uyghak taana Christ-anguuq .
Tawaten Kiyaghneghem aflengakegkaqeghngiisteng , paninang allulluteng efqughsimangilkangat ellnga . Enkaam tumangani Kiyaghneghem tuqustaqluki yugusighqwaaghit mingitkaalghiit kilgaani .
Tamaana qamaglluni pillghat whangkunnun usputaaguq , kelengasaaghiinkut ellngistun piyukefqaan seghleq pisqelluku .
Manigughtengughtegpenasi kiyaghnengllaqanun ilangistun . Akuzitni Igaqegkani igaqegkaaguq , " Yugetlu aghnatlu neghaqut , meghaqut taagken aghulaaqut . " Tawaten maniguutkaagut gold-meng ulimaaghmun kaawaghaghmun .
Seghleghqefqaamta sex-kun ilangistun . Allgeghnegha seghleghqellghita 23,000 yuuk tuqulaghaatkaaguq ataasimi aghneghmi .
Nanghiiqunaqefqaamteggu Atanghem nuqenneghtullgha pilteggu , ilangistun . Nemeghyat tuququqaqiit ilangi sivuneput qayughllak nanghiiqukaqegkangat Ataneq .
Akuzilgaghpenasi ilangistun . Yaqulgem tuqustikayugem tuququqaqii ilangi sivuneput qayughllak akuzilgaatkaqegkangat Kiyaghneq .
Qamaglluki tamaakut sivunemta atuqegkiit , usputaghqaakaagut whangkunnun . Igaqegkaagut kelengasaatnguluteng whangkunnun kiyaghlleghhiinun kingulighni aghneghni , ellngistun pifqaamta pisqelluta .
Enkaam kina alngunak sumeghmini pikumi ugpelleni aghuliinniluku , kelengali luuraq seghleghqesaaghtuq .
Qamaglluteng nanghiiqullesi allakaayagunghitut yugnun . Iwernga Kiyaghneq atasiighmetuq , nanghiiqulleghmun qaasghutesaghqaqenghitii iknaqellesi , iknaqellelitaqnaaghiisi nuqetusighqameng . Enkaam iqitaqellequsi taagken nanghiiqulleghmeng .
Piniqegkamni , maniguutegpenasi kiyaghnengllaqanun .
Aleghqughamsi sumeghnelgulusi , sumeghtaghaatkennakesi sameng pilqa .
Iyamsiqayagunnemteggu qayuusimelnguq wine-a Atanghem Neqenghaghqellghani , nengighaqukut Christ-am aawaneng . Iiggemnneng aavgughluku neqekrangllaq nenemteggu , nengighaqukut Christ-am yugusiineng .
Neqekrangllaq aavguqaaghngaaghmi ataasiiguq . Uglaghllagyaghngaamta , ataasimeng taagken neghaqukut . Enkaam kelgutaqaa nalighnequghniluta ataasimun yugusimun .
Sumeghtaghaatkaghtekiqun Israel-eghmiit ; neneghmeggni aghqutkegkameng , ilataqut maniguullghiinun Kiyaghneghmun aghqefigegni .
Sumeghpesinii kiyaghnengllaqat kiyaghnepiwaat ? Neqetlu aghqutkegkat kiyaghnengllaqanun , maniguusipiwaaqaat ?
Nakaa ! Nallukilghiit Kiyaghneghmeng aghqerraaghaqut tughneghaghnun , nakan Kiyaghneghmun . Ilatngastesunghitamsi tughneghaghnun .
Christ-amun piliitestekaakufsi tughneghaat maliggnaanghitasi . Tamaaken apalluqluku Atanghem qayuusiineng meghegkufsi , tughneghaatlu qayuusiitneng meghnaanghitusi . Tawateghpigaq Atanghem Neqenghaghqellghani neghegkayugukufsi neqekrangllameng Atanghem tipelegkeni , tughneghaatlu tipelngitni neghnaanghitusi neqmeng .
Whangkuta Christ-am piliitkiitni tughneghaat maliggnaqegkumteki , Kiyaghneq qungyaghtesleqaghput . Neqamikluku ellnga iknaqeghllagtuq whangkunneng .
Ilasi pikaagut , " Itagnaghtuq sangwaa piyukelqa piyaghngaamkun . " Iwernga whanga piimsi , ilangi sallesi pininghitut . Aa-a , entaqun , " Itagnaghtuq sangwaa piyukelqa piyaghngaamkun , " iwernga ilangan salleghpesi kayuusiinnaanghitii ugpellesi .
Kina alngunak ellnginaayugtefqaami piiqli , yeghlegi ilanillu sumeghtaghaatkaqluki .
Sangwaa alngunak kemekrak tukfiqaghsi estugaghmeng neghaqiteggu sumeghtaghaatkegpenaan aghqutkegkaatanga kiyaghnengllaqanun .
Qayughllak igaqegkaaguq Akuzitni Igaqegkani , " Nuna , sangwaatlu qamagtengngwaaghluki tawanlenguut Atanghem pikii . "
Ugpeqaanghilnguum neghyaghtiisqegkangisi piyukufsi pilghaasi . Sangwaa alngunak ketfaghtuqaat neghaqiteggu sumeghtaghaatkegpenaan aghqutkegkaatanga kiyaghnengllaqanun .
Iwernga kitum pikangisi , " Taana aghqutkegkaaguq kiyaghnengllaqanun , " neghegpenaan , ungipaatistegpesi ugpellgha kayaalisnayukafsigu , qayughllak ellngani anaggutngalghiinguuq . Entaqun sumeghtaghaghnayalghiisi , " Sangamatuq piyukellemtun piyaghqaanghisinga ? Sangamatuq kitum ineghqughaghaqanga allatun sumeghtaghaqayugem whangamneng ?
Iyamsiqayugvikegkumkun Kiyaghneq neghyaghqamneng , sangan始ngam kitum seghlequughlleqanga neghegkuma iyamsiqayugutkegkamneng ? "
Enkaam qamaglluku salleghsi quulvaasiqaqiteggu Kiyaghneghmun , talwa neghellesillu meghellesillu .
Sagpenasi seghleghqestiyaghqameng Jews-enun , Gentile-enun , ugpeqanunllu .
Efqughhnaqutkaqanka yulgutenka sallemkun alngunak . Whanganginamnun pinilleghqaq pingigataqa , iwernga pinighqelleghqiitnunllu yulgutma piiqunga , uglalghii yugulillengesqelluku .
Enkaam whangamtun piiqitek , katam whanga maligtellemtun Christ-a .
Usuqamsi neqamikegkefsinga , atuqegkesillu apeghtuusanka .
Iwernga liigikesugamsi Christ-a naasquutinguuq tamaghhaanun yugnun , yuguuqlu naasquutilghii nuliighmineng .
Nasqughiitighluni yuuk yughaqumi nalighmeng ungipaqumi Kiyaghneghem ungipaaneng yughaghvigmi , quulvaghyaghqaqenghitaa naasquutilghi .
Enkaam aghnaq nasqughiitighpenani yughaqumi nalighmeng ungipaqumi Kiyaghneghem ungipaaneng , quulvaghyaghqaqenghitaa naasquutilghii . Tawaten pikumi qigughwaaqastun meqesluni ayuqellequq .
Aghnaq nasqughiitighyunghilkumi , kepughli nuyiighulluni . Iwernga aghnani kayngunalghiinguuq qigulleqlu nuyiighullunillu kepulleq , enkaam nasqughiitighngali .
Yuuk nasqughiitighyaghqaanghituq maniguuskumi qayughllak Kiyaghneghem nangaghneghatun ulimaaghuuq , Kiyaghneghem aangellgha esghiisqelluku . Iwernga aghnaq ulimaaghuq yugem aangellgha esghiisqelluku .
Liisimakegkesi yuuk aghnameng ulimaaghunghilnguq , iwernga aghnaq yugmeng ulimaaghulghii .
Yuuk ulimaaghunghituqlu aghnamun iwernga aghnaq ulimaaghuuq yugmun .
Taana apalluqluku aghnaq nasqughiitighyaghqaaguq , enkaam yaqulget liigiklitgu yuuk aghnamun naasquutingutanga .
Iwernga neqamikiteggu Atanghem uspeqellgha , yugenkuk aghnaankuk aklukutngaak .
Aghnaqsuggaaq yugmeng ulimaaghughngaan , taagken kenlanga yuuk qamaglluni allgeqaaguq aghnameng , iwernga aghnatlu yugetlu qamaglluteng Kiyaghneghmeng pinguut .
Sumeghtaghaatkaghtegguqun : ipa anaggutngaa aghnam nasqughiitangunani yughallgha Kiyaghneghmun ?
Yuget quunpeng ugpeqaqaat nuyiightekaghnguq yuuk ukavaghtaquq ellmineng ,
iwernga aghnam nuyaghllani quulvaasiqaa . Nasqughiitaghqaaluni ellnganun pikaaguq .
Paninang kina aaghtiiraaghyugukumi nasqughiitameng , ungipaanneqigtaghllakun taanata apostle-eni apeghtuusaqaqegkefut , Kiyaghneghem yugan atuqaqaat apeghtuusaq naansaghngaaghmeng .
Whaken apeghtughyugamsi qerngughutaqelleghpesineng maniguutelleghmun . Usuqepagningitamsi qerngughutaqelleghpesinun qayughllak aqnighquutaghaghaqusi pinighqutegpenasi .
Ungipaataqaatnga qerngughunneghpesininguq ilasi aafqemeraaghutaqut , ataasistun pigpenateng . Ugpeqekestaghluku lliighaqa .
Entaqun aafquutelleghpesigun liigiksaghqaqasi nalisi ipa qaatkutngatangi Ataneghmun .
Enkaam qerngughunneghpesini Atanghem Neghestillghanun , neghyaghtuunghitaqaghsi .
Neghuunneghpesini tamaghhaghpesi neragkiighaqusi neqegpesineng , ilasi utaqagpenaki . Enkaam ilasi iyataghaqut , ilasi suumaqut .
Neghigatsii-i , meghigatsii-i negpesini ? Nalighmeng ugumikestekii Kiyaghneghem yugi ? Kayngusaghaatesnaqutkaqestekii avangilnguut ? Sameng pilamsi ? Usuqlamsii ? Nakaa , usuqnaanghitamsi !
Sangwaa liitkaqa Ataneghmeng apeghtuusaqaqaqa elpesinun . Atanghem Jesus-em ighivgaghmi tawani uveghpagutelleghqamini tugukaa neqekrangllaq .
Iyamsiqayugviksamigu Kiyaghneq , aavgughluku , pikaq , " Una yugusiqaqa elpesinun pinguuq . Neghaqiteggu neqamikusiiluku whangamneng . "
Neneghmeng taaqsameng , tawateghpigaq tuguluku qayuusiq wine-eghraghaghmeng imalek , pikaq , " Una qayuusiq Kiyaghneghem nutaghaaguq akequsaa aamkun . Awen meghaqiteggu neqamikusiiluku whangamneng . "
Enkaam quunpeng neneghpesini taagken neqekrangllameng , meneghpesinillu taagken qayuusimeng , kelgutngwaaqaghsi Atanghem tuqullgha kenlanga alla tagilleghqaanun .
Kina alngunak temngi neghegkumi Atanghem neqekrangllaaneng , meghegkumillu Atanghem qayuusiineng , quulvaghnaanghitaa Atanghem yugusiillu aawallu .
Tamaaken apalluqluku sivukluni yugem avuteghqutkelliki seghleghqelleni alla piyaghqaafqiita pinaluki . Enkaam neghelghaaq neqekrangllameng , meghelghaaqlu qayuusimeng .
Kina alngunak neghelghii neqekrangllameng , meghelghiillu qayuusimeng , Atanghem yugusii liigiknaqegpenaan sameng pisiitanga nanqigtellengyaghqaaquq Ataneghmeng .
Taana apalluqluku uglaghtusi kayaalngughnillu qinuyugngalghiinillu enkaam qafsinat tuqulaghaatkaagut .
Iwernga ipapighqelluta nanqigtekumta whangkunneng katam enkaam avuteghqutkegkumteki seghleghqelleput , Atanghem nanqiggnaanghitiinkut tawaten pikumta .
Iwernga Atanghem apeghtughyuneghminikut naten kiyaghtelleghqameng , nanqigtaqiinkut . Aghyuughyaghqaafqaamta pinaluta nanqigtikumi ugpeqingigalngughneng .
Enkaam ugpeqaalgutemni qerngughunneghpesini neghnalusi Atanghem Neqenghaghqellghaneng neghekestaghpenasi , utaqatutaqlusi .
Iyatalghiit tamaakut nemeggni neghlit enkaangam Atanghem nanqiggneghilliki . Aglaquma elpesinun ilangi aaptekasi kiimsighnaaghanka .
Ugpeqaalgutemni , liitesugamsi Agleghnalghiim Taghnegham tunusaaneng .
Neqamikaghsi salin ugpellghillusi maniguutestaataqaqegkangisi kiyaghnengllaqanun akuzingigalngughnun . Aaghqutaqestekaalghiisi .
Tamaaken apalluqluku liigikesugamsi kina alngunak whaten pilghii , " Jesus seghleghuuq , " Agleghnalghiim Taghnegham akuzistengngunghitaa tawaten . Iwernga kina alngunak whaten pilghii , " Jesus Atanghuuq , " Agleghnalghiim Taghnegham akuzistengngwaa tawaten .
Agleghnalghiim Taghnegham tunusii allaghhiinaagut , iwernga tunusat qamaglluki taam ataasim Taghnegham tunusaqii .
Uglapigtuq allaaghhiinaq qepghaatilleghqaq ilamun , iwernga taana ataasiq Ataneq qepghaatellengaquq .
Uglaapigtuq allakullghii Kiyaghneghem qepghaqaa , iwernga taam ataasim Kiyaghneghem pistaqii whangkunnun .
Agleghnalghiim Taghnegham liitestekayugaa aghtughyaghqaanghilleni ugpeqatgun tunusalitkamikun . Tunusat kitumun alngunak pinighqusighqaagut .
Taam ataasim Taghnegham yugem ilangi akuzistaqii peghqinelleghmikun , ilangi liisimalleghmikun .
Taam ataasim Taghnegham ugpeqillelitaghaqaqii ilangi yuget , ilangi aghtughyaghqaanghillelitaqii naallghutiyaghqaaluki aqnighneghneng .
Taghnegham tuunegkaqii ilangi yuget allaaghlluwhaghtisighqameng . Ilangan yugem tugukliqaqaa ungipaqilleghqaq Kiyaghneghem ungipaaneng . Ilangan yugem tugukliqaqaa liigikilleghqaq Agleghnalghiim Taghegham nalighmeng tughneghaat igleghutngutanga kina . Agleghnalghiim Taghnegham akuzistaqii ilangi yuget allaaghhiinakun ulukun . Enkaam ilangitnun mumighqughtestaqii akuzillghet .
Qamaglluteng tamaakut tunusat ataasikaghtaghhaghmeng taagken ataasigneng Taghneghagneng pinguut . Tuunyukani tamaakut naliitneng tunusaghqami tuunaqii .
Katam yugusiq ataasiq nalighneghtughllak , qamaglluteng nalighneghet yugusim pikegkangi . Qaywa uglaghngaaghmeng ataasiiguq yugusiq , Christ-allu tawatetuq .
Qamaglluki ugpeqat nalighnequghii Christ-am yugusiin . Ilaput Jews-nguut , ilangi Gentile-et , ilangi qepghaghtelaaghet , ilangi qepghaghtelaaghunghitut . Iwernga qamaglluta paaptaayekaagukut taaggun ataasikun Agleghnalghiignekun Taghneghagnekun , Christ-amun yugusiliitesqelluta . Qamaglluta tugukliqaqagput ataasik Taghneghak .
Yugusiq ataasiinghituq nalighneq , nalighneghtupigtuq .
Itegat whaten pighngaaghmeng , " Iiggengunghilnguunga , yugusim pikenghitaanga . " Taaqnaanghitngwaaghtut yugusimenneghmeng .
Siguta whaten pighngaaghmi , " Iiyngunghitunga , yugusim pikenghitaanga . " Taaqnaanghitngwaaghtuq yugusimenneghmeng .
Yugusiq iyeraaghinaayaqumi , naten始ngam nagaqughnayaghta ? Nalighmeng siguteraaghinaayaqumi , naten始ngam naaghunnayaghta sapagnimeng ?
Iwernga Kiyaghneghem ulimamangitii yugusiput tawatelluki . Nakmikegkamineng nalighnelightuqaqii .
Yugusiq ataasiiyaqumi nalighneq yugusiinayanghituq .
Ipapestaaq yugusiq nalighneghtupigtuq .
Tamaken apalluqluku iyem pinanghitii iigget , " Aklukenghitamsi . " Tawateghpigaq naasqum pinanghiti itegat , " Aklukenghitamsi . "
Ipapestaaq yugusimta natangi kayaatesugnilnguut megnunapigtut .
Yugusimta natangi sumemnni megnunapagilnguut , elngaatall aflengakaqaput . Yugusimta natangi esghaghtesugigalkeput pilugugngaaqaput ,
ilangi tamaakut esghaghyaghngaaghmeng ayuqelghiit pilugugigataput . Kiyaghneghem ulimaaqngamigu yugusiq , megnunaghataghaghtestekaqii megnunapagitesugnilnguut .
Enkaam yugusiq qepghaqayuguuq qerngaghmi . Nalighneghem qamaglluteng aflengakaqiit ilateng tawatengwaaq .
Ataasiq aqninghani qamaglluteng aqniqayuguut . Ataasiq usuqellengenghani qamaglluteng quyakayuguut .
Qamagllusi ugpeqani Christ-am yugusiqiisi , nalighnequghiisi .
Kiyaghneghem ugpeqanun nakmikegkaqii sivukluki Apostle-et aangelleghpigaaluki , tuunglighhii uuknaliqistet ( ungipaqilghiit Kiyaghneghem ungipaaneng ) pingayii apeghtughistet , taagken allaaghlluwhaghtistet , tamaakutlu aghtughyaghqaanghillelitkat naallghutimun , kayusighiyaghqat ilameggneng , pinilghiit igleghutistet , tamaakutlu allaaghhiinaastun akuzikayuget . Kiyaghneghem tuunyukani tamaakut naliitneng tunusaghqami tuunaqii .
Qamagllusi Apostle-ngutsii , uuknaliqestengutsii , apeghtughistengutsii ? Qamagllusi aghtughyaghqaanghillelitkaatsii allaaghlluwhaghtisighqameng ,
naallghutikayugutsii ? Qamagllusi allaaghhiinaastun akuzikayugutsillu mumighquqayugutsillu allaaghhiinaghneng akuzilleghneng ? Nakaa !
Iwernga piyukiteki aangataghalghiit Agleghnalghiim Taghnegham tunusii . Whaa maaten apeghnaqaqa pinighataghalghii taakuneng .
Akuzikayuguyaghngaaghma yugetlu yaqulgetlu akuzillghistun , temngi tengngaagtaghllequnga nalighmeng lengaaghtaghllequnga piniqinghilkuma .
Uuknaliqegkayugughngaaghma , liigikegkayugughngaamki aliinneghilnguut qamaglluki , liisimalleq qamagtekaqsaghngaamkun , ugpeqillelgughngaaghma naayghanun nuugtisighqameng , pitngunaanghitunga piniqinghilkuma .
Tuunyaghngaamki qamaglluki sanka aklumalghiinun , nalighmeng paneghtesaghngaaghma ungipaqilqa Pinilghiineng Ungipaneng apalluqluku , allgeghunnaanghitunga piniqinghilkuma .
Piniqelleq nuqenneghtuuqlu , nangllegtaghtuqlu ; piniqelleq aqinangituq , nalighmeng yamrrangituq , nalighmeng aangaayugneghituq .
Piniqelleq seghleghyugutngituq , nalighmeng ellnginaayugneghituq . Piniqelleq sagiqigatuq piyukelleghmitun pinaluni , qikeghqungigatuq , nalighmeng neqamikingigatuq anaggutelleghmeng .
Piniqellghem quyasiqigataa seghleq , yeghlegi quyasiqaqaa ipapilleq .
Piniqelleq ataasiighmetuq sangwa sayaghngaan . Iiwleng ugpeqingaaq , iiwleng neghyukingaaq , iiwleng nuqenneghtuuq .
Piniqelleq kenlengilnguq . Uuknaliqellghet kenletghuusaghqaagut ; allastun akuzillghet taaqsaghqaagut ; liisimalleq kenletghuusaghqaaguq .
Qayughllak tunusagput liisimalleqlu uuknaliqelleqlu iighwinneghilnguuk .
Iwernga iighwilnguq kaaskan , qamaglluteng iighwinneghilnguut aviighughsaghqaagut .
Taghnughhaalunga akuzikayuguyaghtunga , sumeghtaghaqayuguyaghtunga , liigikegkayuguyaghtunga taghnughhaghestun , iwernga yugughsalghiinga taghnughhaghestun pinanightunga .
Liigikelleghput Kiyaghneghmeng iighwinneghituq , katam tawatetuq esghalghiistun taghneghaghquutelugkun . Qakuqaaqun liigikngwaaghyaghqaghput Kiyaghneq qayughllak esghaghlleqaghput gginasaghqughluku . Maaten liisimalqa iighwinneghituq . Ilangani aghneghem liisimalqa iighwighyaghqaaguq katam tawaten Kiyaghneghem liisimakngwaaqanganga iighwighma .
Enkaangam ukut pingayut kenletghuunnaanghitut : ugpelleq , sighimalleq , piniqelleq ; iwernga piniqellghuuq angelleghpigaq .
Piniqellengyugataghaghyaghqaagusi pakiggulluku sameng tamaghhaaneng . Iwernga piyukitekillu Agleghnalghiim Taghnegham tunusii , wata piyuksaghqaqaghsi ungipaqilleq Kiyaghneghem ungipaaneng .
Yuuk akuzineghmini allastun ulustun aleghqughaqaa Kiyaghneq . Yuget aleghqiigatii qayughllak liigiknaaghitaat . Akuziiquq aghtughyaghqaanghillghakun Agleghnalghiim Taghnegham yugem nallukegkaaneng .
Iwernga yuuk tunusalek ungipaqilleghmeng Kiyaghneghem ungipaaneng akuzikayuguuq yugnun . Akuzitangi kayusighikayuguut , kayemikayuguut , ilutughsaghikayuguut yugnun .
Yuuk akuzikayuk allastun ulustun kayusiitkayuguuq ellmineng katam , iwernga yuuk ungipaqikayuk Kiyaghneghem ungipaaneng kayusighikayuguuq ugpeqaneng .
Qamagllusi piyukaqsaghamsi akuzisqellusi allastun ulustun , iwernga wataqaaghaqtuq tunusalgulghiisi ungipaqsaghqaaluki Kiyaghneghem ungipii . Tamaakut ungipaqikayuget aangataghaghtut akuzikayugneng allastun ulustun . Akuzikayuget allastun ulustun mumighqughtelguyaghqaagut kayusiitesqelluki ugpeqat .
Ugpeqaalgutemni , elpesinun pilunga aleghqughyaqumsi allastun ulustun liigiksaghqaqenghilkegpesigun naten始ngam kayusiinnayaghestemsi ? Iwernga apeghtughyaqumsi Kiyaghneghem kelgutkaaneng whangamnun , nalighmeng ungipaasaqumsi sameng liitkamneng , nalighmeng uuknaliqutkesaqumkun Kiyaghneghem salleghqaa , nalighmeng apeghtughyaqumsi ipapighqelleghmeng elngaatall kayusiinnayaghamsi .
Flute-allu harp-allu seghletun qalghightekayek kitum alngunak liigiknaangitaa sangwaa ilagaan atughaqutanga .
Pilluwaghtem bugle-a qalghightekagu seghletun ilangita pilluwaghtet nallukelleqaat pilluwalleghqaghteng .
Tawateghpigaq akuzikufsi allastun ulustun , kitum alngunak liigiknaanghitiisi sameng piiqutsi . Akuzinghilngughestun piyaghqaagusi .
Uglapigtuq allaghhiinaq akuzilleq , atuqistengita liigikaqiit .
Iwernga liigikenghilkumkun yuuk akuzilghii allakun akuzilleghqun nakumiinguuq whangamni , enkaam whangallu nakumiingunga ellngani .
Enkaangam elpesi , tunusangyupigtekufsi Agleghnalghiim Taghnegham tunusaaneng , tungsightek kayutkaghqameng ugpeqanun .
Tamaaken apalluqluku yuuk akuzikayuk allastun ulustun , yughaghli mumighqughyaghqaaluku sameng pilleni .
Yughaghyaquma allastun ulustun , taghneghagka yughaghllequk , iwernga umyugagma liigiknaanghitaak .
Sanaqsingangam ? Yughaghllequnga taghneghamkun , yughaghllequngallu umyugamkun . Tawateghpigaq ilagaghllequnga taghneghamkun , ilagaghllequngallu umyugamkun .
Qayughllak taghneghagpegun usuqegkuvgu Kiyaghneq allastun ulustun , naten始ngam liigikigalnguum usuqilgusighlleqaten Kiyaghneghmun iyamsiqayulleghpeneng ? Nallukaa sameng piiquten .
Yughallghen piniipigsaghngaan ilanga yugem kayusillengnaanghituq .
Iyamsiqayugvikaqaqa Kiyaghneq akuziiqelghiinga allastun ulustun uglaghataghaghluku elpesineng .
Iwernga yughaghvigmennemni apeghtughiyugaqunga . Tamaaken apalluqluku apeghtughiiqunga qafsinkuuraghhaat akuzitet atuqluki liigiksaghqasi , akuzinaanghitunga allastun ulustun uglapiglluku liigiksaghqaqenghilkegpesineng .
Ugpeqaalgutemni , sumeghtaghaghpenasi taghnughhaghhaghestun . Sumeghtaghaghaqitek anglikastun , iwernga seghleghqesulleghsi taghnughhaghhaghestun ayuquq .
Liilightuusani igaqngaaq : " Kiyaghneq piiq , ' Kayaglleqanka yuget allaneng nunaneng aleghqughyaghtiisqellusi ellngita katam ulungistun . Aleghqughlleqamsi qaanghitgun iwernga paninang nagannaanghitaghpesinga . ' "
Enkaam tunusaa akuzillghem allastun ulustun ipapighqusiiguq ugpeqingigalngughnun , nakaan ugpeqikayugnun . Ungipaqilleq ugpeqilghiinun ayuquq , nakaan ugpeqingigalngughnun .
Enkaangam yughaghvigpesini ugpeqat qamaglluteng akuzisaqumeng allastun ulustun , ilangi yugem nalighmeng ugpeqaanghilnguut iitqumeng nallungughhnilleqiisi .
Iwernga ugpeqaanghilnguq nalighmeng liigikigalnguq yughaghvigpesinun iteghluni nagaskumisi ungipalghiisi Kiyaghneghem ungipaaneng , nagalluni nanqigtengngwaaghllequq seghleghqestenguniluni .
Qamanlliqegkii aksaqngalghiit qayvighqellequt . Enkaam qungughlluni manigughlleqaa Kiyaghneq . Whaten pillequq , " Ipapestaaq , Kiyaghneq whaantuq elpesini . "
Ugpeqaalgutemni , unata apeghtuusaqnaqutkaqegkegka . Qerngughunneghpesini maniguunnalusi ilasi ilagaghaqnaaghtut , kina apeghtughiiqellequq , nalighmeng nalighsi ungipaghllequq Kiyaghneghem ungipaqesqegkaaneng , nalighmeng nalighsi akuzillequq allastun ulustun , nalighpesi mumighqughlleqii . Ugpeqat ugpellghitnun iknaqughusiilit qamaglluteng .
Yughaghvigmi kina akuzinaqngukumi allastun ulustun , maalghuk nalighmeng pingayut pilghaat , utaqaluki ilateng taaqelleghqiit . Kitumllu mumighqughnakangi sameng pillghit .
Iwernga mumighqughtengiskan akuzilghiimun allastun ulustun , akuzifqaami pilghaaq . Allastun ulustun akuziyukumi kavyuguutegpenani akuzilghaaq ellminunllu Kiyaghneghmunllu .
Uuknaliqistek maalghuk nalighmeng pingayut ungipangelghiit Kiyaghneghmeng akuzilit . Qamaglluteng nagallit , liigiklitgu ungipaq Kiyaghneghmeng pingutanga .
Iwernga kina ungipangegkan Kiyaghneghmeng , akuzilghii nepiighli , ungipangelghii akuzisqelluku .
Tawaten pikufsi qamaglluteng ungipaqiyaghqat Kiyaghneghem ungipaaneng akuziiqellequt . Enkaam qamaglluni nagallghii , liilli , taagavenginaallenglillu .
Neqamikluki ungipaqikayuget Kiyaghneghem ungipaaneng , aghtughyaghqaanghillelitkaagut akuzisighqameng , taaqusighqamengllu . Iiwleng aghtughyaghqaanghillelguut akuzisighqameng nalighmeng taaqusighqameng .
Kiyaghneghem alngunak pisugigatiinkut . Qerngughutelleput nekegmetesugaqii . Kiyaghneghem yugi qerngughunneghata ,
aghnat akuzistenguyaghqaanghitut yughaghvigni . Akuziyaghqaanghitutlu igleghutistenguyaghqaanghitutlu qerngughutngalghiini , qayughllak Liilightusanillu igaqngaaq tawaten .
Aapqughaghyukumeng , ugiteng nemeggni aaplitki . Yughaghvigni aghnat akuzilleghqaat anaggutngaaq .
Elpesi Corinth-eghmiit ugpeqat aangaayugneghuusi . Sumeghpesinii Kiyaghneghem akuzitangi elpesineng pingwaat ? Ellnginaghhaghpesinun apeghtuutkaawaat ?
Kina alngunak sumeghmini uuknaliqistenguniluni pikumi , nalighmeng ugpeghllagumaniluni , liigikliki latatkegkanka elpesinun Ataneghem qelghusaqii .
Tuguklinghilkagu una apeghtuusaq , tuguklighpenaan ellnga .
Enkaangam ugpeqaalgutemni , ungipaghtenguyugaqitek Kiyaghneghem ungipaaneng , iwernga taaqestegpenaki akuzilghiit allastun ulustun .
Yughaghvigni sangwaa qamaglluku pinitungwaaq , tawatengwaaq piiqiteggu .
Ugpeqaalgutemni , neqangughsugamsi Pinilghiineng Ungipaneng ungipaqegkamneng elpesinun . Tugukliqaqasi enkaam ugpellesi taaggun nekegngaat ayugilluteng .
Yugulillengegkaagusi ugpeqaqngafsiki Pinilghiit Ungipat , enkaam ugpequmanginaghteki aapqanka . Iwernga ugpeqnaniqufsiki , ugpellesi sasiinaanghitut .
Apeghtuqaqamsi apeghtuusaqegkameng whangamnun . Taakut ugpeqsaghqaqasi : Christ-am tuqutkegkaqii seghleghqelleput , katam Akuzitet Igaqegkat pinaqnillghistun .
Taagken lliifqaqaat , enkaam pingayaani aghneghem unguvaqaaguq Akuzitni Igaqegkani pinaqnillghistun .
Peter-em esghaqaqaa , taagken kingunganeng qamaglluteng qula maalghuk siipneqluku apostle-et esghaqaqaat .
Kingungitneng 500-neng uglalghiim maligsaaghtengita qerngaghllagmeng esghaqaqaat . Kiyang taakut unguvaat , ilangi tuqukaaghngaaghmeng .
Taagken James-em esghaqaqaa , enkaam kinguvaqun qamaglluteng apostle-et esghaqaqaat .
Kinguliilunga esghaqaqaqa , ugpeghyaghqaghpagningitkaaghngaaghma kitumi alngunak .
Ukalighpigaagunga apostle-eni , talwa atighyaghqaanghisaghtunga apostle-meng , qayughllak amyuqetaatqegkaqanka Kiyaghneghem yugi .
Iwernga Kiyaghneghem nangllegtallghakun apostle-nguunga . Nangllegtallgha whangamnun avanginneghituq . Qepghaghataghaghtunga tamaghhiitneng apostle-et , iwernga whangamneng pingunghitaqa , Kiyaghneghem nangllegtallghakun piiqunga .
Qepghaghataghalleghput ilamnneng megnuniituq . Megnunalghiita taana qamaglluta ungipaqegkaqaput elpesinun taakut ataasit Pinilghiit Ungipat , enkaam ugpeqegkaqasi .
Ugpeqngukesi Ungipaq ungipaqegkaghput : Christ-am unguvaghtellgha tuqulleghmeng . Sangamengam ilasi piiqat , " Tuqukat unguvaghnaanghitut ? "
Kina alngunak unguvaghtesimangilkan , Christ-a paninang tuqunganayaghtuq .
Paninang tuqungakan ungipaghqiitukut , enkaam ugpeqsaghqiitusi .
Tuqukat unguvaghtesimangilkata tuqulleghmeng , Kiyaghneghem unguvaghtesimangitaa Christ-a . Enkaangam whangkuta apostle-eni qamaglluta iqlengiqestenguukut qayughllak pikaagukut , " Kiyaghneghem Christ-a unguvaghtestekaqaa tuqulleghmeng . "
Tuqukat unguvaghtesimangilkata , Christ-allu unguvaghtesimangituq .
Christ-a paninang tuqungakan ugpellesi sasiinghitut enkaam aghyullengellequsi seghleghqelleghpesinun .
Ugpeqistet Christ-akun tuqulaghaatkat qamaglluteng iflanayaghtut .
Neghyukilleghput Christ-akun whaninginaghhaq kiyaghtaallemnni atuukan , nangllegnalleghpigaayaghqaagukut yugni kitumeng alngunak .
Ipanguuq Christ-a unguvaqaaguq tuqulleghmeng , tamaaken apalluqluku liisimakngwaaghaghput whangkutallu unguvaghtesaghqaagukut ilangani aghneghem .
Tuqulleq allgeqaaguq ataasikun yugkun , Adam-kun . Tawateghpigaq unguvaghtestelleq tuqulleghmeng allgeqaaguq ilangakun yugkun , Christ-akun .
Adam-kun qamaglluni tuquyaghqaaguq , iwernga qamaglluteng Christ-amelnguut unguvaghtesaghqaagut tuqulleghmeng .
Qamaglluteng tuqulaghaatkat pilleghqateng kaanneghata unguvaghaqnaaghtut : Christ-a sivulighpigaaluni unguvaqaaguq . Taagken taginqigtekan tamaakut ellngan pingi unguvaghyaghqaagut .
Christ-a umiilguyaghqaaguq kenlanga kayaalqelleghminun qamagtengngwaaghluki aghtughyaghqaanghillghet qaatkusugigalnguut Kiyaghneghmun , tughneghaatlu igleghutistet , yugetlu igleghutistet ilalluki . Christ-a umiilguyaghqaaguq kenlanga Kiyaghneghem kayaalqellghanun qamagtengngwaaghluki Christ-am anguyagi . Kingulighpigaq anguyak tuqullghuuq Kiyaghneghem kayaalqesaghqaa . Christ-am tuunegkagu Ataneghpagulleq Kiyaghneghmun Atamun taagken kenla kaallequq . Igaqngaaq Akuzitni Igaqegkani , " Kiyaghneghem sangwaa tamaghhaan itegaan asinganun lliightesaghqaqaa . " Whaten pisiiguq , Kiyaghneghem samun tamaghhaanun qaatkestesaghqaqaa Christ-a . Iwernga Kiyaghneghem qaatkusaghqaaghtestekumigu sangwaa tamaghhaan Christ-amun , qaatkusaghqaaghsaghqaanghituq , ellmineng katam . Tawaten pikan , taagken Ighneq ellmineng katam asiliighsaghqaaguq Kiyaghneghmeng . Elngaatall Kiyaghneghem sangwaa tamaghhaan igleghulleqaa .
Ilangi yuget paaptaayestaqut tuqukat apalluqluki . Tuqukat unguvaghsaghqaanghilkata tuqulleghmeng , sangamengam ilangi paaptaayestaqat tuqukat apalluqluki ?
Liisimakaput tuqukat unguvaqaagut tuqulleghmeng . Enkaangam ungipaqinguukut Pinilghiineng Ungipaneng tuqunnaqsaghngiinkut aghhutanga tamaghhaan .
Ipanguuq tuqusaqleggiinaq ayuqaatnga aghhutanga tamaghhaan . Katam liisimakelleghpesistun quyakelqa ugpelleghsi anglilghii Christ Jesus-kun Atanemteggun . Tawateghpigaq ipapighqutkesaghqaqaghsi tuqusaqleggiinaq ayuqegkangatnga aghhutanga tamaghhaan .
Yuget Ephesus-melnguut pilluwaqanka teghikusastun ayuqut . Allgeghunnalunga whani kiyaghtellemni pilluwaqumki , sameng allgeghunnaanghitunga . Tuqullemta kingunganeng unguvaghyaghqaanghilkumta , " Neghelta , meghelta , qayughllak unaami tuqullequkut . "
Kitumun alngunak puughtestegpenasi ilakumtaangumakufsi seghletun pikayugmeng , atuqsagulleqaghsi sangwaa piiqegkangat .
Sumeghtaghaghaqlusi piniitun , seghleghqennanightek , ilasi akulegpesinilnguut apeghtuumangilnguugut Kiyaghneghmeng . Qayughllak elpesi ugpeqani kaynguyugyaghqaagusi .
Kina alngunak whaten pikan : " Naten tuqukat unguvaghtestaqat tuqulleghmeng ? Natelngughmeng yugusilguyaghqaawat ? "
Uyuq nalluuqaq ! Piituta nunakun peghukuvgu tuquyaghqaaguq sivungani piitelleghqami .
Piitutmeng allanguluni angliiquq . Piitesiighaneghpeni , piitutesquvegaghhaq peghwaaqan nunakun , wheat-kaghqaq nalighmeng sanguyaghqaq .
Piitutesquvegaghhaq taana Kiyaghneghem nakmikegkamineng yugusilitaqaa . Allakullghiit piitutet allakullghiimeng yugusighqalguut .
Tawatelkutngwaaghunghitut yugusit . Yuget , teghikusat , qawaaget , iqalluget allakutut yugusiit .
Qilak yugusightuuq , nuna yugusightuuq . Yugusit qilagmelnguut ellmegestun pinighnaghtut . Yugusitlu nunamelnguut ellmegestun pinighnaghtut .
Siqineq , tanqiq , ighaleqetaaghetlu allakutut pinighnallghit . Talwa ighaleqetaaghet allakaqaghtaghmeng allakutut pinighnallghit .
Tawatesaghqaagut tuqukat unguvaghtestekata tuqulleghmeng : nunami yugusiput tuqaaqut , aghwaaqut , iwernga yugusighraghaput tuqunaanghitngwaaghtut .
Lliifqumeng nunamelnguut yugusiput seghleghughsaghqat kayaaliyaghqat , iwernga yugusiq unguvaghtestekumi pinighnaghyaghqaqlu iknaqsaghqaqlu .
Lliveneghmini yugusiq yugem pikaa . Iwernga yugusiq unguvaghtestekumi taghneghamnnun yugusiiyaghqaaguq . Yugusilgukata yuget yugusighqalguutlu taghneghaput .
Enkaam Akuzitni Igaqegkani igaqegkaaguq , " Yuksuwhaaq Adam unguvalghiingughtekaaguq . " Iwernga kinguliq Adam unguvallelitikayuguuq taghneghaq , Christ-anguuq .
Sivukluta yugem yugusiineng yugusingaqukut , taagken taakwaningani Kiyaghneghem yugusilitaqii taghneghaput .
Yuksuwhaaq nunameng pinguuq , pagulanganeng nunam ulimaaghuuq , iwernga tuunglighhaa yuuk Christ-a , qilagmeng pinguuq .
Yuget kiyaghtekumeng nunami whani , yugusilguut Adam-em yugusiitun ayuqelghiimeng . Iwernga tamaakut qilagmi kiyaghsaghqat Christ-atun yugusilguyaghqaagut .
Adam-etun yugusilgullemtestun , ilangani aghneghem Christ-atun yugusilguyaghqaagukut .
Ugpeqaalgutemni , liitesugamsi yugusiput ukut kemekragmeng , aawmeng ulimaaghet , iteghnaanghitut Ataneghpagullghanun Kiyaghneghem . Ilangani aghneghem ukut yugusiput tuquyaghqaagut . Unguvanaanghitut quunperugllak .
Ungipaataghllamsi qayvighsimangilngughmeng : qamaglluta tuqunaanghitukut , iwernga qamaglluta allangughsaghqaagukut ,
sukatepiglluta qunqallellghestun kingulighpigaq qalghightaq nagaququmteggu . Tawani qalghightalleghmi ugpeqat qamaglluteng tuqulaghaatkat unguvaghtuusaghqaagut nutaghameng yugusilighluteng tuquyaghqaanghilngughmeng . Taagken whangkutallu paninang unguvalghiini nutaghameng yugusingaghaghtaallequkut .
Yugusiput pagulameng ulimaaghet allangughsaghqapestaaghuut naafqesaghqaanghilngughmeng . Ukut yugusiput tuqukayuget simighyaghqaagut yugusimeng tuquyaghqaanghilngughmeng .
Enkaam Akuzitni Igaqegkani igaqegkaq apeghiighllequq : " Tuqulleq naafquq ; kayaalqiilleq iighwightuq ! "
" Tuqu , kayaalqiillghen naagu ? Tuqu , aghtughyaghqaanghillghen aqnighquusin whangkunnun naagu ? "
Tuqullghem aghtughyaghqaanghilleni allgeghtaqaa seghleghqelleghmeng aqnighhnaluta , enkaam seghleghqellghem Liilightuusat aghtughyaghqaanghilqii .
Enkaangam iyamsiqayugvikaqaghput Kiyaghneq qayughllak kayaalqiistekaqiinkut Atanemteggun Jesus Christ-akun .
Enkaangam , piniqegkamni ugpeqaalgutemni , kayaalqiilleghqaghput ipapestaghutanganeng , ugpellesi aghuliitesluki , nuuggaghtafqaafsi , quunpeng qepghaghteggu Atanghem qepghaqaa . Liisimakaghsi Ataneghqun qepghalleghsi avanginneghituq .
Ukut esgha elpesinun qelghusanka manimeng tuunyaghqaghpesineng ugpeqanun Judea-melngughnun . Ungipaatellemtun Galatia-ghmiit ugpeqiit , elpesillu ellngistun pitek .
Sivulighpigaghmi Santillghem aghneghani qamagllusi aaftiiqitek manimeng allgeghneghpesineng . Tuunyaghqaghpesi angtalanga allgeghneghpesi angtalanganeng iikluku tuunyaghqaaguq . Enkaam elpesinun pikuma qerngughtifqaafsi manimeng pilghaasi .
Kaaskuma kayaglleqanka tamaakut nakmikegkasi latatgun aglaatesqelluku tunusaghsi Jerusalem-emun .
Sumeghtaghallemni whangallu pilleghqaqa pinighyaghqaakan , maliggnakangatnga .
Elpesinun laalighhnaqegkuma sivuklunga Macedonia-kun aagllequnga .
Entaqun elpesinitaghaqaghllequnga walluumllu uksulqusiq . Taagken navek pinaqegkuma yataaghqelgusiqaghnakefsinga .
Atanghem piyukelqegkagu maaten pikuma elpesinitaghaghyugaqunga , aagvikaghesnaghyunghitamsi .
Iwernga Ephesus-mellequnga kenlanga Pentecost-em aghneghanun ,
qayughllak megnunalghii , aangelghii qepghalleghqaqa Ataneghmun piiqeftuq . Maanllequnga qaywa uglapiglleghhiim anguyaksaghngaatnga .
Timothy elpesinun pikan , elngaatall upughannakesi , qayughllak qepghaaguq Ataneghmun whangamtun .
Qamagllusi asitnginaaghpenaan , enkaam quyangaan kayaggnakesi whangamnun . Utaqaaqaqa maligulluku ugpeqaalgutnun .
Ungipaataghllamsi ugpeqaalgutemnneng Apollos-meng . Elngaatall qelqaqsaghaqa laalighfikesqellusi maliglluki ilangi ugpeqaalgutet . Iwernga maaten piyunghituq . Laalighfiknaaghiisi pilleghqangegkumi .
Kelengatek , ugpeqilleghpesini aghuliitek , ilututek , iknaqitek .
Piniqelleghqun piiqiteggu sangwaa tamaghhaan .
Ugpeqaalgutemni , liisimakasi Stephanas-enkut nengllugutkullghiit , ugpeqaqsuwhaaghulghiit Achaia-mi . Ataneghmun tuunegkaagut ellmeggneng , ugpeqat ilangi kayusiinnaluki .
Qelghamsi qaatkumanginiisqelluki liilightullghit tawatelnguut yuget , ilangillu qepghalgutangit .
Quyaanga Stephanas-enkut , Fortunatus-enkut , Achaicus-enkut kaallghiit qayughllak kayusiitngwaatnga aviilleghpesini .
Quyastengngwaatnga quyastelleghmegestun elpesi . Kayusiitillghitnun iyamsiqayugvikelleghpesineng liisimakestengngwaaghnakesi .
Ugpeqat Asia-melnguut suumqaqiisinguq . Aquila-nkuk Priscilla-nkuk suumqeghllagiisinguq Ataneghqun , qamagllutengllu ugpeqat qerngughutkayuget elkegkenka mangteghiitni .
Qamaglluteng ugpeqaalgutet whangamnilnguut suumqaqiisinguq . Quyakutaqitek naaghluki Kiyaghneghem piniqellghakun .
Whanga katam iiggemneng una igaqaqa : Suumqamsi . Paul .
Kitum alngunak piniqenghilkumigu Ataneq , naafqellelguuq . " Maranatha , " whaten pisiiguq , Ataneghput , tagi !
Nangllegtallgha Atanghem Jesus-em elpesinilli .
Piniqamsi qamagllusi Christ Jesus-kun . Amen .
Ukut latat Paul-meng pinguut , apostle-nganeng Christ Jesus-em Kiyaghneghem piyukellghakun , Timothy-mengllu pinguut ugpeqaalgutemnneng . Kiyaghneghem yugitnun qerngughutkayugnun yughaghvigani Corinth-em , tamaghhiitnunllu Kiyaghneghem yugitnun iingunaghhaani Achaia-m .
Yeqay Kiyaghneghem Atamta , Atanemtallu Jesus Christ-am tuunlisi quyastelleghmengllu nekeggmelleghmengllu .
Usuqelteggu Kiyaghneq Atanga Atanemta Jesus Christ-am , nangllegtapiglleghii Ata , Kiyaghneghmeng tagiiquq qamaglluni kayutkaghqaq !
Kayusighaqiinkut qamaglluta seghleliillemnni , enkaam whangkutallu kayusighyaqlegwaaput tamaakut allaaghhiinaghmeng seghleliilghiit , atuqluku ataasiq taana kayusilleq allgeghtekaghput Kiyaghneghmeng .
Katam ilatngallemtestun Christ-am uglaapiglleghhiinun ikfiqellghanun , enkaam Christ-akun ilatngallequkut Kiyaghneghem kayusilleghllaganun .
Ikfiqegkumta , kayusilleghpesinunllu yugulilleghpesinunllu pillghuuq ; kayusillengegkumta taawa elpesillu kayusillengellequsi enkaam tuunellengellequsi nekeggmellelighlusi suflughsaghqaaluki tamaakut ataasit ikfiqellghet suflughtekaput .
Enkaam sighimakilleghput elpesinun aghuliituq ; liisimakaghput taana katam ilatngalleghpesigun ikfiqellemnnun , elpesillu ilatngaasi kayusilleghmun allgeghtekamnnun .
Ugpeqaalgutemnni , nallukesunghitamsi seghleliilleghmeng nanghiiqamnneng Asia-mi . Elngaatall seghleghllaguuq uqigtupigtekaaguq , repall sighimananiqaagukut kiyaghtelleghqamnneng .
Ipapestaaq tuqunaqniluta piyaghtukut . Iwernga tawaten aneghtukut whangkunneng sighimakefqaamta pisqelluta , taawanginaghhaq Kiyaghneq sighimakesqelluku unguvaghtestikayuk tuqukaneng .
Elngaatall seghlepestaaghmeng tuqum tevneghaneng yuguliinkut , yugulilleqiinkutlu . Enkaam ellngakun sighimanguukut ellngan yugulilaataghlleqiinkut ,
elpesi kayusiisimaluta yughalleghpesigun . Yughaatkilleghllagsi whangkunneng kiimsillengellequt , enkaam Kiyaghneghem quyasleqiinkut ; uglapiglleghhiitlu iglagtughlluteng iyamsiqayugvikelleqaat whangkunneng .
Una esgha qukaayugusighput , sumeghtaghallemta ungipaatiinkut kiyaghtaalleghput whani nunami ipapighqengngaaqlu piniqingaaqlu , kiyang elpesinun . Tawaten piiqukut Kiyaghneghem piniqingalghiikun kayusillghakun , nakaan yugem peghqinellghakun .
Qamaglluteng lataput elpesinun piyaqniitut atightughyaghqaalutengllu liigiksaghqaalutengllu . Sighimakaqamsi liigikngwaaghesqelluku
sangwaa maaten liigikegkaghpesi nalighneghhiinaa , enkaam Aghneghani Atanghem Jesus-em elpesi qukaayugutkelleqaghpesikut katam whangkuta qukaayugutkellemtestun elpesi .
Qayughllak ipapighqutkegkaqaqa qamaglluku tamaana , sivuklunga elpesinun laalighhnalunga pikaayaghtunga , quyastellengnayukafsi malghughqengngaan .
Laalighfiksukaqamsi aglaatkelluku Macedonia-mun , uteghniitkellukullu tamaaken , kayutengnalunga elpesineng igleghalleghqamnun Judea-mun .
Sumeghpesinii tawaten qakiqniqellemni ataasiighneghisingaa ? Sumeghpesinii qakiqniqelqa nunam yugatun ayuqaa , tawaninginaq piyaghqaq , " Aa-a , " " Nakaa ? "
Ipapestaaq Kiyaghneq ataasiighmetuq , akequsaqa elpesinun " Aang始ghunghituqlu " " Nakaaghunghituqlu " .
Kiyaghneghem Ighnegha , Jesus Christ-a ungipaqegkaghput elpesinun Silas-lu Timothy-llu whangallu , " Aang始ghunghituqlu " " Nakaaghunghituqlu " ; iwernga ellngani quunpeng " Aang始ghuuq " .
Ellnganguuq " Angelleq " tamaghhiitnun Kiyaghneghem akequsiitnun . Tamaaken apalluqluku whangkuta " Amen-aaghaqukut " ellngakun usuqnemteggu Kiyaghneq .
Kiyaghneghem ayepsugighsaghiinkut , maligulluta elpesinun Christ-akun ; Kiyaghneghem ellngan katam aaftiinkut ;
nalluniighiinkut ellminun pinguluta , tuunaaklu Taghneghagni ilumnnun nallangiisaalukek tamaghhaanun akequsaqegkaminun whangukunnun .
Tuqlughaqa Kiyaghneq liisimakistenguluku qayughllak liisimakegkanga qaamna iluka ! Corinth-esugunghitunga seghleliighqesnayukamsi .
Igleghunnaqutkengngunghitaghput ugpeqilleghsi ; qepghalgusighyugamsi quyamasqellusi , qayughllak aghuliitusi ugpeqilleghpesigun .
Taawa umyugagka ataasiighsimaagka alla elpesinun pikuma quyanghitesaghqaafqaafsi pinalusi .
Qayughllak quyanghitestekumsi kitumngam whanga qaqayugtesleqanga ? Alla kitum pinaanghitanga iwerngaqun elpesi quyanghitestekama .
Tamaaken apalluqluku latakaqamsi qayughllak elpesinun piyunghilnguunga quyanghitesnayukafsinga , elpesi quyanghitesnayukafsinga , elpesi quyastistemni . Ipapighqutkengngwaaqa una , whanga quyanganemni taawa elpesillu qamagllusi quyangaaqusi .
Latakaagunga elpesinun elngaatall aangluku qivghullelighlunga qamagun ilumkun , qiyamaghma alla quyanghitestefqaafsi pinalusi taawanginaq liigikesqelluku piniqelleghllaka elpesinun .
Taana yuuk seghleghqelghii tawani , seghleghqenghituq whangamnun . Yeghlegi elpesinun seghleghqengnguuq iwernga nakaan tamaghhaghpesinun . Uniighmighsunghitaqa sameng pillemkun .
Tawatenginaq aghyuughilleghsi itagnaghtuq .
Maaten seghevullukung始ngam kayemiteggu wata iilqennayukan repall iilqayugllagnayukan .
Maniguututaqa elpesinun liigikestesqelluku ipapestaaq piniqniluku elpesinun .
Taana apalluqluku latakaqamsi : liisimaknaluku qaatkutngwaaqutsi samun tamaghhaanun .
Kina seghevunneghpisigu sameng elpesinun pillghaneng whangallu seghevutaqaqa . Sangwaa alngunak seghevusaghqaq seghevusugaqaqa elpesi apalluglusi Christ-a tawantepiglleghhiistun ,
Tughneghaam aaghqutaqnayukanginkut qayughllak liisimakegkefut sangutanga yataaghqegkaa .
Kaasalghiinga Troas-mun ungipaqnaluku Pinilghii Ungipaa Christ-am , Atanghem pilleghqangestengngwaaghumakanganga .
Iwernga pengegllakaagunga qayughllak ugpeqaalgutka Titus aviilnguq tamaani . Enkaam unilluki aghulaqunga Macedonia-mun .
Iwernga iyamsiqanaghhalek Kiyaghneq ! Iiwleng igleghutngwiinkut kayallqiingalleghqun Christ-akun . Kiyaghneghem whangkutgun mingitestengngwaa liisimalleni nani alngunak katam neqnilghiim tepengllaasim tepangan mingitellghatun .
Qayughllak whangkuta tepkegtastun neqnighsaasistun ayuqukut Christ-am aghqutkegkaatun Kiyaghneghmun . Tepevut mengitnguuq yugulikanunllu iflakanunllu .
Tamaakunun iflakanun tepkiinkut tuqullghem tuqutikayugem ; iwernga yugulikanun tepkaa unguvallengestikayugem . Kinangam qepghaghyaghqaawa tawatelngughmeng qepghaqameng ?
Uglapiglleghhiistun kinkustun ayuqenghitukut salin qepghaghyaghqaanghilngughestun tamaaken qepghaqameng . Pinilghiit ungipat piiqiit ilangistun qepghaqastun ayuqniluki allgeghutusighqat kiyaghtaaghusighqamun . Iwernga whangkuta ataasiighmelluta ipapighqelluta qepghaghaqukut ; aapghaqaput ungipat Kiyaghneghem pisqellghatun , kayagtellghatun ungipaghtengulutallu qepghaghtengulutallu Christ-amun .
Whangkuta usuqesaayuggnaqlaataghestaa whangkunneng katam ? Nalighmeng ilangistun aklukingustaa latameng aapghesqelluta elpesinun , nalighmeng elpesineng ?
Elpesi , elpesi katam whangkuta latakamsi , igaqngaasi ilumteggun tamanganun liisimakesqellusillu atightiisqellusi .
Whateghlluwaaq latanguusi Christ-ameng pit whangkunnun tuyuqii . Latatkegkaanghitusi ink-akun nalighmeng lliivneqegtatgun uyghagteggun . Latatkegkaagusi yuget ilungitgun Taghneghagkenkun unguvalghiim Kiyaghneghem .
Tawaten piikut qayughllak neghyullelguukut Kiyaghneghmi Christ-akun .
Whangkunneng pikninaanghitaghput qepghaghyaqleguniluku taana qepghaqaq . Kiyaghneghem piyaqlegughtestaqiinkut qepghaqamun .
Ellngan qepghaghyaqlegughtestiinkut nutaghamun akequsamun . Taana nutaghaq akequsaq igaqngalghiingunghituq liilightuusaq , iwernga Taghneghagneng ayuquq . Igaqngalghiim Liilightuusam tagitaa tuqulleq , iwernga Taghnegham tuunaa unguvalleq .
Liilightuusat igaqegkaagut uyghagteggun , enkaam Kiyaghneghem nighughqellgha aliiqaaguq Liilightuusat tuunaqngata . Moses-em gginaa kuukgutkaaguq taagken nighughqelleghmeng , qaywa gheveghngaan Israel-eghmiit esghaghpagningitkaat gginaa . Liilightuusat tuqustiyaghqaagut qayughllak yuget qaatkenghilkangit . Liilightuusat nighughqestighllagumakata ,
natenmi angkaan qepghallgha Kiyaghneghem Taghneghagkenka nighughqestiighataghaghlleqa !
Liilightuusaq nanqigtiyaghqaakan yugmeng aghyuughyaghqaaluki nighughqengngayaghtuq ; anaggutellghinniluteng yuget pilghiit natenmi angkaan nighughqengngalleghtulleqat !
Tawaten pinguukut qayughllak nighugataghalghiingughtuq nighughqelleq maaten , taana nighughqengngayalghii sivunghani aviighusimaaq .
Nighughqellelguyaqan tawaten mulughraakameng , natenmi angkaan nighughqellegulleqa mulughllagyaghqameng quunperugllak !
Taana sighimakutemnneng tetugigatngwaaghtukut .
Moses-etun ayuqenghitukut , gginani saaputiqaa enkaam Israel-eghmiit esghaamangitaat nighugllak aviighullghii .
Umyugiit liigikepagningiitkaagut , whavemun kenlanga umyugiit saapngaat taagken ataasimeng saaputameng , atightuneghmegteki neghightat akequsat . Taana saaputaq iqisaghqaaguq Christ-anginaghhaghqun .
Talwa aghneghmi whani , atightuneghmegteki Liilightuusat Moses-mun tuunegkat , umyugiit saaputameng saapngaaqut .
Iwernga yuuk qiivneghmini Ataneghmun saaputaa iqitaquq .
Maaten Ataneq Taghneghaalghii , kina alngunak Atanghem Taghneghagkeneng pilgukumi , itemngallelguuq .
Qamagtengngwaaghluta saaputangunaki gginaput esghaghlleqaghput nighughqellgha Atanghem . Taana ataasiq nighughqelleq tagilghii Ataneghmeng Taghneghaaguq , allangughtiinkut ellngasugnightesqelluta aangataghaghluku nighughqelleghmeng .
Enkaam Kiyaghneghem nangllegtalleghmikun qepghaqalitiinkut whaken qepghaghyaghqameng . Tamaaken apalluqluku iilqayugigatukut .
Ighsayagutkaqaput aksaqegkatlu kayngunalghiitlu . Puughsigataput yuget , allangughsigataputlu Kiyaghneghem akuzitangi . Whateghlluwaaqlu apeghtuusaqaqaput Kiyaghneghem ipapillghi , enkaangam yuget liilleqiinkut natelnguutfut esghaamanghani Kiyaghneghem .
Ungipaqegkaput Pinilghiit Ungipat saapngakata , saapngaat iflayaghqaghhiinaghnun .
Ellngita ugpeqigataat ungipaghput qayughllak Tughneghaam , uum nunam kiyaghneghan , ayaastekaqii umyugiit . Esghanghitestaqaa nighuga Pinilghiim Ungipam nighughqellghaneng Christ-am ayuqelghii . Christ-a Kiyaghneghtun ayuquq .
Whangkunneng katam ungipaqngunghitukut , itupill ungipaqngwaaghput Jesus Christ-a Atanghuniluku . Qepghaghtekaghpesikut Jesus apalluqluku .
Kiyaghneghuuq whaten pikaq , " Yeqay nighuk kuukgulli mamlelleghmeng ! " Ellnganguuq ataasiq Kiyaghneq kuukgutestilghii nighugmeng ilumnnun . Taaggun nighugkun liitaghput nighughqellgha Kiyaghneghem , kuukgullghii Jesus Christ-am gginaaneng .
Iwernga whangkunnun Kiyaghneghem kanaghtekaqaa taana nighuk kuukgutesqelluku ilumnni . Whangkuta qikustun qantaghqastun ayuqukut , enkaam tamangan liigikelleqaat aghtughyaghqaanghiteghllak Kiyaghneghtaaniluku , whangkunneng pingunghinniluku .
Seghleliillengaqukut allaaghhiinatun iwernga kayaalqigatiinkut . Ilangakun kukragyullengaqukut iwernga sighimallghiisigatukut .
Amyuqetaatkellengaqukut , iwernga Kiyaghneghem unisigatiinkut ; aqnighqwaallengaqukut , iwernga tuqungigatukut .
Iiwleng tuqullgha Jesus-em yugusimnnituq , esghiisqelluku unguvallgha Jesus-em yugusimnni .
Unguvanguluta iiwleng yakughnallghanitukut tuqullghem apalluqluku Jesus , esghiisqelluku Jesus-em unguvallgha yugusimnni tuqukayugni .
Enkaam whangkuta yakughnallghanitukut tuqullghem qayughllak qepghaatngukefut Kiyaghneq . Iwernga qepghallemta kenlengilngughmeng unguvallengestengngwiisi .
Igaqngaaq Akuzitni Igaqegkani , " Ugpeqaqa Kiyaghneq enkaam akuzitkaqaqa . " Ugpeqilleghput tawatetuq igaqestetun . Whangkutallu ugpeqaghput Kiyaghneq enkaam akuzitkaqaghput .
Liisimakaghput Kiyaghneghem unguvaghtekaqaa Ataneq Jesus . Whangkutallu unguvaghlleqiinkut Jesus-kun . Taagken aglaalleqiinkut qerngaamta elpesillu tawantelleghminun .
Qamaglluteng tamaakut apeghiiqat whangkunnun elpesinun ayuqut . Kiyaghneghem nangllegtallghan nulasleqii yuget ugpeqilghiit Christ-akun . Enkaam iyamsiqayulleghllak Kiyaghneghmun nulallequq , quulvallengeghllagllequqlu .
Enkaam iilqayugigatukut . Qaywa yugusiput kayaalikestaghyaghngaata , taghneghaput nutaghtengnguut aghhutanga tamaghhaan .
Seghleliilleput sasqughhaagut muluyaghqaanghitut . Iwernga tamaakut yataaghqutngwiinkut allgeghtesqelluku Kiyaghneghmeng kenlengilnguq quyalleghllak . Enkaam seghleliilleput avangilngughestun ayuqut .
Sumeghtaghaatkumanginiigataput seghleliilleput . Itupill sumeghtaghaatkaqaput esghaghpagningilkeput . Qantaghaqun seghleliilleput kenletghuullequt , iwernga quyalleghput esghiigalkefut quunpekaghqaaguq .
Whani nunami ukut yugusiput kiyaghfiput tiintastun ayuqut . Liisimakaghput yugusiput tuqukata Kiyaghneq mangteghalguuq qilagmi whangkunnun kiyaghfigkameng . Kiyaghneghem ulimakaqaa mangteghaq , yugem ulimaaqenghitaa . Taana mangteghaq quunpekaghqaaguq .
Ipa ngillegtukut nunametnguluta qayughllak kiyaghsupiglleghhiikut yugusighraghamnni qilagmi .
Aatkastun aalleqaput tamaakut yugusighraghaat amsikaghmenneghinnaluta .
Yugusiput tiintastun ayuqut . Tiintamelluta ngillegtaqukutlu , seghleliightukutlu qayughllak mataghsugigalkeput . Itupill simighyugaqaput yugusinun tuqungigalngughnun .
Kiyaghneghem yataaghqutkaqiinkut whavek allangughtelleghmun . Whangkunnunllu tuunegkaqaak Taghneghagni liisimakesqelluku allangughtelleghqaghput ipapestaaq apeghiighlleqniluku .
Enkaam iiwleng ilutaaqukut . Liisimakaghput nemetnguluta yugusimnni , Ataneghmesigatukut .
Kiyaghtengnguukut ugpeqilleghqun , nakaan esghaqayumteggun .
Enkaam ilutaaqukut . Unisugaqaput yugusiput nemennaluta Ataneghmi .
Nemesaghngaamta nalighmeng nemenneghiteghngaamta , efqughsugaqaghput Ataneq .
Qamaglluta nekevepestaaghyaghqaagukut Christ-am sivungakun nanqigtesqelluta . Ataasikaghtaamta allgeghullequkut pinilghiimeng nalighmeng seghleghmeng apeghiighutellemtestun yugusimteggun .
Enkaangam alikaqaghput Ataneq , tamaaken apalluqluku ugpeghtesnaqutkaqaput yuget Christ-akun . Kiyaghneghem liisimakiinkut natelnguutfut yugni , sunanguq elpesillu liisimakitekut tawatelluta .
Elpesinun tuguklightesnaqutkengngunghitukut allameng . Itupill ungipaataqamsi whangkunneng elpesinun qukaayugutkesqelluta . Taagken apeghyaqlegughlleqaghpesikut qukaayugutkilghiinun yugem qaastulnginaghhaaneng . Waakigataat sangutanga yugem ilumikegkaa .
Nallutuyiqngukumta , Kiyaghneghmun ayuquq , iwernga nallutuyiqngunghilkumta , elpesinun ayuquq .
Christ-am igleghutngwiinkut piniqelleghmikun . Liisimakngwaaghaghput yugem ataasim tuqumatkegkaqaa qamagtengngwaaghluku yuuk . Tamaaken apalluqluku qamagtengngwaaghluteng yuget tuqukaagut .
Christ-am tuqumatkegkaqii qamagtengngwaaghluki yuget . Enkaam kiyaghlleghhiit kiyaghsaqlegullequt ellnganun , nakaan ellmeggnun katam . Tuquluni unguvaghtekaaguq ellngit apalluqluki .
Whaken kenlekluku kina alngunak sumeghtaghaatkennaniimaaghput nunam yugan sumeghtaghaatkellghatun . Qaywa ataasimeng sumeghtaghaatkegkaqaghput Christ-a nunam yugan pillghatun , tawaten sumeghtaghaatkennaniimaaghput .
Kina alngunak Christ-am piliinneghminigu nutaghaghllugughtaquq . Kiyaghtaalleluga aviighutaquq , iwernga nutaghaghlluk kiyaghtaallgha piinlighaquq .
Kiyaghneghuuq tawaten pikaq . Ellngan ilaliighutestekaqiinkut ellminun Christ-akun . Qepghaqalitiinkutlu ilangillu yuget ilaliighutesqelluki ellminun .
Christ-akun Kiyaghneghem ilaliighwii qamagtengngwaaghluki yuget , umyugaghmikegpenaki seghleghqellghit . Enkaangam ungipaghqalitkaqiinkut aapghesqelluki naten ellminun ilaliighutangi ellngit .
Kiyaghneghem kayagtekaqiinkut ungipaghtenguluta Christ-amun , enkaam whangkutgun tagisqellusi ellminun . Akuzistenguukut Christ-amun kayemilghiit ilaliighutesqellusi Kiyaghneghmun .
Christ-a seghleghqumangitngwaaghtuq , iwernga seghleghqellemnnun Kiyaghneghem aghyuuqaqaa seghleghqegkaaluku . Enkaam Christ-akun Kiyaghneghem elqughutngangllaqaqiinkut .
Qepghalgutkututemnneng Kiyaghneqlu , taawa kayemamsi Kiyaghneghem nangllegtallgha tuguklighpenaan temngitwhanguluku .
Kiyaghneq pikaaguq , " Pilleghqaghlluwaaghmi nagaquqaqamken , aghneghani yugulillghem kayusiqaqamken . " Ungipaatamsi , maatenguuq Kiyaghneghem pilleghqaghlluwaagha ; nagatek , maatenguuq aghnegha yugulighillghem !
Kiyaghtaallemteggun naagsaghanglliigataput yuget , seghlequufqaan pisqelluku qepghaqaghput Ataneghmun .
Iwernga sallemteggun tamaghhaakun liigikestaqukut yugnun Kiyaghneghmun qepghaghtekniluta . Tamaaken apalluqluku nuqetutimallemteggun suflughtaghaqaput seghleliillghet , piyaqliillghet , ikfiqellghet .
Qevutquqaagukut , anusimingllaqaagukut , uglaatellengegkaagukutlu . Ughleghiiqaagukut , qavalqumangitukut , iyataqaagukutlu .
Liigikestengnguukutlu Kiyaghneghmun qepghaghtekutfut pinitun kiyaghtaallemteggun , liisimakillemteggun , nuqetutillemteggun , nangllegtallemteggun , piniqipillemteggun , Agleghnalghiignekun Taghneghagnekun .
Qepghaatngwaaghput Kiyaghneq ungipaqellemteggun ipapilleq . Atuqaqaghput Kiyaghneghem aghtughyaghqaanghillgha , elqughutngalleqlu guututkelluku aghenqignemnnunllu saghumignemnnunllu .
Quulvallengaqukutlu ukavaghllengaqukutlu ; seghlequughsighaqukutlu usuqellengaqukutlu . Iqlengalghiinguniiqiinkut , iwernga akuziiqukut ipapigmeng .
Yuget nallukniqiinkut , naqamllu liisimakluta ; uglaghngaan tuquvzighaqukut , iwernga paninang unguvaakut . Aghyuughyaghngiinkut , tuqusigatiinkut .
Qivghungughngaamta , naqamllu quyangaghllawaaqukut ; aklumaghngaamta , naqamllu aklungighistaqaput yuget ; avaqraggiiteghngaamta , naqamllu pilwaaqukut sameng tamaghhaaneng .
Ugpeqaalgutemnni , Corinth-eghmiini , ipapighqullusi ayuqamsi . Ungipaatamsi piniqepigtamsi .
Nuqneghusimangitamsi piniqellemnneng , iwernga elpesinguut nuqneghutikat piniqilleghpesineng whangkunnun .
Maaten aleghqughamsi avaqutaqepiglleghhiistun , piniqeqeghtikut katam whangkuta piniqellemtestun elpesi .
Inglukegpenaki ugpeqaanghilnguut . Elqughutngallghenkuk seghleghenkuk inglukutepagningituk . Nighugenkuklu mamlegenkuklu qerngaghmetepagningituk .
Christ-am itagnaqsaghqaqenghitngwaaghaa Tughneghaq . Ugpeqat piyukellghit allanguut ugpeqaanghilngughneng .
Kiyaghnengllaqat manigughyaghqaanghitut Kiyaghneghem Temple-ngani . Qayughllak whangkuta Temple-kiinkut unguvalghiim Kiyaghneghem , Kiyaghneq pikaalghii , " Ellngitnillequngallu akulngitnillequngallu ; Kiyaghneqelleqaatnga , ellngitlu yukelleqanka . "
" Tamaaken apalluqluku Ataneq pikaalghii , Uniteki tamaakut yuget , aaftek ellngitneng . Saaftegpenaki ukmanginneghilnguut ; enkaam tuguklighlleqamsi .
Atakelleqaghpesinga , enkaam elpesi ighneqelleqamsillu panikelleqamsillu , piiq Ataneq Aghtughyaghqaghhaanghilnguq . "
Piniqegkamni ilakumtaamni , Kiyaghneq tamaakuneng akequsangllaqaatanganeng whangkunnun , ukmangighsaalteki allaaghhiinaat nukeggnii yugusimtallu taghneghamtallu . Pelungightengngwaaghelta qayughllak alikaghput Kiyaghneq .
Ilaliiqaghqut ilugpesigun . Kina alngunak anagngalghiimeng pingigataghput , ugpeqillgha naafqumangitaghput , talwa puughneqguusimangitaghput .
Ungipaatngunghitamsi tamaakuneng avutkennalusi . Sivunghani ungipaatkaqamsi piniqepiggnilusi , enkaam kiyaghtelgusighlleqamsi nalighmeng tuqulgusighlleqamsi .
Neghyukeghllaglusi ayuqamsi , qukaayugutkepigtamsi . Kayemeghllagaqaghpesinga . Enkaam seghleliilleghllamnni paninang tevughaaqunga quyalleghmeng .
Kaataqngamta Macedonia-mun , meghnaalipagningitkaagukut . Seghleliiqaagukut tamangani , yuget aaghtiiraaqaqiinkut , teggellghiiqaagukutlu .
Iwernga Kiyaghneghem ilutughsaghaqii iilqengngalghiit , enkaam ilutughsaghiinkut tagistelleghmikun Titus whangkunnun .
Ilutughtekaagukut tagiiqngan Titus , iwernga ilutughllengataghaghtukut ungipaasinkut elpesinun ilutughsaamaniluni . Ungipaatiinkut elpesinun esghaghyupiggnilunga , qivghuknilunga seghleliighqelleghpesineng , kayusighyupiggnilungallu . Tawaten pilleghpesi wanlegi quyasteghllagaanga .
Qaywa latamkun qivghusteghngaamsi , avuteghqutkengngunghitanka latanka . Sivukun avuteghqesaghtunga qayughllak latama qivghustaghtekangisi .
Quyangunghitunga latamnun qivghusimanilusi . Iwernga quyaghllaguunga qivghulleghpesi allangughtestekaqegkangi kiyaghtaallesi . Qivghulleghsi Kiyaghneghem atuqegkaqaa elpesinun , enkaam naten alngunak whangkuta aqnightellghitamsi .
Kiyaghneghem atuqaqaa qivghulleq yugnun avuteghqelluki seghleghqellghitneng , yugulillengesqelluki . Kitum alngunak avuteghqutkennaanghitaa yugulilleq . Iwernga qivghulleq nunameng pi tuqustiiquq .
Esghaqaghtegguqun sangutanga Kiyaghneghem apeghiiqaa qivghulleghpesigun . Qivghulleghpesi efqughutesugllagiisi Kiyaghneghmun . Elngaatall ipapighqennaqutkegkaayaghtusi anaggutellghinnilusi . Ugumiyagutkaqaghsi anaggutelleq , alingruuqaagusillu . Esghaghyupigtekaqaghpesinga , pinitun pikaagusi , aghyuuqaqaghsillu anaggutkaq . Tawaten pilleghpesigun ipapighqegkaagusi apalliinnilusi .
Enkaam qaywa tawaten latayaghngaamsi , apalluqngunghitaqa anaggutkaq , nalighmeng tawavek seghletun pikaanun . Itupill latakaqamsi liigikngwaaghesqellusi Kiyaghneghem esghaamanghani tuun始ngwaaghlusi whangkunnun ayuqelghiisi .
Tamaaken apalluqluku ilutughtengngaakut . Ilutughtengnginaghpenaamta , iwernga quyaaghataghaghtukut esghaghluku Titus-em quyamallgha . Qamagllusi sumeghyalingiitesimaaghsi .
Qanatkegkaqamsi Titus-mun efquqnilusi . Elpesinun piiqngami liitkaqii ipangutangi sameng pillghenka elpesineng ayuqelghiit , enkaam kaynguyagutellghitanka qanatkillghenka . Iiwleng ipapighqelluta aleghqughaqamsi . Tawateghpigaq ipanguut qanatkilleghput Titus-mun .
Enkaam Titus-em wanlegi piniqaaghtiisi sumeghtaghaatkenneghminigu qaatkutngalleghsi ellminun . Upughatkaqegkesillu alingellelighlusi , ungellegtellelighlusi .
Quyaghllaguunga qayughllak neghyukeghllaglusi ayuqamsi samun tamaghhaanun !
Ugpeqaalgutemni , whangkuta liisimakesuwamsi Kiyaghneghem nangllegtallghaneng ugpeqanun yughaghvigitni Macedonia-m .
Ikfiqliightelleghllagita nanghiighsaghallengesteghllakaqiit . Qaywa aklumaghllagyaghngaaghmeng , paninang quyamaghllakaagut repall ighlegpenateng tuunikaagut kayusighnaluki ilangi ugpeqat .
Ungipaatamsi tuunikaagut tuunyaghqaghtutalmegestun , talwa tuuniighataghaqaagut . Tawaten pikaagut qayughllak ellngit tuuniyulghiit . Kitum alngunak pisqumangitii .
Talwa aapuquuteghllakaagut tuunilgusighinaluteng Kiyaghneghem yugitnun .
Tuunillghat uglaqaaguq sighimakellemnneng . Sivukluteng ellmeggneng pegtut Ataneghmun , taagken whangkunnun piyukellghakun Kiyaghneghem .
Titus elpesinitaqngami piinlighikaaguq qerngughtilleghpesineng manimeng . Enkaam kayemaghput kayusiisaghtiisqellusi apeghiighesqelluku nangllekusaghsi tunusaq .
Salleghpesigun tamaghhaakun pinitun piiqusi : ugpeqilleghpesigun , akuzilleghpesigun , liisimalleghpesigun , kayusighiyukestalleghpesigun , piniqilleghpesigunllu whangkunnun . Maatemillu pinitun piiqitek tuunilleghpesigun .
Qelghunghitamsi tuunisqellusi , iwernga ungipaatngwaamsi naten ilangit tuunimatangi . Enkaam tuunilleghpesi ipapighqelleqaa piniqilleghsi ipangutanga .
Liisimakaghsi piniqingalleghllaga Atanemta Jesus Christ-am . Aklungighllagmini tawalliima ellmineng katam aklumaaghtekaaguq elpesi apalluqlusi . Tawaten pikaaguq aklungighisqeqaghllusi aklumalleghmikun .
Awatangani elpesi qerngughtiyuwhaaqaagusi manimeng , tuunikaagusillu qayughllak tuuniyulghiisi . Sumemni whatelluku piyaqufsigu , itagnaghnayaghtusi ,
nagneghusaqufsigu piinliqaghsi ! Sagiqngakaagusi qerngughtiyuwhaaghaqngafsi manimeng . Enkaam sagiqenqigllusi apeghiighteggu qerngughtekaghsi . Tuunitek tuunilleghqaghpesistun .
Tuuniyupigtekufsi Kiyaghneghem tuguklighlleqii tunusasi . Piyukaqaa yuuk tuunisqelluku tuunyaghqalgukan , iwernga avangiskan tuuninghisaghngaan .
Nuuqragtistesugunghitamsi ilasi nuuqragtinghisimaluki .
Maaten llileghllaglusi ayuqusi enkaam kayusighyaghqaqasi tamaakut aklulghiit . Iwernga aklukufsi taawa ellngita kayusighlleqiisi . Tawaten pikufsi kayusiitullequsi enkaam atunem pillequsi .
Katam Akuzitet Igaqegkat igaqellghistun , " Yuuk saghnaghllakaq suyvaghsimangituq , iwernga yuuk saghnapagumangilnguq aklunaanghituq . "
Iyamsiqayugvikaqa Kiyaghneq qayughllak Titus kayusighiyugtesteghllakanga elpesineng katam whangkutestun .
Titus angeghqumakaaguq elpesinun pisqesamteggu . Elpesinun piyupigtekaaguq , taana ellngan piyukelqaa .
Ugpeqaalgutfut Titus-mun maligutesnaqaghput . Qamagtengngwaaghluteng ugpeqat qerngughutkayuget yughaghvigni usuqepigtaqaat ungipaqillghaneng Pinilghiineng Ungipaneng .
Taananginaagpenaan , ugpeqat nakmikegkaqaat maligutesqelluku whangkutgun , tuuniyaghtuqumta nangllekusameng tunusameng ugpeqanun . Tawaten pinguukut usuqellengesqelluku Ataneq , yugnunllu liitesqelluku kayusighiyulleghput .
Piraamsinguukut kitumun alngunak seghlequufqaamta pisqelluta naten aflengakaqutfut taana tunusaghllak .
Enkaam tamaaken apalluqluku atuqsugaqaghput Kiyaghneghmi elqughutngalghii , yugnillu elqughutngalghii .
Titus-enkugnunllu maligutesnaqaghput ilanga ugpeqaalgutfut . Awen esghaghnaluku natetulanga piiqaghput , piyalghiikut iiwleng kayusighiyukestaghluni ayuqeftuq . Wanlegi maaten kayusighiyugllagughtuq qayughllak neghyukeghllakangisi .
Titus qepghalgutkaqa , qepghalgusighaqaanga kayusiinnalusi . Taakuklu ugpeqaalgutek ugpeqat yughaghvignilnguut kayagtekaqagket . Quulvaghllagluku Christ-a ayuqaak .
Enkaam Corinth-eghmiini , esghaghtesteggu piniqilleghsi taakugnun yugegnun . Taagken piniqilleghpesi ipapighqesleqiit ugpeqat yughaghvignilnguut sangan qanatkellemnneng elpesi .
Latatkenghisaghngaamkun ayuqaqa tunusaq tuyughyaghqaghsi Kiyaghneghem yugitnun Jerusalem-em .
Liisimakamsi kayusighiyuglusi ayuqusi enkaam qanatkaqamsi ugpeqiitnun Macedonia-m . Whaten pikaagunga , " Awatangani ima ugpeqaalgutet Achaia-melnguut yataaghqegkaagut tuuninaluteng . " Sagiqelleghpesi allulluki ugpeqat maanlenguut tuuniyugtestekaqiitlu .
Iwernga kayaggnaqanka ilangi ugpeqaalguteput elpesinun . Apalluqaqa qanatkilqa elpesineng temngingufqaan pisqelluku . Yataaghqesqesugamsi katam whanga pisqellemtun elpesi ,
luuraq Macedonia-ghmiit ilangita maliggnayukangatnga Corinth-mun . Esghaqumisi yataaghqellghillusi tunusaghqaghpesineng , taawa whangkuta kayngusaakelleqiinkut , elpesillu kaynguyugllequsi .
Enkaam sumeghtaghaghtunga sivumni kayagtekestaghnaluki ilangi ugpeqaalguteput . Tawaten kayusiilleqiisi yataaghqesqelluku akequsaqegkaghsi tunusaq . Taagken kaaskuma tunusaghsi apeghiighngallequq , enkaam yuget liisimakelleqaat tuuniyulleghsi , nakaan qayughllak tuuniyaghqaategpesineng .
Neqamikluku una , yuuk palaghhaghmeng piitutmeng piitesighaqumi , palaghhaan saghnallequq . Yuuk uglaghluku piitutmeng piitesighaqumi , uglaghluku saghnallequq .
Tamaghhaghpesi sumeghtaghaatkiteggu tuunilleghqaghtutalesi . Ighlegumaghpesi tuunigpenasi nalighmeng tuuniyaghqaategpesineng . Iwernga quyakusiqluku tuuniiqitek qayughllak Kiyaghneghem piniqii tawatelnguut tuunistet .
Kiyaghneghem tuunyaqlegwiisi aklukegkaghpesineng qaayghulluku . Enkaam iiwleng sameng alngunak pilwaaqellequsi , siipngaanllu kayusiitesqelluki ilasi .
Akuzitni Igaqegkani igaqngaaq , " Ighlellngunani tuuniiquq aklumalghiinun ; pinitun pingallgha nagneghyaghqaaguq quunpeng . "
Kiyaghneghuuq tuunikayuk piitutmeng piitesighaghtemun , neqmengllu neghyaghqameng . Tuunelleqaa qamaglluku piitun aklukegkaghsi , nagusleqiillu . Enkaangam unataghllagllequsi qayughllak ighlegilnguusi .
Sakun tamaghhaakun aklungighisleqiisi , naran始ngunaan tuunisqellusi salleghmi tamaghhaani . Enkaam tuunilleghpesigun whangkutgun uglalghiim iyamsiqayugvikelleqaat Kiyaghneq .
Kiyaghneghem yugita Jerusalem-emelnguut allgeghlleqiit aklukegkateng tunusaghpesigun . Enkaam yulghuteghllaget iyamsiqayulleghmeng tevughallequt Kiyaghneghmun .
Tuunyaghqaghpesigun ipapighqellequsi ugpeqinganilusillu qaatkutnganilusillu Pinilghiinun Ungipaanun Christ-am . Tamaaken apalluqluku yuget usuqelleqaat Kiyaghneq . Usuqelleqaatlu ighlellngunasi tuunilleghpesineng Jerusalem-eghmiinunllu ilangitnunllu .
Enkaangam piniqepigllusi yughaatkelleqiisi apalluqluku piniqelleghrugllak Kiyaghneghem tuun始ngakanga elpesinun .
Yeqay iyamsiqayugvikelteggu Kiyaghneq tunusaanun akuzitet apeghpagningilkangat .
Ilangita yugpesi piiqaatnga tetugtaghnilunga elpesininnemni , iwernga tetugiganniiqaatnga elpesininneghinnemni . Whanga Paul , whangamneng katam , Christ-am qusevegngallghakunllu piniqellghakunllu ,
tetugtesneghitaghhnakefsinga laalighfikenqigtekumsi . Iwernga tetugyaghqaqenghilkumki tamaakut yuget pilghiit kiyaghtengngunilunga nunam yugistun , elngaatall tetugnaanghitanka .
Nunametngughngaamta pilluwiigatukut nunam yugan pilluwallghistun .
Guututet pilluwaasiput nunam yugan guututkenghitii . Guututeput Kiyaghneghem aghtughyaghqaanghillghaneng pilguut . Naafqesaqlegwiit ayepsugilnguut mingllutet anguyagem nekefquqii yuget uvitangitgun .
Taakutgun guututetgun naafqaqaput anguyagem iqlengii , sumeghneghitlu aangaayugneghet . Apeghtughillghita amigighaqiit yuget liitelleghqiitneng Kiyaghneghmeng . Katam pilluwaghtet tugutellghistun anusimingllaghyaghqameng , whangkutallu tugwaaqaput qamaglluki sumeghneghet qaatkutesqelluki Christ-amun .
Christ-amun qaatkutngngwaaqufsi , taawa aghyuughiyaghqaaghllequkut qaatkunneghilngughnun .
Nanqigtiiqusi esghallghiinaghpesigun . Christ-amun pikepestaaghnikufsi , neqamikluku whangkutallu Christ-am pikiinkut , elpesistun .
Kayngukigataqa qanatkivleghapalqa Atanghem igleghutistengughtestekanganga elpesinun . Tawaten pikaaguq whangkunnun kayemesqelluku ugpeqilleghsi , nakaan naafqennaluku .
Sumeghtaghaghpenasi alingesnaqutkengngunilusi latamkun .
Ilangita piiqiit Paul-em latangi seghleghllaguniluki aghsaaghmikaghnganiluki , naqam whangkunninneghmini , aghsaan ayuqaquq , akuziyiitaquqlu !
Tamaakut yuget tawaten pikat liigiklitgu sameng pilleghput latatgun , tamaakunguut ataasit piyaghqaput ellngitnun pikumta .
Inglunnaqutkennaanghitukut tamaakunun aangaayuglleghhiinun . Sumeghtaghaghaqut aangniluteng qayughllak ungipaatutaqelghiit aangniluteng . Nalluughhaghmeng !
Qukaayugutkennaanghitaghput alngunak qepghaqaq Kiyaghneghem kayagusimangilkanga whangkunnun . Iwernga qukaayugutkengnginaghlleqaghput qepghaqaq kayagutkaa whangkunnun . Elpesillu ilatngaasi qepghaqamnnun .
Sivulighpigaagukut ungipaqiyaghtuqani elpesinun Pinilghiineng Ungipaaneng Christ-am . Enkaam alpagigataghput qepghaqaq Kiyaghneghem kayagutkaa whangkunnun .
Qukaayugutkelleqaghput taananginaq qepghaqaq pikaghput , nakaan ilangita qepghaqaat . Ugpelleghtughtekufsi sighimaakut kayusighataghiisqelluta qepghaqamnneng .
Enkaam ungipaqiyaghtughllequkut Pinilghiineng Ungipaneng ilangitnun nunat . Qukaayugutkesugunghitaghput qepghaqaq ilangita apeghiiqaat .
Iwernga igaqngaaq Akuzitni Igaqegkani whaten , " Kina alngunak qukaayugsukumi , qukaayugutkelligu Atanghhiinaq . "
Atanghem tugukliigatii pinighnilghiit . Itupill Atanghem tuguklighaqii tamaakut pinighniluki pikani .
Sighimakamsi nekeggmetutesqellunga akuzikuma temngitwhalghiistun natengiighhaq . Nekeggmetuteqaghtengnga .
Qungyaghaqunga Kiyaghneghem qungyaqellghatun elpesi , qayughllak tuusimaamsi Christ-amun . Pelungilngughestun ugiighnaqelghiistun aang始ghusimaamsi ellnganun , ugikesqelluku ellnginaa .
Iwernga alingutkaqamsi anguyagem puughhnayukangisi , katam tawaten nemeghyam peghqiniqutkelluku puughtellghatun Eve . Enkaam elpesi piniqnanighwaaghnayukafsigu Christ-a .
Ungipaqaqngamteki Pinilghiit Ungipat elpesinun , ugpeqegkaqaghsi Jesus , tuguklighagsillu Agleghnalghiik Taghneghak . Iwernga nagasukestaghluki ayuqegkaqasi ungipaqiyaghtulghiit ilanganeng Jesus-em . Tuguklighiyugtusillu ilanganeng taghnegham , ugpeqsukaqasillu ilangi pinilghiit ungipat .
Tamaakut ungipaqistet apostle-nguniluteng piiqut . Sumeghmeggni aangwaaghuniiqut apostle-et . Iwernga liisimakanka aangwaaghunghitut whangamneng .
Akuzillgiteghngaaghma , liisimaghllagtunga . Uglaghngaan liigikestaqamsi liisimallemneng .
Elpesinun akileghtughsaqumangitunga ungipaqaqngamki Pinilghiit Ungipii Kiyaghneghem . Tawaten pikaagunga qusevegllunga quulvaghnalusi . Seghleghqesingaa-a tawaten pilunga ?
Ugpeqat ilangitnilnguut yughaghviget akileghtuqaqaatnga elpesinillunga . Wayaqallghuughanka maningitneng kayusiinnalusi .
Elpesinitaqngama ughleghiightellghitamsi kayusiitesqellunga aklukegkamneng . Ugpeqaalgutet Macedonia-meng tagitkaqaatnga sameng tamaghhaaneng aklukegkamneng . Enkaam aapfikellghitamsi aklukegkamneng , aapfiknaanghitamsi .
Kitum alngunak Achaia-mi aghuliighhnaanghitaa qukaayugtelqa taagken . Tawaten piinga Christ-am ipapighqellghakun whangamnilngughqun .
Kayutengllanghitutemneng elpesinun , sumeghpesinii-i piniqenghinnilusi pitsi whangamnun ? Kiyaghneghem liisimakaa piniqilqa elpesinun .
Taawa ighsakiivikumanginaghnaqamsi manigpesineng . Tawaten piiqunga qukaayuggnaniisqelluki apostle-esighwaaghet whangkutestun qepghaghnilghiit akileghtuusangunateng .
Tamaakut yuget apostle-esighwaaghuut puughtilghiit yugneng iqlengiqelleghmegteggun . Yugnun sumeghtaghaatkestaqut Christ-amun apostle-epiikniluteng .
Taamengwhaqun . Talwa Tughneghaq allangughtaquq ellmineng katam aliighyaghqaaluni kuukgutngalghiitun yaqulegtun .
Enkaam saghiighaniitut Tughneghaam qepghaghtengi tawaten pikumeng . Yugnun sumeghtaghaatkestaqut elqughutngalghiinguniluteng qepghaghtengi Kiyaghneghem . Iwernga kenlemi Kiyaghneghem aghyuughlleqii elqughutngalghiimeng aghyuulleghmeng anaggutellghitnun .
Alla piimsi , kitum alngunak sumeghtaghaatkenghillinga temngitwhangulunga . Iwernga tawaten sumeghtaghaatkengngukufsinga , tugukliqaghtengnga temngitwhangulunga . Taagken whangallu qukaayugtevleghaghllequnga .
Qukaayugutkelqa whangamneng Ataneghmeng pingunghituq . Itupill akuzinguunga temngi pilghiistun .
Uglalghiit ugpeqaanghilngughestun qukaayugtaqut qepghaqameggneng , enkaam whangallu tawaten qukaayugllequnga .
Sumeghpesini peghqinepiggnilusi piiqusi . Enkaam quyakusiqluku nagataqasi temngitwhalghiit .
Tuguklighaqasi qelellghit nikimqun elpesi qepghaghtelaaghet ellngitnun . Kagukaqestaqusi , teglegvikestaqusi , ukaliqestaqusillu , talwa gginaghpesigun qasaghtestaqlusi .
Kaynguyugtunga kayaatepigtukut tawaten pilleghqamnneng elpesinun tamaakustun apostle-esighwaaghestun . Kina alngunak qukaayugsaghqaakan , whangallu qukaayugllequnga . Iwernga tawaten pilleghqaq temngitwhanguuq .
Taakut apostle-esighwaaghet , Hebrew-ngwaat ? Whangallu Hebrew-nguunga . Israel-eghmiingwaat ? Whangallu Israel-eghmiinguunga . Abraham-em kingunqakii ? Whangallu kingunqaanga .
Christ-am qepghaghtekakii ? Iwernga whanga pinighataghaghtunga qepghaghta ellngitneng . Taawa akuziinga nallekaghnilngughestun . Qepghaghataghaqaagunga ellngitneng , anusiminglaghvigmetaaghaqaagungallu ellngitneng . Kagsagmillengegkaagunga kestekaanghilngughmeng , uglaghngaan tuquvzighaataqaagunga .
Tallimagyagneng Jews-et igleghutistengita kagsagmigtestaataghaatnga . ( 39-ngwaaqut ataasit kagsagmillghet . )
Rome-eghmiit umiilwaaghita pingayuneng anaguleghtestekaqaatnga . Ataasimeng ilangita yuget milughpagaataghaatnga . Pingayuneng angyiighututaqaanga enkaam ataasimeng unulqusiq , aghnelqusiq uughhutkaqaanga kelliini .
Uglapiglleghhiimi igleghallemni elngaatall yakughniightunga kiiwni , wayaghniighteneng , talwa yulgutemnengllu , Gentile-enengllu . Yakughniightungallu neghllagni , kilgaani , kelliinillu . Talwa yakughniightunga ugpeqaalgutesighwaaghneng .
Ughleghiighllakaagunga , piyaqliighaqlunga . Ilangani qavaghpenanga , iyataghngaaqlunga , meqsugngaaqlunga . Awen neqngitaqlunga , azigutiitaqlunga , ghhuutaqlungallu aatkiitem .
Tamaakut saaghwitgun , aghhutanga tamaghhaan sumeghyalitkegkaqanka ugpeqaalgutet tamaghhitni yughagvigni .
Ugpeqaalgutem ugpeqillgha kayaanneghani , whangallu kayaataqunga . Ugpeqaalguta kitum seghleghqesneghagu , sakritaqunga .
Qukaayuggnaqngukuma , qukaayugllequnga kayaalliqusimneng .
Kiyaghneghem liisimakaanga iqlengiqnaanghitunga . Ellnga Atakaa Atanghem Jesus-em , usuqsaghqaq quunperugllak .
Damascus-mellunga , governor-em tugustesukaqaanga . ( Umiilgem Aretas-em governor-ngughtestekaqaa . ) Enkaam tugusqellunga pilluwaghteni kelengakistekaqii neghllagem amigllagitni .
Iwernga ilakumtaaghma ukigtekaqaatnga pasketegnekun mingllutem qergesegkenkun enkaam anakaagunga governor-meng .
Qukaayugsaghqaagunga , aneghneghqusiinghiteghngaan . Paninang ungipaannaqamsi esghaghwaallemneng , Atanghemllu aliighquqaaneng whangamnun .
