Liisimakaqa yuuk Christ-amelnguq . Qula estamat siipneqluki ayumiqulleghni agani naghughtekani Kiyaghneghem mayuutqaghtekaqaa pingayaanun qilagem . Nallukngwaaghaqa yuuk yugusiminitutanga nalighmeng yugusimineng aan始ngakaatanga , iwernga Kiyaghneghem liisimakaa .
Liisimakaqa taana yuuk Kiyaghneghem mayuutqaghtekaqaa Paradise-mun . Nallukngwaaghaqa yuuk yugusiminitutanga nalighmeng yugusimineng aan始ngakaatanga , iwernga Kiyaghneghem liisimakaa .
Tawani nagatkaqii sangwaat apeghyaghqaanghilnguut . Tamaakut iinghutkaagut yugmun akuzitkesaghqaaluteng .
Qukaayugutkennaqaqa taana yuuk , iwernga qukaayugutkennaqenghitunga whangamneng iwerngaqun kayaalliqusiqegkaghhiinamneng .
Qukaayugutkesukuma whangamneng , temngingunaanghitunga qayughllak apeghlleqaqa ipapilleq . Iwernga qukaayugutkennanghitunga whangamneng , qayughllak yugnun sumeghtaghaatkesugtunga elqughllunga esghapallghitgunllu nagatellghitgunllu whanga .
Kiyaghneghem aliightekaqeghngaaki whangamnun uglaapiglleghhiit sangwaat qilagmi , qukaayugtestesunghitaanga . Enkaam Kiyaghneghem qusevegtesqellunga sikughllungestaanga yugusimkun . Taana sikughlluk ungipaghtenguuq Tughneghagh-meng . Taam ikfiqestaanga qusevegngasqellunga .
Pingayuneng ketwell Ataneghmun yughaghaqunga iqitesqelluku .
Iwernga piinga , " Kayusilqa naamaaq elpenun suflughtesqelluku taana ikfiqelleq qayughllak aghtughyaghqaanghilqa iknaqelleghpigaagwaquq kayaalliqneghpeni . " Enkaam quyakusiqluku qukaayugtaqunga kayaalliqusimneng whangamnitesqelluku Christ-am aghtughyaghqaanghillgha .
Taana apalluqluku quyaaqunga kayaalliqnganemni , seghlequullengnemni , piyaqliinemni , amyuutkellengnemni , allaaghhiinaghmengllu seghleliinemni Christ-a apalluqluku . Qayughllak kayaalliqnganemni taawa iknaqaqunga .
Akuzinguunga temngitwhastun , iwernga elpesi tawaten pistaghpesinga . Elpesi pinitun akuzitkesaghqaqsaghaghpesinga ilagpesinun . Qaywa sasiinghiteghngaaghma , tamaakut " aangwaaghet apostle-et " aangwaaghunghitut whangamneng .
Elpesinillunga nekeglluwaan uglaapiglleghhiit allaaghhiinaat allaaghlluwhaghtillghet pikaqanka . Tamaakut ipapighqaatnga apostle-epiigutka .
Sakaqsingi ugpeqat ilangitnilnguut yughaghviget elpesinun pimangilkemneng ? Ataasighhiinaq allanguuq , akilguqumangitamsi . Seghevutaghtengnga anagsimakumsi !
Laalighfiknaqaqamsi pingayiitkun , iwernga ughleghiighutkestesunghitunga elpesinun . Elpesi sumeghmikaqamsi , nakaan saghyasi . Taghnughhaqelghiistun ayuqamsi . Taghnughhaat aflengakiyaghqaanghitut angayuqameggneng , iwernga angayuqat aflengaksaghqaqiit taghnughhateng .
Tuunyaghqaaghtamsi sameng tamaghhaaneng whanga pimneng , talwa whangamneng tuunellequnga elpesinun . Piniqataghanemsi , llangaqa elpesi piniqepagigataghpesinga .
Elpesillu whangallu liisimakaghput ughleghiightesimangitamsi . Iwernga ilagpesi anaggusimaniitnga . Piiqut puughneqguunnilusi iqlengiqellemkun .
Naten tawaten pistemsi ? Sakengegkaazinga elpesineng kayagtaqngamki yuget elpesinun ?
Kayagtekaqaqa Titus elpesinun pisqelluku , ugpeqaalgutfutlu maligutesqaqa . Titus-em puughtekaqisii ? Nakaa , Titus-lu whangkutung qepghaqaghpung ataasiiguq , ataasikun taghneghakun .
Sumeghpesinii-i elpesinun ipapighqennaqutkestegneguu anaggutellghinnilutung ? Nakaa ! Kiyaghneghem nagaquumanghani , akuziiqukung Christ-am akuzisqellghatun . Piniqegkamni , sangwa qamaglluku piiqaghpung iknaqughsaghnaluku ugpelleghsi .
Sumeghyalitkaqamsi elpesinun kaaskuma esghaqumsi allaknayukamsi whanga sighimakellemneng . Elpesillu whanga esghaqufsinga allaknayukafsinga sighimakelleghpesineng . Sumeghyalitkaqamsi aghivatngunayukafsi , aqinakutngunayukafsi , sakraatutngunayukafsi , ellnginaayugutngunayukafsi , seghlequughutngunayukafsi , yiillgitngunayukafsi , qukaayugutngunayukafsi , suuglliqutngunayukafsi .
Sumeghyaliiqunga alla takukumsi Kiyaghneghma kayngusaaknayukanganga sivugpesini apalluqluki seghleghqellesi . Enkaam qivghughllagllequnga qayughllak uglalghiini elpesi seghleghqumanginaagusi avuteghqegpenasi . Paninang sumeghtaghaghaqusi sex-meng pelunginneghilngughmeng , sex-a seghletun atuqaqaghsi , sex-ellghetlu anagngalghiit nuqetusigatasi .
Una pingayiitkaa laalighhnaqelleghma elpesinun . Akuzitni Igaqegkani igaqngaaq whaten , " Yuuk anaggusimanikatgu , maalghuk nalighmeng pingayut liisimakistet ipapighqesaghqaqaat anaggutellgha . "
Tuunglighhaani laalighfikaqngamsi kelengasaaqaqamsi tamaakut sivunghani seghleghqelghiit . Ilangitlu kelengasaaqaqanka , taginqigtekuma aghyuughmiglleqniluki seghleghqumanginaqata . Tamaanneghiteghngaaghma kelengasaaghnaqanka .
Whangamnun ipapighqestesukesi Christ-a akuziiqutanga whangamkun . Christ-a kayaanneghituq aghyuughmikumisi , itupill aghtughyaghqaanghituq .
Qaywa Christ-a kayaatkaayaghtuq qaquuraghaqngamegteggu , maaten kiyaghtengnguuq Kiyaghneghem aghtughyaghqaanghillghakun . Whangkutallu kayaatukut katam Christ-am kayaatkaayallghatun . Iwernga elpesinitkumta kayusiilleqamsi Kiyaghneghem aghtughyaghqaanghillghakun .
Yuvghiightek elpesineng liigikesqelluku ugpeqepiigutsi Jesus Christ-a . Liigikenghistegguu-u Jesus Christ-a kiyaghtengngutanga ilugpesini ? Ilugpesininneghitngukan , taawa ugpeqepiillghitaghsi .
Sunanguq liigikiteggu Kiyaghneghmun itagnaqumaniluta .
Yughaghaqukut Kiyaghneghmun kayusiitesqellusi anaggutefqaafsi pisqellusi . Iwernga yughaangunghitukut ipapighqennaluku elpesinun Kiyaghneghmun itagnaqumaniluta . Itupill whangkuta yughaatkaqamsi elqughutngaan pisqellusi , qaywa yuget pighngiinkut itagnaqellghinniluta Kiyaghneghmun .
Kipullginaaghpagningitaghput ipapilleq ; itupill ilapgayaghqaqaghput .
Quyaaqukut kayaannemta , iknaqnguneghpesini . Enkaam yughaatkaqamsi veghunneqigtesqellusi kiyaghtesqesullghanun Kiyaghneghem .
Tamaaken apalluqluku lataaqamsi elpesinun pivagilgama qayughllak nanqigsunghilkemsi aghyuughmigyaghqaalusi . Atanghem qelqaqaanga nanqigtestengulunga elpesinun . Enkaam nanqigsugamsi kayusiinnalusi ugpeqilleghtughtesqellusi , nakaan kayaalisqellusi .
Ugpeqaalgutemni , tawaten始ngam piinga . Quyangatek . Veghutek kiyaghtesqesullghanun Kiyaghneghem . Pisqesullemtun pitek . Kiyaghtek itagnaqullusi , nekeggmetullusi . Enkaam Kiyaghneq tenemenga piniqellghemllu nekeggmellghemllu elpesinilli .
Quyakututaqitek agleghnalghiikun naalleghqun .
Qamaglluteng ugpeqaalgutet piniqiisinguq .
Nangllegtallgha Atanghem Jesus Christ-am , piniqellghallu Kiyaghneghem , qerngaghmetellghallu Agleghnalghiim Taghnegham elpesinilli .
Ukut latat Paul-meng pinguut , apostle-meng . Yuget nakmikellghitaatnga apostle-ngulunga , talwa kayagtellghitaatnga . Apostle-nguughtekaagunga Jesus Christ-akunllu Kiyaghneghqunllu Atakun , unguvaghtestikaq ellnganeng tuqulleghmeng .
Lataaqamsi ugpeqani Galatia-melngughni . Qamaglluteng ugpeqaalgutma maanlenguut piniqiisinguk whangamnun maligulluteng .
Kiyaghneghem Atamta , Atanemtallu Jesus Christ-am nanglleklisillu nekeggmellelguslisilillu .
Christ-a ellmineng aghqutkegkaaguq seghleghqellemnnun , itemunnaluta whaken seghleghmeng kiyaghtaalleghmeng . Kiyaghnemta Atam piyukellghatun pikaaguq .
Enkaam Kiyaghneq usuqellengli quunperugllak kenlengunaan . Amen .
Saghiighayagutamsi aawallu pegtaghtaghsi tuqlughistezi nangllegtallghakun Christ-am , tuguklighiisi allaneng " pinilghiineng ungipaneng " .
Avaqraggiituq alla " pinilghiineng ungipaneng " . Iwernga ilangita yuget teggellghiightestaqiisi allangughhnaqutkelleghmegteggun Pinilghiit Ungipat Christ-ameng ayuqelghiit .
Qaywa yaqulek qilagmeng , nalighmeng nalimta whangkuta ungipaqegkumteki " pinilghiit ungipat " allanguluki ungipaqegkamnneng elpesinun , taana ungipaqilghi Kiyaghneghem nanqiglligu aghyuulleghmun .
Sivunghani ungipaatkaqamsi , whaa ungipaannaqlaataghamsi , kitum alngunak ungipaqegkumiki " pinilghiit ungipat " allanguluki ugpeqegkaghpesineng , Kiyaghneghem nanqiglligu aghyuulleghmun .
Tawaten akuzillemkun efqughhnaqutkengngunghitanka yuget . Nakaa , Kiyaghneghhiinaaguq efqughsukaqa . Paninang yugnun efqughtinaqutkengngukuma , Christ-amun qepghaghtengunaanghitunga .
Ugpeqaalgutemni , una liisimakesugaqa elpesinun , Pinilghiit Ungipat ungipaqaqegkenka yugneng pingunghitut .
Nagaquqaqenghitanka yugneng , talwa kitum alngunak apeghtuutkumangitii whangamnun . Jesus Christ-am aliightekaqii whangamnun .
Nagaquqaqaghsi natesaatka maligtengnguluki Jews-et kiyaghtaallghit . Elngaatall nangllegyullngunanga amyuutkegkaqanka ugpeqat , taakunginaghhaagneng aviighutesnaqutkegkaqanka .
Ingyaqaqanka allulluki angtaalgutenka atuqnguluki Jews-et kiyaghtaallghit , qayughllak sagiqneghllaguyaghtunga sivunemta nangaghneghitnun .
Iwernga allgeghumangillunga Kiyaghneghem nakmikegkaqaanga , nangllegtalleghmikun tuqluqaqaanga .
Enkaam whangamnun aliightekaqaa kinangutanga Ighneni ungipaqesqelluku Gentile-enun . Kinkunun alngunak akuzitkesaghtullghitaqa taana ,
talwa Jerusalem-etellghitunga akuzitkennaluku apostle-ngughtekanun sivumni . Yeghlegi Arabia-mun piinga . Tagtalmi uteghnightunga Damascus-mun .
Tamaani pingayut ayumiqullghet atughluki Jerusalem-etunga aleghqughnaluku Cephas ( Peter ) . Ellnganitunga akimigaq unuk .
Kina alla apostle-a aleghqunghitaqa iwerngaqun James , Atanghem anglegutanga .
Aapqanka ukut ipanguut , Kiyaghneghem liisimakaanga iqlengiqngunghitunga .
Taagken igleghaanga Syria-munllu Cilicia-munllu .
Tamaani Judea-mi ugpeqat Christ-akun salin nalliigalkangatnga gginasaghqughlunga .
Taawanginaq liisimakaat nagaqulleghteng whaten , " Yuuk amyuqetiqestekegkaghput , naafqiinaqutkegkaqlu ugpeqillemnneng Christ-ameng maaten whaa ungipaqiiquq ugpeqilleghmeng Christ-akun ! "
Enkaam Kiyaghneq usuqaqaat whanga apalluqlunga .
Qula estamat siipneqluku ayumiqulleq atughluku uteghnightunga Jerusalem-emun ; Barnabas-em maligtaanga Titus-lu kelqaqa .
Kiyaghneghem liigikestaanga Jerusalem-etesqellunga . Kaasamta ugpeqat igleghutistenginiit qerngughutaghtesqanka . Tawani ungipamsugutanka naten Gentile-enun ungipaqillemneng Pinilghiineng Ungipaneng . Tawaten pikaagunga luuraq taakut igleghutistet apeghtughillghenka temnginguninayukatki sivunghanillu maatenllu .
Liigikanka apeghtughillghenka tuguklighiit qayughllak maligtisteka Titus , Greek-ngughngaan , circumcise-esqenghilkangat .
Iwernga ilangi ugpeqasighwaaghet aksaqluku ilatut whangkunnun riirnginaluku itemngalleghput Christ Jesus-kun . Qepghaghtelaaghughhneqigtesqelluta piinkut Liilightuusaanun .
Ellngitnun malighqutaqellghitukut talwa natengiighhaq almesiqesqelluki ipangullghit Pinilghiit Ungipat apeghtuusaqellemtestun elpesinun .
Taakut ugpeqat igleghutistengita allangughsimangitiit Pinilghiit Ungipat ungipaqaqegkenka . ( Igleghutistenguyaghngaata , whangamni allangughutngitut qayughllak Kiyaghneq taniillghituq . )
Igleghutistet liigikumaat Kiyaghneghmun neghyukusimaniluki whangamnun Pinilghiit Ungipat ungipaqesqelluki Gentile-enun , katam tawaten neghyukutellghatun Peter-mun Pinilghiit Ungipat ungipaqesqelluki Jews-enun .
Katam Kiyaghneq qepghaqaaguq Peter-kun apostle-kennaluku Jews-enun , whangamkunllu qepghaqaaguq apostle-kennalunga Gentile-enun .
Enkaam taakut igleghutistet , James-enkut Peter-enkut John-enkut , nekevghatilghiit ugpeqanun , liigikaat Kiyaghneghmun tunusalisimanilunga tawaten qepghiisqellunga Gentile-enun . Tamaaken apalluqluku Barnabas-lu iiggepung aghulatiit tuguklighniluku qepghaangulleghpung Gentile-enun , ellngit Jews-enun .
Taananginaq puygusnanighaat kayusiitesqelluki aklumalghiit , taanata nagneghusupigtekegka .
Tagtalmi taakwani Peter Antioch-melluni sameng anaggutkaq . Enkaam sivungitni ugpeqat aghyuughmigaqa anaggutellghaneng apalluqluku .
Peter neghelgusighikayuguyalghii Gentile-et ugpeqiitneng kenlanga James-em yuget Antioch-etestellghitnun . Iwernga kaasata neghelgusighnanighii Gentile-et , aaftekaqlu ellngitneng . Tawaten pikaalghii qayughllak alingelghii taakut yuget sagiqutngukangit Gentile-et ugpeqiit circumcise-eyaghqaaniluki .
Taagken qamaglluteng Antioch-eghmiit Jews-et ugpeqiit maligutkat Peter-em anaggutellghanun , talwa Barnabas-lu ilalluni .
Liigiksamki qaatkunneghitellghit apeghtuusiitnun Pinilghiit Ungipat , sivungitni yuget Peter piiqa , " Elpek qaywa Jew-ngughngaaghpek kiyaghtenguuten Gentile-estun , nakaan Jews-estun . Sangitangam Gentile-et Jews-estun kiyaghtesnaqutkesiki ? "
Jews-nguluta allgeqaagukut , nakaan Gentile-et seghleghqestet .
Naqamllu liisimakaghput Kiyaghneghem elqughutngalleghminun nallghusaghnaanghitaa yuuk qaatkutellghakun Liilightuusanun , tawatenginaq nallghusaghlleqaa ugpeqillghakun Jesus Christ-ameng . Talwa whangkuta Jews-eni ugpeqegkaqaghput Christ Jesus , Kiyaghneghem elqughutngallghanun nallghusiisqelluta ugpeqellemteggun Christ-a , nakaan qaatkutellemteggun Liilightuusanun . Kina alngunak qaatkutellghakun Liilightuusanun Kiyaghneghem elqughutngalleghminun nallghusaghyaghqaqenghitaa .
Jews-eni whangkuta nallghusaghtesugukumta Christ-akun , nakaan Liilightuusatgun , ilangita Jews-et seghleghqestengunilleqiinkut Gentile-estun . Enkaam Christ-anguftaa seghleghqestengughtestilghii ? Yeghlegillu !
Liilightuusat pegtekaqanka , atuqenqigsaguskumki taawa Liilightuusanun anaggullequnga .
Liilightuusatgun tuqukaagunga Liilightuusanun kiyaghsaghqaalunga Kiyaghneghmun .
Qaquuraatkaagunga Christ-amun maligullunga , enkaam whangangunaniimaaq kiyaghlleghhii ; Christ-angughsimaaq kiyaghlleghhii ilumni . Kiyaghtengngughngaaghma yugusimni , kiyaghtengnguunga ugpeqillemkun Ighneghaneng Kiyaghneghem . Piniqegkanganga , tuunegkaalghiillu whangamnun .
Enkaam pakigigataqa Kiyaghneghem tunusaa . Yuuk qaatkutelleghmikun Liilightuusanun nallghusaghyaghqaayaqan Kiyaghneghem elqughutngallghanun , taawa Christ-am tuqullgha temngingunayaghtuq .
Nallughhaghmeng elpesi Galatia-ghmiini ! Kitum puughtisi ? Puygustegguu aapghwaaqaqsaqegka Jesus Christ-am tuqullgha qaquurakun ?
Aaptaghllamsi : naten allgeghtekaqestekek Agleghnalghiik Taghneghak , qaatkutelleghpesigun Liilightuusanun nalighmeng ugpeqelleghpesigun nagatkaghsi ?
Nalluupigetsii ? Agleghnalghiignekun Taghneghagnekun piinlighluku nutaghaq unguvalleghsi , apeghiighnaqestegguu-u elpesineng katam ?
Ikfiqelleghsi temnginguftaa ? Ugpeqepestaaghaqa temngingunghituq .
Kiyaghneghem tuunegkaqisii-i Taghneghagmineng , allaaghlluwhaghtikaawalluu akulegpesini qayughllak qaatkegkesi Liilightuusat , nalighmeng ugpeqegkesi nagaquqaghsi ?
Akuzitet Igaqegkat aapqaqaat Abraham-em ugpeqegkaqaa Kiyaghneq , enkaam Kiyaghneghem nallghusaqaqaa elqughutngalleghminun .
Enkaam elpesi liisimakelleqasi tamaakut ugpeqillelget Kiyaghneghqun Abraham-em kinguneghpigaqii .
Akuzitet Igaqegkat aapqestaqaqaat Kiyaghneghmun nallghusaghnaqniluki Gentile-et elqughutngalleghminun ugpeqillghitgun . Neghighluku Kiyaghneghem aapqaqaa taana Pinilghii Ungipaq Abraham-emun , whaten piiqngami , " Qamagtengngwaaghluteng nunam ramkengi quyastellengnaqnguut elpegun . "
Abraham-em ugpeqegkaqaa enkaam quyastellengegkaq . Tawateghpigaq tamaghhaghmi ugpeqilghii quyastellengyaghqaaguq ellngatun .
Iwernga Kiyaghneghem aghyuughyaghqaqii tamaakut sighimalghiit qaatkutelleghmegteggun Liilightuusanun nallghusaghlleqniluteng elqughutngallghanun . Qayughllak igaqngaaq Akuzitni Igaqegkani whaten , " Kitum alngunak qaatkenghilkaki tamaghhiita igaqngalghiit igiitgun Liilightuusat nanqigtellengellequq aghyuughyaghqaaluni . "
Whateghlluwaaq liigiknaghtuq , kina alngunak nallghusaghyaghqaanghituq Kiyaghneghem elqughutngallghanun qaatkutelleghmikun Liilightuusanun . Qayughllak Akuzitet Igaqegkat pikaagut , " Taana Kiyaghneghem nallghusaqaa elqughutngalleghminun kiyaghllequq ugpelleghmikun . "
Iwernga qaatkullghii Liilightuusanun sighimangunghituq ugpelleghqun , qayughllak Akuzitet Igaqegkat pikaagut , " Sighimalghii Liilightuusatgun kiyaghllequq qaatkelluki . "
Enkaam Kiyaghneghem nanqigtekaqiinkut aghyuughnaluta apalluqluki Liilightuusat , iwernga Christ-am naveghqellikaqiinkut nanqiglleghqamnneng tugulleghmikun aghyuulleghqaghput . Qayughllak Akuzitet Igaqegkat pikaagut , " Nanqigtekaaguq aghyuughyaghqaaluni tamaghhaghmi agaghtekaq uqfigkun . "
Christ Jesus-em naveghqellikaqiinkut enkaam ellngakun Kiyaghneghem quyastekaqii Gentile-et taagken ataasimeng quyastelleghmeng akequsaqegkaminun Abraham-emun . Enkaam ugpelleghqun allgeghtagput Taghneghak Kiyaghneghem akequsaqegkakek .
Ugpeqaalgutemni , ungipaataghllamsi usputaghqameng aghhutanga tamaghhaan piiqelghiineng : yugek akequskumek sameng , igaqluku igakun , ateteklu igaqlukek , kitum alngunak aghuliighsaghqaqenghitaa akeqututellghak nalighmeng ilayaghqaqenghitaa .
Kiyaghneq akequsangllaghteqaaguq Abraham-emunllu kingunghanunllu . Kiyaghneghem akequsangllaamangitii , " Kingunghi , " Akequsangllaghteqaaguq ataasiinaghmun kinguneghmun , taana Christ-anguuq .
Taana liigikesugaqsaghaqa : Kiyaghneq akequsangllaqaaguq Abraham-emun enkaam akequsani pinaqnikaqaa . 430 ayumiqullghet kingungitneng akeqilleghmi , Kiyaghneghem tuunegkii Liilightuusat . Taakut Liilightuusat taana akequsaq satngunanighqennaanghitaa nalighmeng naafqennaanghitaa .
Liilightuusatgun allgeghhnaqngukumteggu Kiyaghneghem tunusaa , taawa akequsaakun allgeghhnaanghitaghput . Iwernga akeqilleghmikun Kiyaghneghem tunusani tuunegkaqaa Abraham-emun .
Sangameng Liilightuusat tuunegkaawat ? Tuunegkaagut yugnun liigikesqelluki anaggutellghit seghleghqellghuniluki . Taakut Liilightuusat tawatetkaagut kenlanga kinguneq tagillghanun . Ellnganguuq Kiyaghneghem akequsangllaqaa . Taakut Liilightuusat Kiyaghneghem yaqulegteggun tuunegkaqii Moses-mun . Taagken Moses-em uygukutistem tuunegkaqii yugnun .
Iwernga uygukutistesughniituq ataasiq akeqikumi . Kiyaghneq ataasighhaatmineng uygukutistesughniituq .
Liilightuusaat tengvimun ayuqatkii Kiyaghneghem akequsii ? Nakaa , yeghlegillu ! Liilightuusam unguvallengesaghqaqsaqumikut , taawa Kiyaghneghem nallghusaghnayaghiinkut elqughutngalleghminun taaggun Liilightuusakun .
Iwernga Akuzitet Igaqegkat pikaagut qamaglluki nunam yugi seghleghqellghem anusimingllaghaqii . Enkaangam Kiyaghneghem akequsaqegkani tuunelleqaa ugpeqikaghhiinaghnun Jesus Christ-ameng .
Salin ugpellghilluku anusimingllaghaayaghtukut Liilightuusanun . Liilightuusat aaghqutaqnguyaghiinkut kenlanga Kiyaghneghem whangkunnun liitestellghanun ugpelleq .
Liilightuusat apaqutisteksaghaput kenlanga Christ-am tagillghanun . Enkaam maaten ugpeqillemteggun Christ-akun , Kiyaghneghem nallghusaghyaghqaaghtiinkut elqughutngalleghminun .
Ugpelleq tagitanganeng Christ-akun Liilightuusat apaqutisteknanighaput .
Ugpeqilleghpesigun Christ Jesus-kun , qamagllusi Kiyaghneghem avaqutaqiisi .
Paaptaayaaqngafsi Christ-amun , aallghiistun Christ-a pikaqaghsi tawaten pilugugaqelleghpesistun .
Allangughutngitut Jews-etlu Gentile-etlu ; allangughutngitut qepghaghtelaaghetlu qepghaghtelaaghunghilnguutlu ; allangughutngitut yugetlu aghnatlu , qayughllak qamagllusi atunem ayuqusi Christ Jesus-kun .
Christ-am pikngukangisi taawa Abraham-em kingunqiisi . Enkaam elpesillu piliilleqaghsi Kiyaghneghem akequsaa Abraham-emun .
Nagneghutaghllakun whaten , ighneq piliitiyaghqaq atami saghyanganeng qepghaghtelaaghestun kiyaghutkayuguuq mekestaaghhaaluni , qaywa ellngan piksaghngaagu sangwaa tamaghhaan atami pinga .
Mekestaaghhaaluku yuget aflengakegkaqaat , sangwaatlu tamaakut ellngan pikaghqii kenlanga atangan piyaghqaaghhnillghanun .
Whangkutallu tawatesaghtukut . Taghnughhaaluta qepghaghtelaaghuyaghtukut nunam igleghutistengitnun tughneghaghnun .
Iwernga Kiyaghneghem nakmikegkaa aghneq kaasan kayagtekaa Ighneni , allgeqaq aghnakun . Ellngan qaatkegkaqii Liilightuusat
itemunnaluta Liilightuusaneng , avaqutaliitesqellutallu Kiyaghneghmun .
Elpesi avaqutaqutmineng Kiyaghneghem , Ighneghmi Taghneghakek kayagtekaqaak ilumnnun , qevullutek pikak , " Abba , Ata ! "
Enkaam Kiyaghneghqun qepghaghtelaaghunanightuten , avaqutaqaaten . Avaqutaqaaghtutmineng ellmi pini elpenun piliitesleqii .
Sivunghani nalluksaghaghsi Kiyaghneq , enkaam qepghaghtelaaghuyaghtusi kiyaghneghunghilngughnun .
Iwernga maaten liisimakaghsi Kiyaghneq , nalighmeng ipapestaaq Kiyaghneghuuq liisimakistezi . Sangafsingam uteghsugetsi kayaalngughnun sasiinghilngughnun igleghutilghiinun tughneghaghnun ? Sangan tamaakunun qepghaghtelaaghughhneqigsugetsi ?
Paninang qaatkaqasi apeghtughallghit aghneghnun , tanqinun , ayumiqulleghnun aghneghnunllu salqumsivikaqegkangitnun .
Alingutkaqamsi , qamaglluni qepghaatilqa elpesinun sasiinghinnayukan .
Ugpeqaalgutemni , tungsighvikamsi , whangamtun lliighesqeqaghllusi qayughllak whangallu elpesistun lliiqaagunga Gentile-estun . Sivunghani ungipaqitaqngamsi Pinilghiineng Ungipaneng seghletun pimangitaghpesinga . Neqamikaghsi tawani takukaqamsi qayughllak qinuyugulghiinga .
Qaywa qinuyulleghma seghleliightesaghngaaghmisi ukavaghsimangitaghpesinga nalighmeng ighsakumangitaghpesinga . Yeghlegi , upughataghpesinga nikimqun Kiyaghneghem yaqulgatun , nalighmeng Christ Jesus-etun .
Naagu quyangalqesaqesi ? Liisimakamsi piyaqleguyaqata iyesi nusugluki tagivaghnayaghasi .
Enkaam anguyiitestengngaa qayughllak ungipaaskemsi ipapigmeng ?
Tamaakut yuget qaatkutesukangisi Jews-et Liilightuusiitnun , piyukepigtiisi ellmeggnun malighqutaqesqellusi , iwernga apallaat pininghituq . Ellngita aaftesugiisi whangamneng , ellnginaghmeng maligtesqelluteng .
Pinightuq yuget suumqegkumegteki yulguteteng , taawanginaghhaq apalliit piniqata . Quunpeng taana ipanguuq , aviisaghngaaghma .
Taghnughhaghhamni , katam aghnam aqnighqellghatun ighniyulleghmini whangallu tawaten aqnighqutkenneqigtengngwaamsi kenlanga Christ-atun lliilleghqaghpesinun .
Whaatuq maaten elpesinilnguunga enkaam liisimaknayalghiinga naten aleghqughyaghqaalusi . Sumeghyalitkeghllawaamsi .
Elpesi atuqiyulghiini Jews-et Liilightuusiitneng , talwa liigikigatasi Liilightuusat sameng pisiitangi .
Igaqngaaq Akuzitni Igaqegkani Abraham-nguq maalghugegneng ighnelguuq , aallgha qepghaghtelaaghqun aghnakun , ilanga qepghatelaaghunghilngughqun aghnakun .
Ighnegha qepghaghtelaaghqun allgeqaaguq yugestun kitutun alngunak . Iwernga ilanga ighneghan qepghaghtelaaghunghilngughqun allgeqaaguq qayughllak Kiyaghneghem akequsaqegkanga .
Taakuk aghnak usputaaguk maalghugegnun akequsagkenun Kiyaghneghem . Qepghaghtelaaq Hagar akequsaatun Kiyaghneghem ayuquq Mount Sinai-mi enkaam allgeqaagut qepghaghtelaaghqaaluteng .
Hagar Mount Sinai-nguluni ayuquq , Arabia-melnguq . Aghneghmimllu Jerusalem-ngatun ayuquq , qayughllak avaqutaqullghiit qepghaghtelaaghuut Liilightuusanun .
Iwernga paamna Jerusalem qepghaghtelaaghituq , ellnga naakaghput .
Akuzitet Igaqegkat pikaagut , " Quyaghllagi , elpek qumingigalnguuten , aqnighqigalnguuten ighniyulleghmeng . Ugigpek uniteghngaaten , araa quyaghllagem angtalanganeng qayughllak taghnughhaghtaaghasaghqaaguten aghnameng ugilegmeng . "
Ugpeqaalgutemni , Isaac-etun ayuqusi qayughllak avaqutaqiisi Kiyaghneghem apalluqluku akequsani Abraham-emun .
Tamaani aghneghni taana ighneq allgeqaq yugestun kitutun alngunak amyuqetaatkegkaqaa ighneq allgeqaq Taghnegham pillghakun . Paninang maaten tawatetuq .
Iwernga Akuzitet Igaqegkat sameng piitgu ? " Qepghaghtelaaq aghnaq , ighneghallu aghulaqestekek . Qayughllak qepghaghtelaaghem aghnam ighnegha nengighnaanghituq atami saghyanganeng maligulluni ighneghanun qepghaghtelaaghunghilnguum aghnam . "
Ugpeqaalgutemni , whangkuta avaqutaqenghitiinkut qepghaghtelaaghem aghnam , iwernga avaqutaqiinkut qepghaghtelaaghunghilnguum aghnam .
Christ-am whangkuta itemutkaqutanganeng , itemepiigumaakut . Enkaangam nekevghatek aghuliilkaalusi , qepghaghtelaaghughhneqigtegpenasi Liilightuusanun .
Nagatek ! Whanga , Paul , ungipaatamsi : circumcise-estekufsi Liilightuusam pisqellghatun , taawa Christ-am apeghiiqaa kayutkennaanghitaghsi .
Alla kelengasaaghaqa tamaghhaan yuuk , circumcise-estekumi taawa qaatkengngwaaghyaghqaqii qamaglluki Liilightuusat .
Liilightuusatgun nallghusaghtesnaqutkegkufsi Kiyaghneghem elqughutngallghanun , aaflequsi elpesineng Christ-ameng , unilleqaghsillu Kiyaghneghem nangllegtallgha .
Agleghnalghiignekun Taghneghagnekun utaqangwaaghput sighimalleghput apeghiighesqelluku . Sighimalleghput taananguuq : Kiyaghneghmun nallghusiisqelluta elqughutngallghanun ugpeqellemteggun Christ-a .
Christ Jesus-em pikngukanginkut , yuuk megnunanghituq circumcise-ekaakumi nalighmeng circumcise-ellghilkumi . Una esgha megnunalghii , ugpeqilleq Christ-akun piniqistilghii yulgutemnneng .
Sivunghani pinitungwaaq pinguyaghtusi . Kitum qaatkunnanightestisi ipapighqelleghmun ?
Kiyaghneghem tuqlughistegpesi pilqenghitaa .
Neqamikluku , " Yeast-angiighhaam ghhuughtesteghllagaqaa akuutaq . "
Elpesillu whangallu pikutanganeng Atanghem , nalluneqsukenghitanka ugpeqnanifqiita apeghtuusanka elpesinun pisqelluki . Liisimakaqallu Kiyaghneghem aghyuughlleqaa seghleliighqilghii elpesineng , kinanguyaghngaan .
Ugpeqaalgutemni , ungipaqingigatunga yuget circumcise-esqelluki . Tawaten ungipaqinguyaquma Jews-et amyuqetaatkennanighnayaghaatnga enkaam qaquuraa Christ-am sugagniighutkennayanghitaat .
Tamaakut seghleliighqilghiit elpesineng circumcise-elleghmeng , ellngistuq circumcise-estengnguluteng eunuch-englallghiit ellmeggneng .
Ugpeqaalgutemni , Kiyaghneghem tagsiqaqiisi itemngalleghmun Christ-akun . Taawanginaq atuqegpenaan itemngalleghsi atughyaghqaaluki seghleghqengngalghiit piyukellghi yugusim . Itupill qepghaateki ilasi piniqelleghpesigun .
Qayughllak qaatkelleqasi qamaglluki Liilightuusat qaatkegkufsigu una Liilightuusaq : " Piniqluku yulguten piniqelleghpetun elpeneng katam . "
Iwernga elpesineng qaniqunnaqngukufsillu pillugunnaqngukufsillu ugighsalghiistun teghikusastun , kelengatek , qayughllak naafqutunnaqusi .
Whaten piimsi , kiyaghtek qaatkellukek Agleghnalghiik Taghneghak . Tawaten pikufsi atuqnaanghitasi seghleghqengngalghiit piyukellghi yugusim .
Qayughllak seghleghqengngalghiit piyukellghi yugusim kipullegngaat Taghneghagnun , piyukellghi Taghnegham kipullegngaat piyukellghanun yugusim . Taakuk anguyakutuk enkaam atuqnaanghitasi piyukellesi .
Taghnegham maghyaghquungukangisi taawa Liilightuusat atuqsaghqaananighasi .
Yugusim seghleghqelleghtuqam piyukellghi nalluniitut . Ukunguut : alngunaseghaq , seghletun atuqutelleq , nuqesigalnguut alngunak atuqimun ,
maniiguutelleq kiyaghnengllaqanun , uyviiniqelleq , anguyiqelleq , pillugutelleq , qungyaqilleq , sakritelleq , ellnginaayugtelleq , aafqemeraalleq , qerngughpagtaatelleq ,
aqinalleq , suumelleq , qerngughulluteng aghsaghpaagtaqut seghletun pilleghmun , ilanganengllu seghleghqelleghneng . Kelengasaaghnaqlaataghamsi sivunghani pillemtun , tamaakut tawaten kiyaghlleghhiit ilatnganaanghitut quyasleghaneng Kiyaghneghem Ataneghpagullghan .
Naqamenraq Agleghnalghiim Taghnegham piitestekii ukunguut : piniqelleq , quyamalleq , nekeggmelleq , nuqenneghtulleq , nangllegtalleq , pinilleq , ataasiighmetelleq ,
yakumangingitelleq , nuqetelleqlu . Taakut iinghutellghitut alngunak liilightuusani .
Christ Jesus-em pingita qaquuraatkaqiit seghleghqengngalghiit piyukellghit yugusimeng .
Kiyaghtengngukumta Taghneghagnekun , qaatkeltekek Taghneghak .
Qukaayugneghufqaamta , qinuyugtifqaamta , aqinakutefqaamta .
Ugpeqaalgutemni , kina seghleghqellghem kaatfallugtekagu , elpesi kiyaghlleghhiini Taghneghagnekun , pinitungwaaq yakuqluku kayusiiteggu maligunneqigtesqelluku Ataneghmun . Elpesillu , kelengangwaaghlusi luuraq nanghiiqullengnayukafsi .
Kayutkutullusi seghleliilleghpesini ; tawaten qaatkelleqaghsi Liilightuusaq Christ-am qelghutkaa .
Kina sumeghtaghaqumi sanguniluni , sangunghiteghngaaghmi , ellmineng puughtengnguuq .
Yeqay tamaghhaghmi yugem yuvghiighwaaghligu kiyaghtaalleni . Enkaam piniqan quyaknakanga ellmi katam apeghiiqani usputaqellngunaan kitum apeghiiqaanun .
Tamaghhaghmi yugem igleghusaghqaqii ellmi piyaghqani .
Kina alngunak apeghtuqaq Kiyaghneghem apeghtuusaaneng , pinilghiimeng tuunili apeghtughisteminun .
Sumeghtaghaquvek puughlleqniluku Kiyaghneq elpeneng puughtengnguuten . Yugem sangwaa piitesiighaqani unataghyaghqaqaa .
Piitesighaquvek efqughhnaluku seghleghqengngalghii piyukellghen , taagken unataghlleqan tuqulleq . Iwernga piitesighaquvek efqughhnalukek Taghneghak , taagken Taghneghagneng unataghlleqan kenlengilnguq unguvalleq .
Enkaam qinuyagutegpenaan pinitun pilleq pilteggu , qayughllak iilqayunghilkumta pilleghqaq kaaskan akileghtuusangellequkut .
Enkaam pilleghqalgunemta iiwleng pinitun piiqelteki qamagtengngwaaghluki yuget , kiyang tamaakut angleguteliitkaput Christ-akun .
Esghaqaghtekiqun yaagtughllaget igallghenka latamalusi !
Yuget esghaghsaqsuneghtuqatlu qanatkiyuneghtuqatlu pinitun qepghalleghmeggneng , ellnginguut circumcise-esquughwaaghilghiit elpesineng . Tawaten piiqut qayughllak alingaqelghiit amyuqetaatkellengnayukameng ungipaqegkumegteggu qaquuraghhiinaa Christ-am , avelghaghluku circumcise-elleq .
Qaywa circumcise-ekaayaghngaaghmeng , ellngit katam qaatkusigatut Liilightuusanun . Circumcise-esqesugaqiisi qanatkepigesnaghnalusi ellmeggnun circumcise-estekaqnilusi .
Iwernga whanga qananaanghitunga sameng alngunak iwerngaqun qaquuraaneng Atanemta Jesus Christ-am . Tuqullghakun qaquurami nuna qaquuraamaaq whangamnun , enkaam whanga qaquuraamaanga nunamun .
Megnunanghituq yuuk circumcise-ekaakumi , nalighmeng circumcise-ellghilkumi . Una megnunalghiinguuq : Kiyaghneghem ulimakaqiinkut nutaghaaluta yugni .
Tamaghhiitnun qaatkullghiinun apeghtuusamnun , yeqay Kiyaghneghem nekeggmellghallu nangllegtallghallu ellngitnilli , Israel-nganillu Kiyaghneghem .
Whaken kenlekluku kitum alngunak alla seghleliightestefqaama pilinga qayughllak yugusimnilnguut maamellghet kelgutngwaat qephaghtelaaghulqa Jesus-mun .
Ugpeqaalgutemni , yeqay piniqingalghii kayusillgha Atanemta Jesus Christ-am tamaghhaghpesinilli . Amen .
Ukut latat Paul-meng pinguut . Christ Jesus-em apostle-kaanga Kiyaghneghem piyukellghakun . Latanguunga Kiyaghneghem yugitnun Ephesus-melngughnun , ataasiighmelnguut maligsaaghtengi Christ Jesus-em .
Kiyaghneghem Atamta , Atanemtallu Jesus Christ-am nanglleklisillu nekeggmellelguslisillu .
Usuqellengli Kiyaghneq , Atanga Atanemta Jesus Christ-am ! Christ-akun Kiyaghneghem quyastengngwiinkut tamaghhaaneng tunusameng qilagtameng .
Nuna ulimallghilluku Kiyaghneghem nakmikegkaqiinkut Christ-akun pelungitesqellutallu avutngitesqellutallu ellminun .
Qayughllak Kiyaghneghem piniqegkanginkut , neghighluku allughqinakegkaqiinkut avaqutaaluta Jesus Christ-akun . Tawaten pikaaguq qayughllak piyukegkanga , efquqegkangallu .
Enkaam usuqaghput Kiyaghneq qayughllak ighlegpenani nangllekeghllagiinkut piniqegkamikun Ighneghmikun .
Christ-am aawakun , Kiyaghneghem itemutkaqiinkut seghleghqellemnneng . Seghevutii seghleghqelleput apalluqluku nangllegtalleghllani
aqeghqusiqeghllakanga whangkunnun . Peghqinghustiinkutlu liigikestiinkutlu
uspeqelleghmineng salin aliighsigalkemmineng sivunghani . Taananguuq Kiyaghneghem uspeqegkaa , pikaqaa Christ-akun .
Kiyaghneghem uspeqelleni apeghiighlleqaa pilleghqaghllugwaaghmi . Qamagtengngwaaghluki ulimaani qilagmelnguutlu nunamelnguutlu qerngughlleqii , Christ-amun igleghutesqelluki .
Christ-akun Kiyaghneghem nakmikegkaqiinkut ellminun yuguluta . Ayumirugllak piyukelleghmitun uspeqegkaqaa . Ellngan sangwaa tamaghhaan piyukelleghmitun pistaqaa .
Whangkuta Jews-eni ugpeqani sighimakiyuwhaaqaagukut Christ-akun . Enkaam kiyaghtaallemteggun usuqesleqaghput Kiyaghneq aangelleghllaganun .
Christ-akun elpesillu nagaquqaqaghsi ipapik ungipaq . Pinilghiinguuq Ungipaq ungipaatilghii yugulilleghpesineng . Ugpeqaqngafsigu Christ-a , Kiyaghneghem nalluniiqaqiisi Agleghnalghiigneng Taghneghagneng , akequsaqegkamineng tuunelleqnilukek .
Agleghnalghiim Taghnegham ipapighqestiinkut pagitaghqamnneng kenlanga whangkuta piliitelleghqamnnun . Enkaam usuqelleqaghput Kiyaghneq aangelleghllaganun !
Nagaquumaaqa ugpeqilleghsi Ataneghqun Jesus-kun , piniqelleghsillu tamaghhiitnun Kiyaghneghem yugitnun . Tamaaken apalluqluku ,
neqamikaqamsi yughanemni , iyamsiqayagunneghmeng taaqigatamsi Kiyaghneghmun .
Ataghllakaa Atanemta Jesus Christ-am . Ellnganun tungsiitaqamsi peghqinghusqellusi Taghneghagkenkun , liigikataghiisqellusi Kiyaghneghmeng .
Yughaatkaqa nighuk kuukgutesqelluku ilugpesinun , liigikesqelluku sighimalleq Kiyaghneghem elpesinun pikestekaa qayughllak nakmikegkaqiisi . Yughaatkamsillu liigikesqelluki kemnaghllaget quyastelleghllaget Kiyaghneghem akequsaqegkii yugminun .
Yughaghtungallu liigikesqelluku seghleghllaguuq Kiyaghneghem aghtughyaghqaanghilleghllaga qepghalghii whangkunni ugpeqilghiini . Taana aghtughyaghqaanghitelleghllak ataasiiguq Kiyaghneghem unguvaghtisiqegkaa Christ-amun tuqulleghmeng . Taagken qilagmi Kiyaghneghem aqumesimaa aghenqigneghmikun .
Kiyaghneghem qulighpigaaghtestekaqaa Christ-a tamaghhiitneng igleghutisteneng , qelghikayugneng , aghtughyaghqaanghillelegneng , umiilegnengllu . Aatgha ingyaatngaghllagtuq ateghyaggaghneng nunami whani , nunaghraghaghqamillu .
Kiyaghneghem llikaqaa sangwaa qamagtengngwaaghluku Christ-am itegaan asinganun , naasquutistengllaqaqaallu samun tamaghhaanun apalluqluki ugpeqat .
Qamaglluteng ugpeqat yugusiqii Christ-am , enkaam ellnga iighwightuq . Christ-am iighwightaa sangwaa qamaglluku nani alngunak .
Sivunghani taghneghasi tuqungayaghtut qayughllak qaatkumangilkesi Kiyaghneq , seghleghqestenguyaghtusillu .
Tawatesaghtusi kiyaghtengngulusi nunam seghleghmun igleghneghanun . Qaatkengnguyaghaghsillu igleghutistengat tughneghaat qilagamelnguut . Ellnganguuq aangwaalleghpigaq tughneghaq igleghutilghii yugneng qaatkusigalngughneng Kiyaghneghmun .
Qamaglluta kiyaghtekaagukut tamaakustun yugestun . Atuqegkaqaput seghleghqengngalghiit piyukellghi yugusimtallu umyugamtallu . Enkaam qamaglluta allgeqaatemnneng seghleghqestenguluta , aghyuullengnaqnguyaghtukut Kiyaghneghem sakraallghakun .
Iwernga Kiyaghneq nangllegtaghllagtuq , piniqepigtiinkutlu .
Qaywa taghneghaput tuqungayaghngiita apalluqluki seghleghqelleput , Kiyaghneghem unguvaghtiinkut maligulluta Christ-amun . ( Yugulikaagusi Kiyaghneghem nangllekellghakun . )
Kiyaghneghem unguvaghtiinkut maligulluta Christ Jesus-mun , whangkunnunllu aqumelgusightestaa qilagmi .
Kiyaghneq tawaten pikaaguq kinguliighaghnun liitesqelluku piniqelleghrukutaaghllani whangkunnun Christ Jesus-kun .
Kiyaghneghem nangllegtallghakun yugulikaagusi ugpeqilleghpesigun . Yugulilleghsi elpesineng pilqenghitaghsi , Kiyaghneghem tunusaqaa elpesinun .
Yugulillghitiisi apalluqluku salleghsi , enkaam qukaayugutkesaghqaqenghitaghsi .
Kiyaghneghem ulimaaqiinkut tawatelluta . Christ Jesus-kun ulimaaqiinkut qepghiisqelluki pinilghiit qepghaqat . Sivunghani taakut pinilghiit qepghaqat yataaghqengngwaaqaqii whangkunnun qepghiisqelluki kiyaghtellemnni .
Neqamikluku Gentile-ngulusi allgeqaagusi . Jews-et atighaqiisi " circumcise-ellghilnguut " , ellmeggneng atiqayuguut " circumcise-ekat " . ( Circumcise-ellghat yugusighhiiniitnituq . )
Neqamikluku tamaani pilleghni nalluksaghaghsi Christ-a kinangutanga . Nunataayaghtusi Israel-eghmiinun enkaam ilatellghisaghtusi Kiyaghneghem akequsaqegkaanun ellngitnun . Nunami whani kiyaghtengnguyaghtusi sighimallngunasillu Kiyaghnengunasillu .
Iwernga maaten pilleghmi Christ Jesus-mun ilasimaasi . Sivunghani awavansaghtusi Kiyaghneghmeng , iwernga maaten pilleghmi tughaaghusimaasi ellnganun Christ-am aawakun .
Christ-a ellnga katam nekeggmelqaghput . Ellnganguuq ataasiightestilghii Jews-enengllu Gentile-enengllu . Naafqegkaqaa minglluta aaftilghii whangkunneng , enkaam anguyakunnanighqegkaqiinkut .
Christ-am tuqulleghmikun atuunanighqegkaqii Jews-et Liilightuusiitlu qelghusiitlu . Tawaten pikaaguq Jews-etlu Gentile-etlu ataasiightesqelluki ellmikun . Enkaam nekeggmellengestekaqii .
Tuqulleghmikun qaquurakun , Christ-am ugumikunnanighqii Jews-etlu Gentile-etlu . Taagken ataasiightestii , ilaliighutestiillu Kiyaghneghmun .
Christ-a tagiluni ungipaqikaaguq nekeggmelleghmeng elpesinun Gentile-enun , awavantengnguyalghiisi Kiyaghneghmun . Ungipaqikaaguqlu nekeggmelleghmeng Jews-enun , qantaghantengngulghiit Kiyaghneghmun .
Enkaam Christ-akun Jews-enillu Gentile-enillu tagiyaqlegughtukut Atamun ataasikun Taghneghakun .
Enkaangam elpesi Gentile-eni nunataananightusi . Itupill nunalgutkaaghtiisi Kiyaghneghem yugita , ilatusillu nengllugutanganun Kiyaghneghem .
Mangteghaatun ayuqusi nekeftekat tunemangllaqiitgun apostle-etlu uuknaliqistetlu . Christ Jesus ellnga katam kangigham uyghakaa .
Qamaglluteng mangtegham nalighneghi nekeghquutngaat qerngaghmeng Christ-akun . Taakut nalighneghet nulayalghiimeng temple-ngughtengnguut Ataneghmun . Taana temple-a agleghnaghtuq .
Ilatngalleghpesigun Christ-amun , maligullusi ilangitnun ugpeqanun nekeftengnguusi mangteghamun Kiyaghneghem kiyaghfiganun Taghneghagmikun .
Tamaaken apalluqluku , whanga , Paul , anusimingllaghvigmetunga qayughllak qepghaaskegka Christ Jesus elpesi apalluqlusi Gentile-eni .
Entaqun nagaquumaaghsi Kiyaghneghem nangllegtalleghmikun qepghaqalitkaqaanga elpesinun .
Kiyaghneghem liitestaa whangamnun qayvightellghilnguq uspeqelleni . Qavnganghhaq latatkaghtekaqaqa taana .
Atightuqufsigu latatkegkaqa liilleqaghsi liigikelqa qayvightellghilnguq uspeqelleq Christ-ameng ayuqelghii .
Sivunghani Kiyaghneghem ungipaatellghitii yuget qayvightellghilngughmeng uspeqelleghmineng . Iwernga ukuni aghneghni Agleghnalghiignekun Taghneghagnekun qayvightaa uspeqelleni agleghnalghiinun apostle-minunllu uuknaliqisteminunllu .
Whatetuq uspeqellgha : Gentile-et ugpeqilleghmegteggun Pinilghiineng Ungipaneng ilasimaat Jews-enun Kiyaghneghem quyastellghanun . Nalighneqaaghsimii ataasim yugusim , enkaam ilatut Kiyaghneghem akequsaanun Christ Jesus-kun .
Kiyaghneghem nangllegtalleghmikun , aghtughyaghqaanghilleghmikunllu tunusalitaanga qepghaghtengulunga ungipaqesqelluki Pinilghiit Ungipat .
Ukalighpigaagunga tamaghhiitneng Kiyaghneghem yuganeng . Tawalliima Kiyaghneghem nangllegtalleghmikun tunusalitaanga whaten : nakmikaanga Gentile-enun ungipaqesqelluki Pinilghiit Ungipat Christ-am aklunginganeng ayuqelghiit . Aklungingi ingyaatngaat yuget liigikellghitneng .
Kiyaghneghem nakmikegkaqaangallu liigikestesqelluki qamaglluki yuget qayvighsimangilngughmeng uspeqelleghmineng . Kiyaghneghem , ulimaghikam sameng tamaghhaaneng , qayvightellghitaa uspeqelleni piinlighyuggaalleghmeng maatemun .
Taagken qilagnilnguut : igleghutilghiitlu , aghtughyaghqaanghillelgetlu , Kiyaghneghem liitesleqii allaaghhiinaghmeng peghqinelleghmineng . Tawaten pillequq yugmikun yughaghvignilngughteggun .
Tamaakunguut Kiyaghneghem uspeqegkii salin nunangllalghilluni . Apeghiighumii Christ Jesus-kun Atanemteggun .
Ugpeqillemteggun Christ-akun aglaghyaghqaaghsimaakut Kiyaghneghmun tetullngunaamtallu alingellngunaamtallu .
Enkaangam iilqayagutegpenaan ugpeqilleghsi apalluqluku ikfiqutkengngukemsi . Ikfiqelleghma quulvaghtesleqiisi .
Enkaam taana apalluqluku segesqughtunga sivungani Atam .
Ellnganguuq atighilghii tamaghhiitneng nengllugutneng qilagmelngughnengllu nunamelngughnengllu .
Yughaghtunga Kiyaghneghmun aklungighllaganeng aghtughyaghqaanghillelitesqellusi iknaqughsiisqeluki ilusi qaamkut Taghneghagkenkun .
Yughaatkamsi Christ-a kiyaghtesqelluku ilugpesini ugpeqilleghpesigun . Yughaatkamsi akulgusqellusillu , tunemalgusqellusillu piniqelleghqun .
Yughaatkamsi , qamagllukillu Kiyaghneghem yugi , liigiksaqlegusqelluku Christ-am piniqellghan , iqetulanga , tagtalanga , uusqaghtulanga , samavneghtulangallu .
Elpesinun liisimakesqesugaqa Christ-am piniqellgha , qaywa piyaqnaghngaan liigikngwaalleghqaa . Taagken piniqellghakun , Kiyaghneghem nangaghneghatun wata lliighllequsi .
Kiyaghneghem aghtughyaghqaanghillghakun qepghalghiikun ilumnni , ellngan piyaqlegwaa qaayghulluku sangwaa alngunak aaptekaghput nalighmeng sumeghtaghaatkegkaghput .
Kiyaghneq usuqellengli ugpeqatgun yughaghvignilngughteggun , Christ Jesus-kunllu . Usuqiteggu quunperugllak kenlengunaan . Amen .
Anusimingllaghaagunga qayughllak qepghaaskegka Ataneq . Kiyaghneghem nakmikegkaqiisi ellminun yugulusi ; tamaaken apalluqluku kayemamsi kiyaghtesqellusi Kiyaghneghem kiyaghtesqesullghatun .
Iiwleng qusevegllusi , yakumangilliqegpenasi , nuqenneghtulusi , tugukliitullusi piniqelleghqun .
Kiyaghneghem Taghneghagkenka qerngughutkaqiisi nekeggmelleghqun . Enkaam nanghiiqughllagtek iiwleng kiyaghtek tawaten .
Ataasiiguq yugusiq , ataasiiguklu Taghneghak , katam tawaten ataasimun sighimalleghmun Kiyaghneghem tagsighiisi .
Ataasiiguq Ataneq , ataasiiguq ugpeqilleq , ataasiiguq paaptaayelleq .
Ataasiiguq Kiyaghneq , Atakaat saam tamaghhaan . Ellngan igleghutngwaa sangwaa tamaghhaan , tamaghhaanituq , sametuqlu alngunak .
Christ-am tamaghhaamta tuunegkaqiinkut tunusameng qepghaqani pisqelluku . Tuunegkaqii taakut tunusat tuunyukelleghmitun .
Tamaaken apalluqluku Akuzitni Igaqegkani igaqegkaalghii , " Mayughaqngami uusqalleghmun tugukaqii uglaapiglleghhiit wayaqat , yugetlu tunusaliquqaqii . "
Sameng pisiiwa , " Mayuqaaguq " ? Whaten pisiiguq , sivukluni ukikaaguq samavek asilighneghanun nunam .
Enkaam ellnga taana ukikaq samavek , ellnganguuq ataasiq taana mayuqaq pamavek ingyaghluki qilaget , imighnaluku sangwaa qamaglluku nayuutngalleghmineng .
Ellnganguuq tunusaliquqaq yugnun : ilangi apostle-nguluki , ilangi uuknaliqistenguluki , ilangi evangelist-nguluki , ilangi yughaghtenguluki , apeghtughistengulukillu .
Taakut tunusalitkaqii apeghtiisqelluki Kiyaghneghem yugi ellngitnun qepghaatesqelluku ellnga . Kiyaghneq tawaten pikaaguq ellngitnun nekeftesqelluku Christ-am yugusii .
Taana qepghaqaq nagneghllequq kenlanga ataasiightellemnnun ugpeqillemteggun , liisimakellemteggunllu Ighnegha Kiyaghneghem . Taagken angtaniitngwaaghluta Christ-atun lliighllequkut .
Enkaam taghnughhaghhaananighllequkut . Tamaaken apalluqluku puughtesnaanghitukut yugnun temngimeng apeghtughillghitgun . Apeghtughillghit anuqestunllu imaghllugestunllu ayuqut nuugtaatalghiit yugneng . Tamaakut peghqinelghiit , iqlengalghiit yuget , iqlengateng ipasugnighsaghaqiit maghyaghquneghlluggnaluki yuget .
Itupill akuzitkelteggu ipapilleq piniqelleghqun , enkaam wata Christ-atun lliighllequkut sallemteggun tamaghhaakun . Christ-a naasquqaat ugpeqat .
Ugpeqani yugusiqiinkut Christ-am . Ellngakun iingunaghmi yugusiq qerngughutkaaguqlu nuverraatkaaguqlu yugusim ivalungakun . Qamaglluteng nalighneghet qepghanneghmeggni qepghalleghqamegestun , taawa yugusiq nagwaaquq , iknaqughsaghaquqlu piniqelleghqun .
Enkaangam Atanghem aatghakun whaten piimsillu kelengasaaghamsillu : kiyaghtegpenasingam Gentile-et kiyaghtaallghistun . Sumeghtaghallghit sasiinghilnguugut ,
umyugiitlu liigikingigalnguugut . Ilatnganghitut unguvalleghmun Kiyaghneghem tuunegkaanun , qayughllak nallukngwaaghaat , pineghlluguutlu .
Talwa kaynguyugyaghqaananiimaat ; atuqaqiitlu sangwaat alngunak seghleghet yugusimeng piyukegkiit . Nagneghusugaqiit qamaglluki seghleghet nuqetutegpenaki .
Iwernga tamaakut liitellghitasi Christ-am apeghtuusiitneng !
Nagaqupestaaqaqaghsi ellnga , qayughllak maligsaaghtekegkangisi . Enkaam apeghtuqaagusi ipa apeghtuusaaneng Jesus-em .
Whaten apeghtuqaqiisi : seghleghet piyukelleghpesi puughlleqiisillu naafqelleqiisillu . Tamaaken apalluqluku pegteki nangaghnelusillu kiyaghtaalqesaqesillu .
Itupill taghnegham nutaghlliki umyugasi .
Enkaam atuqiteggu nangaghneghraghaghsi qayughllak Kiyaghneghem ulimakaqaa ellmitun ayuqluku : elqughutngapiigluku , agleghnaghlukullu .
Enkaam iqlengiqnanightegngam ! Itupill iiwleng apeghteggu ipapilleq ilagpesinun , qayughllak qamaglluta nalighnequghiinkut Christ-am yugusiin .
Sakritek iwernga seghleghqegpenasi . Siqineq tevightestegpenaan paninang sakritngulusi .
Talwa tughneghaq pilleghqalitegpenaan nanghiiqusqellusi seghleghqelleghmun .
Tegleghniighta teglegnanighli . Itupill qepghaghli allgeghusaghqaaluni aklukegkamineng , tuuniyaghqaaghllequqlu aklukilghiinun .
Akuzitkigpenasi seghleghmeng . Itupill aleghqughteki pinitun yuget aklukillghitni . Pinilghiit akuzitet kayemyaghqaqiit , aneghneghqesaghqaqiit nagallghiit .
Qivghustegpenakeklu Agleghnalghiik Taghneghakek Kiyaghneghem . Taghneghagmineng nalluniiqaqiisi ellmi piknalusi . Tawaten pikaaguq elpesinun liisimakesqelluku itemulleqiisi seghleghqelleghpesineng Itemutellghem Aghnegha kaaskan .
Pegteggu ugumikeraaq , sakraa , sakraaghllak , yupighqaghaataq , seghlequuq , qamagllukillu seghleghet .
Yeghlegi nangllegtaghtek , nafughtaghtek ilagpesinun , seghevutullusillu , katam Kiyaghneghem seghevutkaqegkangisi Christ-akun .
Kiyaghneghem elpesi avaqutaqutanganeng piniqepigtekii , ayuqesighaghteggu .
Kiyaghtaallesi aaghqutaqesteki piniqelleghmun , katam Christ-am piniqegkanginkut , tuqumatkegkaqegkanginkutlu . Tuqullgha tepkegtatun tunusatun ayuquq Kiyaghneghmun , aghqutnguuqlu ellnganun .
Elpesi Kiyaghneghem yukegkangisi , enkaam kitumun alngunak allaniightestengunifqaafsi , nalighmeng alngunak sex-kun seghleghqestengunifqaafsi , nalighmeng pakigniightengunifqaafsi . Tamaakut seghleghuut enkaam Kiyaghneghem yugita piyaghqaqenghitiit .
Kayngusaghaategpenasi , temngitwhameng akuzitkegpenasi sex-meng , nalighmeng amyughaaghutkegpenasi sex-meng . Itupill iyamsiqayugviksaghqaqaghsi Kiyaghneq .
Nalluneqnaghhiituq una : Kina alngunak pagisaghqiituq Ataneghpagullghani Christ-amllu Kiyaghneghemllu seghleghqelghii allaniighmeng , alngunak sex-kun seghleghqelleghmeng , nalighmeng pakigniighmeng . ( Pakigneghet manigughtenguut kiyaghnengllaqanun . )
Yugnun puughtestegpenasi ungipaaskangisi tamaakut seghleghqellghet seghleghunghinniluki . Iwernga tawatelnguut seghleghqellghet Kiyaghneq sakraasteghllagaqaat qaatkunneghilnguut ellminun .
Tamaaken apalluqluku ilategpenasi tawatelngughnun yugnun .
Yugestun ayuqsaghtusi kiyaghlleghhiit mamlegmi , iwernga maaten kiyaghtengnguusi nighugmi qayughllak Atanghem pikegkangisi . Enkaam kiyaghtek yugestun nighugmelngughestun .
( Qayughllak kiyaghhneghpesini nighugmi pinightestaqiisi , elqughutngastaqiisi , ipangustaqiisi . )
Liinnaqiteggullu sangwaa efqughnalghii Ataneghmun .
Ilatqaghtaghpenasi yugnun satngunghilngughmeng pilghiinun mamlegmi . Itupill liigikesteki tawaten pillghit seghleghuut .
Kayngunapigtut talwa akuzitkesaghqaaluteng tamaakut piiqegkangit aksaqluku .
Iwernga qamagtengngwaaghluteng aliightekumeng nighugmun , taawa nateteghpigaatangi whateghlluwaaq aliighllequt , qayughllak sangwaa qamaglluni nighugem esghaghyaghqaaghtesleqaa .
Tamaaken apalluqluku yuget pikaagut , " Qavalghiimi , taghtughhaaten . Unguvaa tuqulleghmeng enkaam Christ-am kukeglleqaaten . "
Enkaam kelengalusi kiyaghtek . Peghqinghunghilngughestun kiyaghtegpenasi ; itupill peghqinghestun kiyaghtek .
Pinitun atuqiteggu tamaghhaan pilleghqaghsi qayughllak aghneghni maaten yuget seghletun piiqut .
Tamaaken apalluqluku nallufqaafsi , iwernga liigikiteggu sangwaa Atanghem pisqesullgha elpesinun .
Suumegpenasi wine-meng qayughllak naafqelleqiisi . Iwernga imightek Taghneghagneng ,
aleghquutaqlusi akuzitangitneng psalms-et , ilagaatet , taghneghakunllu ilagaatneng . Ilagaghaqitek ilagaatnengllu psalms-enengllu Ataneghmun , usuqillelighlusi ilugpesigun .
Aatghakun Atanemta Jesus Christ-am , iyamsiqayugvikumanginaghteggu Kiyaghneq Atanga saam tamaghhaan .
Malighqutaqngalusi ilagpesinun qayughllak siivakngukesi Christ-a .
Nuliighni , malighqutaqlusi ugigpesinun katam Ataneghmun pilghiistun .
Qayughllak ugi naasquqaa nulighhan katam Christ-a naasquqegkangat ugpeqat . Christ-a Yugulighistekaat ugpeqat ; ellngan yugusiqii .
Katam ugpeqat malighqutaqellghistun Christ-amun , tawateghpigaq salleghqun tamaghhaakun nulighhet malighqutaqsaghqaagut ugimeggnun .
Ugini , piniqluki nuliisi katam Christ-am piniqellghatun ugpeqat . Piniqepigtekaqii repall tuqumatkegkaqii .
Ugpeqat agleghnaghsaqaqii aghtughyaghqaanghillghakun akuzitmi , pelungighsaqaqiillu aghvigluki meghqun .
Christ-a tawaten pikaaguq aang始ghunnaluki ugpeqat ellminun katam pinighnalghiitun ugiighnaqelghiitun . Tuqukaaguq ugpeqat tagneqriitesqelluki , ungllevregiitesqelluki nalighmeng sameng alngunak afkuyiitesqelluki . Enkaam nuliighqaa agleghnaghllequq , avutngillequqlu .
Ugim piniqsaghqaqaa nuliini piniqelleghmitun yugusini . Ugi piniqilghii nuliighmineng ellmineng piniqnguuq .
Kitum alngunak ugumikigataa ellmi katam yugusini . Yeghlegi , neghestaqaallu aflengakaqaallu , katam tawaten Christ-am piiqellghatun ugpeqanun ,
qayughllak nalighnequghiinkut ellngan yugusiin .
Akuzitni Igaqegkani whaten igaqngaaq , " Tamaaken apalluqluku yugem unilleqaak atanillu naanillu ilannaluni nuliighminun . Enkaam nulighqullghiik ataasiighllequk . "
Taam Akuzitem Igaqegkam qayvightaa megnunapiglleghhii ipapilleq : Christ-allu ugpeqatlu ataasiigut .
Iwernga taana elpesinunllu ayuquq : tamaghhaghmi ugim piniqepestaaghyaghqaqaa nuliini ellmineng katam piniqelghiistun . Tamaghhaghmillu nulighhem siivaksaghqaqaa ugini .
Taghnughhaghni , qaatkullusi angayuqaghpesinun Atanghem pisqesullghatun elpesinun . Tawaten elqughutngaaq .
Akuzitni Igaqegkani whaten Kiyaghneq qelghikaaguq , " Quulvaghluku atanllu naanllu . " Taana qelghusaq sivuliiguq akequsalek .
Whaten Kiyaghneq pikaaguq , " Kiyaghtaallghen itagnaghllequq , taaklukullu kiyaghllequten nunami . "
Angayuqani , sakritestegpenaki taghnughhasi . Yeghlegi anglisteki peghqigsaghlukillu apeghtughaghlukillu Atanghem pisqellghatun .
Qepghaghtelaaghni , alingellelighlusillu ungelegllelighlusillu qaatkiteki piliitistesi nunami whani . Ipapighqellusi qepghaataqiteki , katam Christ-a qepghaatelleghpesistun .
Piliitistesi qaatkiteki qaywa esghapanghiteghngiisi . Qepghaghtek efqughhnaluki piliitistesi katam efqughtelleghpesistun Ataneq . Ilugpesineng atuqiteggu Kiyaghneghem piyukellgha Christ-amun qepghaghtelaaqelghiistun .
Enkaam qepghaghtek sagiqlusi Ataneghmun pilghiistun , nakaan yugnun .
Neqamikluku Atanghem akileghtughyaghqaqii yuget qamaglluki , pinitun pillghitnun . Ataneq tawaten pillequq qepghaghtelaaghnunllu qepghaghtelaaghunghilngughnunllu .
Piliitisteni , pinitun piteki qepghaghtelaasi katam ungipaatellemtun ellngit pinitun pisqellusi . Alingsequgpenaki . Neqamikluku elpesillu qepghaghtelaasillu ataasimeng Atanelguusi qilagmelngughmeng . Ellngan nanqigsaghqaqii yuget qamaglluki taniillngunaki .
Kinguliq apeghyaghqaqa unanguuq , iknaqellengitek Ataneghmeng , aghtughyaghqaanghilleghllaganengllu .
Aatekek iingunaagkenka akulghaaghek Kiyaghneghem yataaghqegkakek elpesinun . Taagken tengvimun nekevghasaghqaaghlleqasi Tughneghaam puughtillghi .
Neqamikluku , pilluwaangunghitaput yuget . Itupill pilluwaangwaaput igleghutilghiit , aghtughyaghqaanghillelget , igleghutilghiit nunam mamleganeng , seghleghetlu tughneghaat qilaganilnguut .
Tamaaken apalluqluku aatekek iingunaagkenka akulghaaghqek Kiyaghneghem yataaghqegkakek elpesinun ! Enkaam seghleliighem aghneghani pilluwaghyaqlegulleqasi anguyagem sughugallghi . Taagken pilluwaneghmeng apeghiiqufsi , elpesi paninang nekevghangullequsi .
Enkaam nekevghamanginaghtek . Ipapilleq tafsiiteggu , elqughutngalleqlu sakimagiitiiteggu .
Pinilghiit Ungipat nekeggmelleghmeng ayuqelghiit , kamiiteki .
Tamaakut saaghwitgun , atuqiteggu ugpeqilleq amiigighaghtaasiiluku qaamsaghqaaluki kumangalghiit aaygungi Tughnegham .
Aateggu yugulilleq naasqughiitaaluku , Taghneghamllu savigpaga , Kiyaghneghem akuzitkaa .
Iiwleng yughaghtek Taghnegham maghyaghquutellghakun . Atuqluki allaaghhiinaat yughallghet , aapniighteklu Kiyaghneghmun . Tamaaken apalluqluku kelengalusi , iilqayugpenasi . Iiwleng yughaatkelluki qamaglluki Kiyaghneghem yugi .
Whangallu yughaatkitengnga Kiyaghneghmun akuzitelitesqellunga . Taagken tetugpenanga apeghlleqaqa sangwaa Kiyaghneghem salin liigikestellghilkanga Pinilghiineng Ungipaneng ayuqelghii .
Kiyaghneghem nakmikegkaqaanga akuzistengulunga ellminun . Enkaam tamaaken apalluqluku anusimingllaghaagunga qiipraghusighlunga . Yughaghtek ungipaqinalunga tetugpenanga katam Kiyaghneghem piyukellghatun .
Liisimakesugamsi natetulemnengllu saaqutemnengllu . Tamaaken apalluqluku kayagsimaaqa Tychicus elpesinun . Piniqegkaghput ugpeqaalgutfut , ataasiighmelnguuguqlu qepghaghtenga Atanghem . Kaaskumi ungipaalleqiisi sameng tamaghhaaneng whangamneng , kayemelleqiisillu .
Kiyaghneghmeng Atameng , Ataneghmengllu Jesus Christ-ameng elpesinun pinguuk nekeggmelleqlu , piniqelleqlu ugpeqillelek .
Nangllegtalleq tamaghhaghpesinun pinguuq piniqilghiini Atanemnneng Jesus Christ-ameng piniqellelighluku naangyaghqaanghilngughmeng .
Ukut latat Paul-mengllu Timothy-mengllu pinguut , qepghaghtekiinkung Christ Jesus-em . Lataaqamsi qamagllusi Kiyaghneghem yugitni , yughaghvigem igleghutistengitni , deacon-enillu Philippi-melngughni , ugpeqilghiit Christ Jesus-kun .
Kiyaghneghem Atamta , Atanemtallu Jesus Christ-am nanglleklisillu nekeggmellelguslisillu .
Iyamsiqayugvikaqaqa Kiyaghneqa elpesineng sumeghtaghaatkennemsi .
Yughaatkennemsi quyapigtaqunga ,
qayughllak neqamikaqa ungipaqilgusiqaqaghpesinga Pinilghiineng Ungipaneng . Kayusiqaqaghpesinga ugpeqiyuggaalleghpesineng Pinilghiineng Ungipaneng whavemun kenlanga .
Liisimakngwaaghaqa Kiyaghneq piinlighikaq pinilghiimeng qepghaqameng ilugpesini , ellngan apeghiighlleqaa Christ Jesus uteghniqan .
Itagnapigtuq whangamni sumeghtaghaatkennemsi tawaten qayughllak ilumnitaqusi . Ungipaqingulungallu ipapighqingulungallu Pinilghiit Ungipat ipanguniluki , maatenllu anusimingllaghvigmellunga , qamagllusi allgeghtengngwaaghsi Kiyaghneghem nangllegtallgha whangamnun maligullusi .
Kiyaghneq liisimakistekaqa esghaghyupigtaqamsi , qayughllak qamagllusi piniqamsi Christ Jesus-em piniqellghatun elpesi .
Yughaatkaqamsi piniqighllagesqellusi , liisimallengataghiisqellusi , liigikellengataghiisqellusillu .
Tawaten lliiqufsi kiyaghtelleghpesini sangwaa pinilleghpigaq nakmikumanginaghyagulleqaghsi . Taagken Christ-a taginqigtekan pelungillequsillu anaggutellghillequsillu .
Enkaam unguvallesi imighllequt ipapestaaq piniipiglleghhiimeng Jesus Christ-anginaghhaam piitestekaaneng . Taagken yuget quulvaghlleqaatlu , usuqelleqaatlu Kiyaghneq .
Ugpeqaalgutemni , elpesinun liisimakesugaqa anusimingllaghvigmetelleghma ipapestaaq uglalghii yuuk nagatestaa Pinilghiineng Ungipaneng .
Tamaaken apalluqluku qamaglluteng umiilgem mangteghaan kelengakistengita liitaat anusimingllaghaagunga qayughllak qepghaghtekegkanganga Christ-am .
Anusimingllaghvigmetelleghma allulluteng ugpeqalghutet ugpeqiighataghaghtestii Ataneghqun . Enkaam wata tetugnanighataghaghtut ungipaqneghmegteggu Christ-a .
Ipanguuq ilangi ungipaqinguut Christ-ameng qayughllak aqinakngukangatngallu aaghtiiraaghukangatngallu . Iwernga ilangi ungipaqinguut Christ-ameng elqughulluteng .
Ungipaqinguut qayughllak piniqegkangatnga . Liisimakegkangat Kiyaghneghem tagistekaqaanga whavek nekevghatesqelluki Pinilghiit Ungipat anguyamnneng .
Iwernga ilangit ungipaqinguut Christ-ameng ellnginaayugtem , ipapighqegpenateng . Sumeghmeggni tawaten pilleghmegteggun seghleliighqataghaghnilunga piitnga anusimingllaghvigmesimalunga .
Itagnaghtuq , ungipaqillghat elqughutngayaghngaan nalighmeng sameng allaneng apallulguyaghngaan , ungipaqillghita quyastaqaanga , qayughllak ungipaqinguut Christ-ameng uglapiglleghiinun .
Aa-a quyangallequnga , qayughllak liisimakaqa aanyaghqaagunga anusimingllaghvigmeng yughaatkelleghpesigun , kayusillghakunllu Jesus Christ-am Taghneghaan .
Piyukelleghllakallu , sighimakelleghllakallu esgha taana , kayngusaghaatefqaama pinalunga Christ-amun . Itupill kiyaghsugaqunga ilutulunga wataqaaghaq maaten anusimingllaghvigmetellemni . Enkaam Christ-a quulvallengellequq unguvaghngaaghma , nalighmeng tuquyaghngaaghma .
Whangamni unguvalleq Christ-anguuq , enkaam tuqulleq allgeghutaghallghuuq .
Iwernga unguvanaqngukuma qepghaghataghaghllequnga Christ-amun . Nalikek nakmikelleghqaqa nallukaqa , unguvalleq nalighmeng tuqulleq .
Kukriqnguunga naligkeneng nakmiilleghqamneng . Aghulaqsupigtaqsaghtunga Christ-amennalunga , qayughllak pinighataghaghyaghqaaguq taana .
Iwernga megnunaghataghaghtuq elpesi apalluqlusi unguvanguunga .
Ipapighqutkumaaqa taana , liisimakaqa wiin unguvanaqnguunga . Elpesininnaqnguunga kayusiinnalusi nagusqellusi , quyamallengesqellusi ugpelleghpesigun .
Elpesinun pikuma , usuqataghaghlleqaghsi Christ Jesus whanga apalluqlunga .
Sayaghngaatnga nagneghuteki kiyaghtaallesi Christ-am apeghtullghatun Pinilghiitgun Ungipatgun . Enkaam esghaghyaghtuqumsi , nalighmeng aviiteghngaaghma nagaququmsi , liigikelleqaqa ataasistun pilleghsi . Liigikelleqaqallu qerngaghpesi nekevghannaqutkellesi Pinilghiit Ungipat anguyagpesineng .
Alikegpenaki anguyasi , quunpeng ilutullusi . Enkaam tawaten pilleghpesi ipapighqelleqaat ellngit kayaalqiinaanghitut . Elpesi kayaalqiillequsi qayughllak Kiyaghneghuuq kayaalqiistilghii elpesineng .
Elpesinun qepghaasaqlegughtestekaqaa Christ-a , ugpeqnginaghpenaan , ikfiqelgusiqesillu .
Pilluwalgusightengnga . Sivunghani esghapakaqaghpesinga piyaqliilghiinga , nagaquqaqasillu piyaqliillghenka maaten . Elpesillu tamaakut ataasit piyaqliighutkennaqngwaasi .
Kiyaghtaalleghpesi Christ-akun iknaqughtisii ? Piniqellghan ilutughtisii ? Quyaaqetsii ataasistun lliilghiisi ugpeqaalgutkullghiini Agleghnalghiignekun Taghneghagnekun ? Pinitun piiqestekii , nangllekaqestekii ilasi ?
Tawatetngukufsi , quyamasteghllagtengnga piniqutelleghpesigun , ataasistun sumeghtaghalleghpesigun , ataasistun pilleghpesigun .
Ellnginaayugneghugpenasi , aangaayugneghugpenasi . Yeghlegi qusevgutullusi , ilagpesineng pinighataghaghnilusi sumeghtaghaghpenasi .
Suumqegpenaki piyukellghiinasi , yeghlegi piyukellesi pakikaghluki kayusiitaqluki ilasi .
Sumeghnesi Christ Jesus-em sumeghneghatun ayuqlit .
Jesus Kiyaghneghtun ayuqsaghngaaghmi sumeghtaghaamangituq Kiyaghneq ingluksaghqaaluku .
Yeghlegi Kiyaghneghulleni pakigluku , qepghaghtestun lliiqaaguq . Yugestun lliiqaaguq , allgeqaaguqlu yugestun .
Yugughsami qusevegtekaaguq enkaam qaatkutkaaguq tuqulleghmun , talwa tuqukaaguq qaquurakun .
Tamaaken apalluqluku Kiyaghneghem nekegtekaqaa Jesus aangelleghpigaaluku , atiqaqaallu Ataneghmeng aangelleghpigaghmeng ateghyaggaghneng .
Enkaangam qamagtengngwaaghluni qilagmelnguum , nunamelnguum , nunam asinganilnguum quulvaghlleqaat Jesus qungughquutelleghmegteggunllu apelleghmegteggunllu , " Jesus Christ-a Atanghuuq . " Tawaten pilleghmegteggun quulvaghlleqaat Kiyaghneq Ata .
Enkaangam piniqegkamni , elpesinillunga qaatkumanginaqaqaghpesinga , maaten aviillemni qaatkataghaghtengnga . Iighwightesqelluku yugulilleghsi qepghaamanginaghtek alingellelighlusillu ungelegtellelighlusillu ;
qayughllak Kiyaghneq quunpeng qepghaaguq elpesini atuqsagutesqelluku piyukelleni , qaatkusagutesqellusillu piyukelleghminun .
Sangwaa tamaghhaan piiqiteggu akuzilgafqaafsi , nalighmeng aaghtiiraaghutefqaafsi .
Enkaam avutngillequsillu pelungillequsillu . Kiyaghneghem avaqutii avutngisaghqaagut kiyaghtengnguluteng akulngitni puughtinghetlu seghleghqestetlu . Kuukgutepestaaghyaghqaagusi ighaleqetaaghestun nunami ,
ungipaqingulusi ellngitnun Christ-ameng unguvallengestikayugmeng . Enkaam taginqigtekan quyasleqaghpesinga elngaatall , qayughllak kiyaghtaalleghpesi kelgusaghqaqaa qepghalqa temngingunghilnguq .
Ugpeqilleghsillu qepghalleghsillu Kiyaghneghmun aghqutestun ayuqut . Tuquskangatnga whani anusimingllaghvigmi quyallequnga , qayughllak tuqulqa aghqutestun ayuqsaghqaaguq tuunelghii elpesi aghqutegpesinun iighwiisiiluni . Taam qamaglluta quyasleqiinkut .
Tawateghpigaq elpesillu quyayaghqaagusi , quyalgusighllagyaghqaqaghpesinga .
Atanghem piyukelqegkagu , Timothy kayagsaghtungestaghaqa elpesinun . Enkaam quyallequnga ungipangegkuma elpesineng .
Timothy-nginaghhaam sumeghtaghaatkaqiisi sumeghtaghaatkellemtun .
Tamaakut ilangi kiyang ellmeggneng katam sumeghtaghaatkaqut Jesus Christ-am qepghaqaa avelghaghluku .
Iwernga Timothy liisimakngwaaghaghsi natetulanga . Ighneghestun kayuusiitkaqaanga ungipaqingulunga Pinilghiineng Ungipaneng .
Liigikaghesnaqumkun aanesaghqaatka anusimingllaghvigmeng kayaglleqaqa elpesinun .
Neghyukaqa Ataneq whangallu elpesinun piyaghtungestaghtunga .
Sumeghtaghaatkaqaqa ugpeqaalgutfut Epaphroditus elpesinun uteghnightesnaluku . Kayutkaghqaghyugumalunga tagistekaqegkesi kayusiitesqellunga . Qerngaamtung qepghaqaagukungllu ungipaqikaagukungllu Pinilghiineng Ungipaneng . Nekevghatkaqapungllu Pinilghiit Ungipat kipullginaalghiineng .
Aglaghtesnaqaqa elpesinun qayughllak aghyuqnguuq . Peng始gaqiisi qayughllak nagaquqaqegkesi qinuyullghaneng .
Ipanguuq qinuyugllakaaguq repall tuquvziqaaguq . Iwernga Kiyaghneghem nangllegyagutkaqaa , whangallu nangllegyagutkaqaanga . Tuqumayaqan wataqaaghaq qivghullengataghaghnayaghtunga .
Tamaaken apalluqluku wataqaaghaq aglaghtesugaqa elpesinun . Kaaskan esghaqufsigu quyallequsi , enkaangam itagnaghillequnga whangallu .
Epaphroditus tuquyaghngaaghmi qepghaqaaguq Christ-amun , aaqun tuquvziqaaguq . Kayusiitkaqaanga qayughllak elpesi kayusiitepagningitkaqaghpesinga , aviilnguusi . Quyakusiqluku upughannakesi qayughllak anglegutkaghsi Ataneghqun . Enkaam quulvaghluki qamaglluki yuget Epaphroditus-etun ayuqelghiit .
Ugpeqaalgutemni , naangniitkun ungipaasuwamsi , " Quyamaaqitek Ataneghqun ! " Qinuyagusigatunga ungipaanneqiggnemsi latatgun igaqegkamneng sivunghani , enkaam ilallequq paqniitelleghpesinun .
Kelengalusi seghletun pikayugneng , tamaakuneng qikmineng , yuguut sagiqutilghiit kepfikesqelluki yugusit .
Whangkutanguukut ugpeqani circumcise-epiiwaaqani qayughllak manigughaqaghput Kiyaghneq Taghneghagkenkun , usuqaqaghputlu Christ Jesus . Neghyungigatukutlu Kiyaghneghmun piliitesqelluta whangkuta katam sallemteggun .
Kina alngunak Kiyaghneghem piliisaghqaqsaqagu ellngan katam sallghakun , whanga piyaghqaayaghtunga . Yuget tawaten piyaghqaayaqata whanga wataqaaghaq pinayaghtunga ukut apalluqluki :
Circumcise-ekaqaatnga pingayuneng inglulek aghneq atughyamkun kingunganeng allgelleghma . Israel-eghmiineng pinguunga , ramkenganeng Benjamin-em . Hebrew-piiguunga , angayuqagkallu Hebrew-nguuk . Malighqutaqngaghllagtunga Jewish-et Liilightuusiitnun , tamaaken apalluqluku Pharisee-ngughtunga .
Sagiqepigllunga amyuqetaatkegkaqanka ugpeqat . Qaatkengngwaaqaqanka Jews-et Liilightuusiit repall anaggutelleghmun avutngitkaagunga .
Iwernga tamaakut allgeghtekaqnikaqsaqenka iflamaanka apalluqluku Christ-a .
Ipa sangwaat qamaglluki iflamaanka apalluqluku megnunaghtulnga liitngwaallemneng Christ Jesus , Atanqa . Ellnga apalluqluku sangwaat qamaglluki egsimaanka . Esghaghanka mallastun ayuqluki allgeghteqeghnaluku Christ-a ,
ilatngwaaghtungallu ellnganun . Ugpeqnaniimaaqa whangamneng pinighnaqelleq qaatkutellemkun Kiyaghneghem Liilightuusaanun . Yeghlegi liisimakaqa Kiyaghneghem pinightestaqaanga qayughllak ugpeqegkegka Christ-a . Una pinilleq Kiyaghneghmeng ayuquq , yuget allgeghtaqaat ugpeqilleghmegteggun Christ-ameng .
Piyukelleghllakaqa , liinnaluku Christ-a , nanghiighnalukullu aghtughyaghqaanghillgha unguvaghtellghan ; ilannalungallu ikfiqellghanun , ellngatunllu lliighyaghqaalunga tuqullghani .
Tawaten pikuma , Kiyaghneq sighimakaqa whangallu unguvaghtesqellunga tuqulleghmeng .
Whaten pingunghitunga , " Christ-atun lliighumaanga nalighmeng Christ-atun kiyaghtaqunga quunpeng . " Iwernga pinaqellghaqa qamaglluku atuqngwaaqa Christ-am piyukellghatun lliighnalunga atuqnalukullu pisqesullgha whangamnun .
Ugpeqaalgutemni , sumeghtaghiigatunga kayaalqelghagtuumaniluku . Iwernga ataasiq piiqaqa , puyguluku sangwaa tunutemnilnguq sivutmiighnaqutkaqunga kaannaluku sangwaa sivumnilnguq .
Enkaam taklaghruketun kilgaaqunguunga kayaalqiisiqnaluku akileghtuusaq , Kiyaghneghem tuqluutkaanun pamavek Christ Jesus-kun .
Tawaten sumeghtaghanghilkufsi , Kiyaghneghem liigikesnaaghii sumeghtaghallesi anaggutngalghiit .
Una megnunapigtuq , nagneghutelteki kiyaghtaalleput maliglluku ipapighqelleq liitkaghput .
Ugpeqaalgutemni , usputaqlunga maligtengnga . Esghapagluki ilangillu kiyaghlleghhiit whangamtun .
Sivunghani uglaghngaan ungipaataataqaqamsi , maaten ungipaannaqlaataghamsi qunituumaghma . Uglaapigtut kiyaghlleghhiit anguyaguluteng Christ-am tuqullghaneng qaquurakun .
Suumqaqiit yugusimeng piyukellghit kiyang , Kiyaghneq avelghaghluku . Kaynguyugusighqaqsaqeteng aangaayugusiqaqiit . Sumeghtaghaatkaqaat nunamelngughhiinaq kiyaghtaalleghteng enkaam naafqellengyaghqaagut hell-mi .
Iwernga ugpeqani whangkuta qilagmiinguukut . Enkaam utaqangwaaghput yugulighista , Ataneq Jesus Christ-a , ukigyaghqaq whangkunnun qilagmeng pamaken .
Tagikumi allangughsaghqaqii kayaalnguut , tuqumun ayuqelghiit yugusiput . Unguvaghtekatun yugusimitun lliighsaghqaqii aghtughyaghqaanghilleghmikun . Taaggun ataasikun aghtughyaghqaanghilleghqun igleghusaghqaaghlleqaa sangwaa qamagtengngwaaghluku .
Enkaangam piniqegkamni ugpeqaalgutemni , esghaghyupigtamsi , quyamasiqamsi , akileghtuusaqamsillu qepghallemnun . Tawaten aghuliitekestaghtek Ataneghqun .
Euodia , Syntyche , qevuullunga qeleghnaqamtek , taaqitek aghivanneghmeng . Ataasistun lliightek , qayughllak ugpeqaalgutkututek Ataneghqun .
Qepghalgutemni Syzygus , elpeklu kayuusiitaghtikek aghnak taakuk taaqesqellukek aghivanneghmeng . Elkegkenka qevuullutek qepghalgusiqaqiinkut Clement-lu ilangillu qepghalgutenka , qamaglluta ungipaqinguluta Pinilghiineng Ungipaneng yulghuteghllagnun . Qepghalgutma qamaglluteng aatghit igaqngaat Igaakun Unguvallghem . Tawantut igani aatghit qamaglluteng kenlengilngughmeng unguvallengegkat .
Iiwleng quyamaaqitek Ataneghqun . Pinaqlaataghamsi , Quyamaaqitek !
Nuqenneghtulleghsi yugem qamaglluni liilligu . Ataneq tagiyaghtungestaghtuq .
Sumeghyalitkegpenaan sangwaa alngunak . Yeghlegi , sameng aklukufsi yughaneghpesini tungsighaqitek Kiyaghneghmun tuunesqellusi . Iiwleng tungsighaqitek igamsiqayullelighlusi .
Enkaam Kiyaghneghem ilusillu umyugasillu nekeggmetesnaaghii Christ Jesus-kun . Kiyaghneghem nekeggmellgha aangeghllagtuq , kitum alngunak liigikngwaaghnaanghitaa .
Enkaangam ugpeqaalgutemni , naangniitangakun latama ungipaasuwamsi sumeghtaghaatkumanginiisqelluki pinilghiitlu usuqsaghqatlu whatelnguut : tamaakut ipapiget , quulvaghyaghqat , elqughutngalghiit , pelungilnguut , piniqsaghqat , tamaakutlu pinitun akuzitkesaghqat .
Sangwaa qamaglluku nagneghuteggu liitkaghsi whangamneng apeghtughillemkunllu kiyaghtaallemkunllu . Enkaam Kiyaghneq nekeggmellelitikayuk elpesinillequq .
Elngaatall quyapigtunga Ataneghqun qayughllak qavngarugllaggaaneng whaa allameng kayusiillaataqefsinga ! Liisimakaqa kayusiisukaqaghpesinga , iwernga pipagningitkaagusi .
Aklungunilunga pingunghitunga qayughllak natesaghngaaghma itagnaghaqunga .
Ilangani nuughngaghma kiyaghtaqunga , ilangani siiptiilunga kiyaghtaqunga . Itagnaghyagusimaanga nani alngunak satulemtun kiyaghhnemni . Itagnaghaqunga kepsughngaghma kiyaghhnemni , iyataghngaaghmallu kiyaghhnemni , talwa aklumaghngaaghmallu , aklunghiteghngaaghmallu .
Sangwaa alngunak piyaghqaqaqa Christ-akun iknaqughsaghtemkun .
Paninang elpesi pinitungwaaq kayusiitaqaghpesinga seghleliinemni .
Elpesi Philippi-yeghmiini , liisimakngwaaghaghsi aghulaqaqngama Macedonia-meng , ungipaqiyuwhaaghaqngama Pinilghiineng Ungipaneng , ellnginaagusi ugpeqani kayusighikat whangameng . Ellnginaagusi ilatngalghiit allgeghutellemnunllu ifliillemnunllu .
Ataasighhaagpenaan aklupignemni manimeng Thessalonica-mellunga , tuyughaqaghpesinga .
Iwernga liigikesugamsi tunusasi manit megnunalleghpigaanghitut whangamni . Megnunalleghpigaqta esgha una : akileghtuusaghqaq allgeghsaghqaghsi Kiyaghneghmeng pinitun pillesi apalluqluki .
Whaa maaten naamaanga , aa-a , talwa siiptiilunga ayuqunga . Tuyuusasi Epaphroditus-kun qamaglluteng kaasimaat , enkaam whaa aklungigatunga . Tunusasi whangamnun aghqutkegkastun ayuqut Kiyaghneghmi efqughtinapiglleghhiit .
Enkaangam Kiyaghneghma yataaghqunnaaghiisi sameng tamaghhaaneng aklukegkaghpesineng aklungitelleghllagmikun Christ Jesus-kun .
Kiyaghnemnnun , Atamun usuqilta , quunperugllak kenlengunaan . Amen .
Ungipaataghnakesi qamaglluki ugpeqat Christ Jesus-kun suumqaqankanguq . Ugpeqaalgutet whangamnilnguut suumqaqiisinguq .
Qamaglluteng Kiyaghneghem yugan suumqaqiisinguq , kiyang taakut Caesar-em mangteghaghmiingita .
Nangllegtallgha Jesus Christ-am taghneghaghpesinilli .
Ukut latat Paul-meng pinguut . Kiyaghneghem piyukellghakun apostle-ngughtekaagunga Christ Jesus-mun . Timothy-mengllu pinguut ugpeqaalgutemnneng .
Kiyaghneghem yugitnun pinguut Colossae-melngughnun , ataasiighmelnguut ugpeqaalgutet Christ-akun . Kiyaghneghem Atamta , nanglleklisillu nekeggmellelisillillu .
Iiwleng iyamsiqayugvikaqaghput Kiyaghneq , Atanga Atanemta Jesus Christ-am , yughaatkennemsi .
Tawaten piiqukut qayughllak nagaquumaaghput ugpeqilleghsi Christ Jesus-meng , piniqilleghsillu tamaghhiitnun Kiyaghneghem yugitnun .
Pinilghiit Ungipat ungipapiguut . Nagaqughyuwhaaghaqngafsiki , liitkaagusi sighimalleghmeng Kiyaghneghem tuunegkaaneng elpesinun . Enkaam sighmalleghpesi ugpeqillelgustaqiisillu piniqillelgustaqiisillu . Qilagmi Kiyaghneghem kagpagumaa elpesinun sangwaa sighimakegkaghsi .
Pinilghiit Ungipat quyastimanginaagut yugnun . Enkaam Pinilghiit Ungipat mingitnguut iingunaghhaanun nunam , katam tawaten quyastillghistun elpesinun nagaqughyuwhaaghaqngafsigu Kiyaghneghem nangllegtallgha . Taagken kenlanga liitaghsi Kiyaghneghem nangllegtallgha .
Liitkaqaghsi Kiyaghneghem nanglleghtallgha Epaphras-meng , piniqegkamnneng qepghalgutemnneng . Ataasiighmelluni qepghaaguq Christ-amun , qepghaqaqaa whangkuta qepghaghyukaqsaqefut .
Ellngan ungipaasimiinkut piniqilleghmeng Agleghnalghiim Taghnegham tuunegkaaneng elpesinun .
Aghneghmeng taagken nagaquutemnneng tamaakut , yughaatkennaniigatamsi . Tungsiitngwaamsi Kiyaghneghmun liisimakesqelluku qamaglluku ellngan piyukellgha . Yughaatkaqamsillu peghqinghusqellusi , liigikesqellukillu sangwaat Agleghnalghiim Taghnegham apeghtuutkii .
Taagken kiyaghsaghqaaghllequsi Atanghem piyukellghatun , iiwleng atuqaqelleqaghsi sangwaa efqughnalghii ellngani . Tawaten kiyaghtelleghpesini allaaghhiinaq pinilghii qepghaghlleqaghsi enkaam wata liilleqaghsi Kiyaghneq .
Yughaatkaqamsi Kiyaghneghmun iknaqughsiisqellusi ilugpesigun aghtughyaghqaanghilleghllagmikun . Tawaten piiquq nuqenneghtughteghllagesqellusi nekeggmellelighlusi samun tamaghhaanun .
Enkaam quyamallelighllaglusi iyamsiqayugvikelleqaghsi Ata . Ellngangulghii elpesinun nengilgutestikaq sameng tamaghhaaneng akequsaqegkamineng tuunelleqniluki yuni kiyaghlleghhiit nighugmi .
Ellngan yugulikaqiinkut aghtughyaghqaanghillghaneng mamlegem enkaam tagitkaqiinkut Ataneghpagullghanun piniqegkami Ighneghmi .
Ellngan tukfiqaqiinkut , seghevutkaqiillu seghleghqelleput .
Christ-a tawatetngwaaghtuq aliinneghilngughtun Kiyaghneghtun . Kiyaghtenguuq sivungani sangwaa alngunak ulimallghilluku , enkaam qulighpigaaguq ulimaaghyaggaghneng .
Ellngakun Kiyaghneghem ulimakaqii sangwaat qamaglluki qilagmelnguutlu nunamelnguutlu . Ulimakaqii esghaqayuput , esghiigalkeputlu tamaakutlu umiilget , atanghet , igleghutistet , pilleghqalgetlu . Kiyaghneghem ulimakaqii sangwaat qamaglluki Christ-akun , Christ-amunllu .
Christ-a tawantekaaguq sivungitni sangwaat alngunak , aghtughyaghqaanghillghakunllu sangwaat qamaglluki ellngan nekaghqaghlluwaaghitnitestaqii .
Ellnga naasquutinguuq ugpeqanun yughaghvigmelngughnun , ellngan yugusiqii . Ellngan yugusiq unguvangustengngwaa . Ellnganguuq unguvaghyuwhaaqaq tuqulleghmeng , enkaam qulighpigaaguq samun tamaghhaanun .
Kiyaghneghem piyukelqaa qamagtengngwaaghluni ellmi katam kiyaghhnaluni Ighneghmi ilungani .
Kiyaghneghem Ighneghmikun veghutestekaqii ellminun sangwaat qamaglluki nunamillu qilagmillu . Enkaam aawakun Ighneghmi tuqaaqngan qaquurami ilaliighutestekaqii ellminun .
Ataasimeng pelleghngayaghtusi Kiyaghneghmeng . Enkaam anguyaksaghiisi sumeghtaghalleghpesigun , seghletunllu pilleghpesigun .
Iwernga Kiyaghneghem ilaliighunneqigtestiisi ellminun Ighneghmi yugusiin tuqullghakun . Tawaten pikaaguq taginnalusi nayuutngalleghminun agleghnaghlusi , pelungillusi , avutngillusillu .
Kiyaghneq tawaten pillequq nagnequfsi ugpeqluki Pinilghiit Ungipat aygughikellngunaki . Iqitegpenasi sighmalleghmeng allgeghtekaghpesineng nagaqughaqngafsiki Pinilghiit Ungipat . Taakut Pinilghiit Ungipat ungipaqnguut tamaghhaani nunam . Kiyaghneghem nakmikegkaqaanga , whanga Paul , qepghaghtengulunga ellminun ungipaqesqelluki Pinilghiit Ungipat .
Ikfiqelleghma yugusimkun elpesi apalluqlusi quyasteghllagaanga . Tawaten kayusighinguunga apeghiighnaluki Christ-am ikfiqellghi yugusiminun . Ellngan yugusii ugpeqaagut yughaghvigmelnguut .
Kiyaghneghem qepghaghtengllaqaqaanga ugpeqanun . Tagivaqaqaa una qepghaqaq kayusiitesqellusi , elpesinun liigikngwaaghesqelluki Kiyaghneghem akuzitangi .
Sivunghani Kiyaghneghem qayvighsimangitaa una ipapilleq tamaghhaanun yugnun , iwernga maaten qayvightengngwaa ellmi yugminun .
Kiyaghneghuuq nakmiilghii yugminun liisimakesqelluku sangwaa qayvightellghilkenni sivunghani . Nakmikegkaqaa liisimakesqelluku aangelleghllaga uum ipapillghem akulngitni Gentile-et . Ipapilleq qayvightekaa unanguuq : Christ-a kiyaghtengnguuq ilugpesini . Christ-anguuq sighimavut kiyaghtesqelluta Kiyaghneghmi ellngan nighughqellghani .
Enkaam ungipaqngwaaghput Christ-a tamaghhaanun . Qamaglluku peghqinelleghqun , kelengasaaghaqaputlu apeghtughaqaputlu qamaglluki yuget . Tawaten piiqukut taginnaluki ataasikaghtiita yuget Kiyaghneghem nayuutngallghanun angtaniitkaaluki Christ-akun .
Taana pinaluku taakunginaghhaagneng ughleghiightunga atuqluku Christ-am aghtughyaghqaanghillgha qepghalghii iknaqepiglluni ilumnni .
Ungipaataghllamsi taakunginaghhaagneng qepghaatillemneng elpesinun , ugpeqanunllu Laodicea-melngughnun , tamaghhaanunllu esghaasigalngughneng whangamneng .
Tawaten piiqunga ilungit ilutughllengesqelluki , ataasiightesqellukillu piniqelleghqun . Enkaam liigikngwaaghlleqaat sangwaa Kiyaghneghem qayvighsimangilkanga sivunghani . Taana Kiyaghneghem qayvightekaa Christ-anguq .
Qamaglluki Kiyaghneghem peghqinellghillu liigikingallghillu Christ-ametut . Taakuk aklungistun ayuquk iighngalghiik Christ-ami .
Ungipaatamsi , kitumun alngunak puughtestegpenasi temngineng apeghtughallghitneng , qaywa ipasugniteghngaata .
Qaywa uyavansaghngaaghma elpesineng , umyugamkun elpesinitaqunga . Quyaanga qayughllak kiyaghlleghhiisi Kiyaghneghem pisqellghatun , ugpeqilleghsillu Christ-akun aghuliilnguq .
Tuguklilleghpesistun Christ Jesus Atanghuluku , tawateghpigaq ugpeqilleghqun kiyaghtek ellngakun .
Ellngakun akulgutek asivanun samavek , ellngakun nekefteki kiyaghtaallesi enkaam iknaqughtek ugpeqilleghpesigun apeghtulleghpesistun . Iyamsiqayugumanginaghtek .
Kelengalusi ! Kitumun alngunak aghulaqutestegpenasi temngitwhatgun apeghtughallghitgun . Tamaakut apeghtughallghet yuget sumeghtaghallghitneng pinguut , tughneghaghnengllu pinguut , igleghutilghiit whani nunami . Christ-ameng pingunghitut ,
qayughllak qamagtengngwaaghluni Kiyaghneq kiyaghtengnguuq Christ-am yugusiini .
Christ-a naasquutinguuq igleghutistenunllu pilleghqalegnunllu . Ilateslusi Christ-amun Kiyaghneghem tuunegkaqiisi unguvallepigmeng .
Ilatngalleghpesigun Christ-amun circumcise-ekaagusi . Circumcise-elleghsi yuget pistellghitaat , iwernga Christ-am pistekaqaa . Enkaam itemutkaqiisi aghtughyaghqaanghillghaneng yugusighpesi seghleghqengngalghiit piyukellghitneng .
Paaptaayaaqngafsi qunguutkaagusi Christ-akun . Taagken maketkaagusi unguvalleghmun Christ-akun qayughllak ugpeqegkesi Kiyaghneghem aghtughyaghqaanghillgha . Kiyaghneghem maketkaqaa Christ-a tuqumeng .
Tuqukaagusi qayughllak seghleghqestenguyalghiisi , qayughllaklu circumcise-elghilnguusi yugusighpesigun . Iwernga Kiyaghneghem unguvaghtestekaqiisi Christ-akun qayughllak seghevutkaqii qamaglluki seghleghqelleput .
Qaatkenghitaqngamteki Kiyaghneghem Liilightuusi seghleghqellghet pikaput igaqegkaagut . Kiyaghneghem iqitkaqii igaquqat seghleghqelleput tuquqaalluki Christ-am qaquuraanun .
Kiyaghneghem wayaghteqaqii guututangit igleghutilghiitlu aghtughyaghqaanghillelgetlu tughneghaat . Tawaten tamanganun esghaghtestekaa kayaalqiilleni tamaakuneng tughneghaghneng .
Kitumun alngunak nanqigtestegpenasi neghelleghmengllu meghelleghmengllu , neqenghaghqellghet aghneghitneng , nutaghat tanqit aghneghitneng , nalighmeng Sabbath-et aghneghitneng .
Taakut taghneghangullghiistun ayuqut taakunun piyaghqanun aga sivumelngughnun . Iwernga tamaakut ipapiget Christ-ametut .
Ilangi yugem qusevegngasugnighqesuneghtuut , manigughaqiitlu yaqulget . Iiwleng akuzitkaqiit esghaghwaalleteng esghaqateng . Ellngitnun ungipaatestegpenasi anaggutnganilusi . Ellngit esleqngaat temngitwhameng qukaayuglleghmeng qayughllak sumeghneghit yugem sumeghneqii .
Ellngit ilannanightut Christ-amun naasquutilghiimeng yugusimun . Igleghutngwaa iingunaan yugusiq , iknaqughsaghaqaallu neghqaqluku . Qerngaghmetestaqaa yugusiq atuqesluki nafliillu ivalungillu . Enkaam yugusiq nagunguuq Kiyaghneghem nagustesqesullghatun .
Christ-a tuqaaqngan tuqulgusiqallghuuqaqaghsi . Enkaam itemutkaagusi tughneghaghneng igleghutilghiineng whani nunami . Sangan始ngam kiyaghtaqetsi nunamun pikepiglleghhiistun ? Sangan qaatkaqesteki liilightughallghit whatelnguut ,
" Saflegpenaan , Naasiighpenaan , Saaftegpenaan ? "
Taakut liilightughallghet yuget neghegkiitnengllu meghegkiitnengllu ayuqut . Enkaam neghegkiitlu meghegkiitlu atuqsaghqaananighaqut . Tamaakut liilightughallghet taawanginaghhaq yuget liilightughalqiitlu apeghtuusaqiitlu .
Tamaakut liilightughallghet apeghtughiit yuget peghqinesighwaaghesqelluki . Apeghtughiitlu amyuutkesqelluki yugusiit , atuqnaniisqelluki yugusiita pikyukellghit . Iwernga tawaten pillghita aghuliighsigatiit atuqnanilleghqameng tamaakut seghleghqellghet . Tamaakut liilightughallghet ipasugnitut iwernga temnginguut apeghtuusat .
Unguvaghtekaategpesineng maligullusi Christ-amun , piyukaqiteki sangwaat Kiyaghneghem elpesinun pikesqelluki qilagmelnguut . Tawani Christ-a aqumgaaq aghenqigneghakun Kiyaghneghem .
Suumqaqiteki tamaakut qilagmelnguut , nakaan tamaakut nunamelnguut .
Tawaten sumeghtaghaghaqitek qayughllak tuqukaagusi . Unguvalleghsi iighngaaq Christ-ami Kiyaghneghqun .
Christ-a unguvalqaghput . Aliiqan , elpesillu aliilgusighlleqaghsi nighughqellghani .
Taaqiteki atuqneghmeng yugusighpesi seghleghet piyukellghit , katam allaniiq , ukmanginneghilnguq kiyaghtaalleq , atuqsullgha seghleghem , pakigniiqlu . Pakigniiq maniguullghiistun kiyaghnengllaqanun ayuquq .
Tamaakut apalluqluki Kiyaghneghem sakraalleghllaga taginguuq qaatkusigalngughnun ellnganun .
Sivunghani tawaten kiyaghtengnguyaghtusi .
Iwernga maaten atuqnanighteki qamaglluki ukut : sakraa , sakraaghllak , ugumikeraaq , seghlequuq , seghleghmengllu akuzitkilleq .
Iqlengiqutegpenasi qayughllak taaqumaaghsi kiyaghtaallelugsi , ayghiitkaqsaqesillu .
Enkaam kiyaghtaalleghraghaq atuqaaghsimaaghsi . Nutaghtengnguusi , Ulimaghistegpesistunllu lliighuusi . Tamaaken apalluquku liigikekestaghaghsi Kiyaghneq kinaghpigaatanga .
Kiyaghtaalleghraghaghmi , allangughutngitut akulngitni Gentile-etlu Jews-etlu , akulngitni circumcise-ekatlu circumcise-ellghilnguutlu , akulngitni barbarian-etlu , Scythian-etlu , akulngitnillu qepghaghtelaaghetlu , qepghaghtelaaghunghilnguutlu . Iwernga Christ-a qulighpigaaguq , kiyaghtengnguuqlu tamaghhamnni ugpeqani .
Kiyaghneghem yukiisi agleghnalghiit , piniqepigtiisillu . Nakmikegkaqiisi . Enkaam nangllegtaghlusi , nangllekilusi , qusevegllusi , yakuqlusi , nuqenneghtulusillu .
Sakritutegpenasi iwernga seghevutullusi . Kinkut anagtekangisi seghevunnakesi katam Atanghem seghevutellghistun elpesi .
Qamaglluteng tamaakut megnunaghtut iwernga piniqelleq megnunalleghpigaaguq . Piniqutellghem ataasiightengngwaaghiinkut .
Tamaghhaghpesi nalighneqiisi Christ-am yugusiin , enkaam nakmikegkaagusi kiyaghtesqellusi qerngaghpesi nekeggmelleghqun . Taana apalluqluku Christ-am nekeggmellghan igleghulliki ilusi . Iyamsiqayugngateklu .
Yeqay Christ-am apeghtuusii kemnaghluteng kiyaghllit ilugpesini . Apeghtuututaqlusi , kelengasaaghututaqlusillu tamaghhaakun peghqinelleghqun . Ilagaghtek Kiyaghneghmun iyamsiqayullelighlusi ilugpesigun , ilagaghtek psalms-neng , ilagaatneng , maniguutmunllu ilagaatneng .
Enkaam sangwaa pikaghsi , akuzitkun nalighmeng qepghalleghqun qamaglluku piiqiteggu aatghakun Atanghem Jesus-em . Ellngakun iyamsiqayugvikiteggu Kiyaghneq Ata .
Nuliighni , malighqutaqlusi ugigpesinun qayughllak tawaten Atanghem pisqesuwiisi .
Ugini , piniqluki nuliisi , yakuqluki piiqiteki .
Taghnughhaghni , qaatkelluki angayuqasi salleghqun tamaghhaakun , qayughllak tawaten pillghem efqughtaqaa Ataneq .
Atani , sakraasaghaghpenaki taghnughhasi luuraq iilqennayukata .
Qepghaghtelaaghni , iiwleng qaatkelluki piliitistesi . Iiwlengllu efqughhnaqluki esghapagughngaata nalighmeng esghapagunghiteghngaata . Qepghaateki ipapighqellusi qayughllak tawaten quulvaangwaaghsi Ataneq .
