Salleghpesini tamaghhaani qepghaghaqitek pinaqellghaghsi qamagtiiluku qepghaatepiglleghhiistun Ataneq , nakaan yugnun .
Neqamikluku Atanghuuq Christ-a qepghaatkaghsi . Allgeghlleqaghsi akileghtuusaghsi ellnganeng . Akileghtuusaq akequsaqegkaqaa tuunelleqniluku yugminun .
Iwernga kina alngunak seghletun pista nallangighyaghqaaguq seghletun pillghanun qayughllak Kiyaghneghem nanqigsaghqaqaa tamaghhaan yuuk tawateghlluwaaq .
Qepghaghtelaaghet piliitistengitni , pinitungwaaqlu atunengwaaqlu piiqiteki qepghaghtelaasi , liisimakluku elpesillu Piliitistelguusi qilagmi .
Yughaamanginaghtek , iilqayugpenasillu yughaghaqitek iyamsiqayugvikumaan Kiyaghneq .
Yughaqufsi , yughaatkennakefsikutlu . Yughaghtek Kiyaghneghmun qelpeghutesqelluta amigmeng mingitesqelluki akuzitangi Christ-ameng ayuqelghiit . Sivunghani Kiyaghneghem qayvighsimangitaa ipapilleq Christ-ameng ayuqelghii . Iwernga Kiyaghneghem ungipaataanga ungipaqesqelluku taana qayvighsimangilnguq ipapilleq . Ungipaqegkaqutemneng taana ipapilleq anusimingllaghaatnga .
Enkaam yughaatkitengnga una ungipaq ungipaqsaghqaaluku whateghlluwaaq katam Kiyaghneghem whangamnun pisqellghatun .
Peghqinghwaaqitek ugpeqaanghilngughninneghpesini . Atuqaqiteggu tamaghhaan pilleghqaghsi ungipaasaghqaaluki Christ-ameng .
Aleghquneghpesiki iiwleng nangllegtaghlusi , akuziiqlusi itagnaghyugnaghlusi , nagasugnaghlusillu . Tawaten piiqitek liisimakesqellusi naten kiimsilleghqiit aapqughaallghit .
Tychicus ugpeqaalgutkaqa , piniqepigtekaqa . Qepghalgutkaqa , qepghaataqaallu Ataneq whangamnun maligulluni .
Kayagtaqa elpesinun , liisimakesqelluku natetulvut enkaam kayemellengesqellusi . Ungipaannaaghiisi whangamneng .
Kayagtaqallu Onesimus elpesinun . Piniqegkaaguq ataasiighmelnguq ugpeqaalgun , elpesineng pinguuq . Tychicus-enkuk ungipaalleqiisi sameng tamaghhaaneng salleghneng maani .
Aristarchus-em anusimingllaghalgutma , Mark-emllu atalgutangan Barnabas-em suumqaqiisinguq . ( Ungipaatkaqamsi latatgun Mark-meng , kaasimakan elpesinun upughatesqelluku . )
Jesus-emllu , alla atelgem Justus-meng suumqaqiisinguq . Taakunginaagut Jews-et ugpeqat , qepghalgusighaqaatnga Ataneghpagullghanun Kiyaghneghem . Ilutuqutkanka elngaatall .
Epaphras , qepghaghtenga Christ Jesus-em , elpesineng pinguuq , ellnganllu suumqaqiisinguq . Iiwleng taakunginaghhaagneng yughaatkaqiisi angtaniitesqellusi , liisimakngngwaaghesqelluku sangwaa Kiyaghneghem pisqesullgha elpesinun , elpesinunllu qamagtengngwaaghluku piyukellgha pikesqelluku .
Ungipaasugamsi Epaphras qepghaghllakaaguq kayusiinnalusi , kayusiinnalukillu Laodicea-ghmiitlu Hierapolis-eghmiitllu .
Luke-emllu piniqepigtekamta aghallegtam , Demas-emllu suumqaqiisinguq .
Ugpeqaalgutnun Laodicea-melngughnun , Nympha-munllu , ugpeqaalgutnunllu qernughutkayugnun maniguunnaluteng mangteghaani , ungipaannakesi suumqaqankanguq .
Atightughnakesi ukut latat ugpeqanun qerngughutkayugnun yughaghvigani Colossae-m . Wataghllaklu atightughnakesi ukut latat Laodicea-ghmiit ugpeqiitnun . Atightughnakesillu latat Laodicea-ghmiit ugpeqiita tuyughyaghqiit elpesinun .
Archippus ungipaataghnnakesi whaten , " Wataghllak apeghiighnaken qepghaqaq Atanghem qelghutkaa elpenun . "
Whanga , Paul , whanga katam iiggemneng una igaqaqa . Neqamiklunga anusimingllaghaagunga , qiipraghusighlunga ayuqunga . Qamagllusi suumqaqamsi . Kiyaghneq nangllegtaghli elpesinun .
Ukut latat Paul-meng , Silas-meng , Timothy-mengllu pinguut , Thessalonica-ghmiit ugpeqiitnun Kiyaghneghem Atam pingi Atanghemllu Jesus Christ-am . Kiyaghneghem nangllekillghallu nekeggmellghallu elpesinillik .
Quunpeng iyamsiqayugvikaqaghput Kiyaghneq tamaghhaghpesinun , iiwlengllu yughaatkaqamsi .
Yughanemta Kiyaghneghmun Atamnnun neqamikaqaghput qepghalleghsi ugpelleghpesigun , qepghalleghsi piniqelleghpesigun . Iyamsiqayugvikaqaghputlu ugpelleghsi nagneghuskesi iknaqluku qayughllak sighimangulghiisi Atanemteggun Jesus Christ-akun .
Ugpeqaalgutemnni , Kiyaghneghem piniqegkaani , liisimakaghput nakmikegkaqiisi
qayughllak Pinilghiineng Ungipaneng tagitaqngamsi , akuziteraaghinaghteggun pimangitukut , iwernga aghtughyaghqaanghilleghqunllu , Agleghnalghiignekunllu Taghneghagnekun pikaagukut . Enkaam ugpeqasi Pinilghiit Ungipat ipangutangi . Liisimakaghsillu naten kiyaghtekaatfut elpesinilluta , tawaten kayusiinnalusi kiyaghtekaagukut .
Enkaam whangkutestunllu Ataneghtunllu lliightek . Qaywa ikfiqeghllagngaaghpesi , tuguklighasi Pinilghiit Ungipat quyamallelighlusi Agleghnalghiigneng Taghneghagneng .
Enkaam usputaaghtusi tamaghhiitnun ugpeqanun Macedonia-millu Achaia-millu .
Atanghem ungipaa mingitnguuq elpesineng Macedonia-millu Achaia-millu . Ugpeqilleghsillu Kiyaghneghmeng liitaat tamangani . Enkaam whangkuta sameng pinghisaghngaamteggu ugpeqilleghsi , qayughllak siingenllu yuget nagaquumaat .
Tamangani aapghaqaat upughatilleghllagsi whangkunneng elpesinitnguluta . Qiivumanilusillu unguvalghiimun Kiyaghnepigmun qepghaannaluku , peglluki kiyaghnengllaqat .
Utaqaaqaghsillunguq Kiyaghneghem Ighnegha , Jesus , tagiyaghqaq qilagmeng . Ellnganguuq Kiyaghneghem unguvaghtekaa tuqulleghmeng , yuguliiqiinkutlu Kiyaghneghem sakraallghaneng kaasaghqameng .
Ugpeqaalgutemnni , liisimakaghsi elpesinun pilleghput temngingunghitkaaguq .
Iwernga sivunghani elpesinun pillemta , liisimakaghsi Philippi-mi ikfiqliightestekaqiinkutlu seghlequuqaqiinkutlu . Tamaanlluta qaywa uglalghiim yugem aghuliighhnaqutkeghngiinkut Kiyaghneghem ilutustekaqiinkut , enkaam ungipaasaghtughamsi Pinilghiineng Ungipaaneng Kiyaghneghem .
Ungipaqilleghput ipanguuq . Iqlengiqngunghitukut elpesinun , seghleghmeng piyukegkiitukut elpesinun , puughhnaqutkigatamsi .
Yeghlegi , ungipaqaqaput Pinilghiit Ungipat qayughllak Kiyaghneghem itagnaqluta neghyukutkaqii whangkunnun . Akuzillemteggun efqughhnaqutkengngunghitaput yuget , iwernga efqughsukaghput Kiyaghneghuuq , nanqigtingalghii ilumta sumeghtaghallghaneng .
Liisimakaghsi usuquughsaghtuunghitamsi nalighmeng sakengviksaghtuunghitamsi . Kiyaghneq liisimakistekaghput .
Usuqesaayugtengngunghitukut yugneng , elpesineng , nalighmeng kinkuneng .
Apostle-ngutemnneng Christ-amun , tungsighniighviksaghqaqsaghamsi sameng alngunak . Iwernga elpesinilluta yakumangilliqutkumangitamsi , yeghlegi mamaghtikayugestun naastun aflengakilghiistun taghnughhaghmeggneng ayuqegkaagukut .
Piniqepigtamsi , enkaam quyakusiqinaghluku elpesinun liisimakesugaput Kiyaghneghem Pinilghiit Ungipii . Pinilghiinginaat Ungipat pigpenaki , quyakusiqinaghluku sameng tamaghhaaneng kayusighyuglusi ayuqamsi , qayughllak piniqsaliitkaqamsi .
Ugpeqaalgutemnni , neqamikaghsi naten angkaan qepghalleghputlu ughleghiilleghputlu ! Qepghaqaagukut unugtuumaan , aghneghtuumaan qayughllak elpesinun uqigtuqutnguyunghilnguukut ; elpesinisimaluta ungipaqikaagukut Pinilghiineng Ungipaaneng Kiyaghneghem .
Elpesillu Kiyaghneqlu liisimakistekamsi . Elpesini ugpeqani kiyaghtekaagukut pelungilluta , ipapighqelluta , anaggutellngunaamta .
Liisimakaghsi katam atam aflengakillghatun taghnughhaghmineng , whangkutallu tamaghhaghpesi tawaten katam aflengakegkaqamsi . Kayemegkaqamsi , ilutughsaqaqamsi , qelghutaataqaqaghput elpesinun atuqesqelluku kiyaghtaalleq efqughnalghii Kiyaghneghmi . Tuqluungwiisi ilatesqellusi ellmi katam Ataneghpagulleghminunllu pinighnalleghllagminunllu .
Iyamsiqayugvikumanginaangwaaghputlu Kiyaghneq una apalluqluku : whangkunneng nagaqughluku tuguklighaghsi Kiyaghneghem ungipaa . Elpesi tuguklighaghsi Kiyaghneghmeng ungipaaluku , nakaan yugneng ungipaaluku . Taananguuq Kiyaghneghem ungipaghpigaa qepghalghii elpesini ugpeqilghiini .
Ugpeqaalgutemnni , elpesi tawatetusi ugpeqistengistun Christ Jesus-em qerngughutkayuget yughaghvigitni Kiyaghneghem Judea-mi . Nunalgutegpesi ikfiqestekaqiisi katam Jews-et ikfiqestellghistun ugpeqat Judea-mi .
Jews-nguut tuqutikat Ataneghmeng Jesus-meng , uuknaliqistenengllu , amyuqetaatkegkaqiinkutlu . Efqughhneghitaat Kiyaghneq , kipullginaaghuutlu tamaghhaanun yugnun
aghuliighhnaqutkelleghmegteggun ungipaqilleghput Gentile-enun yugulillengnayukata . Tawaten pilleghmegteggun ilamanginaghiit seghleghqelleteng enkaam qenwatlu Kiyaghneghem ugumiyaguteghllagluki qantaghaqun aghyuughlleqii .
Ugpeqaalgutemnni , amyuqetaatkistemta aghulaqestaqngamikut Thessalonica-meng , pellghututestaghtiinkut , iwernga paninang sumeghmikaqamsi . Esghaghyupigtaqsaghamsi gginasaghqughlusi
enkaam takunaqutkaqsaghamsi . Whanga , Paul , takunaqutkaataghaqsaghamsi iwernga Tughneghaam amigighaghtaqiinkut .
Elpesi sighimalqamsi , quyasiqamsi , qaghpakamsillu . Taana qaghpa whangkuta qukaayugusiqelleqaghput manungani Atanemta Jesus-em tagikan .
Ipapestaaq elpesi qukaayugusiqamsillu quyasiqamsillu !
Iwernga esghaatusigatutemnneng qavngaghhaaneng pelleghngatutelleghput nuqetutepagningiitaghput . Enkaam agghitkaagukut whanga ellnginaghma Athens-mennalunga ,
kayagtekaqaghpungllu Timothy elpesinun . Ugpeqaalgutkaghpung , qepgalgusighaqiinkung Kiyaghneghmun . Ungipaqilgusighaqiinkung Pinilghiineng Ungipaneng Christ-ameng ayuqelghiineng . Kayagtekaqaghpung iknaqughsaghyaghtiisqelluki ugpeqillesi , kayemesqellusillu ,
qayughllak iilqayugtesunghilkemsi ugpeqilleghpesineng seghleliillesi apalluqluki . Iwernga liisimakaghsi ugpeqani whangkuta seghleliighyaghqaagukut .
Elpesinilluta ungipaatngwaaqaqamsi amyuqetaatkellengelleqniluta ; enkaam liisimakaghsi taawa ipa ikfiqutkegkaqaghput amyuqetaatkelleq .
Tamaaken apalluqluku aghtughyagusama nuqenneghmeng , kayagtekaqaqa Timothy elpesinun liigiknaluku ugpeqilleghsi natetaqutanga . Pengkaqamsi qayughllak Tughneghaam nanghiiqumanayukangisi ugpeqinaniisqellusi , enkaam qepghalleghput temngisugnighsimanayukan .
Iwernga Timothy-m uteghnighluni ungipaatiinkung quyanalghiimeng ungipameng ugpeqilleghpesinengllu piniqelleghpesinengllu . Ungipaataqiinkungllu iiwleng neqamikaqnilutung pinitun , esghaghyugaqnilutungllu katam whangkutung esghaghyullemtestegetun elpesi .
Ugpeqaalgutemnni , seghleliighllagumaluta , ikfiqeghllagumaluta ilutughtukut qayughllak nagneghutngukesi ugpeqilleghsi .
Whaa aneghtaghaghtukut qayughllak aghuliilkaalghiisi Ataneghqun .
Enkaam iyamsiqayugvikngwaaghput Kiyaghneq elpesineng . Elpesi apalluqlusi quyaghllaguukut sivungani Kiyaghnemta .
Taakunginaghhaagneng yughaatkengngwaamsi unugtuumaan , aghneghtuumaan alla esghaghyaghqaalusi , ilayaghqaaluki ugpeqilleghpesi aklukegkiit .
Kiyaghnemta , Atam ellmineng katam , Atanemtallu Jesus-em qantaghaqun elpesinun piyaghqaaghteslikut !
Atanghem , piniqsaliitutestaghaghlisi . Piniqelleghsillu tevughasligu tamaghhaanun yugnun , katam whangkuta piniqellemtestun elpesi .
Tawaten ayepsugighsaghlleqii ilusi avutngitesqellusillu pelungitesqellusillu sivungani Kiyaghnemta Atam , Atanemta Jesus-em tagillghani . Tawani kelqelleqii qamagtengngwaaghluki ellmi yuni .
Ugpeqaalgutemnni , alaghrang whaten pinaqamsi , liitivikegkaqaghpekut naten kiyaghtelleghqameng efqughnaghlusi Kiyaghneghmun , esgha tawaten kiyaghlleghhiisi . Aatghakun Atanghem Jesus-em kayemamsi wataqaaghaq tawaten pisqellusi .
Liisimakasi sangwaat qelghutkaput elpesinun pisqelluki Ataneghqun Jesus-kun .
Whatetuq Kiyaghneghem piyukellgha elpesinun : pelungitesugiisi seghleghqestesunghitiisi atuqutelleghqun .
Liitesugiisillu tamaghaghpesi nuqetutesqelluki yugusisi pinilleghmun enkaam kiyaghllequsi pelungillusi , efqughnaghlusi Kiyaghneghmunllu yugnunllu .
Ilapgategpenasi yugusighpesi atuqiyullghanun ugpeqaanghilnguut pillghistun nallukilghiit Kiyaghneghmeng .
Kitum alngunak sakusiiqefqaan piligu ugpeqaalgutmi inglunga atuqilleghmun . Atanghem aghyuughllaglleqii tawaten pikayuget . Sivunghani kelengasaaghllakaqamsi tamaaken .
Kiyaghneghem nakmikegkaqiinkut kiyaghtesqelluta pelungilluta , seghleghqellngunaamta .
Enkaangam kitum alngunak qaatkenghilkumiki tamaakut apeghtuusat , Kiyaghneghuuq qaatkenghilkanga nakaan yuuk . Kiyaghneghuuq tuunistezi Agleghnalghiigneng Taghneghagneng .
Kitum alngunak latanghisaghngaaghmisi ayuqiisi ungipaannalusi piniqesqelluki ugpeqaalgutesi , qayughllak Kiyaghneghem apeghtuqaqiisi piniqutesqellusi .
Ipanguuq piniqasi qamaglluki ugpeqaalgutesi tamaghhaani Macedonia-mi . Iwernga ugpeqaalgutemnni , qelghamsi piniqutaghiisqellusi .
Pinaqellghaghsi qamaglluku kiyaghtek nekeggmellelighlusi , elpesi sayaghqasi piiqiteki , avelghaghluki ilagpesi sayaghqiit . Qepghaghtek allgeghusaghqaalusi aklukegkaghpesineng katam whangkuta qelellemtestun .
Tawaten pikufsi neghyuknaanghitasi kinkut alngunak aklukegkaghpesinun , ugpeqaanghilnguutlu siivakelleqiisi .
Ugpeqaalgutemnni , liisimakesugamsi ugpeqaneng qavalghiineng qivghukefqiita pisqelluki sighimallghilngughestun .
Ugpeqaghput Jesus tuquluni unguvaqaaguq . Enkaam ugpeqaghput Kiyaghneghem tagilleqii Jesus-kun tamaakut qavaqat ugpeqiluteng ellnganeng .
Ungipaatngwaaghamsi Atanghem apeghtuutkaaneng . Ataneq tagikan , whangkuta paninang unguvalghiini ingyaghaghnaanghitaput tamaakut qavaqat .
Ataneq ellnga katam qilagmeng ukigllequq , yuget nagaqughlleqaat iglagtuqaq qelelleq , menga archangel-em , qalghightaatangallu Kiyaghneghem . Tamaakut ugpeqiluteng Christ-ameng tuqulaghaatkat unguvaghyuggaaghllequt .
Taagken whangkuta unguvalghiini unegtekani , Kiyaghneghem qerngughutesluta , ellngitnun , ghhataghaghtaatesleqiinkut qilagwaaghnun paayghesqelluku Ataneq eslami . Enkaam Ataneghmellequkut quunperugllak .
Tamaaken apalluqluku ilutughsaasiqaqiteki taakut akuzitet .
Ugpeqaalgutemnni , elpesinun latatkenniitut qakun tamaakut piyaghqaatangi .
Qayughllak elpesi liisimakngwaaghaghsi Aghnegha Atanghem tagiyaghqaaguq waakenghillghaghulluni tagillghatun teglegniightem unugmi .
Yuget whaten pimaluki , " Nekeggmellelguukutlu paqniitukutlu , " naafqellghem kaatqaghlleqii katam aghnam ighniyullghan aqnighqellghatun . Yuget anagnaanghitaat taana naafqelleq .
Iwernga elpesi ugpeqaalgutemnni , mamlegllagmenneghitusi enkaam Aghneghan Aghneghem waakenghillghaghhnaanghitiisi tegleghniightetun .
Qamagllusi avaqutaqiisi nighugem , avaqutaqiisillu aghneghem . Unugem pikenghitiinkut nalighmeng mamlegllagem .
Enkaam qavaafqaamta pilta ilangistun , itupill teghumalta , liisimaluta .
Tamaakut qavalghiit qavaghaqut unugmi , tamaakut meghelghiit suumaqut unugmi .
Iwernga Atanghem pikiinkut enkaam liisimaluta kiyaghtelta . Paqniighsaasilleghqamnnun sakimamteggun aatelteggu sighimalleq yugulilleghmun .
Kiyaghneghem piyukelqenghitaa ikfiqesqelluta sakraalleghmeng , iwernga yugulillengesugiinkut Atanemteggun Jesus Christ-akun .
Jesus-em tuqumatkegkaqiinkut ellminitesqelluta unguvayaghngaamta , tuqukaayaghngaamta tagikumi .
Tamaakut apalluqluki kayemututaqiteklu kayutkutaqiteklu whaa maaten pilleghpesistun .
Ugpeqaalgutemnni , siivakiteki Ataneghmun qepghalghiit akulegpesini . Ellngan nakmikegkaqii igleghutistengulukillu apeghtughistengulukillu elpesinun .
Siivakeghllagaqitekillu piniqaqitekillu apalluqluki qepghallghit . Nekeggmetullusi pitek .
Ugpeqaalgutemnni , kelengasaaghteki ighsanitalghiit , ilutughsaghteki alingtalghiit , kayusighteki kayaalnguut , negkeghlluwaan piiqiteki qamaglluki .
Wataghllak akisaqunaki seghletun pistesi iwernga pinitun piiqiteki ilasi , qamagllukillu yuget .
Quyamanginaghlusi ,
yughaamanginaghlusi ,
iyamsiqayuglusi tamaghhaani nekegneghmi . Taakunguut Kiyaghneghem piyukellghi elpesinun Christ Jesus-em piliitkiitnun .
Qaamtegpenakek Agleghnalghiik Taghneghak ,
sasiinghinnigpenaki uuknaliqillghet .
Iwernga sangwaa qamaglluku nanghiiqwaaqiteggu enkaam tuguklighaqluki sangwaat pinilghiit ,
iqitngatek tamaghhaaneng seghleghmeng .
Kiyaghneghem nekeggmellelitistem iighwightengngwaaghlusi pelungighllisi . Avutngitesliki taghneghasi , unguvasisi , yugusisi Ataneghput Jesus Christ-a tagikan .
Tagsiqlightegpesi pilleqii tamaakut qayughllak ataasiighmetuq .
Ugpeqaalgutemnni , yughaatkaqluta .
Quyakaqiteki ugpeqaalgutesi naaghluki Kiyaghneghem piniqellghakun .
Qelghamsi Atanghem pilleghqalitellghakun ukut latat atightiisqelluki tamaghhiitnun ugpeqaalgutegpesinun .
Piniqellgha Atanghem Jesus Christ-am elpesinilli .
Ukut latat Paul-meng , Silas-meng Timothy-mengllu pinguut . Ugpeqanun Thessalonica-melngughnun Kiyaghneghem Atamta pingitnun , Atanghemllu Jesus Christ-am .
Nangllegtalleqlu nekeggmelleqlu elpesinun pinguuk Kiyaghneghmeng Atameng , Ataneghmengllu Jesus Christ-ameng .
Ugpeqaalgutemnni , iiwleng iyamsiqayagusaghqaqamsi Kiyaghneghmun . Elqughutngaaq tawaten pilleghqaghput , qayughllak ugpeqineghtughtaghalghiisillu , piniqutaghaghlusillu lliightusi .
Tamaaken apalluqluku qanatkaqamsi ilangitnun ugpeqat Kiyaghneghem yughaghvigitnilngughnun . Aapghaqaghput nuqetutineghtulleghsillu , ugpeqilleghsillu qaywa amyuutkellengeghngaaghpesi , ikfiqellengeghngaaghpesillu .
Tamaakut ipapighqaat Kiyaghneghem nanqigtillgha elqughutngalghiinguuq . Enkaam Kiyaghneghem aapghiisi itagnaghnilusi kiyaghtesqellusi Ataneghpagulleghmini qayughllak ikfiqutkengngukesi .
Kiyaghneghem piyaghqaqaa sangwaa elqughutngalghii : ikfiqesaghqaqii tamaakut ikfiqestilghiit elpesineng .
Enkaam elpesi ikfiqelghiini Kiyaghneghem meghnaalisnaaghiisi ikfiqelleghmeng whangkutallu maligulluta . Tawaten pillequq aliightekumiki Ataneq Jesus , iknaqeghllalghiitlu yaqulgi . Qilagmeng ukigllequt keneghmelluteng kumaghughngalghiimi .
Taagken Jesus-em aghyuughlleqii tamaakut nallukilghiit Kiyaghneghmeng , qaatkusigalnguutlu Pinilghiineng Ungipaaneng Jesus-meng ayuqelghiit .
Aghyuughnaqngwiillu kenlengilngughmeng naafqelleghmeng , iqitesnaqnguutlu Ataneghmeng , nighuganengllu aghtughyaghqaanghillghan .
Tamaakut piyaghqaagut tawani Aghneghmi Ataneq Jesus tagikan . Qamaglluteng yuget ugpeqikat ellnganeng usuqelleqaat , saghiighayagulleqaatlu . Elpesi akulngitnillequsi qayughllak ugpeqegkesi ungipaq aapqaghput elpesinun .
Enkaam quunpeng yughaatkaqamsi whaten : Kiyaghneghem apeghlisi kiyaghtengngunilusi ellmi kiyaghtesqesulleghmitun . Aghtughyaghqaanghilleghmikunllu naamiglligu qamaglluku piyukelleghsi pinilleghmun , qepghallghillu ugpeqilleghpesi .
Enkaam aatgha Atanemta Jesus-em quulvallengellequq elpesigun , elpesillu ellngakun quulvallengellequsi nafughtallghakunllu nangllegtallghakunllu Kiyaghnemta , Atanemtallu Jesus Christ-am .
Ugpeqaalgutemnni , ungipaasugamsi tagilleghqaaneng Atanemta Jesus Christ-am , qerngughutelleghqamnnengllu ellnganun .
Umyugasi qapragaghtesunghitngwaaghaput nalighmeng kakavesunghitaput nagaququfsigu Aghnegha Atanghem kaasimaniluku . Entaqun kitum uuknaliqutkegkaqaa , nalighmeng kitum ungipaqegkaqaa , nalighmeng kitum latatkumaniluku whangkunnun pikaqaa .
Iwernga puughtestegpenasi ! Taana Aghnegha Atanghem kaannaanghituq kenlanga yuget malighqutaqsugnanilghitnun Kiyaghneghem igleghutillghanun , kaatellghanunllu Seghlepestaaghem Yugem . ( Ellnga naafqesaghqaaguq hell-mi . )
Taam yugem kipullginaaghlleqii kiyaghnengllaqat nalighmeng manigughyaghqat , tamaakuneng ellmineng qulighpigaaghsaghqaaguq . Enkaangam iteghluni Kiyaghneghem Temple-nganun aqumluni Kiyaghneghunillequq .
Neqamikenghistegguu salin elpesinillunga ungipaatkaqegkemsi tamaaken ?
Liisimakaghsi kitum maaten nuqneqaqaa Seghlepestaaq Yuuk tagilleghqaaneng . Wetku aghneni kaaskan tagillequq .
Aawallu qayvighsimangilnguq aghtughyaghqaanghillgha seghleghqellghem qepghaaghsimaaq nunami . Iwernga maaten kitum kimaawistaqaa taana seghleghqelleq . Kimaawististenga tawaten pillequq kenlanga Kiyaghneghem iqitestellghanun .
Taagken Seghlepestaaq Yuuk aliightesllequq , iwernga Atanghem Jesus-em tagikumi tuqulleqaa aneghneghaneng qaneghmi , naafqelleqaallu nighugllagakun tagilleghmi .
Sivutghulluku Atanghem Jesus-em tagilleghqaa , Seghlepestaaq Yuuk tagillequq aghtughyaghqaanghillelighluni Tughneghagh-meng . Taana Yuuk allaaghlluwhaghtisighwaaghllequq allaaghhiinaghmeng saghiighanalghiineng .
Atuqelleqiillu allaaghhiinaat seghleghet puughhnaluki tuquyaghqat . Tuquyaghqaagut qayughllak ugpeqsunghilkangat ipalleq yugulisighqaqsaqeseng .
Tamaaken apalluqluku Kiyaghneghem puughneqguutesleqii ugpeqesqelluki sangwaat ipangunghilnguut .
Enkaam qamagtengngwaaghluteng ugpeqinghilnguut ipapilleghmeng nanqigsaghqaagut aghyuughyaghqaaluteng qayughllak pinighyuugusiqegkangat seghlleghqelleq .
Ugpeqaalgutemnni , iiwleng iyamsiqayagusaghqaqamsi Kiyaghneghmun , elpesi piniqegkiitni Atanghem . Iyamsiqayugvikaqaghputlu Kiyaghneq qayughllak nakmikegkaqiisi yugulisqellusi ima piinlighyuwhaallghaneng nunam . Yugulikaagusi pelungighsallghakun Agleghnalghiim Taghnegham , ugpeqelleghpesigunllu ipapilleq .
Tawaten kiyaghtaalleghmun Kiyaghneghem tagsiqaqiisi Pinilghiitgun Ungipatgun ungipaqegkamegteggun ; tagisqaqiisi piliitesqelluku nengighqaghsi pinighnallgha Atanemta Jesus Christ-am .
Enkaam ugpeqaalgutemnni , aghuliitekestaghtek , ugpeqekestaghteggu ipapilleq apeghtuutkaghput elpesinun ungipaqillemteggunllu latallemteggunllu .
Kiyaghneghem Atamta , piniqistemta , nangllegtalleghmikun tuunegkaqiinkut kenlengilngughmeng ilutulleghmeng , pinilghiimengllu sighimalleghmeng . Atanemta Jesus Christ-am ellngan katam , Kiyaghneghemllu Atamta , elkegkenka
ilutughsaghlisillu , iknaqughsaghlisillu tamaghhaakun pinilghiikun qepghalleghpesigunllu akuzilleghpesigunllu .
Ugpeqaalgutemnni , taaqniitkun sameng piighaataqaghlamsi . Yughaatkitekut Atanghem ungipaa mingirragkiighesqelluku , yugnunllu quulviisqelluku , katam elpesi pilleghpesistun .
Yughaatkitekutlu Kiyaghneghmun yugulisqelluta seghleghneng yugneng , qayughllak uglalghii yuuk ugpeqillelgunghituq .
Iwernga Ataneq ataasiighmetuq ; iknakqughsaghlleqiisillu paqniighsaghlleqiisillu Tughneghaghmeng .
Atanghem nalluneqniighumaa whangkunnun qaatkutnguusi qelellemnnun , qaatkumanginaghlleqaghsillu .
Atanghem liigikeslisi wataqaaghaq Kiyaghneghem piniqellghaneng , Christ-amllu nuqetutineghtullghaneng .
Ugpeqaalgutemnni , aatghakun Atanemta Jesus Christ-am qelghamsi iqitngasqellusi tamaghhiitneng ugpeqaalgutegpesineng ighsanitalghiinengllu malighqutaqigalngughnengllu apeghtuutkamnneng elpesinun .
Elpesi katam liisimakaghsi ayuqesighaghyaghqaqsaghaghpekut ; elpesinilluta ighsanitiqumangitukut .
Tugukliigataput neqet kinkuneng alngunak tukfillngunaki . Iwernga unugtuumaan , aghneghtuumaan qepghaqaagukut , ughleghiiqaagukut uqigtuqutnguyunghitutemnneng nalighhiinaghpesinun .
Elpesinun aapsaqleguyaghtukut kayusiitesqelluta , yeghlegi qepghaqaagukut aflengaknaluta whangkunneng usputaanaluta elpesinun ayuqesighiisqelluta .
Talwa elpesinilluta whaten qelqaqegkemsi , " Kina alngunak qepghaghyunghilnguq neghestegpenaan . "
Tawaten pikaagukut qayughllak nagaqughaqukut ilasinguq ighsanitaghtut , qepghaghyugigatut , yeghlegi yanutqwaaqiinguq yuget .
Aatghakun Atanghem Jesus Christ-am qelghaputlu kayemaputlu tawatelnguut yuget ighsanitiqefqiita allgheghutesqelluki kiyaghusighqiitneng .
Ugpeqaalgutemnni , qinuyagutegpenasi pinitun pineghmeng .
Kina alngunak qaatkusunghilkan sameng pillemnnun ukutgun latamteggun , suumqennakesi kinkungutangi . Enkaam iqitngalghaasi ellnganeng kaynguyugesqelluku anaggutellghaneng .
Iwernga kiyaghutegpenaan anguyaguluku , itupill kelengasaaghteggu ugpeqaalgutkelluku .
Atanghem ellmineng katam nekeggmellelitikayugem , nekeggmellelisilli iiwleng sami tamaghhaani . Ataneq tamaghhaaghpesinilli .
Whanga , Paul whanga katam iiggemneng igaqaqa piniqilqa elpesinun . Tawaten igaghaqunga qamaglluki latamkun elpesinun liisimakesqelluki whangamneng pingutangi .
Nangllegtallgha Atanemta Jesus Christ-am tamaghhaghpesinilli .
Ukut latat Paul-meng pinguut apostle-nganeng Christ Jesus-em . Apostle-ngughtekaagunga qelellghakun Kiyaghneghem Yugulighistemta , Christ Jesus-emllu sighimakegkamta .
Timothy-mun ; ighnepikamken ugpeqillemtegnegun . Kiyaghneghem Atam , Christ Jesus-emllu Atanemta quyasliten , nangllekliten , nekeggmellelguslitenllu .
Aghulaqnaqumalunga Macedonia-mun Ephesus-metesqegkaqamken . Ilangi yuget tamaanlenguut apeghtughinguut ipangunghilngughmeng apeghtuusaneng . Qeleghqi taaqesqelluki
sangillghaatkegpenakinguq akuzimghhutkelluki ungipaghaatengllaqat , sivunelghuteghllagetlu aatghit . Tamaakut aaghtiiraaghusighhiinaagut , kayutngunghitut qepghaqaanun Kiyaghneghem . Ellngan qepghaqaa apeghiighaquq ugpeqillghiinaghhaghqun .
Qeleluugutkaqa ugpeqat piniqutepiigesqelluki , umyugaqeglluki , ipapigmeng ugpeqillelguluki .
Ilangita yuget pegtekaqiit tamaakut enkaam aaghtiiraaghaqut temngimeng .
Apeghtughistenguyugaqut Kiyaghneghem Liilightuusaanun . Iwernga liigikigatiit akuzitkegkateng qaywa apeghtuusaqeghngaaghmegteki ipasugnilluki .
Liisimakaput Liilightuusat pinightut elqughlluki atuqelghiini .
Liisimakaput Liilightuusat ulimaaghunghitut pinilghiinun yugnun . Ulimaaghuut liilightuusaneng naafqiikayugnun , qaatkusigalngughnunllu . Ulimaaghuut Kiyaghneghyugigalngughnun , seghleghqestenunllu . Ulimaaghuut waakigalngughnun Kiyaghneghmeng , legasiighwaatkilghiinunllu agleghnalghiinun . Ulimaaghuut tuqutikayugnun atameggneng nalighmeng naameggneng , yugtaghtenunllu .
Ulimaaghuut sex-kun seghleghqestenun , yugnun yulgutmeggneng atuqikayugnun , yugnun akikikayugnun yugmeng qepghaghtelaaghuluki , iqlengiqestenun , iqlengalghiinun liisimakistenun , kipullginaalghiinunllu Kiyaghneghem apeghtuusiitnun ipapighqengngalghiinun .
Taakut apeghtuusat piniipiglleghhiineng Pinilghiineng Ungipaneng pinguut . Aapghwaat usuqnalghii Kiyaghneq , neghyukutkaqii whangamnun aapghesqelluki .
Iyamsiqayugvikaqa Christ Jesus Ataneghput , iknaqughsaqaqaanga qepghaqamnun . Iyamsiqayugvikaqa esghaqaqaanga ataasiighmellunga nakmiklunga qepghaatesqelluni .
Sivunghani seghlepestaatun akuzitkegkaqaqa Christ-a , seghlepestaatunllu pikaqaqa . Amyuqetaatkaqngamki maligsaaghtengi tawateteftuq amyuqetaatkengnguftaqa ellnga . Tawalliima Kiyaghneghem nangllekegkaqegkanganga qayughllak salin ugpeqigalkegka Christ-a , liigikumangilkegka saaqutka .
Iwernga Atanemta nangllekeghllakaqaanga ! Ugpeqillelitkaqaanga , piniqellelitkaqaangallu Christ Jesus-melngughmeng .
Sameng pilleghqaqa ipanguuq enkaam qamaglluni ugpeqsaghqaaguq , " Christ Jesus tagikaaguq nunamun yugulinaluki seghleghqestet . " Whanga seghlelleghpigaagunga seghleghqesteneng .
Naqamllu Kiyaghneghem nangllegyagutkaqaanga . Enkaam usputaagunga naten tagkaan Christ Jesus-em utaqiilleghqaaneng seghleghqesteneng ugpeqesqelluni . Taana usputaq tamaakunun ayuquq ugpeqiyaghqanun ellnganeng unguvallengesqelluki kenlengilngughmeng .
Umiilegmun kenlengilngughmun , tuqupagningilngughmun , aliinneghilngughmun , ellnginaa Kiyaghneghuuq ; ellnga quulvallenglillu usuqellenglillu quunperugllak kenlengunaan ! Amen .
Timothy-mi ighnemni , qavngaq ilangita uuknaliqistet akuzitkegkaqaaten . Enkaam maaten qelghamken akuzitangit guututkiki pilluwamun . Tawaten pinitun pilluwaghllequten Christ-amun .
Ugpeqikestaa Christ-akun atuqluku liisimakegkan elqughutngalghii . Ilangita yuget atuqigatiit liisimakegkateng elqughutngalghiit enkaam naafqaqiit ugpeqilleteng katam angyaghpagiillghiistun .
Hymenaeus-enkuk Alexander-enkuk tamaakut akulngitnituk . Tuunegkaqagka Tughneghagh-mun liitesqellukek seghlepestaatun akuzitkefqaan Kiyaghneq pisqelluku .
Sivukluku kayemamken yughaatkesqelluki qamaglluki yuget , tungsiitesqelluki Kiyaghneghmun aklukegkiitneng , iyamsiqayagunnaketenllu Kiyaghneghmun .
Yughaatkiki umiilget , qamagllukillu igleghutilghiit , kiyaghsaghqaaluta nekeggmelluta maniguusimaluta , quulvaamalukullu Kiyaghneq .
Tawatelnguq yughalleq pinightuq , efqughnaghtuq Kiyaghneghmi Yugulighistemnni ,
qayughllak qamaglluku yuuk yugulillengesugaa , liitesugaallu ipapilleq .
Taawa ataasiinaaguq Kiyaghneq , ataasiinaaguqlu ilaliighutista Kiyaghneghmunllu yugnunllu . Taananguuq yuuk Christ Jesus .
Ellmineng tuunegkaaguq aghqutnguluni itemunnaluki seghleghqellghitneng qamaglluki yuget . Taananguuq pilleghqaghlluwaaq Kiyaghneghem kelgutillgha yugulillengesugniluki yuget qamaglluki .
Tamaaken apalluqluku Kiyaghneghem nakmikegkaqaanga ungipaqistengulunga , apostle-ngulunga . Kayagtaanga apeghtiisqelluki Gentile-et ugpeqilleghmengllu ipapilleghmengllu . Ipa ungipaatamken , iqlengiqngunghitunga !
Tamaghhaani yughaghvigni yugiinaat yughiisqesuganka . Tamaakungulit kiyaghlleghhit qaatkulluteng Kiyaghneghem piyukellghanun . Yughaghlit nengugulluki iiggeteng sakraallngunatengllu aaghtiiraallngunatengllu .
Piyukankallu aghnat pinighnallghit kelgutesqelluki pinitun pilugullghitgun . Aatkiit mallegngafqiita nalighmeng kayngunaghyaghqaafqiita . Itupill pinighnalleteng kelgullitki aneghneghqilleghmegteggun , nakaan nuyaqegsaghwaalleghqun nalighmeng gold-mengllu pearl-mengllu ullngaqluteng nalighmeng akituqameng aatkameng aalluteng . Tawaten pilleq elqughutngaaq aghnanun maniguutkayugunilghiinun Kiyaghneghmun .
Yuget apeghtughinghata yughaghvigni aghnat nagasaghqaagut nepiighngaghmeng , malighqutaqluteng .
Aghnat apeghtughistesugigatanka nalighmeng igleghutistengusugigatanka yugnun . Nepiighngayaghqaagut ,
qayughllak Kiyaghneghem ulimayuggaaqaqaa Adam , taagken Eve .
Adam-ngunghituq puughtellengegkaq , iwernga aghnaaguq puughtellengegkaq enkaam seghleghqestengughtekaaquq .
Iwernga aghnat ighniightuqumeng taghnughhaghneng yugulillengellequt nagneghumakuyeng neghyukluku Jesus , piniqimanginaqumeng ilameggneng , kiyaghsimanginaqumengllu agleghnaghluku kiyaghtaalleghmeng qusevegtellelighluteng .
Whaten pilleq ipanguuq : Kina alngunak igleghutistenguyukumi ugpeqanun taana qepghaqaq piyukegkaa piniipigtuq .
Igleghutista avutngisaghqaaguq , ataasimeng nuliilguyaghqaaguq , nuqenneghtuyaghqaaguq , sumeghtaghaqegsaghqaaguq , yupiinghuyaghqaaguq , upughanghuyaghqaaguq , apeghtughiyaqleguuqlu .
Suumestenguyaghqaanghituq , suuglluguyaghqaanghituq iwernga nanglleghtaghyaghqaaguq , qanengnaqigasaghqaaguq , maniyuneghtuyaghqaanghituq .
Igleghutistem igleghutngwaaghyaghqaqii mangteghaghmiini , avaqutanillu apeghtughyaghqaqii veghusnaatefqaami qaatkesqelluni .
Igleghutista igleghutillgiskumi ellmi katam nengllugutmineng , naten始ngam aflengakelleqaki ugpeqistengi Kiyaghneghem ?
Igleghutista ugpenghhaanghisaghqaaguq , luuraq qukaayugtepagnayukan enkaam nanqigtellengellequq aghyuughyaghqaaluni Tughneghaghtun .
Igleghutista pinitun kiyaghsaghqaaguq ugpeqaanghilngughnun akuzitkesqelluku itagnaghluku . Enkaam seghlequughpagningilleqaat , Tughneghaamllu kayaalqepagningilleqaa .
Tawateghpigaq Deacon-etlu pinighluki akuzitkesaghqaagut , ipapighqengngayaghqaagut , wine-meng meghepagyaghqaanghitut , pakigneghuyaghqaanghitutlu manimeng .
Pegsaghqaqenghitiit apeghtuusat Kiyaghneghem qayvighqegkii , umyugiitlu seghleghyugisaghqaagut .
Igleghutistet nakmiighvagilgameng deacon-kaghqameng qepghaqalilluki liigiknakangit piniitangi yuget . Taagken deacon-ngughtesnakangit .
Tawateghpigaq aghnatlu pinighluki akuzitkesaghqaagut , yiillgiyaghqaanghitut , iwernga nuqenneghtuyaghqaagut , ataasiighmesaghqaagutlu sakun tamaghhaakun .
Deacon-et ataasimeng nuliilguyaghqaagut , igleghutngwaaghyaghqaqiit avaqutatengllu mangteghaghmiitengllu .
Tamaakut deacon-et qepghaqegtat quulvallengyaghqaagut , nalluneqsuknaanghitaatlu ugpeqilleghteng Christ Jesus-kun .
Sunanguq qantaghaqun elpenun pilanga , iwernga maaten elpenun latatkanka tamaakut apeghtuusat .
Enkaam kimaawimakuma latama liisimakesleqaaten naten ugpeqat kiyaghsaghqaatangi Kiyaghneghem nengllugutanganilnguut . Ellnginguut ugpeqistengi unguvalghiim Kiyaghneghem , aghveghaqetaagut , tunemaagutlu ipapilleghmun .
Nalluneqnaghhangunaki ugpeqaput apeghtuusat Kiyaghneghem qayvightekii seghleghllaguutlu ipapestaaghuutlu : Christ-a allgeqaaguq yugusipiguluni , Kiyaghneghem Taghneghagkenka liisimakestii tamaakut ellngan pikii elqughutngatangi , yaqulgetlu esghaqaqaat . Ungipaqegkaaguq nunataghhaani tamaghhaani , ugpeqegkaqaat nunataghhani tamaghhaani , taagken qilagmun mayuutkaguq .
Agleghnalghiik Taghneghak whateghlluwaaq piik kingulighni aghneghni ilangita yuget peglleqaat ugpeqilleghteng Christ-akun . Tawaten pillequt qayughllak qaatkelleqegkangit iqlengalghiit tughneghaat , apeghtuusiitlu .
Tawatelnguut apeghtuusat iqlengalghiineng pinguut . Iqlengiqelleteng aapghaqiit ipapigsugnighqelluki . Nagannaniqaqiit umyugateng liisimakilghiit elqughutngalleghmengllu anaggutngalleghmengllu .
Tawatelnguut yuget nengughutesnanighiiqut , ilangillu neqem neghesnanighaqiit . Iwernga Kiyaghneghem ulimaaqii qamaglluki neqet neghyaghqaaluki iyamsiqayagutaqluki . Ugpeqat liisimakilghiit ipapilleghmeng liisimakiit tamaakut .
Kiyaghneghem ulimaaghi qamaglluteng pinilghiinguut . Enkaam ighsaksaghqaanghitut tugukliimakumeng iyamsiqayagulluki .
Akuzitangakun Kiyaghneghem , yughakunllu aaftekaagut agleghnaghluki .
Tamaakut apeghtuusat liigikestengngwaaqufki ugpeqaalgutegpenun , pinilghiingullequten qepghaghtenga Christ Jesus-em . Ugpeqillghen iknaqughlleqaa liisimanginaqufki ipapillghet ugpeqat ugpeqaqegkangit , pinilghiitlu apeghtuusat qaatkegkaghten .
Nagategpenaki sasiinghilnguut ungipaghaatet tengvimun ayuqelghiit Kiyaghneghem ipapillghanun . Yeghlegi peghqigsaatkigu Kiyaghneghmun ayuqelghii kiyaghtaalleq .
Yugusim ulapellgha pinightuq , iwernga kiyaghtelleghput Kiyaghneghem piyukellghatun ayuqelghii pinighataghaghtuq . Kayusiisaghqaqiinkut whani unguvallemnni , tuunglighhaanillu unguvallghem .
Taana pilleq ipanguuq , enkaam qamagtengngwaaghluni ugpeqsaghqaaguq .
Tamaaken apalluqluku qepghaghllaguukutlu sagiqliightengnguukutlu yugnun ugpeqesqelluku ipapilleq . Tawaten piikut qayughllak neghyukaghput unguvalghii Kiyaghneq , Yugulighistengat qamaglluteng yuget , kiyang tamaakut ugpelghiit ellngakun .
Qeleghqi apeghtughqi tamaaken .
Kitumun alngunak palaqestegpenaan anglinghhaamallghen . Iwernga ugpeqanun usputaawi akuzilleghpegun , salleghpegun , piniqelleghpegun , ugpeqilleghpegun , pelungilluten kiyaghtelleghpegun .
Kaatellemnun kenlanga , ugpeqat qerngughunneghata atightuutaqiki Akuzitneng Igaqegkaneng , ungipaqitaqiki , apeghtughaqiki .
Atuqaqigu taghneghagnekun tunusaq ilugpenilnguq . Taana tunusaq tuunegkaaguq elpenun uuknaliqelleghqun Elder-et iigtighaqngaten .
Pinaqellghen qamaglluku piiqiki qelghutkanka . Tawaten yuget liilleqaat pillguughlleghhiiten .
Piraamsingwaaghluten kiyaghtaalleghpenillu apeghtughilleghpenillu . Tawaten pikuvek elpeneng yugulillequten , tamaakutlu nagatesteten .
Aghyuughpenaan siivanlleq yuuk , iwernga kavyungunaan nallghusaghaqigu atakelghiistun . Uyuqliit yuget anglegutkelghiistun piiqiki .
Siivanlleghet aghnat naakelghiistun piiqiki , enkaam uyuqliit aghnat nayagestun piiqiki , qiliighyukefqiita .
Kayusiitiki ugingighat aflengakistengiitkat .
Iwernga ugingighaq avaqutaghtukumi nalighmeng eltughaghtukumi , kelgullit nengllugutmeggnun kiyaghsugniluteng Kiyaghneghem kiyaghtesqellghatun . Aflengakelleghmegteggun angayuqateng akinaqelleqiit enkaam efqughlleqaat Kiyaghneq .
Ugingighaq ilakwaaghiitkaq sighimanguuq Kiyaghneghqun . Enkaam unugtuumaan , aghneghtuumaan yughaamanginaaguq kayusiitesqelluni .
Iwernga ugingighaq teghigniqnginaqumi ellmineng efqughhnaluni , unguvaghngaaghmi tuqukastun ayuqsaghqaaguq .
Qeleghqi ugpeqat tamaakut pisqelluki enkaam kitum alngunak seghlequunghillitki .
Kitum alngunak aflengakenghilkumiki ilakwaani , wata ellmi katam nengllugutni , tawaten pilleghmikun pegtekaqaa ugpeqilleni . Enkaam seghleghataghaallequq ugpeqaanghilngughmeng .
Ugingighaq 60 uksughtutkaliimakan , nengughtekaakanllu ataasimeng , aatgha igaqsaghngaaghmi ayuquq ugingighat atelghutiitgun .
Amalleqa tamangan liisimakaat qepghallegtulanga , katam avaqutani pinitun anglistellghatun , upughaneghtulanga , ugpeqaalgutmi itegiit ughvughaqluki , kayusighiiqluni seghleliilghiineng , quunpengllu pinitun piiqelghii .
Iwernga nuteghat ugingighat aatghit igaqegpenaki atelghutatgun . Yugusiita piyukellghan sakniqesneghisteng ugiighyugllequt . Tawaten pimakumeng naafqelleqaat akeqilleghteng Christ-amun .
Enkaam Kiyaghneghem nanqiglleqii aghyuughyaghqaaluki qayughllak naafqegkangat akeqilleghteng .
Taam saaghwakun ighsanitaghtaqii , itghiitughtaqii , yiillgitughtaqii , yanutquneghtughtaqii , akuzitkaqiitlu sangwaat akuzitkesaghqaqenghilketeng .
Enkaam itagnaghataghaghnayaghtut nuteghat uginghighat ugiighyaquyeng , taghnughhangluteng , aflengakesqellukillu nengllugutangit . Tawaten pikumeng anguyak seghlequughvigiitesleqaat whangkunneng .
Aawallu ilangi nuteghat ugingighat ugpeqaananighluteng maligusimaat Tughneghagh-mun .
Ugpeqaq aghnaq ilakwaalgukumi ugingighaneng , ellngan kayusiisaghqaqii . Enkaam ilangita ugpeqat kayusiinneghisaghngaaghmegteki ayuqiit . Taagken ugpeqat kayusiilleqiit uginghighat aflengakistengiitkat .
Elder-et igleghutiyuqat yugaghvigmi , taakunginaghhaagnengllu qepghalghiit apeghtughilleghqun , ungipaqilleghqunllu , quulvaghaqiteki malghughqelluki akileghtuusiit .
Qayughllak Akuzitet Igaqegkat piit , " Ox-a tutmalghii grain-meng malliighnaluki , neghesqelluku grain-meng sugrugiitighpenaan . " Amalleqa , " Qepghaghta akileghtughyaghqaaguq qepghallghanun . "
Nagategpenaki kinkut alngunak avutkilghiit Elder-meng anaggusimaniluku , wetkuqun avutkilghii liisimakistelgukan maalghugegneng nalighmeng pingayuneng .
Kina alngunak seghleghqumanginaqan , aghyuughnaken seghleghqennaniisqelluku ugpeqat manungitni . Tawaten pikuvgu ilangi tamaakut alingellequt .
Tamaakut qelghutanka elpenun qaatkesqelluki , pakiggutifqaavek nalighmeng taniilqifqaavek pisqelluten . Tawaten qelghamken esghaamanghitni Kiyaghneghenkut , Christ Jesus-enkut , nakmikegkatlu yaqulget .
Iigtighaghtegpenaan kina igleghutistekaghqaaluku yughaghvigmi . Taayughqegkuvek ilalkiinnayukavek seghleghqellghanun . Kiyaghtekestaa pelungilluten .
Meghhiinaghmeng meghegpenang , iwernga wine-ngiighhaghmeng meqaghaqluten kayutkelleqan aqsaqughpenun , qinuyugaatalleghpenunllu .
Ilangita yuget seghleghqellghit aliitngwaaghaqut , talwa salin nanqigtellghilluteng . Iwernga ilangita yuget seghleghqellghit aliighsaghqaagut kinguvaqwaaqun .
Tawateghpigaq aneghneghqillghat aliitngwaaghaqut , iwernga tamaakut aliinneghilnguut iighnganaanghitut .
Qamaglluteng qepghaghtelaaghet siivakeghllaglitki tamaakut piliitisteteng , enkaam kitum alngunak seghletun akuzitkenghillikek aatgha Kiyaghneghem , apeghtughilleghputlu .
Qepghaghtelaaghet piliitistengit ugpeqaalgutngukata siivakataghaghlitki qayughllak ugpeqaalgutkegkangit . Enkaam qepghaataghaghlitki qayughllak kayusiingwiit ugpeqaalguteteng piniqegkateng . Tamaakut apeghtuusaqikillu ungipaqikillu .
Kina alngunak apeghtughikumi allanguluku tamaakuneng apeghtuusaneng , itagnaqenghitii apeghtuusapigi Atanemta Jesus Christ-am . Ellngan apeghtuusaan ungipaatiinkut Kiyaghneghem piyukellghatun kiyaghtelleghqameng .
Kina alngunak allatun apeghtughilghii aangaayugneghllaguuq , liigikigatuq sameng alngunak . Aaghtiiraaghyuneghtuuqlu qaniqsuneghtuuqlu akuzitneng . Tawaten pillghem allgeghtaqii : aqinalleq , aghivatelleq , seghlequughutelleq , ugpequnnanilleq .
Tawatelnguut quunpeng aaghtiiraaghutestiiqut . Umyugiit sumeghneghlluugtaqut enkaam liisimaknanighaqaat ipapilleq . Sumeghmeggni qepghaaskumegteggu Kiyaghneq aklungighilleqniluteng piiqut .
Iwernga allgeghuteghllagllequkut kiyaghtekumta Kiyaghneghem kiyaghtesqesullghatun itagnaqluku pitutalvut .
Allgeghaqngamta nunamun kelqutngitukut , tuqukumtallu kelqutelgunaanghitukut .
Enkaam itagnaghllequkut neqelgukumta , aatkalgukumta .
Iwernga tamaakut aklungighiyulghiit nanghiiqullengaqut . Seghleghem piyukellghita tugwaaqii enkaam temngitwhaghllagughtaqut . Taagken piyukellghita sayugaqii naafqelleghmun .
Manimeng piniqilleq akuqaa qamaglluni seghleghem . Ilangita yuget pegtaqaat ugpeqilleghteng qayughllak manitughqaaghllagyulghiit . Enkaam ellmeggneng qivghughllagughtaqut .
Iwernga elpek Kiyaghneghem yukaaten , enkaam iqitngaluten tamaakuneng . Sagiqutiki elqughutngalleq , kiyaghten Kiyaghneghem kiyaghtesqellghatun , ugpeqillelighluten , piniqillelighluten , nuqenneghtuluten , nangllegtaghluten .
Pilluwaatigu ugpeqilleq qayughllak tawaten pilluwalleq pinilghiinguuq . Tugugullu kenlengilnguq unguvalleq . Kiyaghneghem tagsiqaqaaten tugukliisqelluku taana unguvalleq aapghaqngavgu ugpeqillghen ugpeqalghutnun .
Qeleghnaqamken nagasimanghani Kiyaghneghem , unguvallelitikam samun tamaghhaanun unguvalghiinun , nagasimanghanillu Christ Jesus-em , kiimsighilaataqughikam Pontius Pilate-mun .
Qelghamken piraamsiluten qaatkesqelluki qamaglluki qelgutkanka elpenun . Nagneghutiki kenlanga Atanemta Jesus Christ-am uteghninqiglleghanun . Tawaten pikuvek kitum alngunak anagguniluten pinaanghitaaten .
Kiyaghneghem pilleghqaghlluwaaghmini tagisleqaa Jesus Christ-a . Usuqnalghii Kiyaghneq , ellnginaaguq Igleghutisteghllak , ellnganguuq Umiilgat umiilget , Atanghat atanghet .
Ellngiinaaguq tuqungigalnguq . Kiyaghtengnguuq nighugrakegllagmi repall kitum alngunak tughaaghpagningitaa . Kitum alngunak esghiigataa , talwa esghaghnaanghitaa . Kiyaghneghem piklikek quulvalleqlu aghtughyaghqaanghilleqlu quunperugllak . Amen .
Qukaayugtesnanighqi tamaakut aklungilnguut nunami whani , talwa sighimasnanighqi aklungingitgun nalluneqnalghiitgun . Iwernga sighimasqiki Kiyaghneghqun . Ellngan ighlegutegpenaamta tuunaqiinkut sameng tamaghhaaneng pinighyuugusighqameng .
Aklungilnguut pinitun pisqiki , aklungitesqiki pinitun qepghalleghqun , ighlellngunaki tuuniyukestaghluki ilangitnun yugnun .
Tawaten pikumeng kagpaglleqaat aklungi ellmeggnun . Taana aklungi ayugilnguuguq tunemaq aagnakaghqiitnilnguq . Enkaam unguvallengellequt unguvallepigmeng .
Timothy , kelengakluki tamaakut Kiyaghneghem neghyukutkii elpenun . Iqitngaluten ugpeqaanghilnguut temngitwhaneng akuzitngitnengllu , aaghtiiraaghutellghitnengllu . Tamaakut ugpeqaanghilnguut sumeghmeggni liisimallepiilguniiqut , iwernga ipangunghituq .
Ilangita pegsimaat ugpeqilleghteng qayughllak ugpeqegkangat ipangunghilnguq liisimalleq . Kiyaghneghem quyaslisi .
Ukut latat Paul-meng pinguut apostle-nganeng Christ Jesus-em Kiyaghneghem piyukellghakun . Kayagtekaqaanga aapghesqelluku akequsaqegkaq unguvalleq Christ Jesus-melnguq .
Timothy-mun piniqepigtekamnun ighnemnun . Kiyaghneghem Atam , Christ Jesus-emllu Atanemta quyasliten , nangllekliten , nekeggmellelguslitenllu .
Unugtuumaan , aghneghtuumaan yughallemkun iyamsiqayugvikaqaqa Kiyaghneq elpeneng . Qepghaataqaqa seghleghyullngunanga , katam sivunemtun .
Esghaghyupigtaqamken allameng , qayughllak neqamikaqa pellghututaqngamtung qiyakaalghiiten . Enkaam quyaghllagllequnga qerngughunneqigtekumtung .
Neqamikaqa ugpeqillepiigen . Taananguuq ataasiq ugpeqilleq nengyughpek Lois-em , naagpeklu Eunice-em atuqegkangak . Liisimakngwaaghaqa elpeklu atuqngwaan .
Tamaaken apalluqluku neqangughsugamken , atuqumanginaghhu tunusan Kiyaghneghmeng , tuunegkaqaa iigtighaqngamken .
Kiyaghneghem taghneghalitellghitiinkut alingyugnalghiimeng . Itupill Taghneghagkenka imiqaqiinkut aghtughyaghqaanghilleghmeng , piniqelleghmeng , nuqetelleghmengllu .
Kayngukegpenaan ungipaqigu Ataneghput , talwa kaynguyagutegpenanga anusimingllaghaagunga Christ-a apalluqluku . Itupill aghtughyaghqaanghillghakun Kiyaghneghem ikfiqelgusighnga Pinilghiit Ungipat apalluqluki .
Kiyaghneghem yugulikaqiinkutlu nakmikegkaqiinkutlu pelungitesqelluta . Tawaten pikaaguq apalluqluki ellmi katam uspeqellenillu piniqillenillu , nakaan qepghalleghput apalluqluku . Piniqegkaqiinkut Christ Jesus-kun sivutghulluku piinlilleghqaan nunam .
Iwernga whaa piniqelleni liitestaa whangkunnun tagillghakun Yugulighistemta Christ Jesus-em . Christ-am naafqegkaqaa tuqulleq , taagken Pinilghiitgun Ungipatgun liitestiinkut tuqungigalngughmeng unguvalleghmeng .
Pinilghiit Ungipat apalluqluki Kiyaghneghem nakmikegkaqaanga ungipaqistengulunga , apostle-ngulunga , apeghtughistengulungallu .
Taakut apalluqluki ikfiqnguunga . Iwernga kaynguyunghitunga qayughllak liisimakaqa kinangutanga ugpeqegkaqa . Liisimakngwaaghaqa ellngan kelengaksaqlegwaa sangwaa neghyukutkaqa ellnganun kenlanga kingulighmun Aghneghmun .
Maligtiki apeghtuusapiget nagaquqaghten whangamneng . Usputaagut atughqaqaten . Apeghtuusaqiki ugpeqilleghqunllu piniqelleghqunllu allgeghtekaqaten Christ Jesus-meng .
Kelengakigu ipapilleq neghyukutkaq elpenun . Kelengakigu kayutkellukek Agleghnalghiik Taghneghak kiyaghlleghhiik ilumnni .
Liisimakan qamagtevzighluteng ugpeqat Asia-melnguut kayusighyugnaniimaatnga , talwa Phygelus-enkuk Hermogenes-enkuk .
Yughaatkengngwaanka Ataneghmun nangllegyagutesqelluki Onesiphorus-em nengllugutangi , qayughllak uglaghngaan ilutughsaghaqaanga . Kaynguyagusimangitaallu anusimingllaghaamalqa .
Kaataqngami Rome-emun ivan始ghiighutkaqaanga kenlanga naalkelleghminun .
Ataneghmun yughaatkaqaqa Onesiphorus nangllegyagutesqelluku tawani Aghneghmi ! Liisimakan kayutkeghllakaqaqa Ephesus-mi .
Enkaangam elpek ighnemni , iknaqi atuqelleghpegun piniqellgha Christ Jesus-em .
Elpeklu tawantutkatlu nagatkaqasi apeghtuusanka . Enkaam apeghtuusanka neghyukutiki ataasiighmelngughnun . Taagken ellngita apeghtuusaqlegulleqiit ilameggnun .
Ikfiqelgusighqut pinilghiitun pilluwaghtengatun Christ Jesus-em .
Pilluwaghtem ilatngalghiim pilluwaghtenun efqughsugaqaa umiileni , enkaam akumghhuusigatuq pilluwaghtengunghilnguut kiyaghtaallghitnun .
Kayaalqiiraaghta kilgaaqumun malighqutaqenghilkumi liilightuusameggnun , allgeghunnaanghituq qaghpanganeng kayaalqiistem .
Ughleghiighllakaq piitesighaghta nengighyuwhaaghyaghqaaguq unataqata .
Sumeghtaaghaatkiki sameng pillghenka qayughllak Atanghem liigiksagutesleqaaten sameng tamaghhaaneng .
Neqamikluku Kiyaghneghem unguvaghtestekaqaa Jesus Christ-a tuqulleghmeng , kingunqaa David-em . Tamaakunguut ungipaqaqegkenka apenemki Pinilghiit Ungipat .
Ikfiqnguunga qayughllak ungipaqegkenka Pinilghiit Ungipat . Talwa qiipraghusighlunga ayuqunga liilightuusameng naafqiistetun . Iwernga akuzitangi Kiyaghneghem qiipraghutngitut .
Enkaam ikfiqusiqsugluku ayuqaqa sangwaa tamaghhaan Kiyaghneghem nakmikegkii yugulillengesqelluki Christ Jesus-kun . Yugulilleghmegteggun nighughqellengellequt kenlengilngughmeng .
Maakut pillghet ipanguut : Tuqulgusiimakumteggu , kiyaghtelgusighlleqaghput .
Iilqayunghilkumta , igleghutilgusighlleqaghput . Nallunqegkumteggu , ellnganllu nallunqelleqiinkut .
Ataasiighmenneghilkumta , ellnga ataasiighmetaquq qayughllak taaqnaanghituq ataasiighmenneghmeng .
Kitumun alngunak puygustegpenaki tamaakut . Kiyaghneghem nagasimanghani , kelengasaaghqi qaniqututkefqiita akuzitet pisqelluki . Qaniqutellghat kayutngunaanghituq , naafqengnginaghlleqaat ugpeqillghat nagallghiit .
Taakunginaghhaagneng qepghaa Kiyaghneghmun itagnaqesqelluten . Qepghaghtengu kayngukingigalnguq qepghaqamineng . Elqughaghllukullu apeghtuusaqigu Kiyaghneghem ungipaghpigaa .
Iqitngaluten temngitwhaneng , sameng pisiinghilngughneng aleghquutelleghneng . Tawatelnguut aleghquutellghet uyavaataghaghlleqiit yuget Kiyaghneghmeng .
Tawatelnguut temngitwhat apeghtuusat aqnighneghestun ayuqut mingitkayuget maamyaghqaanghilnguut . Hymenaeus-enkuk Philetus-enkuk apeghtughillghik tawatelnguugut .
Pegtekaqiik apeghtuusapiget qayughllak piiquk siingenllu tuqukat unguvaghtesimaniluki . Enkaam ilangitnun ugpeqnanightestekaqaak ipapilleq .
Iwernga ayugilnguq tunemaq Kiyaghneghem nekegtekaa qapragtepagningituq . Taaggun tunemakun igaqngaat akuzitet : " Atanghem liisimakii ellmi pini . " Whatenllu igaqngaaq , " Kina alngunak tuqlughilghii aatghaneng Ataneghem , seghletun pineghmeng taaqli . "
Mangteghaghllagmi allaaghhiinaghmeng salghutaghtuuq : ilangi ulimaaghuut gold-meng , silver-meng , unaghsimeng , qikumengllu . Ilangi salghutat megnunalghiinun atuugut , ilangi samun alngungak .
Kina alngunak ellmineng katam pelungighsaqumi seghleghmeng , salghutaghtun atughqaaghllequq megnunalghiimun . Aaftekaaghllequq atuuluni mangtegham yuganun . Taagken atughqaaghllequq alngunak pinilghiimun qepghaqamun .
Iqitngaluten sameng seghleghmeng anglinghhat atuqsugaqegkangitneng . Quunpeng atuqaqigu elqughutngalleq . Ataasiighmelluten , piniqingaluten , nekeggmellutenllu . Tamaakut atuqiki , maligulluten tuqlughilghiinun Ataneghmun qamaken pelungilngughmeng ilumeggneng .
Iqitngaluten temngitwhaneng aleghquutellghitneng yuget akuzitkilghiineng liigikumangilkemeggneng . Liisimakaten aaghtiiraaghutestikayuguut .
Atanghem qepghaghtenga aaghtiiraaghtengunghituq . Itupill nangllegtaghyaghqaaguq tamanganun . Pinilghiinguyaghqaaguq apeghtughista . Nuqenneghtuyaghqaaguq .
Atanghem qepghaghtenga kavyugisaghqaaguq apeghtughikumi kipullginaalghiinun . Walluumllu Kiyaghneghem avuteghqestaqliki ugpeqesqelluku ipapilleq .
Enkaam liisaaghaghyaqumeng anagnayaghaat Tughneghaam negaghaa . Tughneghaam naapsimaneghminiki aaghqutaqaqii .
Liisimakesugamken kingulighni aghneghni seghleliighllaguyaghqaaguq .
Yuget ellmeggneng piniqellequt , maniyuneghtullequt , yamrratullequt , aangaayugllequtlu . Seghlequughlleqiit ilateng , qaatkennaanghitiit angayuqateng , iyamsiqayugnaanghitut , waaknanighlleqaatlu Kiyaghneq .
Piniqinaanghitut , seghevutinaanghitut , iqlengiqutkillequt , suugllugullequt , amyuqetiqellequt , ugumikelleqaatlu sangwaa alngunak pinilghii .
Uveghpagulleqiit ilateng , nangyiighullequt , qukaayugteghllagllequt , teghigniqelleq piniqataghaghlleqaat pakiggulluku Kiyaghneghmeng .
Qaaymegteggun ugpeqaayugllequt , iwernga kiyaghtaallghita apeghlleqaat avangitulngi Kiyaghneghem aghtughyaghqaanghillghaneng . Iqitngaluten tawatelngughneng yugneng .
Ilangi tamaakut nenun iitghaataghllequt aaghqutaqepigesnaghnaluki nallekaghnilnguut aghnat . Tamaakut aghnat seghleghqellghita uqigtuqusighllaglleqii , seghleghemllu piyukellelghutngita aaghqutaqelleqii .
Tamaakut aghnat nagallequt apeghtughillghanun kitum alngunak , taawanginaq liinnaanghitaat ipapilleq .
Tamaakut apeghtughilghiit ellngitnun kipullginaaghlleqaat ipapilleq , katam Jannes-enkuk Jambres-enkuk kipullginaallghegketun Moses . Umyugaghlluugllequt , ugpeqillghatlu ipangunghillequq .
Iwernga tawaten pillghat mulunaanghituq . Temngitwhallghat aliillequq tamanganun , katam Jannes-enkuk Jambres-enkuk temngitwhallghak aliitngallghatun .
Iwernga elpek liisimakngwaaghaten apeghtughillghenka , kiyaghtaalqa , apallaallu kiyaghtelleghma . Liisimakanllu ugpeqilqa , iilqayunghitelqa , piniqilqa , aghuliilkaamalqa .
Liisimakan amyuqetaatkesilqa , ikfiqelqallu . Liisimakan tawaten pikaqaatnga Antioch-mi , Iconium-emi , Lystra-millu . Uglaghngaan amyuqetaatkellengegkaagunga , tawalliima Atanghem yugulikaqaanga tamaghhiitneng .
Tamaghhaghmi amyuqetaatkellengellequq kiyaghsulghii Kiyaghneghem piyukellghatun Christ Jesus-kun .
Seghleghet yuget , puughtistetlu , seghleghughtaghaghllequt . Puughqughllequt , ellngitlu puughtellengellequt .
Iwernga elpek atuqumanginaghqi apeghtuusat liitkaghten , ugpeqepiikaghten . Liisimakaten ipangutangi , qayughllak liisimakaten kinkungutangi apeghtughistekegkaghten .
Ima taghnughhaategpeneng liisimakegkaqaten agleghnalghiit Akuzitet Igaqegkat . Akuzitet Igaqegkat apeghtughyaqlegwaaten yugulilleghqameng ugpeqilleghpegun Christ Jesus-kun .
Qamaglluteng Akuzitet Igaqegkat Kiyaghneghem aneghziilqii . Enkaam apeghtughisighqaagut , aghyuughusiighqaagut , nallghusaasighqaagut anaggutelleghmun , apeghtughisighqaagutlu pinitun kiyaghtaalleghqamun .
Enkaam atuqluki Akuzitet Igaqegkat , Kiyaghneghem qepghaghtenga peghqigsaghwaaghngallequq , yataaghqengngallequqlu tamaghhaanun aneghneghqilleghmun .
Christ Jesus tagikumi igleghutinaluni Ataneghpagulleghmini , nanqiglleqii unguvalghiitlu tuqukatlu . Enkaam nagasimanghegkeni Kiyaghneghenkuk Christ Jesus-enkuk , qelghamken
ungipaqiki Pinilghiit Ungipat . Sagiqluten ungipaqiki yugnun nagasugughngaata nalighmeng nagasugunghiteghngaata . Nekeggmelluten apeghtughilleghpegun ugpeghtesnaqiki , ineghtiki anaggutellghitneng , kayemikillu .
Pilleghqaq taginguuq yuget nagasugnanighllequt ipapignun apeghtuusanun . Ivaghillequt piyukegkameggneng apeghtughistelghutneng nagatepigesnaghnaluki nagaqughyukegkaghhiinateng .
Nagasugnanighllequt ipapilleghmun , nagasugyagullequt temnginun ungipaghanun .
Iwernga elpek iiwleng nekeggmelluten , nagneghutigu sangwaa piyaghqan ikfiqngughngaaghpek , ungipaqikestaa Pinilghiineng Ungipaneng . Elpek qepghaghtekegkangaten Kiyaghneghem , apeghiighhu qamaglluku qepghaqaq elpenun pisqegkaa .
Whanga aghqutkesaghqaaghsimaanga Kiyaghneghmun , tuqulleghqaqa kaasaghtuumaaq .
Pilluwaamaaqa pinilghii pilluwalleq , apeghiighaqa kilgaaqulqa , ataasiighmesimanginaqaagunga Ataneghmun .
Enkaam taawa Kiyaghneghem utaqiitngwaa whangamnun qaghpanga elqughutngallghem . Atanghem elqughlluku nanqigtistem akileghtughlleqaanga Nanqigtillghem Aghneghani . Whanganginaagpenanga iwernga akileghtughlleqii qamaglluki tamaakut qelanelghiit tagilleghqaaneng .
Pinaqellghaagken qamagllukek tagiragkiighi whangamnun .
Demas-em piniqsaliisimaa nunam kiyaghtaallgha enkaam unisimaanga , aghulaqumaaq Thessalonica-mun . Crescens Galatia-simaaq enkaam Titus Dalmatia-mun pimaaq .
Luke-nginaghhaq whangamnituq . Mark aqfaluku kelqennaken qayughllak kayutkepigtaqa qepghallemni .
Tychicus Ephesus-mun kayagsimaaqa .
Troas-mellunga unitkaqagka qaasligka Carpus-enkuni . Taginaqegkuvek tagitaghhnakegken . Tagitaghhnaketenllu iimgat iganka , kiyang taakut amiirameng ulimaaghet .
Alexander-em siilumeng sangllaghtem elngaatall seghletun pikaqaanga . Atanghem aghyuughnaaghaa tawaten pillghaneng .
Elpeklu kelengakluku tawaten pinayukangaten qayughllak ungipaghput ugumikepigtaa .
Nanqigtistemun aglaasuwhaaghaqngatnga kitum alngunak mesighaasaghtullghitaanga , yeghlegi uniqaghaatkaqaatnga . Yughaatkaqanka Kiyaghneghmun akinaqefqiita pisqelluki tawaten pillghitneng .
Iwernga Ataneq whangamnitkaaguq . Iknaqusiqaqaangallu ungipaqesqelluki iinguniita Pinilghiit Ungipat qamaglluki Gentile-et nagaqiisqelluki . Enkaam Kiyaghneghem yugulikaqaanga tuqutelleghqameng .
Atanghem yuguliyaghqaqaanga tamaghhaaneng seghleghem sughugallghaneng , enkaam paqnanangunaan aglaalleqaanga qilagmelngughmun Ataneghpagulleghminun . Ellnganun usuqilleq quunperugllak kenlengunaan . Amen .
Ungipaataghhnaketen Priscilla-nkuk Aquila-nkuk , Onesiphorus-enkutlu nengllugutkullghiit suumqaqankanguq .
Erastus unegtekaaguq Corinth-mi ; qinuyugutanganeng Trophimus unitkaqaqa Miletus-mi .
Uksughvagilgan taginaqeghllagi . Eubulus-enkut , Pudens-enkut , Linus-enkut , Claudia-nkut , ilangitallu ugpeqaalgutet ungipaatesqiisi suumqaqiisinguq .
Ataneq taghneghaghpenilli , quyaslisillu .
Ukut latat Paul-meng pinguut qepghaghtenganeng Kiyaghneghem , apostle-nganengllu Jesus Christ-am . Kayagtekaagunga kayusiitesqelluki Kiyaghneghem nakmikegkii yuget ugpelleghtughtaghiisqelluki , liitesqellukullu ipapilleq . Taam ipapillghem kayusighlleqii yuget kiyaghtelleghqiit Kiyaghneghem piyukellghatun .
Taagken ataasimeng ipapilleghmeng sighimallelguukut kenlengilngughmeng unguvalleghmeng . Iqlengiqigatngwaaghem Kiyaghneghem akequsaqegkaqaa taana unguvalleq ima ayumirugllaggaaneng .
Enkaam pilleghqaghlluwaaghmini Kiyaghneghem liitestekaqaa taana kenlengilnguq unguvalleq ungipamikun . Whangamnun neghyukutkaqaa ungipani enkaam ungipaqaqaqa qelghutellghatun Kiyaghneghem Yugulighistemta .
Ukut latat Titus-mun pinguut , ighnepikamken ugpeqillemtegnegun . Kiyaghneghem Atam , Christ Jesus-emllu Yugulighistemta quyaslitenllu nekeggmellelguslitenllu .
Unitkaqamken Crete-mi , apeghiighesqelluku qepghaqaghput apeghiillghilnguq . Nakmiightiisqesugamken Elder-kaghqameng yughaghvignun tamaghhiitni town-et . Neqamikluki qelghutkanka :
Elder-kaghqaq avutngisaghqaaguq ; ataasimeng nuliilguyaghqaaguq , avaqutiillu ugpeqaayaghqaagut ; nelliqneghuyaghqaanghitut , qaatkusigasaghqaanghitutlu .
Igleghutistengutmineng Kiyaghneghem qepghaqaanun , Elder-a avutngisaghqaaguq . Yukeghqenghuyaghqaanghituq , nalighmeng kaatqaghtaamanguyaghqaanghituq , nalighmeng suumestenguyaghqaanghituq , nalighmeng suuglluguyaghqaanghituq , nalighmeng pakigneghuyaghqaanghituq aklungighinaluni .
Itupill upughanghuyaghqaaguq , piniqistekaghqaqaa pinillghem . Nuqenneghtuyaghqaaguq , elqughutngayaghqaaguq , taghneghagmikun pelungisaghqaaguq , nuqetutiyaghqaaguq alngunak seghleghmeng .
Ellnga ataasighmesaghqaaguq ipapignun apeghtuusanun apeghtughallengelleghmitun . Atuqluki ipapiget apeghtuusat kayemelleqii yuget , liigikesleqiillu apeghtughistesighwaaghet anaggutnganiluki .
Uglaapigtut qaatkusugigalnguut , temngi akuzilghiit puughtilghiit ilameggneng , kiyang tamaakunguut apeghtughilghiit Gentile-et ugpeqiit circumcise-eyaghqaaniluki .
Taaqestiki tawaten apeghtughillghitneng . Temngimeng apeghtughilleghmegteggun alngunaseghaghqaqiit iinguniita nengllugutet . Apeghtughiiqut apeghtuusaghqaqenghilkemeggneng ; tawaten piiqut aklungighipigesnaghnaluteng .
Ataasim Crete-eghmiim uuknaliqistem pikaqii , " Crete-eghmiit quunpeng iqlengaghtut , ugighsalghiistun teghikusastun ayuqut , ighsanitalghiinguutlu negheghllaget . "
Tawaten pillgha ipanguuq . Taana apalluqluku qevuulluki aghyuughqi Crete-eghmiit ugpeqiit ugpeqesqelluki ipapiget apeghtuusat .
Ungipaatiki nagannanighlitkinguq Jews-et temngi ungipaghaatangit . Qaatkennanighlitkinguq yuget qelghusangllaqiit . Taakunguut ighsakikat ipapigneng apeghtuusaneng .
Sangwaa qamaglluni pelungituq tamaakunun pelungilngughnun . Iwernga sangwaa qamaglluni pelunginneghituq tamaakunun pelunginneghilngughnun . Kiyaghtengnguut seghleghqelleghmi , ugpeqigataatlu Christ-a . Umyugiitlu sumeghneghitlu nukeggnaghtekaagut , enkaam liigiksaghqaananiimaat pinilleqlu seghlelleqlu .
Liisimakniiqaat Kiyaghneq iwernga kiyaghtaallghita ipapighqaqaat nallukutanga : ugumiknipigtut , qaatkusigatut , sasiinghitutlu sangwaa alngunak pinitun pinaanghitaat .
Iwernga elpek apeghtuusaqiki ugpeqanun ipapiget apeghtuusat .
Apeghtughqi nuyekliit yuget nuqenneghtusqelluki , siivaknalghiinguluki , sumeghtaghayusqelluki , ayepsugitesqelluki ugpeqilleghqun , piniqilleghqun , nuqenneghtulleghqun .
Tawateghpigaq apeghtughqi nuyekliit aghnat kiyaghtesqelluki tuun始ngaluki Kiyaghneghmun . Seghletun akuzitkesaghqaqenghitiit ilateng , nalighmeng megheghllafqiita wine-meng . Apeghtughiyaghqaagut pinitun kiyaghtaalleghqameng ,
enkaam peghqighlleqiit uyuqliit aghnat piniqesqelluki ugingitlu avaqutiitlu .
Sumeghtaghaqegsaghqaagut , pelungisaghqaagut kiyaghtaalleghmeggni , qepghaqegsaghqaagut nemeggni , nangllegtaghyaghqaagut , qaatkusaghqaagut ugimeggnun . Enkaam kitum alngunak seghlequughnaanghitii Kiyaghneghem apeghtuusii .
Tawateghpigaq qeleghqi nukalpigat nuqenneghtusqelluki .
Elpek salleghpegun tamaghhaakun , usputaawi ellngitnun aneghneghqilleghpegun . Apeghtughiiqi ipapighqelluten , piraamsiluten .
Wataghllak apeghtuusaqegkan elqughutngali enkaam kitum alngunak seghlequunghillinkut . Tawaten pikuvek kipullginaaghtet seghletun akuzitkennaanghitiinkut , kipullginaallghitallu kaynguyugtesleqii .
Apeghtughqi qepghaghtelaaghet qaatkesqelluki piliitestengit , efqughtengngwaaghesqellukillu . Veghusnaghyaghqaqenghitiit ,
nalighmeng teglegviksaghqaqenghitiit . Yeghlegi quunpeng pinitun , ataasiighmelluteng piyaghqaqiit . Enkaam salleghmegteggun tamaghhaakun piyuknangllaghlleqiit apeghtuusii Kiyaghneghem Yugulighistemta .
Tawaten kiyaghsaghqaagukut qayughllak Kiyaghneghem aliightekaqaa piniqelleni yugulillengesqelluku yuuk tamaghhaan .
Taam piniqellghem apeghtughiinkut pegtesqelluku kiyaghtaalleq Kiyaghneghmun ayuqenghilnguq , ighsakesqelluki nunam yugan piyukellghi seghleghqengngalghiit . Apeghtughiinkutlu nuqenneghtusqelluta , elqughutngaluta , kiyaghtesqelluta Kiyaghneghem piyukellghatun nunami whani .
Tawaten kiyaghtelta utaqiimaluta quyanalghiimeng sighimalleghmeng . Sighimalqaghput nighughqengngalghii aliilleghqaa Jesus Christ-am Kiyaghneghllamta Yugulighistemta .
Ellmineng tuunegkaaguq yugulinaluta tamaghhaaneng seghleghqelleghmeng . Tawaten pikaaguq qayughllak pelungighsaghyukanginkut ellminun yuguluta , sagiqluta aneghneghqisqelluta yugnun .
Apeghtuusaqiki tamaakut ugpeqanun . Kiyaghneghem qelghusii atuqluki kayemiki , aghuliightikillu seghletun pingukata . Yeqay kitumun alngunak ukavaghtestegpenang .
Neqangughtiki ugpeqat malighqutaqesqelluki kavemem igleghutistengitnun , umiilwaaghnunllu . Qaatkutngayaghqaagut , apeghiighngayaghqaagut tamaghhaanun aneghneghqilleghnun .
Ungipaatiki kina alngunak seghletun akuzitkefqaan , aaghtiiraafqaan pisqelluku . Itupill nekeggmetulluki , qusevegngatulluki pisqelluki tamanganun .
Whangkutallu sivunghani nalluyaghtukut , qaatkusigasaghtukut , puughtengngayaghtukutlu . Yugusimta piyukellgha ayghiilluku , itagnaghqusiqluku ayuqsaghaghput . Unguvalleput kiyaghusiqsaghaput seghlepestaaghmun , aqinalleghmunllu . Yuget ugumiksaghiinkut , ugumikusaghtukutlu .
Iwernga Kiyaghneghem Yugulighistemta liisimakestekaqiinkut nangllegtalleghmineng , piniqelleghminengllu .
Yugulikaqiinkut apalluqluku nangllegtalleni , nakaan aneghneghqillemteggun . Agleghnalghiignekun Taghneghagnekun ughvuqaqii seghleghqelleput , nutaghamengllu unguvallelitkaqiinkut .
Kiyaghneghem kuuvegkaqaak Agleghnalghiik Taghneghak kemnapigllukek whangkunnun Jesus Christ-akun , Yugulighistemteggun .
Kiyaghneq tawaten pikaaguq piniqelleghmikun nallghusaghnaluta elqughutngalleghminun . Enkaam sighimallelguukut whangkuta piliinnaluku kenlengilnguq unguvalleq .
Tamaakut pillghet ipanguut . Tamaakut apeghtuusat elpenun sagiqutesqesuganka yugnun qaatkesqelluki . Taagken ugpellelget Kiyaghneghqun aneghneghqipestaaghllequt . Tamaakut aneghneghqillghet pinilghiinguutlu kayutnguutlu tamanganun .
Iwernga elpek iqitngaluten tamaakuneng temngi qaniqullghiineng , aaghtiiraaghullghiineng sivuneghmeng aatghitneng , Liilightuusanengllu . Tamaana sasiinghituq , kayutngunaanghituq kitumun alngunak .
Kina alngunak aafquutestilghii kelengasaaghnaken ataasimeng nalighmeng alghighluku . Naganneghilkan peggnaken .
Liisimakan tawatelnguum yugem ighsakegkaqaa ipapilleq , seghleghqestenguuqlu . Enkaam ellngan katam seghleghqellghan nanqigsaghqaaghtesleqaa aghyuughyaghqaaluku .
Aglaghtestekumkun Artemas nalighmeng Tychicus elpenun , Nicopolis-ennaqeghllaggaaten , qayughllak uksughsugaqunga tamaani .
Kayusighnaqeghllagnakegken lawyer-a Zenas , Apollos-lu igleghalleghqagkenun . Wataghllak yataaghqunnakegken kelqesaghqameng sameng aklukegkagkeneng .
Ugpeqaalgutemta peghqigsaatkellitgu aneghneghqutkaghqaq enkaam kayusighyaqlegughhnakangit aklukegkapilget . Temngi kiyaghtaafqaameng pilit .
Qamaglluteng whangamnilnguut piniqiisinguq . Piniqelleghput aapqaghnaken ugpeqaalgutemnnun piniqistemnnun . Kiyaghneghem quyaslisi qamagllusi .
Ukut latat Paul-meng pinguut , anusimingllaghaq Christ Jesus apalluqluku , ugpeqaalgutemnnengllu Timothy-meng . Piniqegkamtegnun qepghalgutemtegnun Philemon-mun ,
ugpeqanunllu qerngughutkayugnun mangteghaghpeni , Apphia-munllu nayamnnun Christ-akun , Archippus-munllu pilluwalgutemtegnun .
Kiyaghneghem Atamta , Atanemtallu Jesus Christ-am nanglleklisillu , nekeggmellelguslisillu .
Philemon-mi , quunpeng iyamsiqayugvikaqaqa Kiyaghneqa yughaatkennemken ,
qayughllak nagaqughaqaqa piniqellghen tamaghhiitnun Kiyaghneghem yugitnun , ugpeqillghenllu Ataneghqun Jesus-kun .
Yughaatkaqamken ungipaatesqelluki ilaten ugpeqillemnneng Christ-akun . Tawaten pikuvek liigikataghaghlleqaten qamaglluki quyastellghet allgeghtekaput Christ-akun .
Ugpeqaalgutemni , piniqilleghpek Kiyaghneghem yuganun quyasteghllagaangallu kayemaangallu ! Piniqelleghpek quyastii Kiyaghneghem yugi .
Tetugnaanghitunga qeleghnaluten Christ-akun atuqesqelluku elqughutngalghii , iwernga tawaten pinaanghitunga .
Piniqutelleghpung apalluqluku aapfikamken atuqesqelluku elqughutngalghii . Whanga , Paul , nanevgaagunga , anusimingllaghaagungallu apalluqluku Christ Jesus .
Whanganguuq aaputilghii ighnemnun , Onesimus-mun . Anusimingllaghvigmi ataliitkaqaanga Christ-akun .
Sivunghani sasiinghisaghtuq elpenun , iwernga whaa kayutngughtepigsimaaq whangkutegnun .
Onesimus elpenun aglaghtesnaqaqa , leganqun iluka maligunnaquq ellngakun .
Whangamnitesuguyaghaqa kayusiitesqellunga anusimingllaghvigmi , katam elpek kayusiinnayaqevnga maansaquvek . Liisimakegkenqun anusimingllaghaalghiinga Pinilghiit Ungipat apalluqluki .
Iwernga whangamnitesnaanghitaqa wetkuqun sivukluten aaptaghlluten . Itagnaqumakuvgu whangamnitesqelluku taawa elpek piyukelqelleqan , qayughllak qelghunghitamken tawaten pisqelluten .
Entaqun Onesimus iqitaghtekaaguq elpenisaghqaaluni quunperugllak .
Ellnga paninang qepghaghtelaaghuuq . Iwernga qepghaghtelaaghumalleghmineng angliighataghaamaaq qayughllak piniqegkaaghsimaaq ugpeqaalguta . Piniqepigtaqa , iwernga elpek piniqataghaghlleqan qepghaghtelaaghuluku , ugpeqaalgutngulukullu Ataneghqun .
Enkaangam tugukliimakuvnga qepghalgutngulunga , tuguklighnaken Onesimus whangangusluku .
Sameng seghletun pimakangaten nalighmeng asengemakangaten , asengenga whanga llivikelleqaqa .
Whaa , whanga katam iiggemneng igaghtunga whaten : whanga , Paul , llivikelleqamken . Iwernga puygugpenaan unguvallghen asengeluku ayuqan whangamnun .
Aa-a , ugpeqaalgutemni , aapfikamken Ataneghqun tugukliisqelluku Onesimus . Tawaten pikuvek quyasleqaghpenga Christ-akun !
Lataamken liisimakngwaaghluku qaatkesaghqaqan qelghutkaqa elpenun , repall qaayghulluku pillequten .
Atwhay , nekaghqangllaataghhnakevnga qayughllak sighimanguunga Kiyaghneghem kiimsighlleqii yughallesi , enkaam elpesinun pillequnga .
Epaphras-emnguq piniqiisi ; anusimingllaghalgutkaqa apalluqluku Christ Jesus .
Qepghalgutmallu Mark-enkut , Aristarchus-enkut , Demas-enkut , Luke-enkut ellngitallunguq piniqiisi .
Piniqellgha Atanghem Jesus Christ-am tamaghhaghpesinilli .
Sivunghani agani uglaghlukullu , allaaghhiinaalukullu Kiyaghneghem aleghquqaqii sivuneput uuknaliqistetgun .
Iwernga ukuni kingulighni aghneghni aleghquqaqiinkut Ighneghmikun . Ellngakun Kiyaghneq nunangllaqaaguq , nakmikegkaqaallu piliitesqelluku sangwaa tamaghhaan .
Ighneghem kuukgutaqaa Kiyaghneghem nighughqellgha , Kiyaghneghtungwaaqlu ayuquq . Sangwaat qamaglluki nagneghastengngwii tawatelluki aghtughyaghqaanghilnguutgun akuzitmikun . Ighneghem tuunegkaqaa ellmi katam unguvalleni ukmangighnaluta tamaghhaaneng seghleghqellemnneng . Apeghiighyamigu tawaten pilleni , qilagmi aqumegkaaguq aghenqigneghakun Kiyaghneghem , aghtughyaghqaanghitelleghpigaam .
Kiyaghneghem quliightekaqaa Ighneq yaqulegneng , atelitkaqaallu ingyaatngalghiimeng aatghitneng .
Tawaten pikaqaa qayughllak Kiyaghneghem pimangitii nalighhiiniit yaqulget whaten , " Ighneqamken ; aghneghmi Ataliitaghpenga . " Kiyaghneghemllu pimangitii nalighhiiniit yaqulget whaten , " Atakelleqaanga enkaam ellnga Ighneqelleqaqa . "
Kiyaghneghem kayagsaghqaaghsamigu Ighneqsuwhaani nunamun , whatenllu pikaaguq , " Yeqay qamaglluteng Kiyaghneghem yaqulgita manigughlitgu . "
Whatenllu pikaaguq yaqulegneng , " Kiyaghneghem yaquleni anuqestun lliightestekaqii . Qepghaghtengi kumaghulghiistun kenghestun lliightestekaqii . "
Iwernga Kiyaghneq Ighneghmineng whaten pikaaguq , " Kaay Kiyaghneq , aqumutagken kenlengisaghqaaguk quunperugllak ! Igleghulleqan ataneghpagullghen elqughutngallelighluku .
Piniqan elqughutngalleq , ugumikan anaggutngalleq . Tamaaken apalluqluku Kiyaghneq , Kiyaghneghpek nakmikumaatenllu quulvaamaatenllu pakiggulluku ilagpeneng . Enkaangam quyastighllagtuq anoint-eluten mesiighmeng . "
Whatenllu pikaaguq , " Elpek , Ataneq , piinlighyuggaaghmi nunangllaqaaguten , iiggegpenengllu qilagangllaqaaguten .
Qamaglluteng aviighusaghqaagut , iwernga elpek kiyaghsaghqaaguten . Aghyughyaghqaagut aatkastun .
Imegteghlleqaten qaasligetun , simighlleqatenllu aatkastun . Iwernga elpek quunpeng almesiqelleqaaten , aghyughyaghqaanghitutenllu . "
Kiyaghneghem pimangitngwaaghii nalighhiiniit yaquleni whaten : " Aqumi whagun aghenqignemkun , kenlanga anguyagten tunemaliitestellemnun itegaghpek asinganun . "
Sangaawan始ngam yaqulget ? Qamaglluteng taghneghaagut qepghaatilghiit Kiyaghneghmeng , kayagtaqiillu kayusiitesqelluki tamaakut yugulillengyaghqat .
Tamaaken apalluqluku sumeghtaghaatkengngwaaghelteki ipapillghet nagaquqaput luuraq waaknaniqestaghnayukamteki .
Kiyaghneghem apeghtuusii ipanguut ; aapqaqii yugnun yaqulegteggun . Kina alngunak qaatkunneghilnguq apeghtuusanun , Kiyaghneghem aghyuughlleqaa aghyuulleghqaghtutalangatun .
Enkaam ighsakumakumteggu Kiyaghneghem yugulighilleghllaga anagpagningitaghput aghyuughilleghqaa . Atanghem apeghyuggaaqaqaa taana yugulilleq . Taagken tamaakut nagaquutkat ellnganeng , ipapighqaat whangkunnun .
Kiyaghneghemllu ipapighqegkaqaa whangkunnun . Tawaten pikaaguq atuqelleghmikun allaaghhiinaat allaaghlluwhaghtillghet , uyegtelleghmikunllu tunusii Agleghnalghiim Taghnegham piyukelleghmitun .
Kiyaghneghem nakmikellghitii yaqulget igleghutisqelluki sivumelngughmun nunakaghqamun . ( Taananguuq nuna akuzitkegkefut . )
Nalighneghitni Akuzitni Igaqegkani whaten igaqngaaq , " Kiyaghneq , sangaawa yuuk umyugaghmikaqegken , nalighmeng ighnegha yugem aflengakegkan ?
Ulimaaqan ukavaqaanlluku yaqulegneng , qaghpaliqaqan nighughqelleghmengllu quulvalleghmengllu ,
igleghutistengllaqaqanllu samun tamaghhaanun . " Tawanillu Akuzitni Igaqegkani igaqngaaq , Kiyaghneghem ulimaaqaa yuuk " igleghutistenguluku samun tamaghhaanun . " Taana whaten pisiiguq sangwaa qamaglluni ilatngaaq igleghutillghanun . Naqamllu salin esghiigataghput yuuk igleghutilghii samun tamaghhaanun .
Iwernga esghaghaghput Jesus ! Kiyaghneghem natengiighhaq ukavaghtestekaqsaghaa yaqulegneng . Maaten esghaghaghput qaghpaluni nighughqelleghmengllu quulvalleghmengllu qayughllak ikfiqluni tuqukaaguq . Kiyaghneghem piniqellgha apalluqluku , Jesus tuqukaaguq tamaghhaanun .
Kiyaghneghuuq ulimaghikaq sameng tamaghhaaneng ellminun , nagneghastengngwiillu tawatelluki . Itagnapigtekaaguq Kiyaghneghem pinighsaghwaaqaqaa Jesus ikfiqelleghqun piinlightenguluku yugulillghitnun . Enkaam Jesus-em tagisaghqaaghtekaqii yulghutet nighughqelleghmun .
Jesus-em pelungighsaqaqii yuget seghleghqellghitneng . Enkaam ellngallu tamaakutlu pelungighsaqii , qamaglluteng Atakaat Kiyaghneq . Tamaaken apalluqluku Jesus-em kayngukigatii atighyaghqaaluki anglegutnguluki .
Jesus-em pikaqaa Kiyaghneq , " Apeghlleqaqa aatghen anglegutemnun ; usuqelleqamken qerngughutkata . "
Whatenllu pikaaguq , " Neghyukelleqaqa Kiyaghneq . " Pikaaguqlu , " Whaantunga , taghnughhaatlu Kiyaghneghem tagivaqii whangamnun . "
Taakut taghnughhaat yuguut kemekralgetlu aalguutlu , enkaam Jesus ellngistun lliiqaaguq . Tawaten pikaaguq tuqunaluni naafqennaluku Tughneghaq , aghtughyaghqaanghillelek tuqumun .
Enkaam tawaten pilleghmikun itemutkaqii tamaakut qepghaghtelaaghestun ayuqelghiit unguvalleteng qamaglluki qayughllak alikngukangat tuqulleq .
Whateghllugaaghuuq yaqulgunghitut Jesus-em kayusiqii , iwernga Abraham-em kingunghi kayusighaqii .
Tamaaken apalluqluku Kiyaghneghem Jesus lliightestengngwaaghyaghqaqaa whangkutestun . Tawaten qepghaasaqlegwaa Kiyaghneq High Priest-nguluni , nangllegtaghlunillu ataasiighmellunillu . Enkaam tuuniyaqlegughtekaaguq aghqutmeng Kiyaghneghmun seghevutesqelluki yuget seghleghqellghit .
Jesus ikfiqegkaatminengllu nanghiiqullengegkaatminengllu , kayusighyaqlegwii tamaakut nanghiiqullengelghiit .
Enkaangam ugpeqaalgutemni , Kiyaghneghem aaftekaqiisi ellminun yugulusi , tuqluqaqiisillu ellminitesqellusi qilagmi . Sumeghmikluku Jesus . Kiyaghneghem kayagtekaa Apostle-ngulukullu High Priest-ngulukullu aapghaqegkefut ugpeqniluku .
Jesus ataasighmetkaaguq Kiyaghneghmun nakmikisteminun , katam Moses ataasighmetkaq Kiyaghneghmun qepghaataqngamigu Kiyaghneq mangteghaani .
Tamaghhaghmi mangteghaq kitumeng ulimaghistelgulghii , iwernga Kiyaghneghem Jesus-kun sangwaa tamaghhaan ulimaaqaa . Yuget usuqataghaghyaghqaqaat Jesus pakiggulluku Moses-meng , qayughllak yuget usuqelleqaat mangteghangllaghta pakiggulluku mangteghameng .
Moses ataasiighmetkaaguq qepghaghta Kiyaghneghem mangteghaani , ungipaatkaqiillu yuget Kiyaghneq sameng apeghyaghqalguniluku taaganiqaaghaq .
Iwernga Christ-a ighneghuluni ataasiighmetkaaguq igleghutista Kiyaghneghem mangteghaani . Whangkuta mangteghaqiinkut Kiyaghneghem , ilutumanginaqumta , ipapighqutkumanginaqumteggullu sighimakegkaghput .
Enkaangam katam tawaten Agleghnalghiik Taghneghak piik , " Aghneghmi whani nagaququfsigu Kiyaghneghem menga ,
pineghlliqegpenasi sivuneghpesistun . Tamaani aghneghni kilgaanilluteng qaatkesugumangitaat Kiyaghneq , nanghiighsaghaqaqaatlu nuqenneghtullgha . "
Kiyaghneq piiq , " Tamaani 40 ayumiqulleghni sivuneghpesi esghaqaqeghngaaghmegteki apeghiiqanka , paninang nanghiighsaghaqaqaatnga .
Tamaaken apalluqluku tamaakut yuget sakritestekaqaatnga . Enkaam pikaagunga , ' Iiwleng ataasiighmesigatut whangamnun , liigikigatutlu natelluku kiyaghtesqesullemneng .
Sakritngulunga akeqikaagunga allangughsaghqaanghilngughmeng . ' Whaten piinga , ' Iteghnaanghitngwaaghaat meghnaalivigkaq yataaghqegkaqa ellngitnun . ' "
Ugpeqaalgutemni kelengalusi , seghleghmeng sumeghtaghalleghnengllu ugpenghitelleghnengllu , iqitutestegpenasi unguvalghiimeng Kiyaghneghmeng .
Iwernga aghhutanga tamaghhaan kayemutaqitek pilleghqalgumaluku atilqelghiimeng " Aghneghmi . " Tawaten pinghilkufsi taawa seghleghqellghem puughllusi pineghllungllaghlleqiisi .
Iwernga ataasiighmelkumta unguvallemta kenlenganun , neghyukluku Kiyaghneq ugpeghyuwhaallemtestun , taawa Christ-am pilgutkelleqiinkut ellmi pimineng .
Akuzitni Igaqegkani igaqngaaq , " Aghneghmi nagaququfsigu Kiyaghneghem menga , pineghllugugpenasi sivuneghpesistun qaatkusimangilnguut Kiyaghneghmun . "
Kinkungaawat nagaquutkat Kiyaghneghem menganeng naqam qaatkutegpenateng ? Tamaakunguut yuget Moses-em maghyaghquqii Egypt-meng .
40 ayumiqulleghni kinkut Kiyaghneq sakritestatgu ? Tamaakunguut seghleghqelluteng tuqulaghaatkat kilgaani .
Kinkunun Kiyaghneq akeqikaawa iteghnaanghitngwaaghniluki meghnaalivigkamun yataaghqegkaminun ? Akeqegkaqii qaatkusimangilnguut ellminun .
Taawa liigikaghput iteghpagningitkaagut tawavek meghnaalivigmun qayughllak ugpeqenghilkangat .
Kiyaghneghem akequsaa yugnun aghuliituq iitghesqelluki meghnaalivigminun . Iwernga alingelta luuraq nalighsi nuughhunnayukan iteghpenani meghnaaliviganun .
Pinilghii ungipaq Kiyaghneghem meghnaaliviganeng ayuqelghii nagaquqaqaghput katam tamaakustun yugestun Moses-em maghyaghquqiistun Egypt-meng . Iwernga pinilghiim ungipam kayusiitellghitii qayughllak ugpequmangitaat nagaquqaghteng .
Whangkuta ugpelghiini iteghllequkut Kiyaghneghem meghnaaliviganun . Iwernga Kiyaghneghem akuzitkegkaqii ugpeqillghilnguut whaten , " Sakritngulunga akeqikaagunga allangughsaghqaanghilngughmeng . Whaten piinga , ' Iteghnaanghitngwaaghtut meghnaalivigkamnun . ' " Tawaten akuzikaaguq qepghaqani apeghiiqaqeghngaaghmiki ima nunangllalleghmineng .
Naantuq Akuzitni Igaqegkani igaqluni maaghraghvinliitanga aghneghem whaten , " Kiyaghneq meghnaalikaaguq tamaaghhaaneng qepghaqamineng maaghraghvinliitangani aghneghem . "
Akuzitnillu Igaqegkani Kiyaghneq pikaaguq , " Iteghnaanghitngwaaghtut meghnaalivigkamnun . "
Paninang ilangi yuget iteghllequt Kiyaghneghem meghnaaliviganun . Iwernga nagaquusuwhaaqat pinilghiimeng ungipameng , itellghitut meghnaalivigmun qayughllak qaatkutellghilnguut Kiyaghneghmun .
Tamaaken apalluqluku Kiyaghneghem nekegtekaqaa ilanga aghneq , atilqelghii " Aghneghmi . " Kingurugllaganeng Moses-em , Kiyaghneghem akuzitkegkaqaa taana aghneq David-kun . Uteghpagtanka David-em igaqegkii Akuzitni Igaqegkani whaten , " Aghneghmi whani nagaququfsigu Kiyaghneghem menga , pineghlliqegpenasi sivuneghpesistun . "
Joshua-m maghyaghqullghitii yuget tawavek meghnaalivigmun . Liisimakaghput qayughllak taam kingunganeng Kiyaghneghem akuzitkegkaqaa ilanga aghnegha meghnaalillghem .
Tamaaken apalluqluku taawa Sabbath-a aghuliituq , meghnaalivik Kiyaghneghem yugitnun .
Kina alngunak iitqumi Kiyaghneghem meghnaaliviganun , meghnaalillequq qepghaqamineng katam tawaten Kiyaghneghem meghnaalillghatun .
Tamaaken apalluqluku iteghnaqeghllagelta Kiyaghneghem meghnaaliviganun . Qaatkenghitefqaan pilteggu Kiyaghneq sivunemta pillghistun .
Akuzitangi Kiyaghneghem unguvaat qepghaagut . Iipgataghaghtut alngunak inglugtun ipegsaqaneng savigpagneng . Kaaputkayuguut qamaverugllak unguvasimllu taghneghamllu kaatutngallghegkenun , naflutlu paatghetlu kaatutngallghitnun . Kiyaghneghem akuzitangi nanqigtikayuguut yugem sumeghtaghallghanengllu sanaqellghanengllu .
Sangwaa qamagtengngwaaghluni Kiyaghneghem ulimaagha iighnganghituq Kiyaghneghmeng . Aliitut , whateghlluwaaghuutlu iyegkeni . Ellnganun qayvighqesaghqaqaput salleput qamaglluki .
Tamaaken apalluqluku High Priest-elegllaguukut qilagmun mayuqameng . Jesus-nguuq , Ighnegha Kiyaghneghem . Enkaam ugpeqilleghmetekestaalta aapqamnni yugnun .
High Priest-emta liigikngwaaqaqii kayaalliqusiput , qayughllak nunamelluni nanghiiqullengegkaaguq whangkutestungwaaq . Naqamllu seghleghqumangituq .
Enkaam tetullngunaamta aglaalta umiilgusignun aqumutagkenun Kiyaghneghem , allgeghuseghqaaluta nangllegtallghanun . Tawani nangllekelleqiinkut , kayusighlleqiinkutlu aklukillemnni .
Tamaghhaan high priest-a Kiyaghneghem nakmikegkaqaa yulgutanganeng . Kiyaghneghmun aglaghaquq yuget apalluqluki tuunaluki tunusiit aghqerraaghunnalukillu seghleghqellghitnun .
High priest-a kayaalliqegkayugutmineng nangllegtaghyaghqaaguq tamaakunun nallukelghiinunllu ugpeqinanilghiinunllu ipapilleghmun .
Qayughllak kayaalliqegkayugutmineng , high priest-a aghqerraaghyaghqaaguq ellmi katam seghleghqelleghminun , seghleghqellghitnunllu yuget .
Kina alngunak nakmikigatuq ellmineng high priest-ngughhnaluni quulvaghyaghqaaluni . Iwernga yuuk high priest-ngughtaquq Kiyaghneghem nakmikenghatni , katam tawaten nakmikellghatun Aaron .
Tawatenllu Christ-a quulvallghituq ellmineng nakmikluni high priest-ngughtelleghmun , iwernga Kiyaghneghem nakmikegkaqaa . Pikaqaa , " Ighneqamken ; aghneghmi whani Ataliitaghpenga . "
Nalighneghitni Akuzitni Igaqegkani Kiyaghneghem pikaqaa , " Priest-ngullequten quunperugllak , Melchizedek-em priest-ngullghatun . "
Kiyaghneq aghtughyaghqaanghillelguuq yuguliyaghqaaluku Jesus tuqulleghmeng . Enkaam Jesus nunametnguluni , iglagtuluni qunituumaghmi yughaqaalghiillu tungsiqaalghiillu Kiyaghneghmun yugulisqelluni tuqulleghmeng . Kiyaghneghem nagatkaqii yughallghi , qayughllak quseveglluni qaatkegkaa Kiyaghneghem piyukellgha .
Qaywa Jesus Kiyaghneghem Ighneqeghngaatni , paninang liitkaaguq qaatkusimalleghmeng ikfiqelleghmikun .
Apeghiighyagu qamaglluku Kiyaghneghem pisqellgha , Jesus-ngughtuq kenlengilngughmeng yugulillengestiyaghqaq tamaghhaanun qaatkullghiinun ellminun .
Enkaam Kiyaghneghem nakmikegkaqaa high priest-nguluku , Melchizedek-em high priest-ngullghatun .
Apeghyaghqaghllaguukut tamaakuneng . Iwernga apeghtuneghllupigtusi tamaakuneng qayughllak liigikaghaghsigalnguusi .
Neghipigllusi ugpeqaalghiisi enkaam apeghtughiyaghqaaghtekaagusi ilagpesinun . Yeghlegi paninang aklaaqusi kitumun apeghtunqigtesqellusi ugpenghhat liisuwhaaghyaghqiitneng Kiyaghneghem akuzitanganeng . Katam taghnughhaghhaghestun mamaghtughyugaqusi , neqepigyugpenasi .
Kina alngunak mamaghtuqayuk paninang taghnughhaghhaaguq . Salin nallukaa elqughutngalleqlu anaggutngalleqlu .
Iwernga neqepik angtaniitkanun pinguuq . Peghqigsaqaagut liigiksaghqaalukek pinilghiinkuk , seghleghenkuk .
Enkaam liitelteki apeghtuusat angtaniitkanun ugpeqanun ayuqelghiit . Liitngwaaqaqasi apeghtuusuwhaaqat Christ-ameng ayuqelghiit enkaangam liinneqigsaghqaqenghitasi . Liitngwaaghumaasi atuqsaghqaafqiita pinaluki tamaakut tuqumun ayuqelghiit . Liinneqigsaghqaqenghitaghsillu ugpeqilleghmeng ayuqelghii Kiyaghneghqun ,
paaptaayelleghneng , iigtilleghneng , unguvaghtilleghneng tuqukaneng , Kiyaghneghemllu nanqigtilleghqaaneng yugneng aghyuughyaghqaaluki kenlengunaan .
Kiyaghneghem pistekanginkut , apeghtughlleqamsi angtaniitesqellusi ugpeqat .
Tamaa ilanganeng yulguuq allgeghutkaayalghiineng Kiyaghneghem nighuganeng , naasiiqaqaatlu qilagem tunusaa . Allgeghutkaagutlu Agleghnalghiigneng Taghneghagneng . Nanghiiqaqiit pinightulangi Kiyaghneghem akuzitangi , nanghiiqaqaatlu Kiyaghneghem aghtughyaghqaanghillgha nunakaghqamelnguq . Taagken ugpeqnaniqumegteggu Christ-a , avuteghqenqigtepagningiillequt qayughllak qaquuranqigtekangat Kiyaghneghem Ighnegha , kayngusaakegkangatlu yugtuqami .
Nuna meghaquq eslallugughnneghani , piitestiiquqlu nunivagseghameng atughqameng tamaakunun peksighqikanun nunameng . Enkaam Kiyaghneghem pinighqestaqaa nuna .
Iwernga nuna piitestimakumi sikughllugnengllu weeds-nengllu satngunghituq . Yakughnaanituq Kiyaghneghem seghleghunilleghqaaneng , enkaam paneghsaghqaaguq .
Piniqegkamnni , qaywa elpesinun latatkeghngaamteki tamaakut , sumeghtaghaatkigatamsi tawatellusi . Liisimakaghput pinighataghalghiimeng quyastellelguusi yugulilleghpesigun .
Kiyaghneq elqughutngaan nanqigtiiquq , enkaam puygunaanghitaa qepghalleghsillu , piniqilleghsillu ellminun kayusiitelleghpesigun yugi . Neqamikelleqaallu paninang kayusiitngukesi .
Nagneghtesugamsi sagiqlusi qepghaatesqelluku Kiyaghneq unguvalleghpesi tagtalngatun . Enkaam allgeghtepestaaghlleqaghsi sighimakegkaghsi .
