Ighsanitalghiingughtesunghitamsi . Yeghlegi tamaakustun ayuqestesugamsi ugpeqilleghmegteggun , nuqetutilleghmegteggunllu allgeghusaghqat Kiyaghneghem akequsaqegkaaneng .
Kiyaghneghem akeqaqngamigu Abraham , akeqegkaqaa piyaghqapestaaghuniluku . Avangitutanganeng aangataghalghiimeng ellmineng , atuqluku ellmi katam ateni akeqikaaguq .
Abraham pikaqaa , " Quyastepestaaghluten , uglaapiglluku kingunelilleqamken . "
Abraham qelaneghpenani utaqiikaaguq , enkaam allgeghtekaqaa Kiyaghneghem akequsaa .
Kitum neklegsuneghminigu aaghtiiraaghutelleq , akeqiiquq sameng pilleni ipanguniluku atuqluku kitum aatgha ellmineng aangataghalghiim .
Allgeghusaghqat akequsamineng , Kiyaghneghem liigikestesugwii allaangughsaghqaqenghitngwaaghniluki agghilleni . Enkaam akeqikaaguq atuqluku ateni .
Kiyaghneghem tawaten kayemiinkut . Kiyaghneq iqlengiqigatuq akeqineghmini , iqlengiqnaanghituqlu akeqikumi atuqluku ateni ipapighqennaluku piyaghqaqutni . Taakuk allangughteqaghhnaanghituk . Whangkuta anagniiqani Kiyaghneghmun paqniinnaluta , kayemellengeghllagtukut sighimaknaluku Kiyaghneghem akequsaa .
Taana sighimalleq uyghiitnguuq unguvasimnnun , paqnaniighutestiinkutlu ayepsugitestiinkutlu . Taana sighimalleq iteghtuq agleghnalleghpigaghmun nemun safkaaghutem awatanganilngughmun .
Tawavek Jesus iitqaaguq sivumnni whangkuta apalluqluta . High Priest-ngughtekaaguq quunperugllagmun , Melchizedek-em priest-ngumallghatun .
Taana Melchizedek umiilkesaghaa Salem-em , priest-ekaallu Qulighpigaam Kiyaghneghem . Abraham uteghniimaluku pilluwameng kayaalqughluki umiilget , Melchizedek-em nallaghluku quyastekaqaa .
Taagken Abraham-em tuunegkaa qulaghqellghaneng sameng tamaghhaaneng tugukamineng pilluwami . Melchizedek-em aatgha maalghugegneng sameng pisilguuq , sivuliq whaten pisiiguq , " Umiilga Elqughutngallghem . " Umiilkegkaatanganeng Salem-em , aatghan aallgha whaten pisiiguq , " Umiilga Nekeggmellghem . "
Igiituq igaqfikegkameng Melchizedek-em atanganengllu naanganengllu nalighmeng sivunghaneng , talwa allgellghanengllu tuqullghanengllu . Kiyaghneghem Ighneghatun aghuliituq priest-nguluni quunperugllak .
Taawa liigikaghsi Melchizedek-em aangumalleghllaga . Talwa sivuneqsuwhaamta Abraham-em tuunegkaa Melchizedek qulaghqellghaneng tugulaqamineng pilluwami .
Priest-et kingunqii Levi-em . Liilightuusani , Kiyaghneghem qelqaqii priest-et qerngughtisqelluki yulgutangitneng qulaghqelleghmeng allgeghtekiitneng . Priest-et tawaten piiqut , priest-etlu yugetlu Abraham-em kingunqeghngiisteng .
Melchizedek kingunqenghitaa Levi-em , iwernga tugukliqaqaa qulaghqelleq Abraham-em tuunyagu . Quyastekaqaallu Abraham , allgeghutkaalghii Kiyaghneghem akequsaaneng .
Nalluneqniituq taana quyastilghii aangataghaghtuq taagken quyastekameng .
Priest-et yuguut tuqukayuget naqamllu allgeghutkaagut qulaghqelleghmeng . Melchizedek-llu allgeghutkaaguq qulaghqelleghmeng , iwernga kiyaghtengnguuq , Akuzitet Igaqegkat apellghistun .
Levi allgeghutkaaguq yugneng qulaghqelleghmeng . Pinayalghiikut talwa ellngallu llivikikaaguq qulaghqelleghmeng Melchizedek-mun Abraham-kun .
Qaywa Levi allgellghiteghngaaghmi , sivuneghmi Abraham-em yugusiinitkaaguq Melchizedek-em nallaghaqngagu Abraham .
Liilightuusani igaqngaaq priest-et kingunqesaghqaqii Levi-em . Ellngita Liilightuusat apeghtuutkaqiit yugnun , iwernga qepghaqaat Kiyaghneghmun nuughhutkaaguq . Tamaaken apalluqluku yuget aklukaagut priest-meng Melchizedek-etun ayuqelghiimeng , Aaron-etun ayuqenghilnguq .
Levite priest-et simineghmegteki allaneng priest-eneng , taawa Liilightuusatlu allangughsaghqaagut .
Priest-et quunpeng Levi-em ramkenganeng pinguut , iwernga Ataneghput ramkenganeng pingunghituq . Kina alngunak Atanemta ramkenganeng pi qepghiigatngwaaghtuq priest-nguluni aghqefigegni .
Tamaghhaghmi liisimakaat Ataneghput allgeqaaguq ramkenganun Judah-m . Moses-em pimangitii kingunghi Judah-m priest-nguyaghqaaniluki .
Enkaam tamaakut liigikataghaghaput whateglluwaaq qayughllak ilanga priest-em Melchizedek-etun ayuqelghii tagimaaq .
Liilightuusat qelghutkaqaat priest-a kingunqesaghqaqniluku Levi-mun . Ataneghput priest-ngughtekaanghituq Liilightuusat pisqellghitgun , iwernga priest-ngughtekaaguq aghtughyaghqaanghilngughqun unguvalleghmikun kenletghuusaghqaanghilngughqun .
Akuzitet Igaqegkat pikaalghiit , " Priest-nguuten quunperugllak , Melchizedek-em priest-ngullghatun . "
Tamaaken apalluqluku Kiyaghneghem simiqaqaa Liilightuusaq priest-eneng ayuqelghii qayughllak kayaalnguqlu atuunghilnguqlu .
Liilightuusat kina alngunak pistesimangitaa Kiyaghneghem piyukellghatun . Enkaam Kiyaghneghem tuunumiinkut pinighataghalghiimeng sighimalleghmeng . Taaggun sighimalleghqun aglaghyaghqaaghtukut Kiyaghneghmun .
Taam sighimallghem saaghwakun Kiyaghneq allangughhnaanghilngughmeng akeqimaaq .
Iwernga tawatelngughmeng akeqillghituq Levi-em kingunghi priest-ngughtaqngata . Jesus-nginaghmun whaten pikaaguq , " Ataneq akeqimaaq , allangughhnaanghitaaklu umyugagni ; ' Elpek priest-nguuten quunperugllak . ' "
Tamaaken apalluqluku Jesus-nguuq ipapighqelleq Kiyaghneghem akequsani pipestaaghlleqaa . Taana akequsaq pinighataghaghtuq akequsaqegkamineng Moses-kun .
Sivunghani priest-etuyaghtuq . Tuqunghata ilangita priest-et nagneghutaqaat qepghaqaat .
Iwernga Jesus priest-nguuq quunperugllak qayughllak unguvallequq quunpeng .
Tamaaken apalluqluku Jesus-em iiwleng yuguliyaqlegwii Kiyaghneghmun aglalghiit ellmikun , qayughllak quunpeng unguvanguuq maniguutunnaluki tamaakut Kiyaghneghmun .
Jesus High Priest-nguuq tuunikayuk sameng aklukegkamnneng . Agleghnaghtuq , avutngituq , pelungituq , aaftengngaaq seghleghqesteneng , Kiyaghneghem quulvaqaqaa qulighpigaghmun qilagmun .
Jesus ilangistun high priest-estun ayuqenghituq . Aghhutanga tamaghhaan high priest-a aghqerraaghyaghqaaguq , sivukluni ellmi seghleghqelleghminun , taagken yuget seghleghqellghitnun . Jesus tuunaqngami ellmineng katam , aghqutkegkaaguq seghleghqellghitnun yuget , ataasighhaghmeng .
Liilightuusani igaqngaaq yuget nakmiighyaghqaaniluki high priest-ekaghqameng seghleghqegkayugughngaan alngunak yugestun . Kingunganeng Kiyaghneghem apellghan Liilightuusat Moses-mun , tagtalmi taakwani allangughsaghqaanghilngughmeng akeqikaaguq . Taaggun akeqilleghqun Kiyaghneghem Ighneni High Priest-ngughtestekaqaa , afkuyangunaan , quunperugllak .
Aapqaghput elpesinun , whaten pisiiguq : tawatelngughmeng high priest-elguukut aqumgalghii aghenqigneghani saaghwakun Aghtughyaghqaanghitelleghpigaam qilagmi .
Qepghaatinguuq high priest-nguluni sanctuary-mi . Taana tabernacle-epiguuq Atanghem nekeftekaqaa , yugem nekeftekaqenghitaa .
Tamaghhaghmi high priest-a nakmikegkaaguq tuunisqelluku tunusaneng , teghikusanengllu aghqerraaghesqelluku Kiyaghneghmun . Enkaam High priest-evutlu sameng tuunyaghqalguyaghqaaguq Kiyaghneghmun .
Jesus nunamesaqumi priest-ngunayanghituq , qayughllak priest-elguuq nunami tuunikayugneng tunusaneng Kiyaghneghmun Liilightuusat pisqellghistun .
Priest-et qepghaqaagut sanctuary-mi , qilagmelngughtun ayuqesugnilngughmi . Salin Moses-em tabernacle-a nekeftellghilluku , Kiyaghneghem apaqutkaqaa , " Wataghllak sangwaa qamaglluku ulimanaken tawatengwaaq uspeqellemtun kelgutkamtun elpenun naayghami . "
Kiyaghneghem Jesus qepghaqalitkaqaa priest-nguluku . Qepghaqaa megnunaghataghaghtuq Levite-et priest-et qepghallghitneng . Tawateghpigaq akequsaghraghaq pinighataghalghiinguuq akequsalugmeng qayughllak taaggun Jesus-em ilaliighutestekaqii Kiyaghneqlu yugetlu . Pinighataghaghtuq qayughllak tunemiitngaaq akequsatgun pinighataghalghiitgun .
Sivuliq akequsaq afkuyiisaqan , taawa tuungliinnayaghtuq .
Iwernga Kiyaghneghem afkuyalgunikaqii yuni whaten piiqngami , " Aghneghet kaallequt , piiq Ataneq , akequsaghraghaq pilleqaqa Israel-eghmiinunllu Judah-ghmiinunllu .
Akequsaghraghaqa tawatennaanghituq akequsaqegkamtun sivunghitnun tasluqluki aghulaqutaqngamki Egypt-meng . Qaatkusimangitut akequsama pisqellghatun . Enkaam avelghaqiinaqaqanka , piiq Ataneq .
Aghneghet taakut kingungitneng una akequsaghraghaq pilleqaqa Israel-eghmiinun , piiq Ataneq : Liilightuusanka umyugiitnun kanaghlleqanka , igaqelleqankallu qamagun ilungitgun . Kiyaghneqelleqaatnga , ellngit yukelleqanka .
Nalighhiiniita apeghtughyaghqaqenghitaa nunalgutni , nalighmeng nengllugutni liitesqelluku Ataneq , qayughllak qamaglluteng liisimakelleqaatnga , ukalighpigaghhaghneng pingwaaghllagnun .
Seghevulleqanka anaggutellghit , allamengllu neqamiknaanghitanka seghleghqellghit . "
Kiyaghneghem akuzitkaqngamigu akequsaghraghaq , sivuliq akequsaq atuunanightestekaqaa . Enkaam sangwaa alngunak atuunanighluni aghyughluni mulugpenani aviighullequq .
Akequsaqsuwhaaghmini Kiyaghneghem igaqegkaqii qelghusat naten maniguutelleghqameng ellminun , natenllu nekeftelleghqaa sanctuary nunami .
Taana sanctuary yuget ulimakaat tiintanguftuq maalghugegneng nelek . Sivuliim nem aatqeftaa Agleghnalghii Na . Ilunganiteftut kenelghutalghutak , tipelek neqekrangllalgek tuunegkameng Kiyaghneghmun .
Awalighneghani tuunglighhaan safkaaghutem ilanga nem atilqelghii Agleghnalleghpigaq Na .
Ilungani taawa gold-ek aghqefigek paneghreghaasik incense-mun . Taawallu salngagek qaspeghiqak gold-meng , ateghqek ark-ek , neqanguusighqak Kiyaghneghem akequsaanun . Ark-em imaqeftii gold-ek aqimleghutak manna-meng imalgek , Aaron-em ayaviigha piitqughvikegkaq , maalghuklu lliivneqegtak uyghagek igaqughvikngalghiik Kiyaghneghem qelghusaaneng .
Quulngani ark-em taawa gold-ek cherubim-ek , yaqghwik taghneghangullghiik mercy seat-kun . Iwernga uumi pilleghmi akuzitkepagningitaput tamaakut .
Sangwaa tamaghhaan tiintanilnguq apeghiighluku , taagken aghhutanga tamaghhaan priest-et iitghaqut sivulighmun nemun qepghaghnaluteng .
Iwernga high priest-nginaghhaq iteghyaghqaaguq tuunglighhaanun nenganun tiintam . Tawaten piiquq ataasighhaghmeng ayumiqulleghmi . Iteneghmini tawavek nemun iiwleng kelqesaghqaaguq aawaneng aghqutkegkam teghikusam . Tuuniiquq aawmeng Kiyaghneghmun ellmi seghleghqelleghminun , yugetlu seghleghqellghitnun . Taana aawk seghleghqellghitnun pinguuq nallukluteng pikiitnun .
Tamaakutgun Agleghnalghiim Taghnegham liigikestiinkut iteghvik Agleghnalleghpigaghmun Nemun salin qelpeghsigalnguq tabernacle-a atuqnguluku .
Taakut usputaagut maatemun . Liigikestiinkut tunusatlu aghqutkegkatlu teghikusat nallghusaghpagningitaat maniguutistem sumeghnegha .
Tamaakut tunusatlu aghqutetlu atuqegkaagut qaatkesaghqaaluki qelghusat neqnengllu , meghyaghqanengllu , pelungighsalleghqanengllu yugusiitneng ayuqelghiit . Tamaakut qelghusat yugusighhiinaghmun ayuqut . Qaatkesaghqaagut kenlanga Kiyaghneghem akequsaghraghaa atuughtellghanun .
Christ-a tagiiqngami High Priest-nguluni , tagitkaqii qamaglluki pinilghiit quyastillghet whaa maaten whaanlenguut . Iitqaqaa tabernacle-a qilagmelnguq , megnunaghataghalghiillu pinighataghalghiillu nunamelngughmeng tabernacle-meng . Qilagmelnguq tabernacle-a yuget ulimaaqenghitaat enkaam nunam pikenghitaa .
Taagken Christ-a iitqaaguq ataasimeng quunperugllak Agleghnalleghpigaghmun Nemun seghleghqellemnneng itemunnaluta kenlengunaan . Tawaten pikaaguq tuunelleghmikun ellmi katam aawni , atughpenaki aawit goat-etlu , kaawaghaatlu .
Liightuusat qelqaqiit priest-enun sivillagtiisqelluki yuget aawitneng goat-et , bull-et , panellghanengllu kaawaghaam . Tawaten piiqut pelungighsaghnaluki yuget yugusiit tuguklighyugnaghtesqelluki Kiyaghneghmun .
Tamaakut pelungighiyaqlegukata yuget yugusiitneng , taawa Christ-am aawan wata pilleqii . Pelungighlleqii umyugasi satngunghilngughneng ugpeqilleghneng elpesinun qepghaatesqelluku unguvalghii Kiyaghneq . Kenlengilnguugnekun Taghneghagnekun , Christ-a seghleghqellghilnguq , tuunegkaaguq ellmineng katam Kiyaghneghmun aghqutnguluni .
Enkaam Christ-am tagitkaqaa Kiyaghneghem akequsaghraghaa yugnun tuqluqaanun . Christ-a tawaten pikaaguq ellngitnun allgeghtesqelluku kenlengilnguq pagitaq Kiyaghneghem akequsaqegkaa ellngitnun . Allgeghlleqiit pagitat qayughllak Christ-am tuqumatkegkaqegkangi . Enkaam yuget kiyaghtekat akequsaqsuwhaaghmi , itemumaat seghleghqelleghmeggneng .
Igakun yugem igaqughlleqii saghyani kitumun pagisaghqaaniluki tuqukumi . Pagitiyaghqam allgeghhnaanghitii pagisaghqani wetku kitum ipapighqegkagu yuuk tuqumatanga .
Taam yugem igaquqii pitngunaanghitut salin kiyaghtengnguluku . Igaquqii pitngughllequt kingunganeng tuqukan .
Tamaaken apalluqluku talwa akequsaqsuwhaaq pitngumangituq aawngunani .
Moses-em aapqaqii yugnun qamaglluki qelghusat Liightuusanilnguut . Taagken kaawaghaatlu , goat-etlu aawitneng tugulluni meghmeng akumegkaa . Tugulluni kavilngughmeng wool-meng , avayaanengllu hyssop-em neptekii aawmun . Taagken sivillagtaqii igat Liilightuusalghutat , qamagllukillu yuget .
Pikii , " Unanguuq aawk apeghiighilghii Kiyaghneghem akequsaaneng qelghuskanga elpesinun qaatkesqelluku . "
Tawatengngwaaq Moses-em sivillagtaqaqii aawmeng tabernacle-a , qamagllukillu saghyat atuqegkat maniguutelleghmun .
Ipapestaaq Liilightuusat pillghitni , qamagtevzigluni sangwaa tamaghhaghmi pelungiqaaguq aawkun . Kiyaghneghem seghevunnaanghitii yuget seghleghqellghit wetkuqun aawk maaqegkan .
Nunamelnguq tabernacle-a , ilunganilnguutlu saghyat qilagmelngughestun ayuqut . Tamaakut nunamelnguut saghyat pelungighyaghqaagut aawitgun teghikusat . Iwernga qilagmelnguut saghyapiget pelungighyaghqaagut aghqutetgun pinighataghalghiit nunami aghqutkegkaneng .
Christ-a iitghumangituq Agleghnalleghpigaghmun Nemun yuget ulimaaghitnun . Taana ipapigtun qilagmelngughtun ayuquq . Yeghlegi qilagmun iitqaaguq enkaam maaten Kiyaghneghmetuq High Priest-nguluni whangkunnun .
Christ-a nunam high priest-ngatun ayuqenghituq . Ataasighhaghmeng ayumiqunghani high priest-a iitghaquq Agleghnalleghpigaghmun Nemun kelqelluni aawmeng ellmi pikenghilkemineng . Iwernga Christ-a aghqutkumangituq ellmineng uteghpagtiinaq ,
qayughllak ikfiqnayaghtuq ugliinaghluku ima ulimallghaneng nunam . Iwernga ukuni kingulighni aghneghni tagikaaguq ataasimeng quunperugllak iqinnaluki seghleghqellghet aghqutkelleghmikun ellmineng .
Tamaghaghhmi tuquyaghqaalghii ataasighhaghmeng , enkaam taam kingunganeng Kiyaghneghem nanqiglleqii .
Tawateghpigaq ataasighhaghmeng Christ-a aghqutkegkaaguq ellmineng iqinnaluki seghleghqellghit yulghutet . Iwernga alla tagikumi , aghqutkesaghtuunghituq ellmineng seghleghqelleghmun . Yeghlegi yuguliyaghtughlleqii qelanqilghiit ellmineng .
Liilightuusat taghneghangullghiistun ayuqut pinilghiinun kaasaghqanun , iwernga Liilightuusat taakughpigaanghitut . Liilightuusat qelellghistun Jews-et aghqerraaghumanginaghaqut ayumiitanga tamaghhaan . Iwernga tamaakut aghqerraallghet ukmangighwaaghpagningitiit seghleghqellghitneng manigughyaghtuneghmegteggu Kiyaghneq .
Yuget maniguutestengi Kiyaghneghem ukmangipiigumakumeng seghleghqelleghmeggneng , seghleghninanighnayaghtut . Enkaam aghqutkinanighnayaghtut .
Iwernga ayumiitanga tamaghhaan , tamaakut aghqerraallghet neqangughtestaqiit yuget seghleghqellghitneng ,
qayughllak aawita bull-etlu goat-etlu seghleghqellghighpagningitiit .
Tamaakut apalluqluki Christ-a tagiiqngami nunamun pikaqaa Kiyaghneq : " Aghquteyugumangitutenllu tunusaghyugumangitutenllu , iwernga yataaghqegkaqan yugusiq whangamnun .
Efququmangitaten teghikusat iinguniita paneghtekat aghqefigegni nalighmeng aghqutet seghleghqelleghnun .
Taagken whanga piiqa , ' Ii-i Kiyaghneq , tagiinga piyukelleghpetun pinalunga , katam tawaten igaquqaqegkangatnga Akuzitni Igaqegkani . ' "
Christ-a pikaalghii , " Aghquteyugumangitutenllu tunusaghyugumangitutenllu . Aghquteyugumangituten teghikusaneng iingunaghmeng paneghtekaneng aghqefigegni nalighmeng aghqutneng seghleghqelleghnun . Tamaakut efqughsimangitaaten . " Christ-a tawaten pikaaguq Liilightuusat qelghutkaqeghngaatki tamaakut aghqutet pisqelluki .
Taagken pikaaguq , " Ii-i , tagiinga piyukelleghpetun pinalunga . " Enkaam Kiyaghneghem qamaglluki iqiqughluki aghquteluget nengitgun nekegtekaqaa Christ-a aghqutnguluku .
Jesus Christ-am qaatkesaqminigu Kiyaghneghem piyukellgha , pelungiqaqiinkut seghleghqellemnneng tuunelleghmikun yugusini ataasighhaghmeng quunperugllak .
Aghhutanga tamaghhaan , tamaghhaghmeng priest-et nekevghaghmeng qepghaqateng piiqiit . Uteghpagtiinaq tuuniiqut tawatelkullghiineng aghqutneng . Tawalliima tamaakut aghqutet seghleghqellghighiyaghqaghhaanghitut .
Iwernga Christ-am tuunegkaqaa ataasiq aghqun seghleghqelleghnun quunperugllagmun . Taagken aqumegkaq aghenqigneghakun Kiyaghneghem .
Tawani Christ-a utaqiigaquq kenlanga Kiyaghneghem nekegtelleghqaanun anguyagi itegaan asinganun .
Taaggun ataasikun aghqutkelleghqun , Christ-am quunperugllak naamigtestekaqii pelungighsaqat seghleghqelleghmeggneng .
Agleghnalghiimllu Taghnegham ungipaatiinkut tamaakuneng . Sivukluni whaten pikaaguq ,
" Unanguuq akequsaqa yumnun , kingungitneng tamaakut aghneghet , piiq Ataneq , Liilightuusanka kanaghlleqanka ilungitnun , igaqelleqankallu umyuwiitgun . "
Taagken piiq , " Allamengllu neqamiknaanghitanka seghleghqellghit , seghletunllu pillghit . "
Enkaam Kiyaghneghem seghevuskaki seghleghqellghit , aghqutet atuqsaghqaananighllequt seghleghqelleghnun .
Tamaaken apalluqluku , ugpeqaalgutemni , alingillngunaamta itelleghqangukut Agleghnalleghpigaghmun aawakun Jesus-em .
Qelpeghusimiinkutlu tumeghraghaghmeng unguvalleghmun safkaaghutkun ; taana safkaaghun yugusiqaa .
Priest-elegllaaguukutlu igleghutilghii Kiyaghneghem mangteghaaneng .
Tamaakut apalluqluki tughaaghelteggu Kiyaghneq ipapighqelluta , neghyukngwaaghluku . Tawaten pilleghqangukut qayughllak umyugalluput sivillagtaqaagut Christ-am aawaneng ukmangiightesqelluki , yugusiputlu ughvughqegkaagut pelungilngughqun meghqun .
Yeqay ataasiighmelluta sighimalleghmetekestaalta whangkunnun piknikamnnun , qayughllak ugpeqaghput Kiyaghneq ataasiighmetuq enkaam piyaghqaqii akequsani .
Yeqay sumeghtaghaalta naten qiilngumighusaghqaaluta piniqsaghqaaluki ilat , pinitunllu piyaghqaaluta .
Yeqay taaqefqaamta qerngughunneghmeng pilta manigughnaluku Kiyaghneq , ilangita piiqellghistun . Yeghlegi qerngughusimanginaalta kayemutunnaluta . Wata kayemusimanginaalta qayughllak Atanghem Aghnegha tughaalghii .
Seghleghqesugaataqumta kingunganeng liilluku ipapilleq , taawa aghqutkaghqiituq iqitusighqameng tamaavek seghleghqelleghnun .
Tamaakut tawaten pilghiit alingruughmeng utaqiillequt Kiyaghneghem nanqigtillghaneng . Atuqelleqaak uguqnaghllagek kenghek naafqennaluki tamaakut kipullginaalghiit ellmineng .
Maalghuk nalighmeng pingayut liisimakistet aapqatgu yuuk qaatkusimanginniluku Moses-em Liilightuusaanun , nanqigtistem nangllekegpenaan tuqutesleqaa .
Sumeghtaghaatkaghteggu natenmi angkaslugan Kiyaghneghem aghyuughlleqagu yuuk tutmaasghaqiiqelghii Ighneghaneng Kiyaghneghem , piiqelghii satngunghinniluku aawk apeghiighutkaq akequsaghraghaghmeng ( qaywa Kiyaghneghem ukmangiisiqegkaqeghngaagu seghleghqellghanun ) , seghlequughiiqelghiillu nangllegtalghiignun Tagneghagnun .
Liisimakaghput Kiyaghneq ; ellngangulghii whaten pikaq , " Whanganguuq aghyuughiyaghqaq , akisaghqaqanka seghletun pillghit . " Whatenllu pikaaguq , " Atanghem nanqigsaghqaqii ellmi yuni . "
Tatamaataghnapigtuq kina alngunak iigganisaghqaq unguvalghiim Kiyaghneghem Nanqigtillghem Aghneghani !
Neqamikegkesi tamaakut aghneghet sivunghani liisuwhaaghaqngafsigu ipapilleq Christ-ameng ayuqelghii . Aghuliitkaagusi ataasiighmellusi qaywa ikfiqeghllaghngaaghpesi .
Ilangakun yugtuqami yuget seghletun akuzitkaqiisillu amyuqetaatkaqiisillu . Ilangani nekevghalgusighaqasi tamaakut amyuqetaatkesilghiit .
Nangllekaqasi anusimingllaghvigmelnguut . Talwa quyangaaqusi yuget tugulanghatki saghyasi qayughllak liisimakaghsi paninang salguusi pinighataghalghiimeng quunpekaghqameng .
Enkaangam iilqayugpenasi qayughllak ilutumanginaqufsi allgeghullequsi akileghtuusaghllagmeng .
Aklukngwaaghsi nuqenneghtulleq atuqsaghqaaluku Kiyaghneghem piyukellgha . Taagken allgeghlleqasi akequsaqegkii .
Katam igaqngalghii Akuzitni Igaqegkani whaten , " Qantaghaqun taana tagiyaghqaq kaallequq ; kimaawinaanghituq .
Elqughutngalghiit yugenka kiyaghllequt ugpeqilleghqun . Iwernga kitum alngunak pegtekumigu ugpeqilleni , unguvasigma efquqnaanghitaqa . "
Iwernga whangkuta pegtikastun ugpeqilleghmeggneng ayuqenghitukut , naafqellengyaghqastun . Iwernga ugpeqillelguukut enkaam unguvasiput yugulikaagukut .
Ugpeqillghem liisimakestengngwaaghiinkut allgeghsaghqaqniluku sighmakegkaghput , ipapighqusiguq esghaghyaghqaqenghilkemnnun .
Ugpeqilleghmegteggun ayumiim yugi itagnaqellengegkaagut Kiyaghneghmeng .
Ugpeqilleghqun liigikegkaqaghput Kiyaghneghem ulimaaqaa nuna akuzitmikun . Tamaakut aliilnguut ulimaaghuut esghaghyaghqaanghilngughmeng .
Ugpeqilleghqun Abel tuunikaaguq Kiyaghneghmun tuguklighyugnaghataghalghiimeng aghqutmeng Cain-em aghqutkegkaaneng . Kiyaghneq pikaaguq Abel elqughutngalghiinguniluku yuuk ugpeqillgha apalluqluku . Kiyaghneghem ipapighqegkaqaa Abel elqughutnganiluku tuguklilleghmikun tunusii . Ugpeqilleghmikun Abel paninang akuzinguuq , tuqukaayaghngaaghmi .
Upeqilleghqun Enoch mayuutestekaaguq qilagmun enkaam nanghiillghitaa tuqulleq . Kitum alngunak naalkellghitaa qayughllak Kiyaghneghem tugukaqegkanga . Mayullghilluni qilagmun , igaqngakaaguq Enoch-em efqughtekaqaa Kiyaghneq .
Ugpeqillngunani kitum alngunak efqughtepagningitaa Kiyaghneq . Kina alngunak tagiyukumi Kiyaghneghmun ugpeqepestaaghyaghqaqaa Kiyaghnelguniluku , akileghtughyaghqaqiillu ivaghipiilghiit ellmineng .
Ugpeqilleghqun Noah-m nagatkaqii Kiyaghneghem kelengasaaghutkii tamaakut salin pingigalluki . Enkaam qaatkelluku Kiyaghneq angyaghpangllaqaaguq nengllugutni yugulinaluki ulevelleghmeng . Tawaten pilleghmikun Noah-m nunam yugi nanqigtestekaqii Kiyaghneghmun aghyuughesqelluki . Ugpeqilleni apalluqluku Noah-m allgeghtekaqaa elqughutngalleq Kiyaghneghmeng .
Ugpeqilleghqun Abraham-em qaatkegkaqaa Kiyaghneq tuqlughaqngatni aghulaqesqelluku ilanganun nunam . Kiyaghneghem akequsaqaa taana nuna ellnganun tuunelleqniluku . Enkaam unitkaqaa ellmi nunani nallukluku navek pinaqutni .
Ugpeqilleghqun kiyaghtekaaguq nunataaluni nunami Kiyaghneghem akequsaqegkaani . Tiintanitkaaguq katam Isaac-enkuk Jacob-enkuk pillghegketun . Elkegkenkallu allgeghtekaqaak Kiyaghneghem akequsaqegkaa taana nuna .
Abraham tawaten pikaaguq qayughllak utaqiingulghii kiyaghhnaluni neghllagmi tunemaghtuqami . Kiyaghneghuuq uspeqistengallu ulimaghistengallu neghllagem .
Abraham nanevgaghllaghngaaghmi , Sarah-llu qumingyaghqaanghiteghngaaghmi , paninang ugpeqilleghqun Sarah qumingegkaaguq , qayughllak neghyukegkaqaa Kiyaghneghmun pilleqniluku akequsaqegkani .
Tamaaken apalluqluku Abraham tuquyaghtungestaqaaghngaaghmi , paninang kinguneghtughqaaghllakaaguq . Ellngita uglaghtalngit ighaleqetaaghestun qilagamelngughestun ayuqut , kestekaanghilngughestunllu qenaavzeghaatun esnam .
Qamaglluteng tamaakut yuget paninang kiyaghtekaagut ugpeqilleghqun tuqulleghmeggnun kenlanga . Tuqulaghaatkaalghiit allgeghtegpenaki Kiyaghneghem akequsaqegkii ellmeggnun . Iwernga ugpeqilleghqun esghaqaqiit Kiyaghneghem akequsaqegkii uyavanlluki sivumeggnilluki quyakegkaqiitlu . Enkaangam ungipaatkaqiit yuget nunataaniluteng whani nunami , nunamun pikenghinniluteng .
Tamaakut tawaten akuzilghiit , whateghlluwaaq aapghwaat nunakaghqaghyugniluteng ellmeggnun pikaghqameng .
Suumqegkaqsaqumegteggu taana nuna unitkaghteng , uteghtelleghqalgunayaghtut .
Yeghlegi piyukataghaqaqaat pinighataghalghii nuna , qilaghmelnguq . Enkaam Kiyaghneq kaynguyugigatuq Kiyaghneqninghatni . Talwa yataaghqutkaqii neghllagmeng .
Kiyaghneghem akeqegkaqegkanga Abraham , " Isaac-ekun kinguneghllagullequten . " Ugpeqilleghqun Abraham-em neghyukegkaqaa Kiyaghneq nanghiiqwaaqngatni . Enkaam aghqutkesaghqaaghtekaa kezemaghhaq ighneni , Isaac .
Abraham-em ugpeqegkaqaa Kiyaghneq unguvaghtiyaqleguniluku tuqukaneng . Enkaam Kiyaghneghem tuqutesnanighaqngagu Isaac , Abraham-em veghtekallghuuqaqaa Isaac tuqulleghmeng .
Ugpeqilleghqun Isaac-em quyastekaqaak Jacob-enkuk Esau-nkuk , tungsiitkaqaak Kiyaghneghmun quyastesqellukek aagnaqkaghqiik .
Ugpeqilleghqun Jacob-em , tuqunaqnguluni quyastekaqaak allakaqaghtaagkenka ighneghqek Joseph-em . Taagken qungughlluni ayaviighmikun maniguqaqaa Kiyaghneq .
Ugpeqilleghqun Joseph-em , kenletghuunnaqellghani unguvalleghmi , akuzitkegkaqaa aghulaqelleghqaat Israel-eghmiit Egypt-meng . Apeghtuutkaqiillu neghqwaani naten salleghqii .
Ugpeqilleghqun Moses-em angayuqagkenka iighaghtuqaqaak pingayut tanqit allgellghan kingunganeng . Esghaqangak yuukegtepiglleghii , alingumangilnguuklu qaatkunneghisaghqaalutek umiilgem qelghutellghanun .
Ugpeqilleghqun Moses , yugughsami ighsakaaguq ighneqesneghmeng Pharaoh-m paniganun .
Yeghlegi nakmiiqaaguq ikfiqelgusighnaluki Kiyaghneghem yugi , avelghagluku efqughyugnallgha seghleghqellghem muluyaghqaanghilnguq .
Itupill sumeghtaghaatkegkaqaa ikfiqelleghqani Christ-amun itagnaghataghaghniluku aklungilghutanganeng Egypt-em . Sumeghtaghaatkengngwii akileghtuusaghqat aga sivumelnguut .
Ugpeqilleghqun Moses-em unitkaqaa Egypt alingellngunani umiilgem sakraallghaneng . Iilqayugumangituq qayughllak esghalghiistun pikaqegkanga aliinneghilnguq Kiyaghneq .
Ugpeqilleghqun Moses-em qelqaqii yuget Passover-esqelluki , qelghutkaqaallu aakw sivillagtaatesqelluku amigteggun . Enkaam Yaqulgan Tuqullghem tuqutellghitii ighneqsuwhaaghit Israel-eghmiit .
Ugpeqilleghqun Israel-eghmiit aghviqaqaat Red Sea nikimqun qutestun . Iwernga Egypt-eghmiit , aghvighnaqutkengnguluteng pekaqutkaagut .
Ugpeqilleghqun Israel-eghmiit maaghraghvinlegni aghneghni uzivgaqaqaat Jericho-m mingllutanga . Taagken minglluta ulleghaatkaaguq .
Ugpeqilleghqun Rahab-em , yugusimineng akikikayugem , upughatkaqaak Israel-eghmiit riirngistegket . Tamaaken apalluqluku tuqullghituq maligulluni qaatkusigalngughnun Kiyaghneghmun .
Wataqaaghaq ungipamsugullamsii yugneng ugpeqikaneng Kiyaghneghmeng ? Taakeghllagyaghqaagut akuzitkesaghqaaluki Gideon-enkut , Barak-enkut , Samson-enkut , Jephthah-nkut , David-enkut , Samuel-enkut , uuknaliqistetlu .
Ugpeqilleghqun ilangi yuget whaten pikaagut : kayaalqegkaqiit ataneghpagullghet , elqughutngaluteng igleghutikaagut . Enkaam Kiyaghneghem akequsii tugukaqiit . Ilangita lion-et qaanghit meqetestaqiit .
Kumaghughllaget kenghet qaamtaqiit , anagaqlukillu tuqutistekaghqateng savigpagkun . Kayaataqut iwernga ugpeqillghita iknaqughtaqiit . Ugpeqilleghqun pilluwaghtengit iknaqughteghllagaqut enkaam kayaalqaqiit ilangita nunat pilluwaghtengit .
Ugpeqilleghqun aghnat tuqumasliiteng veghtaqiit tuqulleghmeng Kiyaghneghem unguvaghhneghaki . Ilangi elngaatall ikfiqesteghllagaqiit pegtesqelluku ugpeqillghat . Iwernga tuqunaluteng piiqut Kiyaghneghmun unguvaghtesqelluteng pinighataghalghimun unguvalleghmun .
Ilangi legasiighwaatkaqluki , ilangi kagsagmigaqluki , ilangi qiipraghusighluki anusimingllaghaqiit .
Ilangi milughpagaatameng tuqutaqiit , ilangi yugusiit pilagtughluki malghughqaqiit , ilangi tuqutaqiit savigpagkun . Ilangi temgi tamaani igleghtaqut aalluteng penniighemllu goat-emllu amiineng . Ilangi aklumapiglleghhiit , yuget amyuqetaatkegkiit , seghletunllu kiyaghutkiit .
Nunam yugi pinipagunghitut kiyaghtelgusighyaghqaaluki tamaakut elqughutngalghiit yuget ! Ilangi elqughutngalghiit temngi tamaani igleghakaalghiit paaghqillghani , naayghani , kiyaghtaqluteng qayeni , laawaaghnillu .
Qamaglluki tamaakut Kiyaghneghem itagnaqegkaqii ugpeqillghit apalluqluki ! Naqamllu allgeghsimangitaat Kiyaghneghem akequsaqegkaa ,
qayughllak Kiyaghneghem uspeqegkaa whangkunnun pinighataghalghiinguuq . Uspeqillgha whatetuq : akequsani pinaanghitii ellngitnun whangkungunaki . Qerngaamta qamaglluta iighwighlleqiinkut .
Qamaglluteng tamaakut yuget liigikestiinkut ugpeqilleghmeggneng naten kiyaghtelleghmegteggun . Maaten uvitangighluta esghapagaqiinkut . Enkaam kilgaaqustestun iqitelteki qamaglluki uqigkutat , seghleghqellghetlu iglagullghiit whangkunnun . Sagiqlutangam kilgaaqulta sivumnnilngughmun ,
esghaamakluku Jesus , piinlighistengallu apeghiighistengallu ugpeqillemta . Kayngunaghtuq tuqulleghqaq qaquurakun , iwernga Jesus-em pitkumangitaa kayngusaghaatelleq . Yeghlegi nakmiiqaaguq ikfiqnaluni qaquurakun apalluqluku quyalleq allgeghsaghqani . Enkaam maaten aqumgaaq aghenqigneghani Kiyaghneghem .
Sumeghtaghaatkaghtegguqun Jesus . Iilqayugumangituq qaywa seghleghqestet ugumikeraaghllaghngaatni . Tawaten elpesillu ilutullghiinnaanghitusillu iilqayugnaanghitusillu .
Seghleghqenghinnaqutkelleghpesi salin yugnun tuqutesigatiisi .
Puygustekii ilutughsaasit akuzitet ungipaatilghiit Kiyaghneghmun ighneqnilusi ? Akuzitni Igaqegkani igaqngaaq , " Ighnemni , avelghaqiinaghpenaan Atanghem nallghusanghaten , iilqayugpenangllu aghyuunghaten .
Qayughllak qamaglluki piniqegkani Atanghem apeghtughaqii qaatkesqelluni , aghyuughaqiillu tugukliqani avaqutaaluki . "
Tuguklighaqiteggu Kiyaghneghem aghyuughillgha qayughllak ighneqelghiistun piiqiisi . Qamaglluki avaqutateng atangita aghyuughaqiit nallghughqennaluki .
Qamaglluteng avaqutat aghyuullengaqut . Aghyuullengenghilkuvek taawa atangilnguuguten enkaam avaqutapikenghitaaten .
Taam saaghwakun , atamta nunamelnguut aghyuughaqiinkut apeghtughnaluta qaatkesqelluteng , iwernga paninang quulvaghaqaput . Enkaam Atavut qilagmelnguq qaatkataghaghyaghqaqaghput unguvanaluta .
Atamta nunamelnguut aghyuughaqinkut natengiighhaq , sumeghmeggni elqughlluku aghyuughinguniluteng . Iwernga Kiyaghneghem aghyuughaqiinkut pinighqelleghqamnnun pelungiightesqelluta ellmitun .
Quyaniituq aghyuullengnemta qayughllak aqnightaqegkanginkut . Iwernga tagtalmi , liitfiknemteggu , nekeggmellengaqukut qayughllak kiyaghsagutaqukut elqughulluta .
Kevegteki iiggesi qughaghngalghiit , taagken iknaqughsaghteki kayaalnguut segesqusi !
Taklaghtiki tuumngi tutmalleghpek , taagken kayaalnguq ighun aanqaghnaanghituq naflumineng , iwernga naallghullequq .
Kiyaghhnaqitek nekeggmetullusi tamaghhaanun yugnun , kiyaghhnaqiteklu seghleghqellngunasi . Kinkut alngunak pelunginneghilnguut esghaghnaanghitaat Ataneq .
Esghaamakullusi kinkut alngunak luuraq allgeghhneghisaaghaat Kiyaghneghem nangllegtallgha . Nagusaqunaanllu sungaghnilnguq akuq seghleliighqiiluni naafqiiyaghqaq yulghutmeng .
Esghaamakullusi kinkut alngunak seghleghqesaaghtut sex-kun , nalighmeng kinkut alngunak quulvaghinghisaaghtut Kiyaghneghmeng Esau-tun . Akikegkaqegkanga pagitaghqani ataasighhaghmun neghyaghqamun .
Liisimakaghsi taam kingunganeng , allgeghsugaqngamigu atami quyastellgha , atangan ighsakegkaqaa . Esau-m allangughtepagningitkaqaa apeghiiqani , qaywa qunituumaghmi tungsighngaaghmigu atami quyastillgha .
Sivuneghpesistun ayuqenghitusi Mount Sinai-mun pikastun . Esghaghyaghqaat , saafsaghqaatlu . Tawani mamlegllagukaq , naafteghllagukaq , naayghaqlu kumaghughllagulghii .
Nagaquqaat qalghightaan qalghighlleghhii , nagaquqaatlu Kiyaghneghem menga . Iwernga nepiiqiisqegkaat ,
qayughllak tuguklighyunghilkangat qelghillgha whatelnguq , " Taana naayghaq , yugem nalighmeng teghikusam saaftekumigu , tuqusaghqapestaaghuuq milughpagaatameng . "
Moses-em esghaqaa kakavaataghnapiglleghhii repall whaten pikaalghii , " Ellngaatall ungelegtunga alingruughem . "
Iwernga katam elpesi tagikaagusi Mt . Zion-mun , qilagem Jerusalem-nganun , neghllaganun unguvalghiim Kiyaghneghem . Tagikaagusi kestekaanghilngughnun yaqulegnun qerngughutkanun quyallelighllagluteng .
Tagikaagusi qerngughutellghitnun qamagtengngwaaghluteng ugpeqat ighneqsuwhaaghestun ayuqelghiit . Qilagmi aatghit igaqngaat igatgun . Tagikaagusi Kiyaghneghmun nanqigtistengitnun qamagtengngwaaghluteng yuget , taghneghiitnunllu elqughutngalghiit yuget iighwightestekanun .
Tagikaagusi Jesus-mun , ellngakun Kiyaghneq akequsaghraghangllaqaaguq . Tagikaagusillu sivillagtaatkamun aawanun Jesus-em . Pinighataghaghtuq Abel-em aawaneng , qayughllak Kiyaghneghem seghevutii seghleghqellghet Jesus-em aawakun .
Enkaam kelengatek , nagasunghitegpenaan Kiyaghneq akuzilghii . Sivunemta nagasunghitkaqaat kelengasaaghillgha nunami whani , enkaam anagumangitaat aghyuughillgha . Whangkuta aghyuughataghaghlleqiinkut nagasunghilkumteggu kelengasaallgha qilagmeng .
Kiyaghneq akuziiqngami Mount Sinai-meng , mengan ufsugutkaqaa nuna . Iwernga maaten akeqimaaq whaten , " Ataasighhaghmeng ufsugunneqiglleqaqa nuna , iwernga qilaklu ufsugulleqaqa . "
Tawaten akuzillghan , " Ataasighhaghmeng ufsugunneqiglleqaqa nuna , " liigikestengngwaaghiinkut whaten , sangwaat qamaglluki ulimaani , Kiyaghneghem iqilleqii ufsugusaghqat . Tamaakunginaghhaat ufsugutepagningilnguut tamaanllequt quunperugllak .
Tamaaken apalluqluku iyamsiqayugvikelteggu Kiyaghneq qayughllak tuunegkanginkut ataneghpagulleghmeng ufsugusaghqaanghilngughmeng . Enkaangam maniguulteggu Kiyaghneq efqughnalkegkaatun alingellelighlutallu quulvaghillelighlutallu ,
qayughllak Kiyaghneghput naafqiilghiinguuq keneq .
Piniqekestaghteki ugpeqaalgutesi .
Upughamanginaghtek aqiiyagnun qayughllak ilangita upughataqiit nallukluki yaqulgutangi .
Neqamikluki anusimingllaghvigmelnguut , nikimqun elpesillu anusimingllaghvigmetellghistun . Neqamikluki ikfiqngalghiit , nikimqun elpesillu ikfiqelghiistun .
Tamaghhaghpesi siivakiteggu nengughutelleq enkaam ugitlu nulighhetlu ataasiighmetullit . Kiyaghneghem nanqigsaghqaqii gelgaghniilghiit , tamaakutlu ilanganeng sex-kun seghleghqelghiit .
Kiyaghtek pakigneghugpenasi manimun , itagnaghaqiteklu satutalegpesistun . Kiyaghneq pikaaguq , " Uninnaanghitngwaaghamsi ; peggnaanghitngwaaghamsi . "
Enkaam tetullngunaamta whaten pilta , " Ataneq kayutkaqa ! Alingnaanghitunga yuget salleghqiitneng . "
Neqamikluki igleghutistesi ungipaqikat elpesinun Kiyaghneghem akuzitanganeng . Neqamikluki naten kiyaghtekaatangi enkaam ugpellelgunaqitek ellngistun .
Jesus Christ-a almesiqaqaa ighivgaq , aghneghmi , quunperugllaklu .
Iqitutestegpenasi ipapilleghmeng allaaghhiinaghnunllu allakaayagnunllu apeghtuusanun . Nangllegtallghakun Kiyaghneghem ayepsugighsaghteki ilusi , nakaan qaatkelluki Liilightuusat neqneng ayuqelghiit . Taakut neqet Liilightuusiit qaatkegkufsiki ayepsugighsaghnaanghitiit ilusi .
Priest-et qepghalghiit tabernacle-mi ineghtekaagut neghelleghqiitneng aghqutkegkameng aghqefimteggun .
High Priest-em tagitaqii aawit teghikusat Agleghnalleghpigaghmun aghqutkennaluki seghleghqelleghnun . Iwernga kemegkwaaghit teghikusat neghllagmeng iqitulluki paneghtaqiit .
Tamaaken apalluqluku Jesus-llu iqitutkaaguq neghllagmeng . Tawani tuqukaaguq , pelungighsaghnaluki yuget seghleghqellghitneng ellmi katam aawmineng .
Enkaangam neghllagmeng whangkutallu aglaalta Jesus-mun , seghletun akuzitkesqelluta katam ellnga seghletun akuzitkellghistun .
Nunami whani quunpekaghqameng neghllagitukut , iwernga utaqangwaaghput neghllak tagiyaghqaq .
Jesus-kun iiwleng aghqutkilta Kiyaghneghmun . Aghquteput usuqilqaput apenemteggu Jesus Atanghuniluku .
Puygugpenaan pinitun pilleq , tuunutaqiteklu qayughllak tamaakut aghqutnguut efqughnalghiit Kiyaghneghmun .
Qaatkiteki igleghutistesi atuqluki qelghusiit . Kelengakinguut unguvasighpesineng liisimakluku Kiyaghneghmun nanqigsaghqaatseng . Quyanghitestegpenaki igleghutistesi , itupill qaatkelleghpesigun qepghaqateng pilleqiit quyakusiqluki . Qaatkenghilkufsiki kayusiitepagningitiisi .
Yughaatkitekut . Liisimakukut umyugamta anaggutellghinniinkut , qayughllak iiwleng piyukelqaghput elqughutngalghii piyaghqaaluku .
Taakunginaghhaagneng kayagtamsi yughaatkesqellunga qantaghaqun elpesinun uteghnighnalunga .
Kiyaghneghem nekeggmellelitistem Ataneghput Jesus unguvaghtestekaqaa tuqulleghmeng . Enkaam aawmikun Penniighniighteghllagughtekaaguq penniighnun . Aawan atuuyaghqaaghtestekaqaa Kiyaghneghem quunpekaghqaq akequsaa .
Yughaghtunga Kiyaghneghmun tuunesqellusi sameng tamaghhaaneng pinilghiimeng elpesinun piyukellgha pisqelluku . Jesus Christ-akunllu ilugpesinun Kiyaghneghem piligu efqughnalghii ellminun . Christ usuqellengli quunperugllak kenlengunaan . Amen .
Ugpeqaalgutemni , nagatngwaaqaghteki latanka qayughllak kayemyugaqamsi . Tamaaken apalluqluku takestaaghhaaluku lataamsi .
Liisimakesugamsi ugpeqaalgutemnneng , Timothy-meng , aanesimaaq anusimingllaghvigmeng . Kaatelghaghtughyaqan qerngaamtung esghaghyaghtughlleqamsi .
Quyakaghhnakesi qamaglluki igleghutistesi , qamagllukillu Kiyaghneghem yugi . Ugpeqaalgutetlu Italy-meng pit quyakaghhnakiisinguq .
Kiyaghneghem piniqingalghii kayusillgha tamaghhaghpesinilli ! Amen .
Ukut latat James-meng pinguut qepghaghtenganeng Kiyaghneghemllu Atanghemllu Jesus Christ-am . Lataaqunga Jews-et ugpeqiitnun mingitngalghiinun tamangani . Quyakamsi .
Ugpeqaalgutemni , quyaaqitek allaaghhiinaghmeng seghleliineghpesini ,
qayughllak liisimakasi seghleliilleghpesi nanghiiqungwaat ugpeqilleghsi , nuqenneghtughsaghnalusi .
Taagken nuqenneghtulleghsi nagneghngasteggu . Enkaam tawaten pikufsi angtaniillequsi , iighwighllequsi nuughyaghqaagpenasi .
Nalighsi peghqinellengyukumi tungsighli Kiyaghneghmeng . Kiyaghneq ighlegiteghllagtuq , quyakusiqinaghluku tuunegkayuwaa qamaglluku yuuk aapleghhii . Kiyaghneghem tuunelleqiisi tungsiqufsi .
Enkaam aaptek ugpeqillelighluku malghuklillngunaan . Malghuklingalghii imaghllugestun ayuquq , anuqem tengqaataqegkanga .
Malghuklingalghii ataasiighsigatuq salleghmikun tamaghhaan . Tawatelnguq yuuk talwa sumeghtaghaghyaghqaanghituq sameng alngunak allgeghulleqniluni Ataneghmeng .
Yeqay aklumalghii ugpeqaalgun quyali quulvaghtestengngalleghmineng .
Yeqay aklungilnguq ugpeqaalgun quyali qusevegtestengngalleghmineng , qayughllak aviighusaghqaaguq piitesighaghestun .
Siqineq piinneghmini maatneghqwaaghllagaqelghii , piitesighaat palightesluki . Taagken piitesighaat ifkaquutaqut , pinighniighutaqii . Tawateghpigaq aklungilnguq yuuk sakestaghngaaghmi aviighullequq .
Quyanaghhalek yugem nanghiiqulleni nuqetutkayugi . Suflughtekumiki allgeghsaghqaqaa akileghtuusani kenlengilnguq unguvalleq , Kiyaghneghem akequsaqegkaa tuunelleqniluku piniqisteminun .
Kina alngunak nanghiiqullengegkumi whaten pifqaami , " Kiyaghneghem seghleghqesnaqutkaanga . " Kiyaghneq nanghiiqullengyaghqaghhaanghituq seghleghmeng ; tamaaken apalluqluku kina alngunak seghleghqesnaqutkesaghqaqenghitaa .
Iwernga yuuk piyukellelugan nanghiiqullengestaqaa seghleghqelleghmun . Sivukluku piyukellelugan sayugaqaa seghleghqelleghmun , taagken seghleghqellghem naaptaqaa .
Piyukellelugem allgeghtestaqaa seghleghqelleq . Taagken seghleghqelleq anglineghmini tuqullghughtaquq .
Piniqegkamni ugpeqaalgutemni , puughtesighpenasi .
Qamaglluteng pinilghiitlu , sallghwaaghhiilnguutlu tunusat qilagmeng pinguut . Tamaakut Atameng pinguut ulimaghistenganeng qamaglluni nighugem ; allangughsigatuqlu , mamlegtestingigatuqlu .
Kiyaghneghem ellngan katam piyukelqaa , tuunaluta nutaghameng unguvalleghmeng ungipaakun ipapighqellghem . Tawaten pikaaguq , whangkuta megnunalleghpigaasqelluta ulimaaghyaggaghmineng .
Piniqegkamni ugpeqaalgutemni , neqamikluku una : tamaghhaghmi nagasukestaghluni piyaghqaaguq , akuziighaghtafqaamillu sakraagaghaghtafqaamillu ,
qayughllak sakraam kayusiisigatiisi pinitun kiyaghtaalleghmun Kiyaghneghem piyukegkaanun .
Tamaaken apalluqluku pegteggu qamagtengngwaaghluku allaaghhiinaq seghleq atuqaqegkesi . Qusevegngaghpesi tuguklighteki Kiyaghneghem akuzitangi , piitesiighaqii ilugpesigun , qayughllak yuguliyaghqaqiisi unguvasighpesineng .
Nagataghesnaghpenaki Kiyaghneghem akuzitangi itupill atuqiteki . Puughtaqusi elpesineng katam nagataghesnaneghpesiki atuqegpenaki .
Yuuk nagataghesnaqumi Kiyaghneghem akuzitanganeng atuqegpenaki , taghneghaghqulghiistun ayuquq
tunuskumi tawaninginaq puygulleqaa natetuleni .
Kiyaghneghem elqughutngalghiit Liilightuusii itemutestiiqut yugneng . Yugem liinnaqumanginaqumiki taakut Liilightuusat , puygugpenaki atuqegkumiki Kiyaghneghem quyasaghqaqaa sallghakun tamaghhaan .
Yuuk sumeghtaghaqayuk ugpeqaghllaguniluni , naqam akuzitkesaghqaqenghilkemmineng akuzikayuk temngi puughtengnguuq ellmineng katam . Ugpellgha satngunghituq .
Kiyaghneghem Atamta pillghani yuuk ugpellepiilgukumi , kayusighyaghqaqii yaywaalitlu ugingighatlu seghleliinghata , nuqesaghqaaguqlu seghleghaneng nunam .
Ugpeqaalgutemni , ugpeqingutegpesineng Atanemnneng Jesus Christ-ameng , Atanghaneng nighughqellghem sumeghtaghaatkegpenaki ilangi yugem megnunaghataghaghniluki ilameggneng .
Maalghuk yugek iteghyaqayek qerngughutfigpesinun , aallgha aarraghluni , gold-meng alangqughiitightughluni , aallgha aatkalukaghlluni ,
taana aarraghngalghii yuuk pikufsigu , " Whagun aqumi pinillghakun aqumutam , " naqam aklumalghii yuuk pikufsigu , " Tawani nekevgha , " nalighmeng , " Aqumi itegama saaghwakun , "
tawaten pikufsi pakiggulleqasi ilangi yuget enkaam seghleghqellequsi sumeghtaghalleghpesigun .
Piniqegkamni ugpeqaalgutemni , nagataghtekqun . Kiyaghneghem nakmikegkaqii aklumaalghiit nunami whani ugpeqilleghtusqelluki . Nakmikegkaqii tuguklightenguluki Ataneghpagulleghmineng , akequsaqegkamineng yugminun , piniqingalghiinun ellmineng .
Iwernga elpesi aklumaalghiit yuget ukaliistaqasi . Liisimakasi aklungilnguut piyaqliighqaqiisi , aglaataqlusi nanqigtivigmun .
Ellnginguut seghletun akuzitkilghiit quulvaghngalghiimeng aatghaneng Jesus-em , ateq tuunegkaq elpesinun qayughllak ellngan pikegkangisi .
Kiyaghneghem Ataneghpagullghan Liilightusaa unaanguq : " Piniqluku yulguten piniqelleghpetun elpeneng katam . " Qaatqegkufsigu taana Liilightuusaq , taawa pinitun piisi .
Iwernga pakigguskufsiki ilangi yuget seghleghqellequsi , qaatkennaanghitaghsillu taana Liilightuusaq .
Kitum qaatkesaghngaaghmiki qamaglluki Kiyaghneghem Liilightuusii , ataasiq qaatkenghilkumigu , qamaglluki qaatkengngunghitii .
Kiyaghneq pikaaguq , " Gelgaghniighpenang . " Whatenllu pikaaguq , " Yugtaghpenang . " Gelgaghniinghisaghngaaghpek yugtaquvek taawa qaatkengngunghitaten Kiyaghneghem Liilightuusii .
Akuzilleghpesigun , salleghpesigun piraamsilusi qayughllak elpesinguusi nanqigsaghqat megnunalleghpigaghqun Liilightuusakun . Taam Liilightuusam itemutkaqiisi atuqesqelluku Kiyaghneghem piyukellgha elpesinun .
Kiyaghneghem nanqigtekumisi nangllegyagunnaanghitiisi , nangllegyagunneghilkufsiki yulgutesi . Iwernga nangllekegkufsiki yulgutesi Kiyaghneghem nangllegyagulleqiisi .
Ugpeqaalgutemni , kina whaten pighngaaghmi , " Ugpeqillelguunga , " iwernga taam ugpeqillghan yugulinaanghitaa atuqenghilkumigu ugpeqilleni aneghneghqilleghmikun . Sasiilleqangam ugpeqillgha aneghneghqillngunani ?
Sanayaghetsi ugpeqaalgutsi aatkiisagyaqanllu , neqangisagyaqanllu ?
Tuunegpenaan aklukegkaaneng temngi whaten pikufsigu , " Kiyaghneghem quyasnaaghaaten ; sunanguq neghyaghqangillu aatkangillu maqalghiimeng , " sasiilleqan始ngam akuzitesi aneghneghqillngunateng ?
Ugpeqilleqlu tawatetuq , aneghneghqilleghqun atuqenghilkumi sasiinghituq .
Kina pillequq , " Elpek ugpeqillelguuten , whanga aneghneghqellelguunga . " Kelguvikinga ugpeqilleghpeneng aneghneghqillghilngughmeng , kelguvikelleqamken ugpeqillemneng aneghneghqillemkun .
Ugpeqan ataasighhaatanga Kiyaghneq . Taana pinightuq ! Tughneghaatlu ugpeqaqaat taana enkaangam alingruughaqut , ungelegtaqut qayughllak liisimakegkangat Kiyaghneghem nanqigsaghqaqegkangi .
Uyuq nalluuqaq yuuk , paninang liigikigasiguu ugpeqilleq aneghneghqillngunani sasiinghitulanga ?
Sangan Kiyaghneghem tugukliqaqagu sivuneghput Abraham seghleghqumangilngughestun ? Tugukliqaqaa Abraham qayughllak ugpeqilleni atuqegkaqaa aneghneghqelleghmikun aghqutkaqngamigu ighneni Isaac aghqefigegnekun .
Liigiksiguu ? Ugpeqilleqlu aneghneghqilleqlu qerngaagmek qepghaqayuguuk . Tamaaken apalluqluku Abraham-em ugpeqillgha iighwightekaqaa aneghneghqelleghqun .
Enkaam Akuzitet Igaqegkat whaten pillghit Abraham-emeng apeghiiqaagut , " Abraham-em ugpeqegkaqegkanga Kiyaghneq . Tamaaken apalluqluku Kiyaghneghem tugukliqaqegkanga Abraham seghleghqumangilngughestun . " Enkaam Kiyaghneghem Abraham ilakumtaaqniluku pikaqaa .
Kiyaghneghem tuguklighaqaa yuuk aneghneghqillghakunllu ugpeqillghakunllu ; tugukliigataa ugpeqilleraaghinaakun .
Rahab-llu usputaaguq . Akikikayuguyalghii yugusimineng . Iwernga Kiyaghneghem tugukliqaqegkanga seghleghqumangilngughestun apalluqluku kayusighillgha . Joshua-m kayagtekaqegkek maalghuk yugek aksaqluku nunangat yuvghiighesqelluku . Yuget ivaghyatkek , Rahab-em allakun tuumkun anagtestekakek .
Enkaangam yugusiq taghneghangunani tuqungaaq , ugpeqilleqlu aneghneghqillngunani tuqungaaq .
Ugpeqaalgutemni , allullusi apeghtughistengughtefqaafsi Kiyaghneghem Akuzitanganeng , qayughllak liisimakaghsi whangkuta apeghtughisteni nanqigtengngwaaghataghaghyaghqaagukut .
Qamaglluta anaggutaghaneghtughllagtukut . Kina alngunak yuuk akuzilleghmikun anaggusigalnguq elqughutngapestaaghuuq . Yugem elqughutngalghiim talwa yugusinillu agghitkelluku ayuqsaghqaqa .
Savikenghaaghhaat sanitmun ayuqluki kuunit qaanghitnun kanaghtaqaput qaatkesqelluta enkaam whangkuta igleghutaqaput .
Sumeghtaghaatkaghtekiqunllu angyaghpagllaget ; aquutasquvegaghhaam qiiftaqii angyalgem piyukellghanun talwa anuqateghllagyaghngaan .
Ulullu mekestaaghhaaguq iwernga aangaayugneghllaguuq . Kenghhaam uqfilghuteghllaget kumaghsaghqaqii !
Ulullu kenghestun ayuquq . Esleqngaaq seghleghqelleghmeng enkaam seghleghqumallgha mingitkayuguuq yugusimun . Enkaam naafqiikayuguuq kiyaghtaallemnneng qayughllak hell-em kenghan kumaghtaqaa .
Allaaghhiinaat teghikusat , qawaaget , nemeghyat , meghem teghikusii qimugtekayuguut , aaqun yugem qimugtaqii
iwernga kitum alngunak qimuggnaanghitaa ulu . Neklegigalnguuguq , seghleghuuq , esleqngaaq tuqunalghiimeng poison-meng .
Ulu usuqusiqaqaghput Atanemnnun Atamun . Naqam seghleghmeng neghyugtaghaasiqaqaghput yulgutemnnun , Kiyaghneghem ulimaaghitnun ellmisugnilluki .
Usuqilleqlu , seghleghmengllu neghyugtaghalleq aanegkayuguuk ataasimeng qaneghmeng . Ugpeqaalgutemni , tawatesaghqaanghisaghtuq .
Pinilghiillu seghleqlu meq maaqegkayuwaak ataasimeng sengngumeng ?
Ugpeqaalgutemni , figs-em uqfiga piitestinaanghituq olives-meng . Tawateghpigaq grapes-em vine-nga piitestinaanghituq figs-meng . Talwa meghtaghvik taghyughnilngughmeng meqelghii pinilghiimeng meghituq .
Kina akulegpesinita peghqinelghii , liigikimalghiillu ? Tawatetelleni kelgulligu pinitun kiyaghtaalleghmikun , aneghneghqilleghmikunllu qusevegngaghmi .
Iwernga ilugpesigun aqinangakufsillu , ellngiinaayugneghukufsillu iqlengiqutkegpenaan ipapighqelleq , qaghyalleghpesigun liisimanilusi .
Tawatelnguq peghqinelleq qilagtaanghituq , nunameng pinguuq . Kiyaghneghem Taghneghagkeneng pingunghituq , tughneghaghmeng pinguuq .
Nani alngunak aqinallelgunghanillu , ellnginaayugllelgunghanillu taawa kipullginaallelwaaquq , sangwaatlu allaaghhiinaat seghleghet tawantaqut .
Iwernga peghqinelleq qilagtaq kiyang pelungituq . Amalleqaa nekeggmetuq , kavyugituq , malighqutaqingaaq , nangllegtaghtuq , pinistaghhiinatun pikayuguuq , taniillghituq , yupiinghuuq .
Nekeggmelleq piitutestun ayuquq . Tamaakut nekeggmelleghmun qepghaqayuget piitesighaghaqiit , enkaam saghnaaqut elqughngalghiimengllu pinilghiimengllu kiyaghtaalleghmeggni .
Saam aaghtiiraaghutestaqisillu , pillugutestaqiisillu ? Apalluqaqaghsi , seghleghem piyukelleghpesi pilluwaghaqii pinilghiit piyukellesi .
Qiliighaqusi avanginneghpesini enkaam yugtaghyaghqaghtaqusi allgeghhnaluki qiliiqegkasi . Qiliighllagaqusi taawanginaq allgeghtepagningitaqasi enkaam aaghtiiraaghutaqusi , pilluwutaqusi . Allgeghusigatusi Kiyaghneq aapsigatutegpesineng .
Talwa aapteghngaaghpesigu Kiyaghneq allgeghsigatasi qayughllak seghleghmun atughqaaluki aaptaqelghiisi . Piyukegkaghsi elpesi katam piyukegkaghhiinaghpesinun ayuqaqelghii .
Ukughsi ataasiighneghilngughni ! Liisimakenghistegguu piniqegkufsigu nunam seghlegha , ugumikaghsi Kiyaghneq ? Kitum alngunak piniqegkumigu nunam seghlegha anguyaguuq Kiyaghneghmun .
Sumeghtaghaghpenasi Akuzitet Igaqegkat temnginguniluku whaten pillghat , taghneghak kiyaghlleghhiik ilumnni aqinanaqneghtuuk .
Tamaaken apalluqluku Kiyaghneghem kayusiitaghaghaqiinkut nuqetutesqelluki piyukelleluput . Iwernga Akuzitet Igaqegkat piit , " Kiyaghneghem kayusighaqii qusevegngalghiit puuru kipullegmun piiqii qukaayugneghet . "
Tuunlusi elpesineng katam Kiyaghneghmun . Ayaklighteggu tughneghaq , anagniighllequq elpesineng .
Qantaghalliighaghtek Kiyaghneghmun , Kiyaghneq qantaghalliighaghllequq elpesinun . Seghleghqesteni , uughtughtek ! Elpesi ataasiightellghilngughni , ukmangighteki ilusi qaamkut .
Quyanghitek , asemeghqitek , qiyatek ! Nenglaghqiqellesi qiyallghughteki , quyallesi quyanghilnguughtesteki .
Qusevegtek Ataneghmun , quulvaghlleqiisi .
Ugpeqaalgutemni , seghlequughutegpenasi . Kitum alngunak seghlequuqumigu ugpeqaalguteni , seghlequughlleqii Liilightuusat . Nanqigtekumigullu ugpeqaalguteni nanqigtengngwii Liilightuusat . Nanqigtekufki Liilightuusat qaatkengngunghitaten . Yeghlegi Liilightuusat nanqigtistekaaten .
Kiyaghneghhiinaaguq Liilightuusangllaghta , nanqigtisiiluki atuqaqii , enkaam sangan始ngam nanqigsigu yulguten ? Kiyaghneghhiinaaguq yugulighiyaghqaq , naafqiyaghqaq .
Ilasi whaten piiqut , " Aghneghmi nalighmeng unaami tawavek nunamun aghulaqellequnga . Tamaanllequnga ataasiq ayumiqulleq , maningllaghllequnga . "
Iwernga nallukaghsi unaami salleghqaghsi ! Talwa nallukaghsi unguvalleghpesi tagtalkaghqaa . Unguvalleghsi takesqughhaaguq , agepsughruggaghestun ayuquq , mulugpenani aviighutkayuk .
Itupill whaten piiqitek , " Atanghem piyukelqegkagu unguvakestaghllequkut enkaam apeghiighutaqellequkut sameng alngunak . "
Tawaten pinghilkufsi aangaayugllequsillu qanangullequsillu . Tamaakut aangaayugtellghet seghleghuut .
Enkaam kitum alngunak liisimakeghngaaghmigu pinitun pilleq atuqenghilkumigu , seghleghqengnguuq .
Nagatek aklungilngughni ! Qiyakestaghtek , iilqekestaghtek qayughllak seghleliighnaqnguusi .
Aklungisi aghumaat , aatkasi moth-em neghumii .
Gold-esillu silver-esillu anaghtaamaat . Anaghtaallghita ipapighqennaqngwaa ellnginaayugneghulleghsillu , pakigneghulleghsillu nanqigtellengegkufsi . Taagken anaghtaallghem yugusisi naafqelleqii katam kenghestun . Qaywa kingulighnun aghneghnun lliighngaaghpesi , qerngughtimanginaagusi wata aklungighinalusi .
Talwa akileghtullghitasi qepghaghtesi unataqat piitesiighaghvigpesini . Nagateki akuzilgallghit . Atanghem aghtughyaghqaanghiteghllagem nagaquumii akilghuullghit .
Kiyaghtaalleghpesini whani nunami , aklungitutegpesineng sangwaa alngunak piyukegkaghsi allgeghtaqaghsi efqughhnalusi elpesineng katam . Tawaten pilleghpesigun penniighestun ayuqusi . Penniighet qugilisighat nallukaat qantaghaqun tuqutelleghqaghteng . Nallukestegguu qantaghaqun Atanghem nanqigtilleghqaa ?
Elpesinguut nanqigtistikatlu tuqutistikatlu anaggusimangilngughneng yugneng , ellngita ayakliimangitiisi .
Ugpeqaalgutemni , qelaneghpenasi kenlanga Atanghem taginqigtelleghqaanun . Piitesiighaghta usputaqiteggu . Nunami piitesiighaghluni qelaneghyukaghpenani utaqiigaquq uksaaghemllu upenghaamllu eslalluwaneng nagustikayugmeng piisaghqaneng .
Elpesillu qelaneneghllugutek neghyumanginaghlusi qayughllak Ataneq tagiyaghtughtuq .
Ugpeqaalgutemni , seghlequughpenaki ilasi enkaam Atanghem nanqiggneghillisi . Ellnganguuq Nanqigtista kaasaghtungestalghii .
Ugpeqaalgutemni , neqamikluki uuknaliqistet akuzikat aatghakun Atanghem . Usputaqiteki qelaneghpenateng nuqenneghtuluteng ikfiqelleghmi pikat .
Quyanganiiqaput uuknaliqistet qayughllak ikfiqngughngaaghmeng paninang neghyukumanginaqaqaat Ataneq . Nagaquqaqaghsi Job-em nuqenneghtullgha , quyastellghallu Ataneghmeng ikfiqellgha alpagyan . Enkaam Job-kun Atanghem liitestiisi nafughtalleghminengllu nangllegtalleghminengllu .
Ugpeqaalgutemni , apeghnaqegkegka una megnunapigtuq . Akeqineghpesini , akeqigpenasi qilagkun , nalighmeng nunakun , nalighmeng sakun alngunak . Piyaghqaakufsi legan aang始ghhaasi , piyaghqaanghilkufsi legan nakaaghhaasi . Enkaam atuqaqiteki akequsasi , tawaten pikufsi Atanghem nanqiggnaanghitiisi aghyuughyaghqaalusi .
Kina akulegpesini ikfiqngwaa ? Yughaghli . Kina quyangaa ? Ilagaghli usuqilleghmeng .
Kina qinuyuwaa ? Tuqlughliki Elder-et enkaam yughaatkellitgu mesiighqelluku Aatghakun Atanghem .
Yughallghem ugpeqilleghqun naallghusaghqaqaa qinuyulghii yuuk . Enkaam Atanghem yugunqwuughtesneqiglleqaa , seghleghqellghillu seghevulleqii .
Tamaaken apalluqluku aapghaqluki seghleghqellesi ilagpesinun , yughaatkututaqlusi naallghutellengesqellusi . Elqughutngalghiim yugem yughallghi iknaqeghllagtut , allgeghutkayuguut .
Elijah yuguuq whangkutestun ayuqelgii . Taakunginaghhaagneng yughaqaq eslallugughtefqaan pisqelluku . Enkaam eslallugughsimangilnguq pingayut ayumiqullghet alla aghvinlek tanqiq ilalluku .
Taagken alla yughaqaq eslallugughtesqelluku . Enkaam eslallugughsalghiimi nuna piitestikaq neghyaghqameng .
Ugpeqaalgutemni , una kinguliiguq apeghyukegka elpesinun . Nalighsi ugpeqinaniqan apeghtuusapigneng , kitum kayusighligu ugpeqinqigtelleghmun . Tawaten pikumigu yugulisleqaak seghleghqestem unguvasikek tuqulleghmeng . Kiyaghneghemllu seghuvulleqii taam seghleghqestem seghleghqellelghuteghllagi .
Ukut latat Peter-meng pinguut apostle-nganeng Jesus Christ-am , Kiyaghneghem nakmikegkiitnun yugnun aghulaquutestekat Pontus-mun , Galatia-mun , Cappadocia-mun , Asia-mun , Bithynia-munllu .
Neghighluku Kiyaghneghem Atam nakmikegkaqiisi ellminun yugulusi , Agleghnalghiimllu Taghnegham pelungighsaqaqiisi . Tawaten pikaaguk qaatkutesqellusi Jesus Christ-amun , ukmangiightesqellusillu aawakun . Kiyaghneghem kayusillghallu nekeggmellghallu wata nulalik elpesinun .
Usuqelteggu Kiyaghneq , Atanga Atanemta Jesus Christ-am ! Apalluqluku nangllegtalleghllani allgenqigtestiinkut unguvaghtelleghmikun Jesus Christ-a tuqulleghmeng . Taam sighimallengesteghllagiinkut nalluneqniilngughmeng .
Enkaam utaqangwaaput piliisaghqaput quyastelleghllaget Kiyaghneghem aflengakegkangi yugminun . Aflengakngwii qilagmi elpesinun enkaam aghunaanghitut , naavnaanghitut , ghevnaanghitutlu .
Kiyaghneghem aghtughyaghqaanghilleghmikun paqniighsaghlleqiisi ugpeqilleghpesigun . Enkaam kenletghuutelleghmi aliighlleqaa yugulilleq yataghqegkaq elpesinun .
Taam quyamastiisi , qaywa maaten natengiighhaq allaaghhiinaghmeng seghleliighyaghngaaghpesi .
Tamaakut seghleliighet nanghiiqusiigut ipapighqennalusi ugpeqillepiilgutsi . Ugpeqilleghsi megnunaghataghalghiinguq gold-nneng . Gold-et nanghiiquneghmegteki keneghqun naafqegkayuguut . Paninang kenghet atuqaqiit pelungighnaluki . Tawateghpigaq ugpeqilleghsi nanghiiquyaghqaaguq . Aghuliiskan pelungilluni , allgeghlleqaghsi usuqelleq , nighughqelleq , quulvalleq Kiyaghneghmeng aliightekagu Jesus Christ-a .
Esghiigateghngaaghpesigu piniqaghsi , esghanghiteghngaaghpesigu maaten ugpeqaghsi . Enkaam quyaghllaguusi repall aapghwaaghpagningitaghsi angtalanga quyalleghpesi ,
qayughllak allgeghtengngukesi yugulillgha unguvasighpesi . Taananguuq apallaa ugpeqilghiisi Christ-akun .
Neghighluku uuknaliqistet liigikngwaaghnaqegkaqaat taana yugulilleq . Uuknaliqutkegkaqaat tunusaq Kiyaghneghem tuunyaghqaa elpesinun .
Taghneghakek Christ-am uuknaliqistet ilungitnitkaaguk . Ungipaatekestaqaqii ikfiqelleghqaaneng Christ-am , quulvallengelleghqaghllaganengllu ikfiqellghan kingunganeng . Enkaam uuknaliqistet liigiknaqutkegkaqaat kinanguyaghqaatanga Christ-a , qakunllu tamaakut piyaghqaatangi .
Kiyaghneghem uuknaliqistet liigikestekaqii uuknaliqutkegkiit ellngitnun pingunghinniluki , iwernga elpesinun pinguniluki . Agleghnalghiik Taghneghak kayagtekaaguk qilagmeng . Ellngan aghtughyaghqaanghillghakun ungipaqilghiit Pinilghiineng Ungipaneng ungipaatkaqiisi tamaaken . Talwa yaqulget liigiksupigtekaqiit tamaakut .
Enkaangam umyugasi apeghiighsaghwaaghluki ayuqiteki salleghqamun . Umyugasi whateghlluwaaghuluki , sighimakngwaaghteggullu tunusaq yugulillengelleq Kiyaghneghem tuunyaghqaa Jesus Christ-a tagikan .
Qaatkullusi Kiyaghneghmun qayughllak avaqutaqiisi . Enkaam atuqegpenaki seghleghet piyukellesi atuqnguyaqesi . Tawatesaghtusi nallukutegpesineng naten Kiyaghneghem kiyaghtesqesullghan ayuqutanga .
Kiyaghneq nakmikestezi , pelungitutanganeng elpesillu pelungitek salleghpesigun tamaghhaakun .
Akuzitni Igaqegkani igaqngaaq , " Pelungitek qayughllak whanga pelungitunga . "
Yughaneghpesini Kiyaghneghmun Atakniiqaghsi . Nanqigtaqaa atunengwaaq yuuk tamaghhaan salleghtulngatun . Enkaam talluqiteggu nunataamalusi nunami whani .
Liisimakaghsi sivunghani kiyaghtekaagusi sasiigpenasi katam sivuneghpesistun . Iwernga Kiyaghneghem itemutkaqiisi taagken sasiinghilngughmeng kiyaghtaalleghmeng . Tukfillghitiisi silver-meng nalighmeng gold-meng naavegkayugmeng ,
iwernga tukfiqaqiisi megnunapiglleghhiimeng aawaneng Christ-am . Ellnga penniighaghaghtun ayuquq sallwhaaghhiilnguq .
Kiyaghneghem nakmikegkaqaa Christ-a talwa sivungani nuna ulimallghilluku . Maaten kingulighni aghneghni aliightekaqaa elpesi apalluqlusi .
Christ-akun ugpeqaghsi Kiyaghneq . Ellngan unguvaghtekaqaa Christ-a tuqulleghmeng , quulvaghllakaqaallu . Tamaaken apalluqluku ugpeqilleghsi , sighimalleghsi Kiyaghneghmun ayuquq .
Qaatkutelleghqun ipapighqelleghmun pelungightekaqasi unguvasisi , enkaam piniqepiigasi ugpeqaalgutesi . Piniqutekestaghtek ilugpesineng qamaken .
Allgenqigtekaagusi . Unguvalleghraghaghsi tuqukayugmeng pingunghituq , iwernga tuqungigalngughmeng pinguuq . Allgenqigtekaagusi Kiyaghneghem akuzitangitgun , unguvalghiit , kenlengilnguut .
Akuzitni Igaqegkani igaqngaaq , " Qamaglluteng yuget vegaaghestun ayuqut , pinighnallghillu piitesighaghestun ayuqut . Vegaaghet palighaqut , piitesighaatlu ifkaghaqut ,
iwernga akuzitangi Kiyaghneghem quunpekaghqaagut . " Taakusta akuzitet Pinilghiit Ungipat ungipaqegkangit elpesinun .
Enkaam taaqiteggu allaaghhiinaq seghleq atuqegkaghsi . Iqlengiqnanightek , piniiyuggnanightek , aqinananightek , seghlequughunnanighteklu .
Allgenghhaghhaat quunpeng mamaghyugaqut . Ellngistun quunpeng mamaghyugtek pelungilngughmeng taghnegham mamaaneng . Angtaniitesleqaa yugulilleghsi ,
qayughllak naasiighaghsi Atanghem nangllegtallgha .
Tagitek Ataneghmun , ellnga unguvalghiinguuq uyghak . Yuget ighsakegkaat sasiinghilngughestun , iwernga Kiyaghneghem nakmikegkaqaa megnunaghluku .
Elpesillu unguvalghiistun uyghagestun ayuqusi , enkaam Agleghnalghiim Taghnegham nekeftusiqlisi Kiyaghneghem mangteghaanun . Qepghaalleqaghsi aaftekaalusi priest-et tuunilghiit aghqutmeng Kiyaghneghmun . Ellngan tuguklighlleqii aghqutet Jesus Christ-akun .
Igaqegkaalghii Akuzitni Igaqegkani whaten , " Zion-mi nekegtaqaqa megnunalghii uyghak ; kangigham uyghakaa nakmikegkaqa . Kina alngunak ugpeqilghii ellnganeng kayngumiqnaanghituq . "
Taana uyghak megnunapigtuq elpesinun ugpeqilghiinun . Iwernga ugpeqingigalngughnun whatelnguuguq , " Taana uyghak mangteghangllaghtet ighsakegkaat , kangigham uyghakaaghsimakanga . "
Amalleqa , " Taam uyghagem yuget naagtestaqii , iqustaqiillu . " Naagtaqut qayughllak qaatkusigalnguut Kiyaghneghem akuzitanganun . Tawaten Kiyaghneghem uspeqegkaqii .
Iwernga elpesi yugni nakmikegkaagusi , umiilgem priest-ekiisi , aaftekaagusi yugni , Kiyaghneghem ellngan katam yukiisi . Nakmikegkaagusi aapghesqelluki allaaghlluwhaat aneghneghqillghi Kiyaghneghem , tagsighikaq elpesineng mamlegllagmeng ellmi katam allaaghlluwhaghmun nighugminun .
Sivunghani Kiyaghneghem yukenghisaghiisi , iwernga maaten yuliisimiisi . Sivunghani nalluksaghaghsi Kiyaghneghem nangllegtallgha , iwernga maaten allgeghsimaaghsi nangllegtallgha .
Ilakumtaamni , nunataagusillu allaneghtaagusillu nunami whani . Enkaam kayemamsi ilapgategpenasi yugusighpesi piyukellghanun , qayughllak yugusim piyukellghan pilluwaangwaa unguvasighsi .
Pinitun kiyaghtek akulngitni ugpeqaanghilnguut , luuraq ellngita seghletun pistenguninayukangisi . Esghaqumegteki aneghneghqillesi usuqelleqaat Kiyaghneq Aghneghani Christ-am tagillghan .
Ataneq apalluqluku malighqutaqlusi kiyaghtek tamaghhiitnun kavemem igleghutistengitnun . Qaatkullusi umiilegmun ; ellnganguuq angelleghpigaq igleghutista .
Qaatkellukillu igleghutistet ; umiilgem aghyuughiyaqlegughtestaqii seghletun pistenun , usuqiyaqleghughtestekaqiillu pinitun pistenun .
Kiyaghneghem piyukelqaa pinitun pilleghpesigun nepiightesqelluki nalluuqat temngitwhameng akuzillghiit .
Kiyaghtek itemngalghiistun iwernga itemngalleghsi atuqefqaan seghleghmun . Kiyaghtek qepghaghtelaaghulusi Kiyaghneghmun .
Quulvaghluku tamaghhaa yuuk , piniqluki ugpeqaalgutesi , alikluku Kiyaghneq , quulvaghlukullu umiilek .
Elpesi qepghaghtelaaghni qaatkutek piliitestegpesinun siivakellelighlusi . Qaatkegpenaki nangllegtaghhiinaatlu , umyugaqegtaghhiinaatlu , iwernga qaatkaqitekillu amyuqetalghiit .
Kiyaghneghem efquqaqiisi sumeghmikneghpesigu ellnga ikfiqngulusi sameng sapiglleghhiistun .
Iwernga suflughsimakufsiki qevutqullesi , seghletun pillesi apalluqluki , kitum alngunak usuqnaanghitiisi . Naqamenraq suflughsimakufsigu ikfiqelleq pinitun pilleghpesinun , taawa Kiyaghneghem efquqelleqiisi .
Kiyaghneghem nakmikegkaqiisi suflughtesqelluki ikfiqellghet qayughllak Christ-am ikfiqutkegkaqiisi . Ikfiqellgha usputaaguq elpesinun maligtesqelluku .
Ellnga seghleghqigatuq , iqlengiqigatuq .
Seghlequullengaqngami akisimangitii . Ikfiqaqngami akeqsagsimangitii . Itupill neghyukutkaaguq ellmineng nanqigtikayugmun elqughaghlluku .
Christ-am ellmineng katam aglaatkaqii seghleghqelleput yugusighmikluki qaquuramun . Tawaten pikaaguq tuqungasqelluta seghleghqelleghmun unguvasqelluta elqughutngalleghmun . Kiitiqullghakun naallghutkaagusi .
Penniighestun aghulaqaatalghiistun ayuqsaghtusi . Iwernga maaten uteghniimaasi Penniighniightemun Kelengakistenganun unguvasighpesi .
Elpesi ugiiqani , kiyaghtek qaatkullusi ugigpesinun . Ilangi nuliilget ugpeqingigalnguugut Kiyaghneghem akuzitanganeng . Iwernga tawaten kiyaghtelleghpesigun ugpeqaaghhnayukata sameng pinghiteghngaaghpesiki ,
qayughllak esghapakangat pelungitun kiyaghtaalleghsi , alikilleghsillu Kiyaghneghmun .
Nuyaqegsallghem , ullngaqellghem gold-meng , aarrallghem pinighnaghsiigatii ilusi .
Itupill pinighnaghtek ilugpesigun qusevegllelighlusi , nekeggmellelighlusillu . Tawatelnguq pinighnalleq quunpekaghqaaguq , megnunaghllagtuq Kiyaghneghmun .
Sivunghani agani , aghnat maniguutkayuget Kiyaghneghmun pinighnaghsaqayuguut ilumegteggun , qusevegllelighluteng , nekeggmellelighlutengllu . Neghyukegkaqaat Kiyaghneq , qaatkegkaqiitlu ugiteng .
Sarah tawatetkaaguq ! Qaatkegkaqaa Abraham , atanqennikaqaallu . Enkaam elpesi panikiisi pinitun pimakufsi , alingigalkufsillu sameng alngunak .
Elpesillu nulightuqani kiyaghuteki nuliisi liigikluki natetulangi qayughllak kayaataghaghtut elpesineng . Quulvaghluki nuliisi qayughllak atunem allgeghsaghqaqaghsi Kiyaghneghem tunusaa kenlengilnguq unguvalleq . Tawaten pikufsi saam alngunak pillgilliqnaanghitii yughallesi .
Taaqnighnaqanka sameng pillghenka whaten : qamagllusi ataasistun sumeghnelgutek , aqniqututek , piniqutek anglegutkullghiistun , nangllekututek , qusevgututek .
Yuget seghletun pikangisi akitegpenaki seghletun , nalighmeng seghlequuqangisi akitegpenaki seghlequughmeng . Itupill akiteki quyastelleghmeng , qayughllak Kiyaghneghem nakmikegkaqiisi tawaten pisqellusi elpesinun allgeghtesqelluku quyastilleni .
Akuzitet Igaqegkat pillghistun , " Kina alngunak quyangalghiimeng unguvallelguyukumi , quyamalghiinengllu aghnelguyukumi , seghletun akuzineghmeng taaqli , iqlengiqnanighlillu .
Seghletun pinanighluni , pinitun pili . Nekeggmennaqlunillu kiyaghlli ,
qayughllak Atanghem esghapawii elqughutngalghiit , nagataqiillu yughallghit . Iwernga Atanghem tengvimun ayuqii seghletun pilghiit . "
Kitumngam aqnighlleqisi sagiqngukufsi pinitun pilleghmun ?
Iwernga ikfiqeghngaaghpesi pinitun pilleghmun quyastellengellequsi . Alikegpenaki yuget , talwa sumeghyaligpenasi .
Iwernga ilugpesigun manigughaqiteggu Christ-a Atanghuluku . Kitum alngunak aaptekangisi sighimalleghmeng ilugpesinilngughmeng quunpeng liigiknatun kiimsighyaqleggiinaawaqiteki .
Iwernga kiimsighaqiteki qusevegllelighlusi , siivakillelighlusi . Seghleghqenghilkufsi umyugasi seghleghninaanghitut . Enkaam yuget seghlequuqangisi pinitun kiyaghtelleghpesineng Christ-akun , kaynguyugllequt tawaten akuzilleghmeggneng .
Iwernga Kiyaghneghem piyukelqengngukagu ikfiqesqellusi pinitun pilleghmun , taana itagnaghataghaghtuq ikfiqelleghqaghpesineng seghletun pilleghmun .
Christ-a tuqukaaguq ataasighhaghmeng apalluqluki yuget seghleghqellghit . Seghleghqumangituq , iwernga tuqumatkegkaqii seghleghqestet taginnaluki Kiyaghneghmun . Yugusii tuqutkaaguq iwernga taghneghakek unguvaghtekaaguk .
Enkaam taghneghaaluni ungipaghyaghtuqaaguq taghneghanun anusimingllaghvigmelngughnun .
Taakunguut qaatkusimangilnguut Kiyaghneghmun neghighluku Noah kiyaghtengnguluku . Noah ark-engllaaluku Kiyaghneq qelaneghpenani utaqiikaaguq qaatkusimangilngughnun avuteghqesqelluki . Pingayuneng inglullgiinaat yuget iteghluteng ark-mun yugulikaagut meghqun .
Taananguuq meq usputaq paaptaayelleghmun yugulighilghii elpesineng maaten unguvaghtellghakun Jesus Christ . Paaptaayelleq iqangiisiinghituq yugusimun . Itupill paaptaayelleghqun akeqiikut Kiyaghneghmun umyugamnneng seghleghningilngughmeng .
Jesus Christ-a qilagmun mayughluni aghenqigneghanituq Kiyaghneghem . Enkaam igleghutngwii qamaglluki yaqulget , qilagem igleghutistengi , aghtughyaghqaanghillghetlu .
Ikfiqegkaatanganeng Christ-a yugusimikun elpesillu yataaghqitek ikfiqsaghqaalusi Christ-atun , qayughllak kina alngunak yugusimikun ikfiqelghii seghleghqesugnaniimaaq .
Enkaam whaken kenlekluku unguvalleghpesi tagtalngatun malighqutaqegpenasi yugusighpesi piyukellghanun , iwernga atuqiteggu Kiyaghneghem piyukellgha .
Sivunghani seghletun kiyaghtelqinaghtusi qaatkusigalngughestun Kiyaghneghmun . Whaten pikaagusi : seghleghnapiglluku atuqutkayuguyaghtusi , qiliiqutaqlusi , suumuutaqlusi , qerngughutullusi uglapestaaghet seghleghet atuqaqluki , neqenghaghqellusi , meghuuteghllaglusi enkaam alngunaseghaghllagughtaqusi , maniguqaqasillu iinghutkat kiyaghnengllaqat .
Kiyaghhnanilghiisi ugpeqaanghilngughestun , liigikigataat sangan ilannaniitsi seghletun kiyaghtaalleghmeggnun , enkaam seghlequughaqiisi .
Iwernga salleteng ellmeggneng katam apeghyaghqaqiit Kiyaghneghmun , nanqigtiyaqleggiinaghmun unguvalghiinengllu tuqukanengllu .
Tamaaken apalluqluku Pinilghiit Ungipat ungipaqegkaagut talwa tuqukanun . Tamaakut nanqigtekaagut unguvanguluteng nunami whani . Iwernga Pinilghiit Ungipat ungipaqegkaagut ellngitnun , enkaam taghneghiit kiyaghsaghqaaghllequt katam Kiyaghneghem kiyaghtellghatun .
Sangwaa qamaglluni kenletghuusaghtughtuq . Tamaaken apalluqluku whateghlluwaaghuluki umyugasi , nuqenneghtulusi yughaghyaghqaalusi yughalleghqaghpesistun .
Megnunalleghpigaaguq una : piniqutepiiglusi qayughllak piniqellghem seghevutestaqii seghleghqellelghuteghllaget .
Upughanghulusi qikeghqufqaafsi .
Tamaghhaghpesi allgeghutkaagusi tunusaneng atughqameng ilagpesinun . Allaaghhiinaat tunusat Kiyaghneghmeng pisi atuqaqiteki pinitun .
Tunusalget akuzimun akuzilit Kiyaghneghem akuzitanganeng . Tunusalget qepghhaatimun qepghhaatilit iknaqellelighluteng Kiyaghneghem tuunegkaaneng . Enkaam salleghpesigun tamaghhaakun Kiyaghneq usuqellengellequq Jesus Christ-akun . Ellngan pikaak nighughqelleqlu aghtughyaghqaanghilleqlu quunperugllak kenlengunaan . Amen .
Piniqegkamni ilakumtaamni , quupkaghpenasi seghleliighrukutaaghllaget kaaskangisi nanghiighsaghaghnalusi . Nanghiighsaghallesi allakaayagunghitut .
Itupill quyatek ilallghiisi Christ-am ikfiqellghanun quyangaghllagesqellusi nighughqellgha aliightekan .
Seghlequuqangisi apalluqluku maligsaaghtengumalleghsi Christ-amun , quyastellelguusi qayughllak Kiyaghneghem Taghneghakek nighughqengngalghiik kiyaghtengnguuk elpesini .
Ikfiqsaghqaakufsi , ikfiqegpenasi yugtaghtengulusi , teglegniightengulusi , seghletun pistengulusi , nalighmeng yanutqustengulusi .
Naqamenraq ikfiqsaghqaakufsi Christian-ngutegpesineng , kaynguyugpenasi iwernga usuqnakesi Kiyaghneq atiqangisi Christ-am aatghaneng .
Nanqigtilleghqaq kaatuq , sivukluni piinlighllequq Kiyaghneghem nengllugutangakun . Piinlighnaqngukan whangkutgun , salleqan始ngam qaatkusigalnguut Kiyaghneghem Pinilghiinun Ungipaanun ?
Akuzitet Igaqegkat pillghistun , " Elqughutngalghiit pegnem yugulikaakuyeng , avelghasingwaalghiit Kiyaghneghmeng , seghleghqestetlu naten始ngam yugulillengelleqat ? "
Enkaangam tamaakut ikfiqelghiit apalluqluku Kiyaghneghem piyukellgha , elqughulluteng pillequt , neghyukulleqiitlu unguvasiteng ataasiighmelngughmun Ulimaghistemun .
Sameng piighsuganka Elder-et yughaghvigpesinilnguut . Whangallu Elder-nguunga , esghapakaqegkegkallu Christ-am ikfiqellgha , ilasaghqaagungallu Christ-am aangelleghllaganun Kiyaghneghem aliightekagu .
Enkaam qeleghyugamsi Elder-eni whaten : Penniighniightengutek Kiyaghneghem penniighitnun ; neghyukutkaqii elpesinun aflengakesqelluki . Aflengakiteki qayughllak aflengaksukesi , nakaan qayughllak piyaghqaategpesineng . Kiyaghneghem tawaten pisqesugiisi . Aflengakiteki nakaan akileghtuusangepigesnaghnalusi , iwernga qayughllak kayusighyugukesi .
Agghitkaqegpenaki aflengakegkasi , iwernga maligsugnaghqitek ellngitnun .
Enkaam Igleghutistengat Penniighniightet tagikan allgeghullequsi pinighnapiglleghhiimeng qaghpameng qelmeghiisaghqaanghilngughmeng .
Tawateghpigaq elpesi uyuqlighni malighqutaqlusi siivanlleghnun . Qamagllusi qusevgutullusi qayughllak Akuzitet Igaqegkat pikaagut , " Kiyaghneghem kipullegmun ayuqii qukaayugneghet , iwernga kayusighaqii qusevegngalghiit . "
Enkaangam elpesineng katam qusevegngatek Kiyaghneghmun aghtughyaghqaanghiteghllagmun . Taagken quulvaghlleqiisi nakmikegkamini aghneghmi .
Qamaglluki sumeghyalitkegkasi pegteki ellnganun , qayughllak aflengakngwiisi .
Liisimalusi , kelengalusi . Anguyagsi Tughneghaq igleghanguuq uginilghiitun lion-etun , ivaghiiquq kina naafqennaluku .
Ayaklighteggu Tughneghaq ayepsugilngughqun ugpeqilleghpesigun , liisimakluki ugpeqaalgutesi nunataghhaanilnguut tawaten ellngitlu ikfiqnguut .
Iwernga natengiighhaq ikfiqelleghpesi kingunganeng , Kiyaghneghem piniqingaghllagem tamanganun , ellngan katam nallghusaalleqiisi sameng tamaghhaaneng . Ugpeqillesi iknaqughsaghlleqii , ayepsugighsaghlleqii , aghuliilkaaghtesleqii . Kiyaghneghem nakmikegkaqiisi Christ-akun ilatesqellusi kenlengilngughmun aangelleghllagminun .
Qamaglluku aghtughyaghqaanghilleq ellngan pikaa quunperugllak ! Amen .
Silas ataasiighmelnguuguq ugpeqaalguta ; igaataqaanga takestaaghhaghteggun latamkun elpesinun . Latanka Kiyaghneghem piniqellepiiganeng ayuqut . Ungipaatamsillu kayemamsillu kiyaghtekestiisqellusi piniqellghani .
Ugpeqaalgutesi Babylon-melnguut , elpesistun Kiyaghneghem nakmikegkaqii . Ellngitallu , ighneghmallu Mark-em piniqiisinguq .
Quyakutaqitek naalleghqun Christ-am piniqellghakun . Nekeggmelleq tamaghhaghpesinilli Christ-am piliitkiitni .
Ukut latat Simon Peter-meng pinguut . Qepghaghtekaangallu , apostle-kaangallu Jesus Christ-am . Lataaqamsi qamagllusi allgeghutkani ugpeqilleghmeng whangkutestun ayuqelghiimeng . Allgeghtekaqaghput ugpeqilleghput elqughutngallghakun Jesus Christ-am , Kiyaghneqegkefutlu Yugulighistekegkefutlu .
Piniqellghenkuk nekeggmellghenkuk wata nulalik elpesini liisimakelleghpesigun Kiyaghneqlu Jesus-lu Ataneghput .
Jesus aghtughyaghqaanghillelguuq Kiyaghneghmeng . Taaggun aghtughyaghqaanghilleghqun tuunegkaqiinkut sameng tamaghhaaneng aklukegkamnneng kiyaghtesqelluta Kiyaghneghyuneghtuluta . Tamaakut allgeghtekaqaput qayughllak liisimakegkefut Jesus . Tuqlughiinkut ilatesqelluta quulvalleghminunllu pinilleghminunllu .
Aghtughyaghqaanghilleghmikun , Jesus-em tuunegkaqiinkut akequsamineng megnunapiglleghhiinengllu pivagnapiglleghhiinengllu . Tamaagun akequsatgun Kiyaghneghem ilatesleqiisi nangaghneghminun . Taagken anagyaqlegughlleqasi seghleghem piyukellghi nunamelnguut naafqiiyaqleget elpesineng .
Kiyaghneghem nangaghnelitkaqutanganeng elpesi , taakunginaghhaagneng pinaqellghaghsi qamaglluku ilateki ukut ugpeqilleghpesinun : ugpeqilleghpesinun ilateggu pinilleq , pinilleghpesinun ilateggu liisimalleq ,
liisimalleghpesinun ilateggu nuqetutilleq , nuqetutilleghpesinun ilateggu aghuliilkaamalleq , aghuliilkaamelleghpesinun ilateggu Kiyaghneghyuneghtulleq ,
Kiyaghneghyuneghtulleghpesinun ilateggu nangllekututelleq ugpeqaalgutegpesinun , nangllekututelleghpesinun ilateggu piniqelleq .
Tamaakut atuqngukufsiki , nulastekufsikillu kayusiilleqiisi atughqaalusillu kayutkaghqaalusillu liisimakelleghpesigun Ataneghput Jesus Christ-a .
Iwernga kitum alngunak atuqenghilkumiki tamaakut , amugtapigtuq enkaam esghaatepagningituq . Puygukaqaallu Kiyaghneghem ukmangiqaqegkanga seghleghqelleqsaqanganeng .
Enkaangam ugpeqaalgutemni , nalluneqniighwaaghteggu Kiyaghneghem tuqluqaqiisillu nakmikegkaqiisillu . Tawaten pikufsi taawa iqiteqaghhnaanghitusi Christ-ameng .
Enkaam Kiyaghneghem quyakusiqeghllaglusi iteghtesleqiisi kenlengilngughmun Ataneghpagullghanun Atanemtallu Yugulighistemtallu Jesus Christ-am .
Qaywa liisimakeghngaaghpesiki taakut ipapillghet , sagiqutngughngaaghpesikillu qaatkennaluki , iiwleng neqangughlleqamsi taakuneng ipapilleghneng elpesinun apeghtuutkamnneng .
Sumemni itagnaghtuq neqangughtaataqumsi tamaakuneng unguvangulunga .
Liisimakaqa tuquyaghtughtunga qayughllak Atanemta Jesus Christ-am ungipaatekestaqaqaanga .
Pinaqelqa qamaglluku apeghtughamsi tamaaken , enkaam tuqulleghma kingunganeng neqaataqelleqasi .
Atuqumangitaput peghqiniqutngwaaghluki ungipaghaatengllaqat aapghaqngamtekek elpesinun aghtughyaghqaanghillghallu tagillghallu Atanemta Jesus Christ-am . Whangkuta katam iyeghlluwaamnneng esghaqaqaghput ellngan aangelleghllaga .
Jesus-em allgeghtaqngagu quulvalleqlu nighughqelleqlu Kiyaghneghmeng Atameng , nagaquqaqaa menga Kiyaghneghem , Qulighpigaalghii Nighughqengngaghllak . Atam pikaqaa , " Unanguuq piniqepigtekegka Ighneqa , efquqepigtekegka . "
Whangkuta whangkunneng katam nagatkaqaghput ma qilagmeng Jesus-metaqngamta agleghnalghiimi naayghami .
Tamaaken apalluqluku whangkunni nalluneqnaqraggiitut uuknaliqistet uuknaliqutkegkiit ipangutangi . Elpesinun pinighllequt sumeghtaghaatkengngwaaqufsiki uuknaliqutkegkiit , qayughllak kenelghutam kuukgutellghatun ayuqut mamlegmun . Tawatetekestaghtek kenlanga Christ-am tagilleghqaan aghneghanun . Taagken nighuga kuukgullequq ilugpesinun , unaangum ighaleqetaaghatun ayuqluni .
Liigikngwaaghyaghqaqaghsi una : Kitum alngunak ellmineng katam liigikepagningitii sameng pisiitangi uuknaliqellghet Akuzitnilnguut Igaqegkani .
Uuknaliqistet nakmikumangitiit uuknaliqutkesaghqateng . Itupill Agleghnalghiim Taghnegham uuknaliqistet akuzitelitkaqii akuzisqelluki Kiyaghneghtameng .
Sivunghani agani uuknaliqistesiighwaaghet akulngitnisaghtut Kiyaghneghem yugitni , katam apeghtughistesighwaaghet akulegpesinillequt . Nalluneghpesini apeghtughlleqiisi iqlengameng naafqennaluki ugpeqillesi . Qaywa Christ-am Piliitestengita tukfiqaqeghngiisteng itemunnaluki seghleghqellghitneng , paninang piknanighlleqaat . Enkaam nuuskagan ellmeggneng naafqeslequt .
Yulghutet maligullequt apeghtughistesighwaaghnun kayngunalghinun kiyaghtaallghitnun . Enkaam yuget seghlequughlleqiit apeghtuusapiget atuput .
Pakigtelleghmegteggun apeghtughistesighwaaghet aklungighiyugllequt elpesineng . Enkaam apeghlleqiit apeghtuusangllaqateng maningnaluteng elpesineng . Ima neghighhaaneng Kiyaghneq Nanqigtistengatlu Naafqiistengatlu qaviigatuq aghyuughyaqlegughllukillu ayuqii .
Kiyaghneghem aghyuughumanginneghitii yaqulget seghleghqaqngata , iwernga miluutkaqii hell-mun . Tawani pisaghtiighllagmi qiipraghusighngaat , utaqiilghiit Aghneghanun Nanqigtillghem .
Neghighluku Noah kiyaghtengnguluku , Kiyaghneghem aghyuughumanginneghitii yuget avelghasingwaaghikat ellmineng , enkaam ulevestekaqaa nuna . Iwernga yugulikaqaa Noah , ilangillu maaghraghvinlek yuget . ( Noah ungipaghtengukaaguq elqughutngalghiimun kiyaghtaalleghmun . )
Kiyaghneghem aghyuuqaqaaklu neghllagek Sodom-enkuk Gomorrah-nkuk . Naafqegkaqaak keneghqun kenlanga ashes-ngughtellghegkenun . Enkaam usputaaghtekaqaak sayaghqaatangi yuget avelghasighwaaghikat Kiyaghneghmeng .
Lot elqughutngalghiinguyaghtuq yuuk kiyaghtekaq akulngitni tamaakut seghleghet yuget . Aghhutanga tamaghhaan seghleliighutkeghllakaqii unguvasigmikun esghapagluki , nagalluki seghletun kiyaghtaallghit , nuqetegpenatengllu sex-ellghit . Enkaam Atanghem yugulikaqaa .
Taawa liitaghput , Ataneq liisimakuq naten yugulilleghqameng elqughutngalghiit yuget , nanghiighsaghallengenghata . Kelengakngwiillu seghleghet yuget aghyuullengelleghmelnguut , utaqiimaluki Aghneghanun Nanqigtillghem .
Taana aghyuulleq kiyang tamaakunun ayuquq maligullghiinun yugusimeng seghletun piyukelleghllagitnun , qaatkusugigalngughnunllu kitumun alngunak . Tamaakut apeghtughistesighwaaghet tetugigatutlu ellminguyugneghuutlu . Alingegpenateng seghlequughaqiit nighugrakegtat .
Yaqulget iknaqataghaghtut , aghtughyaghqaanghitaghaghtut taakuneng nighugrakegtaneng , paninang sivungani Atanghem anaggusimaninaanghitiit nighugrakegtat .
Iwernga tamaakut apeghtughistesighwaaghet seghlequughaqiit sangwaat liigikegpenaki . Teghikusastun sumeghtaghaghpagningilnguugut . Tuqutellengellequt teghikusastun allgeghluteng teghigtughluki tuqutkat .
Uglalghiit ikfiqestaqiit enkaam Kiyaghneghem ikfiqesleqii . Talwa aghneraaghinaghmi meghuuteghllagaqut , yugusimengllu seghleghet piyukellghit atuqaqiit . Kayngusaghaateghllagaqut neqenghaghqelgusiimalusi , enkaam akulegpesini nukeggnaghqegkastunllu ellmiigutkastunllu ayuqut .
Esghaneghmegteki aghnat qiliiqaqiit . Seghleghqesuneghtuut iwernga seghleghqellelghutangita kepsughsigatngwaaghiit . Manighaqiit yuget puughhneqegtat seghleghqesugesqelluki , pakignepigtutlu . Tamaaken apalluqluku Kiyaghneghem aghyuughyaghqaqii !
Tamaakut apeghtughistesighwaaghet ugpeqnaniqaqiit apeghtuusapiget . Enkaam aghulaqegkaagut Balaam-em pillghatun pinaluteng . ( Ighneqsaqanga Beor-em . ) Quyaaquq yuget akileghtunghatni seghletun pisqelluku .
Iwernga donkey-m akuzipagningilnguum , yugem mengakun ineghtekaqaa Balaam . Enkaam aghuliightekaqaa uuknaliqista sumeghneghiilliqellghaneng .
Tamaakut apeghtughistesighwaaghet paatqastun sengngustun ayuqut , qilagwaaghestunllu ayuqut anuqeghllagem tengtekangi . Kiyaghneghem nekaghqangllaatkaqii pisaghtiighllagmi .
Aghsaaghmikameng aangaayugtaqut temngitwhameng akuzitkelluteng . Piiqut itagnaghniluku malighqutaqelleghqaq seghleghnun yugusim piyukellghanun . Enkaam yuget taaqaqutlu tawaten kiyaghtelleghmeggneng , manighaqiit tawaten pinqigtesqelluki .
Apeghtughistesighwaaghet ungipaatkaqiit tamaakut yuget itemnganiluki samun alngunak piyukellghitnun , ellngit katam itemngangunghiteghngaaghmeng . Qepghaghtelaaghuut seghleghqelleghmeggnun enkaam seghleghqellghita naafqesaqlegwii . Yuuk qepghaghtelaaghuuq alngunak samun igleqataqilghiimeng ellminun .
Yuget liitaqngamegteggu Ataneghputlu Yugulighistevutlu Jesus Christ-a anagyaghqaqaat nukeggnaa nunam . Iwernga uteghninqigtekumeng seghletun kiyaghtaalleghmeggnun aaghqutaqesimakumengllu tamaakunun , taawa kiyaghtaallghit seghleghataghaayaghqaagut piyuwhaalleghmeggneng .
Tamaakut yuget , liitngwaaghluku agleghnalghii qelghusaq allgeghtekaghteng , tunutkaqaat . Itaghnaghataghaghnayaghtut liisimangisaqumegteggu elqughutngalghii kiyaghtaalleq .
Tawaten aneghtellghita ipangughtestaat yuget pillghat , " Qikmim uteghfikaqaa mighyaqani , kurugaqlu ughvughqegkaq aglanqiglluni ugharramun mingughunneqigtaquq . "
Ilakumtaamni , ukut alghiitkii latalleghma elpesinun . Tamaghhaagkenkun latalleghma neqangughtesnaqutkamsi liisimakegkaghpesineng . Sumeghtaghiisqesugamsi tamaakuneng ipapighqellusi .
Elpesinun neqamikesuganka agleghnalghiit uuknaliqistet uuknaliqutkegkiit . Neqamikesugaqallu qelghusaq Atanemta Yugulighistem aapqaa apostle-egpesigun .
Liigikngwaaghyaghqaqaghsi una : kingulighni aghneghni legasiighwaghtelguyaghqaaguq ; tamaakunguut malighqutaqngalghiit seghleghnun piyukegkameggnun . Legasiighwaatkelleqaat Kiyaghneghem akequsaa ,
whaten pillequt , " Jesus akeqikaaguq taginqiglleqniluni . Naagu ? Ima sivuneput tuqulaghaatellghitneng , paninang sangwaa qamaglluni almesiqaqaa nunam piinlillghaneng . "
Nakmiiqaagut avelghasingwaaghnaluku una ipapilleq : neghighluku Kiyaghneghem akuzitmikun ulimakaqaa qilaga , ulimakaqaallu nuna meghmeng , meghqunllu .
Taagken Kiyaghneghem meghmeng ulevesluku nuna naafqegkaqaa .
Iwernga taaggun akuzitkun Kiyaghneghem aflengakaqii qilagallu nunallu naafqesaghqaaluki keneghqun . Aflengaknguut kenlanga aghneghanun nanqigtillghem . Tawanillu aghneghmi naafqelleqii yuget avelghasingwaaghikat ellmineng .
Ilakumtaamni , puygugpenaan una ! Ataneghmi aghneq ataasiq thousand ayumiqullghestun ayuquq , thousand ayumiqullghet ataasitun aghneghtun ayuquq .
