Ataneq egnaanginneghituq akequsani piyaghqaaluku , ilangita yuget sumeghtaghallghistun . Yeghlegi nekeggmetutaqiisi qayughllak kina alngunak iflayugunghilkanga . Itupill tamaghhaan yuuk avuteghqesqesugaa seghleghqellghitneng .
Iwernga Aghnegha Atanghem tagillequq teglegniightetun . Tawani Aghneghmi qilaga aviighusaghqaaguq eftughuuteghllagmeng . Sangwaat qamaglluteng qilagamelnguut kenghem ughuglleqii . Qamagllutengllu nunamelnguut paneghllequt .
Qamaglluteng tamaakut ughugyaghqaatangitneng , elpesi yugni natelnguunaqetsi ? Kiyaghtaallesi pelungillit , Kiyaghneghmunllu ayuqlit ,
utaqiimalusi Aghneghanun Kiyaghneghem . Pinaqellghaghsi qamaglluku pinitun pitek aghneq tagiragkiighesqelluku . Tawani aghneghmi kenghem naafqelleqaa qilaga , maatneghemllu ughuglleqii sangwaat qamaglluki qilagamelnguut .
Iwernga whangkuta utaqiinguukut Kiyaghneghem akequsaqegkaaneng . Pikaaguq nutaghameng qilagangllaghlleqniluni nutaghamengllu nunangllaghlleqniluni . Tawani elqughutngalghiinginaat kiyaghllequt .
Enkaangam ilakumtaamni , utaqiimalusi tawavek Aghneghmun pinaqellghaghsi qamaglluku pelungiteklu afkuyiiteklu Kiyaghneghem esghaamallghani . Nekeggmeteklu Ellngani .
Sumeghmikiteggu Atanemta nuqetutillgha elpesineng yugulillengesqeqaghllusi . Piniqegkamta ugpeqaalgutemta Paul-em aapqaqii taakut ataasit lataaqngamisi peghqinellelighluni Kiyaghneghtameng .
Latatkegkaqii tamaakut qamaglluki latamikun . Nalighneghi Paul-em latangan liigikneghlluguut . Yuget liigikellepagilnguut , ugpeqillepagilnguut allangughtaqiit sameng pisiitangi latanganilnguut . Tawatenllu piiqiit ilangi Akuzitet Igaqegkat enkaam naafqengnguut ellmeggneng .
Ilakumtaamni , liisimakutegpesineng saaqutangi qaatkusigalnguut liilightuusanun , kelengatek . Aghulaqutestegpenasi anaggutngalghiinun apeghtughillghitnun . Tawaten pikufsi malghuklinaanghitusi ugpeqegkaghpesineng .
Iwernga nagneghtek wataqaaghaq liisimakluku Jesus Christ-a , Ataneghput , Yugulighistevut , nagneghteklu wataqaaghaq piniqellghakun . Enkaam Christ-a usuqelteggu , quulvaalteggu maaten , quunperugllaklu ! Amen .
Taana piinlighyuwhaalleghmeng ayuqelghii : nagaquqaghput , esghaqaghput whangkuta katam iyemnneng , esghapakaghput , saaftekaghput iiggemnneng , taananguuq Akuzin unguvalleq .
Taana unguvalleq esghaghyaghqaaghtestaqngan esghaqaqaghput ; enkaam whaa aapghaghputlu ungipaqaghputlu elpesinun taana kenlengilnguq unguvalleq Atamesalghii , esghaghtestekaq whangkunnun .
Aapghaghput elpesinun sangwaa esghaqaghputlu nagatkaghputlu ilatesqellusi whangkunnun , ilatngallemnnunllu Atamun , Ighneghanunllu Jesus Christ-amun .
Latatkaput tamaakut quyalleghput iighwiisqelluku .
Una ungipaq nagaquqaghput Ighneghaneng Kiyaghneghem apeghnaqaghput elpesinun , Kiyaghneghnguq nighuguuq , mamlelleqraggiituq .
Iwernga ilatnganikumta ellnganun naqam paninang mamlegmi kiyaghtengnguluta , iqlengiqnguukut , atuqigataghputlu ipapighqelleq .
Iwernga nighugmi kiyaghtekumta ellngan nighugmetellghatun taawa ilatngaakut ilamnnun , aawanllu Jesus-em , Kiyaghneghem Ighneghan , ukmangiiwiinkut tamaghhaaneng seghleghqellemnneng .
Seghleghqellghinnikumta puughtengnguukut whangkunneng katam , ipapighqellghitukutlu .
Iwernga aapqumteki seghleghqelleput Kiyaghneghmun , seghevusaghqaqiinkut seghleghqellemnneng , ukmangighyaghqaqiinkutlu tamaghhaaneng anaggutaghallemnneng qayughllak ataasiighmetuqlu elqughullunillu ayuqelghiinguuq .
Seghleghqigannikumta , Kiyaghneq iqlengiqestengughlleqaghput , akuzitangillu atuqngunghitaput .
Taghnughhaghhamni , whaten latangwaamsi seghleghqefqaafsi pisqellusi . Iwernga kina alngunak seghleghqegkan Jesus Christ-am elqughutngalghiim maniguututaqiinkut Atamun .
Ellnganguuq iqitusiq seghleghqellemnnun , whangkunginaamta seghleghqellemnnun pingunghituq , iwernga tamaghaghllagan yugem seghleghqellghanun ayuquq .
Esgha whaten ipapighqutkesaghqaghput liisimakilleghput Kiyaghneghmeng , qaatkellemteggun qelghusii .
Kina whaten pilghii , " Liisimakaqa Kiyaghneq , " naqam qaatkegpenaki qelghusii , iqlengiqestenguuq , nallukaallu ipapighqelleq .
Iwernga kitum alngunak qaatkegkumiki Kiyaghneghem akuzitangi , piniqillgha Kiyaghneghmun ipapestaaq iighwiqaaguq , tawaten ipapighqutkesaghqaqaghput ellnganitulvut .
Kina alngunak pilghii kiyaghtengnguniluni ellngani , kiyaghsaghqaaguq Jesus Christ-am pillghatun .
Piniqegkamni , una qelghusaq latatkegkegka elpesinun nutaghaanghituq . Taananguuq neghightaq qelghusaq nagatkayugsi ima piinlighyuwhaalleghmeng , taana ungipaaguq nagatkayugsi .
Iwernga una qelghusaq latatkegkegka elpesinun nutaghaaguq . Taam ipapighqellgha esghaghluni ayuquq Christ-akunllu elpesigunllu qayughllak mamlek aga naghughtengnguuq , nighupik kuukgutnguuq .
Kina alngunak pilghii nighugmenniluni naqam ugumikluku ugpeqaalgutni , paninang mamlegmelnguuguq .
Kitum alngunak piniqegkumigu ugpeqaalgutni nighugmi kiyaghtengnguuq , nighugmetutmineng naagtusighqiituq .
Iwernga kitum alngunak ugumikegkumigu ugpeqaalgutni , mamlegmetuq . Igleghtengnguuq mamlegmi , talwa nallukuq navek pingutni qayughllak mamlegem ayaastekaqaa .
Taghnughhaghhamni , lataaqamsi qayughllak seghleghqellesi seghevutellengegkaagut apalluqluku Christ-a .
Atani , lataaqamsi qayughllak liisimakegkesi ellnga piinlighyuwhaalleghmeng ayuqelghii . Nukalpigani , lataaqamsi qayughllak kayaalqegkaqegkesi Tughneghaq . Taghnughhaghni , lataaqamsi qayughllak liisimakegkesi Ata .
Atani , lataaqamsi qayughllak liisimakegkesi ellnga ima piinlighyuwhaalleghmeng ayuqelghii . Nukalpigani , lataaqamsi qayughllak iknaqelghiisi , akuzitangillu Kiyaghneghem ilugpesinilnguut , kayaalqegkaqegkesillu Tughneghaq .
Piniqegpenaan nuna talwa sangwaa alngunak nunam pinga . Kitum alngunak piniqegkumigu nuna , piniqellghituq Atamun .
Ukut esgha qamaglluki nunam pingi : sangwaa yugusim piyukellgha seghleghqusiqaqelghii , iyem qiliightestellgha , sangwaatlu yuget qukaayugutkaqegkangit nunami whani . Taakut Atameng pingunghitut , nunameng pinguut .
Nuna aviighutnguuq , tamaakutlu seghleghqusiiwaqelghiit yugem piyukaqegkangi ; iwernga kitum atuqegkumigu Kiyaghneghem piyukellgha kiyaghsaghqaaguq quunperugllak kenlengunaan .
Taghnughhamni , kenla qantaghalliighaghtuq ! Ungipaatkaagusi Anguyakilghii Christ-ameng tagilleqniluku , whaa maaten uglapiglleghiit anguyakilghiit Christ-ameng allgeghtuutngwaaghluteng ayuqut , enkaam liisimakaghput kenla qantaghalliighaghtuq .
Tamaakut whangkunnisaghtut iwernga unitkaqiinkut qayughllak ilatngwaaghumangilnguut whangkunnun . Ilatngwaaqaayaqumeng uninnayanghitiinkut . Unitelleghmegteggun liigikestengngwaaghaat ilatngwaaghumangitelleghteng whangkunnun .
Iwernga elpesi , Christ-am kuuvegkaqiisi Agleghnalghiigneng Taghneghagneng enkaam qamagllusi liisimakaghsi ipapighqelleq .
Latangustemsii-i ipapighqelleq nallukutegpesineng ? Nakaa , latangwaamsi liisimakutegpesineng . Liisimakegkesillu iqlengiqelleq ipapighqelleghmeng pingunghilnguq .
Kina iqlengiqestengwaa ? Iqlengiqestenguuq whaten pilghii , " Jesus , Christ-angunghituq . " Taananguq anguyakilghii Christ-ameng qayughllak ighsakegkek Atankuk Ighneghenkuk .
Kitum alngunak ighsakegkumigu Ighneq , Atallu ighsaksaghqaqaa ; kitum alngunak tugukliqumigu Ighneq , Atallu tuguklighyaghqaqa .
Enkaangam iiwleng neqamikluku apeghtuusaq , apeghtuusaqegkaq elpesinun ugpeghyuwhaalleghpesineng ima . Atuqumanginaqufsigu nagaquqaghsi taawa iiwleng Ighneghmellequsillu Atamellequsillu .
Unanguuq akequsaqegkaa tuunelleqniluku whangkunnun , kenlengilnguq unguvalleq .
Latasiqanka elpesinun tamaakut puughtinaqutkelghiit elpesineng apalluqluki .
Iwernga elpesi Christ-am kuuvikegkaqiisi Taghneghagmineng . Taghneghakek ilugpesinitutmegneng alla kina alngunak Apeghtughisteksugnaanghitaghsi , qayughllak Taghneghagkenka apeghtughaqiisi sameng tamaghhaaneng . Apeghtuusii ipanguut , temngingunghitut enkaam Taghnegham apeghtulghatun Christ-ametekestaghtek .
Taghnughhamni , Christ-ametekestaghtek enkaam uka aliiqan ilutuyaghqaaluta , iighnaqefqaamta kaynguyugem ellnganeng pilghaakut tawani Aghneghmi tagillghani .
Liisimakegkesi Christ-a elqughutngalghii . Enkaam liisimaksaghqaqasi kinkut alngunak elqughutngaan pikayuget Kiyaghneghem taghnughhaqii .
Esghaqaghtegguqun Atam piniqimalleghllaga whangkunnun , avaqutaqniiqiinkut ellminun , ipa avaqutaqiinkut . Tamaaken apalluquluku nunam yugan nallukiinkut qayughllak nallukegkangat Kiyaghneq .
Piniqegkamni , taawa avaqutaqegkanginkut Kiyaghneghem , iwernga salin whateghlluwaaq liigikigataghput naten lliilleghqaghput . Iwernga liisimakaghput , Christ-a aliiqan ellngatun ayuqellequkut qayughllak esghaghlleqaghput legan tawatelluku .
Taana kitum alngunak ellmineng sighimakegkumigu Christ-akun pelungighsaghyaghqaaguq , katam Christ-am pelungitellghatun .
Kina alngunak seghlleghqegkayuk qaatkusigatuq Kiyaghneghem Liilightuusaanun . Seghleghqellghuuq qaatkunneghitelleq Kiyaghneghem Liilightuusaanun .
Liisimakaghsi Christ-a allgeqaaguq iqinnaluki seghleghqelleput , ellnga seghleghqellghituq .
Kina alngunak Christ-ami kiyaghlleghhii seghleghqumanginaghnaangituq . Kina alngunak seghleghqumanginaqumi , liigikumangitaallu nallukaqaallu Christ-a .
Taghnughhaghhaghni , kitumun alngunak puughtestegpenasi ! Kina alngunak elqughulluni pikayuk elqughutngaaq katam Christ-am elqughutngallghatun .
Kina alngunak seghleghqumanginalghii Tughneghaam pikaa qayughllak Tughneghaq seghleghqengngulghii ima piinlighyuwhaalleghmeng . Ighnegha Kiyaghneghem allgeqaaguq una apalluqluku , naafqennaluku Tughneghaam qepghaqaa .
Kina alngunak taghnughhaa Kiyaghneghem seghleghqumanginiigatuq qayughllak Kiyaghneghem nangaghnegha ellnganilnguq ; qayughllaklu Kiyaghneq Atakegkanga , enkaam seghleghqumanginaghnaanghituq .
Whaten liisimaksaghqaqaput Kiyaghneghemllu avaqutii , Tughneghaamllu avaqutii : kina alngunak elqughulluni pingigalnguq nalighmeng ugumikingalghii yulgutmineng Kiyaghneghem avaqutaqenghitaa .
Ungipaq nagaquqaghsi piinlighyuwhaalleghpesineng unanguuq : piniqutusaghqaagukut .
Cain-etun ayuqsaghqaanghitukut . Cain Tughneghaam pikaa enkaam tuqutkaqaa ellmi katam anglegutni . Sangan tuqutagu ? Qayughllak sallghi anaggutngalghiit naqam anglegutangan sallghi elqughutngalghiit .
Ugpeqaalgutemni , saghiighayugpenasi nunam yugan ugumikegkangisi .
Liisimakukut tuqumeng alpakaagukut unguvalleghmun qayughllak piniqegkeput ugpeqaalguteput . Kina alngunak piniqingigalnguq paninang tuqumetuq .
Kitum alngunak ugumikegkumigu ugpeqaalgutni yugtaghtenguuq . Liisimakaghsi yugtaghtem ilungani kenlengilnguq unguvalleq kiyaghtengngunghituq .
Whaten esgha liisimakegkefut piniqelleq sangutanga : Christ-am tuunellghakun unguvalleni whangkunnun . Enkaam whangkutallu tuunelteki unguvalleput ugpeqaalgutemnnun .
Kitum alngunak naamaghmi kiyaghtaaghem esghaghluku ugpeqaalgutni aklumalghii nangllekenghilkumigu , naten始ngam Kiyaghneghem piniqellgha ilunganilleqa ?
Taghnughhaghhaghni ! Piniqiyaghqaanghitukut akuziteraaghinaghteggunllu akuzillemteggunllu . Yeghlegi piniqilta ipapighqelluta nangaghnemteggun .
Enkaangam liisimakellequkut Kiyaghneghmun ipapighqelleghmun pikutfut . Seghleghninemtallu Kiyaghneghem sivungani nalluneqsuknaanghitaghput seghevutingallgha qayughllak Kiyaghneq aangataghaghtuq seghleghyugngallemnneng , liisimakegkangallu sangwaa tamaghhaan .
Piniqegkamni , seghleghninghilkumta tetugnaanghitaghput Kiyaghneq .
Aapnemtallu sameng alngunak allgeghutaqukut ellnganeng qayughllak qaatkaqegkeput qelghuusii , atuqaqegkeputlu efqughnalghiit ellngani .
Una esgha qelghusaa : whangkunnun ugpeqesqelluku Ighneghmi aatgha Jesus Christ-am , piniqutullutallu Christ-am qelellghatun .
Kitum alngunak qaatkegkumiki Kiyaghneghem qelghuusii kiyaghtengnguuq Kiyaghneghmi , Kiyaghneq ellngani . Whaten esgha liisimakegkefut Kiyaghneghem whangkunnitellgha : Taghneghagnekun tuunegkamikun whangkunnun .
Piniqegkamni , ugpeqegpenaki qamaglluki taghneghat . Yeghlegi liigiknaqaqiteki Kiyaghneghmeng pingutangi , qayughllak uglapiglleghhiit uuknaliqistesighwaaghet mingisimaat nunami .
Esgha whaten liisimaksaghqagsi Kiyaghneghmun Taghneghaqutkek : tamaghhaghmi taghnegham aapqagu Jesus Christ-a yuguluni allgeqaaniluku , Kiyaghneghtaaguq .
Iwernga tamaghhaghmi taghnegham mesiighaaskagu Jesus yuguluni allgeqaanghinniluku Kiyaghneghtaanghituq . Taakuk taghneghak anguyakilghiimeng Christ-ameng pinguuk nagaquqaghpesineng tagiiyaghqaanilukek . Taawa maaten kaatngwaaghlutek nunamun ayuquk .
Taghnughhaghni , elpesi Kiyaghneghem pikutanganeng , kayaalqegkaqasi tamaakut qayughllak ilugpesinilnguq aghtughyaghqaanghitaghaghtuq nunamelngughmeng .
Tamaakut nunam pikii , apeghtuusiit nunameng pinguut , enkaam nunam yugan nagataqiit .
Iwernga whangkuta Kiyaghneghem pikiinkut , enkaam kitum liisimakilghiim Kiyaghneghmeng nagataqiinkut . Tamaakut ilangita Kiyaghneghem pikenghilkangan nagasigatiinkut . Enkaam tawaten esgha liisimaksaghqagput Taghneghakek ipapighqellghem nalighmeng taghneghakek ipangunghilnguum .
Piniqegkamni , yeqay piniqututelta qayughllak piniqelleq Kiyaghneghmeng pinguuq . Kina alngunak piniqingalghii taghnughhaqaa Kiyaghneghem , liisimakaallu Kiyaghneq .
Kitum alngunak piniqinghilnguum nallukaa Kiyaghneq , qayughllak Kiyaghneq piniqellghuuq .
Kiyaghneghem kayagtekaqaa taananginaghhaq Ighneni nunamun , unguvallengesqelluta ellngakun . Tawaten pilleghmikun Kiyaghneghem kelgutkaqaa piniqelleni whangkunnun .
Piniqelleq akuzitkegkegka whangkuta piniqelqenghitaghput Kiyaghneghmun . Yeghlegi Kiyaghneghem piniqelqaa whangkunnun kelgutkaa kayagtelleghmikun Ighneni iqitusiiluku seghleghqellemnnun .
Piniqegkamni , Kiyaghneghem piniqellgha whangkunnun tawateskan whangkutallu piniqutusaghqaagukut .
Kitum alngunak esghiigatngwaaghaa Kiyaghneq ; piniquskumta Kiyaghneq kiyaghtengnguuq ilumnni , piniqellghallu iighwighyaghqaaguq ilumnni .
Kiyaghneghem tuunegkaqiinkut ellmi katam Taghneghagmineng enkaam liisimakaghput kiyaghtengnguuq whankunni , whangkuta ellngani .
Esghaqaqaghput Ighnegha . Enkaam ungipaqngwaaghput Kiyaghneghmun kayagtekaqniluku Yugulighistenguluku tamaghhaanun yugnun .
Kitum alngunak aapqagu Jesus Ighneqniluku Kiyaghneghmun , Kiyaghneq kiyaghtengnguuq ellngani , ellnga Kiyaghneghmi .
Enkaam whangkuta liisimakaghputlu ugpeqaghputlu Kiyaghneghem piniqillgha whangkunnun . Kiyaghneq piniqellghuuq , enkaam kina alngunak kiyaghlleghhii piniqelleghmi kiyaghtengnguuq Kiyaghneghmi , Kiyaghneq ellngani .
Enkaam piniqelleq iighwightekaaguq ilumnni ilutusqelluta Nanqigtillghem Aghneghani . Tawatetukut qayughllak Christ-atun ayuqelghiikut nunami whani .
Piniqelleghmi alingelleq aviituq qayughllak iighwiqam piniqellghem ighlleqayuwaa alingelleq . Enkaangam piniqelleq iighwiimangituq tamaakuni paninang alingegkayugni , qayughllak alingellelguuq aghyuulleq .
Piniqiiqukut qayughllak Kiyaghneghem sivukluni piniqegkaqiinkut .
Kina pikumi , " Piniqaqa Kiyaghneq , " naqam ugumikluku ugpeqaalgutni , iqlengiqestenguuq . Qayughllak kitum alngunak piniqenghilkumigu ugpeqaalgutni esghaqayuni , piniqnaanghitaa Kiyaghneq esghiigalkenni .
Una qelghusaqaa Christ-am whangkunnun , kitum piniqegkumigu Kiyaghneq , piniqsaghqaqaa ugpeqaalgutnillu .
Kitum alngunak ugpeqngukumigu Jesus , Christ-angutanga , avaqutaqaa Kiyaghneghem , kitum alngunak piniqegkumigu Ata piniqsaghqaqii avaqutii .
Whaten liisimaksaghqaqaghput piniqilleghput Kiyaghneghem avaqutiitnun : piniqellemteggun Kiyaghneq , qaatkellemteggunllu qelghusii .
Una piniqellghuuq Kiyaghneghmun : qaatkutelleghput qelghusaanun . Qelghusii piyaqnaghllagunghitut ,
qayughllak tamaghhaghmi avaqutaliitkaan Kiyaghneghem kayaalqegkaqaa nuna . Whaten esgha kayaalqesaghqaghput nuna , ugpeqillemteggun .
Kinangaawa kayaalqiista nunameng ? Kitum alngunak ugpeqegkumigu Jesus Ighneqniluku Kiyaghneghmun , taanata kayaalqiista .
Jesus Christ-anguuq tagikaq . Tagikaaguq meghqunllu aawhkunllu . Tagimangituq meghhiinaghqun iwernga meghqunllu aawhkunllu tagikaaguq .
Taghnegham aapghaa taana ipanguniluku qayughllak Taghneghak ipapighqellghulghiik .
Taawa pingayuguut aapghistet , Taghneghak , meq , aakwh ; taakut qamaglluteng itagnaqulluteng ayuqut .
Ugpeqngukumteki yuget aapqiit whangkunnun , ipapestaaq ugpeqataghaghyaghqaqaput Kiyaghneghem aapqii . Kiyaghneghem apellgha Ighneghmun ipanguuq .
Enkaam kitum alngunak ugpeqegkumigu Ighnegha Kiyaghneghem qama ilunganituq Kiyaghneghem aapqaa . Iwernga kitum alngunak ugpeqenghilkumigu Kiyaghneq iqlengiqestengllaghlleqaa , qayughllak Kiyaghneghem aapqaa Ighneghmineng ugpeqenghilkanga .
Una Kiyaghneghem aapqaqaa , Kiyaghneghemnguq tuunegkaqiinkut kenlengilngughmeng unguvalleghmeng , taana unguvalleq Ighneghanituq .
Kitum alngunak tugukliqumigu Ighneq , unguvallelguuq ; kitum alngunak tugukliimangilkumigu Ighnegha Kiyaghneghem unguvallengellghituq .
Latasiqanka tamaakut elpesinun ugpeqilghiinun aatghaneng Ighneghan Kiyaghneghem , elpesinun liisimakesqelluku kenlengilnguq unguvalleghsi .
Nalluneqsukigataghput Kiyaghneq ; liisimakaghput nagataqiinkut aapnemteggu sameng alngunak piyukellghakun ayuqelghiimeng .
Liisimakegkumteggu nagatellgha sameng alngunak aaptellemnneng , liisimakaghput allgeghutaqukut tungsiqamnneng ellnganeng .
Kitum esghaqumigu ugpeqaalgutni seghleghqelghii tuqumun ayuqenghilngughmeng yughaatkelligu enkaam Kiyaghneghem tuunligu unguvalleghmeng . Akuzitkengngwaanka yuget seghleghqellghita tuqumun piyaghqaqenghilkangitneng . Seghleghqellelguuq tuqumun ayuqelghiimun . Iwernga yughaatkesqengngunghitaqa tawaten seghleghqelghii .
Qamaglluni seghletun pilleq seghleghqellghuuq . Iwernga seghleghqellelguuq tuqumun ayuqenghilngughmeng .
Liisimakaghput kina alngunak Kiyaghneghem avaqutaa seghleghqumanginaghnaanghituq , qayughllak Ighneghan Kiyaghneghem aflengakngukanga enkaam Tughneghaam seghletun pinaanghitaa .
Liisimakukut Kiyaghneghem pikiinkut qaywa Tughneghaam igleghutngughngaagu qamaglluku nuna .
Liisimakaghput Ighneghan Kiyaghneghem tagiluni liigikestekaqiinkut liisimakesqelluku Kiyaghnepik . Kiyaghnepigmetukut Ighneghanitutemnneng Jesus Christ-ami . Taanata Kiyaghnepiklu kenlengilnguqlu unguvalleq .
Taghnughhaghhaghni , iqitngalusi kiyaghnesighwaaghneng !
Ukut latat Elder-meng pinguut Kiyaghneghem nakmikegkaanun aghnamun , avaqutaanunllu ipapigmeng piniqegkamnun . Ellnginaanghitunga piniqistezi , qamagllutengllu liisimakelghiit ipapighqelleghmeng piniqiisi ,
qayughllak ipapighqelleq ilumnnilnguq . Taana ipapighqelleq ilumnnisaghqaaguq quunperugllak .
Kayusilleq , nangllegyulleq , nekeggmelleqlu whangkunnillequt kiyaghtengnguluta ipapighqelleghqunllu piniqelleghqunllu . Taakut Kiyaghneghmeng Atameng , Jesus Christ-amengllu , Atam Ighneghaneng pinguut .
Quyapigtekaagunga nagaqughluki ilangi avaqutaghten kiyaghtengnguniluki ipapighqelleghqun tawateghpigaq Atam qelellghatun whangkuta .
Aghnami , piimken piniqututelta . Taana nutaghaanghituq qelghuusaq latatkegkegka elpenun ; qelghusaaguq ima piinlighyuggaalleghmeng .
Una piniqellghuuq , qaatkutelleq Kiyaghneghem qelghuusaanun . Qelghuusaq nagaquqaghsi piinlighyuwhaalleghmeng unanguuq : qamagllusi piniqullusi kiyaghtek .
Uglapiglleghhii puughtista nunami mingilluni ayuquq . Tamaakut yuget apeghnaanghitaat Jesus Christ-a yuguluni allgeqaaniluku qayughllak ugpeqigataat . Tawatelnguq yuuk puughtistenguuqlu , anguyakilghiinguuqlu Christ-ameng .
Enkaam kelengalusi , pegsaqunaan qepghaatkaghsi akileghtuusaghqaghsi qamaglluku allgeghsaghqaqaghsi .
Kitum alngunak qaasghuskumiki apeghtuusii Christ-am Kiyaghneq ellnganinneghituq . Iwernga kitum alngunak atuqumanginaqumiki apeghtuusii Christ-am , Atallu Ighneqlu ellnganituk .
Kitum alngunak apeghtughyaghtuqangisi atuqegpenaki Christ-am apeghtuusii , aqelqangllaghpenaan nalighmeng quyakegpenaan ,
qayughllak kitum alngunak quyakegkumigu qepghalgusiqallghuughlleqaa seghleghmeng qepghaqaaneng .
Apeghyaghqaghllagughngaaghma elpesinun latatgun piyunghitanka . Iwernga sunanguq laalighfiklamsi , aleghquunnayaghtukut gginasaghquulluta , enkaam quyateghllagnayaghtukut .
Avaqutiita nakmikegkam aakaghpesi piniqiisinguq .
Ukut latat Elder-meng pinguut Gaius-mun ipapik piniqegkamnun .
Piniqegkamni , liisimakaqa unguvasigken itagnaghtuq . Yughaatkaqamken itagniisqelluten sakun tamaghhaakun , yugunqegtesqellutenllu .
Quyapigtekaagunga ilangita ugpeqaalgutet kaalluteng ungipaasatnga ataasiighmetelleghpeneng ipapighqelleghmun , iiwleng elpesinun atuqnguniluku ipapighqelleq .
Quyapigtaqunga nagaqunemki avaqutaliitkanka atuqinguniluki ipapighqelleghmeng . Alla saam alngunak quyasigataanga tawaten .
Piniqegkamni ilakumtaamni , piniipigtuq ataasiighmelluten qepghallghen Kiyaghneghmun aflengakelleghpegun ugpeqaalgutet talwa tamaakut nallukegkaghten .
Maani yughaghvigmi aapghaqaat piniqellghen . Kayusiitaghtiki nagneghutesqelluki igleghallghit . Kayusighillghen Kiyaghneghem piyukellghatun ayuqluku
qayughllak igleghanguut apalluqluku Christ-a . Tuguklighingigatut ugpeqaanghilngughneng kayusilleghmeng
enkaam whangkuta ugpeqani kayusighyaghqaqaput tamaakut yuget . Tawaten pikumta qepghalgutkelleqiinkut apeghtughinguluteng ipapighqelleghmeng .
Latakaayaghtunga ugpeqanun iwernga Diotrephes-em umiilguyugneghem waakigatii liilightullghenka .
Elpesinun pikuma apeghlleqaqa saaqutanga . Seghletun akuzitkaqiinkut , iqlengiqutkaqiinkutlu . Tawatenginaq pingigatuq upughasugigatii ugpeqaalguteput kaanneghata . Upughatiyulghiit ineghtaqii , upughatinghatallu eflequghaqii ugpeqat qerngughutfigitneng .
Piniqegkamni , seghletun pikayugestun pigpenang , yeghlegi pinitun pikayugestun piiqi . Kina alngunak pinitun pikayuk Kiyaghneghem pikaa ; iwernga kitum alngunak seghletun pikayugem nallukaa Kiyaghneq .
Tamaghhaghmi ugpeqam Demetrius pinighniiqaat yuuk . Ipapighqelluni kiyaghtaallghan ipapighqutkestaa . Taawa whangkutallu tawaten piighput , liisimakasi akuzilleput ipanguut .
Apeghyaghqaghllaguunga elpenun iwernga latatgun piyunghitanka .
Sunanguq qantaghaqun esghaghlaken enkaam aleghquullequkung gginasaghquullutung .
Ukut latat Jude-meng pinguut , Jesus Christ-am qepghaghtenganeng , James-em uyughaaneng . Lataaqunga Kiyaghneghem nakmikegkiitnun . Kiyaghneghem Atamta piniqiisi , Jesus Christ-amllu aflengakaqiisi .
Kiyaghneghem nangllegtallghallu , nekeggmellghallu , piniqellghallu nulali elpesini .
Piniqegkamni , latayupigtaqamsi yugulillemnneng . Iwernga nagaqughyamki apeghtughistesighwaaghet elpesinilnguut , apeghyukaqa elpesinun simighaqa . Liisimakasi Kiyaghneghem kayagtekaqii Apostle-etlu ilangillu yuget apeghtiisqelluta ugpeqsaghqamnneng . Enkaam kitum alngunak allangughsaghqaqenghitiit ellngita apeghtughillghit . Tamaaken apalluqluku latanguunga qevuullusi kipullginaaghesqelluki apeghtughistesighwaaghet . Apeghtughistegpenaki ipangunghilngughneng apeghtuusiitneng .
Qerngughunneghpesini maligutaqut , iwernga ungipaasigatiisi sameng apeghtughyugaqnilusi . Tamaakut yuget tuguklighyugigataat Jesus Christ-a taananginaghhaq Igleghutistevut , Ataneghputlu . Enkaam allangughtaqaat apeghtuusaq Kiyaghneghem nangllegtallghaneng ayuqelghii . Whaten piiqut , " Kiyaghneq nanglegtaghllagtuq , seghevutikayuguuq enkaam itagnaghtuq seghleghqesaghngaamta sex-kun . " Qavngarugllak Kiyaghneghem ungipaatkaqiinkut aghyuughlleqniluku kina alngunak apeghtughilghii tawaten .
Ungipaatkaayaghngaaghpesi sivunghani Kiyaghneghem aghyuughillghaneng seghleghqestenun , neqangughsugamsi allameng taakut usputaqluki . Neqamikluku Atanghem yugulikaqii Israel-eghmiit Egypt-eghmiineng , aghulaqestekaqii Egypt-meng . Iwernga kingunganeng taam ilangi Israel-eghmiit ugpeqinanighyata , qaatkunnanighyata ellminun , tuqustekaqii .
Neqamikluki yaqulget Kiyaghneghem pisqegkaa nagneghusimangitkaat , unitkaatlu neyeng qilak . Tamaaken apalluqluku Kiyaghneghem asighqegkii qiipraghutneng nekegngayaghqaneng quunperugllak , nekegtestekii mamlegllagkun . Tawantesnaqngwii kenlanga aghyuulleghqaminun Nanqigtivigem Aghneghani .
Neqamikluki Sodom-eghmiitlu Gomorrah-ghmiitlu , uvitangitnilnguutlu nunat . Yaqulgestun seghleghqegkaagut . Allaaghhiinaq seghleghqelleq sex-kun pikaat , talwa yuget yulgutkullghiit atuqutaqluteng , sangwaatlu seghleghataghaat atuqegkaqiit . Usputaagut Kiyaghneghem aghyughillghaneng seghleghqestenun kenlengilngughqun keneghqun .
Apeghtughistesighwaaghet tawatetut . Piiqut qavangullghitanguq seghleghqestaqiit sex-kun , qaatkesigatiitlu yuget igleghutistet , seghletunllu akuzitkestaqiit yaqulget igleghutistet .
Naqam Michael , yaqulget igleghutistengita ilangat , tawaten pillghituq . Tughneghaan-kuk aaghtiiraaghutkaqngamegnegu Moses-em yugusii , Michael-em seghletun akuzitkumangitaa , anaggusimanilukullu pillghitaa . Yeghlegi pikaqaa , " Atanghem aghyuughmigliten . "
Iwernga tamaakut apeghtughistesighwaaghet sangwaa alngunak liigikenghilkeseng seghletun akuzitkaqaat . Sangwaa ilanga liigikaqaat teghikusastun sumeghtaghiigalngughestun . Teghikusat piyukelleghmegestun pikayuguut . Tawateghpigaq apeghtughistesighwaaghet pikayuguut . Enkaam seghleghqestengughtaghaghaqut .
Seghleghwaaghunaqnguut ellngit ! Cain-etun pinguut , tuqutkaqaa anglegutni . Allgeghuteqaghhnaluteng manimeng seghletun pikaagut Balaam-em pillghatun . Korah-tun pinguut , qaatkesunghitkaqegkangi igleghutistet Kiyaghneghem nakmikegkii . Enkaam Kiyaghneghem naafqegkaqaa ellnga , apeghtughistesighwaaghetlu naafqesaghqaqii .
Neqenghaghqusaghtuneghpesini , communion-emaghpesi , tamaakutlu apeghtughistet piiqut . Yakughnaghtut ugpeqanun katam tawaten uyghagllak meghem asinganilnguq yakughnalghii angyanun . Neghaqut qerngaghmeng nenglaghqiqusimaghmeng , akuzimaghmeng nepugllaget kaynguyugpenateng . Ellnginaghmeng neghaqut kinkut tuunegpenaki . Sasiinghitut qilawaaghestun eslallugilngughestun ayuqut , anuqem naghughuskangi quulngakun nunam meghisagllagem . Sasiinghitut piitestingigalngughestun uqfigestun ayuqut , unataghvigmi . Piitestingigalnguut uqfiget tuqukastun ayuqut . Tamaaken apalluqluku piitesiighaghtem nusugaqii paneghhnaluki . Enkaam maalghugegneng tuqukallghuughaqut .
Kayngunalghiit nangaghneghit qagighllagestun ayuqut , temngi puugllungllat . Ighaleqetaaghestun qaprakayugestun ayuqut , qayughllak tawatelnguut ighaleqetaaghet nalluniighutnguyaghqaanghitut igleghanun . Tawateghpig-aq igleghusaghqaqenghitaat kina alngunak apeghtughillesighwaalleghmegteggun . Tamaaken apalluqluku Kiyaghneghem yataaghqutkaqii pisaghtiighllagmeng nekaghqameng kenlengilngughmeng .
Enoch-nguq maaghraghvinliitkegkangat kingunghita Adam-em , ellngan uuknaliqutkegkaqii tamaakut yuget . Whaten pikaaguq , " Esghaghtek , Ataneq tagiyaghqaaguq agleghnalghiit yaqulelghuteghllani kelqelluki ,
nanqiggnaluki qamagtengngwaaghluki yuget . Qayvighqesaghqaqii qamagtengngwaaghluki seghleghqestet seghleghqellghit , seghlepestaatunllu akuzitkillghit ellmineng . Tamaaken apalluqluku Atanghem aghyuughyaghqaqii seghleghqesteghllaget . "
Tamaakut yuget quunpeng temngi akuzilgaghllaget , efqughutkigalkangit sangwaat alngunak . Sangwaat alngunak seghleghqusit atuqsuneghmegteki atuqaqiit , piniiyugneghllaget , usuqnguughtaqiitlu kinkut sameng qiliighvikneghmegteki .
Piniqegkamni , neqamikluki Atanghem Jesus Christ-am apostle-ngita aapqiit sivunghani .
Ungipaatkaqiisi whaten , " Kingulighni aghneghni nenglaghyugsaghtelguyaghqaaguq Kiyaghneghem ipapighqellghaneng ayuqelghiineng . Sangwaat alngunak yugusim piyukellghi atuqsuneghmegteki piiqiit . "
Tamaakut yuget aaghtiiraaghutestiyugaqut ugpeqaneng . Maligtaqiit yugusimeng piyukellghit seghleghqelleghmun ayuqelghiit , Agleghnalghiigneng Taghneghagneng avangitutmeggneng .
Iwernga piniqegkamni , wata iknaqughsaamanginaghteggu ugpeqaamalleghsi , ugpeqilleghpesigun Kiyaghneghem agleghnalghiitgun apeghtuusiitgun . Yughaghaqitek Agleghnalghiignekun Taghneghagnekun .
Kiyaghneghem piniqellghanitekestaghtek , utaqiimalusi Atanemnneng Jesus Christ-ameng tuunesqellusi kenlengilngughmeng unguvalleghmeng nangllegtalleghmikun .
Nangllekluki tamaakut malghuklingalghiit Kiyaghneghem ipapighqellghaneng .
Yuguliteki akuqaqallghuulghiistun kenghegneng . Nangllekaqluki ilangitlu iwernga piraamsingwaaghlusi luuraq seghleghqellghistun piiqsaaghtusi . Ugumikluki seghleghqellghit katam ugumikelleghpesistun nukeggnaghqeghllakiit aatkateng seghleghqengnguluteng .
Kiyaghneghem kelengaksaghqaqiisi seghleghqelleghqaghpesineng , seghleghqellghiitesaghqaqiisillu . Enkaam quyaghllagllequsi nekevegkufsi sivungakun nighughqellghan .
Kiyaghneq taananginaghhaaguq Kiyaghneq , yugulikaqiinkut Atanemteggun Jesus Christ-am tuqullghakun . Ima tazimakerugllak , maaten , quunperugllak kenlengunaan Kiyaghneq aangeghllagtuq , aghtughyaghqaanghiteghllagtuq , igleghutngwaa sangwaa qamagtengngwaaghluku , aghtughyaghqaqenghitaa sangwaa qamagtengngwaaghluku . Kiyaghneq usuqli . Amen .
Whani igani igaqngaat Kiyaghneghem aliightekii Jesus Christ-amun . Kiyaghneghem aliightekaqii ellnganun liigikestesqelluki qepghaghteni sangwaat piyaghtungestaghniluki . Enkaam Christ-am kayagtekaqaa yaquleni qepghaghteminun John-mun tamaakut liisimakesqelluki .
Taagken John-em aapqaqii qamaglluki esghaqanillu nagatkanillu . Nagatkaqii akuzitangi Kiyaghneghem , ungipaqlu Jesus Christ-ameng ayuqelghii .
Quyastekaaguq atightulghii iglagtuluni akuzitangitneng uuknaliqellghem . Quyastekaagutlu nagalluteng qaatkullghiit qayughllak qantaghaqun tamaakut pillequt .
Ukut latat John-meng pinguut ugpeqanun qerngughtukayuget maaghraghvinlegni yughaghvigni Asia-mi . Nangllegtalleqlu nekeggmelleqlu elpesinillik Kiyaghneghmeng , maaghraghvinlek taghneghaneng , Jesus Christ-amengllu . Kiyaghneghuuq kiyaghlleghhii maaten , ellnganguuq kiyaghlleghhii sivunghani , ellnganguuq tagiyaghqaq . ( Taakut maaghraghvinlek taghneghat sivunganitut Kiyaghneghem umiilgusiin aqumutaan . ) Jesus Christ-a ataasiighmelnguuguq liisimakista ipapilleghmun . Ellnganguuq Kiyaghneghem unguvaghsuwhaaqaa tuqulleghmeng . Ellnganguuq igleghutistengat umiilgita nunam . Ellnganguuq piniqilghii whangkunneng , aawmikunllu itemutkaqiinkut seghleghqellemnneng . Ataneghpagulleghminitestiinkut , priest-ngughtestiinkutlu Kiyaghneghminun Atamun . Jesus Christ-am allgeghllikek nighughqelleqlu , aghtughyaghqaanghilleqlu igleghutimun quunperugllak kenlengunaan ! Amen .
Ii-i ! Jesus tagiiquq qilagwaagteggun . Tamaghhaghmi yugem esghaghlleqaat , talwa tamaakut panasqelluku pikiita esghaghlleqaat . Qamaglluteng nunam ramkengi qiyaaghuuteghllagllequt apalluqluku ellnga . Aa-a , tamaakut piyaghqaagut ! Amen .
" Whanga Alpha-nguungallu Omega-nguungallu , " piiq Ataneq Kiyaghneq , Aghtughyaghqaanghiteghllak . Ellnganguuq kiyaghlleghhii maaten , ellnganguuq kiyaghlleghhii sivunghani , ellnganguuq tagiyaghqaq .
John-nguunga , ugpeqaalgutkaghpesinga . Ikfiqunga elpesistun qayughllak Jesus-em Ataneghpagullghan pikiinkut . Ellngakun ikfiqelleput nuqetutaput . Aglaghtestekaagunga qiighqamun aatqelghii Patmos-meng qayughllak ungipaqegkenka Kiyaghneghem akuzitangi , ungipaqlu Jesus-meng ayuqelghii .
Atanghem Aghneghani Agleghnalghiim Taghnegham iitghaanga . Taagken tunutemnilluku nagaqughaqa ma iglagtuqaq qalghightaatetun .
Whaten piiq , " Igaqughqi igatgun esghaqaghten . Taagken tuyughnaketen ugpeqanun qerngughutkayugnun maaghraghvinlegni yughaghvigni : Ephesus-melnguut , Smyrna-melnguut , Perga-melnguut , Thyatira-melnguut , Sardis-melnguut , Philadelphia-melnguut , Laodicea-melnguutlu . "
Taagken qiivunga esghaghnaluku ma aleghqughteka . Qiivyalghiinga esghaghanka maaghraghvinleguftut gold-et kenelghutat tunemiit .
Taawa qukiitni kina llangaqa ighnegha yugem akughtughllagegneng atkuyaaqeftuq , sakimagmikunllu tafsingaftuq gold-meng .
Naasqwallu nuyaallu qateghpetuk wool-estun nalighmeng anigustun , iiskeklu kenghem kumangallghatun ayuqlutek .
Itegii qelmeghsaqastun siilustun ayuqeftut pelungighsaqat keneghqun . Mengallu eftughllagatun meghllagem tevughallghan ayuqluni .
Aghenqigneghmineng tugumiiqeftii maagraghvinlek ighaleqetaaghet , qaanghanengllu aanuq savigpak inglugtun gginakek ipegsaqak . Gginaa nighugllak aghneghem qukaan siqinghuughtellghatun .
Esghaghyamkun itegaan manungakun uullghaghtunga tuqukastun . Iwernga aghenqigneghmineng iiggmineng saaflunga piinga , " Alingegpenang , whanga sivuliigungallu kinguliigungallu .
Unguvalghiinguunga ! Tuqukaayaghtunga , iwernga ii-i , unguvanguunga quunperugllak kenlengunaan . Key-lguunga Tuqulleghmunllu Hades-munllu .
" Saaqsin igaqughqi igatgun sangwaat qamaglluki esghaqeten maaten , sangwaatlu kinguvaqun piyaghqat .
Esghaghaten maaghraghvinlek ighaleqetaaghet aghenqigneghma iigganilnguut , maaghraghvinleklu gold-et kenelghutat tunemiit , taakut sameng pisiitangi salin qayvightellghitut . Whaten pisiigut : Maaghraghvinlek ighaleqetaaghet yaqulguut . Kiyaghneghem ungipaghtekii ugpeqanun qerngughutkayuget maaghraghvinlegni yughaghvigni . Maaghraghvinlek kenelghutam tunemii taakunguut maaghraghvinlek yughaghviget .
" Latagu yaqulek igleghutilghii ugpeqaneng qerngughutkayuget yughaghvigani Ephesus-em . Whanganguuq tugumiilek maaghraghvinlek ighaleqetaaghneng aghenqignemkun , igleghtengnguungallu akulngitni maaghraghvinlek gold-et kenelghutat tunemiitni .
Liisimakamsi saaqutsi , ughleghiilghiisi , iilqayunghitelleghsillu . Liisimakamsillu tugukliigatasi seghleghet yuget , iwernga apostle-ngunilghiit liitaqasi esghapagluki temngingutangi . Taawa liitasi iqlengiqestenguut .
Meghniigatusi ikfiqelleghpesineng whanga apalluqlunga , iilqayugigatusillu .
Iwernga piyukenghitusiqa elpesinun unanguuq , piniqnaniimaaghpesinga , ugpeqaalgutesillu sivunghani piniqelleghpesistun .
Tamaaken apalluqluku puygugpenaan piniqeghllagyaqefsinga , ugpeqaalgutesillu . Piniqnanighaghpesinga piiqelleghpesistun . Enkaam avuteghqitek . Piniqenqigtikut piniqsugwhaalleghpesistun . Avuteghqenghilkufsi , takulusi iqilleqaqa kenelghutaghpesi tunemaa nenganeng .
Iwernga una pinitun pilqaghsi : ugumikasi piiqegkangit Nicolaus-em maligsaaghtengita , katam whanga ugumikellemtun .
Sigutelgukufsi , nagatekek Taghneghak sameng piiqutkek ugpeqanun ! Tamaakut kayaalqiilghiit kayaalqiilleghmeng neghesqelleqanka piitestekaaneng uqfigan unguvallghem , tawanlenguq Kiyaghneghem Piitesighaghvigani .
" Latagu yaqulek igleghutilghii ugpeqaneng qerngughutkayuget yughaghvigani Smyrna-m . Una ungipaq whangamneng pinguuq : Sivuliigungallu kinguliigungallu , tuqulunga unguvaqaagunga .
Liisimakanka seghleliillesi , aklumanguusillu iwernga aklungitusi ! Liisimakaqa seghleghet akuzitet ilangita yuget piiqegkangit elpesinun . Jews-nguniiqut , Jews-epigunghiteghngaaghmeng . Yuguut qerngughutkayuget Tughneghaam synagogue-ngani .
Alikegpenaki tamaakut ikfiqutkennaqegkesi . Nagatek ! Tughneghaam ilasi anusimingllaghtesnaqii nanghiiqunalusi . Enkaam ikfiqellequsi qula aghneghnun . Iwernga ataasiighmetek , qaywa tuquyaghqaaghngaaghpesi . Tawaten pikufsi , akileghtuusalilleqamsi kenlengilngughmeng unguvalleghmeng .
Sigutelgukufsi , nagatekek Taghneghak sameng piiqutkek ugpeqanun ! Tamaakut kayaalqiilghiit kayaalqiilleghmeng , tuunglighhaan tuqullghem aqnighhnaanghitii .
" Latagu yaqulek igleghutilghii ugpeqaneng qerngughutkayuget yughaghvigani Pergamum-em . Una ungipaq savigpalegmeng pinguuq inglugtun gginalek ipegsaqameng .
Liisimakamsi naantutsi , tawantusi Tughneghaam umiilgutivigan aqumutagkeni . Whangamnun ataasiighmetusi , ugpeqnanillghitaghpesingallu . Tawatetkaagusi talwa Antipas , ataasiighmelnguq ungipaghteka , kiyaghtengnguluku . Tawani Tughneghaam kiyaghfigani tuqutkaqaat .
Iwernga piyukenghitusinka elpesinun ukunguut : taawa elpesinitut ilangi qaatkullghiit Balaam-em apeghtuusaanun . Apeghtuqaqaa Balak naten seghleghqestesqelluki Israel-eghmiit . Enkaam Balak-em apeghtuqaqii neghyaghngiita pisqelluki neqet aghqutkegkat kiyaghnengllaqanun . Apeghtuqaqiillu itagnaghniluku alngunak sex-kun seghleghqelleghqaq .
Tawateghpigaq ilasi qaatkutut Nicolaus-em apeghtuusaanun .
Avuteghqellusi seghleghqennanightek ! Pinghilkufsi qantaghaqun takulleqamsi . Taagken pilluwaghlleqanka tamaakut yuget savigpagmeng qanemnilngughmeng .
Sigutelgukufsi , nagatekek Taghneghak sameng piiqutkek ugpeqanun qerngughutkayuget yughaghvigni ! Manna-meng iighngalghiimeng , manna-lilleqaqa taana kayaalqiilghii Tughneghagh-meng . Ellnganunllu tuunelleqaqa qatelghii uyghak , ateghraghaghmeng igaqfikegkaq . Kitum alngunak nallukegkaa ateq iwerngaqun allgeghtikaghhiinaam uyghagmeng liisimakaa .
" Latagu yaqulek igleghutilghii ugpeqaneng qerngughutkayuget yughaghvigani Thyatira-m . Una ungipaq Ighneghaneng Kiyaghneghem pinguuq . Iiskek kumaghuuguk kenghestun , itegii qelmeghtutkaat siilum qelmeghsalghatun .
Liisimakamsi saaqutsi . Liisimakaqa piniqelleghsi , ugpeqelleghsi , qepghaatilleghsi , nuqetutilleghsillu . Liisimakanka tamaakut wata piiqasi sivunghani piiqelleghpesineng .
Iwernga ukunguut tengvimun ayuqegkanka elpesinun : Aghuliighnneghitaghsi aghnaq Jezebel apeghtughilghii ipangunghilngughneng . Uuknaliqestenguniiquq Kiyaghneghmun . Iwernga apeghtughilleghmikun puughtaqii yugenka seghleghqesqelluki sex-kun , neghesqellukillu neqet aghqutkegkat kiyaghnengllaqanun .
Pilleghqalitkaqsaghaqa avuteghqesqelluku , iwernga taaqsunghituq allaniineghmeng .
Ii-i ! Miluunnaqaqa qavaghvigmun tawani ikfiqesqelluku . Maligulluki ellnganun miluulleqanka tamaakut gelgaghniilgutangi enkaam ikfiqesteghllaglleqanka . Tawaten pillequnga wetkuqun avuteghkegkata seghletun pillghitneng .
Tuqulleqankallu avaqutii . Enkaam qamaglluteng ugpeqat yughaghvignilnguut liilleqaatnga whanganguuq liisimakilghii yugem tamaghaghhmi sumeghtaghallghitnengllu ilumikegkiitnengllu . Aghyuughyaghqaqamsi tamaghaghpesi seghleghqetulegpesistun .
Iwernga ilagpesi Thyatira-mi , maligtellghitasi Jezebel-em seghleghet apeghtughillghi . Liitellghitasillu Tughneghaam aksaqumtaaghllagi . Tamaaken apalluqluku qelghataghaghnaanghitamsi ,
iwerngaqun ugpequmanginaghteggu apeghtullesi kenlanga uteghnillemnun .
Ellnga taana kayaalqiilghii kayaalqiilleghmeng , atuqilghiillu aneghneghqillemneng kenlemun , aghtughyaghqaanghillelilleqaqa igleghutesqelluki nation-et .
Igleghutesqeluki iron-meng rod-elighluki enkaam kagimnnakangit qikumeng qulmesiitengllaqastun .
Tuunelleqankallu unaangum ighaleqetaaghaneng .
Sigutelgukufsi , nagatekek sameng piiqutkek Taghneghak ugpeqanun !
" Igaqigu una ungipaq yaqulegmun igleghutilghii ugpeqaneng qerngughutkayuget yughaghvigani Sardis-em . Taana Kiyaghneghem maaghraghvinlek taghneghaaneng pilek maaghragvinleklu ighaleqetaalek , piiq , Liisimakamsi saaqutsi . Yuget piiqiisi unguvanilusi iwernga tuqungaasi .
Taghtughlusi , iknaqughsaghteggu sangwaa salin elpesi pizi tuqunaqelghii . Liitanka ukavantut sangwaat piiqegkesi Kiyaghneghma pisqesullghaneng elpesinun .
Neqamikluki apeghtuutkat elpesinun , nagaquqasillu . Qaatkiteki , avuteghqiteklu seghleghqelleghpesineng . Iwernga taghtunghilkufsi , takulleqamsi teglegniightetun . Nallukelleqaghsi qakun tagilleghqaqa elpesinun .
Paninang qafsinggaagut yuget Sardis-mi aatkateng nukeggnaghqellghilkangit . Igleghtelgusighlleqaatnga aalluteng qatelghiimeng aatkameng qayughllak itagnalghiinguut .
Kayaalqiilghii , ellngistun aallequq qatelghiimeng aatkameng . Aatghallu ghevesnaanghitaqa Kenlengilnguum Unguvallghem Igaaneng . Atamallu yaqulganllu sivungitni whangamnun piknilleqaqa .
Sigutelgukufsi , nagatekek sameng piiqutkek Taghneghak ugpeqanun !
" Igaqigu una ungipaq yaqulegmun igleghutilghii ugpeqaneng qerngughutkayuget yughaghvigani Philadelphia-m . Una ungipaq Agleghnalghiimeng , Ipapigmeng pinguuq . Ellnganituq David-em key-nga . Qelpeghtekumigu amik , kitum alngunak umegnaanghitaa . Uumkumigullu amik , kitum alngunak qelpeghhnaanghitaa .
Liisimakamsi saaqutsi , liisimakamsillu kayaatusi . Naqamllu qaatkasi apeghtuusanka , mesighiigatusillu whangamnun maligsaaghteknilusi . Ii-i , qelpeghusimaamsi amigmeng ; kitum alngunak umegyaghqaqenghilkanganeng .
Ii-i ! Tamaakut qerngughullghiit Tughneghaam synagogue-ngani , Jews-nguniiqut . Iwernga iqlengiqestenguut ; Jews-ngunghitut . Elpesinun pisluki qungughtesnaqanka sivugpesigun . Taagken liilleqaat piniqegkemsi .
Qelqaqamsi nuqetesqellusi . Qaatkegkaqutegpesineng qelghilqa paqniighsaghlleqamsi seghleliilleghneng kaannaqelghiineng nunataghhanun tamaghhaanun . Tamaakut seghleliillghet nanghiiqulleqiit qamaglluki yuget kiyaghlleghhiit nunami .
Tagiyaghtughtunga . Ayepsugillusi ugpequmanginaghtengnga kitumun alngunak wayanghitesqelluki qaghpasi .
Kayaalqiilghii aghveghaqetaaghtesleqaqa Kiyaghneghma Temple-ngani , allamengllu aanaanghituq . Enkaam ellngakun igaqelleqaqa aatgha Kiyaghneghma , aatghallu Kiyaghneghma neghllagan , Jerusalem-eghraghaq , ukilghii qilagmeng Kiyaghnemneng . Ellngakunllu igaqelleqaqa ateghraghaqa .
Sigutelgukufsi nagatekek sameng piiqutkek Taghneghak ugpeqanun !
" Igaqigu una ungipaq yaqulegmun igleghutilghii ugpeqaneng qerngughutkayuget yughaghvigani Laodicea-m . Una ungipaq Amen-meng pinguuq . Ataasiighmelnguuguq , ipapighqengngalghiinguuq liisimakista . Ellngakun Kiyaghneghem ulimakaqaa sangwaa qamaglluku .
Liisimakamsi saaqutsi : isekinanghitusi , nalighmeng uguqnanghitusi . Isekinalghiisituq nalighmeng uguqnalghiisituq !
Enkaam maqaghraaggaategpesineng , isekinanghilnguusi nalighmeng uguqnanghilnguusi , qesiinnaqamsi qanemneng !
Piiqusi aklunginnilusi , allgeghuteghllagaqnilusi , aklungigannilusillu . Iwernga nallukusi seghleghwaaghuusi , nangllegnaghtusi , aklumaasi , ayaangaasi , amsikaghmetusillu .
Tamaaken apalluqluku ungipaatamsi aklungighisqellusi gold-tengyaghtughtek whangamnun qigeghtengngwaaqameng keneghqun . Tukfighiteklu whangamneng qatelghiineng aatkaneng saapesqelluki kayngunalghiit amsikaghmetellesi . Tukfighiteklu whangamneng aghakaghqameng iyegpesinun esghaasagutesqellusi .
Tamaakut piniqegkanka nallghusaghaqanka , aghyuughaqankallu . Enkaam sagiqneghughtek , avuteghqellusi seghleghqennanightek .
Ii-i ! Nekevlunga amigmi tenglugtughtunga . Kitum alngunak nagaququmigu meka , amigmeng qelpeghusimakanganga iteghllequnga ellnganun . Enkaam neghelgusighlleqaqa , ellnganllu neghelgusighlleqaanga .
Kayaalqiilunga enkaam aqumgaanga saaghwani Atama umiilgusiikun aqumutagkenkun . Tawateghpigaq kayaalqiilghii aqumesleqaqa saamkun umiilgusignekun aqumutamkun .
Sigutelgukufsi , nagatekek Taghneghak sameng piiqutkek ugpeqanun ! "
Taagken tamaakut kingungitneng taawa esghaghaqa qilagmi amik qelpalnguq ! Ma nagatkaqa qalghightaatetun ayuqelghii , whaten piiq , " Mayaa whavek . Elpenun esghaghtesnaqanka sangwaat piyaghqat . "
Tawaninginaq Taghneghagnitunga . Taawa qilagmi esgaghagka umiilgusik aqumutak , kina aqumgaftuq .
Aqumgalghii umiilgusigni esghaqaaluni iqeghtagketun jasper-enkuk carnelian-enkuk ayuquq . Uvitangani umiilgusim taawa agluk iqeghtakek emerald-etun ayuqlutek .
Uvitangani umiilgusim aqumutaghllagem taawa yuginaq estamat siipneqluki umiilgusit aqumutalghutet . Taakutgun aqumgatngaftut yuginaq estamat siipneqluki elder-et qatelghiimeng atkuyaaghulluteng , gold-mengllu qaghpaluteng .
Umiilgusim aqumutaghllagegkeneng kallugem nighwaagpagtii , leveklugtii , tengngaagtiillu piit . Sivugkeni umiilgusim aqumutaghllagem taawa maaghraghvinlek torch-et kumangalghiit , taakut maaghraghvinleguftut taghneghii Kiyaghneghem .
Umiilgusim aqumutaghllagem sivugkeni taawa kelliisugnilnguq qergesa , meghraakeghtaq crystal-estun . Umiilgusim aqumutaghllagem uvitangani , tamaghhiitni sanigkeni , taawa estamat Unguvalghiit , iyeghllaguftut saaymegteggunllu aqsagemegteggunllu .
Sivuliq Unguvalghii lion-esugniteftuq , tuunglighhaa Unguvalghii ox-esugniteftuq , pingayaat sangwaa Unguvalghii gginalguftuq yugem gginaaneng , enkaam estamiitangat Unguvalghii tengaakayugtun qawaagpagtun ayuqeftuq .
Enkaam estamat Unguvalghiit tamaghhaghmeng aghvinlegneng yaqulgututeftut , elngaatall yugusiit iyeghllaguftut talwa qamavek yaqghwita asingitnun . Aghneghtuuman unugtuumaan taaqigalnguut ilaganeghmeng , " Agleghnalghii , agleghnalghii , agleghnalghii , Atanghuuq Kiyaghneq , Aghtughyaghqaghhaanghiteghllak , ellnganguuq maaten , ellnganguuq sivunghani , ellnganguuq tagiyaghqaq ! "
Taakut estamat Unguvalghiit ilagaghtut ilagaatngitneng usuqillghem , quulvaghillghem , iyamsiqayullghem aqumgalghiimun umiilgusigni aqumutaghllagegni , kiyaghlleghhiimun quunperugllak kenlengunaan . Tawaten pinghata
yuginaq estamat siipneqluki elder-et niinghutaqut sivungakun aqumgalghiim umiilgusim aqumutaghllagegkenun , manigughaqaat kiyaghlleghhii quunperugllak kenlengunaan . Taakut elder-et qaghpateng mataghlluki lliiqiit sivungakun umiilgusim aqumutaghllagegkenka , enkaam ilagaghaqut ,
" Whangkuta Ataneghput Kiyaghneghput ! Elpek tugupestaaghyaghqaqaten usuqelleghllaget , quulvalleghllaget , iyamsiqayulleghllaget aghtughyaghqaanghilleghpenun . Ulimakaqutegpeneng sangwaa qamagtengngwaaghluku , piyukelleghpetun kiyaghllequt enkaam allgeghullequtlu unguvalleghmeng . "
Taagken esghaghanka iimgat igat aghenqigneghan iigganilluki aqumgalghiim umiilgusim aqumutagkeni . Taakut iimgat igat igaghvikegkaaftut inglugtun , umegluteng maaghraghvinlek seal-eneng .
Taagken esghaghaqa aghtughyaghqaanghilnguq yaqulek . Iglagtuluni aaptilghii , " Kina itagnaghyaghqaawa ikughyaghqaaluki maaghraghvinlek seal-ellghet qelpeghsaghqaaluki iimgat igat ? "
Taawa avangituq kitumeng alngunak qilagmi , nalighmeng nunami , nalighmeng nunam asingani itagnalghii qelpeghsaghqaaluki iimgat igat , esghaghyaghqaalukillu ilungit .
Enkaam qiyaaghwaghllagtunga qayughllak naalkenghilkangat kina alngunak itagnalghii qelpeghsaghqaaluki iimgat igat , esghaghyaghqaalukillu ilungit .
Taagken ataasim elder-eneng piinga , " Qiyagpenang ! Ii-i , lion-a . Judah-m ramkenganeng pinguuq , David-emllu kingunqaa . Kayaalqiistenguuq enkaam ellnga itagnaghtuq ikughyaghqaaluki maaghraghvinlek seal-ellghet qelpeghsaghqaaluki iimgat igat . "
Taagken esghaghaqa Penniighaghaq nekevghalghii saaghwani umiilgusim aqumutam . Qukiitniteftuq estamat unguvalghiit , elder-etlu . Penniighaghaq esghaqaaluni nikimqun tuqutkaq . Maaghraghvinlegneng sighunelguftuq , maaghraghvinlegnengllu iyelguftuq . Taakut iyet maaghraghvinlek taghneghaqii Kiyaghneghem , kayagtekii tamaghhaanun nunam .
Penniighaghaam takuluku umiillgusigni aqumutagni aqumgalghii , aghenqigneghan iigganeng tuwii iimgat igat .
Tuguyaki iimgat igat , taakut estamat unguvalghiit , yuginaqlu estamat siipneqluku elder-et sekequutut nunamun sivungakun Penniighaghaam . Tamaghaghmeng tugumiiqluteng harp-meng , gold-mengllu sagneghhaghneng esleqngalghiit incense-meng . Incense-et yughaqiit Kiyaghneghem yugita .
Ilagaghtut nutaghameng ilagaatmeng whaten : " Itagnaghtuten tuguyaghqaaluki iimgat igat , ikughyaghqaalukillu seal-ngit . Tuqutkaalghiiten , aawpenengllu tukfiqaqaten yuget Kiyaghneghmun . Ellngit tamaghhiitneng pinguut ramkeneng , uluneng , yugneng , nunataanengllu .
Enkaam Ataneghpagullghanitestaten , priest-ngughtestatenllu Kiyaghnemnnun , umiilgestunllu igleghutillequt nunami . "
Esghapagumalunga nagaqughanka mengit yaqulelghuteghllaget . Uglaapiglleghhiit kestepagningilnguut . Nekevghatnguftut uvitangani umiilgusim aqumutam , estamatlu unguvalghiit , elder-etlu .
Iglagtuluteng piiqut , " Penniighaghaq tuqutkaq , itagnaghtuq allgeghsaghqaaluku aghtughyaghqaanghilleq , aklungi , peghqinelleq , iknaqelleq , quulvalleq , nighughqelleq , usuqelleqlu ! "
Taagken nagaqughanka tamaghhaghmeng ulimaaghet , qilagmelnguut , nunamelnguut , nunam asinganilnguut , kelliinilnguutlu . Qamaglluteng pilghiit aqumgalghiimunllu umiilgusigni aqumutagni , Penniighaghaghmunllu , " Usuqillengitek , quulvallengitek , nighughqellengitek , aghtughyaghqaanghillelguteklu quunperugllak kenlengunaan ! "
Taagken estamat unguvalghiit piit , " Amen , " elder-etlu sekequulluteng nunamnun , manigughagket Kiyaghneghenkuk , Penniighaghaankuk .
Taagken esghapagaqa Penniighaghaam qelpeghtekanga sivuliq seal-elleq taakuneng maaghraghvinlegneng seal-elleghneng . Tawanteftut estamat Unguvalghiit , nagaqughaqa ataasiq pilghii , " Tagi ! " Menga kallugestun tengngaalghii .
Taagken esghaghaqa qatelghii kuuni . Igleghutistenga ughluvelguftuq , qaghpalitaatlu . Ellnganguuq kayaalqiikaq anguyagmineng , enkaam aanuq kayaalqiimanginaghnaluni .
Penniighaghaam qelpeghsaqminigu tuunglighhaa seal-ellghem , nagaqughaqa tuunglighhaa Unguvalghii pilghii , " Tagi ! "
Ilanga kuunim aanuq , kavilnguuftuq . Igleghutistenga pilleghqalitaat yuget nekeggmetunnaniitesqelluki tuququutesqelluki . Tuunegkaatlu savigpagrugllagmeng .
Taagken Penniighaghaam qelpeghsaqminigu pingayiitanga seal-ellghem , nagaqughaqa pingayiitangat Unguvalghii pilghii , " Tagi ! " Esghaghaqa tagnelghii kuuni . Igleghutistenga aapqaasilguftuq iiggmini .
Nagaqughaqa mestun ayuqesugnilnguq akulngitni estamat Unguvalghiit pilghii , " Quart-em imaa wheat-a akikaa ataasim denarius-em . Pingayut quart-em imii barley-t akikii ataasim denarius-em . Iwernga naafqegpenakek olive-em mesiigha , wine-allu . "
Taagken Penniighaghaam qelpeghsaqminigu estamiitanga seal-ellghem , nagaqughaqa estamiitangat Unguvalghiit pilghii , " Tagi ! "
Esghaghaqa aghsaallaak kuuni . Igleghutistengan aatqeftaa Tuqulleq , Hades-em maligtaa . Pilleghqalitkaaftuk tuquqiisqelluki estamaghqellghan nunam yugi savigpagkun , paneghaatelleghqun , aqnighneghqun , ugwighsalghiitgunllu teghikusiitgun nunam .
Taagken Penniighaghaam qelpeghsaqminigu tallimiitanga seal-ellghem , esghaghanka asinganilluki aghqefigem unguvasiit tuququqat . Tuqutkaqegkangit qayughllak ugpeqegkaqegkangit Kiyaghneghem akuzitangi , ungipaqumanginaqiitlu .
Akilghuughllagtut , " Kaay Aghtughyaghqaghhaanghiteghllak Ataneq , agleghnaghtutenllu , ipapiguutenllu ! Tamaakut nunam yugi tuququqat whangkunneng , naten tagkaan utaqiinnaqsiki nanqigsaghqaalukillu aghyuughyaghqaalukillu ? "
Taagken ataasikaghtiita unguvasiit tuqutkat qatelghiimeng atkuyaalitkiit , meghnaaliightesqegkiitlu . Tawaten piyaghqaagut qayughllak ilangi ugpeqaalgutngit , Christ-amllu qepghaghtengi tuqusaghqaagut ellngita tuqutellghistun . Enkaam meghnaalinaqut kenlanga uglaghtalngit naamigtekata tamaakut tuqusaghqat .
Esghapagaqa Penniighaghaam qelpeghsaqminigu aghvinliitanga seal-ellghem nuna ufsuguteghllagtuq . Siqineq tagneghtaa suvinalghiitun qiipaghaghtun ulimakatun goat-em melqwaneng . Tanqiqllu esleqngalghii aawestun lliightuq .
Ighaleqetaaghet qilagameng ifkaquutut nunamun katam tawaten qigumangilnguut figs-et ifkaquullghiit uqfigmeng anuqeghllagem ufsugutellghatun .
Qilaga aviighutuq iimgat igat imellghistun , qamaglluteng naayghatlu qiighqatlu nuughquutut nemeggneng .
Taagken nunam umiilgi , igleghutistengi , pilluwaghtet umiilgit , aklungilnguut , qiilngumightikayuget , tamaghhaghmeng qepghaghtelaaghet , qepghaghtelaaghunghilnguutlu iightuutut qayeni , akulngitnillu uyghaget naayghani .
Naayghanunllu uyghagnunllu akilghuugut , " Ulleghvikikut iighesqelluta gginaaneng aqumgalghiim aqumutagkeni umiilgusim , sakraalleghllaganengllu Penniighaghaam !
Kaatuq Aghneq aghyuughilleghqaghllagak whangkunnun enkaam kitumngam anaglleqagu ! "
Tamaakut kingungitneng esghaghanka estamat yaqulget nekevghallghiit estamani kangighiitni nunam . Yaqulget nuqneqeftiit estamat anuqet anuqlinghitesqelluku nunami nalighmeng kelliini nalighmeng alngunak uqfigni .
Taagken esghaghaqa ilanga yaqulek mayulghii asivaghmeng tugumiilek nalluniighutanganeng unguvalghiim Kiyaghneghem . Yaqulgem akilghuugii estamat yaqulget Kiyaghneghem tuunegkii aghtughyaghqaanghilleghmeng naafqesqelluku nuna , kelliillu .
Yaqulgem pii , " Naafqegpenaan nuna nalighmeng kellii nalighmeng uqfiget ! Utaqiitek kenlanga seal-ellemnnun qawiitgun qepghaghtengi Kiyaghnemta . "
Taagken nagaqughanka qafsingutangi yuget seal-elaghtuqiit qawiitgun . Yuget uglaghtalangit 144,000-nguftut tamaghhiitneng ramkenganeng Israel-em .
Judah-m ramkenganeng 12,000-nguftut , Reuben-em ramkenganeng 12,000-nguftut , Gad-em ramkenganeng 12,000-nguftut ,
Asher-em ramkenganeng 12,000-nguftut , Naphtali-m ramkenganeng 12,000-nguftut , Manasseh-m ramkenganeng 12,000-nguftut ,
Simeon-em ramkenganeng , 12,000-nguftut , Levi-em ramkenganeng , 12,000-nguftut , Issachar-em ramkenganeng , 12,000-nguftut ,
Zebulun-em ramkenganeng , 12,000-nguftut , Joseph-em ramkenganeng , 12,000-nguftut , Benjamin-em ramkenganeng , 12,000-nguftut .
Taam kingunganeng esghaghanka uglapestaaghllaget yulghuteghllaget kitum alngunak kestepagningilkangi ! Tamaghhiitneng pinguftut nunataaneng , ramkeneng , yugneng , ulunengllu . Nekevghatnguftut umiilgusim aqumutam , Penniighaghaamllu sivugkenkun . Qiipaghaalluteng qatelghiineng , tugumiighlutengllu palm-em uqfigan avayiitneng .
Akilghuuteghllagtut , " Yugulilleq Kiyaghnemta pikaa umiilgusigni aqumutagni aqumgalghii , Penniighaghaamllu ! "
Qamaglluteng yaqulget nekevuutut uvitangitni umiilgusim aqumutam , elder-etlu , estamatlu unguvalghiit . Taagken sekequutut nunamun sivungakun umiilgusim aqumutam , manigughaat Kiyaghneq .
Piit , " Amen ! Kiyaghneghput tamaghhaghmi usuqligu , nighughqelligu , iyamsiqayugvikligu , quulvaghligu qayughllak ellnganguuq peghqinellelek , aghtughyaghqaanghillelek , iknaqelleleklu . Ellnga tawatetuq quunperugllak kenlengunaan ! Amen ! "
Taagken ataasim elder-eneng aaptaanga , " Kinkungaawat qatelghiimeng qiipaghaghngalghiit , nakenllu pingwaat ? "
Kiimsighaqa , " Yuguniiq , elpek liisimakaten . " Elder-em piinga , " Taakunguut suflughutkat seghleliighrukutaaghllagmeng . Penniighaghaam aawakun aghvigluki qiipaghateng , qateghtestekaqiit .
Tamaaken apalluqluku nekevghatnguut sivugkeni Kiyaghneghem umiilgusiin aqumutagkeni . Manigughaqaat aghneghtuumaan unugtuumaan Temple-ngani . Aqumgalghiim umiilgusigni aqumutagni azigutighlleqii nayuutngalleghmineng .
Iyatiqnanighllequt , nalighmeng meqsugyugnanighllequt . Siqinghem nalighmeng alngunak uguqnaghllalghiim ugunnaanghitii .
Penniighaghaq umiilgusim aqumutam saaghwanilnguq penniighniightekelleqaat . Maghyaghqughlleqii sengngulghiinun meghnun unguvallelitikayugnun , Kiyaghneghemllu quningightughlleqii . "
Penniighaghaam qelpeghtaqngamigu maaghraghvinliitanga seal-ellghem , qilagmi qallegnanighwaaghutut entaqun aflum avellghatun tagkaan .
Taagken esghaghanka taakut maaghraghvinlek yaqulget nekevghalghiit Kiyaghneghem sivungakun . Tamaghhaghmeng qalghightaatenguutut .
Taagken ilanga yaqulek , tugumiilek gold-meng sagneghmeng , tagiluni nekevuq aghqefigegni . Tuunegkaat incense-elghutmeng ilatesqelluki qamaglluki yughiitnun Kiyaghneghem yugan . Yaqulgem llii gold-egnun aghqefigegnun sivunganilnguuk umiilgusim aqumutam .
Incense-em agepsaa mayughtuq maligulluni yughallghitgun Kiyaghneghem yugita . Mayughtut Kiyaghneghmun sagneghmeng yaqulgem tugumiighaneng .
Taagken yaqulgem , tuguluku sagneq , imighaa kenghaneng aghqefigem . Sagneghem imii miluutii nunamun . Enkaam kallugughteghllagtuq , kavlegtaghllagtuq , nighwaaghpagtaghllagtuq , nunallu ufsuguteghllagtuq .
Taagken maaghraghvinlek yaqulget , qalghightaatelget yataaghqut qalghightinaluteng .
Sivuliim yaqulgem qalghightaatni qalghightaa . Taagken kaftekragenkuk , kenghenkuk akumlutek aawmeng nunamun miluutagket . Enkaam pingayughqellgha nunam paneghtuq , pingayughqellghitlu uqfiget paneghtut , qamagllutengllu sungaghyulghiit vegaaghet paneghtut .
Tuunglighhaan yaqulgem qalghightaatni qalghightaa . Taagken sangwaa naayghaghllagsugnilnguq kumaghugngalghii , miluutaat kelliinun . Enkaam pingayughqellgha kelliim aawgughtuq .
Pingayughqellghit kelliinilnguut unguvalghiit tuquut , pingayughqellghitlu angyaghpaget naafqengngwaaghii .
Pingayiitangita yaqulgem qalghightaatni qalghightaa . Taagken ighaleqetaaghllak , kumaghughngalghii torch-etun , qilagameng ifkaghtuq pingayughqellghitgun kiiwetlu sengngulghiitlu meghet .
Aatgha ighaleqetaaghem " Sungaghni " . Pingayughqellgha meghem sungaghnightekaq enkaam yulghuteghllaget meghluteng tuqukat qayughllak meq sungaghnightekaalghii .
Estamiitangita yaqulgem qalghightaatni qalghightaa . Taagken saam tenpii siqineq , tanqiq , ighaleqataaghetlu , enkaam pingayughqellghi mamlegtii . Pingayughqellgha aghneghem mamlegtaa , pingayughqellghallu unugem .
Esghaghaqallu nagaqughaqallu qawaagpak tengaalghii quulvani , iglagtuluni pilghii , " Seghleghwaaghunaqnguuq ! Seghleghwaaghunaqnguuq ! Seghleghwaaghunaqnguuq ! Kinguliit pingayut yaqulget qalghighhnaqegkumegteki qalghightaateteng , taagken elngaatall seghlepestaaghunaqnguuq yugnun nunami kiyaghlleghhiit tamaani pilleghni ! "
Taagken tallimiitangita yaqulgem qalghightaatni qalghightaa . Esghaghaqa ighaleqetaaq ifkaqaq qilagameng nunamun , key-litkaaftuqlu qelpeghtesqelluku asilighneghilnguq laawaaq .
Ighaleqetaaghem qelpeghtaa asilighneghilnguq laawaaq . Tesamaken agepsuq aanuq katam agepsaatun egllughllagem repall siqineqlu qilagallu mamlegtaa agepsum .
Taagken agepsumeng aanleghaatut locust-elghutet , nunamunllu ukigtuutut . Kaapigaqleghutekat yugneng , katam scorpion-et kaapiiqellghistun .
Ungipaatkaalghiit locust-et naafqefqiita vegaaghet pisqelluki nalighmeng sungaghyuget nunivagseghat nalighmeng alngunak uqfiget . Aqnightesqegkiillu tamaakunginaat yuget Kiyaghneghem nalluniillghilkangi qawiitgun .
Locust-enun tuququghtesnaniqii tamaakut yuget , taawanginaq ikfiqesteghllagestesqegkii tallimanun tanqinun . Scorpion-et kaapellghistun yuget ikfiqeghllakat .
Taakuni tallimani tanqini tamaakut yuget tuquyupigllequt , iwernga tuqupagningillequt . Yuget tuqunaqeghllagllequt , iwernga tuqunaanghitut .
Locust-et esghaqaaluteng kuunistun ayuqut pilluwamun yataaghqegkat . Naasqwitniteftut llangaqa gold-et qaghpat , gginiitlu yuget gginiistun ayuqluteng .
Nuyiit aghnat nuyiistun ayuqluteng , gguutngitlu lion-et gguutngistun ayuqluteng .
Yugusimegteggun qaltelguftut esghaqaaluteng savikenghaaghet sakimagiitat . Yaqwghitallu sulugtallghit llangaqa chariot-et kuunituqat sukeralghiit pilluwamun .
Papelguftut scorpion-estun kaapikayugmeng . Enkaam tallimanun tanqinun yuget ikfiqesteghllagiit papegmeggneng kapughluki .
Umiilelguftut igleghutilghii ellngitneng , yaqulguftuq esghaamakistenga asilighneghilnguum laawaaghem . Hebrew-stun aatgha Abaddon , Greek-estun Apollyon , ( whaten pisiq , " Naafqiista " ) .
Sivuliq seghlepestaaghllak alpagtuq , taam kingunganeng paninang maalghuk seghlepestaaghllagek piyaghqaaguk .
Taagken aghvinliitangita yaqulgem qalghightaatni qalghightaa . Nagaqughaqa ma gold-egneng aghqefigegneng estamaneng sighunelgegneng tekerqamegnekun Kiyaghneghem sivunganilnguuk .
Taam mem aleghqughaa aghvinliitangat yaqulget qalghightaatelek . Pikaa , " Itemutiki estamat yaqulget asighqengngalghiit kiigwllagegni Euphrates-egni ! "
Enkaam estamat yaqulget itemutkii . Yataaghqegkaaftut taamun aflumun , aghneghmun , tanqimun , ayumiqulleghmunllu tuquqiisqelluki pingayughqellghi yuget .
Ungipaataanga uglaghtalangitneng kuunitgun igleghlleghhiit pilluwaghtet , 200 million-nguftut .
Esghaghwaallemkun esghaghanka kuunit , igleghutistengitlu . Sakimagiitiit kenghestun kaviteftut , sapphire-estun sungaghyukegteftut , sulphur-estun , yellow-nguftut . Kuunit naasqwit lion-et naasqwistun ayuqeftut , qaanghitneng aanut keneq , agepsuq , sulphur-a .
Taakutgun pingayutgun naafqiilleghllagteggun tuququghiit pingayughqellghi yuget . Kuunit qaanghitneng aanleghaatut keneq , agepesuq , sulphur-a .
Kuunit aghtughyaghqaanghillelguut qaanghitnillu paapgitnillu . Paapgit nemeghyastun ayuqelghiit naasqulget kiitiqusiit yugnun .
Ilangi tamaakut yuget tuqutellghilkangit tamaakut naafqiilleghllaget , avuteghqumangilnguut pegsugumangilkangit kiyaghnengllaqateng . Manigughnaniimangitiit tughneghaat , kiyaghnengllaqatlu ulimaaghet gold-meng , silver-meng , siilumeng , uyghagmeng , unaghsimengllu . Tamaakut esghaasaghqaanghilnguut , nagaquusaghqaanghilnguut , nalighmeng piyugyaghqaanghilnguut .
Talwa avuteghqutkumangilkangit yugtalleteng , alignaghtaalleteng , nengughtegpenateng atuqutelleghteng , nalighmeng teglegniilleteng .
Taagken esghaghaqa ilanga aghtiigateghllak yaqulek ukilghii qilagmeng . Pilugugngaftuq qilagwaaghmeng , naasqwan qulangani agluk , gginaa siqineghtun kuukgulluni , ighukeklu kumaghulghiistun pillar-estun ayuqlutek .
Tugumiiqeftii iimgat igaghhaat qelpalnguut . Aghenqigneghet itegani tuutestii kelliim meghan qaayngakun , saghumigneghetlu itegani tuutestii quutkun .
Iglagtupiglluni akilghuuguq lion-em uwighhniillghatun . Akilghuughllagyan maaraghvinlegyaget kalluget tengngaagtaghtut .
Maaghraghvinlegyaget kalluget tengngaagtaghyata igaqnaqsaghanka sameng pillghit . Iwernga nagaqughaqa ma qilagmeng pilghii , " Aksaqiki maaghraghvinlegyaget kalluget sameng pillghit , igaqegpenaki ! "
Taagken esghaghaqa yaqulek nekevghalghii kelliikunllu quutkunllu . Qilagmun nengugutii aghenqigneghet iiggeni ,
akeqiiq Kiyaghneghem aatghakun kiyaghlleghhii quunperugllak kenlengunaan . Ellngangulghii ulimaghikaq qilagameng , nunameng , kelliineng , samengllu tamaghhaaneng taakunilngughneng . Yaqulek piiq , " Pilleghqaq kaatuq .
Iwernga maaghraghvinliitangita yaqulgem qalghighhnaqegkumigu qalghightaatni , taawa Kiyaghneghem apeghiighlleqaa uspeqilleni qayvighsimangilkenni sivunghani . Uspeqillgha ataasiiguq aapqaa qepghaghteminun uuknaliqistenun . "
Taagken nagaquqama mem qilagmeng aleghqughlaataghaanga , " Aglaghluten tuguki qelpalnguut iimgat igat iigganilnguut yaqulgem nekevghalghiim kelliikunllu quutkunllu . "
Yaqulegmun aglaghlunga tungsighanka imegngalghiit igaghhaat . Piinga , " Tuguluki neghiki ; aqsaqughpeni qugaagllequt iwernga qaneghpeni muugallequt honey-stun . "
Yaqulgem iigganeng tuguluki iimgat igaghhaat neghanka , imani qanemni muugatut honey-stun . Iwernga tuufsaqenka aqsaquqa quwaagtaa .
Taagken piitnga , " Allameng uuknaliqutkepestaaghyaghqaqaten yulghutet , nunatalghutet , alaaghhiinaat ululghutet , umiilelghutetlu . "
Taagken kitum ayaviilitaanga usputaasiqesqelluku . Enkaam kayagtaanga , " Usputaghyaghtughhu Kiyaghneghem Temple-nga , aghqefigeklu , kesnaketenllu yuget maniguullghiit tawani .
Iwernga usputaghpenaan Kiyaghneghem Temple-ngan court-nga eslataanilnguq , qayughllak tuunegkaaguq Gentile-enun . Tutmaasghaqnaqngwaat Agleghnalghii Neghllak forty two-ghyagni tanqini .
Ungipaghtegka pilugugngalghiik sackcloth-meng , aghtughyaghqaanghillelelleqagka uuknaliqesqellukek 1,260 aghneghnun . "
Maalghuk ungipaghtek maalghuguuk olive-em uqfigek , maalghuguuklu kenelghutam tunemakek nekevghalghiik sivungani Atanghan nunam .
Enkaam kitum alngunak aqnighhnaqutkegkumikek , qaanghegkeneng kenghem aanluni tuququghlleqiik anguyagik . Kitumllu alngunak aqnighhnaqutkegkumikek taawa tuqusaghqaaghllequq .
Aghtughyaghqaanghillelguuk qilaga eslallugughnaniisqelluku uuknaliqellghegkegni . Aghtughyaghqaanghillelguuk meghet aawughtesqelluki . Aghtughyaghqaanghillelguuklu allaaghhiinaghneng ikfiqnalghiineng seghleliighllagneng , awen tawaten piiqellequk piyukelleghmegetun .
Apeghiiqayek ungipaneghmeng , asilighneghilngughmeng laawaaghmeng aanellequq teghikusalluuk . Pilluwaghlleqaak enkaam kayaalqegkumikek tuqulleqaak .
Kemegkwaaghik tamaanllequk tuumngani neghllagem , Atanghita qaquuraghvigani . Taana neghllak aatqeftuq Sodom-emengllu Egypt-mengllu qayughllak yugi Sodom-eghmiistunllu Eygpt-eghmiistunllu ayuqelghiit .
Yuget nunataghhaaneng , ramkeneng , allaaghhiinaghneng uluneng , nunatanengllu tagillequt esghaghnalukek kemegkwaaghik . Tawaten pillequt pingayunun aghneghnun avellelighluku , kitumunllu alngunak qungughtesnanighlleqagket .
Taakuk uuknaliqistek ikfiqestighllakaalghiik nunam yugitnun . Enkaam yuget quyaghllagllequt , tunquullequtlu tunusameng ilameggnun , apalluqluku tuqullghegkenun .
Iwernga kingungitneng pingayut aghneghet avellelighluku Kiyaghneghem aneghneni iteghtestekaa uuknaliqistegnun . Enkaam nekevyayek , qamaglluteng tamaakut esghaghlukek alingruughuteghllakat .
Taagken uuknaliqistek nagaqughaak iglagtupiglleghhii ma qilagmeng pilghii , " Mayughtek whavek ! " Anguyagik esghapagumaluki mayughtuk qilagmun qilawaaghqun .
Tawani pilleghmi qevuutepiglluni nuna ufsuguteghllagtuq ; qulaghqellgha neghllagem naavuq . Enkaam seven thousand yuuk tuququghaa nunam ufsugutelleghllagan . Tamaakut yuget yaywaasekat kakavaataateghllagluteng usuquughtaat Kiyaghnegha qilagem .
Tuunglighhaa seghlepestaaghllagem seghleliillghem alpagtuq , iwernga esghaghteggu pingayaa seghlepestaaghllagem seghleliillghem kaasaghtungestaghtuq .
Taagken maaghraghvinliitangita yaqulgem qalghightaatni qalghightaa . Iglagtupiglluteng met qilagmi piit , " Ataneghpagullgha nunam ataneghpagulqaaghtaak Atanemtallu Christ-anganllu , enkaam Ellnga igleghutillequq quunperugllak kenlengunaan ! "
Taagken yuginaq estamat siipneqluku siivanlleghet aqumgalghiit umiilgusitgun aqumutamegteggun Kiyaghneghem sivungani , gginateng sekelluki manigughaat Kiyaghneq .
Pikaat : " Iyamsiqayugvikamken , Ataneq Kiyaghneq Aghtughyaghqaghhaanghilnguq , kiyaghlleghhii maaten , iiwlengllu kiyaghlleghhii ! Tugumaan aghtughyaghqaanghitelleghllagen enkaam piinlightuten igleghutimun .
Nunam yugi sakriteghllagtut , iwernga maaten sakraalleghqan kaatuq . Tuqukat nanqigsaghqaaghtut . Akileghtughyaghqaaghtaten qepghaghteten uuknaliqistet , agleghnalghiit yugten , qamagllukillu siivakilghiit elpeneng , ukavanlenguutlu apeghseghutlu . Tuququlleghqan kaatuq tamaakunun tuququqaneng yugneng nunami . "
Taagken Kiyaghneghem Temple-nga qilagmelnguq qelpateftuq . Tawani Temple-ngani esghaghagka Ark-ek Kiyaghneghem Covenant-elghutakek . Taagken nighwaagpagtaghtuk , eftughtaghtuk , tengngaagtaghtuklu kallugek ; nuna ufsuguteghllagtuq , kaftekragughteghllagaallu !
Taagken qilagami sangwaa saghiighanapiglleghhii aliightuq liigikusighqaghput piyaghqamun : Aghnaq pilugugluni siqineghmeng , itegii tanqikun nekeglluteng , naasqumikun qaghpaluni qula maalghuk siipneqluku ighaleqetaaghneng .
Qumilguftuq , ighniyugem aqnighqelluku lliighaa , aanaqellghan taghnughhaam araghqaa .
Taagken qilagami sangwaa ilanga saghiighanapiglleghhii aliightuq liigikusighqaghput apeghiighnaqelghiimun : Taawa kavilnguq dragon-eghllak , maaghraghvinlek naasqulek , qula sighunelek , enkaam qamaglluteng naasqwi qaghpalgututeftut .
Papegmineng saqipgutii nunamun pingayughqellghi qilagam ighaleqetaaghi . Taagken dragon-a nekevegkaq manungakun aghnam neghnaluku taghnughhaa ighniighesnaqagu .
Aghnaq ighnenguq , igleghusaghqii qamagtengngwaaghluki nunam yugi iron-meng anagutalighluni . Iwernga aghnam taghnughhaa akuqaghluku aglaataat Kiyaghneghmun , umiilgusigkenunllu aqumutagnun .
Aghnaq qimagtuq kilgaanun . Tamaani Kiyaghneghem yataaghqutkaqegkanga nekaghqameng , aflengaksaghqaqegkangat 1,260 aghneghet .
Taagken qilagmi pillugutut . Michael-enkut yaqulkullghiit pilluwaghaat dragon-a . Dragon-enkut yaqulkullghiit pilluwaghiit Michael-enkut yaqulkullghiit ,
iwernga Michael-enkut kayaalqaat dragon-a . Enkaam dragon-enkut yaqulkullghiit qilagmesaghqaananightut .
Qilagmeng miluutaat dragon-eghllak . ( Neghightaluk nemeghyaq aatgha Tughneghaq , nalighmeng Tughneghaq , puughqughtenga nunam yugan . ) Miluutaat nunamun yaqulegtuumaan .
Taagken nagaqughaqa ma iglagtuluni qilagmeng pilghii , " Whaa kaasimaat Kiyaghneghem yugulighillgha , aghtughyaghqaanghillgha , ataneghpagullghallu , Christ-anganllu aghtughyaghqaanghillgha . Salin Tughneghaq miluutellghilluku qilagmeng , aghneghtuumaan unugtuumaan anaggutnganiiqii ugpeqaalguteput Kiyaghneghmun .
Ugpeqaalgutemta kayaalqumaat aawakun Penniighaghaam , ungipaqelleghmegteggunllu Kiyaghneghem ipapighqellgha . Talwa tuquyaghngaaghmeng ayuqut Christ-a apalluqluku .
Enkaam qamagllusi kiyaghlleghhiini qilagmi , quyateghllagtek ! Iwernga seghleghwaaghunaqnguusi nunamelngughnillu kelliinilngughnillu ! Tughneghaam ukigvikumiisi , sakriteghllaguuq qayughllak liisimakaa pilleghqiighusaghtughtuq . "
Dragon-em liigiksamigu nunamun miluutelleni , malighqaghaa aghnaq ighnengegkaq .
Iwernga aghnaq tuunegkaat qawaagpagrugllagem yaqugkeneng tengaasqelluku kilgaanun . Tamaani paqniillequq nemeghyameng , aflengakelleqaatlu pingayut ayumiqullghet , aghvinlek tanqit ilalluki .
Taagken nemeghyam ughyuutaa meq kiiwestun ayuqelghii aghnaq maaqutesqelluku .
Iwernga nunam kayusiitaa aghnaq . Nunam agitaghulluku tuuftaa meghllak dragon-em ughyuutkaa .
Taagken dragon-em ugumiyaguteghllagluku aghnaq , enkaam pilluwaghyaghtughii qamaglluki ilangi kingunghi . Tamaakunguut qaatkutngalghiit Kiyaghneghem qelghusiitnun , ataasiighmelnguutlu ipalleghmun apeghtuusaqegkaanun Jesus-em .
Taagken dragon-a nekevuq kelliim esnaakun .
Taagken esghaghaqa teghikusalluuk aanelghii kelliimeng . Qulanguftut sighunghi , maaghraghvinlek naasqulek . Qamaglluteng sighunghi qaghpalgututeftut , tamaghhaghmeng naasqut igaqughvikngaftut ateghmeng seghlequulghiimeng Kiyaghneghmun .
Taana teghikusalluuk leopard-esugnituq , itegii kayngem itegaatun ayuqelghiit , qaangha lion-em qaanghatun ayuqelghii . Dragon-em tuunaa teghikusalluuk aghtughyaghqaanghilleghmineng , umiilgusigmineng aqumutagneng , igleghutiyaghqaaghtestaallu ateni atuqluku .
Ataasiq naasqwa teghikusalluugem tuqutesugnitkaq kiitighluni , iwernga taana kiiyallgha maamegkaaftuq . Iingunaghhaghmeng nunam yugita saghiighayagulluku maligtaat teghikusalluuk .
Qamaglluteng yuget manigughaat dragon-a qayughllak teghikusalluugmun tuunegkanga aghtughyaghqaanghilleni . Manigughaatlu teghikusalluuk , piit , " Kinangam teghikusalluugtun ayuqa ? Kitumngam pilluwaghlleqagu ? "
Taagken teghikusalluuk akuziyaghqaaghtuq . Aangaayugteghllagtuq , seghlepestaatunllu akuzitkaa Kiyaghneq . Aghtughyaghqaanghillenguq igleghutiyaghqaaluni 42-nun tanqinun .
Piinlighaa seghlepestaatun akuzitkilleni Kiyaghneghmeng , aatghaneng , kiyaghfiganeng , tamaakunengllu kiyaghlleghhiineng qilagmi .
Aghtughyaghqaanghillelitaa pilluwiisqelluki Kiyaghneghem yugi , kayaalqesqellukillu . Igleghusaghqaaghtestii qamaglluki ramket , yuget , ulut , nunataanilnguutlu yuget .
Qamaglluni nunami kiyaghlleghhiim manigughlleqaat teghikusalluuk . Iwernga tamaakut aatghit igaqngalghiit Igiitgun Unguvallghem manigughnaanghitaat . Kiyaghneghem igaqegkaqii aatghit nunangllallghilluni . Taakut igat pikii Penniighaghaam , yuget tuqutkiita .
" Nagatek , sigutelgukufsi :
Kina alngunak tuguyaghqaakumi , tugulleqaat . Kina alngunak tuqusaghqaakumi savigpagkun , tuqulleqaat savigpagkun . Taakuk whaten pisiiguk : Kiyaghneghem yugi nuqenneghtuyaghqaagutlu ugpeqillelguyaghqaagutlu . "
Taagken esghaghaqa ilanga teghikusalluuk nunameng aanelghii . Maalghugegneng sighunelguftuq penniighaghaam sighunghatun , akuziiqlu dragon-etun .
Sivuliq teghikusalluuk tawanlluku tunglighhaan teghikusalluugem atuqaa qamaglluku aghtughyaghqaanghillgha . Taaggun aghtughyaghqaanghilleghqun maniguutestii qamaglluki nunam yugi sivulighmun teghikusalluugmun . ( Kiiyallghan tuqutesugnitkaa , iwernga kiiyallgha maamegkaq . )
Tuunglighhaa teghikusalluuk allaaghlluwhaghtighllagaataghtuq , talwa qilagmeng nunamun keneq ukigtestaa yuget esghaamanghitni .
Tuunglighhaa teghikusalluuk aghtughyaghqaanghillenguq allaaghlluwaghtiyaghqaaluni tawantellghani sivuliim teghikusalluugem . Tamaagun allaaghlluwhaghtilleghteggun puughtii qamaglluki yuget kiyaghlleghhiit nunami . Qelghii yuget nangaghnenglliisqelluki quulviisqelluku sivuliq teghikusalluuk . ( Taana tuqutkaayalghii savigpagkun iwernga unguvaqaq . )
Tuunglighhaa teghikusalluuk aghtughyaghqaanghillenguq aneghnengestiyaghqaaluni unguvalleghmeng nangaghneghanun teghikusalluugem . Enkaam nangaghneq akuziyaqlegughtuq . Taagken nangaghneghem qelghii yuget tuquqiisqelluki tamaakut maniguusunghilnguut ellminun .
Tuunglighhaan teghikusalluugem nalluniightiisqii number-meng qamaglluki yuget aghenqigneghitgun iiggitgun nalighmeng qawiitgun . Tawaten qelghii aangwaaghughngaata , ukavansaghngaata , aklungiteghngaata , aklumaghngaata , qepghaghtelaaghunghiteghngaata , qepghaghtelaaghughngaata .
Kina alngunak tukfighiyaghqaanghituq nalighmeng akikiyaghqaanghituq wetkuqun nalluniillelgukumi . Taana nalluniilkutaq teghikusalluugem aatqaa nalighmeng aatghan number-kaa .
Peghqinellelgem liigiknaaghaa una . Sumeghtaghalleghmikun liigikelleqaa sameng pisiitanga teghikusalluugem number-nga . Taana number-a yugmun aatghuuq , 666-nguuq .
Taagken esghaghaqa taawa Penniighaghaq nekevghalghii Naayghami Zion-mi . Ellnganituteftut 144,000 yuget , qagumegteggun igaqfikegkat aatghaneng , Atanganllu aatghaneng .
Nagaqughaqallu ma qilagmeng . Nagatkaaluni llangaqa qallangatun meghllaget , tengngaagatunllu kallugem . Nagatkaqa ma llangaqa harp-estet aynganangallghiistun harp-etgun ayuqelghii .
144,000 yuget nekevghatnguftut sivungani umiilgusim aqumutam , estamatlu unguvalghiit , elder-etlu . Taakut yuget ilagaghaqeftut ilagaateghraghaghmeng . Kitum alngunak taana ilagaan liisaghqaqenghilkanga iwerngaqun 144,000 yuget . Ellnginguut Kiyaghneghem yugulikii qungangitneng nunam yuganeng .
Taakut yuget nukeggnaghqumangilnguugut aghnameng atuqilleghqun . Maligtaqaat Penniighaghaq navek alngunak pinghani . Kiyaghneghem yugulikaqii akulngitneng nunam yugan , tunusaqsuwhaaghuut Kiyaghneghmunllu Penniighaghaghmunllu .
Iqlengiqigatngwaaghtut . Apalliitut .
Taagken esghaghaqa ilanga yaqulek tengaalghii quulvaghpani . Aapghii kenlengilnguut Pinilghiit Ungipat nunami kiyaghlleghhiinun , tamaghhiitnun nunataanilngughnun yugnun , ramkenun , ulunun , yugnunllu .
Iglagtupiglluni piiq , " Alikiteggu Kiyaghneq , usuqiteggu aangelleghllaga ! Yugneng nanqigtilleghqaa kaatuuq . Manigughteggu ulimaghikaq qilagameng , nunameng , kelliineng , sengngulghiinengllu meghneng ! "
Tuunglighhaan yaqulgem maligtaa sivuliq , whaten pimaghmi , " Naavumaaq ! Babylon-eghllak naavumaaq ! Babylon-em seghletun atuqillgha sex-meng wine-etun ayuquq . Wine-mineng meghesqughii qamaglluki nunam yugi , enkaam ellngitallu seghletun sex atuqsagutaat . Enkaam tawaten pilleghmegteggun Kiyaghneghmun aghyuughteslequt . "
Pingayaak yaqulgem maligutuq sivuliignun . Iglagtupiglluni piiq , " Kitum alngunak maniguqumigu teghikusalluuk , nangaghneghallu , allgeghsimakumigullu nalluniilleq qagumikun nalighmeng iiggmikun
meghyaghqaqaa wine-nga Kiyaghneghem sakraallghan . Taana wine-a meliimangilnguq kuuvegkaq qayuusimun Kiyaghneghem sakraalqaa ! Kina alngunak maniguutkaq taakugnun ikfiqeghllagyaghqaaguq keneghmillu , sulphur-millu , sivungitni agleghnalghiitlu yaqulget , Penniighaghaamllu .
Kenghem ikfiqesteghllaglleqii , agepsaa mayughllequq quunperugllak kenlengunaan . Ikfiqnanighnaanghitut aghneghtuumaan unugtumaan , maniguutkaatmeggneng teghikusalluugmun , nangaghneghanun , nalluniiqaatmeggnengllu aatghaneng . "
Tamaakut qamaglluteng whaten pisiigut , Kiyaghneghem yugi nuqenneghtupestaaghyaghqaagut . Tamaakunguut qaatkutngalghiit Kiyaghneghem qelghusaanun , ataasiighmellutengllu Jesus-mun .
Taagken nagaqughaqa qilagmeng ma pilghii , " Igaqigu una : Whaken kenlekluku quyasaghqaagut tuquyaghqat qepghaasimaluku Ataneq ! " Taghneghak piik , " Quyanapestaaghtut ! Meghnaalillequt ughleghiilleghmeggneng , yuget neqamikelleqiit aneghneghqillghit . "
Taagken esghaghaqa taawa qatelghii qilawaaq , qilawaghqun aqumgaftuq llangaqa ighnegha yugem . Naasqumikun gold-meng qaghpalguftuq , tugumiiqeftaallu ipelghii pakregmelnguq savik .
Taagken ilanga yaqulek aanuq Temple-meng . Akilghuughllagaa aqumgalghii qilagwaaghmi , " Pakregmelnguq savigen atuqluku unataa , qayughllak unatalleghqaq kaatuq , nunam piitestekaa unataghyaghqaaghtengnguuq ! "
Enkaam qilawaaghmi aqumgalghiim pakregmelnguq savini unataasiqaa nunamun .
Taagken ilanga yaqulek aanuq Temple-meng qilagmi , ellngallu ipelghiimeng pakregmelngughmeng savilguftuq .
Taagken ilanga yaqulek aanuq aghqefigegneng aflengakistenga kenghan aghqefigem . Akilghuughllagaa yaqulek ipelghiimeng pakregmelngughmeng savilek , " Savigpeneng kepughqi grapes-et nunam vine-nganeng , qayughllak grapes-et qigumaat ! "
Enkaam yagulgem pakregmelnguq savini saqipgutaa nunamun , kepughii grapes-et nunam vine-nganeng . Taagken miluqutaqii grapes-em qageghquusighllaganun . Taananguuq Kiyaghneghem sakritfigllaga .
Grapes-mun qageghquusik eslataanilnguuk neghllagem . Grapes-et qageghqughyalghiimeng aawk maaquq qageghquusineng 180 miles tagtalkelluku , 5 feet uusqaghtulkelluku .
Taagken qilagami aliightuq sangwaa saghiighanapiglleghhii liisimakusighqaghput piyaghqamun . Taawa maaghraghvinlek yaqulget , tagitilghiit maaghraghvinlegneng seghleliilleghllagneng . Taakut seghleliilleghllaget taaqniitkeftii Kiyaghneghem sakraalleghllagan .
Taagken esghaghaqa kelliisugnilnguq meghraakegtaq siqinwaaghestun , akumngalghii keneghmeng . Esghaghankallu kayaalqiikat teghikusalluugmeng , nangaghneghaneng , aatghanllu number-nganeng . Nekevghatnguftut saaghwaghni kelliim , harp-elightuulluteng Kiyaghneghem tuunegkiitneng ellngitnun .
Ilagaghaqeftut ilagaatanganeng Moses-em , ( Kiyaghneghem qepghaghtenga ) , ilagaatanganengllu Penniighaghaam : " Kaay , Ataneq Kiyaghneq Aghtughyaghqaghhaanghiteghllak , qepghalleghten seghleghllaguut , allaaghlluwhaghllaguut ! Kaay , umiilgat nunam yugita , elpek salleghten elqughutngaatlu ipanguutlu !
Ataneq , qamagtengngwaaghluteng yuget alikelleqaaten , quulvaghlleqaatlu aatghen ! Ellnginaaguten agleghnalghii ! Qamagtengngwaaghluteng nunatat manigughyaghtughlleqaaten , qayughllak liisimakegkangat nanqigtilleghten elqughutngalghiit ! "
Taam kingunganeng esghaghaqa qilagmi qelpeghtekangat Temple-a . ( Agleghnalleghpigaaguq Na , ellngan yugita liisimakusiqaat Kiyaghneq tawanniluku . )
Taagken maaghraghvinlek yaqulget aanleghaatut Temple-meng kelqelluteng maaghraghvinlegneng seghleliilleghllagneng . Tamaghhaghmeng atkuyaaghulluteng qateghrakegtameng nighulghiimeng , sakimagmegteggun gold-meng tafsiluteng .
Taagken ataasim unguvalghiim estamaneng taakuneng , gold-meng sagneliqughii maaghraghvinlek yaqulget . Taakut sagneghet imighngaat sakraalleghllaaganeng Kiyaghneghem , kiyaghlleghhii quunperugllak kenlengunaan .
Temple-em ilunga agepsughqaagaa Kiyaghneghem nighughqellghanengllu , aghtughyaghqaanghillghanengllu . Kina alngunak iteghnaanghituq Temple-mun kenlanga maaghraghvinlek seghleliilleghllaget kenletghuutellghitnun , tagitkiit maaghraghvinlek yaqulget .
Taagken Temple-meng nagaqughaqa iglagtulghii ma , ungipaaskangi maaghraghvinlek yaqulget , " Kuuvyaghtughteki nunamun maaghraghvinlek sagneghet Kiyaghneghem sakraalleghllagi ! "
Enkaam sivuliim yaqulgem sagneni kuuvyaghtughaa nunamun . Taagken seghlepestaaghllaget aqnighnapiglleghhiit pupiget piitquutut nalluniillengegkanun teghikusalluugmeng . Tamaakunguut maniguutkat nangaghneghanun .
Tuunglighhaan yaqulgem sagneni kuuvaa kelliinun . Taagken kellii aawatun tuqukam yugem lliighluni , enkaam qamaglluteng unguvalghiit kelliini tuqulaghaatut .
Pingayiitangita yaqulgem sagneni kuuvaa kiigwnunllu , sengngununllu meghnun enkaam aawughquutut .
Nagaqughaqa igleghutilghii meghneng yaqulek pilghii , " Kaay , Agleghnalghii Kiyaghneq , elpenguuq maaten kiyaghlleghhii , elpenguuq quunpeng kiyaghlleghhii ! Nanqigtilleghtenllu aghyuughilleghtenllu elqughutngaat .
Yuget tuququqaqiit yugten , uuknaliqistetenllu , enkaam meghyaghqalitaten aawmeng . Tawaten aghyuughyaghqaaluteng ellmeggneng allgeghtekaqaat ! "
Taagken nagaqughaqa aghqefigegneng ma pilghii , " Aa-a Ataneq , Kiyaghneq Aghtughyaghqaanghilnguq ! Ipanguutlu elqughutngaatlu nanqigtilleghqaghten ! "
Estamiitangita yaqulgem saghneni kuuvaa siqineghqun enkaam Kiyaghneghem siqinghem kenghanun paneghtestii yuget .
Siqinghem uguqnaghllagan paneghtestii yuget . Enkaam sanguughteghllagaat aatgha Kiyaghneghem , igleghutistengutanganeng tamaavek seghleliilleghllagnun . Avuteghqenghitutlu , usuqenghitaatlu Kiyaghneghem aangelleghllaga .
Tallimiitangita yaqulgem sagneni kuuvaa teghikusalluugem umiilgusiin aqumutagkenkun , enkaam ataneghpagullgha mamleghqwaagaa . Yuget ikfiqem uluteng amqeghqughiit .
Sanguughteghllagaat Kiyaghnegha qilagem apalluqluku aqnighqelleghmeggnengllu pupigtaalleghmeggnengllu . Avuteghqenghitutlu seghletun pilleghmeggneng .
Aghvinliitangita yaqulgem sagneni kuuvaa kiiwllagegnun Euphrates-egnun . Kiiwek pateghtuk yataaghqunnaluki tuumkaghqameng umiilget tagilghiit asivaghmeng .
Taagken esghaghanka pingayut nukeggnalghiit tughneghaat frog-esugnilnguut . Aanut qaanghitneng dragon-em , teghikusalluugem , uuknaliqistesighwaaghemllu .
Taakut tughneghaat allaaghlluwhaghtikayuguftut . Aghulaqut umiilgitnun nunataghhaan tamaghhaan qerngughhnaluki pilluwamun aghneghllagani Kiyaghneghem Aghtughyaghqaghhaanghilnguum .
Ataneq piiq , " Nagataghtek ! Taginguunga teglegniightetun ! Quyanaghtuq teghhumalghii , aatkani piiftengngwaaghluki ayuqegkangi . Enkaam igleghhnaanghituq amsikaghmi , kayngusaghaannaanghituqlu tesqagani yuget esghaqumegteggu ! "
Taagken tughneghaat qerngughtiit umiilget Armageddon-mun . Tawaten Hebrew-ghmiistun atillgha ayuquq .
Taagken maaghraghvinliitangita yaqulgem sagneni kuuvaa eslakun . Temple-mi umiilgusigneng aqumutaghllagegneng iglagtupiglluni ma piiq , " Apeghiightuq ! "
