Taawa nighwaagpagtaghtuq , tengngaagtaghtuq , kallituq , nunallu ufsuguteghllagtuq . Taana nunam ufsugutelleghllaga seghlelleghpigaaguq Kiyaghneghem yungllaghyuggallghaneng .
Neghllak pelleghtuq pingayughqelluni . Nunatlu neghllagit qamagtengngwaaghluteng naavuutut . Kiyaghneghem neqamikii Babylon-eghllagem seghleghqellghi . Enkaam meghestaa wine-a qayuusimelnguq sakritelleghllagmineng imaqelghii .
Qamaglluteng qiighqat aviighuquutut , qamagllutengllu naayghat kaavuutut .
Kaftekragrugllaget 100 uqigtutkavzilghiit qilagameng ifkaquutut yugnun . Enkaam tamaakut yuget sanguughteghllagaat Kiyaghneq apalluqluki kaftekragrugllaget . Taana seghleliilleghllak seghlepigulghii .
Taagken yaqulget maaghraghvinlegneng sagnelget , taakuneng ataasim takulunga piinga , " Tagi , kelguviknaqamken aghyuulleghqaaneng apeghseghuum aghnam yugusimineng akikikayugem , aqumgalghii meghllagteggun .
Nunam umiilgi seghleghqaqut atuqaqluku aghnaq . Seghleghet atuqistillghi wine-etun ayuqut , enkaam nunam yugi suumaqut meneghmegteggu wine-nga . "
Taagken yaqulgem Taghneghagnekun aglaataanga kilgaanun . Tawani esghaghaqa aghnaq aqumgalghii kavirrakegtakun teghikusalluugkun . Teghikusalluuk igaqughvikngaftuq uzimun sanguughtusineng ateghneng Kiyaghneghmun . Maaghraghvinlek naasqulguftuq , quulnguftutlu sighunghi .
Aghnaq pilugugngaftuq esneyaaghmengllu kavirrakegtamengllu , enkaam ullngaqluni gold-meng , akitughllagmeng uyghagmeng , pearl-mengllu . Tugumiiqeftaa gold-a qayuusiq esleqngalghii seghleghnalghiineng kiyaghtaalleghneng , nukeggnalghiinengllu sex-kun seghleghqellghaneng .
Qawaani igaqngaftuq ateq qayvighsimangilnguq whaten pisiq , Apeghseghuq Babylon , naakaat yugusimeggneng akikikayuget aghnat , seghleghnallghanengllu nunam .
Esghaghaqa aghnaq suumelghii aawitneng Kiyaghneghem yugita , aawitnengllu tuququqat qayughllak ataasiighmelnguut Jesus-mun . Esghaghluku aghnaq saghiighayugllagtunga .
Iwernga yaqulgem piinga , " Sangavek saghiighayugsin ? Ungipaannaqamken qayvighsimangilngughmeng sameng pisiitkek aghnaankuk , teghikusalluugenkuk . Taana teghikusalluuk igleghutilghii aghnameng , naasqulguuq maaghraghvinlek , sighunelguuqlu qula .
Teghikusalluuk esghaqan unguvayalghiinguuq , Iwernga tuqukaaguq . Mayughllequq Saamnangilngughmeng Laagwaaghmeng naafqellengnaluni . Yulguuq nunami aatghit igaqellghilnguut Igiitgun Unguvallghem nuna piinlillghilluku . Tamaakut yuget esghaqumegteggu teghikusalluuk saghiighayugllequt qayughllak unguvayalghii , tuqukaq iwernga tagiyaghqaq .
" Sumeghtaghayuqam liigikelleqaa una : Maaghraghvinlek naasqut maaghraghvinleguut qemit aghnam aqumgavigi .
Taakut naasqut maaghraghvinleguutlu umiilget . Tallimat tuqukaagut , ataasiq igleghutinguuq , enkaam ataasiq salin tagingigatuq . Tagikumi igleghutiyaghqaaguq natengiighhaq .
Teghikusalluuk unguvayalghii iwernga tuqukaq , pingayuneng ingluliitnguuq umiilek . Taana pingayuneng ingluliita umiilek ilakaat sivuliit maaghraghvinlek umiilget , naafqellengyaghtuuguq .
" Esghaqaghten qula sighunghet , qulanguut umiilget salin igleghutingigatut . Iwernga aghtughyaghqaanghillengellequt igleghutiyaghqaaluteng ataasiq aflu maligulluteng teghikusalluugmun .
Taakut ataasiq umyugaqluku tuunelleqiit teghikusalluugmun aghtughyaghqaanghilletengllu pilleghqatengllu .
Enkaam pilluwaghlleqaat Penniighaghaq . Iwernga Penniighaghaam kayaalqelleqii qayughllak Atanqegkangat atanghet , Umiilkegkangatlu umiilget . Penniighaghaghmelnguut tuqluqaagut , nakmikegkaagut , ataasiighmelnguugutlu . "
Taagken yaqulgem piinga , " Esghaghaten meghet aghnam yugusimineng akikikayugem aqumgavigi . Taakut meghet yulghuteghllaguut nunataghhaaneng tamaghhaaneng pinguut , ulukelghiit allaaghhiinaghmeng .
Esghaqaghpek qula sighunghet , teghikusalluugemllu , ugumiilleqaat aghnaq yugusimineng akikikayuk . Saqraggiighulluku , amsiqaghqelluku , kemga neghluku , taagken siipnegha kumaghlleqaat .
Taakut qula sighunghet tawaten pikaagut qayughllak Kiyaghneghem ellngitnun atuqestekaqaa piyukelleni . Angeghqumatkaagutlu tuunaluki ataneghpagulleteng teghikusalluugmun . Tawaten pikaagut kenlanga Kiyaghneghem piyukellgha apeghiillghanun .
Taana aghnaq esghaqan neghllaguuq igleghutilghii umiilgitneng nunat . "
Taam kingunganeng esghaghaqa ilanga yaqulek qilagmeng ukilghii . Aghtughyaghqaanghillelegllaguftuq , nighughqelleghmineng iingunaghhaan nuna nighugtaa .
Akilghuughllagtuq , " Naavumaaq ! Naavumaaq Babylon-eghllak ! Nekaaghsimaat tughneghaat , nukeggnalghiit tughneghaat , ukmanginneghilnguut kusgenalghiit qawaaget .
Babylon-em seghletun atuqillgha sex-meng wine-etun ayuquq , nunataghhan tamaghhaan meghaa . Nunam umiilgita atuqaqaat , nunamllu akilpegaghtengita aklungighisiqngwaat nuqetusaghqaanghilngughqun sex-kun atuqiyullghakun . "
Taagken nagaqughaqa ilanga ma qilagmeng pilghii , " Yumni , aanleghaatek Babylon-meng ! Ilategpenasi seghleghqellghanun aghyuullengnayukafsi ellnganun maligullusi .
Seghleghqellghi mayughteghllagngaat uusqaghtutkaghmeng qilagtun , Kiyaghneghem neqamikii seghleghqellghi .
Seghletun piteggu Babylon katam ellngan seghletun pillghatun . Malghughqelluku seghletun pillgha piteggu . Qayuusiikun kuuviteggu wine-a iknaqetulnga malghughqengngaan ellngan atuqaqegkanganeng .
Ellmineng usuqeghllagaquq , aklungighllanillu atuqaqaa samun alngunak piyukegkaminun . Enkaam ikfiqesteghllagteggullu qivghusteghllagteggullu atunekiitesluku qaghyalleghllaganun . Ellmineng piiquq , ' Queen-nguunga aqumgalghii umiilgusimkun . Ugingighaanghitunga enkaam qivghunaanghitngwaaghtunga ! '
Tamaaken apalluqluku aghneghhiinaghmi kaalleqaa tuqullghem , qivghullghem , neqangisagllagem . Taagken kenghem paneghlleqaa qayughllak aghyuughistenga , Ataneq Kiyaghneq , aghtughyaghqaanghiteghllagtuq . "
Nunam umiilgi ilatkat atuqillghanunllu qiliighyullghanunllu , esghaqumegteggu agepsaa panellghan qiyakelleqaat , iglagtupigllutengllu qiyakeghllaglleqaat .
Uyavanlluteng nekevellequt qayughllak alingelghiit ellmengllu ilannayukameng ikfiqellghanun . Pillequt , " Seghleghhaghmeng ! Seghleghhaghmeng elpek aangeghllak aghtiigalnguq neghllak , Babylon ! Aghyuullenguten ataasighhaghmi aflumi ! "
Nunam akilpegaghtengita qiyaaghwaatkaat qivghughllagumaghmeng , qayughllak kitum alngunak tukfighnaniqangit saghyangit .
Babylon-mi akilpegaghtet akikaqsaqangit gold-et , silver-et , akitughllaget uyghaget , pearl-etlu ; akikaqsaqangitlu qiipaghaghqat ulimaaghet linen-meng , silk-meng , qiipaghaghqatlu iqeghtaqelghiit esnegyaaghet , kavirrakegtatlu . Akikaqsaqangitlu tepkegtepiglleghhiit unaghsit , ulimaaghet naangquneng , akitughllagneng unaghsineng , siiluneng , savikenghaagneng , marble-enengllu .
Akikaqsaqangitlu cinnamon-et , spice-et , incense-et , myrrh-et , frankincense-et ; wine-et , olive-em mesiighi ; avlawat , wheat-et ; cattle-et , penniighet , kuunit , wagon-et ; talwa yuget akikaqsaqangit qepghaghtelaaghuluki .
Akilpegaghtet Babylon pilleqaat , " Qamaglluteng pinilghiit allgeghsukeghllakaghten aviighutut . Qamagllutengllu aklungighllagten qelmeghllaget aviighutut , allamengllu allgeghsaghqaananighaten ! "
Akilpegaghtet aklungighikat akikiluteng Babylon-mun , nekevghallequt uyavanlluteng qayughllak alingelghiit ilannayukameng ikfiqellghanun . Qiyallequt qivghughllagumaghmeng ,
whatenllu pillequt , " ' Seghleghwaaghuuq ! Seghleghwaaghuuq neghllak ! Aatkayuguyaghtuq linen-meng , esneyaaghmeng , kavirrakegtamengllu , ullngaqegkayuguyaghtuqlu gold-meng , akitughllagmeng uyghagmeng , pearl-mengllu !
Ataasimi aflumi aklungighllagiitaa ! ' " Qamaglluteng angyalget , yugit , passenger-ngit , akilpegaghtetlu igleghakayuget angyaghpagteggun allgeghunnaluteng kiyaghusighqameggneng , angyaghpagit aghuliiqat uyavanlluteng Babylon-meng kumaghaqngan .
Esghaghluku agepsaa kumallghan , akilghuugut , ' Alla neghllagituq whatelngughmeng ! '
Naasquteng pagulalightughiit qiyatkelluku , qivghutkelluku akilghuugut , ' Seghleghwaaghuuq ! Seghleghwaaghuuq neghllak ! Aklungighllaganeng qamaglluteng angyaghpalget aklungighikayuguyaghtut ! Iwernga ataasimi aflumi aklungighllagiitaa ! ' "
Taagken qilagmeng kina piiq , " Kaay qilagmelngughni , quyakiteggu qayughllak Kiyaghneghem naafqaa Babylon ! Quyatek Kiyaghneghem yugitni , apostle-eni , uuknaliqistenillu ! Kiyaghneghem aghyuughaa qayughllak seghletun pikaqegkangisi ! "
Taagken iknaqeghllalghiim yaqulgem kevgaa uyghagrugllak , grain-mun kagimtisistun ayuqelghii . Miluutaa kellimun , whaten pimaghmi , " Tawateghpigaq neghllak Babylon , Kiyaghneghem miluuteghllaglleqaa asitmun enkaam allamengllu esghaghnaanghitaat .
Kitum alngunak nagaqughnaanghitii harp-esteten , pillgughikat aynganangasteten , flute-esteten , qalghightaghtetenllu ! Qamaglluteng pillgughikat qepghaghteten aviighusaghqaagut , grain-meng kagimtesteten allallu nagaqughnaanghitiit !
Kenelghutam nighuga kuukgunnaanighnaquq elpeni . Mengik nulightughnaqelghiimllu ugiighnaqelghiimllu nagaqughnanighnaquk elpeni . Akilpegaghteten aghtiigatngwaaghyaghtut nunataghhaani tamaghhaani . Alignaghtaalleghpegun puughquqaqaten qamagtengngwaaghluki nunam yugi !
Babylon-mi taawa aawit uuknaliqistet , Kiyaghneghem yugi , qamagllutengllu tuqutkat nunami . "
Kingunganeng iknaqeghllalghiim yaqulgem akuzillghan , qilagmi nagaqughanka yulghuteghllaget akilghuulghiit , " Hallelujah ! Yugulilleq , quulvalleq , aghtughyaghqaanghilleqlu Kiyaghnemta pikii !
Ellngan nanqigtillghi ipanguut , elqughutngaat ! Ellngan aghyuuqaqaa apeghseghuq aghnaq yugusimineng akikikayuk qayughllak nunam yugi seghletun pistekangi sex-kun atuqestaqluni . Kiyaghneghem akitkaqaa qayughllak qepghaghtengi tuququghtestekangi . "
Yulghuteghllaget akilghuulaataghtut , " Hallelujah ! Neghllagem kumalghiim agepsaa mayuuguq quunperugllak kenlengunaan ! "
Taagken yuginaq estamat siipneqluki elder-et , estamatlu unguvalghiit niinghuquulluteng manigughaat Kiyaghneq , aqumgalghii umiilgusigmikun . Pikaat , " Amen ! Hallelujah ! "
Taagken umiilgusigneng aqumutaghllagegneng ma whaten piiq , " Usuqiteggu Kiyaghneghput , qamagllusi qepghaghtengani alikilghiini ellnganeng , ukavanlengughnillu aangwaaghnillu ! "
Taagken nagaqughanka llangaqa mengit yulghuteghllaget . Nagatkaaluteng suksugistun tevlughteghllalghiit meghet , kallugemllu tengngaagtallghatun ayuqluteng . Akilghuugut , " Hallelujah ! Ataneq Kiyaghneghput , Aghtughyaghqaghhaanghilnguq igleghutiiq !
Quyatelta , elngaatall quyaghllageltallu usuqelteggullu ! Penniighaghaam nengughtelleghqaa kaatuq , nuliighqaallu yataaghqumaaq .
Kiyaghneghem aasightuumaa ugiighnaqelghii pinighrakegtameng qatelghiimeng linen-meng . " ( " Linen-a " whaten pisiiguq , elqughutngalghiit aneghneghqillghet Kiyaghneghem yugita piiqegkangit . )
Taagken yaqulgem piinga , " Una igaqigu : Penniighaghaam nengughtellghan neqenghaghqellghanun neghyaghtiisqegkat quyastekaagut . " Whatenllu piinga , " Ukut ipanguut akuzitangi Kiyaghneghem . "
Taagken niinghutunga yaqulgem itegaakun manigughnaluku , iwernga piinga , " Tawaten pigpenang ! Manigughhu Kiyaghneq ! Qepghaataqaqa Kiyaghneq elpetun , ugpeqaalgutegpetunllu . Ellnginguut ataasiighmelnguut ipalleghmun Jesus-em apeghtuusaqegkaanun . Ipalleq Jesus-em apeghtuusaqegkaa taananguuq ipalleq Kiyaghneghem Taghneghagkenka uuknaliqistenun ungipaqestekaa . "
Taagken esghaghaqa qilak qelpelghii , taawa qatelghii kuuni ! Kuunikun igleghlleghhiim aatgha " Ataasiighmelnguq , Ipapik " . Elqughutngaat nanqigtillghi , pilluwaqangillu anguyani .
Iiskek kumaghullghatun kenghem ayuqlutek , naasqumikun qaghpalghutelguftuq . Aatgha ellngakun igaqngaftuq kitum alngunak nallukegkanga iwerngaqun ellnginaan .
Atkuyaaghek atukek neptekaaftuk aawkun . Aatqeftaa , " Kiyaghneghem Akuzitanga " .
Qilagmeng pilluwaghtengita maligsaaghaat uuglluteng qatelghiitgun kuunitgun , atkuyaaghluteng iqangilngughmeng qatelghiimeng linen-meng .
Qaanghaneng aanuq ipelghii savigpak , taaggun qamagtengngwaaghluki nakumiit kayaalqughlleqii . Igleghulleqii iron-meng anagutalighluni . Taagken tutmaghlleqii anguyani katam yuget tutmaghaqellghistun grapes-et qageghquusignilnguut . Taana tutmalleq sakraalleghllakaa Kiyaghneghem Aghtughyaghqaghhaanghilnguum .
Atkuyaaghakunllu qugtuqaakunllu igaqngaftuq ateq whaten ; Umiilga umiilget , Atangha atanghet .
Taagken esghaghaqa yaqulek nekevghalghii siqineghqun . Qamaglluki qawaalghutet quulvani tengaalghiit iglagtupiglluni pii , " Tagilaghaallusi qerngughutek Kiyaghneghem neqenghaghqelleghllaganun !
Tagitek , neghyaghtughteki kemegkwaaghit umiilget , pilluwaghtet umiilgit , pilluwaghtetlu . Neghyaghtughteki kemegkwaaghit kuunit , kuunikun igleghtestet , qamagllukillu yuget , qepghaghtelaaghet , qepghaghtelaaghunghilnguut , ukavanlenguut , aangwaaghetlu . "
Taagken esghaghanka teghikusalluuklu , nunamllu umiilgi , pilluwaghtekullghiit qerngughutut pilluwaghnaluku igleghlleghhii kuunikun , pilluwaghtengillu .
Tugwaagket teghikusalluugenkuk , uuknaliqistesighwaaghenkuk allaaghlluwaghtiighaataqaq tawanlluku teghikusalluuk . ( Allaaghlluwaghtiiqelleghmikun puughquqii nalluniillengegkat teghikusalluugmeng , maniguqaatlu nangaghnegha . ) Teghikusalluugenkuk , uuknaliqistesighwaaghenkuk unguvaagkenka miluutaak naayvam kenghanun kumaghulghiimun sulphur-meng .
Pilluwaghtengik kuunikun igleghlleghhiim tuququghii savigpagkun qaneghmineng aanegkakun . Taagken qamaglluteng qawaaget neghiit kemegkwaaghit kepsuqiinalleghmeggnun .
Taagken esghaghaqa yaqulek qilagmeng ukilghii tugumiiqluni key-nganeng Saamnangilnguum Laawaaghem , qiipraghuteghllagnengllu .
Kayaalqelluku dragon-a tuwaa . ( Dragon-a taananguuq ayumightaq nemeghyaq , aatgha Tughneghaq , Tughneghaq . ) Taagken yaqulgem asighqaa qiipraghutneng thousand ayumiqulleghnun .
Miluulluku Laawaaghmun , taagken amigmeng uumgulluku maghqatutkaa seal-eluku . Enkaam Dragon-em puughsaghqaananighii yuget kenlanga thousand ayumiqullghet alpallghitnun . Alpakata itemutaghlleqaat .
Taagken esghaghanka umiilgusit aqumutat , aqumgalghiitlu taakutgun . Kiyaghneghem nanqigtiyaghqaaghtestekii yugneng . Eshaghankallu unguvasiit tamaakut naasqwightuqiit apalluqluku Jesus . Ungipaqegkaqegkangat ipalleq Jesus-em qayvighqegkaa , akuzitangillu Kiyaghneghem . Taakut maniguusimangitut teghikusalluugmun , nalighmeng nangaghneghanun . Talwa qagumegteggun , nalighmeng iiggmegteggun allgeghtellghitaat nalluniilkutaa teghikusalluugem . Unguvaghtuulluteng igleghutilgusighaat Christ-a thousand ayumiqulleghnun .
Taana sivuliiguq unguvaghqulleq . ( Ilangi tamaakut tuqukat unguvaghtuunnaanghitut kenlanga thousand ayumiqullghet alpallghitnun . )
Tamaakut Kiyaghneghem unguvaghtekii unguvaghtuusuwhaalleghmi quyastekaagutlu agleghnaghtutlu . Tuqunaanghitut tuunglighhaani tuqullghem . Iwernga priest-ngunaqnguut Kiyaghneghmunllu Christ-amunllu . Igleghutilgusighlleqaatlu Christ-a thousand ayumiqulleghni .
Thousand ayumiqullghet alpakata , Tughneghaq anusimingllaghviganeng itemusaghqaaguq .
Enkaam aanluni puughqughlleqii nunatat mingitngalghiit nunataghhaani tamaghhaani . Tamaakut nunatat aatqiit Gog-enkuk Magog-enkuk . Yugik uglaghllagtut qenaavzeghaatun esnem . Taagken Tughneghaam qerngughlleqii pilluwamun .
Tughneghaam pilluwaghtengi iqelmun mingilluteng igleghllequt nunakun . Kaalluteng kangllulleqagket nunaaqlu Kiyaghneghem yugita nayaat , neghllaklu Kiyaghneghem piniqegkaa . Taagken qilagmeng Kiyaghneghem keneq ukigtesluku paneghtekii pilluwaghtet .
Taagken Tughneghaq puughtikaq nunataneng , Kiyaghneghem yaqulgita miluulleqaat naayvamun kumaghulghii sulphur-meng . Tawavek miluutkaqegkegket teghikusalluugenkuk , uuknaliqistesighwaaghenkuk . Tawani ikfiqeghllagllequt aghneghtuumaan unugtuumaan quunperugllak kenlengunaan .
Taagken esghaghaqa Kiyaghneq aqumgalghii qatelghiignekun umiilgusignekun aqumutaghllagegnekun . Nunallu qilagallu qimaaguutuk Kiyaghneghem tawantellghaneng , allallu esghaghyaghqaagpenatek .
Esghaghankallu tuqulaghaatkat , ukaliiwaqlutengllu aangwaaghwaaqlutengllu ayuqelghiit . Nekevghatnguftut sivungani umiilgusim aqumutaghllagem . Taagken igat qelpeghtiit , Igii Unguvallghem , igaqughvikegkat aatghitneng tamaakut unguvayaghqat quunperugllak . Ilangillu igalghutet qelpeghtiit igaqughvikegkat tuqukat kiyaghtaallghitneng ayuqelghiit . Kiyaghneghem nanqigtii atuqluki igaquqat igatgun .
Taagken kelliim tuqumasliini pegtii . Tuqullghemllu Hades-emllu tuqumasliitek pegtiik . Qamagtengngwaaghluki Kiyaghneghem nanqigtii kiyaghtaallghistun .
Taagken Tuqulleqlu Hades-lu miluutagket naayvam kenghanun . Naayvam kengha tuungliqaa tuqullghem .
Kitum alngunak aatgha igaqumangilkan Igaani Unguvallghem , miluutkaat naayvam kenghanun .
Taagken esghaghagka qilagraghaqlu nunaghraghaqlu . Qilaksuwhaaghiisimaaq , nunaksuwhaaghiisimaaq , kelliingiitkaaguqlu .
Esghaghaqallu Agleghnalghii Neghllak , Jerusalem-eghraghaq , ukilghii Kiyaghneghmeng qilagmelngughmeng . Neghllak yataaghqelluni ugiighnaqelghiim ullngaqellghatun ugiminun .
Nagaqughaqa ma iglagtupiglleghhii umiilgusigneng aqumutagneng pilghii , " Esghaqaghhuqun , Kiyaghneghem kiyaghfiga yugnituq ! Kiyaghfikelleqii enkaam ellngit yukelleqii . Kiyaghneq ellnga katam ellngitnillequq enkaam ellnga Kiyaghneqelleqaat .
Quningighlleqii qamaglluki . Tuqungiilleqaa , qivghungiilleqaa , qiyangiilleqaa , talwa aqnighqengngiilleqaa qayughllak tamaakut atuqsaqangit atuqnanighlleqiit . "
Taagken umiilgusignilnguq aqumutagni piiq , " Esghaqaghqiqun , ulimaaqanka sangwaat qamagtengngwaaghluki nutaghaaluki ! " Whatenllu piiq , " Igaqiki tamaakut aapqanka elpenun qayughllak tamaakut akuzitet ipanguut , ugpeqsaghqaagutlu . "
Piingallu , " Apeghiightuq ! Whanga Alpha-nguunga Omega-nguunga , whanga piinleghuunga kenlenguunga . Kina alngunak meqsulghii , akingunaan meghsilleqaqa sengngulghiimeng unguvallengestikayugmeng meghmeng .
Kitum alngunak kayaalqiilghiim allgeghlleqii tamaakut whangamneng . Kiyaghneqelleqaatnga enkaam ellngit avaqutaqelleqanka .
Iwernga tamaakut quyughtalghiit , ugpeqillghilnguut , seghlelleghpigaghneng seghleghqelghiit , yugtaghtet , nengughtegpenateng atuqullghiit , alignalghiit , maniguutkayuget kiyaghnengllaqanun , qamagllutengllu iqlengalghiit , nekaghqaat naayvaaguq kumaghulghii keneghmengllu sulphur-mengllu . Taananguuq tuunglii tuqullghem . "
Taagken yaqulget maaghraghvinlegneng sagnelget esleqngalghiineng kingulighneng seghleliilleghllagneng , ataasim taakuneng takwaanga . Piinga , " Tagi , kelguviknaqamken Ugiighnaqelghiimeng , nuliighqaa Penniighaghaam . "
Kiyaghneghem Taghneghagkenkun yaqulgem tugulunga aglaataanga uusqalleghpigaanun naaygham . Tawani kelgutaa Jerusalem , Agleghnalghii Neghllak ukilghii Kiyaghneghmeng qilagmelngughmeng .
Kuukgutngaghmi Kiyaghneghem nighughqellghaneng . Neghllak kuukgutuq akitughllalghiitun uyghagtun , jasper-etun , meghraakegtutkaghmi crystal-etun .
Uusqaghllagmeng mingllutelek , qula maalghuk siipneqluku amigllalgaataq . Qula maalghuk siipneqluku yaqulget amigllagniteftut . Ataasikaghtaghmeng amigllaget igaqfikngaftut ateghmeng qula maalghuk siipneqluku ramkenganeng Israel-em .
Mingllutanga neghllagem qula maalghuk siipneqluku amigllalek , pingayut asivaghmi , pingayut aywaani , pingayut ikevaghmi , pingayut pakfallami .
Neghllagem mingllutanga tunemiqaaftuq qula maalghuk siipneqluku uyghagneng . Ataasikaghtaghmeng uyghaget igaqfikngaftut ateghmeng qula maalghuk siipneqluku apostle-nganeng Penniighaghaam .
Yaqulek aleghqughteka gold-meng usputalguftuq usputaghnaluku neghllak , amigllagillu mingllutangallu .
Neghllak ulluviighrakegteftuq tagtalnga , pateghtulngatun ayuqeftuq . Yaqulgem neghllak usputaghyaqminigu : 1,500 miles tagtalkeftaa , pateghtulkeftaa , uusqaghtulkeftaallu .
Mingllutangallu usputaghyaqminigu , 216 feet-nguftuq uusqaghtulnga . Yaqulgem usputallghatun ayuqeftuq yugem usputallgha .
Mingllutanga ulimaaghuftuq jasper-meng . Neghllak ulimaaghuftuq gold-eperegwaaghmeng . Gold-a meghraakegtepiglleghhii siqinwhaaghtun .
Neghllagem mingllutangan tunemii pinighnaaqusighluteng allaaghhiinaghneng akitughllagneng uyghagneng . Sivuliq jasper-nguftuq , tuunglighhaa sapphire-nguftuq , pingayiitangat agate-nguftuq , estamiitangat emerald-nguftuq ,
tallimiitangat onyx-nguftuq , aghvinliitangat carnelian-nguftuq , maaghraghvinliitangat chrysolite-nguftuq , pingayuneng ingluliitangat beryl-nguftuq , estamaneng ingluliitangat topaz-nguftuq , quulngughutangat chrysoprase-nguftuq , qula ataasiq siipniitangat jacinth-enguftuq , qula maalghuk siipniitangat amethyst-nguftuq .
Qula maalghuk siipneqluku amigllaget pearl-nguftut , tamaghhaghmeng amigllaget ataasimeng pearl-meng ulimaaghuftut . Neghllagem tuumngi gold-eperegwaaghuftut ; gold-a meghraakegtepiglleghii siqinghwaaghtun .
Neghllagmi esghaanneghitunga Temple-meng , qayughllak Temple-nga Atanghuuq Kiyaghneq Aghtughyaghqaghhaanghilnguq , Penniighaghaaguqlu .
Neghllak siqineghsughniituq , nalighmeng tanqighsughniituq nighugkameng , qayughllak nighughqellgha Kiyaghneghem nighukegkanga , Penniighaghaqlu kenelghutaqegkanga .
Qamagtengngwaaghluteng nunam yugi kiyaghllequt nighugakun kuukgutngalghiikun . Nunamllu umiilgita aklungiteng tagiquutiit neghllagmun .
Neghllagem amigllagi umegnaanghitut aghneghem naangneghani qayughllak unugnaanghilnguq tamaani .
Nunam yugita neghllagmun tagiquulleqiit pinighnaghllaget aklungiteng .
Iwernga neghllagmun iteghyaghqaanghituq sangwaa seghleq , talwa kina alngunak seghleghnatun pista , nalighmeng iqlengiqesta . Iwernga neghllagmun iteghyaghqaagut tamaakunginaghhaat aatghit igaqngalghiit Igaakun Unguvallghem . Taakut Igat Penniighaghaam pikii .
Taagken yaqulgem kelguvikaanga kiiwegneng maaqelghiik Kiyaghneghemllu Penniighaghaamllu umiilgusigkenka aqumutagkeneng . Unguvallelitikayugmeng melgek , meghraakegtutkalghiik crystal-etun .
Maaqngalghiik qukaakun tumangan neghllagem . Kiiwek inglugtun uqfigtuqak unguvallelitikayugneng . Tamaghhaghmi uqfik piitestikayuguuq fruit-neng tanqiinaghqun , ayumiqulleghmi , ququngiitlu naallghutusiiftut nunataanun .
Sangwaa alngunak Kiyaghneghem nanqigtekaa aghyuughyaghqaaluku , neghllagmennaanghituq . Kiyaghneghenkuk Penniighaghhaankuk umiilgusik aqumutagket neghllagmesaghqaaguk , Kiyaghneghemllu qepghaghtengita manigughlleqaat .
Gginaa esghaghlleqaat , aatghallu qawiitgun igaqngallequq .
Tamaani unugnanighlleqaa , kenelghutaghsughniighulleqii , nalighmeng siqineghsughniighulleqii , qayughllak Ataneq Kiyaghneq nighukelleqaat . Igleghutillequtlu umiilguluteng quunperugllak kenlengunaan .
Taagken yaqulgem piinga , " Ukut akuzitet ugpeqsaghqaagut , ipanguutlu . Atanghem , Kiyaghneghem igleghutilghiim taghneghiitneng uuknaliqistemi , kayagtekaqaa yaquleni kelguvikesqelluki qepghaghteni sangwaat piyaghtungestaghniluki . "
Jesus piiq , " Nagatek ! Tagiyaghtughtunga ! Quyastekaagut qaatkullghiit uuknaliqelleghnun igaqngalghiinun ukutgun igatgun . "
Whanga , John , nagatkaqankallu esghaqaqankallu tamaakut . Nagaqughaqngamkillu esghaghaqngamkillu tamaakut , niinghutunga yaqulgem itegaani manigughnaluku , kelguvikisteka tamaaken .
Iwernga piinga , " Tawaten pigpenang ! Whangallu qepghaghtenguunga elpetun , ugpeqaalgutegpetunllu uuknaliqistestun , qaatkullghiistunllu akuzitangitnun ukut igat . Manigughhu Kiyaghneq ! "
Piingallu , " Aksaqegpenaki uuknaliqellghet ukut igat aapqiit , qayughllak tamaakut pilleghqiit kaasaghtuumaat .
Kina alngunak seghletun pilghii nagneghli seghletun , enkaam kina alngunak nukeggnameng suumqelghii nagneghli nukeggnameng suumqelluni . Kina alngunak elqughutngalghii nagneghli elqughutngaluni , kinallu alngunak pelungilnguq nagneghli pelungilluni . "
Jesus piiq , " Nagatek ! Tagiyaghtughtunga ! Akileghtuusaghqanka kelqelleqanka nallangightughnaluki yuget kiyaghtaallghistun .
Whanga Alpha-nguunga Omega-nguunga , whanga sivuliigunga kinguliigunga , whanga piinleghuunga kenlenguungallu . "
Quyastekaagut tamaakut atkuyaateng aghvikiit iqangiitesluki . Tamaaken apalluqluku neghyaghqaaghtekaagut piitestekaaneng unguvallelitikayugem uqfigem . Iteghyaghqaaghtekaagutlu neghllagem amigllagitgun .
Iwernga neghllagem eslataanilnguut qikmiigut , alignalghiinguut , nengughtegpenateng atuqistenguut , yugtaghtenguut , kiyaghnengllaqanun maniguutestenguut , iqlengiqsuneghtuut , iqlengiqumanginaghaqutlu .
" Whanga , Jesus , kayagtekaqaqa yaqulka elpesinun ugpeqanun yughaghvignilngughnun . Apeghlleqaak ukuk elpesinun , ' Whanga David-em kingunqaanga , whanga nighugrakegtaagunga unaangum ighaleqetaagha . ' "
Taghneghaklu Ugiighnaqelghiillu piik , " Tagi ! " Tamaghhaghmillu nagallghii pili , " Tagi ! " Kina alngunak meqsulghii tagili ; tuguklighligu akingilnguq meq unguvallelitikayuk .
Whanga , John , kelengasaaghyuganka nagallghiit uuknaliqelleghnun igaqegkatgun ukutgun igatgun . Kitum alngunak ilaraaqaki uuknaliqutkegkat ukuni igani , Kiyaghneghem aghyuughlleqaa . Ellnganun ilalleqii tamaakut seghleliilleghllaget igaqngalghiit ukutgun igatgun .
Kitum alngunak ikuvikegkaki uuknaliqutkegkat ukuni igani , Kiyaghneghem iqilleqii nengighqii piitestekat uqfiganeng unguvallelitikayugem . Kiyaghtesnaanghitaallu agleghnalghiimi neghllagmi . Taakuk apeghngaak ukuni igani .
Jesus-nguuq aapghilghii tamaaken qamaglluteng ipanguniluki . Piiqlu , " Ipapestaaq tagiyaghtughtunga ! " Amen . Tagi , Ataneq Jesus !
Nangllegtallgha Atanemta Jesus-em tamaghhaghpesinilli . Amen .
